MAT 1:1 Bifimer naniya Yecu Kiritti bibwe Dauda, bibwe Abrahame.
MAT 1:2 Abram co te Icaku, Icaku te Yakub, Yakub te Yahuda kange Yitub ceb.
MAT 1:3 Yahuda co te Farica Kange Jera fiye Tamar wiye, Farica nyori te Hacruna. Hacarua co te Arame.
MAT 1:4 Aram co te Aminadabe, Aminadab co te Nacone, Nacon co te Calmone.
MAT 1:5 Calmon co te Buaja fiye Rahab wiye, Boaja co te Obida fiye Rut nine. Obida co te Yeece.
MAT 1:6 Yecce co te Liya Dauda, Liya Dauda co te Culemanu fiye wii Yuriya wiye.
MAT 1:7 Culemanu co te Rehobwame, Rehobwam co te Abija, Abija co te Aca.
MAT 1:8 Aca co te Yehocafa. Yehocafa co te Yorame, Yorame cote Uziya.
MAT 1:9 Uziya co te Yotame, Yotam co te Ahaze, Ahaz co te Hezekiya.
MAT 1:10 Hezekiya co te Manacca. Manacca co te Amone, nyori Amon co te Yociya.
MAT 1:11 Yociya co te Yekoniya kange yitub cebo, dong-dong fiya cuwo ci yem ci, ci yaaken kici biten Babila.
MAT 1:12 Bwiko ci yem ci, ci yaken ci biten Babila. Yekoniya co te Ceyaltiyele. Ceyaltiyele co te Zarubabele.
MAT 1:13 Zarubabel co te Abihudu. Abihudu co te Eliyakime, nimre Eliyakim co te Azuru.
MAT 1:14 Azuru co te Caduku. Caduku co te Akimu, nire Akimu co te Aliyudu.
MAT 1:15 Aliyudu co te Ali'azara, Ali'azara co te Matana. Nimre Matana co te Yakube.
MAT 1:16 Yakubu co te Yucubu bwe Maryamu wo fiye ci wiye ci bo Yecu wo ci cuwo ti ki Almaciu.
MAT 1:17 Core tau Ibrahim nin yaken ciko Dauda nineu kaltito kwob culombo naar, kange wo tau fiye yeka ciko ci yaken ki ci Babilau yaken ciko Kiritti nin, kaldo kwob culombo naar.
MAT 1:18 Bor Yecu Kiritti ko bwi nyo wo. Nece Maryamu ciya an nam Yucufu, naci nakangiri Maryamu kweri tum fer yuwa tangbe wucake.
MAT 1:19 Yucufu bwece nii cakcake, cuibo ci neco kwenduwe nuwe nobe, nyori cuiti naci nyangum kang cinen daar.
MAT 1:20 La ci kwa diker buro tiri, bibwe tomange kwama wucake cerkangu cinen mor dukume. yi coti “Yucufu bi bwe Dauda nuware tai, tum Maryamu wimwe, wori dike ci tum ciko fwereu ca fiya yuwa tangbe wucake nen.
MAT 1:21 can do bwe, mwa cuwo dencere ki Yecu, co ca fulo nubo ti fiye bwiran ker ciye.
MAT 1:22 Gwam wo an bwi na dim diker teluwe be toke nyii nii tomange, tokti ki,
MAT 1:23 “To bubya an tu fwer, naci bo bwe ciya cuwo den cero ki Imanuel” Dike dendo nungeu “Kwama wi kange bo”.
MAT 1:24 Yucufu kwenu dumbo nineu, maani na wo bwe tomange kwama yiceu, cin kuni con tu wice.
MAT 1:25 Yucufu Nyomombo wice wi co bom bwe La con co dendo Yecu.
MAT 2:1 Bwikako ci bo Yecu Baitalami biten Yahudiya ki core wo Hirudu Liyau, Kangem nob nyomka bifumer kwama bo Urcalima. Tokti ki.
MAT 2:2 “Fee wo ci bo Liya Yahudawa? nyon to bitiren cero twar, nya bo na nyi wabka.
MAT 2:3 La Liya Hiridu nuwa nyori, kwom co kambo ken kange hwam nubo Urcalima.
MAT 2:4 Hiridu mwer Liyab wabe kwama gwam kange nob mulankab nibe. me ci “kiriti a bo fe?” Cin yi co.
MAT 2:5 “ Mor Baitalami Yahudiya nyo won co dike bibei tomange kwama mulange”.
MAT 2:6 “Mo Baitalami mor biten Yahudiya mo kebo wo duwal-duwali tiber Liyab yahudiya. more mwe an fiya nii a ca Liyar tiye wo a yila nii biyuwar nobo Lomi Iciraila”.
MAT 2:7 La Hiridu cwo nob nyomka bifumer reu, yurangum Yurange, me ci “Fiyang bitiren do cerkanguwe?”.
MAT 2:8 Con twom ci Baitalami, yiciti, “Kom ya ki fuwa bwe biduware ki Lima ki Lima, no kom fiya ri, ko bou kom yiye, na mo ken nan ya nan wabco.”
MAT 2:9 Bwikako ci nuwa diker Liya yi ciye ri cin kwen ci ta nure, bitiren do wo ci to twareu yakenti ka ci ya yan titi dor luwe bwe bi duware wiye.
MAT 2:10 La ci to bitirndo ri cin bilangi ki bilankako dur.
MAT 2:11 Cin do mor luwe, nen cin to bwe bi duwareu kange nece Maryamu. cin cung bitine cin wabco. cin kwim cwaye ciye neco Lima nerek, mwinek kange lubban kange mor.
MAT 2:12 Kwama yi ci mor dukume, ciya yilare fiye Hiridu nine. yori cin yilaken bitine ciye nure kange.
MAT 2:13 Bwikako ci kweneu cin to nii tomange teluwe cerkangu Yucufu nin yi co, “Kwen tu bwe bi duwae wo kange bece cwa cu ciko biten Masare.
MAT 2:14 Kume cuwo Yucufu tu bweu kange nece u Masar. yi ken firen yinen di na nimre, wori Huridu cuiti na twalum bweu.
MAT 2:15 Cin yike fire Hiridu Bwiyati. Wo na dim diker teluwe be tokeu nyi nii tomange, “Min cuwou bi bwemi Masar”.
MAT 2:16 Hiridu to nob nyomka Bifumereu bwanten bo ker cero ri mam funer ducce, cin twomi a twalangum bi bei nabarubbe bi duwartini gwam, wo Baitalami kange buro bi dom kange ce tati coro yob yirau ciko bitine.
MAT 2:17 Fiya cuwo la dike nii tomange Irimiya toke dimme.
MAT 2:18 Cin nuwa diro kange Rama ci wiye ti kinero fir cilong-cilonge, Rahila ci wiye dor bi beiyo locer. Mani ca fiya birum nere ti wo mani.
MAT 2:19 Fiya cuwo Hiridu bwiyame, nii tomange teluwe cerkangu Yucufu nin mor dukume mansar. yi co,
MAT 2:20 Kweni tu bwe bi duwarewo kange nece yakan Iciraila, nyori niwo do dume bwetiye bwiyam”.
MAT 2:21 Yucufu kweni tu bwe bi duware kane nece cu biten Iciraila.
MAT 2:22 La ci nuwa Akilayu bi bwe Hiridu Ca liyar ti biten Yafudiya, con nuwa tai lakako firen. Bwikako kwama yi co ker mor dukume, cin tiyangum biten Galili.
MAT 2:23 Yiken fiye kange ci cuwo ti ki Nazaret wo na dim dike ci toki nyii nob tomange ki, “Ciya cuwo co ki bwe nazare re.
MAT 3:1 Kume ni wo Yuwana yu mwem kwamam tiyeu yau ne fulen ker kwama ro ti.
MAT 3:2 Ko yiloten wori, liyar do lo kwama dadom.
MAT 3:3 won co wo nii dukume kaya tok kerce reu, “Dir nii kanger co bi cor ti kii, toki, “ko Yuwel Teluwe nin nureceu, fuwak ceko atim.
MAT 3:4 Yuwana merum ki belle yiri teleme, bwam ki dk teak fer cer. Cari ceu, kwake kange yuiti to kiyeu.
MAT 3:5 Co rubo Urcalima kange wo Yahudiya gwam, kange bitine tinim bo kong Urduneu, ci bou ti ka bo ka tuje co wiyeu.
MAT 3:6 Na ci yuu cinen mwem kwamam caji Urdun, kambo ci tok bwira kerer ce tiyeu.
MAT 3:7 La co to Faricawa kange cadukiyawa kila cirangum ti na co yu'u cinen mwem kwamamedi co ca ciye, “Kom berin nacuwe ki mwan neu, we wer kom ko cuam funero wo au tiye.
MAT 3:8 Ko ne bituti wo a nung yila ka kume ko tiyeu.
MAT 3:9 Ku kware mor ne kume kom ki Abram te kume! be ma yi kom ti, kwama wi kibi kwan do wo a kung Abram nin bibeiti fo tetendo wuro neneu.
MAT 3:10 Na wonyeu yoti biteye dimer tiniro nan, na cori tiyowo ne bo bituti keneti, an tom co na merken mor kire.
MAT 3:11 Ma Yukumen mwem kwamam bo ki mwem, ya ciko yo laka kumekeu. Niwo bouti bui mi yeu layeki dur, woro ta ceu ma labo nan tu'u. co ca yu'u kumen mwem kwamam bo ki yuwa tangbe kwama, kange kira.
MAT 3:12 Kwele yu'u ka ceko tam kang cek, can nyinagum teneu wiyak, na murom bikateceu na yo ken binico.”
MAT 3:13 La Yecu bou biten Galili, ya caji Urdun fintange Yuwana nen, na yu'u cinen mwem kwamam.
MAT 3:14 La Yuwana mani naco kicim co, tok ti ki, mo wo ma cuiti na yu'u mwem kwamam meu, mom bou minen?”.
MAT 3:15 Yecu yila yi co a ma nyo na dim cak-cakeu gwam. Co Yuwana ciya cinene.
MAT 3:16 Buiko ci yu'u cinen mwem kwamam be di, Yecu cerum can duwo mor mwenge, La dii kwama wo cinen. La co to yuwa tangbe kwamako yirau ti docer na nagumfiye, yira yiti dorcer.
MAT 3:17 La diro kange lo kwama ceru toki, wo bi bwemi ma cui cuiyeu, ma nuwa luma cek ti.
MAT 4:1 La yuwa tangbek kwamako tu Yecu yaken ciko mor yere na bwekelkele na cuwaco.
MAT 4:2 Bwiko co yi yim Ngakem kakuko kwini na'ar kumeu kwini na'ar di wura tam co.
MAT 4:3 Nii cuwa kako bou cinen yico ki, “No mo bibwe kwamari yi tero wo ayilam cari”.
MAT 4:4 Yecu yila yic mulagum mulange, Nii mani a dwiti ki cari ki kwace ce kange ker kwamar.
MAT 4:5 La bwekelkele to co yaken ciko mor cinan lor wucakeu. La kung ken co dor ku waber.
MAT 4:6 La yii co ki “No mo bibwe kwama ri, mwou bitine wori mulangum-mulange, ki “Can yi bibei tomange ce wucakeu na cer nen” La ci an kungum nen dii mor kani ciye. be na mo kware na mwek ter”.
MAT 4:7 Yecu yi ten co mulangum mulange mani mwa cuwa teluwe mwe kwama ti ko.
MAT 4:8 Tak, di Bwekelkele tu co kungken co bang ko wo cwem-cwemeu, La nung cenen Liyar do kaleweu gwam kange duktanka ciye ko.
MAT 4:9 La yico ki dike wo gwam man neken nen no mon cung cunge mo wab yeri.
MAT 4:10 La Yecu yico ki “kubom fou bwekelkele be mulangum mulange, Wab ka teluwe mwe kwama co win.
MAT 4:11 La bwekelkele dobco, La wo bibei tomange wucakeu bou cinen (wabco).
MAT 4:12 La Yecu nuwa cin tam Yuwanari, con cerum yilan ken Galili.
MAT 4:13 Co dubom Najaret cin yaken Kafanahum, wuro knog caji Galiliyeu, yii ka bitinek Jebulun Kange naftali.
MAT 4:14 wo ma nye na dim kero Icaya nii dukume tokeu.
MAT 4:15 biten Jebulune biten Nabtali wo kong Cajiyeu, kange dinge caji Urdun neu, Galili nob kumtacili.
MAT 4:16 Nubo wuro yim kumtacili yeu, cin to filanko dur, la buro yim wi fiyeceu, knage kakulok bware keu, dor cir fiya filanko ti kweni.
MAT 4:17 La fiyaco di Yecu yoten fulonka ker kwama ro, ko yolaten wori liyaro loh Kwama biyeken bidom.”
MAT 4:18 co yakenti knog caji Galili, con to yitob butib yob, cimon wo co tiki Bitru, kange Andrawu yii ce mer biliyar ti mor caji, cin nobtaka jingeb.
MAT 4:19 Yecu yii ci, kom bou ko buang menten, an yo ka ta men nob.
MAT 4:20 Dang jang ci dubom liyar cero cin buang ten co.
MAT 4:21 La Yecu dubom wi yaken tiri con to ten yitobbo kange ci yob, Yakubu bi bwe Jabali knage Yuwana yii ce, ci yim mor nabire mwenge kange jabal Tee ciye yulang biliyar ceroti.
MAT 4:22 Con co ci dang jang cin dubom nabire mwengeu kange jabali tee ciye, cim bwang ten co.
MAT 4:23 Yecu kentangum Galili gwam, merang cinen ti mor bikur waber, tok fulen ker liyar kwamaro ti twa'a mwanti tiire ti gwam kange nubo nuwabo lumau.
MAT 4:24 La fulen kere ro dor cereu yake kale mor nubo ciriya, co nubo co ci bou cinen ki nubo wo kalati ki wang ki wang kange kwirom bwi kange buro kelkelibo o cinen ti bwiyeu, kange nob juibe, kange nubo kani kange nani bwiyarangumeu, Yecu twm ci.
MAT 4:25 Nubo nawo kila kilau bwang cinen ten Galili kange dika foli kange Urcalima kange biten Yahudiya, yaken ciko dinge Urdun neu.
MAT 5:1 Kambo Yecu to mwerkang ka nubo ducceri kwiken dor bang-er. La cin yikenwi, nob bwankacebo bou cinen.
MAT 5:2 Wumom mor nerer ciro takri to merang cinen.
MAT 5:3 Bi bwiyer kiniwo bwini na yuwa tangbeceu nyori liyar kwama ki cii.
MAT 5:4 Bibwiyer kiniwo kibwatummeu, wori ciyatin macinen dangnee.
MAT 5:5 Bibwiyer ki nubo wo ki kunne wori kwalito dorbitinero ki cii.
MAT 5:6 Biwiyer ki nub wurab kange dulo mwe wucakke wori atin bwam ki cii.
MAT 5:7 Bibwiyer ki nub cika bwinib wori, atinci bwinicito.
MAT 5:8 Bibwiyer ki nubo nero wucakkeu, wori ciyen to kwama.
MAT 5:9 Bibwiyer ki nubo ki fuwer nerereu, wori a cociki bi biylo kwama.
MAT 5:10 bibwiyer ki nubo wuro cii ne cii dotangeti ker caccaker, liyar kwama ki cii.
MAT 5:11 Bibwiyer ki kom no nubo to komtiri, yila cii ne kom dotange ti ka kaa cii kwakomti kiner kan-nge bi kulentito bwir wo cuwer keceu, kermin.
MAT 5:12 Kom ma bilangtum bo man ki dii kau, wori Bitininge kumeu na dur dii kwama. Nan wo nubo ne bibei tomange dotange biro yii kaale na nyime komeu.
MAT 5:13 Kom mam dor bitinerembo cano mambo lem lumacekori, bi'amanyi na yilau cuko tak? mani ani yilamti kinan'ngen tak dila atin cutan wi na fuwarangum kina nubek.
MAT 5:14 Kom filang dor bitinero kowo cinar loro tom bidukleu mani yurangek.
MAT 5:15 Nubo mani kwer talkire tire dokken mor bulene, nyori ca kunnyii cayo fiye tikacek nane nubo luweu filang.
MAT 5:16 No nyori filang kume k acera kabum nubem ciya tom yorak na ngenek kumekotiyeu naci caklang tee kume wo dii kwama.
MAT 5:17 Km kware komki mabou nan bubam werfun nobto mangebo. ma boubo nan bubamci Dila nan dimci.
MAT 5:18 Wori bilenker miyi komti, diko kange bitineu an dim dila kiker biduwar kakaa denka win wo mani dimti mor bolang atin dim dikero kang.
MAT 5:19 Nawori niwo kimwo duwal duwale mor werfunen wonine kakaa ci merang kangum ciya manyeri, aciioco nawo duwal-duwale mor liyar kwamar.
MAT 5:20 Lari miyi komti miki “cawo-cawo cakcake kumeu tano labo cakcake nob mulangkab kange faricawbori, mani kakadokanti liyar kwamareu.
MAT 5:21 Kom nuwa kam inyi nubo nan duweu, kom taide dor, cano wo twaldoreri cikino cito warka.
MAT 5:22 La min yi kom ti woma funer kange keceri, kino mor cito warka. woyi kece, mun nifiro bwireri! cikino mor cito doka mor kirak kwamak.
MAT 5:23 Nawo nyori mwane funer nerer ti. tanyi landi kwabi kemwe wiki kwomka dorek kange mori,
MAT 5:24 Dubom luman nerok kabum tan nyi lanem, yaa yam mwem. ki kabana, fuwang kangum kange kemwe na nyi me nabou na ne funer nerer mwero.
MAT 5:25 Maa yuelka kange nii kiyangnye mwe kambo mudor nurer yaa kabum bolangem, ka nii kiyange mwe neken nen nii bolange nin nibolange an neken nen nii tomange ciyatin merkennen furcina.
MAT 5:26 Bilinker mi yinenti, mani mwa certi wi firen dila mwatin yati kemero ci bwang mwenten tieu.
MAT 5:27 Kom nuwa toki mare buraka.
MAT 5:28 Dila miyi komti, tona niwo to nawi ye, ki dilanka nuwa keri, cin kweri cin mam buroka kange co mor nerece.
MAT 5:29 Ca no nuwa me cacciyoro an dok nen kottankari, kurangum co, minangwi fiye muwiyeu. La diker win mor ayak cam, ca merbo curen buyet mwero gwam mor kira kwamak.
MAT 5:30 Kakaa kom mweko cacciyero tano atin atim dok nen kottang kari, mwattumco miranwi fiye muwiyeu. wori in La diker win mor a yakcam, kange merka buye mweko gwam kirak kwama.
MAT 5:31 Yilam to ki niwo ywa wice ri, a neco bifumer nyaka kangeko.
MAT 5:32 Dila miyi komti tano wo ywa wiceri, cano nobo dor kangka diker kayakardi, cin yilam kico ni burokak.
MAT 5:33 Kom nuwa ten cin yi ki nubo burombo nan duwoo kom werde weri cwerke, dila kwama werka kumeko kwamanin.
MAT 5:34 Dila miyi kom ti komti kom werde weri di kwamaka wori Nkunjala kwama;
MAT 5:35 kakaa kange dorbitiner fititim nanice, kakaa Wurcalima, wori biten liya dur.
MAT 5:36 Ca bu nano ka werweri ki dor kumerdi, la mani ka dolti kom yilam ki yiri duwekume fuwoje kakaa fije.
MAT 5:37 Dila Ker kumero a yilam NYO Nyo, nonindi 'Nyonin, nyonin. Cano dikero cumweri, kino bwirkonin.
MAT 5:38 Kom nuwa toki ki, Nuwe nyii nue nundo tak nyii nunne.
MAT 5:39 Dila miyi komti kom mare Kwobkangka kange niwo na bwireu, nyiyoco nyeu, no cii malicom dan-nge cattiyereri, kom yilam cinen wineu ken.
MAT 5:40 No ni kannge wii a yakenti ki kiyange kume kabum boulangem meriwori naci yo belle kueri kom netten nii wo lalan kumeko.
MAT 5:41 Cano ni dokkom yam nako kwininugri kom ya kannyace yob.
MAT 5:42 Komne nii wo mekomeu, tak kom kware niwo do naan ti kumeneu.
MAT 5:43 Kom nuwa dike tokeu, mwan cii ni bidome mweu mwanko ni kiye mweu.
MAT 5:44 Dila min yi kom ti kom cii nob kiyeb kume bo, kom kwob nubo nekom dotannge tiye nin dilo kom ma nubowuri, cil komenin bibuyer, komma nubo wo ko kom tiyeu nin dikoro ken.
MAT 5:45 Naweu nakom yilam bibiyo lo tekume wo dikwamau. wori dok kakuko wennii bwirninti kannge nii ken twom wucakke kannge nii maakenin mwom dikwamati.
MAT 5:46 Wori cano kom ki cwi nubowuri cwikom tiyeri, nyii dikedde kom fiya? kebonyo nob yoka doreko matiya?
MAT 5:47 Kume keneu tano kom yarum ka 'Kebkumebri, yekamani la tangece? kobonyo nubo nyombo kwamau matiya?
MAT 5:48 Dila naweu nyi lam nyo kom yilam cikocok nawo tekumu wodiyeu.
MAT 6:1 Kom yilam yiber dover ko mare luma kume ko kabum nubem be naci tokom, no kom ma nyori, mani ka fiya cuneti fiye tee kume wo dii kwama wiyeu.
MAT 6:2 La naweu, no kama luma tiri kom cure cume kambo nubo bwirko mati ku wabe kannge dor nurereu wori na nubo caklang ci. Bilinker miyi kmo ti cin fiyam nyii diker cero.
MAT 6:3 La tano kama luma tiri kam kume moutkeu anyomde dike kango cattiyero matiyeu.
MAT 6:4 Wori na lumake meko na yilam yurangum yurannge. Tee kume wuro to dikeroti yuragum yurangeu, atin makumen cuner.
MAT 6:5 Tano kmbo ka kwob diloti takeri, kom yilam de na nubo bwirko, wori ci cwikwoka diloti timotiye ku wabece kannge cuga nurek tak, wori na nubo toci. bilenker miyi kom ti cinn fiyam cuner ceko fou kale.
MAT 6:6 La tano kom kakwob dilotiri, kom doken mor kuwe. Kom nungum nyiloko, kom kwobdilo Tee kume wo yurangum yurange an nekom cuner kumero.
MAT 6:7 Ca no ka kwob dilotiri, kom libride diker manki nagenneu. nawo nubo nyombo kwama matiyeu. wori kwanererceu ciyatin cuwa tuuki keticro dukceu.
MAT 6:8 Na weu ko yilamde naci wo Tee kume nyimoum bwini kumero kikinning nanyime kom kenco.
MAT 6:9 Na wori kom kwobdilo nawo Tee bewo dii kwamau, ane den mwero dur wucak.
MAT 6:10 Liyar mwero a dou ner nuber.
MAT 6:11 Ne nyo carto na dume ce kume -kume.
MAT 6:12 Dob Nyinen bwirang kert nyero. nawo nyi dob nubowo ma yinentiyeu.
MAT 6:13 Yare kinya Fiye cuwaka, dila cok nyo nii bwir konin (kanng Liyar kannge bikom liyaret kange duktanka ka na mwe diri diri ati nyo).
MAT 6:14 Wori no kom dob nubori bwira kerer cirori, Tee kume wo dii kwamau an dobkumen ken.
MAT 6:15 Ca no ka dobbo nubonen bwirang keretinin cirori Tee kume mani a dob kumen ti.
MAT 6:16 Nyotak, no kama nyak tiri, kom yilam kitikob na nuwoma mwamangtu tiye kambo nubo bwirko matiyeu, wori ci kwuob kang yirom cimboti wori naci dannyi kabum nubem mwincimen Nyak ti. Bilenker miyi kom ti ci fiyam cuner cero.
MAT 6:17 Dilacano kom ma Nyak tiri kom beltu nuwan der kom nirum tikob kumebo.
MAT 6:18 La nanubo nyumde kom ma Nyak ti, lakan Tee kume wo to dikero kom matiyeu yurangumeu ati makumen.
MAT 6:19 Kom mwerde dor kumero nii cuweka for dor bitinet, fiye kerkere kange cnkume a kanngum tiyeu, fiye nob kubbo bani werti do kuumme.
MAT 6:20 Nyiyoco Nyeu, kom mwer dor kumer kange nii cuwaka firen dii kwama fiye kerkere kannge cankume mani yeu. nawo a kanngum tiye fiye tak nuu kuyee mani werti na kumme.
MAT 6:21 Fiye cuweka mweu wiyeu ner mwero ki nowi ken.
MAT 6:22 Nuweu co talkire bwiyeu. Nawori cno nuwemweu yorari, bwiyo kwarub dimki filang.
MAT 6:23 la cano nuwemweu dikero kendi bwiyo kwarub dimki kumtacile.
MAT 6:24 Nii mani bwiya bwnagten, Tee yobe La catin ciya wi ci ko win mani nyori can ciya kanyenin win ci cuyekangum wiceu.
MAT 6:25 La na weu, miyi kom ti kom kwomre dor yimer kumer kidiki kacati yeu, kannge diker na netiye kakaa bwikume dike kama kulenti cikeu. Naweu dume labo carita, bwiyo labo kulanda.
MAT 6:26 Kom to bilibenti dii kwama maci fi fik kakaa biyeka maci mwerank tak mor bine, Tee kume wo diyeu. No nyori kalancibo yorankka.
MAT 6:27 we more kume a cob dorcero ninten cwemka kumetik kiker dikerowo kwom cotiye?
MAT 6:28 La nya ko kwom dor kumeroti ker kulenerer? kom to funti nimbo kiyeu, kambo ci dwitiyeu. maci du kulent.
MAT 6:29 Gwam kange wuru miti kom ti, culemanu ken mor dukktanka mabo nawin more birombonen.
MAT 6:30 Cano kwma maa yera ko kiyenen bwa yilendi, wuro duwei notiyeu firuri ciyan merken yiri infe Danka Yorakko. kom dobbo dubo ki bwini bilin kerereu?
MAT 6:31 Nawo nyeu ko kwomde kom ki “Ye ba catiye, Ye ba dutiye
MAT 6:32 Na weu nubo nyombo kwama wuyak ci do dukum kulenenmbo woti, Tee kume wo diyeu nyimom kom ti citi.
MAT 6:33 Dila kom do liyar cero ki kaba kannge ladi kulendowo kwarub ciyan nekom.
MAT 6:34 Nawue. kom kwomre dor kumer ko bwikume kwarub kumeniu ci dontanngece.
MAT 7:1 Kom mare warka, na cii makumende Warka.
MAT 7:2 Ki Warkako kom ki wardeu, ciya warmwen ki kwele mwa cuwa, ki kwele cu ciya cuwamwen cuko
MAT 7:3 Ye bwi muto cukkum bwatiye ti nure kemwe dila mutobo we mweu nure mwe?
MAT 7:4 Kaka ca manyi mwayi kemweti Berin cok mwe be dikoro nuwe mwe, wendi cuktom bwatiyeu wo nuwemwe?
MAT 7:5 Mwo nii bwir teri cokum cuktum bwatiyeu nuwe mwe, na yimde mwatin dolum mwan tom yor, kambo mwa cukom cuktum watiye ti nuwe kum mwe
MAT 7:6 Kom nere bicurle dikerowo wucak wucakkeu. la ki kom merde bilerinin cari bwayilenner kumer kebo nyo ri ciya fuawrumci.
MAT 7:7 Kii ni ciya necom do mwatin fiya kwabi tak, an womwen.
MAT 7:8 Ca niwo keneri atin yo, wo kwaberi atin wom ci nen.
MAT 7:9 Kakaa weni more kume, bibwece a kenco Tilitari la a ne co ta tiye?
MAT 7:10 Kakaa no kenco jinge tiri a ne co na cuwetiye?
MAT 7:11 Nyori ca no kom bwirembo, ko yumum kambo kane bibiyo lokume lumako tiye, kambo Tee kume diyeu a ne kom dikero kentiye.
MAT 7:12 Na woro di gwamra dikero kom ci ti nubo amakume neu, kom macinen ken.
MAT 7:13 Kom doken nure wo dwaldwaleu, wori nure buareu kuya in nurewo bwaibo doka nob dokabo moreceu ci kila kabo.
MAT 7:14 Di la nureu yaken dumeu kwati kabo, nureu na wo bwai doka nub fiya kaceco kila bou.
MAT 7:15 Kom nyimi ki nob tomangeb dukumeb cuer kobe burombo bokumentiki curen kwamereu, bilinke cin nyece-nyece burombo kuyamtiye.
MAT 7:16 Ka tin nyumom ci kibi tuttuice nubo cok mwembo twiber ko bwi cuike kakaa nying bwi cilannge ka.
MAT 7:17 Nyo kwarub Tini yoken kitu bi tuttuie ken tiyo bwirko ki tuttuice bwir.
MAT 7:18 Tiyo yoryoreu mani tu bi tuttwi bwirti, yo tak tiyo bwir mani tu bi tuttwiy ken.
MAT 7:19 Tano tiyowo mani ne bituttuti kentiyeri laciya tom ciya merken mor kire.
MAT 7:20 La nyori kin duku bibiyem bowo anyomcitiye.
MAT 7:21 Kebo nubo wuyak yiye tiki Tee, Tee adokenti o kwama dila niwo bwanteng ker tee mire dii kwama.
MAT 7:22 Ki ka koko wo ducce an yi ki Tee, tee nyori nyamabo ker dukkumer kiden mwer nya cobo niya kiden mwer. nya mabo nangen do durbitineu ducce kiden mwera?
MAT 7:23 La man yici ma yomkombo ko dubomye, kom nob make bwira kerer.
MAT 7:24 La naweu Manang cemen cukotakeu, can dang kengco na ni nyomka wuro mu kuceu bangereu.
MAT 7:25 La mwembo cuweri yuwako kunou kwa luweu dila yarbo wori ci muco dor bangek.
MAT 7:26 Di la niwo nuwa kermirori mabo nange cike, ciya dan co kannge kulenii wo mu loceu dorbi ti nere.
MAT 7:27 Mwembo cuire mwem wurmamkako bou dila yuwa ko kwenu kwa luwe yalam bukti.
MAT 7:28 La kambo Yecu dim tokka keti ceri mwerkan kako nyimang merang ka ceko.
MAT 7:29 wori meran ci nen ti ki bi kwan liyarer, kebona mulangkab.
MAT 8:1 kambo Yecu yirau do doweri nubbo ducce bwancinenten.
MAT 8:2 La nii ki wale kung diro kibi kwan ki no mwi ciu tiri mwatin yilam kimo wucak.
MAT 8:3 La Yecu tar kang ceko kico ri ki “miki cui”. La yilam wuccak, la dang jang dang jang cii yilam wucak ki wale ceu nen.
MAT 8:4 Yecu yico “yire nii ka nge diker” tame nureu ya nung dormwero nii wabenin na mwi ne lumacere ko werful muca ko tokeu. wo buka kanger ce ko.
MAT 8:5 kambo ci yilau ti kafanahum meri, nii dur nob kweneo bou cinen ken coti.

MAT 8:8 Nii dur nob kweneb bo ciya co ki “Teluwe mi labo wo mwi bou to lo miyeu. Tok kaker dila bwe canga ni atin twam.
MAT 8:9 wori no mo ken min nii ciyo dur biwan keret, tag ri min wiki nob kwenebo min dur dor cere. Miki yi w miki ya ri ci yaken, ki kanage 'bou ri ci bow kange ki canga mi, ma wuro dila cimam.
MAT 8:10 Kamo Yecu nuwa weri, cin nyi mangi la cin yi biro bwang cinnen ten tiyeu, “bilenker mi yi kom ti mi fiya bo kange win wo ki bilenker nawo mor Iciraila.”
MAT 8:11 Min yi kom, kila atin bou twaar kange me la ciyan ca wari kange Ibrahim, Icaku kange Yakubu mor Liyar kwamar.
MAT 8:12 Yilo bibei liyareu atin cor ke mor kumta cilero kiring kiring fiye cika wiyek kange kika nuneg?
MAT 8:13 Yecu yi dur nor kwenebo, “ya nawo mwi le bilenkeu, la a mamwen nyo dila cnagau twam ki kwama don-dong (Yila mwenyo).

MAT 8:15 Yecu tai kang cekori la kwirom bwim bo dubom co. Dila cin kweni cin ter maka cinen carito.
MAT 8:16 Kambo meu dome ri nubo bow Yecu ki nubo kila wo ki kelkelitini yeu. Ciin cikangum yuwa tangbe tinito ki ker yila cin twam wiyak biro nuwabo lumau.
MAT 8:17 Ki nure wo la diim digero toku nyi kaya nii tomange, tokti ki “co ciki bwico yem bwii nuwa ka luma beko ri yila cin tum twirak beko”.
MAT 8:18 L kambo Yecu to mwerkako duce ken tangum ceri cin neci nyal naci yabken kong wimak ko Galili.
MAT 8:19 La ni mulankak bow cinen di to ki ki, “nii meraanka, matin bwang mwentn {Bwen no mwiki yang fye mwi yakenti wiyeu gwam feri}”.
MAT 8:20 Yecu yi co ki” wiki buwak cek, kange bilibetinim wo dii kwamau wiki lo cece dila bi bwe nii fire mani ki fiye wo ci yom dor tiye.”
MAT 8:21 kange mor nub bwang kab cebo yico, “Teluwe dob ye bwiri nan ya nami fwerum teni”.
MAT 8:22 Di la Yecu yi co ki “Bwangmenten na dob nubo bwiyamen na fwerum bar cero.
MAT 8:23 Kambo Yecu dogen tukom bwatiyeri, nob bwangka cebo bwang ci nen ten more ce.
MAT 8:24 La yuwako durko kwenu mor wima, tokum bwantiyebo cimon ki yuwa mwengeb. La yecu dam dum.
MAT 8:25 Nob bwang kab ceko bow cinen di yunco tokti ki “Cer nyo Teluwe, yan bwiya rangum.
MAT 8:26 Yecu yi ci “Ye bwi kom cua tai tiye, kom wo ki bilenkere biduwaru?” Di la cin kweni la werang yuwako knge wimau. la cinge dur tam.
MAT 8:27 Nubo nyimangi la ciki “nage nii ko wini wuro, wo ki yuwa ce kange wima nuwa co tiye?”.
MAT 8:28 Kambo Yecu bow dinge wineu kange mor biten gadara nubo yob wo ki ninga tininyeu wab kam co. ciki ceru mor tuwe, la ci bwi kabo wo nob yameb mani cu nure wiyeu.
MAT 8:29 La cin kwa kiyakye ki dir cin yi ki “ye yo nen kange nye, bibwe kwama? mwi bo fo namwi nenyo dotange nanyumde kwama nye lauwa?”
MAT 8:30 La nyere tini duce ca canak ti fiye co, kwitangbo ducce kange fiye ci niyeu.

MAT 9:1 Yecu dogen nabire mege, yabken dingeri la cin bou mor cinanlor cer.

MAT 10:1 Yeco co nob bwangka wari, la cin neci bikwan keret dor yuwa tangbeko bwir naci cukangwi ci, kane naci twam tuwirantini gwam kange nuwarangka luma ko maniyeu gwam.
MAT 10:2 La den nubo tomangebo kwob cilombo yobeu co buro ki kabou Cimon (wo ci cou tak ki Bitru) kange Andirawu kece, Yakubu bi bwe Zabadi, kange kece Yuwana.
MAT 10:3 Filibu, kange batalamawu, Toma, kange Matiyu nii yoka dorek, Yakubu bi bwe Alfa, Kange Taddawu.
MAT 10:4 Caminu Bakairawau, kange Yahuza Ickarioti wo miyem Ceu.
MAT 10:5 Kwobcilombo yobeu wo Yecu tomci cin yici ki nyal la ciki, “Ko yare fiye kange wo nubo yim kumtacileu, kom dore kange cinanlor nubo Camariya.
MAT 10:6 Ko ya nyori kwame wo lo Iciraila lem meu.
MAT 10:7 La kambo kom ya kom yii fulenker kom ki Liyar kwamak bow bidom.
MAT 10:8 Ko Twam wo nuwabo lumau, kon kungum wo bwiayameu, nako cokum ten ninga. lima nee ko yoke ko neken ki lima neek.
MAT 10:9 Ko tur kange mwin, azurfa kaka tagulla mor cuwaye kime.
MAT 10:10 Ko ture cuwaye Yam kimembo ce, kaka kulen, kaka taa wori nii nagenne daten cari cor.
MAT 10:11 Ki cinan loro kaka mwan loro ka doweri, ko do nii datenne more ce, ko cer locona nyim de ko dob fiye co.
MAT 10:12 Kambo ko do mor luweri, ko ma yarume.
MAT 10:13 No luweu da tendi kom dob fur neret kumeu ayirati, no ci datenbori fur neret kumero ayilau kumen.
MAT 10:14 Nubo wo yo kombo kaka cuwa tu nuwa ker kimereu, Kambo kom cerum luwe nen kaka cinan lor cero ri kom fugom kwerdo nakume keu nen.
MAT 10:15 Bi lenke miyi komti Biten codoma kange Gomara atin fiya jire duwe ki kakuk bolanger kange cinan loro co.
MAT 10:16 To min Tomkom na kwame mor ngece ngece, ko yilam kiyiilam na nacuwe tini ri la ko wii re na nagum fe?
MAT 10:17 Ki yi ki bati kange nubo, ciyan neken kob kan nob yimnom dila ciya tin malliki kom mor bikur wabeb cer.
MAT 10:18 Ciyan bou ki kom kabum nob bolangeb kanage liya, ker mir na warkan cinen kange nubo yim kuntacileu.
MAT 10:19 Kambo ci neken komeri kom kwom de ki kambo kange dikero ko tok tiye, wori atin nekom di diker ko tok tiyeu ka kwama co.
MAT 10:20 wori kebo kom ko tok ker tiye, dila yuma tangbe te kume a tok kerti kumene.
MAT 10:21 Kece atin ne ken kece nai twalum, dila Tee ceu bibwe ce. Bibeyo atin kwinag Teb cebo nen tien ci doki ci twallagum cii.
MAT 10:22 Nubo duce an ko kom ker denen miir. Dila wo mwirom yaken ciko di ka ri ni cou atin fulo ka.
MAT 10:23 No ci nekom dotange cinar lor wori koom cuaken cinan loro bdomeu, la miyi km bilenke ti, mani kom kentange cinan loro Iciraila ti wiyak nangimde bibwe nifire n bou.
MAT 10:24 Ni bwanka duwi bo la nii merrang cinen tiyeu kaka canga dor Teeluwe ce.
MAT 10:25 Dong dong ni bwanka a ylam a nii merang a ceko, kange caga na teluwe ce. Ta no cin cou Tee luweu Ba'al zabuba ri, la an bwira dendo wo ciya com numo loceu ti cike.
MAT 10:26 Nyori, ko cua cire, wori yurke mani wo mnaiya tok tiye, kange dikero mni wo yurangum yurangeri mani a coku ti yanglang.
MAT 10:27 Di kero mayi kom kumta cileu ko toki ki Kakkuk kange dikero mwi nuwa bi luma mor tuwe meu, toki ki dir dor lor.
MAT 10:28 Cuwa re nubo wo twallum bwiyo ri la mani a twal dume tiyeu. Na wori cwa ni wo a twallum bwiyo ti kange dume mor kira kwama.
MAT 10:29 Kebo bilibe yob ci miyeti dor wina? Duwal kange ce man o a yarti bilineri kebo ymka Teku mek.
MAT 10:30 La yiri duwe kumeu kiyem kiye.
MAT 10:31 Ko cuwa re tai km la bilibetini yroka.
MAT 10:32 La nyori gwam niwo ne warke me nuwe nuberi matin na warke ce ken kabum temim wo dii kwamau.
MAT 10:33 Niwo ko neka warke dor miir kabum nuberi mo ken man neka warke dor ceer ka Tee mii wo dii kwama.
MAT 10:34 Ko kware komki min yau ri nami bou ki fuwor neret dor bitinr. I yau bo nabi bou ki fuwor neret, dila kulen.
MAT 10:35 Min bou na mi dok nii kiye kange tece, kange Kiye biber bubiyak kange nece kange bifire bwe bubiya kiye kange fer e nawiyeu.
MAT 10:36 Nii kiye niu atin yilam co wo mor luwe ceu.
MAT 10:37 Co wwo cui tece kaka nece laye re ri daten bo na mii wo ciu bwe kaka bwe bubiyaceu, layere da ten bo na mii.
MAT 10:38 Co wo tu bo kwoblom bwatiye ce na bwang men teneri daten bo mii.
MAT 10:39 Nii wo cui ti naci fulo dume ceri, an lem dume ceu. la wii dume ceu kermireri an fiyam co.
MAT 10:40 Wo yokomeri yo mo, dila nii wo yo yerri, yo co wo tomou yereu.
MAT 10:41 Wo yo nii tomange ki den nii tomangeri an yo cuner nii tomangero, la co wo yo nii cak cakke ki den nii cak-cakke ri atin yo cuner niiwo cak-cakeu.
MAT 10:42 wo ne win more bi duwartini buru kwel mwenge yibe nano ki den ni bwangkake ri, bilenke mi yi komti mani a le cuner cero ti”.
MAT 11:1 Bwikako Yecu dim biweret bi bei tomange ceri, cin dibom bi kole cua na co merang, na cin yi ci fulen ker kwama cinnr lor cer.
MAT 11:2 La Yuwana nuwa co fiya co, ci fucinu dikero Yecu matiyeu, con tom bi bei tomange ceu na co yi co.
MAT 11:3 Mon co nii boutiye kaka nyo ningtang kange ka?
MAT 11:4 Yecu yi ci ki, kom ya ko yico dika ka towe kange dike ka nuwa!
MAT 11:5 Fukma ti toi, kilendo yayamti, walebo cin twam ci nubo mani nuwareu to nuwai ci kung nubo bweyameu ti nob bunebo ci neci fulen kerero ti.
MAT 11:6 Nii wo nuwabo funer kange me ri nob bibwiyer.
MAT 11:7 Kambo nubo wuro cuweri Yecu yi nubo mwerumeu ker dor Yuwanar.
MAT 11:8 Ye no kom cer yerak di kom ki tore, Yerako Yuwako moktiya? lan ye ka ciri ka towe nii dum ki kulendo fila-fila? Bilenker nubo dum ki kulendo Fila-fila ki daa lo liyabe.
MAT 11:9 Ye ka ceri ri ka towe bwe tomange kwama? ong mi yikomti, bwe tomange kwama.
MAT 11:10 Wo cowo ci mulang dorcer ki “to mi tom kimen nii tomange miti ka kom nuwe kime, wo a Yulang nure mwe tiye.
MAT 11:11 Min yikom bilenke ba kange ci kung more kime wo natum bowe la Yuwana nii yuka mweme ke. Nyori bi duware gwam mor liyar kwamareu laco.
MAT 11:12 Ta ti kumeni Yuwanan nii yu mwemtiye yau ciko caneu, liyar kwamaro nuwa dotange kwiklki-kwilkiye, nob wilki-wilkiro tu kibi kwang.
MAT 11:13 Fiya na Yuwana na bou gwam nob tomangeb kwamaro kange werfundo tak ker dukumero woti.
MAT 11:14 No mwan ciya mo yuwo ri con Iliya wo a boutiye.
MAT 11:15 wo ki tuweri a nuwa.
MAT 11:16 Ma bonkan kwaldo wo ki ye? ci nabi ma lor ti fiye miyeka dike, wuro yirongm cuwo butici tiye.
MAT 11:17 Toki bin cii mwen lira mwa yelbo yila. Nyo yi kwan bwa, mwe cibo wiye.
MAT 11:18 Wo Yunana bou mani ca cari, ma no nyom kom yi ki to ciki bwekelkele.
MAT 11:19 Bibwe nifire bou, ti cai ti noi ri, kom ki to wi ki nii kucunu knge ni o nyom tiye, far nob yuwaka kiyeme kange nob bwiranke! Nyori yilang ki fiya yuwoka ki nangendo co matiye.
MAT 11:20 La Yecu yoten werang cianr loro wo co man diker nyimankar wiyeu ducceu wori cin yiloka.
MAT 11:21 kwamen mo karangcimun kwamanen mo Baptcaida naki diker nyimankaro wori ci ma kimeneu, cimam taaya kange cindo di, kin yiloten kutan -kutange mor yakca yilanga kange bi tuwam.
MAT 11:22 Na cuwori an la Tayanin kange cidon dor kimer, kakuk bolanger.
MAT 11:23 Mo kafanahum, mo kwatiri man fiya duktonka lo kwama ka? or ong an cukken nen bitine, hadec. mo codom naki nyimangeu manue, ma muneg di, no ki wi duwal.
MAT 11:24 Mi yikomti a yilam bwai biten codome min, na kimeu.
MAT 11:25 Ki fiya co Yecu toki, “Min cakakom ti, Tebe, teluwe lo kwama kange kaleu, wori kom yurangen dike buro ka fiya nob yalannereu kange nyomka, la ka wom biyeyo bi dwartini nineu.
MAT 11:26 Ong, te wuro yori kaba nuwe mwe.
MAT 11:27 Dikero gwam cin neken ye fiye temi wiya ni kange mani wo a nyom bwe tiye, nyombo teu, nyo tak ni kange mani wo a nyom teu na bi bwece, kange wo co cokum naci nun cinene.
MAT 11:28 Bou minen kom wo ki nuwa dotange tiye, wo ki kulendo tutue, nan ne kom fubi.
MAT 11:29 Tu kulen miro, ki merangi mineng, wori mi lom-com, miki nero yiber mwan fiya fobka dume mwe.
MAT 11:30 Wori kulen miro bwaibo, takeu kulen miro tubo.
MAT 12:1 Ki fiya cuwa, Yecu kwen yam ki kakuk fobka mor tankini. Bibei tomange ceu nuwa wura ti, la ci kwer dor cangero ti citi cai.
MAT 12:2 La fariciyawa to nyori, cin yii Yecu, “To be bei tomange mweu diker ci matiye werfundo ciyabo a mani ki kakuk fobka.
MAT 12:3 La Yecu yi ci ki ka karanta bo diker Dauda mane kange nobo loce ki fiya cuwo ci nuwa wura tiya?
MAT 12:4 Con doken bi kur kwamar, con ca cari wiye wo werundo ciya cinenbo kange nobo cineneu, ciyam kin nob wabeb koni.
MAT 12:5 Ka mor werfuna, ki kakuk fobka, nob wabbe kwama mor kikur kwamare ma dike werfundo ciyanbe, nyori, ci tacibe ki kero bwia?
MAT 12:6 Min yi kom niwo la bikur kwamareu wo fo.
MAT 12:7 Na ki ka nyimom ye wuro nuntiyeri, 'miki cwi cire duwe kebo twika nuwange ko wucake, no kom ki warbo ker dor niwo man ki bwiran kereu.
MAT 12:8 Bibwe nifire co teluwe kakuk fobka ke.
MAT 12:9 La Yecu dubom bikole cuwo, doken bi kur wabbero Urcalimau.
MAT 12:10 wori, nii kange kanko nom nowe wini. Fariciyawa me Yecu dong dongka a twa ni ki kakuk fobka ka? o na cin taco ki ker bwiranke.
MAT 12:11 Yecu yi ci we fo more kume no kwame ce yarken bouk ki kakuk fobka ri mani a tau ti cokumme?
MAT 12:12 Na wine la kece kwame kaka nifir? nyori werfundo ciya a ma diker ken ki kakuk fobka.
MAT 12:13 La Yecu yi niwo, “Taruu kangeko, la con taruu kang ceko, la kango yilaken kwamer na wineu.
MAT 12:14 La fariciyawa erken kale cin mwer kangi dor Yecu. ciki do nure ciya twalum Yecu tiye.
MAT 12:15 Yecu to nyori co ci dubom bi kole cuwe. nuwe. nubo ducce bwanteng ce, con twam ci.
MAT 12:16 Con yi ciki nyial ciya yire nii.
MAT 12:17 wo na ci dim dike ci tok nyii nii wabe kwabe Icaya, tokti ki.
MAT 12:18 Too Yii tomange me wo ma cok ceu, ma bilankange ceu, Man ne co yuwa tangbek miko naci yii nubo wo kebo Yahudawa.
MAT 12:19 Mani ca kwobkan ker ti, Mani ca ci wiye ti ki diir, mani a nuwa dircer ti nure.
MAT 12:20 Ma ca kyan dike fwinongum ti, ma ca dom kra ko dadom bwiyakau, can ya ki warka turani.
MAT 12:21 Mor dene ce nubo kumtacile an fiya yim yo neri.
MAT 12:22 Nyori cin bou ki nii kange, fukma, mani nuwa tuu, wiki ninga fiye Yecu wiye. Con twam cona wo Nyori nii cuwo tok ker, ti toi tak.
MAT 12:23 Nubo wmerkangum gwamme nuwa nyimangka la me, wo co bibwe Dauda ka?
MAT 12:24 La fariciyaa nuwa diker nyimankako Yecu maneri cin yi ki, “Nii wo ki cok ninga kin bahalzabu liya kelkelebe.
MAT 12:25 La Yecu nyimom dike ci kwati ner cere, yi ci ki, Liyar do wo yalkangum me ri, mani a ti-ti cinar lor tikangum yobe mani a titi, kako luwe fwemme ri, an wurom.
MAT 12:26 No bwekelkele cok bwekele ri ki maa kiiye ki dor cero. La a mangyi na liyar do wo ti?
MAT 12:27 No miki cok ninga kin Ba'alzabu ri, bi bei kimeu ki cok ki ye? nyori ci ciya yila warka kimek tiye.
MAT 12:28 No miki cok ninga ki yuwa tangbe kwama wucake ri, nangi liyar kwamaro bou kimen.
MAT 12:29 A man nyii nii doken lo nii bikwanne na ku kwi, co co bwam cobo ri? na nimre kange me ri ki ma kiiye kange mo, takeu, niwo mwerbo kange me ri, ki watangken.
MAT 12:31 Na wori mi yi kom ti, “bwirangke kange dilanka gwam an curanwi. La dilanka yuwatangbeko wucake mani a curang ti wi.
MAT 12:32 Ni wuro tok dikro bwir dor bibwenifireu a cutang wi wo tok kero bwir dor yuwa tangbe wucakeu a curang cinen ti wi fo kale wo kange wo boutiye.
MAT 12:33 Ywel tiyo a yori, bi tuti ce an yori kaka ywel tiyo a bwira bi tuti ce a bwira.
MAT 12:34 Kom bi bei na cuwe, kom nubobwir a ma nyii ka tok dikero keng tiye? Mor dikero ducce nereu co nyiiyo toktiye.
MAT 12:35 Ni ken ki coku dikero kendo ner cereu, nii bwir ki cok dikero bwir ko ner cereu.
MAT 12:36 Mi yikom ti ki kakuk warka nubo an ne warke dor dikero bwir ko ci toke.
MAT 12:37 Ki kero nyii mweu an coknen ki kero nyii mweu an kuwa nen.
MAT 12:38 Nyori kangem nob mulang kar kange Fariciyawa ciya Yecu nin ki “nii merangka, nyi cwiti nayi to yirom muneng”
MAT 12:39 la Yecu yi ci ki, “Kom nubo bwir, kom nob burotumbo kaldo weu, ko do yirom ti mani k fiya ti no kebo ka wo Yunana nii tomangeu ce ri.
MAT 12:40 Nyori Yunana da kuma taar, kakuko taar mor fwer jingi dur, na cuwo bi bwe nii an daa kume taar, kakuko taar mor bitine.
MAT 12:41 Nubo niniba a kweni an tii kange nubo kaldo we ki kakuk wara, ci an kuwa ci wori cin yiloten ki fulen kerek Yunana ro, la to nii kange wo la Yunana wo.
MAT 12:42 Liya bangeu an kweni kane nobo kaldo, an kuwaa ci. ca bou cile kale wo na ci nuwa yilen Culemanu ro, la to nii kange wo laa Culemanuweu wo.
MAT 12:43 No yuwa tangbe ko bwir cerum nii nen di ki yaya fiyeni wo mwem mani yeu na ci fiya fobke, mani ca fiyati.
MAT 12:44 La yi ki man yilaken lomiyo ma cerueweu. No ci yilaken di, can fiya luwa, nyinangum Yulangum yora.
MAT 12:45 La con tuten kange kebceb niber wo bwira la ceu bou ciko na ci yi nyo, la cwile nii wo an bwira la wo fiyau, a yila nyo kange kaldo bwir ko wuro.
MAT 12:46 La Yecu dibo tokka kereko nubo mwerum cineneu ri, nece kange yitobcebo bou tim kale, cwiti na cin to co.
MAT 12:47 Kange yico, “To nemwe kange yitub mweb tirangum kale, cwiti na ci tok ker kange mo.
MAT 12:48 Yecu yi co nii wo yico kereu, we nemi, we yitub mibo?
MAT 12:49 La con taar kang ceko fiye be bei tomange ce nineu yico, “To” buro co nemi kange yitob mibo.

MAT 13:1 Ki kume cuwo Yecu cerum luwe nen, yan yiken kong caji.
MAT 13:2 Nubo kila, kila mwerkani cinen la con doken mor na bire mwenge con yiken more ce tangne nubo ducce tiranken konge.
MAT 13:3 La Yecu yici dikero kila-kila or dangke. Con yi ci “Nii fike kange yaken fik dumek.
MAT 13:4 Kambo co fi tiye ri, kangum dumembo yarangken nure, bilibatine bou cibangum cuwo.
MAT 13:5 Kangumbo yaranken fiye terentiyeu bitine mani yorau tabbo bwi cin kim wori bitine cuwabo.
MAT 13:6 La kakuko kwiuri cin comam wori ci manki niyeten cin kucom.
MAT 13:7 Kangum dumembo yaranken tiber cuiyaktini, la cuiyakko dwiyangum di cakkangum ci.
MAT 13:8 Kangum dumembo yarangken bitine ken, ma nuni kangumbo kwini kwob, kangumbo kwini nukkun, angumbo kwini taar.
MAT 13:9 Niwo ki tuweri ca nuwa”
MAT 13:10 Bibei tomange bou yi Yecu “Ye bwi mo yi nubowo keroti mor dangke?”
MAT 13:11 Yecu yii ci “Kom wi ki nure wo ka nyimom yurke liyare loh kwama, la ciye ci nencibo.
MAT 13:12 Niwo cike an neten co naci fiya ducce, La nii wo mancike, bi dure cinneu an yumom cinnen.
MAT 13:13 wori co dike bwi mi yici keroti ki dangke. To na ci ti toi ri mani ciya toti, tano citi nuwei ri ma ciya nuwati kaka nyimom.
MAT 13:14 Cine neu dike Icaya to tokeu dim. Wo tokki, no mo nuwatiri, mwan nuwa la mani mo nyomti, toka kan to mani ka nyomti.
MAT 13:15 Wori ner nubo wori wi ki kumtacile bwai na ci nuwa, cin kumom nuwe ciye naci tore ki nuwe ciye kaka ci nuwa ki tui ci kaka ci nyimom ki ner cir, la naci yilau nan twam ci.
MAT 13:16 Nuwe kime iker bibwiyer wori cin to, tu kime wori cin nua.
MAT 13:17 Bilenke mi yi komti nob dukumeb kange nubo wucake ducce cin cui naci to dike ka towe, ci tobo, cui naci nuwa diker ka nuwa ci nuwa bo.
MAT 13:18 Kom nuwa dangke niwo ya fi fikeu.
MAT 13:19 No kangumbo fulen liyar kwamar nyombe ri, nii bi cirene an bou bo yuwom dike ci finer cereu. won co dumbo ci fi nureu.
MAT 13:20 W ci fi fiye bitine ki terentiye, co niwo nuwa kero ri yuwa wulom-wulom ki for neret.
MAT 13:21 La wori ci man ki niye bwici can ti biduwar la no co fiya kalaka kange dotange ri, wulom-wulom co yarum.
MAT 13:22 Wori ci fi mor cuiyakeu co niwo nuw kereu la cuikko kalek kange kiyemer cakacangum kero la co mabo.
MAT 13:23 Dumbo wo ci fi bitine keneu, co nii wo nuwa kero ri, nyimome ma ken kange kwini kwob, kange kwini nukkun, kange kwini taar no wo ci fi ciyeu.
MAT 13:24 Yecu bo cinenten ki kang dangke. con toki, “Liyar kwamaro ki no na nii wo fi dumbo kem takeceu.
MAT 13:25 La nubo da dumtiri, nii kiye ce bou fiti yerako wi mor bikate ce, la cu ce.
MAT 13:26 Kambo Cuiko duyom meri, la ma ce bitwiti ceu ken
MAT 13:27 Cangam nii take bou yi co, nii dur, mwe fi bo dumbo ken take mwe ka? Man nyi yerako wiye?
MAT 13:28 Con yi ci “nii kiye ma we” cangam cebo yi co, la muki cui nyo ya nyo kubangum ka?
MAT 13:29 Nii take kii, O-ong, no com kubang yerako tiri kang kubangum ten kange bi kateu.
MAT 13:30 Kom dobci gwam ciya dwi nyo gwam ya cinko bika. La no lam bito ri man yi nob bitobbo, “Kom kwon yerako ki kaba, kom bwam ki blak na kom twim, kom mwer bikateu mor bini mi.
MAT 13:31 La Yecu bo cinen ten ki kange dangke. con toki kii, Liyar kwamaro nan nun bikate (Musta) wo nii kange tu ya fi ta kece.
MAT 13:32 Nuni wo co bi duware gwam tannen nunim bo nin. La no dui ri la tannem nunim bo gwam, yilam ti wo bilibe dii kwama an yulng loni ciye kani ce nin.
MAT 13:33 Yecu yi ci kange danke tak, co tur duwo mim taca taare na fuu ci gwam.
MAT 13:34 Gwam dike boro Yecu yi nubo mwerume kin dangke, co cibo kange diker wo kebo dangke.
MAT 13:35 Wuro na yilam dike ci toke nyii nob tomangeb, ba na dim, wo co yi ki, “man wumon Nyii mi mor dangke. Man tok dikero wo yurangum. yurange nawo a yom fer-kur kalereu.
MAT 13:36 Yecu dobom nubo mwerumeu. doken mor luwe. Bibei tomage ceu cinen cin yi co, Fwetan nyinen dangke yere wo takeu”.
MAT 13:37 Yesu ciya la yici “wo fi dumbo keneu, so bi bwe nii fireu.
MAT 13:38 Takeu so dor bitinero, la dumbo ken ko ci bi bei liyar kwamaro. yerako co bi bei nii kiyeu.
MAT 13:39 Ni kiyeu fi fikkeu so bwekelkeleu. Bitou so cuile kaleu, nob bitobbo ci nob tomangeeb kwama wusake.
MAT 13:40 Nyori yerako ci macangum ci tuimeu co cuile kaleu.
MAT 13:41 Bi bwe nifir an tom nob tomangeb kwama wusakeu ci an bwabangum naci cokum liyar kwamar gwam dike buro dok bwiran ketiye kange buro wo mani bwanten werfun tiye.
MAT 13:42 Ci an merken ci mor kra cillen, fiye ciya ci wiyeti kange kironka nunnek.
MAT 13:43 La ubo wusakeu ci an buwa na kakuk mor liyar kwama teciye. wo ki tuweri, can nuwa.
MAT 13:44 Liyar kwama nan cweka yurangum yurange takeu. Nii kange fiyari yurangum cu ki bilangtum, yan miyem dike co cikeu gwam. La tiyenum take wo.
MAT 13:45 Takeu, liyar kwamaro na nii kyeme do yoryore tiye.
MAT 13:46 No co fiya kange wo yoryore ri, co ya ci miyem dike co cike gwam co tiyenum.
MAT 13:47 Nyo tak liyar kwama nan bi liyar ci mer wima, la mweru dikero ducce.
MAT 13:48 La dim ri nii taka jinge ko kwou konge, La con yiken con mwerum kenko mor kole, Bwirtinim bo ci miranwi firen.

MAT 13:50 Ciyan merkeng ci mor kira cilong-cilonge fiye ciya ci ti ka wiye kange kironka nunek.

MAT 14:14 Yesu bo kabum cem to tenanka mwerka nobe ko, cii cimen, co twam nubo nuwabo luma mo re ciye.

MAT 14:23 Bwiko co yo mwerkako cuwe, co ci kwiken dor bange kwobka dilo kume fim co firen ki kwace.

MAT 14:27 Di la Yesu yi ci ker can nawo co ki kom ma bi kwan neret, mo kom nuware tai.

MAT 15:23 Yesu kar cienbo ker, bibi tomange ce bo kenan co ciki yoken co bwang binen ti ki kiyange.

MAT 16:1 Nob dingli kange Sadukiya ci b cinen, ci cwiti na cin cwa co, cin kenc co ca nung cinen yirombo ii kwama.
MAT 16:2 Kari yi ci ki meri, kom ki fiye an lumi wori dii kwama fiye je.
MAT 16:3 Ta ke ki bwiri kom ki fiye lombo, wuro dii kwama fiyeje, dim dii ka? kom ynomom kabel yirom dii kwama la kom fwe ki jyomka keneko.
MAT 16:4 Kaldo bwir, nubo man ki taka bwiti, ci do yiromti di la yirom kange man wo a nungtiye ka wo Yunusa ce”. Yesu cu.
MAT 16:5 Bibei tomange ce bo dinge wureno di la cin tabum ci tu bo cirato.
MAT 16:6 Yesu yi ci kom cibi kom yiki bati, kange dige fuu nob dinlibo kange Sadukiyawa.
MAT 16:7 Bibei tomange ce yateen ti tokkan bwiti ci, keno wori cari mani di.
MAT 16:8 Yesu nyomom co yi ci ki kom nob bwinin bilenke, ye bwi kom tokkan ti bwiti kume, keno ker carito bo, bocikeri?
MAT 16:9 Kom nyombo kom bulangbo carito cendo nung wo ca ki nobe bi kate nunge, bulen di nyi kom mwere?
MAT 16:10 kaka carito cwendo niber, nubo bikate na'ar, kange bulendo niber, nubo bikate na'r kange bulendo nyi kom tume?
MAT 16:11 Ye bwi kom fwe ki nyomkako kom ki kebo cari ma kom cubi kom ka bati ki camfuwam, nob dinlibo kange Sadukiyawa.
MAT 16:12 La wo ciya bulangti, tok bo amfuwambo mor cariye di la ki yi ci ciya cub merangka nob dinglibo kange Sadukiyawa.
MAT 16:13 Fiya Yesu bo kai cariya Filibus me bibei tomange ce, wobo ki tok bi bwe nifire nyi?
MAT 16:14 La ci ki “Knagem ki yi ki Yuwana nii yuka mwenge, kangembo ki Iliya, kangembo ki Irimiya, kka win mor nob tomange.
MAT 16:15 Yi ci, kume we kom yi ti ki me?
MAT 16:16 Saminu Bitrus ciya kari mo Almaciya, Bibwe kwama ki dume.”
MAT 16:17 Yesu kari yi co nibi bwiyer mo Saminu bibwe Yunusa, kebo nange kange bwiyale fwetang mn dige we Te mi mor dii kwama.
MAT 16:18 Ma yinenti mo Bitrus dur tere do wo ma mo bikur wabe mi tiye. Nyilo bwiyare man a fiya turinikiditti dor cer.
MAT 16:19 Man nenen yilo dii kwama ko diker mo bwabi fo kaleri, yilam bwambwabe firen dii kwama. Dikero mo kwim fo kale, yilam kwim firen dii kwama.
MAT 16:20 Yesu yi bi bei tomange ce ci ya yide nii con Almasihu.
MAT 16:21 Tabti fo Yesu ter yika bibei tomange ce tamyo co ya Ursalima co nuwa dotange dutce kan nubo durko nen kange nubo dur wabero, kange nob mulangka werfunedo, ci twallum co an kun co dume bwiko kume wari.
MAT 16:22 La Bitrus yaken ki co cungagin werangco, ki wuro a kutangi kange mo teluwe, wuro mani a bwiti kange mo.
MAT 16:23 Di Yesu yila Bitrus, yila kenbwi mi, bwekelkele. mo ter kottanka minen, wori kwom nen bo kange diker na kwama ce ka na nubo ce.
MAT 16:24 Yesu yi bibei tomange ce ki ni wo cwiti na bwagmentneri ca ko dor cer na co tu bwatiye bware ce na co bwangmenten.
MAT 16:25 wuro cwiti naco fulo dume ce ri, co lemco, Wo lem dume ceri dormire di can fiya ti.
MAT 16:26 Ye yori ni na fiyam kaleo na lem dume ce? Bibwe nii an bo mor duktanka Te cer wari kange nob tomange cak-cak ke, nimde na ya nubo gwam dor dike mo mane.
MAT 16:27 Bibwe nii an bou ki luma te ceko kange bibie tomange ce, an ne nii dikero ca mani fo kaleweu.
MAT 16:28 Bilenker mi yi komti, kangem komem bo tim feu na mani twi bwarti, Di ci an to bibwe nifire boti mor liyar cer.
MAT 17:1 Ki kume nukkundi Yesu tu Bitrus kange Yakubu kange Yuwana yiciye yaken ki co bangko cweem cwemeu, ki bwico.
MAT 17:2 Yirom cembo tii ba kabum ciyembo tikob cebo, ti bibai na kakuk, kange bellece ti tibai na filang.
MAT 17:3 Katten di Musa kange Iliya cerkangu cinen, tak.
MAT 17:4 Bitru kari, yi Yecu Teluwe yori bo fo fiye wo bo wiye. Tona mon cwitiri man ywel bi kurdo tar, win kimo win ki Musa, win ki Iliya
MAT 17:5 Co mor takka kerer biloro tia nyi cumo co diro coro bi loromi yici kiwo bi bwini mi cwiye coni fumen nen tiye kom nuco.
MAT 17:6 La bibei tomange ce nuwa yori cin mwelken dorcero bitene wori cin cwatai.
MAT 17:7 Yecu bo ke ci yici ki kweni kom nuware tai.
MAT 17:8 Ci kum dore ciyero, cito bo nii.
MAT 17:9 Fiyaci yirouti bang Yecu nyiki kom yire ni dukkum bowo fico bi bwe nii kwanen.
MAT 17:10 Bi bei bwangka ce me ki yebwe ni mulanka a tok ti ki Iliya yo boteye?
MAT 17:11 Yecu diye cinen ki Iliya an boragu ki dikero.
MAT 17:12 Di miyi kom ti iliya kweri bou dila ci yomkombo nyori cin macinen diker ci cwiye. nurewo, bi bwe nifire an nuwa dotange kan ciye.
MAT 17:13 wo bi bei tomangece ci nyme ki tok cine kero tok Yuhana nii yuka mogen.
MAT 17:14 Ci law fiye mwirkanka ko weyenri kange nii bo cine, cunguge kabumce toki.
MAT 17:15 Teluwe ci bi bwemi wori ki juwe takeu, nuwa dotangeti kwabi ki yalti mwem kange kira ngit.
MAT 17:16 Maboki ci bi bei tomange nin cin dor bo twaka.
MAT 17:17 Yecu, Kari tokki nom bwini birinke kange cwatanka kle fiya fiyang mayi ti ki kome ko bo ki co fiye mi wiye.
MAT 17:18 Yecu kwenancinenten la ning bwice celum bwi fiya tai ka?
MAT 17:19 Bi bei tomange ce bo Yecu nen yulum yurang me ki yebi nyo fweki co kake?
MAT 17:20 Yecu yiciki bilenker kumero nyo bi duwar mi yi kom ti naki kam wii ki beilenker na nun bi katairi kam nyi tiyo kamki kwam yaken fire tiyo an kom dike kange mani wo ala bi gwamm ki matiye.
MAT 17:21 La iren kelkeliyo wo mani a certi ciya kwobka dilo.
MAT 17:22 Ciyim Galili, Yecu yi bei tomange ce ki ciyan ne bi bweni kan nii.
MAT 17:23 Ci nyi mom twirum co ki kume tar an kwenum bibei tomange ceu nero kayam.
MAT 17:24 Ci lam Kafanahum nubo yo dortiyeu wumer cekeltiyeu cin bo Bitru. ciki nii merankakumeko, ne wumer cekeliti. Na dore ce?
MAT 17:25 Co toki ong dila Bitru do ken mor luwe Yecu ter kero kange co, nye mo kwatiye Saminu? liyam karero ciki nyo kemer doren wine kika kemer mweng fiye nobfuwai.
MAT 17:26 Bitru kar cinen fiye Fabubo wiye Yecu yic nyori citu nob finyige keben yakako dila kari.
MAT 17:27 Bi don nyo ka doreka bwirangke, kam ya wima, mam ker bibumo kom tau jinge wo ter bo kakeri. tano kom wom niceri, komfiya cekelo kumtu kone nubo yodoro tiyeu mi kange mwin.
MAT 18:1 Ki kwama co bibe bwingka Yecu me ki co wining durko mor di kwama.
MAT 18:2 La Yecu co bwi bi duren kange tiber ciyer.
MAT 18:3 Ki miyi kom ti na kam yirambo na bi bitiuttiri mani kom kuti di kwama.
MAT 18:4 Na ni wo yoken dur cero na bwi bi duwareri cu dikero dur ko di kwama.
MAT 18:5 No kom yo bwibi duware wo ki den mir di kom yomye.
MAT 18:6 Wuro dok win mor bibeiyo wo ne bilengke bwiranke, la diker a ye cinnen ti ter nerer kwir cer, na merken. Co wima cuwa.
MAT 18:7 Gwam dor bitinero, wo kwantangka a fiya ciye gwam wiwo kume ni wo abotiye.
MAT 18:8 Na kangmweko kaka namweko an donen kotankeri mwatum co di mirangco wi. Na wori La mwen diker kange wo ciya tunken nen ti kira ki kanko yobeu, Lamwen diker do lokwama ki kanko win ko nako win.
MAT 18:9 Na nuwe mweu an dok nen kwentanka ri cokum co na mirank cowi fiye mwi wiyeu an lamwen diker mo doken dume ki nuwe win kange yarka mor kira ki nuwe yob.
MAT 18:10 Kom burange kom cwinkande bibei bi durti nen bo bibwe tomange kwama to ti com tii ciwo di kwama.
MAT 18:11 Bi bwe ni bou na cok dike lemeu.
MAT 18:12 Ni ye burangeka kime bou? na nii ki kwamagwini kom win la win reb maciya dubam tenwini ter cuo tereti naco dou woreme ka?
MAT 18:13 Na fiyam wo winenri miyi kom ti furner cero an lawo kuni tereo co dobeu.
MAT 18:14 Yo na wori yori kebo di wo tekume wo dii kwama nuge naco kun mor bi durdunen dowo na bwiyam.
MAT 18:15 Tano kenmwe kom mwendi yico tiber kumer mokange co kub biyo tano nunenddi moyirau.
MAT 18:16 Tano kam nukang bo bwitikimiri, kiya ki nubo yo kaka tar naci yiram warke, fi nob warka ko yau be kaka tare nunge kiro gwam dong dong.
MAT 18:17 Na ko nuwa ka ciye kori ya cuko nob kwama bone nako na nuwa ciri. tuken co na nubo yombo kwama.
MAT 18:18 Mi yi kom ti dike kom bwam bitineu bwam bwabe di kwama kike kom wineri gwin-gwine di kwama.
MAT 18:19 Mi yi kom ti na nubo yau an ciya ki dike kom kinantiyeu te mi wo di kwama an makimen.
MAT 18:20 Fiye nubo yau kaka, taar ci mwerum ki denmireri mi we kange ci.
MAT 18:21 Bitrus bow Yecu nen ki kwama kiri to nyi kemi ama men burang ke manciten wiye? in lam kirito ni bwirka?
MAT 18:22 Yecu diye cinen ki mi yi nen bo mii kirito niber, miki niber kiriti kwini niber.
MAT 18:23 Nyori liyar kwamaro kino na liya kange o cwii naci kiyem kemer cereu knage cangam cere.
MAT 18:24 Kambo ci ter ri cin bow cinen ki canga kange wo ci bwang tenti talent do bikate kwobbe.
MAT 18:25 Dila kambo ci man ki nureu ci yam tiyeri, te kuwece ne wrfunendo ca a myim co, kange wii ce kange bibeyo kange dikero ci cikeu gwam dila na yam nan cero.
MAT 18:26 La cangau yarken bitine, cungi kabum cem la ki “Teluwe, ma biner kange mo, dila man yi nen dikero gwam.
MAT 18:27 La teluwe canga co kambo cin dim ki cikakeu nyem kang cinen di la citang cinen nan cero wi.
MAT 18:28 Dila canga co cei ya fiya kange kece canga, wo ci bwang ten denani ti kwini kwob wiine cin tam co ri yoten bukka ceko la ciki yam ye dikero mi bwang mwne ten tiye.
MAT 18:29 Di la kece cangau yarken bitine la kinog co ki “nuwa bi neri kange mo, ri man ya tinen wi”.
MAT 18:30 Di la canga wo ki kaba ko, Nyori, cin ya ci merken co mor fucina no cin yam co dikero ci bwang cinen ten tiye nyimde.
MAT 18:31 Kambo kebcebo canga bo to dikero bwiyeuri, cin kangum ner duce cin bou la cin yi teluwe ce dikero bwiyeu gwam.
MAT 18:32 La Teluwe canga co, cou co rila yico “mo bwe canga bwir, mi tab mwen dikero mi bwang mweng ten tiyeu gwam, wori mwin kinong ye.
MAT 18:33 No mwiki nungbo kemwe nin cireduwa, na wo min nung mwen cireduwe?
MAT 18:34 Teluwe ceu knagum ner duce la neken co kang nubo ne dotange tiye no ciyam gwam dikero ci bwang cinen ten tiyeri nyimde.
MAT 18:35 La nyo Te me di kwama ama kimen tiye ken no kom cutangbo kebkumebo nin wi mor nere kumer ri.”
MAT 19:1 Lam bou kambo Yecu dimkero buro di co ca dubom Galili con yaken ti yii kar Yahudiya, dinge caji Urdune.
MAT 19:2 Nubo kila-kila bwan cinneten con twan ci finange cuwo.
MAT 19:3 Faricawau bouragum cinen ci cuwancoti ciki “daten nyo nii kambo wer funen nageu, ni a twal wii ce nin naaka ki kange dikerka?
MAT 19:4 Yecu Yii ci ka kiye bi wika tok ki co ni wo fule ci fiya kabu fuel, ci yob bwayile kaange nawiye.
MAT 19:5 Co niwo fule ciyeu tok ki kiwuro nii an dubom Teece kange Nee ce na murom kange wee ce, ci yobeu cin yilam win.
MAT 19:6 Ci man yob tak la buiyo win Na nyori dike kwama mureu, kange nii a yalkande.
MAT 19:7 Co ci yice, “La ye bui Musa yinyo ki nyiyal nyo tual nawiye nin na'aka nyo ywaco take?
MAT 19:8 La co yici bikwan nerer kumer, co dok muca ciya kumen ko tual nawiyenin Na'aka ki kaba kebo nyo.
MAT 19:9 Ma yi kom ti nii wo tual wii ce nin neu naka, na kebo borutom.
MAT 19:10 Bibei tomangeceu yico nawo nyo nii kange wii ce di, yorbo a na'aka.
MAT 19:11 La Yecu yi ki “Kebo kwarub a yo merang kako tiye, la kan co nubo cia cinen cia yowe.
MAT 19:12 Kangem wii wuro bou ci Teeni (Combilome) Nyo tak di kangem wi buro yilamTeeniu ki ker Liyaro lo kwama. wo a yo merangka ko wo tiyeu ayo.
MAT 19:13 Co ci bou cinen ki bibeiyo biduwatinim na ci yo cinenkang dor, kwob cinen dilo, “La bi bei tomange ceu erang ci ti.
MAT 19:14 La Yecu Yii ci, ko dob bibeiyo bidu wattinum bo ko ywa cire bou kako kami wori liyaro lo kwamau ki wang ciko.
MAT 19:15 La con yoti ka'ani ceu dor cir na nimde co dob fiye co.
MAT 19:16 La nii kange bou fiye Yecu wiye tok ki “Nii meranka, nangen do ken do wini ma matiye nan fiya dume dii yeu?
MAT 19:17 Yecu yi co ye bwi mo meye kerti dor nangen nero kene? win cuwab dong dong, no mo cuiti mo do ken mor dumedi, bwnag ten wer funero,
MAT 19:18 nii co yii co ki wer funero wini? Yecu yico “Tuwalde nii mare buro tum, kuure kwi, ma'are warke niyer ker,
MAT 19:19 Ne Tee mwe kange Nee mwe dur, na cui nii bi dom kange mweu na dor mwer.
MAT 19:20 Bwe bwantn yile wo yi co, mim man buro gwam yee ma mati take?
MAT 19:21 Yecu yii co, na mo cuiti na yilam dong dong di, ya'a miyem dike mo cike gwam, na kabkang nob bune bo nen di na mon fiya ciwekako dii Nimde na bou na bwanten ten
MAT 19:22 La be bwa yile wo ki fir nerer wori con nii cuwe cuwe.
MAT 19:23 Yecu yi bi bei tomange ceu, Bi com ma yikom ti, a yilam bwai yo na nii cuiwe-cuiwe na do liyar kwamar.
MAT 19:24 Yila ma yi ten komti an la telem bo min a doken buwak bilifirak kange wo nii cuiwe -cuiwe a do liyar kwamar tiyeu”
MAT 19:25 bibei tomange ceu nuwa nyori, yila cinen ki nyomanka bicom cikii we a fiya cerka tiye?
MAT 19:26 Yecu to ti cici, fiye nubo wiye man i a mati, la fiye Kwama wiyeu dikero gwam ki maman.
MAT 19:27 Bitru karu ki, Nyon dubom dikero gwam nyon bwangten nen. La ye ya fiya tiye?
MAT 19:28 Yecu yici bi com ma yikom ti, kom wo ka bwang men teneu, ki boro fuir ko kwama wo bi bwe Nii a yi kenti kutile Duktangka ceu, kom keneu ka yii dor kutileni kwob cilombo yobe nin, kom ma tuwe luweu kwob cilombo yobeu Iciraila nin bolangti.
MAT 19:29 Na nubo dubom loni, yitob cib, bayilob natub, Tee Nee, bibei kange tanki ni ki den miredi, an fiya kirito kwini kwob can fiya dume dii ri Yeu.
MAT 19:30 La nubo ducce buro kabou na weu ci an yilam buiyok, nubo ducce wo buiyeu ci an yilam kabak.
MAT 20:1 liyar do kwama ki na nii Ta'ake kange wo cerki kimuomje do nob nangeneb buro ama nangenti taake ceu
MAT 20:2 kombo ci tokka ngum kange nob nangenebbo ti naiyo win ki diye, ci tung ci taake cecia ma nangendo
MAT 20:3 lacon certen ki kam kaneko tereu lacon to nob nangeneb kangem tirangum konimiye kulenek
MAT 20:4 laco yici ko ya'a tabke mi man ne kom dike dong dongeu co ci ya cima nangende.
MAT 20:5 yika con certen tak ki kang keneko kwob yob, con fiya kangem co ma na kabau
MAT 20:6 yila con certen ka kiyaka naku ked, co ya con fiye kange nob tiram koni laco yici ye bui ka tirangum koni na kwam kakuko we?
MAT 20:7 won kange nii mani wo tu'u nge. lacon yici kom keneu ko ya ta'a ke mi
MAT 20:8 kanbo mee lame di nii ta'akeu cou betomangene ceu nob nangeneb na ya'a ci nan nangener ciyero, terti nubo cuwa bwireu naya ciko nobkababo.
MAT 20:9 kambo nob nangerneb wo ca tu'u ciki kumji yadi lane ci naiyo win-win.
MAT 20:10 kambo nob nangeneb kababo bou weri, cikwati cina ocum nyo la ci keneu cone ci naiyo win-win.
MAT 20:11 kambo ciyom nan nangener ciyereri, laci ti funan dor nii ta'a ke donin
MAT 20:12 cikii nob nangenebbo wo cowa bwireu ma kan kenko wimbiwine fiye nangne la yila mon tu'u kenci dong-dong kange nyo, wo nya twal bwiyeu kange cilon.
MAT 20:13 la nii ta'a ke kari yiciki farub, ma ma kumembo kange dike kebo dong-dong geu ka ciya men bo kama naiyo win-win ka?
MAT 20:14 Tamdike na mweu na ta nure mweu. macui co ma ne nob nange nibo cuwa bwireu dong-dong, na wo mane komeu.
MAT 20:15 wendi kebo dong- dong nama dike cuiye ki dike namiye ka? kaka kor kamatiye ki dike mamani dong donge ka?
MAT 20:16 cuwo nyo, nob bwikob cia yila nob kabab, nob kababo ayila nobo cuwa bwireu. conubo duccu nubo biduwar kwakwabe cokcoke
MAT 20:17 kanbo Yeecu yakenti wurcalima di con yaten kange kwob cilombo yobeu cungeca, dor mirer laco yici.
MAT 20:18 ko to bo ki kwin mor wurcalima, an ne ken bibwe nifire kan liya nob wabeb kange tual kak
MAT 20:19 cian neken co kang nubo kumtacilib na ci buo cona malli co, na kungum co
MAT 20:20 la weebe beyo lo Jabadiu bou Yeecu nin kange bibei bayulobe ce yobe beu co cung cunge naco la con me kange diker cinen.
MAT 20:21 Yeecu yico yee no cuitiye / lacon, toki moki bibeyo lomi wo yobe ayi, win kangko catiyere win kangko mokere, mor liyare mwe.
MAT 20:22 la Yeecu yico mo nyom dike wo mo metiyeu. mon dolum mo nomki kwelmwenge woma dadom nokaka? lacin yii co nyan dolum.
MAT 20:23 co yii ci kwelmwenge miu cuwo kan dolum noka, layimbo kangko catiyere kange mokeu, ke bo ma ne tiye, na nubo buro na ciye teemi yuelum yuele.
MAT 20:24 kambo tanggnim bibei tomangeceu kwobeu mwo wodi, cin man funer kange yitob bo wo yobeu
MAT 20:25 la Yeecu coci fiye cowiyeu yii ci kom nyom liyabbo tam ki nubo kuntacili yeu nung cinen liyarti, nubo dorko cinen loreu nung cinen bikwanti
MAT 20:26 mani ayilati nyo tiber kumer. tano nayori nii wo cuiti na co yilam du'ur more kumedi tamcan yila canga kume.
MAT 20:27 la nii wo cuiti na co yilam nii kaba kumedi co a yilam canga kume
MAT 20:28 kanbo bi bwe nifire boubo na ci co dur, lana cone dur na co ne ken ten dume ce fanka nubo kila-kilau.
MAT 20:29 la ci cer jenko, mwerkanka nubeko ducce bwang cinen tene
MAT 20:30 la cin to fukmatini yob yirongum kong nure, la fukmatinim bo nuwa Yeecu ciu tiyedi, lacin kung dirciro citi toki, Teluwe bi bwe Dauda nuwa cini nyeu.
MAT 20:31 la nubo ca cinen tor yii ci cia kamangum. kico nyeu, fukmatinim bou wo, yokten kung ka direk ciko laã wo kwatti yeu, tokti Teluwe bi bwe Dauda nuwa cini nyeu.
MAT 20:32 la Yeecu tin cok, cok, doki cin cou ci, la me ci ye co cuiti nan ma kume ne?
MAT 20:33 co ci yii ce, Teluwe nyo cuiti na nyo fiye to ka fiye
MAT 20:34 la Yeecu bulangi ciko neercer, coke nuwe ciyeu. ca canduwo cin fiye toka fiyek. yila cin bwang ten co
MAT 21:1 kanbo Yeecu kange bi bei tomangeceu dadom kange wurcalimari, ci yaken betafaji fiye bang jaitun ne. co Yeecu tuom bibei tomange ce ci yob.
MAT 21:2 co yii ci ko doken muan loro kakumeu, kan to kelba kange be ce ci wari. ko kwiu ci kom bou men ciko.
MAT 21:3 na kange nii yii kom dike kange dor nyo di, ko yi co Teluwe cui citi. nii co an tomu kom kici danjang.
MAT 21:4 wo mani nyo na din dukum nii duku membo toke
MAT 21:5 ko yi bi butobo ci yo na, ko to liya kume bouti kumen nii cukka duwek yim dor kelbar dor be lunjuge kelbar.
MAT 21:6 co bi bei tomangeceu cu yaci ma dike Yeecu yi ciye.
MAT 21:7 ya cin ki kelbau kange be kelbau ci miranti kulenciro cere, Yeecu kwii la yii ti dor kulenro nin.
MAT 21:8 dur nuber mirang ti kulen ciyero dor nurer, kangem bo kiyangu alu tiniu cin miranti nure.
MAT 21:9 nubo mwerum we kaco kange buiceu, cin kung dirciyero citi toki Hocana fiye bi bwe Dauda wiye, ni bibuiyere co, wuro bou ti mor dene Teluweu. Hocana fiye Teluwe wiyeu,
MAT 21:10 kambo Yeecu doken wurcalima cinarloro dim, la ci merangi we wo?
MAT 21:11 nubo lankar cinen, won Yeecu, nii durkume wo Najaret mor Galili.
MAT 21:12 co Yeecu, doken mor bi kurwabere, con yuwabkan nubo miyaran diker tiye kange buro ten dikerti moreu. co yalangum dengila nubo wo fuion kiyemer tiyeu, kange kutile nubo miye nagum fiye tiyeu.
MAT 21:13 con yii mulangum mulange lomi a yila lo dilor, lakom yilam buwak nob kub ciko.
MAT 21:14 co fukmatini kange kilenti bourangu cinene mor bi kur waber, con twan ci.
MAT 21:15 lanob bi wabero durko kange nob meranka werfunereu, cin to diker nyumankaro wo co manange cin nuwa tenbibeyo ci kun dirciro ti mor bikur waber, tokti Hocana fiye bibwe Dauda wiyeu, cin nuwa buwarum nem.
MAT 21:16 coki yii ce, mo nuwa dike ci tok tiye? Yeecu ciya ci oo laka nuwambowika, nyibibeyo bi du wadinim an buro no yiir tiyeu man dokti dur tangkako wi?
MAT 21:17 la Yeecu dubom ci cerum mor cinan lor yaken betani kuma co ca da'a wi.
MAT 21:18 la con buri kanbo ca yilau cinan loreri co nuwa wuranti
MAT 21:19 la con to tii nyingcin kong nure, con ya dimertironin laca fiya bituti mani kan layu. lacon yii tiye, betuti no nin we munen tak, danjang ko cuwo tii nyingcin dor kwicim
MAT 21:20 bibei tomange ceu tonyori, cin nyumangi ciki manyi tii nying cindo kwiddim dangjang nye.
MAT 21:21 Yeecu yila yii ci, bicom ma yii kom tii na kom wiki bilanke kwaneri manidi, kebo ka ma tii nyingcin do nine ka ma tiye, lakom toki bwen nan co bang ko wori, kom ki akom co dii, na mob ken mor caji, la an manyo
MAT 21:22 bwen na yeka keneri, kone bilenkerirti, kam nyo.
MAT 21:23 kambo Yeecu bou mor kur bi waberedi, liya wabe nubo dur nubero bonrangn cinen kambo co ma meranka tiyeu, cin toki, ki bikwan kerero wuni moma dike buro tiye, we nenen bikwan kero ce?
MAT 21:24 la Yeecu yii ci, na miu keneu man me kom ker. na kom yii yeri, man yii kom keno ki bi kwan kerero wini ma manan dike buro ti cike.
MAT 21:25 yuka mwengek yuwanako yau fe? yau dii kwama kaka, yau nubo nin? la cin tokkangi bwiti ci, ciki na bou yii boki dii kwama an yibo, ye bwi ka ne nebo bilener kange ce?
MAT 21:26 bwen bo yi bou ki bou nubo nindi, bou cuwa nuboti, wori ci gwam citu Yuwana na nii dukume.
MAT 21:27 co co la ci yii Yeecu ciki nya nyombo. co keneu con yii ci, mikeneu mani ma yii komti keno kibi kwando wini ma manangum dike buroti yeu.
MAT 21:28 lan ye ka kwabe? nii wi manangen do take duwen
MAT 21:29 bweu yii co mani ma ya ti, la ki con fulong nercero con yaken.
MAT 21:30 la nii wo ya be yobe nin tok dike co yiwo kabau. lacon manciya Tee laco yabo.
MAT 21:31 wemor be beyo wo ma dike teciye cuitiye? ciki wo kabau, Yeecu yii ci, bicom ma yii kom ti nuboyo dorti kange nob burotume an do kenten liyar kwamaro namimde kom.
MAT 21:32 Yawana bou kumen kin nure cak-cak ka ne bo bilenker kange co nubo yõ dor tiyeu. kange natub ma burotum tiyeu ne bilenker cinen. lakume bwiko wo ka tom dike wo mane, ka yoloten bo ki bui nako ne bilenker kange co.
MAT 21:33 ko cuwa tu kange danke. ma kange ni take, con fi fik take nin, con kwarum takeu, con wob bicunge yamka inabikowi, con mu dengila cuwen cuweme wo atom take tiyeu, lacon neken nubo kangem takeu kambo ci tokkangum kiyemereu, lacon cu kange bitine kange.
MAT 21:34 kambo cuwa kiye inabi ko lameri con tom canga ce kangem na yo cinen carin cari to co mor takeu.
MAT 21:35 la nob nangenebo wo tacanga buro buk wineu, ci tualum wineu, mobang wine ki ter
MAT 21:36 nii ta'ake tung ten kangem cangam, lawo ki kabau, la nob nange nebo ma cinen na wo ki kabau.
MAT 21:37 bwiko cuwo nii taãke tuom ten bibwe ce, cinenr, tokti
MAT 21:38 kambo nob nagenebo to bibwi nii ta'ake di citi tokkangi buiti ci, won co nii aca kwali to tiyeu kom bou bi twalum cona bou cam kwalito,
MAT 21:39 la cin tam bweu, ci mobkenco buim taken laci tualum co.
MAT 21:40 la nii ta'akeu boudi, ye cama nob nangenebo wuro nin tiye?
MAT 21:41 la cin yico, an tualangum, na yila ta'ake ne nangene bo bwirko buro ki mare cilong cilonge, na yila ta'ake ne kangem nob nageneb buro a yam co tiki cuakiyar inabikeu.
MAT 21:42 Yeecu yii ci ka tobo mor bifimere, tero wo nobo nin kuweti koweu, coyilan ter culangere. woki no Teeluwe nin, la yilam diker nyiman kar nuwebe?
MAT 21:43 na weu ma yi komti, antum liyar kwamaro kumer, na bitine wo ne bituti tiyeru.
MAT 21:44 nii wo yarti dor terero wori can yakcangum ki fiti. la nii wo tero yae cineti dore di ankuwan co.
MAT 21:45 la nii liya re kange faricawa cin kwa ki dike ci toktiyeri la cin nyom ki tok kange ci.
MAT 21:46 ci do tika cekori, lacin cuwa tai nubo mwerum meu, wori nubo tum co con nii dukume.
MAT 22:1 kiritti yila yici kerti ki dangke. cuki

MAT 23:1 la kiritti yi tartare kange bi bei tomangece
MAT 23:2 coki nob werfundo kange faricawa ciyim fiye muca

MAT 23:6 ki cwi yulangka fiye ti nin yimem ciyem tolnyiyer kange yulangka fiye yime ciyeu bikur kwama

MAT 23:12 gwam niwo kung dor mwor dige gwam niwo tubo dorr cere ci kebo kange ni dur
MAT 23:13 di la daten bo nyo nob mulanka kange faricawa nubo bwit kom ten nubo nin yilok doka lo kwama kom dobo kom dobbo nubo cwi doka tiyeu na dou
MAT 23:14 daten bo nyo kom nob mulanka kange faricawa nyo kom nuwa natub kwilibti do tange
MAT 23:15 da ten bo nyo kom mulanka kange faricawa nobo bwit kom bwilangti digge wimer kange tineni du wonka ni merangka win bi wine na ki kom fiyam kom mamco konidi lengtidi yulan kumero nyo di yilam ni kere ne kom
MAT 23:16 da ten bo nyo kom fukma bo yame kom wuro kom tokti niwo werum kange ku kwamari kebo kange diger lagwam niwo werum kange mwindo ku kwamari weri ce fiyem fiye yime.
MAT 23:17 kom kula fukwa tinim na wini la bidwi yere mwindo kakka ku kwama wiyeu na wo manki dwitiye mwindo
MAT 23:18 tano wo werum kange tanjilandowu cakke kebo diger tano niwo werum ki kiye mero ci yoti dor cereri weri ceu tomco
MAT 23:19 kom fukma ti nimbo na wini wo durke kimer ku kwama kakka win mwabe wuro mwer kwama nin kiyemer tiye?
MAT 23:20 tano nyo gwam niwo werunki tanjilando wucakke werum gwam co kange dige dorcere
MAT 23:21 tano niwo werum ki kwamari werum kango co wo fwer cereu
MAT 23:22 tano gwam niwo werum ki di kwamari liyar kwama kange wo yim dor cereu
MAT 23:23 daten bo faricawa kange nob mulang kanb nobo bwit kom cokkom luma renek ywerek kange kule kange lam cur la kom mirang bilengke wuro tu nyo weu. yona wucak, cire duwe, bitinke cu wura daten ka matiye kebo na wuro kom cutang. tang nini bo wiye
MAT 23:24 fukma yame mwem nuwa kungkunge nin kange dige kangem nyori mwon mim tecembo
MAT 23:25 daten bo kom nob mulangka kange faricawa nubo bwit kom nir bwim kwimkwelmwengeti kange kwele la mordi dimka bwirangke kange fitrerer
MAT 23:26 no fukma nubo bwit ter yiwelka bwim kwele kwelmweu na bwim ciyemba yimki yorak
MAT 23:27 daten bo kom nob mulankab kange faricawa nubo bwit na tuweti nim kumembo tami bitine fwor wiye kum ma curo nobo to yaran kume ko kale firer mwordi kom kuk nubo bwiyam kanga dwiti dimer kidimen
MAT 23:28 nyo fo nuwe nobo kom la firer mwor di kang bwirankeret kange nero fit mwor.
MAT 23:29 daten bo nyo kom nob mulang kab kange faricawa kom ki tuwe nob dugumeb la kom yulangum tuwe nob bilike
MAT 23:30 kom tokti komki no yitin nowi ki kwama teb nyebe nin nonyiti necibo filan curka bwi yale nob dugume

MAT 23:35 maka ko nyeu dige kom manange dwiti bwile nobo kendo gwam wo curi fo kaleweu yileken fo dor kimer tau fo bwiyale tabila yaken cuko zakka bi bwa bara kiya wuro kom twqlum co tiber kur bi wubir kange tanjilan do wuca ke

MAT 24:4 Yecu ciya, yi ci kom de kom tiyangum.

MAT 25:1 la liyar kwamaro na bi butobbo kwobbeu wo tu talkire ce la cin yaken naci to nii kibineu
MAT 25:2 nung more ce kuletini rila nug more ce yula kabo
MAT 25:3 la kambo kuletini bi butobe tutal kire ceu ci tubo nuwango kange cinen dila bi butobo yula nyeu tu nuwanger cero kange calkiretini ceu
MAT 25:5 lakambonii ki bineu tabum bwiyeri ci dugo dumti gwamceri cin darangum dum
MAT 25:6 dila kina cii kumeri cin nuwa kwaka diregi to nii bineu ko ceri, nakom co gwam wabkanco,
MAT 25:7 dila bi butobo co gam kwinangiri la cin ywellangum talkiretini ceu
MAT 25:8 la kule bi butobeu yi nubo yula, kon ne nyinen nuwang kumeko bi duwar wori talkire nyeu lombamti

MAT 25:10 kambo ci yake tiyenkakeri nii ki bineu begen dila nubo ki batiyeu cu tange co fiye nakakonin dila cin nungum nyilogo
MAT 25:11 kutang bori tangni bi bibutoi, bow la ciki te luwe, teluwe wom nyi nen
