MAT 25:13 nyori ko yi ki bati wori kon yombo diye kaka kwama
MAT 25:14 la kino na nii wo darum na yaken mor bitine kange. cin co canga tini ceuri lacin neken dige ci cikeu kanceg
MAT 25:15 win more ce cin ne talen ti nung, ki kange cine yeuri la ki kange tak cin ne talenti wiin la ci yorang talenti dong ikwan cer yila nii co yaken yamcembo
MAT 25:16 la wo yo talenti nungeu yaken cuko win dor ken cii mor nangene lacin fiya mwem talntibo kange nung
MAT 25:17 nyo takri wo yo talenti yobeu fiyau bo yob
MAT 25:18 dila canga wo yo talenti win neu cu ya wob buwakko bitineri lacin yurangum kiyeme teluwe cero
MAT 25:19 kambo kutangeri tee luwe cangetini co yilau naci kiye kemero kange ci
MAT 25:20 cange wo yo talenti nungeu, bou ki mwem talenti nung tak. ciki te luwe mwi neye talenti nung. to min fiyau mwembo talenti nung tak
MAT 25:21 teluwe ce yico ki yori kabo canga ken ki bilenke mwin ma bilnke dor digero bi dobeu matin yo nen dur dor digero duce dogen mor lumor talen mwek canga wo yo talen ti yobeb yau rki,
MAT 25:22 teluwe mwin neye talenti bokange yob too min fiyau ten mwemb talent bo kange yob
MAT 25:23 teluwe yico ki yori kabo canga ken ki bilenke mwin ma bilenke dor digero biduware matin yo nen dor digentiro duce digen mor luma te luwe mwek
MAT 25:24 la canga no yo talenti wiineu yau la cin yiki teluwe min nyimom mwin cilongi nye. lamwiki biyem fye mwi fiibe nyori mwiki mwerumnyo fiye wo watangbe
MAT 25:25 min cuwam tai rila ya min yurangum talenti meu mor bitine to wo digero na meu
MAT 25:26 dila teluwe ce ciya lanyi co ki mo canga bwir, kange dilime mwin nyumom miki biyem fiye mi fibe take miki mwerum nyofiye me watang be
MAT 25:27 nyeu mokin neken nubo ma nangen ti ben keme, mi yilau na weu miki yom kiyemer miro ki mwem
MAT 25:28 nyori yom talenti cinen di na kom neken canga wo ki talenti kwobbeu
MAT 25:29 la gwam niwo cikeri/ atin cobcinen ten la can yilam cuko duco. cike. dila kinii wo manki digereu, digero cimeneu atin tum cinen
MAT 25:30 kom merken canga bwirko kale mor kumta cii fiye ciya ci wiyeti ki kika nunekeu
MAT 25:31 ki kwama bi bwe nii fiye bow mor duktangka ceke kange nob tomangebo kangeceu, dila cin yii dor kutile duktangka
MAT 25:32 ka bumcem an mweru bitinetini gwam,
MAT 25:33 ca tin cikangum nubo win nawo nii bicire cokum dekwama mor nibetiniye catai yoken kwameu kamko cattiker, dila nebetini kanga mokke.
MAT 25:34 dila liyau an yi burowo kango cattiyer ceu ko bou wo ko fiyer temi nineu, ca kwali liyarreko ci ywel kumen ki kwama wo ci yo kwar kalereweu
MAT 25:35 wori min nuwa wura la kom neyi cari, min nuwa dilomwe la kom neye noka, min bow fabe la kom doken ki mo mor
MAT 25:36 min ya kwancer la kom dumen kwileni min nuwa bo lumauri kom cib ye mi lofucina kom ya mini
MAT 25:37 dila nubo cak -cakkeu an ciya ciki teluwe, fiyang we tonen ki wura la nyi camkimwe? kaka mwi nuwa dilo mwe tiri nyi nenen noka?
MAT 25:38 fiyang nyi tonen faberi nyi cib nene? kaka mwi kwancer di nyi du mwilene?
MAT 25:39 fiyang nyi to wi nuwa bo lumari kaka lofucinari nyi bou mwinene?
MAT 25:40 la liyau atin ciya na yiciki bilenke mi yi komti dige wo kom ma wii mor-mor kebmibo bidu war tininbo wuro ninu, ko man ki mo
MAT 25:41 la can yi buro kanko mor cekkeu, ko kubom min, kom wo ciikau ko yaken mor kire wo manki dikako ci ywel bwe kelkelenin kange nob bwangkab cekeu,
MAT 25:42 worimin nuwa wura dila kom neye bo cari, min nuwa dilo mwe, dila komneye bo noka,
MAT 25:43 min ya fabe, dila kom dobo kimo mor luwe, kwancer, dilakom dumen bo kulen, dam twirem kange lo fucina dila kom cib yebo
MAT 25:44 la ciyan ciyaken ki teluwe, fyang nyi to ki wuro kaka ki dilomwe, kaka fabe, kwancer, kaka nuwabo luma, kaka focina rila nyi mwen bo nangenne?
MAT 25:45 la can ciya cinen ciki, bilenke mi yikom, diger wo ko mabo kange nin wii mor bi duwar tininbo weri, kom ma membo
MAT 25:46 buro atin go gen mor mwe kako manki dige dila nubo cak -caeu mor dume manki dika.
MAT 26:1 kombo Yeecu dim tok ke ti towo kange ciyeri co ca yii bei tomangeceu,
MAT 26:2 kon nyomom kum kume yob na duklume yabkako na lami, laci an ne ken bibweni na ci kulken co
MAT 26:3 lanob wabeko durko kange, nubo dur nubero cin mwerkangi karak nii wabero durko coti kikayafa.
MAT 26:4 cin tokkangum nure ci tam Yeecu ti yurangum yurange na ci tallum co.
MAT 26:5 la ci ti tokiki kebo ki duklumeu kati kwalkanke kweni tiber niber,
MAT 26:6 kamob Yeecu ki no betanya lob caminu waleu
MAT 26:7 dong dong kambo co yim cunga kobiomero ci cam. cori tiyeri, co nawiye kange dou kiwer nuwanger wo kikiyemereu cor Yeecu nin ti dorcer
MAT 26:8 kambo bibei tomange cru to wo nyeri nercer. ron kaya, kim yebwi a yakcang wo ti nye?
MAT 26:9 woro tin miyem ki kiyemero ducce na neken nob bune bou
MAT 26:10 la Yeecu nyomom wuro lam yii ci, ye bwi ka ne nawiye wo dotange tinye? wo con mamen dikero yor yore
MAT 26:11 kom kir-kir kange nob bunebo, la maka fiya, yeti kir-kir.
MAT 26:12 na wo co corti nuwangko wo bwimi yeu, co mamna furka miko ce.
MAT 26:13 bi com ma yii komti na fe atok fulen ke do wo tiye fo dor bitinero wo dike nawiye wo mane an toki ken na kwa ki co.
MAT 26:14 la win mor kwob cilom bo yobenin coti Yuhuda kar yoti yeu yaken liya wabe nin.
MAT 26:15 con toki, yemo cuiti mwa neye tiye naneken niwo kangmuek di? cin cuwa cinen mwin do kwini ta'ar.
MAT 26:16 la nyeu con ta do ka nureko wo ca neken coti kang cikeu,
MAT 26:17 la kume kaba wo duklume yabkako neu bi bei tomange ceu bou cinen, la ci me co, fe mo cuiti nyo yulangum na mo camcari durlume yabkaro we?
MAT 26:18 co yii ci kom durlume cinan lor, kan fiya nii kange, ko yii co ni do mor ka toknyo kangkene takako dom, maca cari durlumer yabkaro lomo bibei tomangemiu.
MAT 26:19 bibei tomange ceu mani kanbo co yii ciyeu, ci yuelagum cari duklume yabkaro.
MAT 26:20 la ki mee con yii kange bibei tomange ceu kweb cilombo yobeu na ci can cari to.
MAT 26:21 kanbo ci ca cari to tiyeri, con yici, bicom ma yii komti win more kume an miyem ye
MAT 26:22 cin ma fir neorer, cinter meka ceko kiwinti min nyumom ke bomo na teluwe?
MAT 26:23 la co yii ci, wuro dor kangti kange mo mor kwele wineu co nii a miye yetiye
MAT 26:24 bibwe nifire an u kanbo mulangi dorcereu la kwanco nii kercer ci miye bibwe nii ye tin yor ni conin na cibou co bo di.
MAT 26:25 Yahuda wo a miye co tiyeu me co, ma nii merangka? la con yi co, mon tokum ki bwimi.
MAT 26:26 kanbo cica carito tiyeri, Yeecu tu carito yoten bibwiyer an kabkangum. con ne bibei tomange ceu, con tu cam wuro bwimi,
MAT 26:27 con tu kwelmwenge, con ma buka kangek co ca nee ciye, yii ci ko nom gwam kume
MAT 26:28 won bwiyalemi wo noro ceu wo corena tab ka bwiran kerer nubo kila-kila
MAT 26:29 la ma yii komti, mani ma no mwem inabim bo wo ti tak mano kange okm fuije mor liyare Teemi.
MAT 26:30 la ci okm nuweu, co ci cu bang jaitune
MAT 26:31 la Yeecu yii ci, gwam kume kan kottangi ker mir ki kume wo, wori mulangum mulange. man tumom nii to tiyeu, kwame ten do an yalam
MAT 26:32 la bwiko wo ma kwenunmeri, man yaken ten kumen Galili.
MAT 26:33 Bitru yii co bwentano tangnim bo anyarangum ker mwer di, mi mani ma yarti
MAT 26:34 Yeecu yii co bicom ma yinenti mor kume wo bicake na manb kiyangeri mon yi moki mo nyom yebo kirito ta'ar
MAT 26:35 Bitru yii co, bwentano ma bweya kange mori, mani ma yiti mi ma nyomnenbo la tangunim bi bei tomange cembo tokti nyo ken
MAT 26:36 co Yeecu yaken kange ci fiye wo co tike Getca maniyeu laco yii bi bei tomangeceu ka yim fo miki yankab ma koub dilo
MAT 26:37 con tu Bitru kange bibeyo lo Jabadi yobeu, kange co, con ter bulankako kange tutum nerem
MAT 26:38 la co yii ci, dumemi ki no mor bulanka wo a lamti ki mo bwareu ka yim for koma corka kange mo
MAT 26:39 con kutaken tenkab biduwar la con yarken ki tikob ceb. laco kob dilo con toki, mo Teemi na an mamdi, kweie wo a cum ye, kebo mi a bwang tentiye la an bwanten dike mo cuiyeu.
MAT 26:40 con yila bibei tomang ce nin co fiya ci dam dum lacon yii Bitru mo maka cor ti kange mo bwen na nang kenoko wina?
MAT 26:41 kom cori kom kwob dilo kati ko yarken cuwaka, yuwa tangbe kwama kom ciya, la bwiyo kwambo
MAT 26:42 coca yila yobece co kob dilo, con tok mo Teemi nona kwele wo cunin man nocori, be dike mo cuiti ye a mani
MAT 26:43 con yilau ten co fiya ci da dumti wori nuwe ciyeu tu'u kabo
MAT 26:44 con dubangum ci tak nako ta'areu, co kob dilo ti co tok tika dike kitanca tokeu
MAT 26:45 Yeecu yila bi bei tomangkace nin, la con yii ci, ko damdum duwal komti fuobi? koto kwama con dadom, la cin neken bi bwe nifire kange nob bwiran ker.
MAT 26:46 ko kwen bi ya to niwo a miye yetiyeu won lambi dom
MAT 26:47 kambo co tok keretiyeu, yafuda win mor kwob cilom bo yobeu kange nubo dur nubero. cin bou ki kulenti kange kulki
MAT 26:48 na weu, nii wo amiye Yeecu tiyeu tiibum ci yii ci nii wo ma teiceri co, ko tam co
MAT 26:49 na con bou Yeecu nin con toki, yarume nii merangka laco tei bwiciu
MAT 26:50 Yeecu yii co, farmi, ma dike mo bo makau, co ci bouwe ciyoti kanko dor Yeecu de laci tamco.
MAT 26:51 la kange, kange Yeecu ter kan ceko coku kulendo cuwalum tu'u canga nii wabe durko,
MAT 26:52 co Yeecu yii ce dokken kulen mwero fiye ce [loco] nubo wo tu kulene di a dwiya kin kulen
MAT 26:53 mo kwatiri mani maco tee mi ti ya, la can tommer dike cum wenange kwob cilombo yobeu wo nob tomangeb cebo wucakkeu?
MAT 26:54 la a ma nyi na bifumero na dim na wo tam nar ma nyeu?
MAT 26:55 la Yeecu yii nubo dim wiyeu, ka bou kin kulen kange kulki bou ko ta ye na nii kwiye? mati yii ma meranti kir-kir kur waber la ka ta yebo.
MAT 26:56 wo gwam ma nyo na dike nob dukumero na dimla bi bei tomange ceu gwam dubom co cuakkanyi cu.
MAT 26:57 nubo buro ta co Yeecu yaken ki co kayafa nin nii wabe durko, fiye nob muiangkabo kange nubo durko mwerkangum wari yeu
MAT 26:58 la Bitru bwang cinen tenti ku tan kange karak nii wabere durko con do ken mor co yii na co to dike a matiye
MAT 26:59 na weu laya wabeu kange nob tikali cebo ki to warke cuerker dor Yeecu na ci tualum co.
MAT 26:60 la fiya bo win wo. na duwaleu nob warker cwerkero kila bou kab.
MAT 26:61 la ciki nii wo ki canwerum kur wabe kwamaro na co muti mor kume ta'ar.
MAT 26:62 nii wabe kwen titiye lanme, co, mo man ki diker kar kaka? warke wini ci war ti dor mwere
MAT 26:63 la Yeecu kumom. nii wabe durko yii co mo yii nen ti ki nyal kange kwama wo ki dumeu, yii kenon mo kritti bi bwe kwama
MAT 26:64 Yeecu karcenen, mon to kum ki ko kab mon to bi bwenii yim kang ko catiyer bikwanrd, la yiranti dor bi loro dii kwama.
MAT 26:65 la nii wabe durko worbangum belleceu, ki tok kero bwir, ye bwi bou do nob warker ti dualla? koto na wo kom nuwam kero bwirko.
MAT 26:66 ye ko kwatiye? cin ciya ciki con daten buar
MAT 26:67 ci tuom cinen ti bi tom bo tikob, yila cibukten co. ci kwabanco ki kani ceyeu.
MAT 26:68 la ciki, yii bo ker dukumer mo kiritti. we wo kwa nene?
MAT 26:69 la Bitru yim kale mor karake, la bubya kange canga bou cinen yii mo ki no kange Yeecu wo Galiliu”
MAT 26:70 la Bitru kanangum kabum ciyem gwam tokti ki, ma nyombo dike motokker ti dorce reu.
MAT 26:71 kanbo co cerken nyi lo ko kaleri, kange bubya toco la yii nubo wiyeu, nii wo ken kino kange Yeecu bunajare.
MAT 26:72 yila con kanangum ten kange weri, ma nyom bo nii co
MAT 26:73 kakten nyo bi budar di nubo wo tirangum wiyeu bou yii Bitru, bicom mon wi more ciye ken wori kero mo tok tiyeu nugum nen.
MAT 26:74 la con yoten kan cilka kange weri manyombo nii co, ladanjang bi cukeu mob kiya ngeu,
MAT 26:75 Bitru kwabi ki kero Yeecu tokeu. bicake na mob kiyangeu mwan kanang ye kiro ta'ar. la con cerken kale cociwiye kefir neerer.
MAT 27:1 kambo fini celummeri, liya wabe kanga nubo dur nubero cin fuwakang nureu ciya tam Yeecu ti naci twalumceu.

MAT 27:12 dila nob webebbo durko kange nubo durko cin mwelcinen, tokbo ker,

MAT 27:22 Bilatu yi ci ye ma ma Yeecu ninti woci cuwoti kiritti dila gwamceu cii ciya akulken co.

MAT 27:25 nubo kwarub yiki, dila buyaleceu a yii ken dor nyo kange bi beyo lokyeun
MAT 27:26 la nya cinen Banaba dila ma Yeecu nin balyanyeri neken co cinen na yekom co

MAT 27:28 cin marancinen meke na nyime ci dokcinen kulendo fiyere.
MAT 27:29 cin me cinen lalam duwek cuakkek cin dok cinenti dorcer, yila cineco dango ciya tam kamce ko cal ciyere cin cunyii kabumce ci ma ci nen buuomti, ci yi ti ki dume mweu akutan nyi liya yafudawar'
MAT 27:30 cin tuomcinenti betuombo bwitak, ci yom damngo ci mweco ciko dor
MAT 27:31 kam cidim buo kace keri, cin cokum lalango cin dok ci nen kulencero, cin cin ca cin kaba ya ken kica fiye ciya kulen cotiyeu
MAT 27:32 kambo ci ciro kalere, cin kwabti bue ni bakurame kange dencero caminu, woci dokco ayakangeci natum bwatiye kulkake
MAT 27:33 cin lau fiye kange ci cuotiki goltau, wuro yitiye, kweldu wee,
MAT 27:34 cine neco mwem mwerum kange dike tweitweyeu naci nom kanbo citwiyeri lako nobo

MAT 27:36 lacin yiken ci too coti
MAT 27:37 cin mulang dike kange cin yei ci nenti dor cer yiiki wonco liya yafudane
MAT 27:38 cin yenkeco wari kange nob kub nyo yob, win neu kango cacci yerece wneu kango mwokece
MAT 27:39 burombo cutiyeu too co t, fok doroti,
MAT 27:40 laciti tokii, mwo muki mwom wurom lo kwamau yila mu mum mor kume ta'ar fulom dor mwero cile no munbi bwe kwamari yarau cuktom bwatiye nin
MAT 27:41 nyoken durem nob wabebo macinen kange nob mulamgkab kange liyab bo durembo, ciyi tiki,
MAT 27:42 fulom kangumbo la fueki fuloka dorek ceko co liya jorilawa. ciya yirau dor cuktum bwatiyem nabi ne bilinke fiye ciwuyeu
MAT 27:43 kambo ca ciya kange kwama. kwama a cerco wori cinyi ciki cimbi bwe kwama
MAT 27:44 nyo naco nob kubbowo nyo yob ci kulkenci wari yeu ci toce.

MAT 27:47 kanbo birombo timbo dmmen muwari nyeri, lacin yiki, nyi bicuor Iliyaro

MAT 28:1 ki kume kakuk fobka fiini, dadonm celti na kume winneu mor nibere. maryamu makdaliya kange maryamu, ya naci tuwe Yeecu
MAT 28:2 la bitine muka ducce, wori yuwa tangbe kwama wucake yirau di kwama bou tungum tero, yiti dor cer
MAT 28:3 yirom cembo na milbangka, la kulen cero na cuno
MAT 28:4 nubo to tuwe tiyeu cwa tai duccu, cin yilam na bilenti nibe

MAT 28:6 mani fo, kwenum na woco tokeu, tofiye teluwe daa wiye

MAT 28:9 la Yeecu fiya ci, ci ki yarume natubo bou tam naceko, wabco

MAT 28:11 fiye natubo wuro mor yameri. nobo to tuwe tiye doken cinar lor, cin yi liya nob wabeko dike maneugwam,
MAT 28:12 nob wabe kwama mwerkangi kange nubo durko, cin tokkan dike wo cange ci, cin ne nob toka tuweko kyemer duccu
MAT 28:13 cin yi ci tanne nubeu, be bei tomange ceu bou bon kum bilen cero, fiya cuwo kom da dumti

MAT 28:17 la cin to cori, cin wab co, di kangumbo ciyabo

MAT 28:19 kom ya ki dok nobo a yilam bi bei tomange ka le wo gwam kom yu'u cinen mwem ki den te, kange bwe kange yuwa tangbe wucake
MAT 28:20 kom meran cinen ciya bwangten dikero gwam wo ma yi kom ki nyial leu to mikange kom ya ciko cwile kale.
MAR 1:1 Wo co terka fulen kerer Yecu kritti bi bwe kwama.
MAR 1:2 Nawo mulangnum mwor icaya nii tomangeu, To mi tung nii tomange mii ti kabum mwem wuro a ywel mwen nure tiyeu.
MAR 1:3 Diro wo cuo bi cuor ti mwor yere ywelum nure kwamau, kom ywel nure cew na tiken cer.
MAR 2:1 kambo ci yilau kafanaum kume tini biduwar cumeu lan nuwam ki cii wii lo.
MAR 2:2 ducce mweri wi wo fiye kumbo wiyeu ki nyilocek, la Yecu yicii kero.
MAR 3:1 La Yecu yila ten mor bikur waber la nikange wo Yecu kanko nom-nokeu.
MAR 3:2 Nubo kangem cii cinen ten niwe naci to keno can tam niwo ki kakon fobka di na ci mwelcinen ti dor.
MAR 4:1 La con ter merankako kong caji. nubo kilakila mwrum wi kentangum co, ta con doken mor nabire menge mor caji con yiken morcer. Nubo mwerum wiyeu yim ciye dukle kong caji.
MAR 4:2 La co merang cinen dikero ducce ki dangke, mor merangka ceko con yiki.
MAR 5:1 Cin beken dinge caciyo wineu mor Gerasenes.
MAR 5:2 Na wo dang Cang, la Yecu yiram mor nabire kange nii kidwiti yuwa cerou mor twe tinin con wakanco.
MAR 6:1 Nobom ci con dou cinanlorciye, bi bei tomange ceu bwangu co.
MAR 6:2 Bi diye fobkako bo con do bilkur waber co merang cimenti. Nubo duce nuwa meranka ceko diger nyomanka tam ci. ciki fiya merankakowo fee? Yilen do wini kwama nece nye? nangen nyomanka ko wini co mati ki kang ceke?
MAR 6:3 Kebo bibwe nii kwanka kuweko wabi bwe maryamu, yii Yakubu kage Yoci kange Yahuda kange Caminu? Kebce bo natubo wo bo wari kange ci? ci nuwa bo luma nerciyer ki Yecu.
MAR 7:1 Faricawa muri yecunin kange nob mulankabo firen Urcalima
MAR 8:1 ki kumetin dowo, nakali mwer kangka nubek, laciman kicari
MAR 8:2 Yecu cwo nob bwang kaceb yiciki mici bwini nubo wuroti wuri lamkume taar ciwari kan-nge moo cari mani. n
MAR 8:3 non yokenci miniya yilarenggen loci cari maniri ciyan cuwela nure wori loniceu kutagnyii kabo.
MAR 8:4 nob bwangka cebo ciya yiki, ba fiya tillita wurofe mor kiye wuro alam nubo wuro nyeu?
MAR 9:1 cin yici bibicum min yikom kangem ki membo wii timfo mani ciya to bwar ti na nimde ci to liyar kwama bou cinen kibi kwan,
MAR 9:2 kume nugkun cume Yecu tu yowana filibu kange Yakubu kange co dii dor banger do cwemet ki kwaci
MAR 9:3 la fulongum bwici kabum ciye ni kulendo bwiceu fuwo kulek miblanti miblanti cum na dige kange forkalewo
MAR 10:1 Yeecu dubonm fiye cure yakin chinge biten urdun la nubo nya cinen co meran cinen kambo yilam na dum ci ceyerm be.
MAR 10:2 Lafaricawa bou ci nen citokki, dong dongka nina twal wice nin naka? me kewo cimane naci cuwa co.
MAR 10:3 Ciya cimen nye mu ca yi ko na kom ma ne?
MAR 10:4 Muca ki mulang bifumer twalka naka yiken wi mweca cirli.
MAR 11:1 nawo cibo Urcalima cibi dom kange Betafaji kange Betanya fiye bang zaituneke. yeecu tom bi bei tomange ce yob
MAR 11:2 Yi ci ki kom domor cunkurdo wo bi dom kange be, yo kodoti nyori kan to beikelba tekum, wo nii kwimbo wiye, kom kwiu combõmen ciko
MAR 11:3 Tano kange yi co kom ki nye bweiye, kom yi co kom ki teluwe co cwitiye, an yilau ciko comnawo
MAR 12:1 Yecu yo meranka cinenti ki dange, coki nii kange wii twi take ce, kwarum, con wob buwak yamka? biti kam no maka naneg mor take. lam cuken bitine.
MAR 12:2 Cwakiya law con tom kange ya ayocinen bitungtunge mor take.
MAR 12:3 Nom takebo taco buk cu ywico kam koni.
MAR 13:1 Yecu Ceru bikurwab wiin mor nom bukacebor yi cui ni meranka. to iker yumaka yabraka terek ko wo kange yobraka luwatimuwo.
MAR 13:2 Yicu ki, mun to yobraka luweinbowura? bero nakye man wu a dob ti dr kece, mana buubatiye.
MAR 14:1 Duklume yabka, wo carito camfuwmbo maniye kum kume yob, durtinin nob wabebo, kange nob mulangkab werfunero cin do kambo ciya tam Yecu tiyeu yurangum yurange na cin bwalum co la.
MAR 14:2 ciki kebo ki duklume kari bouki kyan tiber neber.
MAR 15:1 La ki kwomceri nubo durko cin mwerkanye kange nubo dur mulanka, kange nubo durko. Cin tam Yecu cinyo cou kab, cin neken cou kan Bilatu.
MAR 15:2 Bilatu mee cou mwo dur liyar Yahudawa ka? con ciya ci kii ywo nawo mwa tikeu.
MAR 15:3 La nubo dur firitoci cin bou kii cwarum cembo ci ma co Yecu neneu.
MAR 16:1 Kambo diye fufkako lame di Mari kange Magdaline nee Jame, colomi tenou nowan beltika wo ciya belti Yecu nen tiyeu.
MAR 16:2 Kii kwamce kume wine na kume nibere, cin yari tuwe wumom na nimde kakoko curou.
LUK 1:1 Nubo ɗuce wo tum nangen mulangka dor digero wo tim ɗong ɗong more beu,
LUK 1:2 Nawo bou binen kang nubo wo kaba tom nuwe kanga nuweu kange cangatini kereu.
LUK 1:3 La yilam yarak tak minen wori min fuwam ɗigero wiyak ki kaba, nan mulang mwen ɗigero wo wank ki wank nii la ɗureu Tiyofila.
LUK 1:4 Nyori na mwi nyimon bilenke dikero ci merang mweneu.
LUK 1:5 Ki kumeni Hiridu liya Yahuda, nii wabe kange wi dendo Zakariya wo mwanlor Abija; Wice Alicabatu ken naniyak Haruna.
LUK 1:6 Gwam ce ci cak-cak ka kwama (ci manki) kurom mor werfun kange bidoti te luwe.
LUK 1:7 Dila ciman ki bwe wori Alicabatu Combilome, ri cin cirarangum gwance.
LUK 1:8 La kambo Zakariya ka kwama ma nangentini nii waberti wo bwangten cokka ce keu.
LUK 1:9 Ki nure ciki bwangten de naci cok nii wabe wo a wabtiyeu, la cin cok co ki dajen naci doken mor bi kur wabe Teluwe naci tui nuwanko ficange.
LUK 1:10 Mwerka nibe ko gwam kuob dilo ti kale ki kwama wo nuwanko ficangeu tui tiye.
LUK 1:11 La bwetomange Teluweu cer cinen lan tiken cattiyer tancilan ficanger.
LUK 1:12 Kambo Zakariya toceri, kwomco, la taito tanco.
LUK 1:13 Dila bwe tomange kwama yico “Cuware tai Zakariya, wori cin nuwam dilo mweu. Wi mwe Alicabatu an bo mwen bwe. Mwi Co dencero Yowana.
LUK 1:14 Mwan yikam ki bilangtum kange fuwor nere, la nubo kila a bilangti ki borcere.
LUK 1:15 Wori Canyi lan ki dur kabuni Te-luwe. Mani co no mwem bi tuittuibti kaka diker no karo kwam kwame, Catin din ki yiwa tangbe ko wucakeu mor fwiye nece.
LUK 1:16 Naniyak Iciraila ko duce wo a yila cuko Teluwe kwama Cenen.
LUK 1:17 Can ya kabum Teluwe mo yu wa tangbo kange bikwan Iliyak, Na yilau ki ner tebembo bibeyo nen kange wo bongi nyeu na ya mor nyomka cak-cake -na ci Ywel te luwe nin nubo wo ci cok cineneu.”
LUK 1:18 Zakariya yi Bwetanange wucake “Ma nyom dike wo nyi? wori min cele ri wimi coro kilam”.
LUK 1:19 Nii tomangeu wucakeu Ciya yicoki “Mo Jibrai'lu, wo tire kabum kwamau. Cin tomu ye nami yinen ker, nan bo mwen ki kero lomlome.
LUK 1:20 La to! Mwan yilam cōk, mani mwa dol tokka kere ti, dila diya dikero buro dimmeri ntimade. Wori mwi nebo bilenker ker miro nin, wo a diiti ki kwama dong-donge
LUK 1:21 La nubo ningtang Zakariya ti. Cin nyimangi wori cinti lenger mor bikur waber.
LUK 1:22 Dila ki kwa'ma ci ceruweri, dolbo yici ker. La ciin nyimom ki cin to dukum ki kwamawo ci mor bikur-wabereu. La cin nungkancinen ti ki kank worimani citok ker ti.
LUK 1:23 La yilam kambo kumeni nanger cero cume ri, cin cu lo co.
LUK 1:24 Kambo kume ni wo cumeri, wice Alicabatu tum fwer la cin yu rangum dorceri na cuwako nunge ce. Cin yiki,
LUK 1:25 “Wo lo diker kwama mamene kambo ci toye ki corciniyeu, naci tum kwenduwe miu ka nobe.
LUK 1:26 Ki ciwako nukkune, kwama tom nii tomange wuccake Jibrailu mor Cinanlor Galili ci coti ki Nazaret,
LUK 1:27 bubiya nin wo cine ken nii kange wo den cero Yucufu, wo naniyak Dauda, la bubiya dendo Maryamu.
LUK 1:28 Cin bow Cinenri ciki, “A Ysrumnen, mo wo fiya cini ducce! Teluwe wi kange mo”.
LUK 1:29 La cin kulongum duce, ki kercero la cin kwabi, ya rume ye wo.
LUK 1:30 Bwe tomange wuccake yicoki, “Cuware tai, Maryamu, wori mwin fiya cini kwama nin.
LUK 1:31 To, mwan tu fwed ri na mwi bo bwe. Mwa cun den cero 'Yecu'.
LUK 1:32 Can yilam nii dur la ci cuu ki Bibwe nii dur re. Teluwe kwama atin ne co kuti le liyare Tekwace Dauda.
LUK 1:33 Can ma liyar dor lo Yakubu diiri, Liyar cero manki dika”.
LUK 1:34 Maryamu me bibwetomange wuccake ki; “Dike wo a bwinyi la mi nyumumbo nii na bare wiyeu?”
LUK 1:35 Bibwe tomange kwaama ciya ri yi co ki, “Yuwa tangba kwamako an bow mwinen, ri bi kwan nii dur reu atin bow dor mwer. La wucakke wo mwi bo tiyeu a coki Bibwe kwama.
LUK 1:36 To, na niya mweko Alicabatu tu fwer ki ciraka ceko. Wo co cuwiyak ceko mukkune, co wo no ci cuoti ki combilomeu.
LUK 1:37 Di kero kange mani wo mani a mati kabum kwama”.
LUK 1:38 Maryamu yi ki, “To, min bubiya canga kwama. A yila men na tomange meu”. Dila bwe tomange kwama dob co.
LUK 1:39 Dila Maryamu kweni ki kume tini co wulom wulom yaken mor bi ten kongtini, yaken bi ten Yahuda.
LUK 1:40 Ciin yaken mor luwe Zakariya ri cin yarum Alicabatu.
LUK 1:41 Yilam kambo Alicabatu nuwa yarume Maryamu ri bwe mor fwe ce mokangi la Alicabatu diim ki yuwa tangbako wucake.
LUK 1:42 Ciin kung dir cero kibi kwan ciki, “Mwin nii bi bwiyere mor natube, ri nii bwiyere bwe wo mor fwiye meu.
LUK 1:43 Ye bwi wo fiya yenye, la ne Te luwe mi a bou ti mi nene?
LUK 1:44 La ta kambo diir yaru mer mwero bou tu miyeri bwe fwe.
LUK 1:45 Nii bi bwiyere co nawiye wo ne bilenke ki digero wo ciyi co fiye kwama wiye atin dii me.
LUK 1:46 Maryamu yiki “Dume miu caklang Te luwe
LUK 1:47 re, yuwa tangba miu bilangi kwama nii cyer yerenin.
LUK 1:48 Wori cin to cukka dorek bubiya canga ce. La to, nawo kange kab kaltini gwam a co yeki nii bi bwiyere.
LUK 1:49 Wori co, wo nii bi kwaneu, ma men digero dur, la den cero wucak.
LUK 1:50 Jire duwe ceu tii nyo kal ya ciko kaleu ki buro wo nuwa taicero tiyeu.
LUK 1:51 Cin nung bi kwancero ki kank cek, cin yalum buro ki kunka duwek keu ki dike ci kwati neer cere.
LUK 1:52 Cin cukkangum bi bei liyabbe dor kutile cero nin, la cin kungum nob fuebbo.
LUK 1:53 Cin cam ki nob wurabbo ki diketi no ken, dila nubo cuwe cuweu cin yoken ci kang kwicer.
LUK 1:54 Cin ne canga ce Iciraila tikali, nyori naci kwabi naci nung jire duwe
LUK 1:55 (Nawo ci yi tebbe beu) ciyi Ibrahim kange naniyak ceke diri.
LUK 1:56 Maryamu yi kange Alicabatu cuyako ta'ar ri cin yilaken lo co.
LUK 1:57 La kwama bou na Alicabatu a bom bwi bwece, la cin bou bwe bwayile.
LUK 1:58 Nubo bi dom kange ca kange na niyak ceko nuwa ki kwama nung cinen Jire duwe ce durko, la cin bilangi kange co.
LUK 1:59 La yilam ki diye naruberi cin bow naci mwatum lar bwero. Ciikin cuom co “Zakariya”, na den te cero.
LUK 1:60 Dila neele ciya ki o, onga. “A cuoco ki Yuwana”
LUK 1:61 Cin yicoki, “Nii kange man mor naniya kumek wo cico tiki dendo we”.
LUK 1:62 Cin nung tece ninki kang kambo ci cuiti naci ne co dendeu.
LUK 1:63 Tece me ci ya neco ter mulankar la cin mulangi, “Den cero Yohanna”. Cin nyimangi gwam dor dikero wo.
LUK 1:64 Dangjang dangjang nyi ceu wumom ri la biyen cero fiya cyer ka. cin tok ker la cin cak lang kwama.
LUK 1:65 Taito bou dor nubo gwam wo yim Cunga cekeu. Kerowo yalati gwam mor biten kongni Yahuda.
LUK 1:66 Nubo gwam wo nuwa ri, yoken mor nere ce, tokti ki “La ye bwewo a yila tiye?” La kang Te luwe ko wi kange co.
LUK 1:67 Tece Zakariya diim ki yuwa tangbe ko wuccake la tok ker dukumer, ki
LUK 1:68 “Caklanka fiye Teluwe wiye, kwama Iciraila, cin bow naci ma tikali la cinma nob cebo nin cerka.
LUK 1:69 Cin kung binek cume fuloka lo canga ce Dauda,
LUK 1:70 (nawo ci tokki nyi nob tomange ceu kwattiye),
LUK 1:71 fuloka nob kiyeb beu kange nubo wo kwerbo nyeu.
LUK 1:72 Can ma wuro naci nung, tebbe bo nin jire duwe ri la naci kwa nor cero wucak keu,
LUK 1:73 weri wo ci yii tebo Ibrahim.
LUK 1:74 Cii weri naci nebo co kambo ci cokum bo kange nob kiyeb bekeri, nabi bwangci nenten kibi kwan neret
LUK 1:75 mor wucakke kange cak-cake kabum cem ki kumetinibeu kale we nin gwam.
LUK 1:76 O, kange mo, bwe, ciya co nen ki bwe tomange nii durre, la mwan yaken kabum tikobe Te-luwe ri na mwi ywel nure ceu, na mwi ywel nubo ki boka ceko
LUK 1:77 na ne nob cebo nyom ka fulokak ki tab ka bwirank kerer cero.
LUK 1:78 Wo an bwi wori jire duwe kwama beu duwi kabo, wo kercer di filango ceru dii yeu atin bou na tikangbo,
LUK 1:79 na ne filang ki nubo wo yim kumta cilenen kange kakulok bwareke. Ca tin ma wuro na bwangten ki nabe ko mor nure lima nereke
LUK 1:80 La bweu dwi la yilam ki bi kwan mor yuwa tangba, la ciki no mor yere na nyimde diye ci ter cerkako yanglang Iciraila.
LUK 2:1 La ki kumetini co, kaicar Augusta tung tomange cin toki ciki a kiyeu nubo gwam wo yim dor bitinereu.
LUK 2:2 Won co kiye ka kaba maneu ki kwama wo kiriyuc ma liyar ti curiya.
LUK 2:3 La nubo gwam yarangen cinanlor cer naci mulangum ki kiye kakor.
LUK 2:4 Yucufu ken kwenu Galili wo mor cinanlor Nazaret la cin yaken Yahuza, cinanlor Dauda, wo cuoti Baitalomi, wori ciki no naniyak Dauda.
LUK 2:5 Cin yaken wi naci mulangum dercero kange Maryamu wo ci bob beu la ki fwer.
LUK 2:6 La kambo ci wi ye ri, kwama lam wo ci bom bwe tiye lam.
LUK 2:7 Cii bo bwe bibare, bwe kaba ce, la cin kwomum co ki yilang ko cuwe mer la yoken co mor tokum nennem wori ci man ki fiye wi.
LUK 2:8 La nob biyuwareb bo wi cungako co ci dami ner bitibere to bi cir cero ti ki kume.
LUK 2:9 Bwe tomange Te luweu cer cinen, la duktangka Te luwek ko tebum cunga ceko, la cin dim ki tai ducce.
LUK 2:10 Dila Bwe tomange kwama yici “Ko cuware tai, wori mi bo kumen ki kero ken wo a bou hi ki fuwor nerero dur nubo nin gwame.
LUK 2:11 Duwen cin bo kimen nii fuloka mor cinan lor Dauda! Cin Kiritti Te luwe!
LUK 2:12 Wo co yirombo wo ci nekom tiye, kam fiya bweu kumon mor yilango cuwemer, yom mor tokum nennem.
LUK 2:13 Dangjang ri bwe tomange kwama kange mwer kamka dur ko dii kwa'ma caklang kwama ti ciki
LUK 2:14 “Duktanka ki kwama firen dii, rila fuwor nere a fiya tiber nubero co (Kwama) ciyacike.
LUK 2:15 La yilam kambo bi bei tomange kwama dubom ci yilaken dii lo kwamari, nob bi warebbo yi bwiti ci, “na weu ko biya Baitalami nabi to dikero wo bwiyeu, wo Teluwe nung bi neneu”
LUK 2:16 cin cu wulom-wulom wii dila cin fiya Maryamu, Yucufu kange bwe fiyerko dam mor tokume.
LUK 2:17 Kambo ci tom ceri, cin yi nubo dikero cii yi cii dor bwe fiyerko weu.
LUK 2:18 Gwam wo nuwari, ma nyimanka dor dikero nob bi yuwarebbo yi ci yeu.
LUK 2:19 Dila Maryamu ki bulangi dor digero ci nuwa gwam, la cin yoken mor nerece.
LUK 2:20 Nob bi yuwarebo yilaken ci duktangi ri ci caklank kwama ti ki dikero gwam woci nuwau kange wo ci toweu dong-dong nawo ci yi ciyeu.
LUK 2:21 Kambo kume narube dimeri, fiyaco ci biye cinen lareu cin ne co dendo Yecu, dendo bwe tomange kwama ne na nyinde cii tu fwer cereu.
LUK 2:22 Kambo kumeni wucakeu ce cumeri, na wo mor wer fun mucaro, ciin bou ki co bikur waber mor Urucalima naci neken co kwama nin.
LUK 2:23 Nawo mulangum mor werfun Te luwe “Gwam bwe kabo wo bwayileri, atin cokum co ki dimen, cina kwama ce.
LUK 2:24 La cin ma wabka nawo ci toki mor werfun Te luwe re, “nagum fe yob kakaa kalti nawurmero yab”
LUK 2:25 La Nii kange wi Urucalima wu dencero cimon ne, ni wo cak cak laci ne dor bwanka kwama. Ciki ningtan nii a bii Iciraila nin neer tiye, la yuwa kange kwamak wi kange co.
LUK 2:26 La yuwa tangbe kwamako nungcine ki mani ci bwiyati ne citom Kiritti Teeluweri nyinde.
LUK 2:27 La yuwa tangbe kwamako ya ki co mor bi kur waber. Kambo Teb bwe fiyerko Yeco bou kice, naci macinen nawo werfundo nungeu,
LUK 2:28 cin tu beu kangcek ri cin caklang kwama, ciki,
LUK 2:29 na weu dob bwe canga meu akubo ki fuwor neret Teluwa nawo mori tokeu.
LUK 2:30 La nuwe mi tom fuloka mweko,
LUK 2:31 wo mwi yweli nuwe nubo gwammer:
LUK 2:32 filang dukumek wo nubo kumta cili cee kange duktangka wo nubo lomwe Iciraila ce.
LUK 2:33 Tee ce kange nee ce ma nyimankka ki dike ci toki dorce reu.
LUK 2:34 Cimon yocinen bibwiyer, ri yi Maryamu nece ki “Nuwa Yora, bwewo cin co ki na boki yare kange kwenka nubo duce Iciraila na yirome wo ci kowe
LUK 2:35 kange kulen wo abiye ken mor nere mwetiye rila bi kwarum nerem bo kila atim ceruu”.
LUK 2:36 Nawiye tomange kwama ci cuo ti ki Anna wiwi. Cibi bwe Panuel naniya Acar. La cin duyom ki cotini duce, cin yi kange bwece coro kwini niber,
LUK 2:37 la cin nawi ye kwale coro kwini narub-cilombo na'ar. La mani ci dob mor bi kur wabe ri ci wab kwama ki ngak ngake kange dilo kume kange kakuk.
LUK 2:38 Ki kwama co dondong cin kwitau laidom kange ci, ri cin ter buka kau kwama, la cin yi nubo ningtang fuloka Urcalima kotiye ker dor bwero nin.
LUK 2:39 Kambo ci dim digero da ter cin matiye nawo mulangum mor werfun Teluwere di, cin yila keu Galili mor cinanlor ceer Nazaret.
LUK 2:40 La bwen duyom yilam kibi kwan, kange nyomka, la luma kwama wii cinen.
LUK 2:41 Ki cor teb ce bo ki yam nyo Urucalima ki duklume yabka.
LUK 2:42 Ki kwamawo ci dim coro kwabcilom bo yebeu, cin yaken tag duklumenin.
LUK 2:43 La kambo ci diim kumeni duklume gwame ri, cin ter yila kako loweu. La beu Yecu tim ce bwi mor Urucalima ri la teb cebo nyombo.
LUK 2:44 Ci kwotiri ciki no mor mwerka nube kowo ci yaken ti wari yeu. La cin ya yam kume wiine. Di cin ter doka ceko mor naniya cek kange farub cek.
LUK 2:45 Kambo ci fiya ceberi, cin yila ken mor Urucalima la cin ter doka ceko wi.
LUK 2:46 La bwiko kume taare ri cin fiyamco mor bikur waber, yim tiber nob merangkab merangci ke tiniti.
LUK 2:47 La gwam wo nuwa ce ri, ma nyimangka ki nyomka ceko kange ciyaka ceko.
LUK 2:48 Kambo ci toceri, nyimankako tamci, la nee ce yico ki ““ye bwi mwa manyo nye? To, tee mwe kange mo nyi do nen ti ki kwomka duce.” Cin yici, “Ye bwi kom doye tiye? Ko nyombo kambo mamanangen mira?”
LUK 2:49 Con yi ci, ye bwi kom do ye tiye? kom nyomba tam nyo ma nangen Temera?
LUK 2:50 Di ci nyombo dike co yi ti kange kero co toke.
LUK 2:51 La cin yaken lo kange ci mor Nazaret la ci nee ci dur ti. Nee ce yoken diker buro gwam mor nere ce.
LUK 2:52 Dila Yecu ki duwi mor nyomka kange cuwemka la cin fiya cor cini kwama nin kange nob.
LUK 3:1 Mor coro kwob cilombo nung wo liyar Tibariyuc, la Bilatu Buntu bwangtentiki Yahuda, Hiridu co liya Galili, yice Filibu liya cungako Ituriya kange Tirakonitic, la Licaniyac liya Abiliya,
LUK 3:2 ki kwama Annac kange kayafa nob wabe bo dur keu - ker kwamaro bou Yohana bibwe Zakariya nin mor yere.
LUK 3:3 Cin ya mor bitenni gwam wo cunga caji Urdun ne. Ne fulen ker yika mwenge yilokati na fiya tab ka bwiran kerer.
LUK 3:4 Nawo mulangum mor bi fumer Icaya nii tomange dukumeu, “Diro wo cuo bicor timor yere ko ywelum nure Teluwe, kom tim ki nure ceu ciyer.
LUK 3:5 Bunglunge gwam atim dim, la bangtini gwam kange dukletini atin daken, nureni nyon langi nyeu atin tiken ciyer, fiye bweyang bweyangeu atim twilangum na yilam nure,
LUK 3:6 la nubo gwami auto fuloka kwama”.
LUK 3:7 La Yohanna ji nubo bouti cinen naci yu cinen mwembeu “Kom biwei fangeb! we yi com ki kom cuwa funer wo yautiye?
LUK 3:8 Nyori, kom ne bibeyo wo daten yilaka kumeke, la ko yire dor kimero kom ki “nyin wi tee nye Ibrahim”. La mi yi komti, kwama atin kung Ibrahim nin naniya teren ti wo nin.
LUK 3:9 Wo na weu, biliyeu yom niti tiyer. La tiyo wo nebo bi tuttiyeri atin tom na merken mor kire.
LUK 3:10 Dila nubo ti meka ceko “Ye nya matiye?”
LUK 3:11 Cin ciya cinen ciki, “No kange kume wi ki belle yob ri, ca ti kangum kange nii womancike, wo ki cariyeri a mani nyo ken”.
LUK 3:12 Nob yoka doreb bou ken naci yu cinen mwembo, la cin yi co ki “Nii merangka, ye nyi matiye?
LUK 3:13 Ciin yi ci, “Ko yore kemero a cure dike ci yi kom ko yoweu”
LUK 3:14 Kangem nob kweneb me co ken ki “La nyeu? Ye nyi matiye?” Cin yi ci “Ko yore kemer nii nin kibi kwam ri, ko mwelde nii nin ker ki cuwerke. Ko bulang ki kemer cuwakek kumeko
LUK 3:15 La kambo nubo ningtang bo ka Kiritti tiye ri gwam ce ki kwai mor nere ce dor Yohanna keno co Kritti ri.
LUK 3:16 Yohanna ciya cinen gwam, “Miu, miki yu kumen bwembo ki mwem la kange wi ber wo laye bikwaner, ma labo wo ma kiwi duka ta ceko tiyeu. Ca yu kumen mwembo ki yuwa tangbe kwama kange kira.
LUK 3:17 Kwel yuka ceko kino kang cek na nyinangum tene ceu na mwerken bikate mor bini. La ca tin twim fwirito ki kirako man ki domka”.
LUK 3:18 Ki weranka duce tak, Yohanna yi nubo fulen kerero ken ti.
LUK 3:19 Kambo ci werank Hiru liya ki naka wi yi ceko Hirudiya, kange dikero bwiir tini kangem bo Hiridu maneu.
LUK 3:20 Cin cob ten ki buro gwam, ri cin kum Yohanna fucina.
LUK 3:21 La kambo nubo gwam yum mwem beri, cin yu Yecu nin mwembo ken. La ki kwama ci kwob dilo tiyeri dii kwama wumom,
LUK 3:22 Dila yuwa tangbe kwamako yirau cinen na nagumfe, la diro ceru dii kwama “Mwi bwe nere mii, mi nuwa luma mwek ti?
LUK 3:23 Ki kwamawo Yecu ter nangen cere, can lam coro kwini ta'ar. Cir bi bwe (nawoci kwabi bereu) Yucufu, bi bwe Heli,
LUK 3:24 bi bwe matat, bi bwe Lewi, bi bwe Malaki bi bwe Yanna bi bwe Yucufu.
LUK 3:25 Yucufu bi bwe Mattatiya, bibwe Amoc, bi bwe Nahum, bi bwe Idacli, bibwe Najjaya,
LUK 3:26 bibwe Ma'ata, bibwe Mattatiya, bibwe Climeya bibwe Yoceku, yo ceku bibwe Yoda
LUK 3:27 Yoda bibwe Yowana, bibwe Reca bibwe Zerubbila bibwe Ciyeltiyele, bibwe Niri
LUK 3:28 bibwe Malki, bibwe Addi, bibwe Kocama, bibwe Almadama, bibwe Er,
LUK 3:29 bibwe Yoci, bibwe Aliyeza bibwe Yorima, bibwe Matat, bibwe Lawi,
LUK 3:30 bibwe Caminu, bibwe Yahuda, bibwe Yucufu, bibwe Yohanna, bibwe Aliyakima,
LUK 3:31 bibwe Malaya, bibwe Mainana, bibwe Matata, bibwe Natan, bibwe Dauda,
LUK 3:32 bibwe Yesse, bibwe Obida, bibwe Calmon, bibwe Nacon.
LUK 3:33 bibwe Amminadab, bibwe Adimi, bibwe Arama, bibwe Hezruna, bibwe Feresa, bibwe Yahuda,
LUK 3:34 bibwe Yakubu, bibwe Icaku, bibwe Ibrahim, bibwe Tera, bibwe Nahor,
LUK 3:35 bibwe Cerug, bibwe Reyu, bibwe Feleg, bibwe Abiru, bibwe Cela.
LUK 3:36 bibwe Kainana, bibwe Arfakcada, bibwe Cem, bibwe Nuhu, bibwe Lamek,
LUK 3:37 bibwe Methucela, bibwe Anuhu, bibwe Yaret, bibwe Mahalel, bibwe Kainana,
LUK 3:38 bibwe Enoc, bibwe Citu, bibwe Adamu, bibwe Kwama.
LUK 4:1 La Yeecu dim ki Yuwa tangbe kwama, yilam firen caji Urdun la yuwa tangbe kwama ko tu co yakanciko yerak.
LUK 4:2 Fiye kume kwini na'ar bwekelkele cuwaco tiyeu. co ca diker ki kumeni co, la ni connuwa wura.
LUK 4:3 Bwekelkel yii, na mo bibwe kwamri yii tero wo a yilam cari,
LUK 4:4 Yeecu yii co, mulangum mulange “ke bo ka cari ni ama dumetiye”.
LUK 4:5 La bwekelkele kung ken Yeecu dii nung cinen liyaro kaleweu gwam.
LUK 4:6 Bwekelkele yii co, “man neken nen Bikwankero gwam kange duktanka ceko, wori cin neyen dike buri gwam, la man weken nii wo ma cuitiyeu.
LUK 4:7 Na ceu na mwan cung cunge mo wab yeri gwam ka mwe”.
LUK 4:8 La Yeecu karci nen yiico, mulangum mulange mwa wab “Teluwe kwama mwe, co ki kwace mwa- Bwangtentiye”.
LUK 4:9 So bwekelkele yakan ki Yeecu Urucalima, kung ken co diiku'u wabe la yii co na mo bi bwe kwama di yarubitine
LUK 4:10 wori mulangum mulange, can ne be bei tomange wucakke cenin dor mwer bou na cer nen.
LUK 4:11 La ci an kungum nen dii na mo fwere biwure, tero nin.
LUK 4:12 La Yeecu yii co, “tokum toke, mani mwa cuwa Teluwe mwe kwama ti”.
LUK 4:13 La kambo bwekelkele dim cuwa Yeecu keri, concu dubomco biduwar bwiri.
LUK 4:14 La Yeecu yilaken Galili ki kwan yuwa tangber kwamari. La fulen dor ce reu curongi cinanloro kentangum wiye.
LUK 4:15 La can yoten merengkako bi kur waber, La gwam caklang co ti.
LUK 4:16 La con bou Nazaret fiye ci yom co wiyeu la kambo ci lerum maka, con doken mor bi kur waber kakuk folokak, la kwen con titiye na kiye kiye ka ki dir.
LUK 4:17 Cinne co bifumer Nii Dukume kaya, la con fiye wo mulangi,
LUK 4:18 Yuna tangber kwamaka wi dor miri wou cin cor meu timuwang dor na ne fulen kerero ken fiye nob bwen wiyeu. con tuom ye nan kwa dir fiye nubo ci tabangtabangeu, kange nee ka tokak fukmatinimbonin na kwin nubo ci neten dotange tiyeu.
LUK 4:19 Nan kwa dir cor cini kwamar
LUK 4:20 La con cumom bifumer ne riwo timwiyeu. La con yii ken, nuwe nubo gwam bi kur wabero rime ki tokanco.
LUK 4:21 La con yoten kan co yii ci keroti duwen bifumer wo dim fo ki nuwaka kumek.
LUK 4:22 Nubo gwamwi tok kero ken dor cer la citi Nyumangi kange luma kereko ceru ti Nyiceu. La cin me”wo kebo bi bwe Yucufu ka?”
LUK 4:23 La con yii ci, “Bicom kam yii dangke wo kom ki Nii Twaka Twam dor mwero. Dikewo ma duwa ma ma kafarnam meu, ma dong=dong nyo cinan lormwer.
LUK 4:24 La con toki Bicom ma yii komti, nii Dukume kange win wo fiyom bo yoka we cinan lor cer.
LUK 4:25 La mor bilenker ma yii komti, natub kwalebo kila kabo mer Icraila, tiberoco Iliya wiyeu, la biloro mungum na coro ta'areceu kange cuiyakko mukkun, la wura dor bou bitine corin.
LUK 4:26 La ci tun bo Iliya win ciye nin. La tunco Jerefat cidone, nawiye kwale kange yimwiyeu.
LUK 4:27 Walebo kala kabo mor Icraila kwama Ilica nii dukumeu, win wo ci twabo, kan Na'aman wo ciria.
LUK 4:28 Nubo gwam mor bikur wabereu funero tamci kambo cinuwa kero weri.
LUK 4:29 Cin kweri cin cokken co buiko cinan lore ci ya ken kico kong cueli wo ci mum cinan lor ciro dor cereu na ci tungu co bitine.
LUK 4:30 La ca ci cum tiber ciyer co yaken kange fiye.
LUK 4:31 La con yiraken kafarram cinan loro kange mor Galili, la con yoten kange co merang cinenti ki kakuk fobkak.
LUK 4:32 Cin ma nyumanka ki merankaceko, wori co ki tok kero ki Bikwanked.
LUK 4:33 La mor bi ker waber nii kange wi wo ki yuwa kelkelike, la con cii ki dira dur.
LUK 4:34 E' ye nya mam ti ki mo Yeecu Banajara, mo bou na mo twalangum ne? min nyumom mo co nii wucak kwama ce.
LUK 4:35 Yeecu ca kelkeliyomin tor, yii, tok re ker, ceru mor nii wo. kambo kelkeliyo jwa nii wo mer ken bitine tiber ciyer la ce rum mor nii wo, nuwa cinen bo tura ki kange nure.
LUK 4:36 Nubo gwam ti nyumangi, citi tokkami buiti ciye lan ker ye na wo? Co yii kelkeliyo kero ki nyial kange bi kwankered lan cerum.
LUK 4:37 La nyou, cin ter tokka fulen cero cinan loro kantangum wiye gwam.
LUK 4:38 La Yeecu dubom bikur waber ro doken lo cimonne, la fer cimon kalati ki kwirom bwi, la ci ken keri dor cer.
LUK 4:39 La kwen con titye dor cer, co ca kwirum bwi min tor, kwirum buiyo dubomco, dandang con kwemim con ta maka yiroko.
LUK 4:40 Kambo kakuko yar ken tiye ni, rubo bou cinenti kirubo nuwa bo luman tuirako ki dimen ki dimen, con yo ti kang ceko dor ciyer gwam con twam ci.
LUK 4:41 Kelkelibo cerangu mor nubo kila kila ken. Cii wiyeti ci ti toki, “mo bi bwe kwama,” Yeecu ca kelkelibo ca dob ci bo tok ker, wori cin nyumem con co Kritti.
LUK 4:42 Kambo fini celumen con cokum dor ce ki kwace fiye nob mani yeu, nubo ducce docoti co lo ci bou fiye co wiye, cin mani na ci kicim na dob cire.
LUK 4:43 La con yii ci man nee fulen kerer liyar kwamaro tangrim cinan Lorenbo. Won co dike bwi ci tumum ye fe.
LUK 4:44 La con ter neka fuleneko mor bi kur wabero Yuhudiya gwam.
LUK 5:1 La yilam kambo nubo mwerum fiye Yeecu wiyeri ci nuwa ker kwamaro, la co tim kang catiyo Janisarat deu.
LUK 5:2 Con to na bire mwenge yo tirangum wi kong caji nin, nubo ta'a jinge cerangum morece nir biliyar ciyer ti.
LUK 5:3 Yeecu kwiken mor Nabire mwengek ro win wuro ki cimonreu, la con yii co a kutaka ten ki nabira mwenge bi dob mor mwenge. La con yii ken mor nabire mwengek ronin, la co merang nubo ninti.
LUK 5:4 Kambo co dim kere di, con yi cimon, kob babire mwenge yaken ciko fiye cuwa cuwau, na mer ken biliyar mwero na taka jinge koce.
LUK 5:5 Cimon yii co “Teluwe, nyo ma nangen kume del nyo taba kange diker wi. La ki ker mwero mamer ken biyaro mor.
LUK 5:6 Kambo ci maweri, ci ta jinge ducce la biliyar ciyero ti biyetangi.
LUK 5:7 Coci ken farub nangeneb ci bo buro nabire mwenge wineu bo na tikanci, cin bou cin dirongum nalire mwengeu ciro yabcite, la cin teri kulkako.
LUK 5:8 La Bitru kambo to Yeecu ri, yarken bitine duwen yeelur la coki, kubom minen, wori min nii Bwiran ke “Teluwe”,
LUK 5:9 wori con nyumami, kange nubo buro kange ceu, ki kilaka jinge ko ci tabe.
LUK 5:10 Wuro mwerum kange Yakubu kange Yuwana bi beyo lo Jabadi farub nangeneb cimaneh. Yeecu yii ciman cuware tai, wori nawo kange kab mwa ta nob.
LUK 5:11 Kambo ci cokum nabire mor mwengecin yoken konge, cin dubom dikero gwam cin buangcinenten.
LUK 5:12 Kambo co ki no win mor cinan lonironineu, kange nii wi dim ki tuirak walek, kambo co to Yeecu ri con yar ken ki tikob ceb la conken co, tokti, “Teluwe” Namo ti ci ri mwantuamye cerum”.
LUK 5:13 La Yeecu ta'ar, kang ce ko keco toki mati cui, yilam wucak, dangjang waleu dubom co.
LUK 5:14 La con yi nii co a yi kange nii, la yii co, ya mure mwe, na nung dor mwero nii waber nin na ne tii kako ficang ngeu. Wo nir mwe ko ceu kambo muca tokeu, na warkero ce cinen.
LUK 5:15 La kero dor cereu yaken ten kutan, la nuba kila kilau bou wari cinen na ci nuwa co ti merangi na twam ten ci twirani ciyeu.
LUK 5:16 La mani co cerum ki kwace co yaken ki kob diloti
LUK 5:17 Yilam win mor kumeniwo co merangkatiyeu faricawa, kange nob merangka wer funer ci yiirongum wi buri ci bourangu muan loro Galili kange Yahudiya kange Urchalima gwam. Bekwan Teluwero wi kange co na co twam.
LUK 5:18 La nubo kange tu kilen do kange dor bilirir, la ci to nure wo ci a dokenti co moreu, na cin yoken co bitine kabum Yeecu.
LUK 5:19 La ci fiyabo nure ci a dor ti ke ceu wori nubo dim kabo, la cin kwiken dor lor la ci cuku co kibi cirico yirau ciko tiber nuber, dong-dong kaa Yeecu.
LUK 5:20 La co to bilenker ciyereri, Yeecu toki nii luwe, cutan mwen bwiran ker mwero wi.
LUK 5:21 Nob mulankabo kange faricawa ter meranka keko wo, we wo tok ker Dila karo wo tiye? we a cutan bwiran keti wi kebo kwama win di?
LUK 5:22 La Yeecu nyam dike ci kwatiyeu, kari yii ci, yebwi ka me wo ti neer kumere?
LUK 5:23 Co wini bwai be na toke, bwiran ke mweu cutang mwenwi, kwen titi ye yayambo.
LUK 5:24 La na kom nyumom bi bwe “Nifire” we ki be kwan kere ro for dor bitininer na cutang biriran ker wi, con yii kilendo, man yii nen kwen, tu bicirimeu, na yaken lomo.
LUK 5:25 Dangjang ko co, co kweri ka bum ciyem la tubiciri ceu wo co dam dor cereu. La cu loco, duktankwama ti.
LUK 5:26 Nubo gwam wi ti Nyumangi, la ci duktang, kwama cin dim ki tai citi toki, loon to diker nyumankar.
LUK 5:27 Kambo dike buro ma nyeri, Yeecu cerum kateb con to ni yo der tiyeu dencero Levi yii ku'u yoka duwek, Lacon yii co bwang menten.
LUK 5:28 Co Levi kwenti bwang cinen ten dubom tangnimdikerenbo gwam
LUK 5:29 La Levi co cika dur loco, la nob yo ka doreko wi kange tangnim nubembo, kentangum fiye caka carikeu ca carito ti kange ci.
LUK 5:30 La fariciwa kange nob mulangekab ciyebo wi fuen bibei tomange ceminti toki, ye bwi ko co ko no kange nob yoka duwek kange nob bwirang kere?
LUK 5:31 Yeecu karci nen, Nubo buro kwamereu mani a do nii Twa ka ti kan co buro nuwa lumau?
LUK 5:32 Ma buobo na nubo dong dongeu, lan nob bwiran kerek na ci yiloten.
LUK 5:33 Cin yii co, bibei tomange Yuwana ki, yim, yim Ngak nyo, ki kuom dilo nyo la bi bei tomange faricawa ki manyo ken. La mweu bi bei tomange meu ti cai ti noi.
LUK 5:34 Yeecu yiici, Nii kange wi wo adok farub bwa yilo na nawite na yii Ngakke, la bwayile na nawiyeu wi kange ci?
LUK 5:35 La kumeni wi bouti wo ci a tum bwayile ti cineneu, la ki kumeni co ci an yii Ngak.
LUK 5:36 La Yeecu yiten ci ker Nyuman kar, nii mani a wor fiti kulenti kulen do fuir na curum carko ciko na co ma nyori, can wobrangum kulendo fuir ko, fiti kulene fuir ko mani a datenti carko nin.
LUK 5:37 La ni kange mani wo a cor ten mwem inabim bo fuir ti mor kole care, naco mani nyo nyori, mwem inabim bo fuir ko an corum koltiye an wuroragum.
LUK 5:38 La tam a cor inabi fuir mor koltinon fuir.
LUK 5:39 Nii kange mani wo nuwa kum mwem inabim bofuir tiye, na kweri con nom car kori. La can toki carko la fuir ko
LUK 6:1 la ma nyo kakuk fobka ko kange, Yeecu yakenti mor to cang ko kange, kange bibei tomange ceu, ci kyang dor canger ti citi kui
LUK 6:2 la kangem mor faricawa tokiki, ye bwi ka ma dike yorbo ti a mani bi diye kukuk, ka kiye for ka?
LUK 6:3 Yeecu kar cinen, toti, ka kiye ba dike Dauda mani kwama co co nuwa wuri ti co kange nubo wari kange ceu?
LUK 6:4 ya mor luwe kwama, con tu cari to tanji laneu ca morece, con nabarubo wari kange ceu ciu cam, bwen no na mam kin nob wabereu ki kwaci cia ca
LUK 6:5 la con yii ci, bibwe nifire co teluwe kankuk fobka ko
LUK 6:6 kange bi diye kakuk fobka con doken mor bi kur waber la co meranmbo minti wi, nii kange wi wi wuro kance ko catiyero bwiyam-bwiya
LUK 6:7 nob mulangkabo kange faricawa to co tibi dor kero can twa nii ni kakuk fobkari na cin fiyan mure wo ci a tamco tiyeu,
LUK 6:8 la con nyumom dike ci kwa tiyeu la con yii nii wo kangko bwiyame kwen ti fo tiber nubero gwam la nii wo kweni titi wi.
LUK 6:9 Yeecu me ci yori kebo bi diye kakuk fobka a dike yor yoreu, kaka a ma dike wo yorbeu a cok dume kaka a tual dume?
LUK 6:10 la con cto ci gwam la co yii nii wo yarken kangmweko, la con manyo, la kang cebo twam
LUK 6:11 la neer ciyero kayaragum, lacin tok kanti bwiti ciye dike ca ma Yeecu nin tiyeu
LUK 6:12 lan yilam mor kumeni wo con ceri con yaken bang ca kob dilo con ta kobka dilo kume del co ken kwama ti
LUK 6:13 ki kakuk la con co bibei tomange ceu cinen la con cokum kwob cilom bo yobeu, wo co co cibitikali,
LUK 6:14 denti bi beitomange ceu co buro cimon [wo co caten tak, Bitru ] kange yii Andrawu, Yakubu, Yuwawana, Filibu, Bartalomi,
LUK 6:15 Matta, Toma, Yakubu bibwe Afa, cimon wo ca co Jaloti
LUK 6:16 Yafuja, bi bwe Yakubu, kange Yafuja ckaryoti wo miye co tiyeu,
LUK 6:17 la Yeecu yirau dor banged kange ci laci tim fiye tuared deu, kange bi bwi tomange ce wila kange nubo kila wo borongu Yafudiya kange wurcalima kange nubo kong caji taya
LUK 6:18 ci bou na ci buro wo nuwa co na co twam twirani ciyeu, nubo buro nuwa dotange ti ki yuwa kelkelikeu con twam ci ken.
LUK 6:19 nubo mwerkangum we gwameu dotina ci kem co wori bikwan twa ka ro ceru ti cinen, la con twan ci gwam.
LUK 6:20 la con to bi bei tomangeceu. con yii ci bibuyer kume kom wo nob bune beu la na kume liyar kwamaro
LUK 6:21 bi buyero an kume, kom wo konuwa wurati naweu, la ci an bwa kumen fuer bibuyer na kume, kom wo ko ci wiye tina weu, la kan nung nungi
LUK 6:22 bibuyero na kume to kom la ci ko denkumero na dikero bwir, ki ker bi bwe nir
LUK 6:23 ko bilangi diye co ko yilam ki for neerer, wori kan fiya cuner dikwama nubo carem cim ma nob du kumebo nin nawo
LUK 6:24 la kwan nen mo nii mwa cuwe-cuweu, la mom yom mwe dangne mweu
LUK 6:25 kwan kom nubo wo fuero bwam bwabeu, kan ci wura for kob kwan kom wo ko nung nungi ti na weu, yii kan buwa kan ci wiye ki bui.
LUK 6:26 kwan kom na nubo tok ti ki wo dong dong di, nubo carem cimbo tok nyo nob dukumeb cwerkebo
LUK 6:27 la ma yii komti nubo ko nuwa ye tiyeu, cui nii bi dom kange mweu, na ma nubo konene nin dike ro ken
LUK 6:28 yo nubo cilnen tiye nin bibuyer, na kob nubo buro culong nen ti dor bilenkereu
LUK 6:29 wo na kwanen ki kang tangal do wineri, neco wineu na kange tum belle mweri tamde mwe
LUK 6:30 ne nuwa wuro meneneu gwam na kange tum dike kangen na mweri me core moki a bou mwen ciko
LUK 6:31 kambo mo cuilti nubo a ma mweneri, mo keneu ma ci nen nyo
LUK 6:32 na moki cuim ka co ka co nubo cuinen tiyeri, in jye yokka fiye mo wiye? bwen na nob bwirang kerer di cui nubo cui ci tiyeu.
LUK 6:33 na moki mam dikero ken kan co nubo ma mwen dikero ken tiyeri ye yokka fiye weye? bwen no nob bwirang keri ki mam nyo ken
LUK 6:34 na wo ki ne cen kan nubo mo totiri an yam neneri, ye yokka munen? bwen no nob buiran kerer di ki nem nob bwiram kerero nyou na ci fiya dike ci ne dng-dong
LUK 6:35 la cui koneneu, na ma cinen dike dong-dong ngeu. ne ken kware kange diker yilau ti, la cuner, kumero na dur, kan yilam bi beyo lo nii dii ko na co con ni lomjome fiye nubo man ki buka kangek kange nubo bwirko
LUK 6:36 yilam ki cini na wo tee kume nii ciniu
LUK 6:37 kom mare buolang la mani a ma kumen buolang ti kom kuwa re mani a kuwa komti, tab kangem bo la mweu an tab mwen
LUK 6:38 kom ne la an ne kom kwele dimdiye, cuwam cuwa, ki bi funger ti con ci an cor kumer ti kan bellik ki kwele ka cuwameu a cuwa kumen ciko
LUK 6:39 la yila con yii ten ci dangke kange, con toki, fukma an ta fukma nin kangka? na co ma nyon, yaramken buwar gwam citi cimanin nyoka?
LUK 6:40 bwe tomange labo nii merang ka ceu dur la nubo gwam an yilam na nii merang kako na merang cinendi
LUK 6:41 ye bwi mo toti ka be yere nuwa kemwe, lamwa tobo cuwemero wo nuwe mweu
LUK 6:42 mwa yii yimwe myi, moki yii mi tumwen be yere dam mor nuweu, lamoki bwi mwa tobo kukko cuwe mero dam mor nuwe mweu? kom nubo bwir, teri cokum batiye durko nuwe mweu na mo tom yora na mo cokum be yere nuwe yiim weu
LUK 6:43 la tiyo kendo kange mani wo tu bi tutiyo fuyem fuye tiye, kaka tiyo wo fuyemeu na ne betuti ken
LUK 6:44 wori tiyo moki nyomco kin bitutico tutiyeu la nubo mani we bituti nying cire ti cuiya ke kaka nubo inabi fiye cilange
LUK 6:45 nii ken mor dikero kendo dume ceu a bou dikero yor yoreu, nyou nii bwirko mor dikero bwirko mor neere ceu, a bou dikero bwir wori dikero bwirko ducce mor neere ceu co ci ceu toktiye
LUK 6:46 ye bwikaco yeti kom ki, teluwe laka bwantenbo dike ma tok tiyeu?
LUK 6:47 nii wo na bou minen la nuwa ker mereu laco bwang tenen, man yii dii ke co cerkange
LUK 6:48 co ki no nan nii luwe tiye, woru wobken cuwa mor bitinen la co mu kwar loro ki terenti kwamer lana mwembo dur bouri la came mwegweu kwanan kwar kumeroti laluwe cuwo mani a muka ti wori mum co yora
LUK 6:49 la nii nuwa ker miro bwang ten beu no nan co nii wo mu luwe dor bitinereu man ki kwar ca na came mwem bo kwanan kwar kuro di la can can duwo an yarum, yarke luwe kowo
LUK 7:1 bwiko Yeecu dim dikero gwam ca yi nobo tiye cin do ken kafarnaum
LUK 7:2 fiya cuwo nii kwene durko nuwa diker dor Yeecu ri, contwom nobo dur yahudawa ro, a ken co na bou na twam canga ceu
LUK 7:3 la cin bou Yeecu nin cin ken co yi co ti ki “nii wo lam wo ma macinen wo tiye
LUK 7:4 wori ci cwi bitene nye ti co ca munyinen bi kur kwamaro urcalimau
LUK 7:5 nyori Yeecu bwan cinen ten. la fiya cuwo ci dadom kange kuweri, nii kwene durko twom farub cebo a yi co, teluwe kwom de dor mwero, wori ma labo wo mwabouti lomiyeu
LUK 7:6 nyori ma tubo dor miro na nii wo lami mwa bouti cinen, tok ka ker koni, canga mi an kwam.
LUK 7:7 mo keneu, mi nii woki bi kwang kere dor nob kwenebo kang mikeu, nyi wo mi yari, co ya kange mi bouri, co bou, canga miu no ca ma wori can mani
LUK 7:8 la Yeecu nuwa wori, co nyiman nii wo, con yila nobo bwan cinententiye, con yii ci, “miyi komti, mor kiraila gwam, ma fiyobo nii ki bilen ke na weu.
LUK 7:9 fiya cuwo nobo ca twome a yilaure loweri, ci fiya canga wo twam
LUK 7:10 kutanbo bwiko cuwori
LUK 7:11 Yeecu yaken cinar loro kange ci cuwoti ki Naim, nob tomange cebo fiya nob ducce woya kange ceu
LUK 7:12 la ci bi dom kangenyilo cinar loreu di, cin ki nii kange wo bwiyam meu, cobwe wiin nece nin [wuro] nawiye kwale nubo ducce cinar loron wo kange co.
LUK 7:13 Yeecu to cori, cin bunang co cin yii co, “ciire wiye”
LUK 7:14 la conyaa con tei kwanni wo ci tuu bilen do cika nobo tum ki bilen nen tim cok con yico, bwe, mi kwenu”
LUK 7:15 bilen do kwenum, nyoten tok ka kereko, Yeecu neken co nece nin
LUK 7:16 la tai to tam ci gwam, cin yoten ci caklang kwama ti,” nii tomange kwama dur kwennu more nye kwama to nobo loceu
LUK 7:17 fulen kere wo dor Yeecu yalti bi ten yahudiya gwam kange buro bi dom kange ceu
LUK 7:18 bibei tomange yuwana yi co dike buro gwam
LUK 7:19 la yuwana cuwo bi bei tomange ce yob, tom ciYeecu nin ciya me co” mo nii bou tiye kakaa nyo nintang kane?
LUK 7:20 cin bo bidom Yeecu nin di cin toki, “yuwana nii yuu mwem tiye tom nyo munen ki nyi me, “mo wo bou tiye kakaa nyi nintang kange?”
LUK 7:21 tabbo cin twabangum nubo ki twira kange wo ki yuwa kelkeleb beu, nobon fukmau, cin neci toka fiye.”
LUK 7:22 la Yeecu ciya cinen ki, kom ya ko yi yuwana, dike nuwa kime towe kange dike ka nuwa fukma tofiyeti kilendo ya yamti, walebbo cin twam, nubo mani nuwa tiye ti nuwai, nobo bwiyame kwennum, fuwabbo nuwa fulen keret
LUK 7:23 nii wo ne bilen keret dikero mi matiyeri nii bibwiyer,
LUK 7:24 bwiko bi bei tomange yuwana cuwe, Yeecu yici kerdor yuwana,”ye ka crr yera ka totiye? yerayuwana moktiye ka
LUK 7:25 ye ka cer yera ka owe? nii ki kulendo twaba nyeu to, nubo ki kulenkyemereu, ci nuwa lima ti loni liyabe
LUK 7:26 ye ka ya yera ka towe? nii tomange kwama ong mi yi komti la nii tomange
LUK 7:27 wuro co nii ci mulangi cer ki “to mi tom mweu ni tomange ti kaa mo wo a ywelmwen nuretiye
LUK 7:28 mi yi komti mor nubo natub bowe, mani na yuwana, nyori nii wo na bi duware mor liyar kwama reu laco
LUK 7:29 la nubo gwam, ki nob yuwana kyemerek nuwa nyori, cin ciya kwama nii wucake, wori cin yuu cinenen mwembo ki yuu mwemer yuwana
LUK 7:30 la fariciyawa kange nubo nyimom werfundeu cin dike kwama yo keb dor circu, nyori ci yuu cinen bo mwem yuwanam bo tiye? cinan ye?
LUK 7:31 “kange ye ma mwer nubo kaldo wo canne tiye? cinanye?
LUK 7:32 cina bi bei malorti fiye miyeka dikereu, wo yim yiye la cuwo kange yi co ki,”min cuu lira mwa yelbo yila, min ka nuwe bware, mwa cibo wiye
LUK 7:33 nyo yuwana nii yuu mwem tiye bou mani cati, mani noti, ki wi ki ninga “
LUK 7:34 bi bwe nifire bou, ti cai ti noi ri, kom ki kucunu kange nii no nyom tiye, farnob yuwana kyeme kange nii ki bwiran kere,
LUK 7:35 nyore yuleng bi beyo loce ki warke
LUK 7:36 na wori, wiin mor fariciyawa cuwo Yeecu na ci ca cari wari la bwiko Yeecu doken lon fariciyawari, cin yiken fiye caka carik, na cincam cartori,
LUK 7:37 nawiye kange wii cinar lor wo nii bwiran ke kambo cin nyimom Yeecu doken loh bwe fariciyawa ca kacarik di, cin bou ki nuwan alabata, kundo limi yeu
LUK 7:38 contibidom kange Yeecu fiye na ceko wiye co ci wiyeti, con yoten yibong na Yeecu ko ti ki mwem num cem, belti nuwang na cek
LUK 7:39 la fariciyawa wo cuwo Yeecu, to nyori, co ti kwabi ner cer ki, na nii wo bwe tomange ri no cikin nyimom we nawiye tiye nii bwiran ke'
LUK 7:40 Yeecu yi co cmon min wi dike ma yi nen tiye, ciki toki nii meranka
LUK 7:41 Yeecu ki nii neka cennek ne nubo yob cend, wiindinari kwini kwob nung, wiineu nung
LUK 7:42 la cin fwe ki yakako, cin dobcinen gwam nyori we more ciye co cwiti wo ducce?
LUK 7:43 ciman ciya ki, “mi kwatiri nii wo co dob cin kyemero ducceu. Yeecu yico co ki munwarker dong-dong
LUK 7:44 Yeecu yila nawiye wonin yi ciman, mun to nuwiye wamin do lomo, mwe ne yebo mwem nirka nam, na wiye wo yibong namiko mwem num ceu, con ki yiri co
LUK 7:45 mwa ma membo ka cikko ma dou feu na wiye wo dobbo beitika na miko
LUK 7:46 mwa beltimen bo nuwandor, nawiye belti menti nuwan dor
LUK 7:47 nyori mi yinenti bwiran kece ducceu cutan wi, wori con nan cwikaducce nii wo cicutan bwiran kece bi duware ri, cwika ceko bi duwar
LUK 7:48 la con,” yi co, bwiran kemwe cin cutang wi
LUK 7:49 nubo ci yim wariyeu yotan tokkan kerek butici, we woro cutan bwiran ke tiye
LUK 7:50 Yeecu yi nawiye wo, bilenke mwe coknen, ya ki nero fwor
LUK 8:1 la yilam nyo kambo Yeecu ter yam cembo cinar lor kange mwanti lore ki kang ki wang, tok fulen kereroti kange fulen liyar kwama kwob culombo yobeu wi kange co,
LUK 8:2 kange natubo kange wo ca twam ci yuwako kwir kange twira kila-kila. maryamu wo ci cuwo ti ki makdaliya, wo ci cokten ninga nibereu,
LUK 8:3 kange yuwana wii kuza, nawiye tomange hiridu, cuzanatu, kange kangumbo kila nyeu, kin dike kang cike ci ma mangen ti cikr
LUK 8:4 la nubo ducce mwekangu ti, kange kangum nob bouti cinar lor-cinar lor reu, cin yii ci dangke,
LUK 8:5 nii fike kange ciri a fii dum la coti fii ri kangum bo yarken kong nure, cin fawarangum ki na, bilibeu diyeu yirau bon com.
LUK 8:6 kangumbo yar dor terenti, la kii ri kucom, dula mani
LUK 8:7 kangumbo yarken mor cwiyaka la cwiyak kii kange dumbo ri, cwiyakko cakkangum co
LUK 8:8 la kangumbo yar bitine kenneu ma ken, wo lam kiriti kwini kwobbe. bwiko Yeecu dim tokka kere keu, cuwo ci, “ki tu nuwaka kere, ca nuwa
LUK 8:9 bi bei tomange ce meco dang kewo nuntiye con yici, la kangum bo ciye me yici ki dangka, nyori ci ti toi maci toti citi nuwai ma ci nyomti
LUK 8:10 con yici, nyomka yurke liyar kwamar cin nekom, la kangum bo ciye ma yi ci ki dangka, nyomti
LUK 8:11 dike dangka nuntiyeu co wo, dumbo ker kwamar
LUK 8:12 buro yar nureu, wori nuwa ri bwekelkele bou yuwom kero ner cireu, nyo na ci nere bilenke naci fiya fuloka
LUK 8:13 buro yar do terentiyeu, co buro no ci nuwa kero dici yuwo ki nero for, la ci man ki niti, cin ne bilenke, kutan bori, cuwakako bou ri ci yarum.
LUK 8:14 dumbo wo yar mor cwiyakeu, ci nobo wo nuwa ri, la ci yakenti ri, cwika kalek, kyemer kange nuwaka lima ca kkangum ci la ci mabo ken
LUK 8:15 woro dor bitinero keneu, ci buro ki bilnka kange nero kenne, tam yoran, ma dikero ken mor birum nere.
LUK 8:16 nii mani a kwer kirati na cumom, kakaa yoken bok kwannik, ca yo codor diker, na nobo doutiye to kirako
LUK 8:17 mani dikero yurangum yurange mani a nyomtiye, kakaa yurke kange wii wo ba nyombe a bou ti kira
LUK 8:18 nyori nuwa, yora, nii wo ki diker ducceu ri an yok cinen ten woro man cikeu, bi duwar ci cikeu an yuwom cinen.
LUK 8:19 la nece kange yitub ceb bou, cinen, la ma ciya fiya nure lakati cinen, wori nubo ducce
LUK 8:20 cin yi co, nemwe kange yitub mwem tim kale, cwiti na ci tonen”
LUK 8:21 Yeecu ciya ci yi ci, nemi kange yitub mib co nobo wuro nuwa ker kwama di ma namgen cike.
LUK 8:22 bi con doken mor nabire mweme kange be bei tomange ce, con ci,”bi yabken dinge wure no cin yoten yambo,
LUK 8:23 la ciyakentiri, co dam dum yuwa kibi kwama kwennuncayi, mwembo yoten dim na bire mwenge ciyeuti, ciki no nyi kware.
LUK 8:24 la bi bei tomange Yeecu bou cinen cin yunco, ciki “teluwe, nyo nyi bware con kweni, yuwako kange mwelanka mwemek ko, wori cin tim
LUK 8:25 la con yi ci ki fe ke kimeu? cin nuwa tai ci myimam dike woti ci me buti citi we nii wuro werang yuwati kange mwembo ki nyial neco dure?
LUK 8:26 la cin yaken Garacinawa wo kino dinge caji Galili
LUK 8:27 fiya cuwo Yeecu doken bitene, cowari, con wabkan nii kange cerum cinar loreu ki ninga kwutangi cinen la wormangum kulen cero. mani dã lo ki dã tiber tuwetini
LUK 8:28 la con Yeecu ri con kwa dir yarkan ka Yeecu, cin tok ker kwang ka, ki mo Yeecu bi bwe kwama nii duktonka, mi kennenti neyere dotange
LUK 8:29 wori Yeecu cokkan yuwakeliko ki nyial nii cuwo nin kiritti ducce ki ta core bwentano cin bwam cori cin yoti nii atocotiri, kiyangum diker bwakaro, ningau ywa co yaken ciko yera
LUK 8:30 la Yeecu me co, “we den mwero? ki dencero muri, wori kelkelibo ducce do bwiciye
LUK 8:31 ci ken Yeecu ti a ywa cire ki nyial mor buwoke
LUK 8:32 na wen, ngiyere ducce ca cariti fir banger ninga buro ken co ca dob ci ciya doken bwi ceru la cin ne ci nure
LUK 8:33 nyori ninga buro ceru bwi nii wuro doranken bwi ngiyere tini cin cwakkangi yaranken mor mweme cin bwiyarangum
LUK 8:34 la nubo to ngiyere buro tiye, dike wo mane ri, cin cwakkan ken mor cinar lor cin yi nubo dikewo bwiyeu
LUK 8:35 la nubo cecu naci to dikero maneu, cin bou Yeecu nin, cin fiya nii wo cokten ningau yim bi dom na Yeecu, dumki kulen, wo kwamer tak. lacin cwa tai
LUK 8:36 la nubo to dikero maneu, yi dike maneu, yuwa kelkelibo wo cerum bwi nii we
LUK 8:37 la nubo gwam biten Garacinawau yi Yeecu a dobom bitine ciyeu wori taito dur tamci nyori cin doken nabire mwenge naci yilaken bwi.
LUK 8:38 nii woci cokten ningau ken Yeecu na cin ya wari, la Yeecu yi co,
LUK 8:39 yilaken lo na yii nubo dike kwama ma cineneu nii woro kentangum cinar loro gwam, tok dike Yeecu ma cinenu
LUK 8:40 na weu Yeecu yilaken neu nubo duccu nawo yuwoce, no ci nintang coti
LUK 8:41 la nikange wi dendo ki Yariyu, ciki no mor nubo durer kwamaro Urcalima, bou bidom kange Yeecu cungen naa Yeecu, con ken co ca ya loco,
LUK 8:42 wori, bi bwece bwebubya, coro kwob culombo yob, kan co wiin cineneu ki no nyi kware laYeecu yaken tiri nubo ducce tunkanti bwiti ciye kentangum co
LUK 8:43 la nawiye kange wo cor gwam dike ci cikeu bwiyale ti coro kwob culomo yobe, twalum gwam dike ci cikeu, co fiyabo twaka nii kange nin
LUK 8:44 co bou bwi Yeecu con tei nyii belliceu, wii dancan kwiyele ceu tim.
LUK 8:45 la Yeecu yiki we kece? la nii wo ciya cinen wii more ciye gwam di, bituru yi co, nii merangka, nubo duccu kantangum mo, tunkanti bwimi
LUK 8:46 Yeecu yi co “kange nii ke ye, min yimom, bikwan ceri minen.
LUK 8:47 na wiye wo to nyo ma ca fiye cerka ti ri con bou fiye Yeecu wiye, cungi kaco, nuwe nube gwan, con tok ca fiya dikero gwam wo dok co ca ke ce, la nyoro, ca kfiya twaka
LUK 8:48 la con yi co, “bwe, bilenke mwam nen, yaa ki for nerek
LUK 8:49 con wi co tok ker ti duwal di kange bou bi kur kwama nubo dure, ki bi bwe mwe bwiyam, ki nere ni meranka dotange tak
LUK 8:50 Yeecu nuwa wori, con ciya yariyu nin nuwari tai neka bilenke, bi bwemwe atwam
LUK 8:51 la ca ya luwe cori ca dobbo nii a do mor kange co kange Bitru kange Yuwana kange Yakubu te kange ne bweu
LUK 8:52 nubo wiye ci ti wori bweu bwiyami la con yi ci kom cire wiye co bwiyabo, ki dadum
LUK 8:53 la cin mung co, wori cin nyimom bwiyam
LUK 8:54 co tu bwe kang cer, cin cuwo ki bi kwang bwenu yi ci ciya fiya cinen dike ca catiye
LUK 8:55 dume ce yilaken, dancan con kwenu con yi ci ciya fiya cinen dike ca catiye
LUK 8:56 teekange nece nyimangi, con yici ciya yi re nii dike wo maneu.
LUK 9:1 con cuwo bi bei tomange ce kwob culombo yob, neci bikwang kange bikwang keret naci cokum ningga gwam, ci twam tiratini
LUK 9:2 con twom ci kele na ci tok fulen keret liyar kwamaro, naci twam nubo nuwabo liman
LUK 9:3 con yi ci kom ture diker yam kimembo nin dang mani cwaye mani, cari mani, kyemer mani tak ko ture diker kwabkar yob
LUK 9:4 luwe wo ka dowe ri, ko yi wii yaken ciko diye ka dubom tiye
LUK 9:5 fiye ci yuwo kom be ri no ka dob ninar loro cuwo tiri ko bum kwero na kime keu warke dor cir
LUK 9:6 nyori cin kweni, ci bwanten cung-nukur, cunkur ci tok fulen kerero ti, twa nob ti fiye gwam
LUK 9:7 la Hiridus liyau nuwa dike ydken tiye ri, ma nyimantum, wori kangum bo tiki kin Yuwana kwenu bware
LUK 9:8 kangum bo ki Iliya cerkangu we, kangum tak ki wiin more nob tomangeb bo fiya cuwo kutaneu kwenuwe
LUK 9:9 Hiridu ki, min mwatum dor Yuwanaro, we wori mi nuwa dikero woti dor cere? nyori con do nure ca to co tiye
LUK 9:10 la be bei tomange Yeecu yilauri, cin co dikero gwam ci maneu la con cin yaken yurangum, yurange cinar loro ci cuwo tiki Batsaidau
LUK 9:11 la nubo mwerumem nuwa dike wuro nyori cin bwangten co con yuwo ci, con ci diker dor liyar kwamare, com twam buro cwi twaka tiyeu
LUK 9:12 lakume dadom a bouti cwile, kwob culombo yobe bou cinen, cin yico,”yi noboro ci yaken mwan loro buro mor tangini naci fiya fiye dame kange cari nyori fiye biwiye nob mani
LUK 9:13 la con yi ci, “ko neci dike ciya ca tiye. ciki, be dike nyo cikeu cwen carito nug kange jinge yob ma nya fiye carito wo a lam nubo wuro ti gwame
LUK 9:14 nubo lam bikate nung ka nabarub con yi bi bei tomange ceu ki yi nubo a yiken ki mwam, kimwam nubo kwini nung, kwini nung
LUK 9:15 nyori cin mani nyo, yo nubo yiken yiye
LUK 9:16 co n tu cwen tiyero nungeu nunge jinge yobe, cin kunken nuwe ce di kwama, yo cin nenti bi bwiyer wi con wulangum ka bi duwartini con ne bi bei tomange ceu naci tikange nubo mwerume nin
LUK 9:17 cin ca gwam ciye cin bwam, tanne ceu numeu, cin yee bulendo kwob culombo yob
LUK 9:18 la kakuko kange Yeecu kwob diloti ki kwace, bi bei tomange ce wi cinen con me ci ki nubo wuro mweru meu ki yii ki min wee?
LUK 9:19 cin ciya co yuwana nii yuu mwem tiye, kangumbo ki Iliya, la kanugumbo ki kange wiin mor nob tomangebo nanduwe
LUK 9:20 con me ci la kime kom ki yi ki min wee? Bitru ciya cinen kiritti bi bwe kwama
LUK 9:21 cin werang ci ciya tok re wo nikange nin
LUK 9:22 yi citi bi bwe nifire an nuwa dotange dike ducce, ko co, ci an twalum co, ki bi kume taare an kwenum
LUK 9:23 con yi ci gwam, nii wo cwiti na bwanten yereu, an ko dor cero, can tun bentilen bwantiyer ki cero, ki ca kicatecca bwan teng
LUK 9:24 ni wo cwiti na ci fiya dume ce ri an lem dume ce, wo lem dume ce ki 25ker mire ri an fiya dume ceu
LUK 9:25 yee nii a fiya tiye no ci fiyam kale wo gwam la co lem dume ceri
LUK 9:26 wo no nuwa kwenduwe mi kange ker mirro ri, bi bwe nifire an nuwa kwenduwe ce ken diye bi bwe nifire a bou ti mor dukfongka ce, duktongka tee, kange yuwa tangbe kwama wucake
LUK 9:27 mi yikom bilen ke ti, kangembo wii tirangum fo, wo mani a twi bwer tiye nimre ci to liyar kwamaro
LUK 9:28 ki kume narub Yeecu tok kero bure ri, cin tuu Bitru, kange Yuwana kange Yakubu, cin kukendor banger na ci kwobdilo
LUK 9:29 la ci mor kwobka dilo ri, tikob ce bo fulongum, kulen cere yilam fwoje ti milbangi
LUK 9:30 nyori, nubo kange yob tokkang ker ti kange co, muca kange Iliya,
LUK 9:31 wo cerkengu ki duktonka, tokkan ker kiboka cer ti wom dadom a bou ti cwile urcalima
LUK 9:32 Bitru kange buro kange ceu nuwe ciye tuu ki dum, la cin kweni ri, ci to duktonka kange nobo yob tim kange co
LUK 9:33 fiya cuwo ci dob Yeecu ci yakentiri, Bitru yi co teluwe yor nyinen nyi feu, bi ywel bikur taar, wiin ki mo wiin ki muca, wiin ki Iliya [co nyombo dike co tok tiye ]
LUK 9:34 la co tok kero ti nyori, bi loro yirau cumom ci, cin nuwa tai kambo bilora kantangum ciyeu.
LUK 9:35 diro kange ceru mor bilore nin ti toki ki, wo bi kwemi ma cikeu, ko nuwa co
LUK 9:36 fiya cuwo diro dim tokka kere keu, Yeecu tim ki kwace la cin kumom ci yi bo nii mor kumeni curo dike ci towe
LUK 9:37 cel fini ri cin yirau dor banger, nobo duccu bou cinen
LUK 9:38 wori nikange mor nibe nin cuwo co ki diri, nii merangka, mi cwiti na to be bweme kange co bweu mi cike
LUK 9:39 yuwa tangbe bwir doken bwici, co ki kwa kang kiyange, mok co ti kibi kwang, funi fwiuti nyii co, bwai na dob co, nuwaran cinen twira ti bwira-bwira
LUK 9:40 min ken be bei tomange na cokum, cin fwe ciko
LUK 9:41 kom kaldo woka tiyangum nure, kom man ki bilen kereu, fiyan ma yiti kange kome, mi mwirimum ner ti kange kome? bou kibi bwe mwe fo
LUK 9:42 la bwe bou boutiri ninga kwa co merken bitine, mor coti kibi kwang Yeecu werang yuwa tangbe ko wo, con twam bweu yila cin neken tece
LUK 9:43 nubo nyimang bi kwan kwamaro laci tokkanti butici dikero gwamco matiye, con yi bi bei tomange ceu,
LUK 9:44 kom dor kero wo a yiraken tuu komi ciyang miyem bi bwe nifire kang nubek
LUK 9:45 la ci nyombo dike co tokeu, yurangum, yurage cinen, laci nyombo dike nuntiye, ci cwa tai ti na ci me co kerowo
LUK 9:46 kwobokanka do tiber ciyer ki kerowo kin we a yila nii dur tiye.
LUK 9:47 Yeecu nyimom dike ci kwati ner cireu, tuub bwe bi duware bi dom kange co.
LUK 9:48 la con yi ci, niwo yuwo bwe bi duware ki den mire ri, yuwo mo, na wo yuwo yere yi, yuwo niwo tomu yereu nii wo bi duwar more kume gwamme co durko
LUK 9:49 Yuwana ciya co, teluwe, nyon to nikange cok ninga ti ki den mwer, co nya ywace wori bwang nyinen ten bo.
LUK 9:50 Yeecu yi ki, ko ywa core, wori nii wo ciya kombe na kume
LUK 9:51 la kumeni kum bi duwar wo ci yilaken diye, con yoken ner yamer urcalima
LUK 9:52 con twom bi bei tomange na yaken ten cinnen, cin ya cin doken mwan lor camariyar na ci ywel cinen fiye firen
LUK 9:53 nii bo wiye yuwo cobo wori ciki yang urcalima
LUK 9:54 la bi bei tomange ceu Yakub kange Yuwana to nyori yi ki, “teluwe muki cwi nyo dor kirako a yirau di kwama na twim ci ka?
LUK 9:55 con yila con werang ci,
LUK 9:56 la ci yaken mwam luwero kange
LUK 9:57 ci mor yamme dor nuret, kange. yii co, “mwan bwang mwen ten fiye mo yaken ti wii ye
LUK 9:58 Yeecu yi co, “bi cwe kiye wiki buokti, bi libe di kwama wii ki loci, la bi bwe nifire man ki fiye ca nyom dor tiye
LUK 9:59 la cin yui kange, “bwangmen ten, la con yi co ki, “teluwe dob ye yan fwerum temi buri”
LUK 9:60 cin yi co, dob bilendo cika fwerum bilen ciyer mweu ya kutan kange fiye kwiya kye na tok fulen liyar kwama.
LUK 9:61 dila kange yi ki man bwanten nen kwama dila dob ye yan nem nubo lomembo nanme”
LUK 9:62 Yeecu yi co, ni kange mani a yoton kanti cinonri la yi la yila nuwe bwiye daten bo lokwama.
LUK 10:1 Bwika dike wuro Yeecu cok kwini niber cilom yoh, co tom ci yob-yob na ci ya cunnukur kange bettinimbo wo co cwija. Ya ka ti wiyeu.
LUK 10:2 La yi ci bituwe wi dutce di la nob nangnembo biduwa, no nyori kom kwob dilo kom kinong nii take na tom cimen nob nangenembo mor take ce.
LUK 10:3 Kom ya to man tom kom na be kwame mor bitilo.
LUK 10:4 Be kom ture kiyemer, cwaye kange Taa. kom yarumde nii dor nuret.
LUK 10:5 Luwe kom do wiyeudi, kom ter tok kako kom ki, funeret a no fo luwe wuro.
LUK 10:6 Tano ni funeret wi luwe nen di, fu neret kumero an yiti luwe nen, no mani dii fowor neret kumero an yila fiya kom.
LUK 10:7 Kom yi i luwe co, kom ca kom no, dike ci ne kome. Ni nage do daten cor cero, kom dore luwe-luwe.
LUK 10:8 Bero ci yo komeri kom ca diker ci ti ki kabum kumene.
LUK 10:9 Kom twam nubo ki bwarakeu wii bitine cuwo, kom yici liyar kwamaro bo bi dom kange kom.
LUK 10:10 Bitine wo kom do no ci yokom di yaken dor nuret ciyer, kom yi nubo cuwo kom kii ka kwero bitine kume tam na nye ko.
LUK 10:11 Nyo ferkumen, co warke dor kumer. Be kom nyom liyar kwamaro bo bi dom kange kom.
LUK 10:12 Ma yi kom bi diye bolange caduma an la bero wo, fiyaka luma.
LUK 10:13 Kwannen karacinu, kwannen Baitcaida: nangedo tenangi wo ma mo re kume, na cin mani nyo Taya knge cidon di na cikin kiya ciko ki kinin, ci yim mor bituwamekange yilan kangbuwa.
LUK 10:14 Di la biye bolang taya kange cidon ci an La kom fiya ka luma.
LUK 10:15 Mo kenne kafanaum mo kwati moki yaken ciko dii kwama ciya duktang nen tiye? O-ong an cukken nen bwiyar.
LUK 10:16 Wuro cutu fiye kom wiyedi, cuwantu minen, wo ko kom medi, koye, wo ko yere, ko niwo tomwo yere”.
LUK 10:17 Ci kwini ibere yilau ki fwor neret, ci yiti ki Teluwe, bwekelkele ken nyo durti. mor denen mwe?
LUK 10:18 La Yeeecu yici man to bwekelkele yaruti dii kwama na miblanka.
LUK 10:19 To min ne kom bi kwan kom fuwa na cwiwetininm kange birngetinim kange bikwan nii kiyer gwam, take ci makom nin ki diger ko bi dob.
LUK 10:20 Bwen nyeu kom bilangde nyo kom ki yuwa ko bwirko nuwa komti, Di la kom bilangi la den kumer mulangum mor dii kwama.
LUK 10:21 Na wo ri Yeecu dim ki for neret mor yuwa tangbe ko wucakke, coki man ne nen dur Te Teluwe dii kwama kange bitine. wo mo cumom dige worombo nob Yilenebbo nin kange nyomka, mo na fwetang ci nen nubo worombonin merangbe. na bibei bi dwartinim. Ong, Tee nyo dong dong fiye mon wiyeu.
LUK 10:22 Dikero gwam ki no fiye Tee me wiyeu, ba nii win nyom bwe curoweu, La ka Tee win kange kangumbo wo bwe ciya ki nyomom ceu.
LUK 10:23 La cin yilam fiye bibei tomangeb cebo con cogi cunnka. Caklangka ki no nubo wo tom dikere cin toweu.
LUK 10:24 Min yii komti nub wabero kange liyab kila ciyan to diker muu toweu, la ma ci to cii ti, ciyan nuwa diker muu nuwau, la ma ciya nuwati
LUK 10:25 Kange nii merangka bolange Yahudawa na co cwa co, cike na co cuwa co, cike nii meranka, Yeecu ma matiye na fiyam dume diiye?
LUK 10:26 Yeecu yi co ki moki kiye nyi dike mulangi mor bolange? co ciya coki.
LUK 10:27 Bilang te mwe kwama ki ner mwero gwam, dume mwe gwam, bikwan mwer gam, kange dike mo kwabe gwam, na mo bilang nii bidomeu na dor mwero.”
LUK 10:28 Yeecu ciya co mo tok dong dong, ma wo nyo na fulo
LUK 10:29 Nii merang ka cwiti na co cukum dorcero, ki Yeecu we nii mi bidome?
LUK 10:30 Yeecu ki nii kange kwen yam Ursalima, yakenti Jeriko. Con yar ken kan nub kwiyeb, ci cukum co, ci yom dike co cike kwarub ci bukco dob co tamwi bwiyam.
LUK 10:31 Nii wabe kange dou wi nure co, to co di kwen tiyagum cungagin cuken.
LUK 10:32 Nyo tak ni tikali dur bikur wabe dou wi nure cwo, la to co kwen tiyagum cunaggin cuken.
LUK 10:33 Di la kange bwe Basamariya nure tou co wi.
LUK 10:34 Con bou fiyentange niwo wiye, bwacinen deti ya ci nuwa cinen neu, belti cinen nuwanko kange mwem bitutti (Inabi) kunn ken co yoken dor kelba cer yaki co fiye dami, na to co.
LUK 10:35 Ki elfini con boki dinari yob ne ni luwe, yi co ki to twa cinen dero, tano mo twalki cum dige ma ne neri, na yilauri man ya nen.
LUK 10:36 Mor nubo wuro we nii mo to ci nii bilang kange ce?
LUK 10:37 Ni merangka ki nii wo nuncinen bilangtum, Yecu yii o ki ya manyo ken.
LUK 10:38 Di ci yaekn ti Yecu doken mor conunkur kange nawiye kange dencerro Marta yo co lo co.
LUK 10:39 Con wiki korya ce den do Maryamu, wo yi na Teluwe nuwa ti ka dike co toktiyeu.
LUK 10:40 Marta ki ma yiri, la con bo Yecu nen ki Teluwe kwm nen bo, korya mi dob ye ma, m nage do tiki kwami? yi co ca tikang ye, Yecu ciya, la yi co Mart, mo kwon dor mwero dor diker dutce.
LUK 10:41 La Nii durko ciya co ki “Marta mon yumom diker kila.
LUK 10:42 Di la diker win tam yo maryamu tom ce diker yor yore, wo, nii mani a yo cimenti.
LUK 11:1 Bi dikange Yeecu kwob diloti fiye kange, kambo co dimeri, win mor nob bwanka ceko, Teluwe merang nyinen kwob ka dilo ko, na wo yuwana merang nob bwnag ka cebo nineu.
LUK 11:2 Con yi ci ki no ka kwob dilo tiri kom tok ki. Te den mwero na tii wucak, Liyar mwero bo.
LUK 11:3 Ne nyo dike nya ca tiyeu na kakuko ce.
LUK 11:4 Cutang nyinen bwirang keret nyero, na wo nyo cutang nobo wo ma nyinen bwirang keretiye, yare ki nyo fiye duwaka.
LUK 11:5 Yecu yi ci ki we more kume ki bi farak, an ya fiye cowiye ki dila la yi co ki farmi niye cen cun cari ta'ar.
LUK 11:6 Wori kange farmi bo yam can nawo, ma manki dike ma ne coti na ca.
LUK 11:7 La niwo more ciya ki kom yere, kweri man nungum nyilo miko, take mo kange bibeiyo lomi nyon daken. mani ma dol kwenka ti nan nenen carito.
LUK 11:8 Mi yi kom, bwen co kwen co ne bo cari di, bifarako tiber ciyere mo nua kwenduwe, mo cinti mo kenan coti, an kweni nenen dike mo cuitiye?
LUK 11:9 Mi ma yi komti, kom keni atam ne kom, kom do kan fiya, kom kwabi an wumkumen.
LUK 11:10 Wuro kentiye ti yoi wuro dotiye ati fiya, take wuro kwa tiye an womcinen.
LUK 11:11 We Te wuro bibwece kin jinge a ne co nacuwetiye nyi jinge?
LUK 11:12 Kangeri ken co far di a neco bininge.
LUK 11:13 na wo nyori kom nobo bwit kom nyom kom ne bibeiyo lo kume dike yori nye ye bwi Te kume wo mor dii kwama, an ne kom yuwa tangbe kwamako, nubo ken ce.
LUK 11:14 kange diye Yeecu cok kange bwekelkele nyo tamtabe, la bwekelkele cirum niwo la a tok erti. Dike nyimankar tam nubo.
LUK 11:15 Kange bo mor nobe ciki, “Kibi kwang Ba'alzabuba liya kelkeli cok kelkeli bo tiye.
LUK 11:16 Kange bo cuwa co, cin do na cin nung cinen yirom dii kwama.
LUK 11:17 Yeecu kweri nyomom dike ci kwati ner cire, la yi ci ki “Liyar do ti kangum yoberi, ki ma kiye ki bwiti ci, kayan. Tano luwe tikangum yobri, ki ma kiye an yarum.
LUK 11:18 Tano bwekelkele tikangum yobri, kiye kange dorce, la liyar cero a ti nyi? kom ki maki cok. bwekelele ki bi kwan Ba'alzabuba.
LUK 11:19 Tano man cok bwekelkele fiye ba'alzabuba, la kibi we burombo bwan kumen ti cok kelkelito tiye? nyori ci, ciyilam nobo a makumen bolang.
LUK 11:20 Tano fiye kwama ni ma cok kelkelelito tiyeri, Liyar kwamaro biyeken kumen.
LUK 11:21 Tano nii bikwangne ki kulen kiyener, ki cum lo cue kulen cere bi bu.
LUK 11:22 Tano kange nii lamco ki bi kwan kuwam cori, an yom kulen kwener cero.
LUK 11:23 wuro mani wari kange mo, kiye mati kange mo, take woro mani murti kange mo, watanka co matiye.
LUK 11:24 Tano yuwatangbe ko bwir ko ceri bwi nii, ki do fiye kucer, ki do fiye ca fubom tiye. No fiya bori a yi ki, man yilaken lomi fiye ma do boweu.
LUK 11:25 Na yilauri co fiya cin nyenum luwe, cin ywelum co.
LUK 11:26 Ya an tou kange kelkeli niber wuro la co bwiranke ci bo ci yiken wi, cile nii wo an la kabako bwiraka.
LUK 11:27 Kambo Yeecu tok tiyeri, kange nawiye mor nobe, kung dir cero ki, “Nii bibwiyere fwero bo neneu kange yori mo nowe.
LUK 11:28 Nob bibwiyere wori nuwa ker kwamaro tiye ci bwnagtenti take.
LUK 11:29 Fiya nobo yo ten mwerkako ti la co ki, kallo wo duwo, kallo bwir, do yiromti, bwen duwal yirom mani a nung cinentiye, kan yirom Yunusa.
LUK 11:30 Na wo Yunusa yilam yirom nubo nineba, nyo bi bwe nifire a yila yirom ti fiye kalllo wo wiye.
LUK 11:31 Nawiye wo ca liyar kudu an ti na ma bolang kange kaldo wo an twalum ci, ceru fiye kutan na co nuwa yilen suleimanu, la kange wo wuro la suleimanu fo.
LUK 11:32 Nubo ninea an ti bolang kange nubo kaldo wo an kuwan ci. Cin nuwa fulenke Yunusa, cin yiloten, kange La Yunusa wo.
LUK 11:33 Nii kan mani a kwer talkeri ti na yurangume, kaka Cimon ki tale, dil au yo denkila, be na ne filang mor kuwe.
LUK 11:34 Nuwe mwe co talkire bwi mweutana nuwe mwe yora ri, tang num bwiyombo a fiya filang tano nue mani to ti yorari bwi kume a dim ka kumtacile.
LUK 11:35 Kom ma yora kati filang ko kume nen yilam kumta cili. Tano bwi kume dimka filang di, kumtacile man.
LUK 11:36 Tano bwi kume gwam dimka, kumtacile man biduwarece, la bwi kume a yilam na talkire wo ne filang cekoti durkumere.
LUK 11:37 kambo Yecu dim kereri, kange nii dingle (Bafarice) cwo co na bo lo cona co cam cari, Yeecu dou yi.
LUK 11:38 Kambo nii dingli (Bafarice) To Yeecu ca carito ti nirbo kang, la ti nyimange.
LUK 11:39 Yeecu yi co ki, “Kom nod dinglibo” (Farisawa) kom ki nirum ka bwim kwelem more dimka duti kange chil.
LUK 11:40 Kom kule nobe, wo ma bwimbe kebo wo ma moreka?
LUK 11:41 Kom ne nob bwinebo dike more. Dikero gwam na nir kimen.
LUK 11:42 Kwan kom nob dinglib Farisawa kom yo wine ti dor kwobe na kule, tibi kange tangnim laluwo, dila kom citan wucake kange cwika kwama ko. tam nyo na ma dike dong dong a cwi tangnin dikero tak.
LUK 11:43 Gwam kume kom nob dinglib Farisawa kom cwiti a nekom fiye ken mor kurwabe, take a ne kom dur yarume fiye fene.
LUK 11:44 Gwam kom nob dinglib Farisawa Kom ki no na tuwetinin bo ci yo cinen bo kange diker na yirome nobo ti fuwarangi kebo ki nyomka cek.
LUK 11:45 Kange nii meranka mor bulange Yahudawa ciya karcinen ki Nii meranka dike mo toke, kangum ner nyera.
LUK 11:46 Kwan kom nob meranka bulangeb dike kom kung nobo nin kulen do tuu lambi kwan tuka ke. Kom mok bo kulendo kibi wer kange kume.
LUK 11:47 Kwankom, kom mu diker kulomkati fiye tuwetinin nob tomange kwama bonin.
LUK 11:48 Bwikoko ten kwanib kumeb twallan ciye.
LUK 11:49 Yilam ka nyom nangen tenkwanub kumebo, ci twalan nob tomangebo wo kom bulanti ki ciye,
LUK 11:50 Kaldo a tuu tutum bwiyale nob tomangebo gwam wo ci twal fiya kale wo fwele.
LUK 11:51 Tabti bwile habila ya tam ciko Zakariya ciko wo ci twal tiber tanjilan kwamero fiye wuccak. ong mi yi kom an do dike tam na ciye kaldo wo wiye.
