LUK 11:52 Gwam kom nob merangka bolangeb wo Yauhdawa ceu, wori kom tom nyilo yomka, kom ki bwikimi kom do bo. kom Yuwan do ka ko doka.
LUK 11:53 Bwikako Yeecu dob fiye co nob mulankab kange nob dinglib (Farisawa) cin tu kurom kange co cin kwokangi kange co dor diker dutce.
LUK 11:54 Ci doti na cin cii cimen kore, na ci tam cco mor dike co toktiye.
LUK 12:1 Kutang bo nyori bwikako nubo dutce mwerkang fwarang bwititi, La con ter tokak kererko kange bibei tomange ceu. Kom cire kange canfuwambo nob diglibo (Farisawa) wo co yulkako.
LUK 12:2 Diker mani nawo cummome nawo mani a wom tiye, kange mani nawo yurangume, mani a nyomtiye.
LUK 12:3 Diker mani wo ka tokti balumbale, wo mani a nuwati nyanglange, Dike kom toki kiyelange, an kwaki dir fiye gwam.
LUK 12:4 Farub mib ma yi komti O-n nure tai wuro a twalum bwiyotiye. bwikako nye ci manki diker makar.
LUK 12:5 Mi makumen biweret, wo ka nuwa tai cero tiye, kom nowo tai wuro twalum di an mwerken kom mor kira. “O” man yi kom ti kom nuwa tai co.
LUK 12:6 Ke ciki meye berin bilebe nung anini yob? gwam nyo kwama mani a tabti ki wi more ciye.
LUK 12:7 Kange yirito dor kumere nyomom kilatum ciyembo. Kom nuwa re tai kom la bilibetin do yorka fiye co wiye.
LUK 12:8 Mi yikom ti Nii wo tok fulen miro kabum nobomeri, Bibwe nifire an warkercer kabum nob tomangeb kwama.
LUK 12:9 Tak Nii wo koye kabum nobomeri man ko co kabaum nob tomange kwama.
LUK 12:10 Nii na tok ker kiyer dor bibwe nii fireri an cutan cinenwi. La niwo tok kwilangka dor yuwa tangbeko wucakeri, mani a cutang cinenti.
LUK 12:11 Tano ci bo ki kom kabom bikur waber di, kange kabum nob bulange kange kabum liyabem kom bwende kange dike ka kartiye nawo ka cerum dor kumerotiye; kange diker ka tok tiye.
LUK 12:12 Yuwa tangbe ko wucake an meran kumen dike ka tok ti fiya co.
LUK 12:13 Kange mor mwerkanka nin yi co ki Nii merangka yi kemi na tikangum kwalito kange mo.
LUK 12:14 We yo yi nii bolange, kange nii do kertiye dor kumer?
LUK 12:15 Kom yilam ki cini kari kom yilam nob kucunu kebo dike nii mweri co la dike yurak mor dumece.
LUK 12:16 La Yeecu yici kero ki danke ki take ni kange ni carito dutce,
LUK 12:17 Nii wo kwabi neer cer ki, ye ma matiye, wo ma mani ki fiye ma yom carito wo tiye.
LUK 12:18 Ma nyo mom di ma matiye man werum binitin miro na mwirangum na yoken cari mito kang tannung dikro.
LUK 12:19 La na yi dumek mi mike dume mi, mo wi ki diker dutce wo ci yomneneu fubom ca no ma bilantum.
LUK 12:20 Di kwama yico nii wo mor kume wo ci ci dume mwetimunen. kulen do mo mweri mo yo dor mwero nineu a yi la na wee?
LUK 12:21 Nyo niwo mwer dor ceronin cwika, tano co man ki cweka kwamamnin
LUK 12:22 Yecu yibibei tomangece, Di nyo ma yi ti ki kome, kom bwende ki dume dike ka ca ti kaka wo ka dukti bwiyeu.
LUK 12:23 dume la cari, bwiyo la kwilen.
LUK 12:24 Kom to karce nii mani fi fik mani biye bituwe. Ci manki bentini kaka kuni murka carik, dila kwama catikici, kom kon la bilibe yorka?
LUK 12:25 We more kume, ka tii dilanka a yok dor cero nin ten kumeni tiye? tana kom dolbo ko yok dorkumero ninten dikero bi duware. Ye bwi ka kwom dor kumero ti kange tangnim dikereu?
LUK 12:27 Kom to funti mor kiye kambo ci duyantie. ma ci ma nange, ma ci ma kange diker. Mi yi komti bwen Culeimanu ki bwayilen cero dwal di, du bo kulen do la ciye yerake.
LUK 12:28 Tano kwama dii yerako nin kulen yori na nyori, den i, fini an dokken co kira, la a bwi nyi kwama a fweti mani ca dukumen kulentiye, kom nubo ki dwal ka bilenkere.
LUK 12:29 Kom bwende ki dike wo ka catiye kaka wo ka notiye, kom kimang deu.
LUK 12:30 Nyo nubo dor bitinen gwam ci do dike wuroti, take Te kume nyomom kom ti cwi dike buromboti.
LUK 12:31 Kom do liyar cero, kullendo wuro ciya yok kumenti.
LUK 12:32 Kom nuware tai, kom bi beiyo bi duwattinim wori ki bilang tum Te kume a ne kom liyartiye.
LUK 12:33 Kom miyem dike kom cike kom ne nob fuwabbo. kom ma dor kumero nin bilantin we mani a kayatiye kom yoken di kwama fiye dike cuwo mani a difiye, fiye nob kub mani a dol yaka tiye, nakunkunge mani a kanti.
LUK 12:34 Fiye cweka mwe wiye firn nermwero wiye.
LUK 12:35 Kom mwatumen cwentum kulen kumero ko cakkangum, talkire kume ata cai kang kang.
LUK 12:36 Kom yilam na nuboro wuro nintan teluwe ciye na yilau lo cika, la tano bo kwa yilokori can can do wo ciya kweni ci wobcicnen yiloko.
LUK 12:37 Bilenker ma yikom ti an cakkangum kulencer na yo ci yiranken la na ceci carito. ki bwici.
LUK 12:38 Bwen Teluwe ciya a bo ki kume keno, kaka ki dii ca biyerci ki bati ci ningtan co ti. Nobbibwer cnga buro.
LUK 12:39 Ko nyomom na nii luwe nyomom boka nii kwiye kori, mana a dobti ci wercinen luwe, ci doken.
LUK 12:40 Kom ti ki bati wari kom nyomom filang Bibwe nii a yilautiye.
LUK 12:41 Bitru yi co ki teluwe nyo mwo yin danke wotiye, kaka nubo gwam ka?
LUK 12:42 Teluwe to ki nii durko wuni ki cini nii yilen wo Teluwe ce ne co canga ceti kangeceke, na to ci na ne ci carito fiya daten ne?
LUK 12:43 Nii bibwiyer canga wuro Teluwece a fiiya co na dike ci yoce ca mane.
LUK 12:44 Bilenke mi yikom ti aneken co lo ceu kang cek.
LUK 12:45 Ta no canga wo toki mor nerci ki Teluwe m lakken boka ko, la con ter bukka tang nim cangambo nabarub kange natub, farub nagenebce.
LUK 12:46 Teluwe canga wo an yilau, fiya co nyombo, La torangum co ki mwan ki mwan na mwe co kange nubo manki ciniye.
LUK 12:47 Canga wo nyomom mulen Teluwece, di la ka bo bati mabo dike teluwece yoco ca mane diker wo Teluwe cwitiye, a nuwa bibuker kange banjange dutce.
LUK 12:48 La niwo nyombe, la ma dike kebo dong dong, mani a nuwa bi buker kange banjange dutce. Nii wo ci neco dikero ducce a do dikero ducce cinen. Tano ni wo ci neco diker ducce na takako ce, na a do dike ducce kambo ken cinen.
LUK 12:49 Ma bou be na dukti kira dor bitiner, man cwi na ki kweri tam di.
LUK 12:50 Mo man wi ki yuka mwenge ko wucake wo ciye mamentiye ciko, la ma cwi mwini mam.
LUK 12:51 kom kwa netti, ma bo dor bitiner na boki for neret? ma yi kome o-ong dila yalkanka.
LUK 12:52 Tabti nawo an fiya nubo nung mor luwe wiin di ciya tikangum, nubo ta'ar makiye ti kange nubo yob, yob makiye ti kange ta'ar,
LUK 12:53 Bwe kange te ciyan ma kiye kange bwiti ci, bwe an makiye kange Tece, Ne an makiye kange bibwece bobya, bobya kange nece, bifire kange ferce, wi bibwe ce kange ferce.
LUK 12:54 Yecu yi nubo mwerummeu, no kom to yuwa mwengek kwenu meri komki mwembo an cwe, nyo a matiye.
LUK 12:55 Tano yuwa ko ceru bangdi komki an ma cillen kambo ken, nyo matiye.
LUK 12:56 Nubo bwir, kom yumon fwetanka kabal kalero kange dii kwama, dila lakom nyom bo fwetanka dikeko bwiti nawo nyeu?
LUK 12:57 Ye bwi kom nyombo dike a tikankomtiiye?
LUK 12:58 Tano mwi yaken ti kubolange kange kobkanka mweri, ken co kom ywellum don nuret kari ya kinen kabum nii bolange. Kari nii bolange neken nen nii wo to fucina tiye mani a nung mwen nyomkankati fucina.
LUK 12:59 Mi yimnen mani mo ceru ti, mon yam kiyemero ci bwangmwen tiyeu.
LUK 13:1 Ki kwama curo nubo kangem wi yico ker dor nobo Galiliye wo Bilatu ceikangum bwiyale ceu kange wabi.
LUK 13:2 La kiritti yici, “kom kwatiri Galatiyawambo bwiran kere ka?
LUK 13:3 Nyonin, min yi komti. No kom dobbori gwam kume kom bwiyarangi na ci.
LUK 13:4 Kakaa nobo kwobcilombo naurube ciloam wo luwe cwemi nyeu yar cinenti dorceer ci bwiyarangume, kom kwatiri ciin la tangnum nobeu urucalimau biranke?
LUK 13:5 O-ong, miki. Lano gwam niwo ko dobka ri ciyan bwiya rangum.
LUK 13:6 Kiritti tok dangke wuro,”Nii kange wi ki tii nyongjong wo ci fiken mor take ce la cin bou na ci ca bituttuiyeri la tiyo man ki cari.
LUK 13:7 Dila nii curo yi nii tokako,'to, coro ta'ar naweu, ma do bituttuiti fo nyongjongo nin di mafiyabo tom co ye bwi ba dob coti ten fiye ti koniye?'
LUK 13:8 Co nii tokakko ciya toki neye kumeni nyo bi dob na kam nan yoti cinenti kilongwi
LUK 13:9 No mabi tuttidi cortini boti yeri tano mabobi tuttiri nan mwatum co.
LUK 13:10 Bi di kange Kiriti ma mrngkati fiye bi wabe kange bidiye fob ka.
LUK 13:11 Di la naweu kangee bou wo dii curo kwob cilombo narub wiki twirak yuwa bwir gwam kange fwinka mani do taka ti.
LUK 13:12 Kambo Kiriti to ce cin cuwaco yico cin cukum twirako wo.
LUK 13:13 La kiriti yoti kanko dor ce tabbo. buri can cando cin tarken cet co ter bilonge liyar kwamma.
LUK 13:14 Di ni kur biwaro manfunerr dige bwiyeu Kiriti nangen bi Fob ka di ni bi wabiro nyi nubo kume ni wi nyo nukku na nangen do ce kom bow na makimen ddi La kebbo ki bidiko fobka.
LUK 13:15 Di la teluwe kar cimen ki kom nubo bwir no nyori mi wor tiber kimer mi kange wo ca ki gelbati na fiye ci tekume nemwem bidiye fobka ka?
LUK 13:16 No nyori wuro bibwe Abrame wo be kelkele no bwamco ki coro kwab culom nanrube, tano nyo mania kwi cati kibi diye fubka ka?
LUK 13:17 Kambo co tokki nyo weri nubo ma kwab kangka ti kange coweu cin nuwa kwenduwe. Gwam tare al cin ma fur nener ki dikero kendo wuro ci mane.
LUK 13:18 Kiriti toki kiye ba tak liyar kwama ti cike yilo ye ba dang ti cike?
LUK 13:19 Wi nyo na nun nying cin wuro ni kange wabi takece Landim nyo gili gili la bilibe tini manag cor tini kani ce nen.
LUK 13:20 Yila con tokko liyar kwararo ba tok kiye?
LUK 13:21 Wi nyo ca fuwam di la kange nawiye mwe kange mim murduwe bidigle tar na fumco.
LUK 13:22 Kiriti ker kan cinar lor kange bwar lor, wi nuro wo yakenti Ucalima ci mernag cinneti.
LUK 13:23 La cin yi co teluwa nubo biro ciya fiya dob kakko bi dob nyo ka? La cin yici.
LUK 13:24 Ki ma dige dateneu. ki do nure bwa ki do nure bwabwa leli nyori mi nyi kom, nudo ducce ci cwi doka ti di la ci fiyabo doka.
LUK 13:25 No niluwe kwri kwenum nungum yilokko la kan tiken kale kom kwa kwabang nyi lokkoti teluwa, teluwe do nyo nyi do mour di cin ciya cotaki mi nyomkombo keno kom cirou feri.
LUK 13:26 Di la ka tok komki nyim ca nyin no for kabum mwem. di la mun merang nyinen dor nure nyim bo nin.
LUK 13:27 La can ciya ci tokki.
LUK 13:28 Ciyan ci wiye kange kuka nunne ki bidiye kom to muca, kange Isaku kange Yakubu gwam nob dugume firer liyar kwama kumeu ciyan merken kom kale.
LUK 13:29 Ci ya bo twat mee, bang, kole ci ya ca tokam cari iyar kwama.
LUK 13:30 Ki nyim comm wuro nob kaba nyim lam nubo cuwa bwire nubo cuwa bwireu co nubo yilam kaba.
LUK 13:31 Di kutabo kangem faricawa cin bou ciki Musa, kubom fo dike bwiyeu Hiridus cwi twalka mwekti.
LUK 13:32 Kirititi tokki com ya Bicura kom ki to min co kom ninga nubo fiya fulo ki di ki kume take cwiti a murangu bibeiyo na wuro bicate ki murang de bi bei loce mwor tangum cem la kom ciyabo.
LUK 13:33 To ci miran lomwe la mi, yikomti mani ka to yeti tano diye ki tokke luma drek tam nyo ki den kwamar.
LUK 13:34 Bwentano a manyiri yam mimbo ya kenti duwen, fini cike daten bo ciya twalum teluwe kutom kange Ursalima.
LUK 13:35 Kom to lo kumeu cin cwutanwi No kom tok kumki luma ki no kan bibwe nii wo bilang kwama yeu.
LUK 14:1 Di fubka cin do ko lo ni wo mor farisawa na cin ca cari la nubo cor ci nenten nuwe.
LUK 14:2 Di la ikange wo ka co wo ki der na cekke.
LUK 14:3 Kiriti me nobbi finero durko kange fari cawa daten na fulani bidiye fobka nyo kakka mani nyo ka?
LUK 14:4 La cin kumom Kiriti ta co fulo co di nyico ca yakenti
LUK 14:5 La kiriti me ci wetiber kimer ki bwe kange, bi curan di yraken bwire bidiye fubka la mani ca cokk ti ka?
LUK 14:6 Di la dol bo tokker diger buronin.
LUK 14:7 kambo Kritti to nubo ci cuowu d ti ka fiye yime keneu tok kerg dangke ci nen.
LUK 14:8 no ni kange cowonner fiye nakarim yire dur ni kange wi ci cuwoco kenne lanen ki dur.
LUK 14:9 Di la no niwo cuwo kom bou an yinen nub niwo mi fiye yimemweu na coyeu mwan kweni mu yiken kutule bi duware.
LUK 14:10 No cin co nen fiyeri, yiken kutule biduware la no niwo co nenu bouri atin tooki farmi kweni yiken fo cwemer na fiya bi duyet nuwe nubo wuro nokom yi wariye.
LUK 14:11 Gwam nitu dor core ci kebo diker ciyan bilange co tano niwo dor cero cin diker nubo mani a bilank coti.
LUK 14:12 Kritti yila yi nii wo co cue no mo neni cari na ti na cwentiri yire muki mwan cowo for nener yimom ki namwe, niwo bidom kange mwe di dike ci ca mani nyo.
LUK 14:13 No mwon cuwofiye nakari cuwang kang niwo mani cike fukma, kilen wale kange bibei.
LUK 14:14 Mwan fiya luma dike bwiyeu ci ma bilantum dikero wo mwa ma cineneu ma ci ya neneti na bilank Yeecu maneu mwan fiya bilanka kibi diye kwenka nob bi bwiyer kwama.
LUK 14:15 Kambo ni win mor nubo ca carito kom wari kange kiritti nuwa nyori ki lima nubo biro a ca cari liyar kwama.
LUK 14:16 La Kiriti yi co ki ni kange wi cowo nubo ducce ki cika dur
LUK 14:17 Kambo di cika ko lameri tom cange ceu yaca cowo nubo wuro co ne tomanage ciya bour dikero kwarub ywelu.
LUK 14:18 Gwam ciye cinter neka dige bwiyeu. wo kiba yico min tiyen takke daten yamman to mi kinong nenti dobye.
LUK 14:19 La ni kange tokki min tiyen nne nung mi cwiti nan cuwa mi konog nenti dobye.
LUK 14:20 Ni kange ki nia na nawiyeu mani ma dol yakati.
LUK 14:21 Kambo bwe canga ce bo yi teluwe ceri yaken tiyeri la teluwe ceu mam funer nyi canga ceu ki ya wulom bwangten nure cinar loreu kange wo kebo cinar loreu. congawu, fukma, kilen celeb, waleb.
LUK 14:22 La canga ceu tokki i lomi dike mo tikke timi mam dila corbo bwini.
LUK 14:23 Di la ni luweu nyi canga ceu ya bangten nureu cinar loreu kange wo bwar lor bolange ciya dou na ci dim lomi.
LUK 14:24 Tano nyi mi yi komti win more kume cowo ki kaba bakeu, kange ciye mani a c ci kamiti.
LUK 14:25 Nyo tere yakenti kange co la con yila bwi yi ci.
LUK 14:26 Gwam niwo bou fo fiye weu tano kobo tece, nece, wice, bibiyoloce, yitum cebo nina bare kange wice nyo kange nercero ri, mmani ca yila bibwemiti.
LUK 14:27 Gwam niwo tuba bwatiye na bwangmenten neri kebo bibwemi.
LUK 14:28 We tiber kumer wo cwi muka luweti la yibo na nyi mom diek ca kwale ki kaba tano cin wi ki kiyemer tak kakkori?
LUK 14:29 Tano nya ci yo kwar kuwero ci takbo dikakori nubo biro toeu nung coti.
LUK 14:30 Ci tokti kii niwo ter muka la fwem ki di kakko.
LUK 14:31 No nyori liay wini wo yakenti kange liya kange nyombo bi kwama nubo loce keno nyiri daten bikwan tin mamdi na ci nyi mom keno niwo ki nubo bikeate kwab ki culomeu catin mam kange niwo bikate kwini yoberi.
LUK 14:32 Tano mani ca doltiri ki kwama kece firen kutaneu ca tom canga na meu yaka nanneko na ka kwendo mani.
LUK 14:33 Nyori ni kange mani tiber kumer wo ca dubom kulen cero tiri mani ca yila bibwe miti.
LUK 14:34 Mam dike yora tano carum bitineri mwa ma ye?
LUK 14:35 Man ki luma bi tine tano amnyiri dam cutangka gwam niwo kitu nuwa kange ca nuwa
LUK 15:1 La yuwak nob merangkab kange nob yoka kemer doreko bouti Yeecu nen cin nuwacoti.
LUK 15:2 Farisawa kange nob mulangka bo cima fwenati bwitici ciki” Niwo yo nob bwirangkebti ci ca caitoti waritak.
LUK 15:3 Yeecu tok danke wo yici.
LUK 15:4 Canno kange kume ki kwame kumi kwo lawin more ce lem, mani ca dob kwini Teer culombo teere ti naci bwanten meka wuro win lemeu naci fiyam.
LUK 15:5 Tano ci fiyam ri naci tuu ci yaken Lagwamcem ci no fuwor nerer tiye.
LUK 15:6 No ci yilaudi naci cwo farubcebo kange nubo biom kange ceu, naci yici, kom ti kanye fuwor nerer min fiya kwame mi lemeu.
LUK 15:7 Miyikomti nyo a ma fuwor nerer tiye dii kwama don ni bwiranker win kange nobo kiner luma kwini taar culombo teereu wuro dobo ywelka bwirange keu cereu.
LUK 15:8 Kaka we nawiye, ki kemer nai nyo kwob no lemdi manica wentalkire ti ci nyina yum mor kuwe la citi doi naci fiyam me?
LUK 15:9 Noci fiyam laci mwer farubcebo kange nubo bidom kange ceu ciyicii kom tikanye fuwor nerer min fiyam kwame meu.
LUK 15:10 Nyo mi yi komtiye, diker fuwer nerer nob tomangeb kwamab cano, ni bwinrangke winn dob bwirangkerori.
LUK 15:11 La Yeecu yici “Ni kange wi ki bibei bayilob yob.
LUK 15:12 La bi duwareu yi teece Tee neye miu kwalito mor cuweka mwekonin. Dila Tee ce kabkamm cinen kwalito.
LUK 15:13 Ki Kumeni kilabori dila bwe biduware murance kwalito yaken biti kange katangi. cin yakcangum kwalito tie nen bikulentiti yakcangum kemero cero noranka diker.
LUK 15:14 Kambo ci yakcangum kwalitori la cin ma wura kambo ken bitine con ni lam doken bwini.
LUK 15:15 Yacin neken dorcero nangen ni kange bitineco, la twamom mor tangini ce nacinen Bilerce cariti.
LUK 15:16 La cin cari ca do dike bilerece a catiyeu, wori ni kange mani neco cariti.
LUK 15:17 Dila kambo yulancero bwiceri yice ki cnga Tee mi cingile cike cari la cinnen bo dila mi fo ma bwiyati ka ker carity.
LUK 15:18 Man kweni neken Tee mi in yico “Tee Min ma dikwanin bwirainke min kangmwen.
LUK 15:19 Ma datenbo coya muki bibwemiri yokenye min yilam win mor cangabtinim mweb?”.
LUK 15:20 Lacin kweni, cibou tecemin. Dila kambo ci kutanneri, la Tee ce tomco cibwini ceto yaki cwak, yan bwabco, lata macinen cuika.
LUK 15:21 Bweu inyico Tee, mi ma dii kwama nen bwiranke, min kangum mwen. ma labo coten ye muki bi bwemwe.
LUK 15:22 Di la Teece yi cangab cebo, kom bouki bellewo yor yoreu, kom ducinen kon dok cinen keneu kange cek kange ta nacek.
LUK 15:23 la ko bou ki neneu mobiyeu kom biyem bima cenen bilengtum ciko.
LUK 15:24 Na weu bebwemi bwiyam fiyeco dila naweu yilau ki dume. Lem fiyeco dila fiyau. lacin teer cika.
LUK 15:25 Ki kwama co bibwece durko ki kambo dadom loweri cin nuwa ci kwaban dikerti kange nuwetinin.
LUK 15:26 Lacin com kange bwe canage loceu meco dikerowo mati loriyeu. neneu mob mobeu wori cin yilau lo kwamer.
LUK 15:27 Bwe cangau yico kemwe yilau lowe, Tee mwe biyem neneu cin yilau lo kwamer.
LUK 15:28 Di la kece bwe durko mam funer ko do kako mor luwe Tee ce ceriu kale kinang co.
LUK 15:29 Bwe durko ciyace Tee ce ki to ka cotiyowo mi ari kange mo ki komwem bo tomange nii wucak kange wo mune yob be nibeni wo ma cati kange farub mibeu.
LUK 15:30 Di la bwe wuro ya cutang bicir mwer dor mun biye cinen kalnenero mob mo bo.
LUK 15:31 Di la Teece yico ki “Bibwemi, mu wari kange mo gwam dikero na mi yeri na mwe.
LUK 15:32 Di la dong dong cimamwen luma kange fur nerer, wori kemwe wo buyam dila nawori ki dume, fiayco lem la nanweu, bin fiyam.
LUK 16:1 Yeecu yi nobbwankecebo tak, “nii cuwekako kangeni ki ni toman'nye, Lacin kwa kiyan nye ki nii toman nyewo kang cineut cuwekacokob.
LUK 16:2 La nii cuweka wuco yico, “fulan yer minuwa dor mwere? bowki kiyeka tomange mweke, wori mari mwa yila nii tomange mititak.
LUK 16:3 Lamitomange toki neren, ma mangi, nilomi anyam tomanyewo kangmik? Wo, mimanki bikwantonet lami cwa kwenduwe meka cekoti.
LUK 16:4 Minnyumwom dike ma matiyeu noci cukumye mor tomanye nindi, nubo ayoye lonici.
LUK 16:5 Dila nitomannye cwuningangum nubo teluwece bwanteng centiyeu, yi nii kaba, Nyi nii lomi bwangmwenten tiye?
LUK 16:6 yiki, 'nuwannye kwini kwob' Isryico, Bifumer mwerowo, canakowo yikenyiye, mulangum kwini nung.
LUK 16:7 Yilan yikannye, ciki bwangmwentuniyi? Yiki, cwayi bikate kwini kwob, 'bifumerwo mulangum kwini narub'.
LUK 16:8 Dila niwo caklang nii bwini bilengewo ki yulancero. Bibeyo kaleweu nyimem maka nyinong nubo ko kaleweu la bibei filange yulang.
LUK 16:9 Miyi komti komma bifarak kannge cuweraka kannge buni bilinke, cawo cin dimri, naci yokom lonici wuro manki diks.
LUK 16:10 Wo madikerti dongdong dor dikero biduwareri, cin nii dongdonge dor dikero dur, wo kebo nii bilinke don dikero bidurure, kebo ni bilinke dor dikero dur.
LUK 16:11 Tano kommabo dike dongdonge di cuwekako kebo wucakeri, we aciya kumenti kicuweka wabilinkece?
LUK 16:12 No komma dike dongdonge ki kemer niidir we anekom kemer kumer tiye?
LUK 16:13 Kange mami wo a wob nii luweti yobe, catin kowini, ci cui win kakka ci ciya winening, ci cuwe kangum wineu. mani ka wab kwaamatiri kom wab cuwekati.
LUK 16:14 Kambo faricawabo wuro cui cuwekatiyeu nuwa dikero biombori, cin macinen cuwelangka.
LUK 16:15 Inyici, “Kom ko tiki dor kumero kabum nubem, dila kwaama nyumuom nerkumero. Dikero nubo nedurketiye nyeu diker yeika fiye kwaama wiye.
LUK 16:16 Biwerer bifumer nob tomangebo inwi yakenciko Yahaya nin. Kwama wuro cin bwanten ker liyar kwaaranarotiye, kwarub kutannyi kwamacuo ci bwangten ker liyar kwaamarotiye, kwanrub ci ma bwi dokka dorekti morece.
LUK 16:17 Gwamm kangero, atin yilam bwaibo diko kange bitineu nabecum, na diker win nabi weretro na dim.
LUK 16:18 Niwo nyankan wucenin naukangeri inma buroka, ken niwo nau nawiyewo cinyam kanngeri inma buroka.
LUK 16:19 Nii cuwakakko kanngenwi, wo dukulen kemero yoryoreu nuwa luma kalecokoti.
LUK 16:20 Cin yoken nii kini kannge nyiloco, dencero Liazaru, wo bwiceu ka deti.
LUK 16:21 Ceu ci cuiti naci bwam fwercero ki fiti cari yarangum ti fiye caka carik nii cuweka nyo kibi cuwetincer bom biyablam bwiceti.
LUK 16:22 Laniwo bwiyamri, nobtomangeb kwaamabo tu co yakenciko Ibrayim nin. Ni cuweks buyam, cin fwerumco,
LUK 16:23 ci mor Adece ci nuwa dotange ti, la cin kun doro cinto Ibrayim kutan, kan'nge Liazaru cantangcek.
LUK 16:24 Lacin cobicoro ciki, Tee Ibrayim, ci bwinni mito, twomun Liazaru adokti biwurece mwem abelti menti biyenmin, wori indotange minuwati mor kirewe.
LUK 16:25 Dila Ibrayim yico, Bwe, kwabi ki kwamawo mu kalemweu munuwa luma cuweka mwekobi, munyo kulentinimbo ken, La Liazaru nuwati ka dotange. Dila naweu luma cinecotide, mwe munuwa dotangeti.
LUK 16:26 Nobo nyori dila buwako cuwa cuwau inwi, wori birombi coi yabkati kumeneu nadolde, tak kannge na yabuurefo nyinnen.
LUK 16:27 Lamicuweks yiki, Lami kennenti Tee Ibrayim, twornco lo Tee ni-
LUK 16:28 wori minweki keb mib bi beibayilobe nyo nung, amincinen biweret kayilo cibuo fiye dotangewo.
LUK 16:29 Dila Ibrayim yiki, cin wiki Musa kannge kannge nob toman'ngebi nyori ciya nuwaci,
LUK 16:30 Dilla nii cuweka ciyaki, 'O, on, Tee Ibrayim, cano kan'nge mor birombo biyam biya yacinendi, ciyam yiloten.
LUK 16:31 Dilla Ibrayim yico, cono ci Musa kan'ge nobtoman'gebo ri, cabunano kan'nge fulou duwendi maciya nuwacoti”
LUK 17:1 La Yeecu yi nob bwankacebe, “nyimaka mami ter kottangka wo adokbo maka bwirank kektiye dila cilkakiniwo a yilam cotiyeu!
LUK 17:2 Can nyimiri kin yei cimenti ner kuwaka kwircer amerkanco mor fara kan'nge wo ca yilam diker kottanka biduwatinimbo wuronin.
LUK 17:3 Kom yabki dor kumer. No kemwe kanngumdi, werangco, cano ciyilotendi dobcinen.
LUK 17:4 Cano kanmwen kiriti niber kikakukowimdi yilam bou munen kiriti niber yiki, min yiloten, yilam nyo dobcinen”
LUK 17:5 Dilla nobtoman'gebo cinyi Teeluwe, “cuob nyienten bilingkeu”.
LUK 17:6 Teeluwe lanyiki, “Cano komki bilinke duwali na nun bikateri, mwanyi tiyowo, kwomfo, ya kulken mor caji”, atim manyo.
LUK 17:7 Canwe more kume carno wiki cawonya wuro cuo cinen tomboti kakaa tocinen kwameti, cano yilam kiri, ayicoti, canokono bouyifo na camcarito?
LUK 17:8 Mani co yicoti ki mamen diker nan cam, na bwam dak mwekori maman na'nyend benan dimcaka carito kan'nge noko mu'ngeko?
LUK 17:9 Manica ma cariya cewonin buka kamin yekti wori madikeci dokco ciya mane, keno am mani nyori?
LUK 17:10 Nyo, cano kom bwanten ciyikomemri, lakom toki, 'nyin can'nya manki nanyene. Nyim ma dikewo tam kang'eu”.
LUK 17:11 Kakuko kamnye ciyakenti Wurcalimani lacim bwanteng beten Samariya kan'nge Galili.
LUK 17:12 Kambo cidokenti cunnuku kan'nyeri, dila bayiloto kan'ngerobo kwob ki wale citim kutan cinkicico.
LUK 17:13 Lacin kun diro “Yeecu, Tee kwama, cibwini nyeto”
LUK 17:14 Kaci tociyeri, yici, “yakom dang dor kumero nob waberonin”. Yilam kambo ciyakentiyeri lacin yilam wucak.
LUK 17:15 Wiri morece kacito cin cerco wucak keri, yilanken, duktang kwama kidiro kwamer.
LUK 17:16 Cin yari kabum Yeecu, cin bucinen kamti. Cin ba Samariye.
LUK 17:17 Yeecu in ciya toki, “kebo kwob ci ceri wucakka? infe tanneceu?
LUK 17:18 Kan'nge mani wo yilam nekwaama durke kanco fabewo kikwaca?”
LUK 17:19 Lanyico, “Kwoni yayam mwem. Bilinke mweu ceerner”.
LUK 17:20 Kambo Faricawa meco kwamawo liyar kwamaro aboutiyeu, Yeecu ciya nyiki, “Liyar kwaamaro kobo nyomka maticike.
LUK 17:21 Mani atokti, 'iriwo!' Kakaa, 'wurenhim!' Wori Liyar kwaamaro kino tiber kumer”
LUK 17:22 Yeecu yi nob bwankabo, “Kumeni wi bouti nawo ka yoner toka kume win mor kumeni bi bwe niggire, dilla mani ka toti.
LUK 17:23 Ciyan yikon, “Tofiren! 'Tofuo!' Dila kom yakomtore, kakaa kom bwangten cire.
LUK 17:24 Nawo meblankako Nefilanti nafo cunya di kwamaka wori ya ken cunya di kwamako wureno, Nyo bi bwe nii a yilanyo ki kume bokaceko.
LUK 17:25 Dila kang catin nuwe dotangetinim kidimen kidimen bwiriri, nubo kaleweu ankoco.
LUK 17:26 Kambo bwi kal Nuhu re, nacuwo tak a bwiuti ki kwama bibwe nii aboutiyeu.
LUK 17:27 Citi cai, citi noi, citi nai, cinakenti yaken di ye Nuhu doken Nabire kwama la mwom wermakabo bow twalan'gum ci kwarub gwamm.
LUK 17:28 Nyo cimani ki kwama lutuwe, citi cai, citi noi, citinenii, citi miyei, ci fi fikkoti, cimuran'ngi.
LUK 17:29 Dila kikakuko Lutu, cerum Saduma, lakira kwaamako caruu dikwama, twalan'ngum ci gwamm.
LUK 17:30 Nyotak abwiuti ki kume bibweni aboutiye.
LUK 17:31 Kikakuko wori, niiwo dor kureu ayiraure kica tu kulencer mor luwe. Nyotak niiwo kiyeu ayilaure.
LUK 17:32 Komkwaki wii Lutu.
LUK 17:33 Niwo cwidumecetiyeu, anlemco, lano niwo lem dumeceri, anfiyanco.
LUK 17:34 Miyikomti, kumewo amfiya nubo yob kwangni win. Atim tumwin nadubomwimeu.
LUK 17:35 Atim fiya natubo yob ci kuwa nerti ware. Atim tum win na dubom win.”
LUK 17:36 
LUK 17:37 Atim to nubom yob kii, “Antum win nadubom win”.
LUK 18:1 Yilam netenti dangke kwange ki yori kabo nyirinyir ciya kwo diloti ciya cwaretai,
LUK 18:2 toki, “Bitine kam'nge nii bolan'nge kam'ngenwi baniki tai kwaama, takri manito yorinubek.
LUK 18:3 Nawiye kwale kam'nge inwi bitineco, wobou cinenneu, yicoki, 'Tikanaye ka ma manob kiyeb mibonin luma tiyeu.
LUK 18:4 Inkutan'nyi mani cwiti citikanyco, dila kibwiri toki mor nerece, cano mani cwatan kwaamati, takri mami mito yorak nubekti,
LUK 18:5 kwarub kan'nge wo nwori nawriye kwalewo kwomye, mantikameo nacifiya luma, kambo marice luwayeti kiboko minenneu.”
LUK 18:6 Dila Tee kwaama jiki, komuwa dikero nii bolangewo manki tokkeu.
LUK 18:7 Lanawo kwama mani cor nubolocemboni birombo cicnen wiyeti kume kan'nge kakuke bwini citotika? Anmabwi fiye tikalicika?
LUK 18:8 Miyikomti, comcorcinen bwimicito wulom. Dilla kambo bibweni bouweri, an kwobti bilam ke nii dor bitinen”
LUK 18:9 Yilam neten Dankewo kange nubonin birombo ciya ki dorcireu, ki cimnob lumabeb, laci cuwekamten tankne nuboti,
LUK 18:10 “Nubo kan'ngumbo cin doken mor lo kwama naci kwob dilo-win bwe Faricawa, wineu inni nye dotiye.
LUK 18:11 Dila bwe Faricawa kweminti, kwodila dor dikero birombo dorcer, kwama, min buwen kang, mikebo natangne nob kwiyeb, nubo mamki cakcakeu, nubo ma burokatiyeu, kakaa namiwo yodotiye.
LUK 18:12 Mimana kyak kiriti yob mor kume niber. Mine wineuti dorkwobberonin mordike mafiya.
LUK 18:13 Dila niwa yodiker dorertiyeu tiken kutan, ciyabo nacikun dorcedil, dila kwa cangeang cekoti titokiki, kwaama, ci bruini bwinimito, minni bwiranke.
LUK 18:14 Miyikombi, niwo yilaken loco fiyam cerke, kebo nawineu, cawo niwo kunderceri ciyatim yirau kico, lano niwo yiran kidor cero takeri ciyatin kumkenci.
LUK 18:15 Dila nubo bocinenti kibi beyo naci teici, kambo nob bwankacebo to yeuri cin werankci.
LUK 18:16 Dila yeecu cuoci fiye ciwiyeu, toki, “komdob bi beyo biduwartinimbo abou fiye niwiye, kom ywacire. Liyar kwaama na kalciroce.
LUK 18:17 Bilinke miyikomti. canowo yobo liyar kwaamaro bwebi duwari, mani cadoti”.
LUK 18:18 Kan'age dur nubere kan'nge mecoki nii meranka dike yoryore”, ye ma mati nsa fiya dume mankidike?
LUK 18:19 Yeecu ciyaco, “Yebwi mucoye ni madike yoryoretiye? Nikange mani womadike yoryoretiyo nobons kwaama win cardi.
LUK 18:20 Mwa nyimom werfudo-mare kayaka, twaldini, kure kwii, cwerde cwerke, ne Tee mwe kan'nge Nee mwe durko”.
LUK 18:21 Di liyawo yiki, minmamwo kwarub kikwama min bwebwoyileu”.
LUK 18:22 Kambo Yeecu nuwa nyeri, yico. Dikero win cwar kumwene. Miyem dike mucikeu kwarub, neken nubowe mancikeu, manfiya lo kwaama-ladina bou nwangmenten.”
LUK 18:23 Kambo nicuwaka nuwa dikero biromberi, kan'ngum nercerobicom, wori cinni cuweka kamboken.
LUK 18:24 Kambo Yeecu tonercoro kayommeri, lantoki, “An bwai nob cuwakab nidokin liyar kwaamar.
LUK 18:25 Atim yilam bwarinin naa Telemeko nadoken buwak bilifarak, kan'nge ni cuweka doken liyar kwaamar.”
LUK 18:26 Nubowa nuwa keroweu nyoki, “nokino nyori we abumtiye?”
LUK 18:27 Yeecu ciya, nike lambi kwannifireu, deker makar fiye kwaama nuyeu.”
LUK 18:28 La Bitru intokiki, “Nwo, nyin dubom dike nyicikeu kwarub nyin bwangtennen.”
LUK 18:29 Yeecu nyici, Biki cwom nikan'nge nani dob locuti, kakaa wice, kaka kebcebo, kakaa Teebcebo kakaa bibiyoloceu, ker liyar kwaamar.
LUK 18:30 Lamamica fiyati kiriti kiriti fo kalewenin, kan'nge dume diriye kalewo boutiyenin.
LUK 18:31 Kamboci mwerci kwocilombo yoberi, nyici, “Inno, biyakenti wurcalima, kwarub dikoro ci mulan'ngi dor bi bwe niner kan'nge kang nobtoman'ngeb dukumebeb atim dim.
LUK 18:32 Ciyar nekanco kan buboko yombo kwaamau, ci buwoco, cineco dofan'nge, citwomcinen bitom.
LUK 18:33 Ciyam malico, citwalumco, ankwenum ki kume taareu”.
LUK 18:34 Dilaciyom winwo mor dikerobirombonin, wori kerowo yuran'ngum yuran'nge fiyeciwiyeu, ci yomtenbo dikeci tokeu.
LUK 18:35 Kambo cidadom Jeriko, ri fukwa kan'nge inwo yimcun'nya nurek, kenkiniti,
LUK 18:36 kacinuwa kalinube cukentiyeri, lacinme nye bweitiye,
LUK 18:37 Yeecu Banazret cuken tiye.
LUK 18:38 Dila fukmau kundir kibikwan tokkero, “Yeecu, bibwe Dauda, Cibwini mito. Dala birombo kabeu werangco, ciyicoki kumwom.
LUK 18:39 Dila kunten diro kibi kwan kamboken inyiki, “Bibwe Dauda cibwini mito.
LUK 18:40 La Yeecu tim inyici ciyaboukico cinen. Kambo fukma bou bidomer, La Yeecu meco,
LUK 18:41 ye mu cwitin mamwene? “inyiki, Tee kwaama, micwitin tofiye.”
LUK 18:42 “Yeecu inyico, “yotoka fiyeko, bilinkemweu nirumnen.”
LUK 18:43 Wi dangjang fiya toka, kwangteng Yeecu, duktang kwaamati. Cito nyori, lanubo kwarub caklang kwaama.
LUK 19:1 Yeecu do yarico la cukenti morece.
LUK 19:2 Nikange wi deu cero zakka, dur nobo yo dortiye, nii cwika,
LUK 19:3 Con mani no co to keno we yecudi. La co dol bo toka wor, nobo durce, take con nii bi kwen.
LUK 19:4 Laco cukken kab ya con kwiken tii nyincin naco tom co, wori Yeecu acuwi fonure cuwonin.
LUK 19:5 Kambo Yeecu lau weyeri kung nuwe dii layico ki zakka yi rau wulom daten mwo da lomo.
LUK 19:6 La yilau wulumm-wulum yuwo co ki fuwor neret.
LUK 19:7 La gwam ciye cin to wori, ci ma fwennati ki, ya fura lo nii bwiranke.
LUK 19:8 Zakka kweni tii, ki to Teluwe, man. Kabkangum cweka miko more yob nane fuwa wine tana man yodiger nii cum wo ma yotiyeri, ma yila neti kiriti na'ar.
LUK 19:9 Yeecu yi coki duwen fuloka bou fo luwe wurini nii co bi bwe Ibrayim.
LUK 19:10 Bi bwe nii bo na do kange fuloka nobo leme.
LUK 19:11 Di di nuwe digewo digewo nyer. Con yoten coti tokki ki danke, wori co bi dom kange Urcalima. Cin tuken liyar kwamaro biyeken nawo.
LUK 19:12 La con yiciki nii dur cu bitine kange, ya ca yo liyar na co yilam.
LUK 19:13 Con co, cangace kwob, la yi ciki kom yila kangi, ko tiye kom miye nakom fiya mwen dorcet, mimale yilau.
LUK 19:14 La nobo loce ko co, cin twom nob bwiko cek ki manya ciya ti niwo a ca ciyar dor nyer.
LUK 19:15 La ci ne nii wo liyoro, kambo co bou lo weri co tomi ki ciya cucine ne congetini na co nyomom kiyemero co ne ciyeu ki ciya yila kalakangtiyeu.
LUK 19:16 Wi kabako be cinen ki Teluwe fam mwem bo we ma fiya mwen dorcet, fambo kwob.
LUK 19:17 Liya yi co ki dong dong canga ken, wuri mo, maken dor dike bi dure, man nenen tako cunnucut do kwob.
LUK 19:18 Na yobe ce bo yitiki fam mwembo Teluwe ma fiya mwembo fam bo nung.
LUK 19:19 Liya yicoki tom cunnukirning mwo tamciko.
LUK 19:20 Na taarece bo yitiki, fam mwembo wo man yo ken co yora mor kulene,
LUK 19:21 man nuwa tai mwe to, wori mor ni funere, moki to tike mo yobe, mo biye dige mo fii be.
LUK 19:22 Liya yi co ki ki ker mwer ma mamwer bo langtiye, mwo cange bwit mo nyomon moki mo man nii maki to re dike ma yobe,
LUK 19:23 ye bwi mo yobo ki kye miro fiye bini kiyeme no bwiko ma bori na yo co ki mwen.
LUK 19:24 Liya yi nobo tin wiye, kom yom fam bo co tan cike, kom niken niwo ki fam bo kwobbe.
LUK 19:25 Ciki Teluwe, wii ki fam bo kwob.
LUK 19:26 Miki niwo ki dikereri, cin yok cinen ten, niwo man cikeri an yom tangnin bo cine nen.
LUK 19:27 Ki nobo biro koki yilare liya ciye kom bo ki ci fiyemi wii na twallangum ci fo kami.
LUK 19:28 La kambo co to kan nyeri cui ken Urcelima.
LUK 19:29 Kambo cibo bidom kange Betafaji kange Betani dor bange ci coti ki zaitun, co tom nob bwangka coko nyo yob.
LUK 19:30 Yi ciki, kom ya cuinukur do wureno ka kome. No com yari kanto be gelba kange tekum we kom kwiu. Kom bou men ciko.
LUK 19:31 No nii kange me kom ki, 'Ye bwiyi kom kwi tiyeri? kom yi co ki teruwe cuitiye.
LUK 19:32 Nobo biro cu tom ciyeu yaci, fiya be gelba na wo Yeecu yiciyeu.
LUK 19:33 Kambo ci kwi be gelba tiyeri, nob gelba me ciki, ye bwi ci kwi gelba tiye?
LUK 19:34 Ciki teluwe cuii tiye.
LUK 19:35 Ci bo Yeecu nin ciko, cin miti kuleu ciye ro dor be gelba, co ci kun Yeecu ci yoti dorcere.
LUK 19:36 Kambo yaken tiyeri cimiten kulen ciyero ti dor nure
LUK 19:37 Di con dedom yirakako kong zaitun, la nob tomange ceu cin ter bilantumbo ci wab kwamati ki diro dur wori nangeu nyo mamka ci to we.
LUK 19:38 Bibwiyer lamiyo fiye liya wiyewo boti den Tere fuwor neret firen dii kwama kange yorkako wo na duk kakoce.
LUK 19:39 Kangum Fariciyawa mor nob mwe kanka nyico ki ni murangka kwanan nob bwingka mweko.
LUK 19:40 Yeecu yilci miyikum bi rin keti bwenteno nobo biro kumom di terentiyo ki bwiyici ciya bi lange
LUK 19:41 Fiya Yeecu bou bidomri la ci lam bero cori la com ciwiyeu dor cer
LUK 19:42 tok ki, waki kom nyomom dike abou ti ki furnare di dila cumom nuwi kime mani ka to ti.
LUK 19:43 Dila diye boli mwinen, wo nob ki Yeecu mwe, ciyan mu ki yalange kentangum nen, ciyan kwenang mwenten culang ko gwam.
LUK 19:44 Ciyan kun kom bitine wari kange bi beiyo lomwe. Mani ciya dob kange terti dor kecer wori mo kabo bati fiya kwama cwinco tiken nenen.
LUK 19:45 Yeecu do bicor wabe co la tir yuwanob miyankake,
LUK 19:46 yi ci ti ki mulangum mulange lomi a yila lo diko, kom yilam bwak nob kwiyeb.
LUK 19:47 Yeecu wi merang kang kang mor bikur waber. Dila dur wabero kange nob mulanka kange nobo dor noberoci cwiti na ci twallumco.
LUK 19:48 Di la ci fiya bo nor maka, wori nobo cuwati ti cinen kambo ken.
LUK 20:1 Kange diye Yeecu merangti mor bi kurwabe, la tok furen kereuti nubo wabereu kange nubo dur ko.
LUK 20:2 Ci tokeroti ciye coti yiyo kibi kwan kero wini mon mam nan do wotiye. We nenen bi gwamdo woo.
LUK 20:3 La co ciya ciki meki kero mangmekom tiye nyo.
LUK 20:4 kange yuka mwen Yohana yerau di kaka nii fire nenka?
LUK 20:5 Cin kobkanti, bwetici ciki tonou biki di kwamari anyiki yebwe bo nebo birinke cinenen.
LUK 20:6 Na la duwareu bi yi biki nifiro nendi no bo gwam cinye mobangbe ki ter, wori cin ciya mor mereciye Yohana nii to mange
LUK 20:7 Cin ciya ciki yombo keno ki no feri.
LUK 20:8 Yeecu yi ciki moken nyo mani yikamti keno kibo gwando wini ma man dike biromtiye.
LUK 20:9 Yi dubo danke wo kange nii yunkake inabi co ne kange nom tonen toka takeko conyaken bi ti ne kange ya daranyi kutangnyi.
LUK 20:10 Ki cwakiya bika bituweka ram cuii tom kange ceka ce ayo nob tone bone, beri naci neco mor dikero teige neneu. Di nob tonebo ci bunk, ci yoco kang koni.
LUK 20:11 Tom cenge ce tak ci bungco, cine co dotange, ci yweco kan koni.
LUK 20:12 Tomtange na ta'ar ce cin nuwacine der, cin merkeco kare.
LUK 20:13 La nii take Inabi ki, nye ina matiye? ma tom bi bweni macui.
LUK 20:14 Dila nob tone bo toco citokange bwitici, wo co nii coka gwarito bo twallum na kwalito yilam be.
LUK 20:15 Ci mwobken co bwiyim taken cin twallum co. Nyen teeluwen taken Inabi amaciticuke.
LUK 20:16 An bou na twallungum nob take bo wo na yila na neke nubo kenge takeu. Kambo ci nuwanyeri ciki, kwama acukum.
LUK 20:17 La Yeecu toci layiki.
LUK 20:18 Nii wo yar ti dor terero wonineri, an wurorangum. No nii wo tero yelti dorowonineri anfwoyok tamgum co.
LUK 20:19 Ci nob murangkako kange nobo dur waber cin cui naci tomco nawo wori an nyomom ki tokerewo dor ci, la ci cut an rubero.
LUK 20:20 Ci derangecoti cin tom nobo atoutiyeu wor ranyonri nubo weceke, na cifiya lentanke mor lekamor kercono ni, naci nekenco borank kange bi gwam nii dure.
LUK 20:21 Ci meco, ki Nii merangkan nyo yumom muki toka kange meranka dike donge donge tekeu kange nii men nawo dong bwinge kerdiye, muki merangka birin ket dor nure kwama.
LUK 20:22 Mino werfune ka no ya kemer dor kaicar, nin kaka o ong?
LUK 20:23 Yeecu nyomom yulkar yici.
LUK 20:24 Nugmen dinari wuro wee, takeu munranka we dor cereu? ciki, “ki kaicer dike na kaiceroce komne kwama dike na kwace?”
LUK 20:25 Nob murangka kange dur tini nob wabe bere cifiya bo diker bitore mur keu ceroni.
LUK 20:26 nubem. Cin nyemruki ki cuka kan cone, ci tobo kangeker.
LUK 20:27 Kam cadukiyawa cibo ficowege, nobo wo yitiki gwamka tuke mani.
LUK 20:28 Cin meco ciki “nii merangka” Musa mulang nye nen ki, no ni yiki no yini bwi yamdi, nii ki nawe la manki bibwe, nyice anan nawiye, afiya nyicenin bwe.
LUK 20:29 Kakum bi yiten wii niber wo kaboko nab nawe, lam bwe yam menki bwe,
LUK 20:30 Inyo wo yobeu.
LUK 20:31 Wo ta'ar naco, nyo tangka wo nibe re dombo bi beiwi kom cin bweyam.
LUK 20:32 Ki bwili na wiye bwimken.
LUK 20:33 Be diye gwanka duri, wiweco yira tiye. Wori cin nab na weye gwam ciye
LUK 20:34 Yeecu yiciki biberyo dor bi dinene nakangetiye, cine cine citi naka.
LUK 20:35 Nyo kallo wo abou tiyeu, nobo wuro ne bilenke na kwen ka ko ceci nabaruboci manki na ka nawiye.
LUK 20:36 Mani ciya bwi yatiki tok, ciya yilam na biwei tonange kwama.
LUK 20:37 Dila co lam bidom kang bange zaitunedo bei tomangeco lacin teer bi langkako ci cenk lang kwamati ki diro dur. Wori nagen yumankako co mane.
LUK 20:38 Ci ki bi bwiyet atinyo liyowo aboutin mor den tee bei furneret di kwama kanae yor ka la duntanka.
LUK 20:39 Kagum Faricawa bor mwerkanka ciyico ki nii merangka, kwameu nob bwankar mwekoninten.
LUK 20:40 Yeecu ciya ciki, miyikom bi len keti no noboburo kamom di terotinibo andunktange.
LUK 20:41 La Yeecu lambidom ka kange berocori la ciweyeu.
LUK 20:42 Naki kom nyom kakuwo kange dikewo abokimenti ki fawor neredi, naweu cin yurangum nuwe kume.
LUK 20:43 Kakuko we bo ti fiye kom wuyi wo nob kyeb kume bo a mu tiyak tiye, kentangum nen ciyam kwenang mwen ten, culangko gwam.
LUK 20:44 Cin kacimnen bitine wari kange biweiyo Lomewe, ma ciye tob tero kange dor kecer, wuro mo kabo bati fiya kwama cwiti na co fulone neu.
LUK 20:45 Yecu do mor bikurwabe la yuwa nob miyeka.
LUK 20:46 Yi citi ku mulangum mulange Lomi a yila fiye kwobka dilo, di la kom yilam buwak nob kwiyeb.
LUK 20:47 Yecu meranti kang kang mor bikurwaber nebo dor wabero kange nob mulankab kange nobo durko cwiti twallum co. Di la ci fiya bo nure, wori nobo cuwatci ti cinen kambo keu.
LUK 21:1 Yeecu, kun nuweri to nobo cuwe cuwe, buro mer luma mor bala yoka lumak.
LUK 21:2 To kange nawiye bune, fuyai mer aniniyoti yob mor.
LUK 21:3 Bilenke ma yi komti, nawiye bune, fuyai, meri la ciye gwam.
LUK 21:4 Gwam nobo wuro ne luma ciyeke mor cuweka ciye ko tenange nyeu. La nawiye fuyai bune, mor bune ce co merken kiyemer cero gwam, wo co cike.
LUK 21:5 Na wo kamenbo tok ker bikurwabe, kambo ci ma cimen bwayileneu ki tero keneu, neka luma.
LUK 21:6 Dike wo kom to tiye, kakuko wi boti wo tero mani a yito dor kecereu na wo mani a bubatiye.
LUK 21:7 La cin me co ki, Nii “Meranka, fiyan dike wo a bwitiye? Ye a yilam yitom ti na dike borombo na yoten na bwikari?
LUK 21:8 Yeecu ciya, ki kom ti ki bata, kari kange bol kom, diitce an bou mor dene mi, ci yi ti ki, “Man co”, na we dadom, kom bwang cinentende.
LUK 21:9 Tano kom nuwa ker kwenerdi kom kange dii bwali, kom cure, tamyo dike borombo a bwi bwiri, dila cwile mani a boiti nyo na wo.
LUK 21:10 Nyori con yi ci bero an kwenan bero ninten, liyar an kwenan liyaro ninteu.
LUK 21:11 An ma mukaka bitine ko wo tenang tenange fiye ki dimen ki dimen, take an ma wura kange wurolo. An maran yiromtaiyer kange yirombo dur dikwama.
LUK 21:12 Fiya na dike wuro gwam, ciyan tam kom, ci ne kom dotange, ciyan neken kom mor kurbiwaber kange loni furcuna, ciyan boki kom kabom liyare kange nobo durtinim ki ker denemir.
LUK 21:13 A yila kumen fiye ka tokom fulen miro tiye.
LUK 21:14 Ko to fo nerkumer, kom kade batito wo ya ko toktiye.
LUK 21:15 Mo ma nekom kero kange yilendo, wo nob kurome kume gwam, mani ciya dol kobkanka ti kange kome, kaka ci kim kerkume ro.
LUK 21:16 Kange Te, kange yitub, kange naniyak kange farub, ciyan kan kom, ci twallum kangem kumen.
LUK 21:17 Nobo gwam ciyan kokom kiker dene mi.
LUK 21:18 Yiri kume win wo mani a kwob ti,
LUK 21:19 Mor birum nekume kan fiyau dumetinim.
LUK 21:20 Tano kom to Urucalima kentangum ki nobo tee kwentiyeri kom nyomom yarka ceko dadom.
LUK 21:21 Nobo Yahudiya a cu ci yaken diyele kange, nobo tiber cinanlore ciya cu, ciya dobre nobo mwanlore ci dou mor.
LUK 21:22 Kakuko wo na yaka cunere ce, beri dike ci mulange gwam na dim.
LUK 21:23 Kwanci nubo ki fwereu kange nobe ne yir tiyeu mor kumetinwo! Annuwa dotange kambo ken wo tenang tenange bitinim. Ki funer fiye nobo wo wiye.
LUK 21:24 Ciyan yari ki caka kulener take a yaken ki ci canga bitine nin gwam, nobo manki kwama an duwarangum Urucalima ya ciko fiya nobo nyombo kwama ciye a dinitiye
LUK 21:25 Atan yirombo mor kakuke kange cwiyak, kange bitiren. Dorbitine tak nobo nyombo kwama cin nuwa dotange, fwer ciyero an burom temi dir mwenger wima.
LUK 21:26 No a fumom ki ten kange kwaka neret dike a bwi dorbitinero, min. An mok kibikwam dii kwamaro.
LUK 21:27 Nimde ciyan to bibwe Nifire bo ti mor bilore ki bi kwan kange. Duktankako dur.
LUK 21:28 Dila nimde dike wuro ci ter bwikari. Kweni timtiye, la kun dor kumero dii, wori fuloka kumeko dadom.
LUK 21:29 Yeecu ne dangke, “To tii nyencen do kange tiini gwam.
LUK 21:30 Na ci ter fu ka laluko, kan tom ki bwikom, komki Tirakko dadom tak.
LUK 21:31 Nyo tano kom to dike wuro ter bwikakori, kom nyomom liyar kwamaro dadom.
LUK 21:32 Bilenke ma yi kom ti kaldo wo mani a cuti, dike wuro an bwi gwam.
LUK 21:33 Dii kok kange bitini an cum dila kermiro mani a cuti.
LUK 21:34 Di kom kom ka bati ki dor kume, kati kom ne nerkumero tutum ki kwomka dorbitinero kange norangka, kange komka kwarcek. Dila kakuko an bo bati man.
LUK 21:35 Mwinin cito. Dila an bo dor nober gwam wo kwarce tikob dor bitinero nin gwam.
LUK 21:36 Dila kom yi ki bati kang kang, kom kwob diloti bena kom fiya bi kwam do ka torum dike woti gwam a bwitiye, kange kambo katimti kabum Bibwe Nifire”.
LUK 21:37 Ki kakuk, ki merangi mor bikurwabe, kume del yakenti bang ci cotiki zaitune.
LUK 21:38 Nobo gwam tura yaka fiye co wiyeki bwiri cin nowa co bikur waber.
LUK 22:1 Na wo nyori, duklume ma ci ca cari to yoten diker kunkar wiyeu, ci cuwoti yabkau dadom.
LUK 22:2 Liyab wabebo kange nob mulangkabo, cin mwerkan dor, na ci fiya ci twalum Yeecu, La ci nuwa tai nibeti.
LUK 22:3 La bwekelkele dokenmor Yahuda Iccariyati, wo wiin mor kwob culombo yobeu.
LUK 22:4 Yahuda ya Liyab wabebo kange nabarub kwenebo nin, cin tokkangi kambo ca miyam Yeecu ti cineneu.
LUK 22:5 Cin bilangi, takeu cin ciya ciyan ne co kyemer.
LUK 22:6 Con ciya, La co do nurewo ca nekeng co ti cinen neu wo kebo tiber nubereu.
LUK 22:7 
LUK 22:8 Nyori Yecu twom Bituru kange yuwana, yici ti, “kom ya ko ka bati cari yabka ko, wo ba catiye.
LUK 22:9 Cin yii co, “Fee mu cwiti nyo ka bati cuwe?”
LUK 22:10 Con ciya ci, “to no kom doken cinar lor di, kange wabkan nii kangetum ki tabwir mwenger, ko bwanten co luwe ca domtiye.
LUK 22:11 “Ko yii nii luwe kom ki, “nii meranka yinen “fe ku fabubeu, fiye ma cam cari ti kange bi bei tomange me?”
LUK 22:12 Can nung kimen kuwe dur ywelum ywela dii. Kom ka batiyo wi.
LUK 22:13 La cin ya, cin fiya dong-dong na wo co yii ciye, cin kam bati cari yabkako.
LUK 22:14 Fiya ca ka cariko lam, con yiken kange bi bei tomange ceu.
LUK 22:15 Con yii ci, “mi dilanti ducce nan ca corito wo kange kom, nyim re nan nuwa, dotange.
LUK 22:16 min yi kom, “ma ma cati tak yaken ciko bi diye Liyar kwama a dim tiye.
LUK 22:17 Yeecu tu kweleu, bwikoko ca ne buka kange ri, cin tiki, “tu wo na kom tikangum bwiti kime.
LUK 22:18 Min yi kom man ma no mwem bi tutti ti tak yaken ciko bi diye Liyar kwamaro a boutiye,
LUK 22:19 Yeecu tu carito bwiko ca bu kange ri con wulangum cin neci, yi ci ti, “wo bwimi ci ne komme, ko ma wo na bulanka mi ko ce.
LUK 22:20 Cin tu kweleu bwiko cariko, con toki, “kwele wo na norro fwir ceu, bwiyale mi wo ci a corti ker kimereu.
LUK 22:21 Dii ko ti yora, kang niwo ko a miye, ye tiye wii kange mo fiye caka cari.
LUK 22:22 Bi bwe nifire an cu na wo ci yowe. La kwannen mo nii wo ma miye tiyeu.
LUK 22:23 La cin yoten ci ti tokkangi bwitici we nii curo a miye co tiye.
LUK 22:24 Kwalkange kwenu more ciye dor, we nii na dure.
LUK 22:25 Con yi ci, Liyab nubo nyombo kwama, teluwe dor cir kange buro ki bi kwang kere dor cireu, ciki cuwo ci ki nubo ma dikero keng tiye.
LUK 22:26 Mani a yilati nyo kange kom, nyori nii wo na dur more kime ri a yilam bwe biduware, kange nii wo yori La gwammeu, a yilam canga.
LUK 22:27 Nyori wo na dur gwammeu, co ci yime kaka na wo canga makimen nangen tiye?
LUK 22:28 Kimeu kom kange mo, cuwa mik.
LUK 22:29 Min yoti kom dor liyarek na wo temi yoti ye dor Liyareu,
LUK 22:30 na ko ca, nako no kange mo, mor Liyare mi, kom yi kutile dumbo kwob culombo yob wo Iciraila ceu.
LUK 22:31 Siman, siman, bulangi, Bwekelkele do a neco mo, na co kwom nen na bi kate.
LUK 22:32 Min kwob mwen dilo bilenkere mwe a yarde, no mo yilau tak ri, ne keb mwebo be kwamer.
LUK 22:33 Bituru yi co, “teluwe min kam bati man ya kange mo Fucina kange bwar.
LUK 22:34 Yeecu yi co, “min yii neng Bituru, fiya na bicake mob kiyange ri, mwan ko nyomka mik kiriti taar.
LUK 22:35 La Yeecu yi ci, “Fiyo cuwo ma twom kom, man ki Liinge, cwaye kime kange tau, ye ka fiya be? Cin ciya co, “Mani”
LUK 22:36 La con yi ci, “caneko, wo ki cwaye kimere ca tu, kange cwaye kulene. Wo man ki yari ca miyem belle ce ca tiyenu.
LUK 22:37 Mi yii komti, “dike mulangum dor mire an dim.
LUK 22:38 La cin yi co ki, “teluwe, to kero kange wo yob”. Con yi ci, “La dim”.
LUK 22:39 Yecu cu bang zaitun na wo ciki mare, bi bei tomange ce bwanten co.
LUK 22:40 La ci Lamri, Yecu yi ci, “kom kwob dilo kati kom doken mor cuwaka.
LUK 22:41 Con dubam ci kutanbo yora, con cunken bitine, kwob dilo,
LUK 22:42 ki. “Te no mun ciya ri, tum kwele wo minen, kebo cwika mik, womweu a mani.
LUK 22:43 La bi bwe tomange kwama wusake cerkangu dii cinen, neco bikwanti.
LUK 22:44 La co mor dotange dur, con yokten kwobka diloko, La mukti cero yilam na bwiyale yaru ti bitine.
LUK 22:45 La con kwenu fiye kwobka diloko nin, con yilaken fiye bi bei tomange ce nin. Co fiya ci da dumti wori ciki fir neret.
LUK 22:46 Con me ci, “Ye bwi ki da dumtiye? Ko kwen ko kwob dilo kati kom doken mor cuwala.
LUK 22:47 Co tok kero ti wiri, nubo ducce cerkangu kange Yahuda, wiin mor kwob culombo yobe ti cinen kaba. Con bou bidom kange Yecu con korkan co.
LUK 22:48 La Yecu yi co “Yahuda, muki miye bi bwe nifire ki kor kanka ka?”
LUK 22:49 La nubo woro wari kange Yecu to dike wo bwitiye ri, cii ki, “teluwe nyo to ci ki kuleng ka?”
LUK 22:50 La wiin more ciye to canga liya wabe, to cewo caktiyereu mwatam.
LUK 22:51 Yecu ki, “Cuwati nyo”, con ke tu ceu, nyori twam”.
LUK 22:52 Yecu yi liya nob wabe kange nubo durko bi kur kwamareu kange nubo durko ci ciya co beu, 'ki, ka ceru ki kulenti kange danti ka ta nii kuye ka?
LUK 22:53 Fiya cuwa mika kom kang-kang mor bi kur kwama reu ka yo bo kang minen. Wo kakuk kimek, kange bikwan kumtacile.
LUK 22:54 Cin tam co, cin yaken ki co Lo nii wabe durko. Bituru bwen cinen ti kutang.
LUK 22:55 Biko ci kwerum kira tiber lor bolange reu, cin cin yironken yiye, Bituru yiken tiber ciyer.
LUK 22:56 Kange nawiye canga to co, wori ci yim cunga kirak, con to co ti con toki, “Nii wuro wii kange co”.
LUK 22:57 La Bituru webkangum, ki nawiye ma nyom cobo.
LUK 22:58 Bi cor di, kange to co, yi ki. “Mo wiin more ciye” Bituru ki “bwayile, ma kebo”
LUK 22:59 Bwiko kene wiineu, kange ywim metenco, “Bilenke, nii wo wii kange co.
LUK 22:60 Bituru ki, nii man nyom bo dike mo tok tiye”, dancan ca dibo tokka kereko bar bi cake mob kiyange.
LUK 22:61 Teluwe, yila to Bituru, La Bituru kwa ki kero Yecu yi ceu, fiya cuwo ci wariyeu, “Fiya na bi cake mob kiyange duwen ri, mwan wengkan ye kiriti taar.
LUK 22:62 Bituru yaken kale cii wiye kambo ken.
LUK 22:63 La nubo ci yo to Yecu tiye buwo malli co.
LUK 22:64 Kambo fini celtiye ri, nubo dur nibero mwerkangi fiye wiin, Liya nob wabe bo kange nob mulangkab, cin doken kico fiye nyime ciye, ciki, “no mo kiritti di yi nyo”
LUK 22:65 La con yi ci, “no nyikom di mani ka ciyati”,
LUK 22:66 Kakaa me kom di kan kar men ti.
LUK 22:67 Min yi ki no mwo Krisiti ri yi nyo, La con yi ci ki “No yi komri mani ka yonmti.
LUK 22:68 Tano mwe kom kerdi mani ka yiye ti
LUK 22:69 Fo ya ciko kab, mi bwe nifire an yiken kanko caktiyer kwama.
LUK 22:70 La gwam ciye cin yi co ki, mo bi bwe kwama ka? Yecu kar cinen “Kom ka tiki nye”.
LUK 22:71 La cin toki, “ye bwi ba do kange warke tiye? Bo ki bwibi ban nuwa nyi co”
LUK 23:1 La mwer kanka ceko gwam kweri cin bouki Yecu kabum Bilatu.
LUK 23:2 Cin teri ci mwel cinen ti, ciki, “nyim fiya nii wo lentang ti ki bi tineu beu, ywam neka dorek ti kaicar nin la ciki toki ciki “Co ki bwico cin kiritti, Liyau”
LUK 23:3 Bilatu me co, ki “Mo liya Yahuda wa ka?” Yecu ciya cinen ciki “mwi tok nyo”
LUK 23:4 Bilatu yi nob wabebo, dortinibo kange mwer kange kako ducce, “Ma fiyabo bwirang ke nii wonin.
LUK 23:5 Dila ciin tii tokkako ciiki, ci kung nubo nin neer ti, ciki merangi mor Yahuda gwam tabti Galili bou ciki fiye wo nin.
LUK 23:6 La kambo Bilatu nuwa weri, cin me keno Yecu nii Galili ri,
LUK 23:7 kambo ci nyimonki Yecu ki no biten liyare Bilatu weri cin tungken Yecu Bilatu nin, wo ki bwiico yim mor Urucalima ki kumeni curo weu.
LUK 23:8 Fiyawo Hiridu to Yecu, cin bilangi wori ci cui, toka Yecu ti ki kwitangka. Cin nuwa ker dorcerla ci cuiti naci to diker nyimankako Yecu ma tiye.
LUK 23:9 Hiridu merang Yecu kero kila kila dila Yecu karci nen bo ker.
LUK 23:10 Nob wale bo durtini kange nob mulangkabo tii, mwelco ti kibi kwam.
LUK 23:11 Hiridu kange nob kweneb ceko torang Yecu, yila ci buo co. La cin du dinen kwilen do yor yore ricin yilaken kico Bilatu nin.
LUK 23:12 La Hiridu kange Bilatu yilam bifarak ki diye curo, no cin nob kiyeb bwitici.
LUK 23:13 Bilatu la cou nob wabeb durtimbo kange nob liyare bo wari kange nubo duce.
LUK 23:14 La cin yi ci, “Kom bo men ki nii wo na nii lentangti ki nube, la kom to, min merangco kakom ri mi fiya bo bwiranke cinen dor diker wo kom mwelcinen tiyeu
LUK 23:15 Mani, Hiridu ken yila binen ki co, la koto, kange diker mani wo nii wo mani lam bwere.
LUK 23:16 La man macinen bi mwerum nami nyem kang cinen”.
LUK 23:17 La nanger Bilatu na cok Yahuda wa nin nii wiin ki duk lume.
LUK 23:18 Dila gwamce cin kung diiro cuko wiin “ko cu ki nii wo, na ko cok nyinen Barabbal.
LUK 23:19 Barabba nii wo ci dok ken Fucina ki kungka kiyana cinanlor kange twalka nobek.
LUK 23:20 Bilatu yiki ker tak, nui ti naci nyengun kang Yecu.
LUK 23:21 Dila cin kung diro, ciki “kulken co, kulken co”.
LUK 23:22 Cin yici tanre ceu, “Ye bwiye, dikero bwirko wuni nii wo man? ma fiya bo bwiranke wo lam bware cinen. La kambo mi macinen bi mwerume ri man nyengum kang cinen”
LUK 23:23 La cin titen ki duro dur cii cuito na kulken co. Diir cero dok Bilatu ciyaka.
LUK 23:24 La Bilatu ciya kini cero,
LUK 23:25 ciin nyengum kang wo ci meu nin, wo ci dok ken fucina ki kungka kiyancek kange twalka nubeke. Dila cin neken Yecu ki cuika ceko.
LUK 23:26 Kambo ci yaken ti kice ri, cin tam nii kange ciman wo kwane, ci ceru cinan lor, dila cin yo cinen ti kwoblom bwatiyem bo duncer, ci bwangten Yecu.
LUK 23:27 Mwerka nube ko duce kange wo natubo ceu wo ii co Hiridu, ma kang bwaa ti dor cereu.
LUK 23:28 Dila cin yila cinen di, Yecu yiki, “Bi wutobo Urucalima, kom cire wiye dor miirm dila kom cii wiye dor kumer kange dor bibeyo lakumeu.
LUK 23:29 La kom to, kumeni ber wo ciya tok ti ki, “Bi bwiyer ki nubo burombo combulome kange burom bo ci nom bo yiir cero wiyeu.
LUK 23:30 La ciya teri ci yi bangtini ko ti, “Yaru dor nyer' kange dunletini, cumom nyo.
LUK 23:31 La no ci yan ma dikero buroki kwama wo tiyo yibereri, ye a bwi tiye no ci kwicimri?”
LUK 23:32 Nubo kangem bo, nob bwirankereb yob cin yaken kici kange co naci twalci wari.
LUK 23:33 Ki kwama wo ci bou fiye ci cuo ti ki “Kwace duce” wi ci kui co kange nob bwirangkebo yobeu wiin kanko catiyer cer la wiin mok ceko nin.
LUK 23:34 Yecu yi ki, “kwama, yabcinen wori, ci nyombo dike ci ma tiyeu”. La ciin mer dacen, ciin tikangum belle ceu.
LUK 23:35 Nubo tirangum ki toi kambo liyab cebo buwo co ti ken ki “cin cer kangeribo. Ca cer dur cero no cin kiritti kwama, wo ci cokke ri!”
LUK 23:36 Nob kwenebo nung co ken, bouti cinen, cine co mwembo fuwar ti,
LUK 23:37 ciki toki ki “No mo liya Yahudawari cer dor mwero”.
LUK 23:38 La yirome wi dor ceer, “Wo co liya Yahudawa”.
LUK 23:39 Wiin mor nob bwirangke wo ci kulken ci wari yeu to co ki “Mwi kebo kiritti ya? cer dor mwero kange nyo”.
LUK 23:40 Dila wincu werank co, ki, “Mani mwi cua tai kwama, kambo mwi mor bolang bwarek ko dong-dong kange ca?
LUK 23:41 Be bifo weu dong-dong, wori bi ki yo diker date kange dike bi mane. Dila nii wo mabo dikero kange yorbe”
LUK 23:42 La coki, “Yecu, kwi kimo no miw bou mor liyar mwek ri
LUK 23:43 Yecu yi co ki “Bilenke ma yinenti, duwen mwan yi kange mo mor dii kwama”.
LUK 23:44 La ki kwama wo kan kene ko nukkune, la kumta ciliu cumom dor bitinero gwam yaken cuko kang kene ko teer,
LUK 23:45 kambo meu dome ri, yilanko mor bikur kwama re woran more yob.
LUK 23:46 Ki wiye ki diro dur Yecu yiki, “Te, min neken dumemi kang mwek”, kambo ci tok we ri, cin bwiyam.
LUK 23:47 La kambo nii dur nob kwenebe to diker maneri cin duktang kwama, ciki, “bicom, wo nii cak-cake”.
LUK 23:48 Ki kwama mwer kangka nobo duce wo bou na ci to dikero bi mane ri, cin yilaken ci kwa cang-cang ti.
LUK 23:49 Dila nubo gwam wo nyumom ce, kange natubo bwangu co Galili yeu, cin tim kutan, cii to dikero buroti.
LUK 23:50 La nii kange wi dendo ki Yucufu, wo wii mor nobo dure. Cin nii ken, ri cin nii cak-cake.
LUK 23:51 Nii wo ciyabo kange dikero ci fuwa kangeu kakaa dikero ci mancu. Ci ceru Arimatiya, bi ten Yahuda, la ciki nintang liyar kwamak.
LUK 23:52 Nii wo, ya Bilatu nin, la cin keni na neco curen bwi Yecu.
LUK 23:53 Cin cuku, cin cumon ki yilank linin ko ken. La cin yoken mor tuwe wo ci cuwe cuwe mor tere, wo ci fwerum bo nii wi yeu.
LUK 23:54 Kakuko co kakuk ywelkak, la kakuk fobka Yahudawa ko dadum.
LUK 23:55 Natubo wo bou kange Yecu Galili ye bwangten lacintom tuweu. Kange kambo ci yom bwi ceu.
LUK 23:56 Cin yilaken la cin ywellang kwilendo Ficange kange nuwang. La ki diye fobka Yahudawak ri cin fubom nawo werfundo to keu
LUK 24:1 Ki kwomje kikume kume niberece cin bo tuwenim, cinbouki kulen tuika kuneko ficang ficang woci ywelleu.
LUK 24:2 Ci fiya tero tun ken tunngen cunge tuwek.
LUK 24:3 Cin doken morece, dilaci fiyabo bwi Yeecu.
LUK 24:4 Inbwiu kambo cimor kwobtangka dikekebwiuweri, nubo yob tirarim kabumci ki kulendo fuwe cukcukke.
LUK 24:5 La natubowo cunken ki dorciro bitine worintai, cin yo natuno, “yebwi komdo nikidumeti nor buware?
LUK 24:6 Manifo lan kwennum! kambo ci yimko ker ki kwamawo ci Galili, intoki,
LUK 24:7 ciyan nekan bi bwe niffire kang nob bwiran keb la ciyan yei kenco, kikume taare ankwenumtak”.
LUK 24:8 La natubo kwaki kercero!
LUK 24:9 Lacin dubom tuweu cin yilakeng laciyi kwobculombo winneuwuro dekero birombo kanngu tangneu gwamm.
LUK 24:10 Maryamu magdaliya, yuwana, Maryamu ne Yakubu, kan'nge tangne natubo ci wariyeu cine nob toman'ngeb cebo fulen dikorowuro bwiyeu.
LUK 24:11 Dila nobtoman'ngebcebo tu kero muni kebo diker maka nangenek, dila cinebo bilinke natubowonin.
LUK 24:12 Kwarub kan'nge wo Bituru kweni, cwayya tuwenin, cunken torang moreuti, lacinto lalanggo fuworgo kikwace. Lana nyime Bituru yaken loco, lata nyimang di bweweuti.
LUK 24:13 Kikakucori, inwonyo yob wo more yakanti cinarloro kan'nge dende Imawu wuro kutankaceko nan.
LUK 24:14 Citi fuwakan'ngi ko bwitici kangediwo yaa bwiweu.
LUK 24:15 Yilam kambo ci fuwakamti wari kange meka kerekeri, Yeecu ki bwico boubidom cinen yakenti kanyeci.
LUK 24:16 La nuweceu dolbo nyobkaceko.
LUK 24:17 “Yeecu yici, inye kom tokkerti dorcere kambo kom yakentiyeu?” Cintinwifiyeco laci cii bwatumbotiwi.
LUK 24:18 Kaci tun kan'nge morece nendo kiliyobac, lan ciya cinen, “Mwowin cwar niwo Wurcalima wo nyombo dike birombo bwiuwe firen kikabake ki kumenicuo?
LUK 24:19 Yeecu yico, “bikulentito wini?” Cin ciyaco, dikerotin kan'nge Yeecu bwe Nazaret, wuro buwe tomanye, woki dikerotinimbo dur, kan'nge kertinimbo dur fiye kwama wiyeu kan'nge nob.
LUK 24:20 Ki ciyaka nob wabero dur kan'nge nob li yareb nyebo ci nekenco naci warco naci kulkentencotak.
LUK 24:21 Dila nyin yoner nyiki cowo a cer Icerelatiyeu. Nyo, nobo nawori, naweu kume Taar dikero birombo bwiuwe.
LUK 24:22 Dila aa di duweno kowo, kamnyum natubembo nyi wariyeu ma nyinen diker nyimankartinim, ki yancimbo tuwe kiburiceu.
LUK 24:23 Kambo ci fiyabo bwiceri, cinbom, ciki cikeneu cinto dukum nobtomanyebo burombo yici ki wi kedume.
LUK 24:24 Kannyum nabarob wuro wari kannye nyeu cinya tuwenin, yafi kwabti nawo natubo tokeu. Dila ci tocibo.
LUK 24:25 Yeecu yici ki, “Kom nob kuleneb nubo nebo bilinke dor dikero nob tomanyeb dukumebo tokeu!
LUK 24:26 Yilabokang kiritti anuwa dotannge dikero biromba, laken mor duktang kaka?”
LUK 24:27 Dila kikab wi mucanim yaken ciko nobtoma'ngobonin kwarub. Yeecu futang cinen dikero kaminge co. Wibe fumertinimbonin gwamm.
LUK 24:28 Kambo cilam cinar loroce fiye ci yakenti wuyeri cabunane Yeecu maa nadike muncan cuken.
LUK 24:29 Dila cin dokco ki, “yiken kan'ngeci, wori wori meu dadom kakuko do dikati. “La Yeecu ya yiken kan'nge ci.
LUK 24:30 Bwiuki, kambo ciyiken ci naci cacarite, intu Tiilita, kambo ci yoten bibuyer wiyeri, kiyannyi, lanneci.
LUK 24:31 Lamwo nuweceu wumwom, kambo cinyimocin ciri, lalem kaci,
LUK 24:32 Cin yi butice, wendi mani twirangbobo mornerber, kambo citok keroti kan'ngebo dor nurereu, kambo ci wombinen bifumertinnimbeu?”
LUK 24:33 Lacin kweni ki kwamaco, cin yiken wurcalima. Cinfiya culombo wineuwo wari, kan'nge birombo ciwari kan'nge ciyeu,
LUK 24:34 “Ki, kibicom kwama kwenum, inbow cimanin”.
LUK 24:35 Laci tok dikero birombo bwiu nureu, kan'nge kambo ci fwetang cinen Yeecu kambo kiyan Tilita.
LUK 24:36 Kambo citikang dikerobirombo tiyeri, dila Yeecun tii tibercir, dilla yici, “fuwer nerer kumer”.
LUK 24:37 Dilla cin fakla cin dimkitani, cikwatiri cin tom wulo.
LUK 24:38 Yeecu yiciki yebwi kom kwomdortiye? yebiro meke kunouti morner kumere?
LUK 24:39 To kanimiu kan'nge Nanimiu, la muo kan'nye muo. Teiye nakomto. Wulo manki bwi kan'nge yiri, kambo komto nicikeu”.
LUK 24:40 Kamboci tokweri, lacin nung cinen kaniceu kan'nge naniceu.
LUK 24:41 Kamboci dimki fuwer nerereu, kan'nge nyimanka, Yeecu yici, “Komwiki kan'nge cariya?”
LUK 24:42 Lacin neco jinnge belumbeleu.
LUK 24:43 Yeecunyo cam kabumcim.
LUK 24:44 Lanyici, “Kambo miwari kan'nge komeu minyikom miki gwamm nike cimuleng wertun mucar kan'nge nentomanngeb kan'nge zaburau atin dii kang”.
LUK 24:45 Lacin wumwum nerciro naci nyimwom bifumertininbo.
LUK 24:46 Yici, “mulangum mulannge, kiritti annuwa dotange, amkwenum an kwenum tuwe ki kume taare.
LUK 24:47 Komwab dencero kan'nge dobka bwirang kerer mor denece gwamm mor nube, komteri wurucalima.
LUK 24:48 Kom nobwarib dikero birombo.
LUK 24:49 Too, mi twomutiki nor Teemiro dor kumer. Dila kom cini bitinece, catin tunkumen bikwan firen dii.”
LUK 24:50 Lananyime Yeecu yaken wari kna'nyeci yaa cilam Betani. Lankun kanceko yocimeti bibwiyerwi.
LUK 24:51 Yilam kamboci yocinten bibwi yerotiyeri, dubomci lacim tumco cin yakenkico dikwama.
LUK 24:52 Lacin wabco, cin yilarangum wurucalima kifuwor nerer ducce.
LUK 24:53 Kicatec cimor lokwama cine dencore bibwiyerti.
JOH 1:1 ki kaba kero wii, lakero co kino kange kwama, la kero co kwama
JOH 1:2 co wuro kange kwama ki kaba
JOH 1:3 dikero gulam kebo ci nen la dikero kange mani wo ci mani kebo ci ne ne.
JOH 1:4 dumi kino cinen, la dume cuo co filank nubo ko gwam
JOH 1:5 filanko weni mor kumta cili, la kumta cili labo bi kwan cero.
JOH 1:6 nii kange wi kwama tomu we, wo dencero Yohanna.
JOH 1:7 ci bou naci war kedor filangeronin lana nubo gwam na ne bilengke ki warke ceu.
JOH 1:8 Yohanna kebo filanko, la ci bou ri naci ne karke dor filankero nin
JOH 1:9 filanko kendo, wo ne nubo gwam filangeu, bou ti dor bi tiner.
JOH 1:10 cin wi dor bitiner, cii ma dor bitinero cinen la dor bitinero nyom co bo.
JOH 1:11 cin bow wo cee nin di, wo ceu yõ co bo.
JOH 1:12 dila gwam wo yoceri, wo ne bilenke ki dencereri, cin ciya cinen cii a yilam bi bei kwama
JOH 1:13 buro ci ka bo ci kebe ki bwiyele kaka a ki cii ka bwiyek kaka cui ka niik la ki cui ka kwama
JOH 1:14 kero wo yimla bwi la yi kange bo. bin tom duktanga ceko, duktanga nawo wiin cuar bow kwamanine, diin ki lima kange bilen ke.
JOH 1:15 Yohanna ne warke dorcerla toki kibi kwan ki “wo co wo mitok ker dorcer miki “cuo wo bou bwikom mikeu laye dwika la cin beken ten minen.”'
JOH 1:16 wori mor diika ceko gwambe bin yo luma dor lumar.
JOH 1:17 la werfundo bou kang mucak. luma kange bilenkeu bou kang Yeecu kiritti.
JOH 1:18 kange man wo tom kwama wiye, kwama wiin cuar wo yim cunga tee, la cin nung binen kwama
JOH 1:19 won co werka Yohanna, ki kwama Yahudawa mor Urucalima tuom nob wabeb kange lewiyawa cinen naci me co “mwin we?”
JOH 1:20 cin toki, ci cuerbo cuerke, la cin tok bilenke “mi kebo kiritti.” ciki, “mi kebo” cii ki, mo nii tomange dukume?” cin “o-ong”
JOH 1:22 la cin yico ki mwin we, la nanyi fiyam dike nyi yi nubo tuomou nye ti? mwiki tok mwiki ye dor mwer?”
JOH 1:23 ciki “min diir, cuo bi cuor ti mor yere, kom ywelum nure kwama ciyer, dong-dong nawo kaya nii tomange dukumeu tokeu.”
JOH 1:24 ciin tom kangenbo mor nob dinglingeb,
JOH 1:25 la cin me co, ri cin yi coki, “yebwi mwi yu mwem tiye no mwi kebo kiritti kakaa, Iliya kakaa nii tomange dukumeri?”
JOH 1:26 Yohanna ciya cinen ki miki yu mwembo ki mweb. dila kange wi tim more kume wo kom yom beu
JOH 1:27 co wo bou bwi miyeu, duka taceko mi labon kwi.
JOH 1:28 ci ma dike buro baitanya dinge urdun ne wi neu, fiye Yohanna yum mwembo tiyeu.
JOH 1:29 cyel fini ceri Yohanna to Yeecu bou ti cinen la ciki, “to, be kweme kwama wiren wo tunm bwirnan ker dor bitineu.
JOH 1:30 co wo mi yi kom miki, wo bou bwikob mike laye, wori ciki no kabum minin
JOH 1:31 mi nyom co bo, la na nung Iciraila nin co, mibou mi yu mwem kwamambo tiki mweme.
JOH 1:32 Yohanna ne werke ki min to yuwa tangbeko yirauti dii kwama na nagumfe ri yi ken dor cer.
JOH 1:33 mi nyom cobo, dila cuo wo tom ye ki yu mwem kwamambo ki mwemeu yi ye ki, dor nii woro mwi to yuwa tangbeko a yirauti na yitiyeri, cou wo ayu mwem kwamambo tiki yuwa tangbeke
JOH 1:34 min tom ri. min ne werke wo bi bwe kwama.”
JOH 1:35 tak, ki cel fini, kambo Yohanna tim kange yob mor kwanka ceke,
JOH 1:36 cin to Yeecu cuken ti, dila Yohanna ki to, be kwame kwama,”
JOH 1:37 nob bwankab ceko yobeu nuwam dila ci toke la cin bwangten. Yeecu
JOH 1:38 la Yeecu yila nuwe to cii bwang cinen ten firi ci ki “ye ko cuii tiye?” cin ciya co, “rabbi (wo no yila kangum ri co “nii merangka”), “mwi ki da fe?”
JOH 1:39 cin yici, “kom bou nako to,” la cin bow cin to fiye ci dam tiyeu, cin dam wi kange co ka kuko cou la darum kange kang kenekko teer.
JOH 1:40 wiin mor nubo yobeu wo nuwa Yohanna tok ker di bwangten Yeecu, andiranwuc yi cimon Bitruc.
JOH 1:41 cin terri ci fiyan kece Bitruc la yi co ki” nyin fiyam Almacihu (wo no yilangum ri co; kiritti)
JOH 1:42 cin bou ki co Yeecu nin, la Yeecu to cori ki “mwin ci monbi bwe Yohanna. ci ya co nen ki Kefac “(no yila kangumri Bitruc)”
JOH 1:43 ciel fini ce ki kwama wo Yeecu cui naci cu cielili, cin fiya Filibuc lanyi co ki, “bwang menten.”
JOH 1:44 la Filibuc ceru'u Batcaida, cinan lor Andrawuc kange Bitruc.
JOH 1:45 Filibuc fiya Natana'ilu yi coki, “co wo muca mulangi dor cer mur werfuneu, kange nob tomangeb dukumere, nyim fyam co, Yeecu bi bwe Yucufu wo Nazaret.”
JOH 1:46 Nataniyelyi co ki dikero ken antin ceru mor Nazaret ka? “Filibu yico, “bou na to.”
JOH 1:47 Yeecu to Nataniyel yauti cinen la tok ker dor cer “to nii Iciraila kendo, wo cuwer ke mani cineneu.”
JOH 1:48 Nataniyel yico “ma nyi mwi nyimom yere?” Yeecu ciya co la yico, na nyimde Filibuc co nen ki kwama wo mwi yim dimer tiir nying cine min tom nen.”
JOH 1:49 Nataniyel ciya cinen, nii merangka mwibi bwe kwama mo liya Iciraila “
JOH 1:50 Yeecu ciya lan yico, wori min yi nen miki min tom nen dimer tiir nying cin, mwi ne bilenke? mwanto dikero dur tini la weu.”
JOH 1:51 la cin yici ciki bilenke, mi yi komti, kom to dii kwama wumom la nob tomangeb kwama ki kwii ki yirai dor bi bwe nii fire.”
JOH 2:1 kanbo kume ta'ar cuineri, naakak wii mor kana wo Galili la nee Yeecu wi wi.
JOH 2:2 la cin yi Yeecu kange nob bwangka cebo naci fiya yaki ken
JOH 2:3 kanbo mwem Inabi dimmeri, nee Yeecu yi co ki “ci manki mwem Inabim.”
JOH 2:4 Yeecu yi co ki, nawiye, ye bwi mwi bou minene? kwama mi la bo bwirin”
JOH 2:5 nee ce yi canga tininbo ki “bwen no ye ci kom meri, ko mani
JOH 2:6 la cir mwenge tereko wi nyo nukkun wo Yahudawa ki manade nangen ciko wo niir kako wuccake ci le rum makake, cikin tuum nyo ceer leer ro kwob-kwob gwance
JOH 2:7 Yeecu yii ci, “ko dirongum ceer mwengero buro ki mwem “la cin diirongum cuko mer-med
JOH 2:8 la cin yi canga tinimbo, “ko bwi naweu ya ki nee duur cika ro la cin bwengten wo yilam mwem Inabi ye, dila ci nyom bo fiye ci bow cikeu (dila cangatinimbo buro tuwau mwembe nyumom). la cin cou nii na nawiyeu
JOH 2:9 la duur cikaro twi bwembo wo yilan mwem Inabi ye, dila ci nyom bo fiye ci bow cikeru (dila cangatinimbo buro tuwau mwembe nyumom) la cin cuo nii na nawiyeu
JOH 2:10 la cin yi co “nubo ki ter neka mweb Inabim bo kenko ki kaba nanum de wo lombo yorau bwangten. dila mwein yoken kenko la mwi coku ti na wonyo”
JOH 2:11 woco diker nyiman kako Yeecu mani mor kaka wo Galili yeu, la cin nung dur tangka ceko, la nob bwangkab ceko nee bilenke cinen
JOH 2:12 bwikom wuro ri Yeecu, nee ce keb cebo, kange nob bwangkab ceko yira ken kafar nahum, cin yi ken wi kume ni bi duwar
JOH 2:13 la dukluma yahudawa ka dadom, Yeecu yaken Urucalima.
JOH 2:14 cin fiya nob miye ka nennek kange kwama kange nawurme mor bikur-waber, kange nubo fulong kemer tiye yirongum wi.
JOH 2:15 la cin ywel belyange ki duka, lacin cikangum ci gwam mor bikur-waber, kange kwama, kange nennetini. cin watangen kemer nubo fulog kemer tiye wi cin tungagum tabur tini ceu
JOH 2:16 ki nubo miye nawurme tiye ciki, “kocer ken ki dike buro. ko dubom yila kako ki lo temi fiye miyeka dikere.”
JOH 2:17 nob bwangka ceko kwabi ki mulangum mulange” kor lo mwero cam ner miro “
JOH 2:18 la nubo dur Yahuda ciya, yi co ki, “yirom bo wuni mwanung nyinenti wori mwi marang digero buro tiye?
JOH 2:19 Yeecu ciya, “ko werum bi kur wabero wo, la mor kume ta'ar mang kung ti
JOH 2:20 la nubo dur tini Yahuda ki bi kur wabero wo to cotiro kwini na'ar culombo nukkun na nyi me ci mu la mwan mum co mor kume ta'ar?
JOH 2:21 la, ciki tok kange bikur-waber bwi cero.
JOH 2:22 ki kwama wo cii kungu ki cin co bwanreu, nob bwangka ceko kwabi ki cin tok ker nyo, la cin ne bilenke ki bi fumero kange kero wo Yeecu tokkeu.
JOH 2:23 la ki kwama wo Yeecu mor Urucalima ki cika yabka, nubo duce ne bilenke den cero kanbo cii to diger nyimanka ko ci manen la Yeecu ciya bo kange ci wori cin nyimom ci gwam.
JOH 2:25 kange ayi co diker dor niir, la cin nyimom dikero mor niireu.
JOH 3:1 la ni dinglime kange wi wo den cero Nicodemu, nii dur Yahuda.
JOH 3:2 nii wo bow Yeecu nin ki kume la yico, “Rabbi, nyin nyumom mwin nii merangka wo bou kwama nine, wori nii kange mani wo ama diker nyimangkako mwi mane ri no kwama mani kange cori.”
JOH 3:3 Yeecu ciya cinen, “bilenke, no cii bo nii takri, mani ci to liyar kwama ti”
JOH 3:4 Nicodimu yi co “ciya boten nii nyi ki kwama ci cirame? mani ca do mor fwiye nee ce ti kiritti yob naci bo ten co, can do wa?
JOH 3:5 Yeecu ciya,”bilenke, bilenke, no ci bo bo nii ki mwem kangi yuwa tangberi mani ci do liyar kwamak ti.
JOH 3:6 wo cii bo mor nange ri nange, la wo cii bo mor yuwatangberi, yuwatenbe.
JOH 3:7 Niyimangde wori min yi nen miki tam nyo cia fulongum boka mweko.
JOH 3:8 yiwako ki cui fiye ci fobi, mwan nuwa diir cero, dila mwi nyombo fte cibow wiyeu kaka fiye ci yaken tiyeu. nyo kange nubo gwam wo ci bo co mor yiwu tangbeke.”
JOH 3:9 Nicodimu ciya lan yi co “dikero wo a manyi?
JOH 3:10 Yeecu ciya lan yi co “mwin nii meranka Icirailari durwal mwi nyombo digero wa?
JOH 3:11 bilenke, bilengke ma yinenti tok ike nyi nyomeu, nyi nee to-e. di duwal kom yo bo warke nyeu.
JOH 3:12 no min yi nen diker dor kalere mwi ne bo bilenke ri, mwa nee bilenke nyi no yinen dor diker dii kwama ri?
JOH 3:13 nii kange mani wo kwiken dii kwama no cum co wo yirau dii kwamari bi bwe nii fiye.
JOH 3:14 na wo ci yam kung bi bwe nii fiye dii,
JOH 3:15 ri la gwam wo nee bilenke atin fiye dume di riye.
JOH 3:16 kwama ciu kale wo ri cin neken bibwe ce wiin cuar, la wo ne bilenke cineneri mani a bwiya ti la wi ki lai dume diriri.
JOH 3:17 kwama tungu bo bwew mor kalewo na kume dor bitinero dila na dor bitinero fiya fuloka fiye ci wiye
JOH 3:18 wo ne bilenke cine neri mani a bwiya ti, wo nebo bilenke cine neri, kweri bwiyam bwiya wiro ci nebo bilenke ki den bi bwe kwama ro wiin cuwareu.”
JOH 3:19 Won co dike bwi bolang filang ko bou dor bitiner, nubo cwi kuntacile la filang ko, wori nangen cero cile.
JOH 3:20 No wo ma bwirang keri ko filang ko, bou bo filang nin wori nangen cero nungi yanglang.
JOH 3:21 Bwen dwal nyiri, niwo ma bilenkeu, bou filang ko nin na nungi yang lang, nangen cero na kwama ce co mane.
JOH 3:22 Bwikowo Yeesu kange bibei tomange ceu cuu biten Yahudiya, co yim wi lenger kange ci kange yuka mwengek kwamak.
JOH 3:23 Yuwanna yuu mwem ti Ainon bidom kange Salima wori mwembo bidom wi. Nubo bouti cinen con yuu cinen mwembo.
JOH 3:24 Fiya Yuwana ci tung bo furcuna bwiri.
JOH 3:25 Kwalkang ke kweni tiber bibei tomange Yuwana kange Yahudawa, ker maka duklumek.
JOH 3:26 Cin ya Yuwana nin cin yi co ki, “nii merangka, nii wuro kange mweu dinge kon caji Jordaneu dor we? mo ware, too, co yuu mwem ti, takeu gwam ci yaken ti ci nin.
JOH 3:27 Yuwana kari, “Nii mani a yoo kange diger ti, tano ci ne co dii kwamari.”
JOH 3:28 Mo ki bwimi mwan wari, man toki ma kebo Kiristi', dila cin twomou ye nimde co.
JOH 3:29 Bine ki nii bine, dila fakuwe nii bineu wo ti nuwa ceu, bilange ducce ki dir nii binero, wuro, co bilangtum mimbo kambo ken.
JOH 3:30 Ca yokten miu man yiram.
JOH 3:31 Nii wo bou diyeu, la gwam. Nii wo dor bitenereu, ki no dorbitinerer, tok diger ti dor, dorbitinere. Nii wo bou dii kwamau la gwam.
JOH 3:32 Co war kerti dor digero co toweu kange co nuwau, dila kange man wo ciya warke ceu.
JOH 3:33 Nii wo ciya warkeceu, co nungi kwama nii bilenker.
JOH 3:34 La nii wo kwama tun ceu tok ker kwamar ti. Co nebo yuwa tangbe ki cuwaka.
JOH 3:35 Tee cwi bi bwece, neken co digero gwam kang cak.
JOH 3:36 Nii wo ne bilenke ki bweri, dume na ce, nii wo nuwabo bweri mani ca to dume ti, cwika kwama ko a yii kange co.
JOH 4:1 kambo Yeecu nyumom tancawa nnwam co fiye ten bi bei tomange ti, co yii' cinen mwem kwama ti lan wo Yuwana ceu,
JOH 4:2 (bwen no na kebo Yeecu ki bwici yu cinen mwembo tiyeu, bi bei tomangece.)
JOH 4:3 con dubom Yahudiya con yilaken Galili
JOH 4:4 la tam co tiyangi camariya.
JOH 4:5 la con bou cinen lor camariyaro kange wo coti, cika, bidom kange fiye Yakubu ne bi bwe ce Yucufu.
JOH 4:6 bwir Yakubu ro ki no wi. kanbo luwam Yeecu ki yamcem be ri la con yii ken kong bwirie. dong dong kamg keneko nukkun.
JOH 4:7 nawiye camanya kange bou a tuwa mwem, la Yeecu yii, neye mwembo nan nomwi,
JOH 4:8 nyeu bibei tomange ceu doken mor cinan lor a teyer cari.
JOH 4:9 la nawiye camiriya yii co la a manyi mo mon bayafude mwa me yeti mo min nawiye camariya mwem no kam tiye? Yafudawa mani yabkan na kange camariyawa.
JOH 4:10 Yeecu kar cen cinen na mon nyumom luma kwama ri, kange co nii wo yii nenti ne ye mwem nokameri, namotin ken co yii nentin ne nen mwembo ki dumeu.
JOH 4:11 nawiye yii co, nii merangka, mo manki tabwir, bwiro cuwa kabo, la mwa fiya mwembo ki dume fe?
JOH 4:12 be mwa la bo tenge Yakubu, mon la ca, co woca ne nyo bwireu, co ki bwici con no more ce. bibeyo lo ce no wi, kange bicir cero?
JOH 4:13 Yeecu yii co kange nii wo na no mwembo weri an nuwa dilo mwe tak
JOH 4:14 la nii mane co tiyeri, mani a nuwa dilomwe ti tak. yila nyen, mwembo ma ne co tiyeu an yilam kwen mwenger cinen ti bui yaken ciko dume diinyeu.
JOH 4:15 nawiyeu yii nii merangka neye mwembo wo nari nuware dilomwe tak. nan boure tuwaka mwengek fo.
JOH 4:16 Yeecu yii co, ya cou bwemwe. na kom bou fo.
JOH 4:17 nawiye yii co, mi man ki bwayile. Yeecu yii co mo tok dong-dong, mi man ki bwayile,
JOH 4:18 wori mon nam nabarob lam nung wo mo ciko na weu ke bo bweme. dike “mwa tokeu bilenker.
JOH 4:19 nawiye yii co, “nii merangka, ma to timon nii dukume.
JOH 4:20 tebnye bo wab fo bang ko wo, la mweu moki wurcalima co fiye daten nubo yam wabka ti wiye.
JOH 4:21 nawiye, ne bilenker kwamaco bouti wo mwa wab “Teeti fo dor bangero wo, bwenno wurcalima di.
JOH 4:22 kom ki wab dii ke ka nyombeu. nyeu nyo ki wab dii nya nyumom me wori fulokaka yau Yafudawa nin.
JOH 4:23 na co nyeu, kwama co wi bouti, na weu wo fo nob wabkako kendo an wab “tee mor yuwa tangbekcek kange bilenker. na teeu ki do co nubo buro na yilam nob wabbeceb.
JOH 4:24 kwama yuwa tangbek la nubo buro wabco tiyeu, tam wab co ki yuwa tangbek,
JOH 4:25 nawiyeu yii co “man nyumom kiwo maciya bouti (wori cu wo ti kiritti yeu) na co bou, can fuitang binen dikero gwam.
JOH 4:26 Yeecu yii co, “mo co, ceu yinen ker ti yeu.”
JOH 4:27 la na ceu bibei tomange ceu yilam. la ci nyumangi ye bwi co tok kan kerti kange nawiyeu, la kange ciye tok bo, “ye mo cuitiye? “kaka ye bwi mo tok kerti kange ce?
JOH 4:28 la nawiyeu dubom tabwir mangero, yilam ken mor cinan lor, la yii nubo.
JOH 4:29 bou kom to nii wo yii ye dike wo ma gwameu. wuro yilanin kiritti an yila ka?”
JOH 4:30 cin dubom cinan loro cin bou cinen.
JOH 4:31 na ceu bi bei tomange ceu yii co ti nii merangka cam carito.
JOH 4:32 la con yii ci min wi ki carito ma catiyeu wo ka nyom beu.
JOH 4:33 la bi bei tomange ceu ti tokkangi bwitici, kange nii bou cinen bo diker cakar for, lan wi ka?
JOH 4:34 Yeecu yii ci, canmiti co wo nan ma dike nii wo tomu ye maneu, la nan takum nangen cero.
JOH 4:35 ka tok bokum cuiyak na'ar la nanimde cuiyak ko bou ka? ma yii kom ti, kung nuwa ko to tanginiu, kweri bimye na cua kaba bi tokko ce.
JOH 4:36 nii wo biye butuwe tiyeu, yo nan nanger ceroti, la mur bi tutiyo wo ya ken dumen dii riye. wori niwo fiyeu, ci bi langi wari.
JOH 4:37 fo wori min, tokkako, wineu fi, la kange biyemeu bilenker.
JOH 4:38 man tuom kom ko ya biyeka. fiye koma bou nangen wiyeu. kangem bou mam nangendo kumeu kon do ti dotange ciyerin.
JOH 4:39 camariyawa ducce cinan loroco ne bilenker kange co ki ker nawiye wo ne warke dor ce reu. “con yii ye dike ma maneu gwam.”
JOH 4:40 la kambo camariyawa bou cinenu, cin ken co na yii kange, con ciya com dam kange ci kume yob.
JOH 4:41 nubo duccu tok ne com dam kange ci kume yob
JOH 4:42 cin yii nawiyeu, mani nya ne bilenker ti ka kero woma toku, wori nyo ki bwinyi nyon nuwam, la nyumom nii wo co nii fuloka dor bitiner.”
JOH 4:43 bwiko kume yobeko, la con kobum we con yaken Galili
JOH 4:44 Yeecu ki bwici toki, nii dukume mani fiya dur bitinece.
JOH 4:45 kambo co bou Galiliri, nubo Galili yo co. cin tom dikero co manangi wurcalima, ki duklume, wori cin ya'a duklumeu keu.
JOH 4:46 la yila con bou ten kana mor Galili, fiye yila mwem yilam mwem inabimmeu. kange nii wi wo ma nangen lo liyaru bibwece mor kafarnam nuwa bo luma.
JOH 4:47 kambo co nuwa Yeecu dubom Yufudiya yaken Galili di, co ya'a Yeecu nin la co me co no bou na twam bibwece, woro dadom bwiyakau.
JOH 4:48 Yeecu lam yii co na ka to bo yirom kange diker nyumankardi, ma ka ne bilenkerti.
JOH 4:49 nii nangen ne wo yii co “nii merangka, yirau nanimre bibwe mi bwiyam
JOH 4:50 Yeecu yii co “ya bibwe mwen bum.” nii co ne bilenke kange kero Yeecu. Yeecu yii ceu, la con cu.
JOH 4:51 kambo co yiraken tiyeri, canga ceu wabkang co yii co bibwe bum ki dume,
JOH 4:52 co ca me ciye kang keneko nibereu, kwirum bwiu dubom co.
JOH 4:53 co teeu la nyumom kin co kang keneko co Yeecu yii co, “bibwemwe bum” la co ki bwici kange loceu gwam cinne bilenker.
JOH 4:54 wuron co diker nyuman karo Yeecu manau kambo co ceru Yafudiya co yaken Galili.
JOH 5:1 bwiko nyeu duklume Yafudawa wi, la Yeecu yaken wurcalima. wi wurcalima nyilok bi fwa tatik bele caji wi, wo ki nyi Ibraniyawa ki co ki Baitacda, wi ki bitukko nung cumamgum cumange
JOH 5:3 nubo kila-kila buro nuwa lumau, fukma, kilen, bwen co wo nani kange kani bwiyameri da rangum wi.
JOH 5:4 la be tomange kwama wucakeu, ki yam nyo ya bur mwembo kwama ce, la nawo yira kenten mur mwenge bureri fiya twaka bwen non twiraye co kala ticikeri.
JOH 5:5 nii kange wi ni wo nuwa bo luma coro kwini ta'ar cilombo narub.
JOH 5:6 kambo Yeecu toco ca dom wiyeri, la con nyumom nii wo dam wi coti kila-kila, la con yii co, mo cuiti na yilam kwamara?
JOH 5:7 nii nuwa luma toki nii meramgka “ma man ki nii wuro a dokken yeti mor mwenge na ci mok mwembori. nan bou ri kange yira kenten minen.
JOH 5:8 Yeecu yii co “kweni, to kwangni mweu mwa yakenti.
JOH 5:9 dangjang nii con twam lan tu kwani ceu cu. la diye co diye kakuk fobka,
JOH 5:10 la Yafudawa yii nii wa twameu, kakuk fobkak, yorbo tu kwangni mweu,
JOH 5:11 la con yii ci, nii wo twa yereu, yii ye tu kwama ni mwe mwa yakenti
JOH 5:12 cin me co, we nii co yi nen ki tu kwangni mweu mwa yakengtiye?
JOH 5:13 la nii wo ci twa beu nyombo we Yeecu, la Yeecu cerum da'ar, wori nubo kila kabo fiye co.
JOH 5:14 la kaktenri Yeecu ya fiya co kuwabe, la yii co to mon yilam kwamer, mare bwirangke tak na kange dike bwiraneu fiya nen de.
JOH 5:15 nii co cu yan yii Yafudawau, Yeecu twa yere.
JOH 5:16 lan co dike wo Yafudawa ne Yeecu dotange, won co ma nan dii keburo kakuk fobkak.
JOH 5:17 Yeecu yii ci teemi ma nangen ti bwen na wori, mo keneu ma manangenti.
JOH 5:18 co dor Yafudawa do na twalum co ciki kebo ka kanuk fobka ca kimeu, yila con co ten kwama ki te ce, tu dor ceroti dong-dong na kwama
JOH 5:19 Yeecu kar cinen, bicom ki bicom bwe mani a ma diker na dor ceroce kima kima kan co dike ca to tee ma tiyeu, wori dii ke na tee matiyeri, bwe kima co co ciko win.
JOH 5:20 wori tee cui bweti, lan nun dikero gwam wo ca matiyeu, la an nung cinen dike burombo tenang tenangeu wo la buro la na ko nyumangi.
JOH 5:21 kambo teeu kungum nubo bweyarangume yila ne ci dumeu, nyo ken bweu ne dumeti nii wo ca cuiyeu.
JOH 5:22 la tee ma bo nii nin buolang, la con neken buolangko kang bwek
JOH 5:23 la na nubo gwam na ne bwe dur, kanbo ci nem tee tiyeu. nii wo na nebo bwedurre di nebo teeu wo tuomceu.
JOH 5:24 bicom, bicom nii nuwa ker mire la ne bilenker nii wo tuom yereri wi ki dume diiri yeu, la mani a kangco ti la con cum buar con yabken dume.
JOH 5:25 bicom, bicom ma yi kom kwama co wi bouti, wuro nubo bwiyameu a nuwa dir bi bwe kwamaro tiyeu, la nubo buro nuwa an da.
JOH 5:26 na wo tee wi ki dume coki bwici, la con ne bweu na yilam ki dume ki bwici.
JOH 5:27 la teeu ne ken bweu bikwan kerero na mwatum bolanko wori co bibwe nii fire.
JOH 5:28 ko nyuman de ki wo, kwama kange bouti wo nubo wo tuweti numeu an nuwa dircero.
JOH 5:29 la ci an cerangu, buro mana kenneu ki yan kwenka dumek, la buro mana bwireu kiyan kwenka buolangek.
JOH 5:30 mani ma makange diker ti ki bwimi, nawoma nuwau, ma mabuolangko nyo, buolanmiko dong-dong, wori dike ma matiyeu kebo mo, na nii wo tuoma yerece.
JOH 5:31 na man warker dor mir di, warke miumani a yila bilenkeretti.
JOH 5:32 kange wi wo awarker ti dor mire. la man nyimom warkeu ca ne ti dor mireu bilenker.
JOH 5:33 kan tuom yuwa na nin, con ne warker bilenkerer.
JOH 5:34 la warke wo ma yoweu kebo nii fir nin, ma tok kere wo na fiya cerka.
JOH 5:35 yuwana kira wo titi re filang tiyeu, la kom cuiti na ko ma bilangtum mor filange ce nin biduwar.
JOH 5:36 dual, warke ma cike tenangi la yuwana ceu, ki nangendo wo tee ne ye nan dimeu, nangen do buro matiyeu, warker ti dor mir, nung teeu tuom ye
JOH 5:37 tee wo tuom yereu ki bwici warker dor mir. ka nuwambo dir cer wi ko tom bo cerkanka ceu wi.
