JOH 5:38 kercero mani yim mor nee kume, wori ka nebo bilenker ki nii wo ca tuomu weu.
JOH 5:39 kom kiyerang bifumeroti kom kwatiri more ciye kan fiya dume dii ri yeu, wentati cici warkerti dor miro.
JOH 5:40 la kom cui bo ko bou minen nako fiya dume.
JOH 5:41 mani ma yo cak-lanka fiye nubo wiye.
JOH 5:42 la man nyumom ka man ki cuika kwamak neer kumer.
JOH 5:43 ma bou mor dene teemi la ka yoyebou, no na kange an bou ki den cer di kan yo co.
JOH 5:44 la ka nebilenker nyi kom wo ciya caklangka bwi ti kumeu, lamanikado caklankako wo bou kwama nin win ki kwaceu
JOH 5:45 kom kware neer fiye teemi wiyeu niiwo muca woka yoneer cineneu.
JOH 5:46 na kom ciyaki mucari, kan ciya kimo, wori con mulangi dor mir.
JOH 5:47 na kom ciya bo ki mulangka cerkori, la kom mani na ko ciya ki kermiro.
JOH 6:1 bwiko dikeburoko, yeecu cu yabken dinge caji galili, wo coti caji tibariya
JOH 6:2 nubo kila-kila bwang cinententi, wori cinto yirome wo ca mati dor nubowonuwa lumau.
JOH 6:3 yeecu kwi ken bang la wi co yii kange, bibei tomange ceu.
JOH 6:4 na weu yabkako, duklume yafudawa dadom.
JOH 6:5 la kambo yeecu kungnuwe to nubo ducce bouti cineneri, la con yii filibu, ba ya fe na bo ten nubo buro nin cari na ci cam.
JOH 6:6 la yeecu tok wo na co cuwa filibu, woricoki bwici con nyomom dike can matiyeu.
JOH 6:7 filibu yii co carito naiyo kwini kob yobeu mani a lati bwen bidob, bidobri.
JOH 6:8 win mor bibei tomangeceu, andarawu yii cimo bitru yii yeecu.
JOH 6:9 bwe kange wi fo ki kuntulun cari to nung, na bikatece kange jinge yob. i an ye wo, nubo wo kila nyeu.
JOH 6:10 yeecu toki, ki yi nubo a yii ken, la yerako ducce fiye co nin. la bayilobo yii ken, nubo bi kate nung, kila ciko.
JOH 6:11 la yeecu tukuntulen cari ye do la kambo co nem buka kangeri, con ne nubo yirongume. con ma ti nyo ki jingeu, kambo ci cuitiyeu.
JOH 6:12 kambo fuer nobero bwabangumeu, loco yi bi bei tomangeceu, ko mwerum buro wularangi kumeu na kange na lere.
JOH 6:13 laci mwerum gwam la dim bulendo kwob cilom bo yob, ki wo wularange, mor kutulun cari ye to nungeu, wo kum nubo ca.
JOH 6:14 la kambo nubo to dker nyuman karo wo la maneri la cin toki, bilenker wo co ni dukume a bou ti mor dorbitinereu.
JOH 6:15 kambo yeecu nyumom cin dadom bouka na ci ta co kibi kwan na ci neken co liyau, la con cerum tak, kwi ken bang ki bici.
JOH 6:16 la kambo meu domeri, bi bei tomange ceu yira rang ken caji.
JOH 6:17 cin doken mor nabire mwengek, ci yabken kafarnam la kume fun fiya co yeecu boubo cinen.
JOH 6:18 la yuwa kwam kwam ti cuici, la caji ti mwenlangi.
JOH 6:19 kambo ci ya yambo na kang keneko kwini yob cilombo nung, kaka kwini ta'are di la cin to Yeecu yau dor mwenger caji bouti bi dom kange nabire mwengeu, la cin cuam tai.
JOH 6:20 la con yi ci, “niri mo” kom cuare tai.
JOH 6:21 la cin ciya ci yo co mor nabire mwengekro nin, ko co nabire mwengeu lam konge.
JOH 6:22 celfini, nubo buro tirangum dinge caji wineu, tori kange nabire mwenge mani, wi, la kan co win, la Yeecu do bo mor kange bi beitomangeceu cu ki kwa ci
JOH 6:23 la kangem nabire mwengem bo wi buro nyu tibeya, bi dom kange fiye nubo cam canyeu, bwiko teluwe nem bukakange keu.
JOH 6:24 la kanbo nubo nyumom Yeecu kange bibei tomangeceu mani fiye ceu, ci ki bwici cin doranken nabiren mwengero buro cin cu kafanam doka Yeecu.
JOH 6:25 kambo ci fiya co wi dinge cajiu, la cin yi co, “ni merangka” mwa bou fiyang fo?
JOH 6:26 la Yeecu kar ci nen, bicom kom ki do mo, kebo yirome ka to, wori kon cam carito wo fuer kumero bwam.
JOH 6:27 ko dob maka dotangek dor cani to wo kaya ti kaya, la ko ma dotange dor tiyero diiri yeu, la co wo bi bwe nii a ne kom tiye, wori tee kwaama kwa cinen ti kange dor cer.
JOH 6:28 la cin yi co, yee, nya mati na nyo ma nangen kwaamare?
JOH 6:29 la Yeecu kar ci nen, wuro co nangen kwamaro kom ciya ki wo co tomuweu.
JOH 6:30 la cin yi co diker yirome ye mwa mati na nyo to na nyo ne bilenker ki mwe?
JOH 6:31 ye mwa ma tiye? ten kuwa nib nyebo ca manna ki na wo ci kiyeu ne ci cari to yirau diiyeu cin cam.
JOH 6:32 co la Yeecu yi ci, “bicom,” bicom” ma yi komti kebo muca ne kom carito co diiyeu, lan tee ne kom cori to wo bilenkero ce lo kwama.
JOH 6:33 cari kwamaro co wo yirauti dii lo kwama, wuro ne dor bitinero dume tiyeu.
JOH 6:34 la cin yi co nii merangka,” mwa ne nyo mwan cari to woti kir-kir.
JOH 6:35 Yeecu yi ci, mo cari dumero, wuro bou mineneri mani a nuwa wurati, la wuro ne bilenker mineneri mani a nuwa dilomweti.
JOH 6:36 la man yi kom, bi com kom tom ye, la ko ne bo bilenker,
JOH 6:37 nii wo tee ne yereri an bou minen nii wo bou mineneri mani ma yuwa coti ki duwar.
JOH 6:38 wo ma yirau bo dii nan ma cuika dor mirek, la dike nii wo tuomu yere,
JOH 6:39 won co cuika nii tuomu yereu, kange a lemde wi win mor nubo ca neyere, la can kung ci diye kwenka liyar kwamak
JOH 6:40 la won co cui ka tee miko, na wi wo to bwe tiyeu la ne bilenker kange ceu an fiya dume diiri yeu, la kun co ki dii ka kumenik.
JOH 6:41 la yafudawa, to kanti ka fitike, dorcer, wori Yeecu toki co tiyo yirauti lo kwama.
JOH 6:42 la ci ti toki wo kebo Yeecu bibwe yakubu we wo teece kange neece nyo nyumom ci ya? la ma nyi com ca tok ki ma yirau lo kwama?
JOH 6:43 Yeecu karci nen, “ko dubom fiti keti to bwiti kom
JOH 6:44 nii mani a bou ti minero, no tee wo tuomu yere cou cori, miu la na kunco kakuk kwen ka liyar kwamak.
JOH 6:45 mulangum mulange mor bifumer nob dukumeb, toki, gwam ciye kwama an merang cinen. nii wo nuwa la merangeri, an bou fiye mi wiyeu,
JOH 6:46 la kebo nubo gwam tom tee, lakan co wo wi tee nineu. co ca to tee.
JOH 6:47 bicom, bicom no nii wo ne bilenkereri, wi ki dume diiriyeu.
JOH 6:48 mou cari dumeu.
JOH 6:49 tebkumebo cin ca manma mor kiye cin buyarangum
JOH 6:50 la cari to wo wo yirau lo kwama, la nii wo ca more ceri la man ki bwiyaka.
JOH 6:51 mo cari to ki dume wo yirau lo kwama, la nii ca cari to weri an fiya dume kwatti diiriyeu. cari to womane tiyeu bwimi wo cerka kaleko wo ce.
JOH 6:52 la yafudawa mam funer bwitici, la cin yoten citi kwobkangi cin toki, la nii wo a nebo nangece nyi na bo wo.
JOH 6:53 la Yeecu yi ci, bicom, bicom na mo wo nange bibwe nii fireri, namo nom bwiyale ceri, mani mwa fiya dumeti bwimwi.
JOH 6:54 nii wom nangemiula nom bwiyale mi yeu wi ki dume diiri yeu, la man kung co, kakuk kwenka liyar kwama.
JOH 6:55 wori nange miu co cari to ki bicomeu, la bwiyalemiu diker no karo bi comeu.
JOH 6:56 nii wo wom nangemiu la nom bwiyalemiyeri a yii more mi mo mi more ce.
JOH 6:57 kanbo tee ki dume tuom yereu, la kambo ma yimeu ma yii co teeu. la nii wo cam yereri, la can yii ker mir.
JOH 6:58 wuro co cari to wo yirau lo kwama, kebo na tebbo ca la bwiyarangumeu, nii wo ca cari to weri an da diiri.
JOH 6:59 la Yeecu tok dike buro kambo co merangti bi kurwabereu kafarnam.
JOH 6:60 la bibei tomange ceu ducce wo nuwari, ki wo tokkako bwaibwaye, we a nuwa tiye?
JOH 6:61 Yeecu lan nyimom ki bwici, kambo bi bei tomange ceu, ti funan bwiti ci yeri, la yi ci, wo yilam kayaka kekka?
JOH 6:62 la ye no kanto bi bwe nii fire kwikenti fiye kwatti co wiyeu?
JOH 6:63 la co yuwa tangbe ko ne dume tiye, bwiyo mani ma kange kero ma yirang komeu yuwa tangbe kwamak, kange dume,
JOH 6:64 la kangem kumem bo wi wone bo bilenkereu, wori ki kaba Yeecu nyimom nubo ne bo bilenkerereu, kange wo a miye co tiyeu.
JOH 6:65 con toki, co dike bwi ma yi kome, kange nii bou nin fiye ma wi, la tee nin
JOH 6:66 bwiko nyeu, ducce mor bi bei tomange ceu yilam ki bwi, ci yatenbo yam kange co tak.
JOH 6:67 la Yeecu yi wo kwob cilombo yobeu, kameu mani ka cu kume ti kenka, kebo nya?
JOH 6:68 Bitru kar ci nen, “mo teluwe” nyo ki yang we nin? mo moki ker dumero diiriye.
JOH 6:69 nyeu nyon ne bilenker, la nyon nyumom, mo nii wucak ke wo kwamaceu.
JOH 6:70 Yeecu yi ci, kebo mo ma cok kome kwobcilombo yoba? win more kume bwekelkele?
JOH 6:71 la co ki tok kerowo dor yafuda bi bwe cima ne kkaryoti, la co, win mor kwob cilombo yoben, nii wo a miye co tiye.
JOH 7:1 bwiko dike buro gwam, Yeecu bwiylanti mor Galili, nyori ca cwibo na ya Yahudiya, wore Yahudawa cwiti na cin twallumco.
JOH 7:2 la duklume Yahudawa ci cuwo ti dodom.
JOH 7:3 kecebo la yico ki, “dubom fo, yaken Yahudiya, na be tomange na to nangendo mwa maneu,
JOH 7:4 nii kange man wo a ma diker ti yuran yurange no co cwiti na ci nyimom co nyanlang, wori mo ma dike buroti, nang dor mwero kale nin.
JOH 7:5 wori yitub mwebo kene nebo bilenke muneng.
JOH 7:6 Yeecu nyori yi ci, “kume ni mi bou bo buri, kime kange kom kicatec.
JOH 7:7 kale mani a ko komti, an ko ye mi wori mi tok bilenke ti dor cer nangen cero na bwir.

JOH 7:9 bwiko co yi ci dici dike bure di con yiken Galili,
JOH 7:10 la yitok ce bo cu fiye dukulumeri, cin bwan cinen ten da'ar.
JOH 7:11 Yahudawa do coti fiye dukulumi, cikin fe co?

JOH 7:13 nyori nii man wo tok ker ti dor cer nyanlange wori ci cwa Yahudawa ti.

JOH 7:15 la Yahudawa nyimanti, ki ma nyii nii wo nyirnom diker ducce.” wori ca yabe fiye meranka.
JOH 7:16 Yeecu ciya ci nen ki “meranka kebo na mi, na nii wo tomu nyere ce.”
JOH 7:17 no nii cwiti na co ma dike co cwitiye co cwiiye di can nyimom meranka ko wo. keno bou kwama nii di, kaka miki tok ker dorek ki dor cere di ki do duktonka dor cer,

JOH 7:20 nii bo mwerume ciya co, “muki ninga, we do ti na co twalnene?
JOH 7:21 Yeecu ciya ci ki min ma nangen wiin di kom ti myimangi
JOH 7:22 muca nekom mwatika lakeko. wuro nungbo ki na muca ce na teb kime bo ciye kikume fobka kom ki biyere larre.
JOH 7:23 no nii ci biyeten lar bi di fobkari, kebo dikoro bwir werfun mucad. ye'e ka kangum ner wori min twabni ki bi dii fobka ka?
JOH 7:24 kom warde ker diko wo ceru kalleu, ki wer dor bilenkeret
JOH 7:25 kangumbo bou urcalima yi ki, “wo kebo wo ci doti na cin twalume ka?
JOH 7:26 to co tok kerti nyanlang, ci yi cobo diker. kangeri nob bitine bo nyombo ki wo kiritti na ma nyo ka?
JOH 7:27 nyori bon nyimom fiye nii wo bou we. no kiritti bouri, nii mani a nyom fiye ca bouweti.
JOH 7:28 la Yeecu kung dir biur kwama meranti ki “kom nyimom fiye ma bou wiye, ma bou bo ki dor mir, nii wo tomu yere bilenke, ka nyom co bo.
JOH 7:29 min nyimom co wori ma bou fiye cin wiye
JOH 7:30 ci cuiti na cin tam co nyori ni yobo kang dor cer wori kumeni bou bo buri.
JOH 7:31 ducce mor nubo mwerume ne bilenke cinnen ne, cin tok ki “no kiritti bou ri a ma dike la'a nii wo ce ka?
JOH 7:32 fariciyawa nuwa nubo mwerume ti tokangi dike wuro ti Yeecu ki lima, la liya wabbe kange fariciyawa tom nobo dur ci a tam co.
JOH 7:33 Yeecu yi ci ki kom bi duwar na yilaken fiye nii wo tom yere.
JOH 7:34 “kan doye mani ka fiya ye ti, fiye ma yatiye mani ka yati.”
JOH 7:35 Yahudawa yi bwiti ciye ki fiye wiini nii a yati la mani ba nyomtiye? co ki yang fiye Hilenawa watangum na co meran Hilenawa nin ka?
JOH 7:36 “ye dike co to keu” kang doye mani ka fiya ye ti, fiye ma yatiye mani ka yati.

JOH 7:43 la nobo mwerume yalkani yob ker ceu.
JOH 7:44 kangum cin bo no ki tan co, la nii mani wo yoti kang dor cere.

JOH 8:1 Yeecu ya zaitunek.
JOH 8:2 ki kwomjece yilau kuwabi, nubo kwarub bou cinen, yiken meran cinenti.
JOH 8:3 dila nob mulangkabo kan, nge faricawa ciin bo cinen ki nowiye ciitau mor kayakau. ciinyoco tiber.
JOH 8:4 la ciin yico ki ni merangka, nawiye wo mor kayaka.
JOH 8:5 mor bifure, musa ne, nyo nyal kinyi mubang nubowo, mweu yemutoke
JOH 8:6 cii toknyo nacii fiya fiye ciiya tamcoti ki kere, la yeecu cungken bitine mulang dikero kibi wure ce.
JOH 8:7 kambo cii merangco kerotiyeri, yeecu kweniti yicii, niwo more kume manki bwirangkeu ater mobka tereko.
JOH 8:8 yila cungken bitine mulang dikero kibi wureco.

JOH 8:15 kom mabolangkoti ki cwika durek, mi mabo ninin bolang.

JOH 8:18 mo mima warke dormittiye takri tee wo twomu yereu ni warketi.”

JOH 8:21 yilanyitenci, man yaken kandoye mani kafiyati, kan bwiyam mor bwiramker kumer. fiye miyakentiyewiyeu mani kom yati.”

JOH 8:24 co dikebwi matoki mi bwirangke kume.
JOH 8:25 la ciin meco” we mwo?” yeecu yicii, dike miyikom kikabau.
JOH 8:26 miki dikero duce mayi komtiye, ma makumenten bolangti dor cere. dilanaweu, niwo twomu yereu, nibilingke, dikero manuwa cinenneu, co dike miyi dor bitinero tiyeu.
JOH 8:27 cii nyombo kiyicii kero dor teer
JOH 8:28 Yeecu yi cii kanbo kom kun bibwemi diyeri, lakan nyimom in mo, lami mabo diker dorermir. kambo tee merange, meneu, nyo mitok dikero birombo tiye
JOH 8:29 co nii ci twomu yereu, wiwari kange mo mani dob yeti, wori mima dike fuwociner tiyeu.

JOH 8:32 kan nyimom bilengke, bilenkeu atin cokkom.”

JOH 8:34 Yeecu yi cii, bilenke, bilenke, mi yikom nii wo ma bwirankeri canga bwirankerer.
JOH 8:35 canga mani yi lo diri; bweluwe kiyi lo diri.
JOH 8:36 canno bweu ceer nendi, bilenke munfiya ceerka.

JOH 8:38 mitok dike mito Tee minine, kume keneu kom ki madike kom nuwa Tee kume nine.”
JOH 8:39 Ciin ciya ciiki, “Tee ce Ibrahim.” Yeecu yi cii ki, na kom na Ibrahimece ri komki ma dike Ibrahim maneu.
JOH 8:40 Naweu kom cwiti nakom twallum ye, nii wo yikom dike ci nuwa Kwama ninneu. Ibrahim mabo wuro.
JOH 8:41 Kom ma nangen tee kumerti. Ciiki, “cii bo nyobo mor kayaka, nyi ki tee wiin Kwama.
JOH 8:42 Yeecu nyi cii, “No Kwama Tee kumeri kom ki cwi ye, wori mi bou Kwama nin lamin wo, mi boubo dor miir, co ci tomu yere.
JOH 8:43 Yebwi kom nyombo ker mire? Wori mani kom dol nuwaka kermiroti.
JOH 8:44 Kom na tee kume bwe kelkele ce lari kom cwiti nakom dike ner tee kumereti. Cin nii twalka ki kaba dila ci tibo mor bilenke wori bilenke mani more ce. Kambo citok cwerke tiyeri, ciki tok ker dike ci matiye wori cin nii cwerke, tee nob cwerkeb tak.
JOH 8:45 Wori mitok bilenketi kom ko neka bilenkek fiye mi wiyeu.
JOH 8:46 We more kume taye ki bwirangke? No matok bilenkeri, ye bwi mani kom ne bilenke tiye?
JOH 8:47 co wona Kwama ceu nuwa ker Kwamarti, kumeu mani kom nuwa ker Kwamaro ti wori kom kebo na Kwama ce.”
JOH 8:48 Yahudawa ciya co yiki, “Nyo tokbo bilenke kambo nya yi nyiki mun Nii Camariya la mwiki kelkeli ya?”
JOH 8:49 Yeecu ciyaki, “Mimanki kelkeli, dila miki ne Tee mi dur, la kom neyebo dur.
JOH 8:50 mani mido duktangka dorekmik, nii dotiyeu wi co nii ma warka tiye.
JOH 8:51 bilengke, miyikom, nubo wo bwangten ker miro tiyeu, mani buyati.”

JOH 9:1 la Yeecu cukentiri, con to ni kange ci bo fukma.

JOH 9:4 Tam nyo bi ma nangen niwo tomu yere fiya kakuko wi. kume bouti wo nii mani a nangen tiyeu.

JOH 9:21 cane ko ci totiyeu nya nyombo kange we wumom nuwe ceu nya nyombo ki me co cin duyom. can tokker dor cer.”

JOH 9:23 nyo ri tebcebo yi ci ki “cin duyom, me co”

JOH 9:25 ni wo kar cinen, “ma nyombo no con nii bwirang ke ri, dikero wiin ma nyimeu, “min fukma can miti toi.”

JOH 9:32 ka cikko ci ywel kaleu, ba nuwam bo wi ki kange nii wumom nuwa nii ci bo fukmau.

JOH 10:1 bilenke, bilenke, ma yi komti, wo na dobo yiloko yaken klan kwamero nineri, la co kwi kange nureri, nii wo nii kwiye kange nii werka.
JOH 10:2 wo do nure co nii mobka kwama ko
JOH 10:3 nii yiloko an wom cinen, kwama nuwa dircero ti, co ki co kwama ki dencir, na ya ki ci kale.
JOH 10:4 kambo co bo ki kale gwame, co tiken kab, kwama bwancinententi, kweri ci nyomom dircero.
JOH 10:5 mani ciya bwang ten fabeti, cwa co, wori ci nyombo dir faber.
JOH 10:6 Yeecu yi ci kero ki dangke, di la ci nyombo dike borombo co yi ci tiye.
JOH 10:7 Yeecu yila yiten ci. bilenke, bilenke, ma yi kom ti mo yilok kwameko.
JOH 10:8 kangem bo nimde mori, nob kub, kange nob werka, la kwama nuwa ci bo.
JOH 10:9 mo yiloko, wo gwam wo alo fiye ma wiye di an fiya fukma, can do co ceri, can fiya fiye cana.
JOH 10:10 nii kwiye mani bower, ki bo kan kwii, co twallum kange kanka. ma bo na ci fiya dume, take na ci fiya dutce.
JOH 10:11 mo nii biyuware kendo, nii biyuware kendo ne dume ceu dor kwamarce.
JOH 10:12 wo bwe tomange, kebo nii biyuware wo kebo nii kwame, tono to bicwara bo tiri an cwa dobti kwame wii, la bicwara tam, kwame, yalumten ci.
JOH 10:13 cwo wori con nii nangen kiyeme, take yo co bo kange kwameru.
JOH 10:14 mo nii biyuware kendo, ma nyomom mi, wo mi nyomom ye.
JOH 10:15 te nyomom ye, mo ken ma nyomom te ma ne dume mi ker kwame.
JOH 10:16 mi wi ki kwame, kebo mor kilan do wo. birombo tam, bo ki ci, ciken ciyan nuwa dirmiro, beri ciya yila kilando win kange nii biyuware win.
JOH 10:17 nyo won co dike te cwiye tiye ma ne dume mi, beri na fiyaten co.
JOH 10:18 kange mani na wo a tum co ti minene, di la miki ne ki beimi. mi wi ki bi kwan ne kako, miwi ki kwan tuka ceko tok. ma you ciya kako te nin?
JOH 10:19 yalkako yila kweni tiber yahudawa dor kero woro
JOH 10:20 dutce more ciye ciki wiki kelkeli, takeu twelum, ye bwi ko nuwa co tiye?
JOH 10:21 kangem bo ki wurombo kebo ker nii ki kelkeli an wumom nuwe fukma?
JOH 10:22 duklume wucakke mor urcalima lau.
JOH 10:23 la miyalale, Yeecu yakenti wi karak bikurwabe culaimanu.
JOH 10:24 Yahudawa kentangum co, cin yi co fiyan mwa dob nyo ti mor nyomanka, tano mo mwa Almanciya di nyim nyo nyanglang.”
JOH 10:25 Yeecu yi ci, “ma yi kom di kom ne bo bilenke. nangen do ma ma tiye mor den te mir, ci, ciwarkeroti dor mire.
JOH 10:26 kang wo kom ne bo bilenke, dike bwiye kom kebo kwame mi.
JOH 10:27 kwame mi nuwa dir miroti, ma nyomom ci, ci bwang mententi ken.
JOH 10:28 mi ni ci dumeti diri, mani ciya bwiyati, ni mani a yociti kanmik.
JOH 10:29 te mi wo ne ye ciye, la nobo gwam duwi ka, ni mani a yociti kan temi.
JOH 10:30 mo kange te mi win.
JOH 10:31 la Yahudawa tu tero na cin mobang co ciko.
JOH 10:32 Yeecu ciya la yi ci ki, man nung kumen nangendo yoryori dute fiye te mi wiye la co nangendo wini mor nangendo ma mane, kom mobanye tiye?
JOH 10:33 Yahudawa kari ciya, kebo ki ker nangenero ken nyo cwiti, nyo mobangene, dila ker dilaka, mon nifir dila mo to dor mwero mo yilaken na kwama.”
JOH 10:34 Yeecu ciya ciki mani mulangum mulange ka, mor bolange kume, nace kom bwel ka? 36 tano co ci ki bweldi, la wurombo ker kwamaro bo cinene (mani a dolti ki kero mor bifumere)
JOH 10:36 kom ki yi niwo te cuki, tungu fo dorbitinereu, mon dillam, wori ma yi miki ma bebwe kwama ka'?
JOH 10:37 tano mani ma, ma nange temiro tiri kom nere bilenke.
JOH 10:38 tano mati mairi, bwen kom ne bo bilenke ki nangendo wori kom nyomom kom futangum kom ki te more mi, mi kenneu ma more te.”
JOH 10:39 cin maten na ci tam co, di la ta yamcem, cirum kangcik.
JOH 10:40 taka yamcem, yaken kab kange caji urdun, fiye Yahuda yum mwem bo wucakke tiye, yiken wii.
JOH 10:41 nobo ki la ci bo fiye co wiye. ciki bilenke Yahuda mabo kange yirom, di la gwam dike Yahuda to ki dor mi wuro bilenke.
JOH 10:42 nobo dutce ne bilengke cinen fiye co.
JOH 11:1 ni kange wi dendo Liazaru ma' twirak cin ni baitanya, la ki no bwar lor bi Maryamu kange yi tubcebo Mata.
JOH 11:2 Maryamu woro beltang teluwe nin nuwang yila nir cinen na ko ki yiri duwece. wuro yice Liyazaro dam ki twiranke.
JOH 11:3 yitub Marta tom tomange kirittin coki, tee, to co ni wo mwo cwitiyeu nuwabo luma.
JOH 11:4 kambo kiritti nuwa, la ci tokki mani yatico bwar, la tuka liyar kwama nyo, dige bwiyeu na bi bwe kwama fiya layar cer cinen.”
JOH 11:5 Yeecu cwi Martati, kange yice kange, Liazaru nuwa luma co ci tiyang yi.
JOH 11:6 na curori cin nyi bi beiyo lo ce, ban ya yafu diya tak
JOH 11:7 la bi beiyo loce cin nyi co, teluwe yafu diya tak
JOH 11:8 la bi bei yo lo co cin nyi co, teluwe yafuda donen ti wi duwal naci ya naci mubangnen ki ter yilo mu cwi yila kati witak?”
JOH 11:9 kiritti ciya kebo kene kwab culombo yob na ka kaku ko win ne ce ka?
JOH 11:10 ta no ni yayam ki kumeri an kottange dige bwiyeu filang ko mani kange co?
JOH 11:11 co tok ki na wuro di ki bwi nyori con nyi ci, forkume layijaro daken dum. laman ya na kungum co mwor dume.”
JOH 11:12 co bibeiyo loco nyi ki no dum ci datiyeri cin yuram
JOH 11:13 la kiritti ciyeu ci tok ker bwar Liyazaru dila ci kwetiri ki ker dume wo fubkakko ce.
JOH 11:14 la kiritti fwetang ci nen, “Layazaru bwiyam.
JOH 11:15 mi bilangti ki den kumer. na ki mi mani wiri na kom ne bilingke di la biya cinen.”
JOH 11:16 to wuro ci ciwoti ki bi bwe wo ci bo yob di wine nyi tangnim bi beiyo biya nabi bwiya wari kange kiritti.”
JOH 11:17 kambo kiritti laweu la con kwabti dam kume nar tuwe
JOH 11:18 baitanya yilo ki no bi dom kange uracalima, be yame nyo bidom ti beryer.
JOH 11:19 Yafudawa ducce cin bou na ci fiya co na ci ma cinen dangneri bibwei yiciye.
JOH 11:20 kambo nuwa ki kiritti bou ti yori yaken na ci fiya co nan di Maryamu yim mwor luwe.
JOH 11:21 matta nyi kiritti. teluwe naki mun wi fori no yimi ti bwiyabo.
JOH 11:22 bwentano can na wori min nyimom gwam dige mu kinongi kang kwamari atin ne nen.”
JOH 11:23 kiritti nyi co, “yimwe atin kwenum kwarce.”
JOH 11:24 la matta nyi co ki min nyimom bidiye kwenka nob bware an kwenum.”
JOH 11:25 kiritti nyi co Matta mo mi kunga nob bware, mo mi dume ni wo ne bilengke, mi neneu bwantano bwiyamri, can kwenum;
JOH 11:26 gwam ni wo ki dume no ci neya bilengkere mani ca bwiyati dong. mon ciya kange wura?”
JOH 11:27 la can nyi co ong min ciya mwo Almaciya, bi bwe kwama wuro bouti fo kalewo.”
JOH 11:28 ki kwama co tok ki nyo, la con yilaken con cuwo yice Maryamu dinge win co ki, teluwe biyegen, yilo cu wo nenti.”
JOH 11:29 kambo co nuwa nyeri la con kweni con yaken cinen wulom.
JOH 11:30 kiritti kweri doubo bwaror nwi fiye Matta yafiyaco wiyeu.
JOH 11:31 kange yafudawa wuro ci wari kange Maryamu we in co nubo buro ne ka cekko dangneri to cin ciri mwor luwe. wulom, la cin bwangten co, ci kwatiri cin cu cin ci wiye tuwe.
JOH 11:32 kambo Maryamu lam fiye tuwe wiyeri, la cin yarken kabum nace konin co ki teluwe, naki wo wari kange nyori yiye ti bwiyabo.”
JOH 11:33 kambo kiritti to co ci wiye tiyeri kange Yafudawa wuri ci bwangten ceu, co ci nyimangi yuwa tangbe kange co wi kange co.
JOH 11:34 la co to ki fiye wuni ki daken ci ke?” la cin nyi co ki teluwe bouti.”
JOH 11:35 kiritti ci wiye.
JOH 11:36 la Yafudawa ciki to kambo co cwi Liyazaru tiye; “
JOH 11:37 dila nubo buro ciki, nii wuro ne fukma toka fiyeu noti kobo bwiyak ni wuroka?”
JOH 11:38 kiritti dim ki yuwa tangbe ki bwici la cin cuken tuwe nin tuwe cim mummuwe nyi tuweu cin comti terowi.
JOH 11:39 la kiritti ki okm tungum tero Matta yi liyazaru wo bwiyame nyi teluwe, can neu bwiyo fuyem ki kume ta'ar can ki bwi yaka cekko.”
JOH 11:40 kiritti tok ki mi nyi nen bono mu ne bilengkari mwan fiya liyar kwama ka?”
JOH 11:41 di la cin kungum tero. kiritti kung nuwe ce dii tokki tee mi, min bumwen kang dige bwiyeu mu nuwa yeti,
JOH 11:42 min nyimom bwen tano ki kwama wuniri mu wari kange timfo ker kangum yere mi tok tiye, mi naci bilengke mwo mo tomuyere.”
JOH 11:43 kambo co tok kero wuro nyeri la con kung diro coki, “Layazaru di cerou.
JOH 11:44 la ni wo bwiyammeu cereu naceko kange kangko bwabe ki yi lang. tigom ce bo yi co canji langum ki yakka yi lange. kiritti ki nyi ci ki kom kwim co na cu.”
JOH 11:45 la nubo ducce mwor Yafudawa nin wo bo maryamu ni nen ci to dige bi bwe kwama mane cin ciya kange co.
JOH 11:46 la kangem bo yi la ken Faricawa nin cin nyi ci dige kiritti mane,
JOH 11:47 la nob werfun durko kange Faricayawa cin mwen dor ciyero, fiye win ci tok ki nye ba matiye, ni wuro madigerti ducce.
JOH 11:48 no bo dobco koni nawori, nubo ducce atin bwangten co. Ramawa an bou yom fiye beu kange bitine beu.
JOH 11:49 gwam nyo tak ni kange wi tiber ciyer, kayafa co ci ni bifumero durko ki coro wuro, nyi ki nyom bo diger.”
JOH 11:50 ki nyombo daten ni win na bwiyam ki den nubo ducce na bwiya kange wo kale kwarum a kwenum tiye.”
JOH 11:51 tok digewuro kebo na dor cero la kambo cin dur ni bi wabir, tok kero dur coki deten, kiritti na bwiyam ki den nubem.
JOH 11:52 la kebo ki den nubo kwarub la ki den na murangu bi bei kwama wuro merangum fiye kutanrange nyo weu na mweru ci fiye win.
JOH 11:53 di la ki kume di coru ci ter doka nure wuro ciya twal kiritti tiye.
JOH 11:54 di la na co kiritti mani nyo yanglang tiber Yafudawa dila ci yaken kange fiye bidom kange kii na kange cinar lor kange ci cuwoti Ifraimu. la ci beiyo loce.
JOH 11:55 tano yab karko na Yafudawa lau bidomdi la nubo ducce firin Uracalima nyo bitine dinge wine bidi idi na yulang bwi ci.
JOH 11:56 cin ter doka kiritti ci tikkang ker ti ki kwama ci tirangum tirange ku kwama, tokti. nye kom kwaatiye? mani a bo iditi ka?
JOH 11:57 ni dur wabiro kange Faricawa kweri cin neken nyel no ni wo to kiritti ri nyi ci na ci tam co.
JOH 12:1 kum kume nukkun nakwak yabkaka, Yeecu bou betani, fiye Lizaru wiyeu wo Yeecu fulouweu
JOH 12:2 cin macinen cariwi, matta nima carike, Liazaru wi mor nubo yimwiyeu kange Yeecu.
JOH 12:3 dila matta tuwango ficangeu ciyweki nad, ci belti Yeecu ninti nacek. laci wauki yiri duwecek. mor luweu dimki kundo ficang ficangeu.
JOH 12:4 Yafuda kari yoti wiin mor nob bwankaceb niwo ane konco fiyeu, yiki,
JOH 12:5 yebwe mani miyeu nuwango ficang ficangeti nai kwinikwo ta'arti naneken nubo manki dikere?
JOH 12:6 citok kero wo nobkici cwinubo manki dikereti, wori cin nikuye: cociyo kemerotiye, takri kudike ciyokangce keti.
JOH 12:7 Yeecu yiki, dobco ciya yoken dike cidou na fwekami koceu
JOH 12:8 kwatti kom wari kange nob bwinibi, kommani wari kange mo.”
JOH 12:9 kambo Yafudawa ducce nyumom Yeecu wini yeri la cin bou, kebo Yeecu nin ki kwace, cibou nacin to Liazaru, wo Yeecu fulou buwareu.
JOH 12:10 la liya wabetin do dou nuriti ciya twalum Liayazaru ti kencu,
JOH 12:11 inkercen Yafudawa ducce yane bilnike Yeecu nine.
JOH 12:12 celfiniceri namor ka nubeko ducce cin bou fiye Idii. kaci nuwa ker Yeecu bouti wurcalima,
JOH 12:13 la cin yeu bilu dibin cin ceru'u cin ker co dila cin kun diro citi toki Hosana; be buyer kiniwo bou kiden kwamareu, liya Yafudawa.”
JOH 12:14 Yeecu fiyaube Gelban kwiken dorcer kambo bulangeu,
JOH 12:15 cwaretai mo cihiyona, to liya kume bouti yimdor gelbar.”
JOH 12:16 nob bwankan cebo yombo dikowo kikabe, kambo ci duklang Yeecuri, la cin kwabidikewo mulangi nyo dor Yeecur, la cin ma cinen dikerowo.
JOH 12:17 la nubowo wari kange Yeecu ki kumewo ci cuwo Liyazaru mor tuwe cin fuloucou, cinen bilenke.
JOH 12:18 wonco dike bwi nubo cirou yaercou, wori ciin nuwa cin ma dikewo.
JOH 12:19 la Firicawa yoten kero bwiti ki, “to mani ka ma dike kangeti, komto dorbitinero bwangtenco.
JOH 12:20 morece Helinawa wi birombo yakentiwi fiye wabka Idii.
JOH 12:21 cin yaken Filibu nin, inni becaida yim Galili, “cii ki, nii merangka, nyin cwiti nyin to Yeecu.
JOH 12:22 Filibu yanyi Andirawu yaken wari kange Filibu yacin yi Yeecu.
JOH 12:23 Yeecu ciya yicii, kang keno ko din wo ciya ne bibwe nii duktang tiye.
JOH 12:24 bilenke, bilenke, miyikomti, la nu'u bikateu an yarken bitine na buyam, cannowi cike kwaco, cano cibuyamri, canne bituttitui.
JOH 12:25 niwo cwi dume cetiyeu, an lomco lano ko dumece kalereri atin yoken co dume wo diri diriyeu.
JOH 12:26 ni wo wabyetiyeri, la abwang menten. fiye miwiyeu. bwe can nya miu anowinken. niwo wabyeti yeri, kwama an neco duri.
JOH 12:27 naweu dume mi kino mor kwomka, yemama tiye? tee cokye ki kwama wo? wonco dike bwi milau kwama.
JOH 12:28 tee, duktang den mwero “la diro yirau di kwama ki, min duktangce, man duktangcotak.
JOH 12:29 la nyori nubo murom wiyeu nuwa diro, cin yi ki kwama kwabi. kanyembo ki nii tomangeu tokker kange co.”
JOH 12:30 Yeecu ciya ci ki, dirowo boubo minen, bou kumen.
JOH 12:31 naweu ciyatin warkaleu: na weu atin ywa nii liyar kalero.
JOH 12:32 na nyime mo, canno cii kunye dorbitinerdi, man bou ki nubo kwareub fiye mwiyeu”
JOH 12:33 ci tokwo nadong dara buwareu ca bwiya tiyeu.
JOH 12:34 nubo ciyaco yiki, nyin nuwa mor werfuner kiritti a yi nyo diri. ye bwi mutok muki atin kun bibweni ye? we bibweni ciro?
JOH 12:35 Yeecu inyici, “kakten biduwardi kam yi ki filang kamyi kange filango ki kwama wo filango wari kange komeu, ka kumtacileu cumomkom. wo yam mor kumtacileu, nyombo fiye ciyakenti wiyeu.
JOH 12:36 komne bilenke filanko wonin kambo kom wari kange filange nakom yilam bebei filang. Yeecu tokwori colem ya Yuranngum me.
JOH 12:37 cano Yeecu inma diker nyiman kar ducce kabumcim. kwarub kange wo, cinebo bilinki anen.
JOH 12:38 naker dukumer Icayarodin, woki, kwama, we nebilinke ker nyere? kang kwama ko bou wenin?”
JOH 12:39 wonco dike bwi ci nebo bilinker, Icaya toktentak,
JOH 12:40 cin cumom nuweceu, cin kwamum nerciro, wore na ci tore ki nuwece, naci nyomde ki nercer, yilau minen nan nirimci.
JOH 12:41 Icaya tok kerowo inwori cinto duktanka Yeecu kon tok ker kangeco.
JOH 12:42 nawo duwoleu, ducce mor duremcin nin nebilinke Yeecu nin dila Faricawa, ci dambo yomka ceko dangla.
JOH 12:43 cin cwi caklangka la caklangka ko bou kwama ninneu.
JOH 12:44 Yeecu kung diro yiki, niwo bilenke mi nen neure keboka minen cine bilenke kange niwo two mu yerou,
JOH 12:45 niwo to yereu, tom niwo two mu yereu.
JOH 12:46 me bou nan filang dor bitiner, canowo nebitinke minendi mani yiti mor kumtacile.
JOH 12:47 ni wo nuwa kermiro nebo bilenkeri, mani maci nen bolangti, mi bou bo nan ma dor bitinero nin bolang, bi bou nan fulo dor bitinero.
JOH 12:48 niwo keya, koten kermireu, niwo a maci nen bolangko tiyeu wi kero matokeu an maci nen bolang ki kume cwile.
JOH 12:49 ma tokbo ker doret mer inker teero twomu yereu, niwo yiye dike ma matiyeu kange dike matok tiyeu.
JOH 12:50 min nyimom nyalcero nawo diriye, co dike bwe matoke-nawo tee tokeu, nyo matoke.”
JOH 13:1 nyo na nyim de bi caro cuwam bwireu kiritti nyimom kume ce an dim wuro ca dubom kale wotiye cwi nubo buro fo kaleweu cwici gwam.
JOH 13:2 bwekelkele kwerin dor ner Yafuda Ikarouti bi bwe Caminu ne ken kiritti
JOH 13:3 nyimom te kwama neken digero fo kancek di ci bou tenin di ci ki yang tenin.
JOH 13:4 con kwenem caka cari konin con cukom bellece cin tu yilangko con kwarum bwici ciko
JOH 13:5 la con bwi mwembo ki kwel mwengye com ter nirka na bi bei yolo ceu co wamti ki yilangko wo co kwarum bwici cike.
JOH 13:6 cin bo Bitru, Caminu, la Bitru yico ki teluwe mwaten nirmin naka?
JOH 13:7 kiritti ciya yico ki dige mi ma tiyeu mani mwa nyomti can nawonyo di la ki mwan nyimom
JOH 13:8 Bitru yi co ki mani mwa nirmer nati kiritti nyi co ki no mi nirmwen bori mu man ki teluwe ke bo ka namik koni mwa nirtiye la kange kang miko kange nami ko.”
JOH 13:10 kiritti nyi co ki gwam ni wo yum mwengeu di nyo ka na la com manki dwiti cuko win kom nirum dor kumero la kebo gwam ki me.
JOH 13:11 di la bwiye kiritti nyimom niwo aneken co tiye co dige bwi ci tokke kebo gwam ki me man ki dwi tiye.”
JOH 13:12 kambo kiritti nir cinen nakeri tubellece nyinken tak yi ci ki kom dige mi makime na?
JOH 13:13 kom cuwo yeti kom ki teluwe kange kwama kom tok dong dong mina conyo
JOH 13:14 tana teno teluwe kange kwama nir kimen natiri daten kom keneu ki nir bwiti ki min na.
JOH 13:15 nyori min nyikom ki dangke kom ma kambo mi maki meneu.
JOH 13:16 tano nyori mi yi komti canga mani labo teluwe ce ki dwira bwe tomange labo ni wo tomuce ki dwika.
JOH 13:17 no kom nyimom dige buro kom nob lumam tano kom manangen cukori.
JOH 13:18 ke bo dor ki mer gwam mi tok kero tiye mi nyimom niwo ma cikeu dina kero.' di dor cer co ni wure cakwel mwengye win kange mowe con kungmen ker.
JOH 13:19 mi yi kom ti can nawo na nimde fiye kom tano fiya komdii kom ne bilengke mo.
JOH 13:20 bilengke mi yi kom tiye ni wo yo wuro mi tomuweri yomo niwo yeri yo ni tomu yere.”
JOH 13:21 kambo kiritti tok ki nyeri yuwa tangbe kwom co cuwa ci yici bilengke mi yi komti win tiber atin neken ye.”
JOH 13:22 bi bei loceu torangti bwitici la ci nyimangti keno dor we ci tok tiyeri.
JOH 13:23 win mwo bi beiloce wuro kiritti cwitiye wi to kombo nin bimumwi can kiritti.
JOH 13:24 ci mon Bitru yi tangnim bibeiyo lo yinyo mu tok kange weri.
JOH 13:25 di yila bimtibwici kiritti nin ci tokki teluwe weno le?”
JOH 13:26 co la kiritti ciya co niwo ma dokten cari to bikwen nanne co kom co dokti carito wiyeri la cin ne Yafuda bi bwe cimon Ikariyoti.
JOH 13:27 kambo ci cam carito weri, bwekelkele do co di kiritti yico ki dige mu matiye ma wolom.”
JOH 13:28 ni kange mani mwor caritonin wo nyimom dige bwi co yi co nyowe.
JOH 13:29 kangebo kwatiri tamwi Yafuda tamki cwaye kiyeme kiritti yi ce mun tiyen dige nyi cwitiye na toka nuwece kangeri me diger ki den celeb.
JOH 13:30 kanbo Yafuda yo cariton di can do wo cerum ki kume.
JOH 13:31 kambo Yafuda cuwe kiritti tokki cin duktong bibwe niifit morece.
JOH 13:32 kwama an dugtang co. co ki bwici yila na dugtung co can na wo.
JOH 13:33 bibei bi dwadti nubo mi wari kange kom nyo bi dob kan doye tak na wuro miyi Yafudawa. fiye ka dolyakati can na weu min yi kom.
JOH 13:34 mi ne kom werfunero fwirti kom cwi bwiti na wuro mi cwi komme dila nyo kom cwibuti.
JOH 13:35 na curo nyo nubo a nyimom kom bi beiyo lomiye no kom cwi bwitiri.”
JOH 13:36 cin mon Bitru nyi co teluwe mu ki yangfe? kiritti ciya cari fiye mi yakentiyeu mani mwa dolyakiti can nawo dila ki bwi mwan bwang menti
JOH 13:37 Bitru nyi co ki teluwe nye bwi mani ma dol bwangka mwerti can nawe? man ne dume mi ki den mwer.”
JOH 13:38 kiritti nyi co ki mwan ne dume mwe ki mwan ki den mirdi? kibi cuwom mi yinenti cire bar bi cake mob ki yeri mwan kanangyi kiritti ta'ar.”
JOH 14:1 “dobre ner mwer na kayam kom ne kwama bilengke na kom neye bilengke
JOH 14:2 firen lo temi yime wi ducce naki mani nyori no mitingyi kom dige bwiyeu man cu na ywel kimen fiye.
JOH 14:3 tano nya ywelkumen fiyeri. man yilau nan yo kom nyaken cu ko fiyeco dige bwiyeu fime wiyeu no ka nowiken.
JOH 14:4 na kom nyimom fiye miyakenti wiye
JOH 14:5 toma nyi kiritti ki teluwe nyo yombo fiye mwa yaken tiyeu nyori nya nyom fiye co nyi?”
JOH 14:6 kiritti nyi co mou mi nure mou mi bilengke mou mi dume nii kange mani ya yati tenin ca dou minen.
JOH 14:7 no kom nyimom yeri kom nyimom tee. kambo can nawo nyimom yereu kom tom co.”
JOH 14:8 Filibu nyi kiritti ki teluwe nung nyi nen teu wuro cuwa nyinenu.”
JOH 14:9 kiritti nyi co mi wari kange kom ki kutangka dina wo can neu mu nyomyeba? Filibuc gwam niwo to yereri tom temi mwo tok mwo ki ye? nung nyi nenteu'?
JOH 14:10 mwa nebo bilengke mworte, yilo te mwor mi ra? kero buro mayikom tiyeu, kebo liyar mir kom ticike co teu yim fwermir co ma nangen cero tiye
JOH 14:11 kom bilengke miki no fwerte co tee ki no fwer mira? tano nyori kom ne bilengke nangnan ciyero min.
JOH 14:12 bilengke mi yikom tiye gwam niwo ne bilengke mkange moweu can ma nangen do mi matiye can ma nange do la wure mi miki firen tenin.
JOH 14:13 gwam dige kom ki nonge ki den mireu man mani na caklang tee mwor bwe.
JOH 14:14 no kom me bwentano nye ki den mirdi man mani.
JOH 14:15 no kom cwiyeri can ciya werfumermiro,
JOH 14:16 nan kwab ki men dulo ki tee catin ne kom ni kange wuro a yob ki men nertiye na yi wari kange kom diri.
JOH 14:17 bweldokendo kale daten a yotiyeu, kambo ci tobeu ci yombeu dila kumeu ki nyomco dige bwiyeu ci wari kange kom catin no wari biber ki mer.
JOH 14:18 mani ma dob komti ki kwakom man yilau kimen.
JOH 14:19 tangnim kumenim bikwen ce kale an bwan na toye tak dila kume ki toyeti dige bwiye mi kwarce kume kenen kan fulo.
JOH 14:20 ki diye kume wuro kan nyomom miki no fuwet te'e mir kom keneu kom ki no fuwer mir miyu keneu fuwer ki met.
JOH 14:21 co ni wuron ki werfun mireu yilo ci bwangtenti co ci bilangye tiye yilo ni wo cwiyetiye te'emi an no kange co. mo kenneu bilang co nan nung bilangka dor miro cinen.
JOH 14:22 Yafuda (kebo Ickariyoti ba) can yi kiritti teluwe nye bwi mwa nung dor mweroti yinene la mu nungbo kalenine?”
JOH 14:23 kiritti ciya, yi co wo bi langyetiyeri can tam kermiro yora temi an cwico. banbo cinen na bi yi wari kange co
JOH 14:24 ni wo bilangyebeu ci bilangbo taka kermiro kero ci nuwau cerubo minen ceru firen teminin wo to mu yere.
JOH 14:25 min yi kom dege wuro gwam ki kwama bi wari kange kome.
JOH 14:26 kan co niwa ki bi bwiyer bi com wo kendo te'e tomu ki dencer na yi kom digero gwam mi yi kome
JOH 14:27 ma dob ki fuwarnerer, mi ne kom fuwor nerer. kebo nawo kale tiye netiye nyo ner kumero a kayare yilo ki cware twai.
JOH 14:28 kom nuwam mingyikom. man cu yilo fo kumen, no bilangy yitiri kan fuwor nerer na yaken firen te'e-nin wori te'e laye bi dwiyer
JOH 14:29 can neu min yim kom na yim de bwi, tano bwiri kom ne bilengke.
JOH 14:30 mani ma kwab tokka kerekti kange. kom cho nyeu nii toka kalewuro wi bouti. chi man kibi kwan dormir,
JOH 14:31 na cho nyeu kaleu an nyimom dor cher me chwii teemi, mi ma nyeu cho te'e neye bi kwan kerede. daten bi kwenum chii nabiya na fiye wuro.
JOH 15:1 “mo mi ti biyuware bicom te'e mi ni tome.
JOH 15:2 co ki cukom cwangko wo gwam mani ne bi tutti wuro ne bitutti tiyeu an yulangum na ne bitutti yora,
JOH 15:3 com caneu witi mani bwikimi na kere kendo mi yimkom yiye.
JOH 15:4 ki yi fwermir mo keneu nan yi fwerkumed. tami kani tiye wuro mani ne bitutti ki kwaco ki no tiwi bwitiyen na numde, nyo kume ken mani ka do makadi ka no bwimi.
JOH 15:5 mo mi te'e kom ki kani ceu. wuro wi bwimiyeri la mo mi bwici, can ne kani ducce, tano mi maniri mani mwa dol digerti.
JOH 15:6 tano ni win ko yika bwimiri catin mirangcowi na cwang di kucum.
JOH 15:7 no mun wi bwimi la kermiro wi munen di, me'e diye mu cwitiye, di ciya tin mamwen.
JOH 15:8 nyo ciki bilangde bi bwiyer temire nakom nyimom bi beiyo lomiye.
JOH 15:9 kombo te'e mi bilang komeu kambo mi bilang kome, kom yi mwor bilangka.
JOH 15:10 no kom bwangten werfundodi, kangyi mwor cwika nawuro mi bwangten mi bwangten werfun te'e miro la min yiken mwor cwikacer.
JOH 15:11 mi yi komti na kulentini dige buro fuwor ner kumero na nowi biber kimet la fuwor ner kumero na dim diye.
JOH 15:12 muro co kermiro na kom cwii buti kumi nawo na wo mi cwi kome.
JOH 15:13 ni kange mani cwi kakko cum nawe naco neken ner cero kiden farub ceb.
JOH 15:14 kom farub mib na kom ma digewu miyi komeri.
JOH 15:15 ferer kab mani ma yog cuwoka kumeti, bi bei canga dige bwiyeu bwe canga nyombo dige teluwe ce matiye. mi cuwo kom farub mib nan nyi kom dige gwam ma nuwa te'e mi nin ne'e.
JOH 15:16 kebo kom ki cok yere lamo mi cok kome, mi tom kom na kom ya na kom ne bi bei, ma tom kom ki ne bibeiyo na wo cokke.
JOH 15:17 ker bifumero mayi kome nakom cwi butikimi.
JOH 15:18 no kale ko komdi, kom nyomom koye na nimde ko kom.
JOH 15:19 na ki kom na kale cedi, no kale tin cwikom tami nace.
JOH 15:20 kom kwa ki kero ma yi koe, ki ciya kermirori la kan ciya kermiro.
JOH 15:21 ci yan ma kimen dige tinimbo wuro ki den mir, la ci nyombo niwo tomuyereu.
JOH 15:22 na ki ma bou bo nan nyi ci kerdi no ci manki bwirangke, la canneu ci manki kangke kan bwirangke.
JOH 15:23 gwam ni wo ko yereu ko te'e mi.
JOH 15:24 na ki mi mabo nangendodori no ni kange mani momwi tiber ciyere. no ci manki bwirangke la canneu cintom la cin ko nye kange te'e mi gwam
JOH 15:25 dige wuro ci maneu nadim kero mulangum mwor bifumere, cin koye manki tuwer kercer.
JOH 15:26 kambo nii birumreri we ma tomki menti firen tee nin, bilengke bibwiyer woki cetde bwi tee ninne an bo na ne warka dormir
JOH 15:27 kume kom ne warke na wo kom wari kange mo nyo ki kaba.
JOH 16:1 “mi yi kom wo ka kom kottangi
JOH 16:2 ciyan cokom loniwabi dilla keneber, wuro cano kange twalkom, amkabi ciki ma nangen kwamar.
JOH 16:3 ciyan mani nyo wori ci yombo te'eu kaka'a mo.
JOH 16:4 miyi kom dikero brombo cano ki kwama dico abwiutiyeu lamri, kom kwabi min yi kom minyikom.
JOH 16:5 na weu miki yang wo twomuyerenin, kom kwarub more kume kange me yobo. muki yangfe?'
JOH 16:6 wori minyi kom dige birombo, finnerero dimkom.
JOH 16:7 la min yi kom bilengketi. an lakumen diger noncuri. can no mi cubori, nii birim nerembo mani bouti kumen, incuri, man twomuco kumen.
JOH 16:8 no bouri andang kale nin digero bwir kange bwirangke, kange luma, kange warka.
JOH 16:9 la bwirangkeu, wori ci ciyabo kange mo,
JOH 16:10 la lumako, wori miki fiye tee wiyeu, dila mani ka toten yeti,
JOH 16:11 la kange warka, wori cin mwati ni liyar kalero woni warka.
JOH 16:12 dikonwi kila wo ma yi kom tiye, dila mani kanyomti cana ko wo.
JOH 16:13 no wori, kanbo yuwa tambe bilengke bou weri, an bwanteng ki kom mor bilengke kwarub, wori mani tokker dorer certi, kandike can nuwa, catok tike a bwiutiyeu.
JOH 16:14 anduktangye, wori antu'u digerowo namiyeu yikom.
JOH 16:15 kwarub dige tee cikeu, nami. wonco digebwimiki atu'u dige na miyeu yicom.
JOH 16:16 “katen biduwardi, mani kato yeti tak. kakten biduwar takri, kantoye.”
JOH 16:17 la kangum mor nob bwanka cebonin me bwiti ceti, ye wuro yibo tiye, kakten biduwardi mani ka toyeti, kakten biduwardi, kamtoye? takri man yaken teenin?”
JOH 16:18 lauki inye wuro tok tiye,” kakten biduwardi? nya nyombo dige ci yi nyo tiyeu.”
JOH 16:19 Yeecu tori ci cwiti naci meco, lan yici “lakomki me bwiti dikirowo ma toki mii. kakten biduwar mani katoyeti, kakten biduwar takri kantoye'?
JOH 16:20 bilengke, bilengke, mi yi komti, kanciwiye kange bwatum, dila dorbitinero anma fuworneret, kandim ki neret, dila firneret kumero an yilam fuwor neret.
JOH 16:21 no wiye an nuwa buwarum ki kwama bore wori kwama boreu lam. lakambo cibom bweri, mani ca kwati ki buwarum tak, wori cima fuwor nererti cinbo nifir dorbitiner.
JOH 16:22 naweu kom firnerer, la matoten kom, ni kange mani ciyomfuwor nerero wotiye.
JOH 16:23 ki ka kuwo, mani kom meye diger. bilengke, miyi komti, kwarub dige komken tee mor den mirori an ne kom.
JOH 16:24 wo diduwene kowo ka kenbo diger mor den mir. ko keni, kanyo, na fuwor nerer kumer yilam cikocok.
JOH 16:25 mi yi kom dige birombo mor danke. dila kume wiber nawo mani ma yentenkom kerti mor danke, nyori mayikom kero denemi lama yibo miman kwobdilo nyamglang dor tee mir.
JOH 16:26 ki kakuwo, ka ken kenito mor denemi lama yibo miman kwobdilo nyikom tee minin,
JOH 16:27 wor tee ki bwi komti, wori kom cwiye, kom ne bilengke micirou teenin.
JOH 16:28 ma ciro teenin lama dou dorbitinere. man dob dor bitinerowo miki yilang teenin.”
JOH 16:29 nob bwankacebo yiki, to,”can lamu tok keroti nyanglang, kebo mor danke'
JOH 16:30 na weu nyin nyumom mwa nyumom digero kwarub, kange nonin menen. la nyo nya nebilengke mwa coro kwama nin.”
JOH 16:31 Yeecu ciyaci, naweu kane bilengke?
JOH 16:32 to, kwama winber, nyo, kwamaco lam ciya cutangten kom fiweu, kan yilarangen loco, kadobye ki kwami. naweu miki kwami nin tee wi kange mo.
JOH 16:33 ma tokwo na kume fuwor nerero dim. kom nuwa dotangeti dor bitiner, dila kom biner wori min can kaba kange dor bitiner.”
JOH 17:1 kambo Yeecu tok nyeri, kun nuweceu dii. yiki, kan keneko lam, duktang bikwe mwe, na bweu duktangnen.
JOH 17:2 kambo nuwa neco bikwan dor bibwe nifireu naci necii dume wo mwa neco manki dika.
JOH 17:3 won dume manki dika: ciya nyimom nen, mun kwama wincwar nii bilengke, kangeco mwa twomuweu, Yeecu kiritti.
JOH 17:4 min duktangnen dor bitiner, mindim na'nyendo muneyereu.
JOH 17:5 naweu tee kwama, duktangye wari kange mo kiduktangka ko miciko wari kange mo kikaba nyime dor bitinero no wiyeu.
JOH 17:6 min fwetang nubowo mwaneye dor bitinereu den mwero. cine mwe, mun neken yeci, cin yo mwero.
JOH 17:7 canneu cin nyimom dikero mwaneyereu munen kwarub,
JOH 17:8 min neken ci kero muneyereu gwam. cin yo cin nyimom ma cirou munen, dicine bilengke mwo mu twom yere.
JOH 17:9 min kwob cinen dilo. miki kwom dilo kici nubo muneyere kebo dor bitiner, wori cina mwe.
JOH 17:10 wuyak dike na mweu nami, dige namiyeu na mwe, min duktangci.
JOH 17:11 naweu mimani dorbitiner, nubowe kino dorbitiner, miki yang munen.
JOH 17:12 Tee wucakke. tannci mor dene mweu mwaneyereu naci yilam win, kambo bi wiwineu.
JOH 17:13 mi bouti munwn, dila mi tok dikewoti dorbitiner na fuwor nerer miro dim.
JOH 17:14 min neci ker mwero, dila dorbitinero koci wori ci kebo na dorbitineroce, kambo mi kebo na dorbitineroceu.
JOH 17:15 miken nenbo na tumci dorbitiner, dila na tamci yora fiye nubo bwirko wiyeu.
JOH 17:16 cikebo na dorbitineroce, kambo mi kebo na dorbitineroceu,
JOH 17:17 yo kenci nadore mwece dorbilengker. ker mwero bilengke.
JOH 17:18 nawo mu twomye dorbitinreu, mi twomci nyo dorbitiner.
JOH 17:19 min yoken dormiro munen kercir, na cekenciyoken dor ciro ker mwer.
JOH 17:20 kebo kawo mi kwob dilo tiye, kange birombo a ne bilinti keti minen ki ker mwereu,
JOH 17:21 naci yilamwin tee kwama kambo mu more miyeu, miti keni naci nowi more be na dorbitinerowo nebilengke mwo mu twomu yere.
JOH 17:22 duktangkako mu neyereu, min naci, yilam win, kambo biwineu.
JOH 17:23 ci moremi, mu more me. nabe ci yilam win, na dorbitinero nyumom mwo mu twomyere, na cwici kambo mu cwiyereu.
JOH 17:24 tee mi cwiti nubo muneyereu a no kange mo fiye mi wiyeu, nacito duktangkako mu neyereu. wori mun cwiye ki kabo ywelka dorbiner.
JOH 17:25 tee wucakkeu, dorbitinero nyom nenbo, la min nyumom nen, labirombo nyimwom mwo mu twom yere.
JOH 17:26 min dokci cin nyimwom den mwero, man yitenci na cwikako mu mameneu na morece, mi keneu nan no more ce.”
JOH 18:1 kambo Yeesu tokum kero weni, ceri kange nob bwangka cebo cin yaken cu'nga cunnukur kidiron, fiye fotewiyeu cindo kenwi ci kange nob bwangka cebo.
JOH 18:2 naweu Yafuda niwo a nekoncotiyeu, nyumom fiyeco, wori Yeesu ki bow nyowi kange nob bwangke cebo.
JOH 18:3 la Yafuda, tinobda keboni kaba kange durem cimbo kanye fiye liya wabe ni kange farisawa, cin ki kira wenka kange kulen kiyaned.
JOH 18:4 kambo Yeesu nyimom digero yaken dorcereuri, ciro kab meci, “we ko dotiye?”
JOH 18:5 cin ciya co “Yeesu bwe najanret.” Yeesu yicii, Inmo.” Yafuda niwo neken cen tim kange no dakebo.
JOH 18:6 kambo ciyi cii ki” inmo,” ciin yilanken bwii ciin yarken bitine,
JOH 18:7 yilam meten ci tak, “we kom dotiye?” cin ciyaco Yeesu bwe najaret?”
JOH 18:8 Yeesu ciya ci, min yikom inmo. non mo citiyeri, kom dob birombo a yakenti.”
JOH 18:9 wonadim kero citokeu. “mor nubo mwa neyereu, winwo lebo.”
JOH 18:10 Simon Bitrus niwo ki kulenneu, coku kwalum tuwo cacci yere wo bibwetomange nii wabe. den bwetomange co markus.
JOH 18:11 Yeesu inyi Bitrus, dokken kulendo morloco. mani ma no kweelmunge tee neyeretiya?”
JOH 18:12 dila nob dakebo kange duciro kange nob dirlor Yafudawa ko tam Yeesu, ciin bwamco.
JOH 18:13 ciin yakico kikaba Annas nen tee kon Kayafas nii wabe durko choroceu.
JOH 18:14 Kayafas coni ne Yafudawa yuiande ki ladiker nii win abuyam kange nubo kilanyeu.
JOH 18:15 Simon Bitrus bwangtang Yeesu, nyo kange nii bwangka mane. nii bwangka kowa nyumom dur webebo, doken kange co mor luwece.
JOH 18:16 dila Bitrus tim nyilo kalek. dila nii bwangka ko nyimom liya wabe durken coru'u kale tokker kange nawiye to nyilok tiyen la dubom Bitrus dom mor.
JOH 18:17 dila nawiye to yilok kotiyeu yi Bitrus, mumani mor nob bwangka niwo ka?” yiki, kebo mo.”
JOH 18:18 naweu can nyabo kange nubo to lowabe tiyeu tirannyumwi, ci cukirati, wari cweto wi Bitrus tim wari kangeci cukirati.
JOH 18:19 dur lowabero me Yeesu nob bwangka cebo kange merangka ceko
JOH 18:20 Yeesu ciyaco minyi dorbitinero kero nyanglang. kwati bak mi ma merangketi mor bikur kwamar fiye Yafudawa mwerumti gwammeu matokbo diger yurangum yurange. ye bwi mu meryere? ye bwi mu merere? me birombo nuwa dige mi tokeu. nubo nubo wuro nyumom dige mitokeu.”
JOH 18:22 kambo Yeesu tok weri, kange mor nobdirlob tim wi cwuwa Yeesu in yiki, mu ciya durwebero ninti nyo.”
JOH 18:23 Yeesu in ciyaco toki, “nomatok kero bwirdi yiye tano kebo naki yanecer, yebwe mwa cuwatiye?
JOH 18:24 la Hananiya tungen Yeesu Kayafa nin niwabe dur.
JOH 18:25 Simon Bitrus tim we cukirati. nubo meco, “mu mani mor nob kwangka ceba? wengkangum ki, kebo mo.”
JOH 18:26 win mor canga ni wabe, inke wiwo ci cwalum tuwo, yiki, mi to nenbo kange co mor foti?
JOH 18:27 Bitrus wengkangum tak, dangjang bicakeu mob. kiyyangeu.
JOH 18:28 la cin yaken ki Yeesu karak lirya ko durko. kin kwomce, ciki dorcer cidobe karak lirya ko durkonin, wori ci cwibo ci fwe ki caka kwaka ciko.
JOH 18:29 la Bilatu ceru'u bom meci kom bou ciko dor niwore?”
JOH 18:30 “cin ciya ciki,” cano nii wo mani ma dige bwira bwiratiri, diger mani a dok yoti nya bouti ki kiyange ce munene.”
JOH 18:31 Bilatu yicii, kom yanken kico kibwikom ko warco nawo. warka kume tokeu.” dila Yafudawa yico, nyi man ki bikwan nyin warni nin bolang.”
JOH 18:32 citok wuro nadim kero Yeesu tokeu, wuro dang dorabuwa wo ca matinyeu.
JOH 18:33 la Bilatus yilam doken karak cou Yeesu yico ki, liya Yafudawa?”
JOH 18:34 wontok mwek kaka'a kannyemnob yinen ker miro?
JOH 18:35 Bilatus ciya coki mi kebo “Bayafudeka?” innubo lomwe kange liya wabe cibou ki nen, “ye mu mane?”
JOH 18:36 Yeesu yico, “liyar miro kebo na dorbitineroce. liyar miro na dorbitineroceri, nob bwangka miko kin tekwen katiyolo cinekenye kang Yafudawa liyar miro kebo fo”

JOH 18:38 kambo cito kweri, Bilatus meco, “kerbilengkeryer?” yilam cerin ya Yafudawa nin yici, mifeyabo niwo ki bwirangke.

JOH 19:1 Bilatus mali Yeesu.
JOH 19:2 nob gwam nebo ku yilang duwe la cin yo Yeesu neti dor cin mer ciyene beller liyar.
JOH 19:3 cin bo fiye co wiye ciki dumwe a kutange liya Yafudawa. la ci tee co.
JOH 19:4 Bilatus yila ceri kale yi ci to man bo kumen ki nii co be no kom nyomom mafiya cubo ki kange bwirangke”
JOH 19:5 Yeesu cero ki yilangk duwek cwakek kange kure na liyaro ce Bilatus ki nii co wo.
JOH 19:6 kange nobo dur webero wali kange tikertiyeu cin tam Yeesu, dila ci kwakiyyangti ciki a kulkenso, kulkenso la Bilatu ki kom tuco kom kulken mi mafiya chobo ki kerobwidi.”
JOH 19:7 la Yafudawa ci yi coki yonweki bwirangka kange nurwarka con daten bwar wori cin nyoken dorcero na bi bwe kwama”

JOH 19:9 yila daten bwar kun gwam na, nyi Yeesu mocelufe?” layecu bciya cinen bo.

JOH 19:11 Yeesu diye cine, mo manki be gwam dor mi naci, ne nefiren di kwamari, nyori wo neke ye moneneu co nii bwirangkeu,”
JOH 19:12 dila co nuwa nyori, la Bilatu mani naci yemgum kancine, la Yafudawa kun dir ciyero ciki na mo nyongum nii wo nindi bo kebo farar kaicar no nii wo tuken dor cero na liyari, in kan kaicar ni.
JOH 19:13 la Bilatu nurank kero belonabo la celu ki Yeesu kare nyara. nyike kabum kutirece fiye cico tike fiye bwirangke wo Yafudawa co tiki Gabbata”
JOH 19:14 ki kakukowo ci yelank, lank dulubme yamkati, ki kwama kene nukune. la ki kakun, Bilatu yi Yafudawa “liya kume wo”

JOH 19:16 la Bilatu nici Yeesu naci kulken co.
JOH 19:17 la cin yeken ki Yeesu cero ki beteren bwiti yakenti cuika fiwo Yafudawa coti ki golgota”
JOH 19:18 cin kulken Yeesu fiye co nobo kangum nyob, kulken ci Yeesu la tiber cinyer.
JOH 19:19 Bilatu mulangti yurombo dor bentilen bwetiye YEESU BANAZARE, LIYA YAFUDAWA.
JOH 19:20 Yafuda duco cin kiye yurom bowo wori fiye ci nyom Yeesu wiyeu bi dom kange cinalou.
JOH 19:21 la nobo dur waber Yafudawa, ci yi Bilatu ki mulangti muki liya Yafudawa. mulang moki yiki co liya Yafudawa.””
JOH 19:22 Bilatu ciya, ki dii kewo co.
JOH 19:23 la nob bi gwanem cin kulken Yeesu ci worangum billeceu kifiti nyo nar, nob bigwanebo ki ciye, yilank ciyegu woranm tau dii yanken cu co bitine.
JOH 19:24 la ciyi bwiti tii cike bo worak bilengke ci nyib dige co toke birinka wori kom ki kom ne bilengke
JOH 19:25 nob bigwan nebo balangum dikge wo no Yeesu, kange yitim cobo kange maryamu weikilofa, kange maryamu magadaliya. natuwo tim bidom kange fiye ci nyom Yeesu wii ye.
JOH 19:26 la Yeesu to neceri kange nii bwangka wo co cwitiye tem bidom, yiki to na we to be bweme.”
JOH 19:27 la to nii bwanka, to nemwen nob bwangka ce co tuco yangke co ko lo.
JOH 19:28 na wo nyeu Yeesu nyumom digero mor kwamare ma dim. la nyi ciki co nuwa durometi
JOH 19:29 cwi kanciyen kollo timwe ki mwebo fur cin doti cukko mwero bwotiye kange cin neco nico.
JOH 19:30 la Yeesu cun mobowo furi nyori “laye ciki dim la cunke ki dor cero lademkan dume ce ni.
JOH 19:31 la Yafudawa, wori kakun yerank kari ci domti bwiciye dor bantilank bwe tiye na yaken kaku foka (wori kakun furkako nyori fiyeci weye) cin kinan Bilatu na ciyeco na cugum ci
JOH 19:32 la nob bigwannebo bo. kiyalum na nubo burumbo nii kaba nii yobe bulo ci yuci wori kange Yeesu.
JOH 19:33 cin bou cifiya Yeesu bweyam ci keyanbo na ciyeko.
JOH 19:34 dila wii nob bi gwanne boning gwico kiya dange buyare kange mwebo ti ceri.
JOH 19:35 buro towo ciya yilam nii warka. warka ceco birinke.
JOH 19:36 ci tokwo naci dim bifumer kwamaro kunko kange mani wo ciya kiyan tiye.”
JOH 19:37 kange bifumero toki, bon nii wo cikwareu.
JOH 19:38 bwiko dige borumbo, Yusufu nii Armatiya, con wi win mor nob tomange Yeesu, dila temi tai Yafudawa, yaken Bilatu a naco bwi Yeesu. Bilatu neco, Yusufu bõti bwiyo.
JOH 19:39 ni ko dimu ken bõ wuro ki kabo bõ Yeesu nin ki dila bõnuwan ficange womur doceu kange alul wo lam tutum cwanka kweni kwabe.
JOH 19:40 dila ci tuti bwi Yeesu ciyoken co yilanforka kange nuko ficen ficenye. naci yimkan bõ na nur banka Yafudawa ceu.
JOH 19:41 fiye ciya ci yumce we kange tekewi, muro tekeu tuwe kangewi woci forumbo nii weye.
JOH 19:42 du waleu kaku yolanka Yafudawa tuwe bi la ci dogken Yeesu borece.
JOH 20:1 ki kwamaco kangko win mor kume nibere tangum kumebo we, maryamu Magadaliya bo tuweu ni co fiya cin berum tero tuwenin.
JOH 20:2 yila takacon fiya Saminu Bitrus wari kange nob nanetbowo Yeesu cwitiyeu con yici cin tom teluwe we tuwenin yo yombo ciye ci yomco.
JOH 20:3 la Bitrus wari kange nob tomangeceu cin ceri, yakanke tuwenin,
JOH 20:4 gwam ciye cin tacoke wori, dila win mor bibei bwenkaco yulum Bitrus lakaco tuwe.
JOH 20:5 la tolari fiyaka yilang fwerka la dobo morece.
JOH 20:6 la Saminu Bitrus yauki bwiyi la do tuweni to ka ye lank fwerka yomwi.
JOH 20:7 kan yilanko wene dorcero ciyabu wari kange yilan fwerkaka cin kumu cin yoke co ki kwace.
JOH 20:8 dila bei tomangece wo yaken ten wolom tuwetinen danuwe to la ne bilengke.
JOH 20:9 yaken ki kwama wo ci nyobo bifumer wo yiki ankanu bore.
JOH 20:10 la bi bei bwonkace cin yelanken lo'o tok.
JOH 20:11 la Maryamu tim we tuwene ciwuyeti. co mor wuyeri cunge to tuweu.
JOH 20:12 Yeesu yico “Maryamu” laco yilak yico ki a mani ya na “rabboni” nii merangka.
JOH 20:13 Yeesu yico ki mana wiye meyere, mikubo dii kwama, yauce wifiye kemwebo yici muki yanfiye tekume wiye, kange tekume kwama mi kange kwama kume”
JOH 20:14 Maryamu Magadaliya yayi bibei kwangka ce ko, man to teluwe” nyila yiki co diroke buro.
JOH 20:15 diye kaba win na kume niberoce, bi beibwangka ceka cin dokenku ciki coya Yafudawa, Yeesu boti tiber ciyer ki bi bwege fu kume.”
JOH 20:16 con to bi bei tomangce wucakeu nyo yob tiram ki kulle do fwewor win tim dorcer, win nacek fiye ci fwerum Yeesu.
JOH 20:17 cin meco ki nawiye yemocitiye? ki wori cin tum teluweceu man yombo fiye ci yamki co weyeu.
JOH 20:18 Maryamu Magadaliya cin bou ci yi bi beitonga cin to teluwe la tokke nyo cinnen.
JOH 20:19 Diye co kime, kume win mor nibere nyiloko wo bibei tomange ce wiyeu nungun -nunge, tai Yahudawa ci nuwatiye, Yesu boun ti tiber ciyer, Yii cii fuwor neerer kumen.
JOH 20:20 Kambo co tok nyeri con nung cinen kang ceko kange cu-nka ceko, bibei tomange bilange kambo ci to Yeesu.
JOH 20:21 Yeesu yi ci ki bibweyed ki no kumen”nawo teluwe tomyere, moma mi tomkomti.”
JOH 20:22 dila Yeesu dim tonkageli la funci ki yuwa komyo tembekoma.
JOH 20:23 nii wo kom citanci nen bwerangke ceu wiyeri, cin citencinen wi, nii wo kan tim bwirangke keceri cin tim bwirangkeceu”
JOH 20:24 tomawin mor kwob cilombo yobe, wo ci cuti ki biboyetagwai, mani ki kwama wo Yeesu bou cinenen.
JOH 20:25 tangnum nob tomangebo yico ki nyo to teluwe” tano ma tõ bo buwak tinim to terangkangce kiri, na dor bi wer kange mi buwak ko terange nineu, take nan dokti kangmico yare cank cank cekdi mani ma ne bilengketi.
JOH 20:26 kume nalub bei bokangceko wuranin mor luwe, toma wi wari cange ci nyiroko nuwang, nuwage cin to Yeesu tiber ciyet ki bi bwiyet ki kom”
JOH 20:27 layi toma to kangmiko. naneu kang mwe ko tenye nabo ne birinke? bi bwiyet ki nii wo toyebe lane birinke mine.”
JOH 20:28 toma ciya ki, teluwe mi kange kwama mi.”
JOH 20:29 Yeesu yi co ki lamuto comunen bilengke? bi bwiyet kine wo teyebe lane bilengke mine.
JOH 20:30 Yeesu ma yunbom kilang kilang fiye nob bwangka ce wiye, wo ciye murangbo mor bifumer kwamaro ninen
JOH 20:31 la ci murang wo nyo na kong ne birinke Yeesu co Almacihu, be bwe kwama ki bilengke be boneyeu co bi fiyam dume ki dencere.
JOH 21:1 ki bwii nyori dang dorcero nobbwangka cebo ni nyi caji tibariya. Yeesu dang dorcero nawo.
JOH 21:2 Simon Bitrus wari kange tomas wo ci cwiti ki dan tangwai, kange Natanai'ilu wuro biten Galiliyeu, bibwe Zabedi kange nob bwangka Yeesu nyo yob.
JOH 21:3 Simon Bitrus yiciki,”miki yang taka jinnye.” cikin “nyiki yang wi ken kannyeco.”yacin doken mor tukomem dila citabo diger winwo kume co.
JOH 21:4 kanbo fini dadom celkari Yeesu bou ti kabum munyem, dila nob bwangka cebo nyombo kin Yeesu.
JOH 21:5 la Yeesu meci, Nabbarob, kom wiki dige ka catiya? cin ciya co, mani
JOH 21:6 lamyici, kom merken biliyan kumerofo kangko catiyer tukomero nin, kantau. cin merken bilinyaro la cii dolbo kwoba wori jinye ducce.
JOH 21:7 la ni bwangka ko wo Yeesu cwitiyeu yi Bitrus ki won kwama”kambo Simon Bitrus mor mu nye (wori ci kwanger), yanken mor munye.
JOH 21:8 la tangne nob bwangka cebo bou cinen mor bentilen mwemmer, wori ci kutangbo kange kong munyeu, kutangka ceko nako kuni kwobyob yaken dii ci kwobkang biliyaroti dimki jinnye.
JOH 21:9 kambo ci ceruweri, cnto korkirero jinye kange tiilita yomwe dorcer.
JOH 21:10 Yeesu yicii ki “ko bou ki jinye kotau canakeweu,”
JOH 21:11 la Simon Bitrus ya kwom biliyaro dimki jinye kadur, 153 morece, kange kilaka cikowo, biliyaro worabo.
JOH 21:12 Yeesu yicii “bokom camcarito.” Nimani mor nob bwangka cebo nin maco ki “munwe?” cin nyimom kwama
JOH 21:13 Yeesu boutu jinnye kange tiilita neci.
JOH 21:14 wonco taareceu Yeesu bouti nobbwangka cebo ninne kambo ci twenum tuweri.
JOH 21:15 kambo ci cam cariteri, Yeesu yicii, “Simon Bitrus bi bwe Yuwana, mucwiyeti lawa? Bitrus ciya nyo kwama mun nyumom mi cwinenti” Yeesu yico, “munyumom mi cwinenti.”
JOH 21:16 yitenco yõbem, man bibwe Yuwana, mu cwiyeti ya?” nyo kwama munyomom mi cwinenti.” Yeesu yico, Ato kwama niti.”
JOH 21:17 yitenco ta'arecou, “Simon bebwe Yeesu Yuwana, mu cwitiya? ner Bitrus ceco kanyam wo Yeesu meco kiriti ta'ar, “mu cwiyetiya?” la cin toki, “kwama, mun nyumom digero gwam, mun nyumom micwinenti Yeesu in yico, “ne kwamemiu carito.
JOH 21:18 bilengke bilengke, miyinenti, ki kwama mun bwe bwayileu, mu bwador mweronin dakko tiye, nanyime muya fiye mu cwitiye. tano mu ciramdi, mwantar kangmwoko nakange bwamwen dakko, nakinen fiye mu kwabo yaka.”
JOH 21:19 Yeesu tokkerowo na ci dang Bitrunin na nyomom buwaro camatiyeu na duktangka kwama keceu. kambo citoki nyeri lamyi Bitrus, bwangum ye.”
JOH 21:20 Bitrus yila nuwari to nii bwangkakowo Yeesu cwitiyeu bwangcinentinti, niwo nyimom diger ki kaba dor Yeesur ki kwama wo cica caritori yiki, “kwama we niwo a neken nentiye?”
JOH 21:21 Bitrus toco lanyi Yeesu, “kwama, inye wuro matiye?”
JOH 21:22 Yeesu yila yico “no mika ciya nintangye nanbouri, yeyonen wiye? bwouye,”
JOH 21:23 dila kerowo yatti kebcebo nin ki ni bwangkakowo mani buyati, Yeesu yibo Bitrus, ki ni bwangkakowo mani buyati, la cano mi cwiti nayi kange mori yeyonen wiye?”
JOH 21:24 wonco ni bwangka kowo tok keroburombotiye, woci mulangeu, la nyin nyimom kecoro bilengke.
JOH 21:25 dikero kan nyumbo witak wo Yeesu maneu. nacin bulangi kwarub kiwinti kiwintiri, miyi komti nero kibroco mani tu bifumero a mulangtiyeti.
ACT 1:1 Bifumero mi mulanyi kika, Theophilus in tok dikero Yesu ter makau la merange.
ACT 1:2 Na nyime diye cii tumou yaken dii kwama. Wo kambo cine nob tomangeb cebo cidoweu yuwatangbeke.
ACT 1:3 Kambo cinuwa dotangeri yadangu dorcero ciinen, ki yiromtinim dukce wo nyomkace. kume kwini naar ci dangu dorcero ciinene yi cii ker liyar kwamar
ACT 1:4 Kambo ci yi kange cii yeri in yi cii, ciya dobre wursalima dila ciya ningtang nor Teero, woci yiki, “Kom nuwa fiye mi wiyeu”
ACT 1:5 Yiti ki, cwerke man Yahaya yucinen mwembo kin wmom, dila ayukumen mwembo ki yuwa tangbeko wucakke, kume fo kutangbo”.
ACT 1:6 Kambo cii wariyeri cin meco Kwama ki kwamawo mwa yilauti ki liyar Israila ka?
ACT 1:7 Yi cii ki, a keno nakume nakom nyimom kan kenekowo kwama yo morbikwan durcereu.
ACT 1:8 Dila kom yo bikwando cano yuwatangbe kwamako bou dor kumerdi, lana nyime kan yilam nob wabebkeb min mor wursalima kange mor yahudiya gwam kange samariya, yaken ciko cwile dor bitinere”.
ACT 1:9 Ki kwama wo kwama Yesu tok kero birombem, kambo cito dii kwamatiyeri, dila cii tumco ciin yaken kico dii kwama, biloro yurangum co nuwece.
ACT 1:10 Kambo cii to dikwama ciya kenti yeri, dang jang nubo yob tim kaci ki kulendo fuwor.
ACT 1:11 Kom nabarubbo halili, yebwi kom tirangum fo komto dii kwamatiye? wuro Yesu yaken dii kwama, kambo kom tom yamcembeu dii kwamau ayilaunyo
ACT 1:12 Kambo cii yilau bany Zaitun cii yoten yilau wursalima wuro bidom kange wursalimau, yam kume nukkune ki dimen.
ACT 1:13 Kambo cii lameri, ciin yabken tiyak fiye cii yimtiyeu. ciin bi Bitrus, Yahaya, Yakubu, Andirawus, Filibus, Tomas Bartholomew, Matta, Yakubu bibwe Alfa Siman Yahuda bibwe Yakubu.
ACT 1:14 Gwam ce ciin mwerkang dorceo win, kambo cii ca kaba ki kwob dilo. Matta, Maryamu wo bo Yesu kange kebcoba cii wari.
ACT 1:15 Ki kume niwo Bitrus kweniti tiber kebceber, nubo kwini kwob toro kwini yob, yi cii.
ACT 1:16 keb mibo nii inwi wo ticiinen kaba ciitam Yesu.
ACT 1:17 Wifo morebe lan yom dike naceu dor dike cimaneu.
ACT 1:18 Niwo tenum bitine ki kemero cifiyau mor nagen bwirantum nerer cero, cin yaru wi kidor fwercero wurom, yeicero coru kale.
ACT 1:19 Nubo yimwi wursalima nuwam wo lacii cuwo fiyeco kin yicii “Akeldama” (Kiyiki fiye bwiyale).
ACT 1:20 Wori cii mulange mor bifumer Zaburad Lafiyeceu ayilam kamlo adobeni ayifiyeco kange atum nangen cero.
ACT 1:21 Nawori tamnyo win mor nubo wo wari kange bo ki kwama Yesu ma doka kange cerka ceko yeu, morebe.
ACT 1:22 Terti ki yuka mu ngek Yahaya yakaken ciko kakukowa cii tumco binenneu yaken dii kwama a yilam, win morebe fiye tokka ker kwenkacek.
ACT 1:23 Ciin dang nubo yob Yusufu woci choti ki Barsabbas, wotak ci cho dendo ki Justus kange Matthias.
ACT 1:24 Ciin kwob dilo ciiki, kwama mo mun yob ner nubere. dan nyinen wo mu coke morece yobewo.
ACT 1:25 Na tu nyi Yahuda fiye yahuda tiyangum meu yaken fiye”
ACT 1:26 Ciin mer dacendo dor ciir, dacendo yardor Matiyas dila ciin kiyeti co mor nob tomangeb Sulombo yobeu.
ACT 2:1 Kambo kume fentikos co bouwori, kwarubce ciin mwerum fiye win.
ACT 2:2 Nawo nawo diro kange wi dikwama na yuwako dur, yiram dim luweu cii yim wiyeu.
ACT 2:3 labiyondo kange na biyen kiret layiron cilnenti dor.
ACT 2:4 Ciin dimki yuwa tangbe kwama lacin ter tokka kereki nyini kangum kambo yuwa tangbe kwamako dang cinenneu.
ACT 2:5 Ki kwama co Yahudawa kangum wi yim wursalima, nob kwamabo fo dorbitiner.
ACT 2:6 Kambo cii nuwa diroweri, nubo gwam mwerum cii mor ciin nuwa nubo tikkan keroti kin yici.
ACT 2:7 Ciin to diker nyimankar laciiki, kibi chom birombo kebo Galiliyawaka?
ACT 2:8 manyi bi nuwa citi wiyak wuyakce cii tok nyowo cii bombotiye?
ACT 2:9 Fisiyawa kange mediyawa kange Elimawa, kange Yahudawa kange Kafadokiya, mor Pontus kange Asia.
ACT 2:10 Phrygia kange Pamphylia, mor Masar kange sunga libiya wo sur receu, kange fabubbo Roma.
ACT 2:11 Yahudawa kange proselyte, cretans kange arabian, be nuwa tokkeroti kin nyibo dor nangebdo durembo kwama maneu.
ACT 2:12 Gwam ciin nyimangi ciin yi bwiticeu, Yewo toktiye?
ACT 2:13 Kan nyumbo buwocii ki, ciin diim ki nyom.
ACT 2:14 Dila Bitrus kweni kange sulombo yobem, kundiro tok kerki “Nubo yahuda kange kom kwarub kom yim wursalima, kom nyimomwo, ko suwatuu ker mironin.
ACT 2:15 Nubowo ci dimbo diye ki nyom kambo kom kwatiyeu, wori kene Teer na burice koni.
ACT 2:16 dila won co dike toki ywel neneu nii ker dukumer.
ACT 2:17 Kwama ki nyo a yilati cwile kume, man coru yuwatangbeko dor nuber, bi biyolokumeu bayilob kange natub ciyan tokker dukumer.
ACT 2:18 Nyo tak dor caan yabmib bayilob kange natub, kikuke tindowe man corum yuwatangbe miko, laciyan tok ker dukumer.
ACT 2:19 man madiker nyimakar dii kwama kange dor bitiner, bwiyale kange kira, kange yilom.
ACT 2:20 kakokko an yilam kumtachile, chuwakko ayilam bwiyale nanyime kume durkowo kwamaceu nabou.
ACT 2:21 an yilam woco den kwama an fiya fuloka.
ACT 2:22 Nubo Israila kom cuwatuu kero birombonen. Yesu banzared niwo kwama nekom wuro kwama ma nangen durem more kume fiyeci wuyeu, nawo komki bwikom kanyimeu.
ACT 2:23 Nii wo ciin neken co kan nage kange yobka kwama cii neken co kom keneu kang nubo yombo ker kwamareu cii twalum ki kuldange.
ACT 2:24 Wo kwama kungun co cokeinen twirak buwareko cinenneu, wo mani natamce.
ACT 2:25 Dauda tokker donce ki kwamati kami ngir wori cin wi cunga kange cattiyeri katin mikannge.
ACT 2:26 Lanyori nermiro ma fuwer nerti biyel miro ti bilenke. Labwimiu anyi kibi kwan.
ACT 2:27 mani mu minang dumemitiwi manu do wucakke mweti a to fuyenin.
ACT 2:28 Dang men nure dumeu, nawo tikob mwebo adim yeti ki fuwor nereu.
ACT 2:29 Keb mibo man yikom ker nyanglang dor Tee Dauda: buyam ciin furomco dila tuweceu wifo wari kange bo di duwenokowo.
ACT 2:30 Nyori wori cin nii ker dukumer dila nyimom kwama macinen nor kiweri ki, mor tuwe luwe mwe man yoti kange kutile liyar cero nen.
ACT 2:31 Cin tou dikero wo dila tok kero dor kwentka kriti mani cii ma bilankiya kange co fiye morka dumek, bwiceu tobo fuyeka.
ACT 2:32 Wo Yesu wo kwama kunco wuro wuyakbe bin nyimom.
ACT 2:33 Nyori kambo cii kunco yaken kanka cattiyere kwamau dila nyo mor yuwa tangbe kwamako fiye Tee wiyeu coci corbinenneu wo komtoti takri kom nuwatiyeu.
ACT 2:34 Dauda kwibo dii dila yiki kwama dila toki kwama nyi Teeluwemiu yiken kango cattiyeremi.
ACT 2:35 Dila man yoken nob kiyeb mwebbo diker fuwaka namwek.
ACT 2:36 La nyori, naweu lo Israila a nyomom kang Yesu wo cii kulkenen kwama yoken co kwama kange kritti.
ACT 2:37 Cii nuwa nyori la kwerci nercer cii yi Bitrus kange tannineu nob tomangeb cebo. “Keb mibo ye ba matiye?”.
ACT 2:38 La Bitrus yiki Kom dubom bwiranker kumero nakom yumbom, mor den Yesu kristi na wam bwirangker kumero tak kan yo neken yuwatangbek kwama ko.
ACT 2:39 Wor noro ki kom kange bibeyo lokume, kwarub kange birombo kutaneu, gwam nubo tee be kwama a coutiyeu”.
ACT 2:40 Kero ducce cii ne warke naci chuwaci ki cii nayiki, “Kom fulom dor kumero mor kalewo bwiranyeu.”
ACT 2:41 Lakom yo kercero nacii yukumen mwembo, kume ciin fiyaten nubo cabten bikate taar.
ACT 2:42 Lacii ca kaba ki merangka no tomangebbo kange yimbo winneu, mor caka tiilita kange dilo.
ACT 2:43 Taito bou dorcir la cin ma diker nyimankaro kan ya yiromboti kila fiye nob tomangebo wiyeu.
ACT 2:44 Gwam nubo nebilinker cii mwerum fiye win diker ciro na bwiticiyece.
ACT 2:45 La cii tokang dike cii cikeu kang dike cii ciko wiyakkeu laci kabkange dong dong kange cii cwitiyeu cii cikeu.
ACT 2:46 Fini win cii ca kabati ki nero mor lo wabe cii kiyan tiilita lonice cii kabkang caritoti bwitice mor fuwor nerer kange kungne necer.
ACT 2:47 Cii caklang kwamati ciin fiya yokati kabum nubem gwam. kwama cob cinenten nubowuro fiya dumetiyeu.
ACT 3:1 Na wo Bitrus kange Yuwanna yakenti kuwabe kwama ki kwma kwobka dilo kan keno taar.
ACT 3:2 Ni kange kilen ci bouciko nyo cii ki tuu kwaticobak nabou ciko nyilo kuwabka wo cii coti ki yoryoreu ki ken kim nubo dokenti mor kuwabi kwamau.
ACT 3:3 To Bitrus kange Yuwanna doken mor kuwabi kwama, kenci luma nerer.
ACT 3:4 Bitrus kange Yuwanna ciin cii cinenten kanuwe Bitrus yiki, “To nyo”.
ACT 3:5 kilendo to cii kwatiki keno can fiya diker ciinen na.
ACT 3:6 Dila Bitrus yiki cilfa kange mwiin, kange nai mi mani ciko, Dila dike min cikeu co manetiye. mor den Yesu kristi bwe Nazaret, ya yam”.
ACT 3:7 Bitrus tam kanceko cattiyero kunco nawo nawo naniceu kange kutile naniceu fiyam bikwan.
ACT 3:8 La kilendo kweni tari teryambo doken kuwabe kange Bitrus kange Yuwanna citi fuwai citi mwai ci ne kwama durkoti.
ACT 3:9 Nubo tou co yayambo, caklang kwama.
ACT 3:10 Ciin nyimom ki coni kiyire nyilo lo wabi yoryori la ciin dim ki nyimanka ki dikero bweyeu.
ACT 3:11 Kambo ci tamki kang Bitrus kange Yuwanna nubo kwarub kutauten ciinen, cunnge Tangilang sulemanu Cii ti nyimangi kambo ken.
ACT 3:12 Kambo Bitrus to nyeri in cinya nubow kom nubo Israila yebwi kom nyimang tiye? Yebwi kom cii nyinenten duwenye, mumi nyo nyi dokco co ciya yambo tiye kibi kwan dorer nyer kaka'a ki luma nyak?
ACT 3:13 Kwama Ibrahim, kange Ishaku, kange yakubu kwama teebnyebe ne bwe cannya ceu durko Yesu co kom koweu takri ka nekenco kabum Bilatus wo noncwi naci nyam kang cinen neu.
ACT 3:14 Kom ko niwo wucakeu nii lumake nyori lakomki a nya kumen kang niwo twal dore.
ACT 3:15 Kom twalum niwo ne dumetiyeu, wo kwama kunnyu tuweu, nye nyim nob neka bilenker dikero bwiyenen.
ACT 3:16 na weu, bilenker ki dencer niwo kom toti takri kom nyimom kinco dende wo cifiya bikwaneu. Bileng mor Yesu neco luma ceko cike cok, kabum kumem.
ACT 3:17 Kebmibbo min nyimom kom mayeu mor bwini nyomka, kambo liyab kumeb maneu.
ACT 3:18 Dila gwam dikero kwama tokanyi nob tomangeb dukumemcembou ki, Kristi an nuwa dotange landim.
ACT 3:19 Nawo yeu kom dubom bwirang ker kumero kom yilau dabe wam bwirang ke kumeu, wori kwama ywelkako fiye kwama wiyeu lam.
ACT 3:20 Na cii tomuu ki kristi wuro cii yokumen lan, Yesu.
ACT 3:21 Co wuro intam kang dii kwama a yoceu yaken lam tureni bo kacek kange dikero gwam dor dikero kwama toki fiyaco nyi nob tokkaker dukumer wucakeu.
ACT 3:22 Musa tok bilenker yiki Tee kwama an kunkumen kange nii ker dukumer na mo mor kebkumebo. kam nuwa dike cayikomtiyeu gwam.
ACT 3:23 An yilam niwo nuwabo nii ker dukumer wurori ciiyan tungumco ciko win nubo locem
ACT 3:24 Nyo nob ker dukumebo terti dor samailar kange burom bou bwiko cekeu cin tokker ciin cwungkang kumetinimbo wuro.
ACT 3:25 Kom bibei nob kerdukumerowo kange noroceu wo cima kange Tengwanub kumubeu, kambo ciyi Ibrahim mor tueluwe dor bitiner gwam ciyan fiya bibwiyer.
ACT 3:26 kambo kwama kun nyum bwe tomange ceri ci ter tomangekaco kumen wori nekom bibwiyer kambo yilam kikom fiya maka bwirankerer.
ACT 4:1 Kambo Btrus kange Yuwanna cin yi nubo kero tiyeu nii wabeu kange, nii durko kuwabeu, kange Sadukiyawa cin bou dor cer.
ACT 4:2 kwomci bichom wori Bitrus kange Yuwana merang nubo nenti dor Yesu, la ci ne fulen kwenka cekoti buwareu.
ACT 4:3 La cin tam ci cin kuken ci lo kuka na finin celum. wori men dom.
ACT 4:4 La nubo buro nuwa tomange ciyeu cin ne bilenker kilaka nubeko nabarobbo bikate nung wuro ne bilenkere.
ACT 4:5 Celfini ceri nubo tam ki ciyeu kange nubo durko kange nob merangkab cin mwerkangi wurcalima.
ACT 4:6 Ana nii wabe durko wi wi, kange kayafas, kange Yuwana, kange Alexanderi, kange nob naniya nii wabeko durko.
ACT 4:7 Kambo ci bou ki Bitrus kange Yuwana tiber cer la ci me ci ki bi kwando wini kaka dendo wini ka mam woticike?
ACT 4:8 La Bitrus dim ki yuwa tangbe kwama yi ci, “Kom ko tam ki nobeu kange nubo dur nubero.
ACT 4:9 Na nyo duwen kom ki me nyo ker nagenero kendo ma niwo nuwa bo lumanineu-Lama nyi nii wo yilam kwamere?
ACT 4:10 la kom kange nubo Israila la wuro a yilam nyam nyome kimen wo nii wo tim fou ka kom kwamer mor dene Yesu Kiriti wo nazaret deu, wo ka kulkenceu, la kwama kungum co bwar.
ACT 4:11 Yesu kiriti cou tero wo culang kuwekeu wo kom nob mukabo ka koweu la co yilam tero culang kuweke.
ACT 4:12 Fuloka mani nii kange nen wori dendo kange mani dimer di Kwama wo ci ne niffire na fiya fuloka kercere.”
ACT 4:13 Kambo ci to bikwan nerer Bitrus kange Yuwana ri cin nyumom fuwai nube koni ma bo kiye ka. La citi nyumangi la cin nyumom Bitrus kange Yuwana cin yii wi kange Yesu.
ACT 4:14 La cin to nii wo ci twabeu tim kange ci, la ci fue ki diker tokkar.
ACT 4:15 La kambo ciyi nob tomange a dubangum fiye yime nub dirlorembedi. La ci tokkangi bwiti ci.
ACT 4:16 Ba ma nubo buro nyi? kwaka nerer man, nangen nyumankar mani kang chek. La nyumom nyume nubo yim wurcalima nin gwam. La be man kibi kwan do ba kanagum tiye.
ACT 4:17 La kati ta ca kaba ti ki wakako mor nobe labo yi cikero ki nyial, ci a tokre ker kange nii dor denerowo.
ACT 4:18 La cin co Pita kange Yuwana mor cin yi ci kero ki yial cia tokre ker kaka merangka gwam kiden Yesur.
ACT 4:19 La Bitrus kange Yuwana yici keno dong dong nuwe kwama na nyo bwnangten kom la'a kwamari, kom warkero.
ACT 4:20 Mani nya dob tokka kerti dor dikero nya tomeu, kange wonya nuwameu.
ACT 4:21 Bwiko ci yiten Bitrus kange Yuwana kero ki nyialri, la cin dob ci cin cu'u. Lafiya bo nure wo ci a tam citi ki kang keu. wori nubo gwam duktang kwama ti ki dikewo bwiyeu.
ACT 4:22 Nii wo ki nyumka dukumero wo ki fulokau, chor cero kwini naar.
ACT 4:23 kambo ci nyamkan cineneri, Bitrus kange Yuwana bou nubo lo cinin la ci yii ci dike liya nob wabebo kange nubo durko yi ciyeu gwam.
ACT 4:24 La cin nuwa ri cin kung dir ciyero wari kwama nen cin toki “Teluwe” mo wo mo ma dii kwama moma dor bitinereu, kange caji kange dike more ceu.
ACT 4:25 Mon tok kero ki yuwa tangbek nyi canga mwe tee nye Dauda, yebwi nubo yim kumtacile? fwingan ti nye la nubo ki kwa kan dikero bwir.
ACT 4:26 Mon yiki “Liyabbo dor bitinereu mwer kangum dor cer wari la nubo dur cero mwerum na ci ma kiye kange Teluwe”.
ACT 4:27 Bichom Hiridus kange Pontius Bilatus kange kumta cileyeu kange nubo Israila cin mwerkangi fo mor cinan lor na cin kwobkangi kange canga mweu wucakeu Yesu, wo corten nuwageu.
ACT 4:28 Cin mwerkangum wari nacin mam dike kang mweko kange namweko amatiye.
ACT 4:29 Na weu mo teluwe to kercero ki nyial ne cangab mwebo bi kwan tokka kerek mweko.
ACT 4:30 Ta'aru kang mweko na twam la na ne diker yiromer kange diker nyumangkar a mani ki den canga mwe wucakkeu Yesu.
ACT 4:31 Kambo ci dim kwob ka dilokeri, fiye ci mwerum wiyeu muka, cin dim ki yuwa tangbe kwamak cin tok ker kwamaro ki bikwan.
ACT 4:32 Nubo ducce ne bilekereu dor ciro mwerum mwere. la kange nii yi bo ki diker cer na ce la nyeu dike na ciyeu win.
ACT 4:33 Ki bikwan nob tomangebo ma kwaka diyek warkerer ciyero dor kwenka teluwe “bwareu, luma ko dur wo dorciyere.
ACT 4:34 Nii kange mani wo fiyabo dikere wo ci buni kange dikere. wori nubo ki tang kini kange loni miyerangum la bou ki kyemer dikero wo ci miyeu.
ACT 4:35 La cin yotina nob tomangeu nen, la kabkang nubo nen gwam dong dong kange dike ci cwiyeu.
ACT 4:36 Yusufu wo nob tomangeb coti Barsaba (bwe bika nerek) Balewi nii Kubrus.
ACT 4:37 Miyem take wo na ceu la bou ki kyemero yoti na'a nob tomange nen.
ACT 5:1 La nii kange wi Anatiya wice safiratu, cin miyem take ciyeu.
ACT 5:2 ananiya yurangum kangem wi mor kyemer takero (La kin nyom ka wicek) La ci bou ki tangnim kyemembo kabum nob tomangebo nen.
ACT 5:3 La bitrus yi ki “Ananiya ye bwi mwa dob bwekelkele dou ner mwere na cer yuwa tangbek kwama nen cuerke na tam tangim kyemer takero.
ACT 5:4 Na miyebeu, kebo na mwe, la miyemmeu bikwankero kebo na mweka? we nii coo dokti nangen do wo mor neere mweu? mwa cuerbo nob nen cuerke mwa cuerum ki kwama.
ACT 5:5 Ki nuwa ka kere kowo Ananiya yari la bwiyam, la taito dur tam nubo wo nuwau gwam.
ACT 5:6 Bibweyile kange bou tum co chom cinen bwiceu ki lalang ya cin furum cho.
ACT 5:7 Kambo kang kenero ta'areri wicen dou nyombo dike yaken tiyeu.
ACT 5:8 La Bitrus yii co “yii ye kenoka miye takeu nan nyo cen”. La chon toki ong na nyo ce”.
ACT 5:9 La Bitrus yii cho, la manyi ka ciyam wari na kom cuwa yuwa tangbek Teluwe? To nani nubek kowo ya fuer bwemeu wo nyilo la na tuken nen kale.
ACT 5:10 Danjang chon yar ti na cek chon bwiyam. Kambo bibei bayilobeu douweri bocifiya chon bwiyam, la cin tu cho ci cerken ciko kale cifuerti cho cunga bwece ko nen.
ACT 5:11 Taito dur bou kuu kwama nen kange dor nubero gwam wo nuwa dike wo gwameu.
ACT 5:12 nangen yiromer kange diker nyumankaro ducce matiye mor nobe kange nob tomangek ci mwer kangum gwam bentilen colomoner.
ACT 5:13 La kangem mani ki bikwan neerer do wo a mwer dorti kange ciye. La cin wi ki bwiyale foh ducce kabum nubem.
ACT 5:14 La nyeu, nubo buro ne bilenker yuktenti Teluwe nen, nubo kila-kila na barub kange natub.
ACT 5:15 La ci turang nubo nuwabo lumau, ci yaken cike kong nure ci yokenci dor kwangnir, kangembo biciri, worina Bitrus cuu tiri, wuloceu cuuti dor kangem.
ACT 5:16 Nubo ducce borangum ti ci nan lor kentangum wursalima la ci bou tiki nubo nuwa bo lumau, kange buro kelkelibo kwomci tiyeu. lan twam ci gwam.
ACT 5:17 La nii wabe durko kwenu kange nubo wari kange ceu (nubo bwangten Sadukiyawa tiyeu) cin dimki kor ducce.
ACT 5:18 Cin tabang nob tomangeu cin kuranken ci lo kuka.
ACT 5:19 Mor kumeu bwe tomange kwama wucakeu bou wumom nyiloni lo kukako. La cho kuci kale, lan toki.
ACT 5:20 Kom ya koti kabum nyilom ku wabe koyi nubo ker dumerowo.
ACT 5:21 kambo ci nuwa weri la cin cuu kuh wabe ki celka finik cima merangkati, la nii wabe durko kange nubo loceu cin bou bo cin cho yim kange nob dir loreb, kange nubo dur nubero Israilau, cin tuken ci fiye kuka
ACT 5:22 La nob nangebbo ya lo kuka konen ci fiyabo nii.
ACT 5:23 nyon fiya lo kukako nungum nunge, nob chorkabo tirangum nyilok la wumi ri nya fiyabo nii mor,
ACT 5:24 La nii dukro kuh wabeu kange nob wabebo durko nuwa ketito weu, la ner cero kwenum cin nyombo dike a bangum bwiko tiyeu. La ciki ye ba matiye.
ACT 5:25 La kange bou yici nubo buro ka kumeu tirangum kuh wabe merang nubo nenti.
ACT 5:26 La nii dur ko kuwabeu ya kange nob nangeneb ceu yan bou ki ci. Kebo ki kwobkanka kati yilo nubo mobangci.
ACT 5:27 Kambo ci bou ki ciyeu cin nung ci kabum nob dir loreb, la nii wabe durko me ci ker.
ACT 5:28 Yii ci “Nya yi kombo ki kibikwan tak kom mare merangka mor denewo? la wo kom dim mor wursalima ki merangka kumek La kom doti na ko yo buyalenii wo na yiram dornyer”.
ACT 5:29 La Bitrus kange tangnim nob tomangebo toki tam nyo ne kwama dur kebo nob.
ACT 5:30 Kwama teb nyebeu kung Yesu woro ka tualumeu ka kulken dor bwatiyer.
ACT 5:31 Kwama duktangka cho kange catiyere ce na yilam liya kange nii cerka na ne Israila yiloka kange tabkan bwirang kerer.
ACT 5:32 Nyeu nyon nob warkeb dike bwirangeu nyo yuwa tangbek kwama ko wo kwama ne nubo wo bwanten tiyeu, gwam.
ACT 5:33 Kambo nob dir lorebo nuwa we di nerciron kayam ki bichom, la cin do na ci twalangum bibei tomangeu.
ACT 5:34 La bafarice kange wi dendo Gamaniel nii merangka werfumer, wo nubo gwam necho durtiye, la chon kweni tok kero ki nyial a chokken bibei tomange kale biduwar bwiri.
ACT 5:35 La chon yici kom nubo Israila ko to yora ki di keko cuiti na ko ma nubo buro neneu.
ACT 5:36 ki kumeni wo Theudas kweni tii tu dorcero na kange diker nubo kwini kwob naar bwang cinenten la ci twalumchori nubo bwang cenententiyeu gwam cin yilam kange nii nuwa bo fulen ciyaer wi tak.
ACT 5:37 Na chori kange nii Galilee dendo Yahuda wo ki kumeni kiyeka bou bolang nubo ducce, cho keneu kayam nubo buro bwang cinen tentiyeu yilam.
ACT 5:38 Na wo ma yi komti ko dubang nubo buro, ko dob ciki kwaciye, na no yukan ciyero kange nangen ciyero na nubo ciyeri an kayam.
ACT 5:39 La na dike wuro na kwama ceri mani ka kangti kati yilo yilam ko ma kiye ti kange kwama. La cin ciya.
ACT 5:40 La cin cho nob tomangeu mor la ci buk ci la yici kero ki nyial a tok re ker ki den Yesu.
ACT 5:41 La cin cerum kabum nob dir lorembonen ci ti bilangi wori cin daten ci nuwa dotange ki ker denero.
ACT 5:42 Bwiko nyeu citi yai kur waber kir-kir. Ci bwang ten ti luwe ci ne fulen ker kwamaro ti, La ci ma merangka ti ci kurong bowi citokti Yesu Cho Kritti.
ACT 6:1 mor kumeniwo kilaka bibei tomange yoktenti la yafudawa yim biten Elenawa cin ter fuenna dor Yafudawa Israila wori ci cuwa bo tu kange natub buneb cibo, fiye kabkanka carik kabkangti kir-kireu.
ACT 6:2 Kwob chilombo yobeu cho bibei tomangeu kila kila cinen la yici yorbo dubom nangen kwamar na yila kabkanka carik.
ACT 6:3 La nyeu ko chok nubo niber na barubbo more kume, nubo ki ciniyeu din kiyuwa tangbe, kange nyonka, buro ba yotenti dor nangenero weu.
ACT 6:4 ka nyeu, kwobka dilo kange tokka kerek ceko kir-kir.
ACT 6:5 Ker chiyero lom nubo nen gwam, la ci chok Istifanus nii dim ki bilenkere, kange yuwa tangbe kwamak, kange Filibus, kange Prochorus, kange Nicanor, kange Timon, kange Parmenas, kange Nicolaus nii Antakiya wo ma yiloka Yahudanci yeu.
ACT 6:6 Nubo ne bilenkereu bou ki nubo buro kabum nob tomangeb, la kwob cinen dilo ci yo cinen
ACT 6:7 La ke kwamaro yoten kang ti wai, la kilaka bibei tomangeu wursalima yokten ducce, la nob wabebo ducce yilam nob neka duwek fiye bilenkero wiyeu.
ACT 6:8 La Istifanus dim ki luma kange bikwan ma diker nyumankar ti kange diker yiromer mor nobe.
ACT 6:9 La kangen nob kweni wo na bi kur wabero ce, choti bi kur waber cerka, wo kuramiyawa kange Iskandariyawa, kange biten kili kiya, kange Asiya. Nubo buro kwob kangi kange Istifanus,
ACT 6:10 La cin mani kibi kwan ker nyomkar kange yuwa tangbe ko Istifanus tokkero ti cikeu.
ACT 6:11 La yurangum yurange ci bol nubo ya a tok ki, Nyo nuwa Istifanus tok keti dila kati dor Musa kange kwama.
