ACT 6:12 Cin bol nubo durko kange nob mulankabor, lan cin lam bidom kange Istifanus cintam cho, cin bou ki cho kabum nob dirlorem.
ACT 6:13 Chin borangu ki nob warker cuiker, wo toke, nii wo dobbo tokka kereko bwir dor fiye wucakkewo, kange werfuner.
ACT 6:14 La nyon nuwa chon toki Yesu wo najaret reu an wurongum fiye wo na fulongum dam Musam bo dob bineneu.
ACT 6:15 Nubo gwam yim dir loro neneu yo cinenten nuwe ciyero La chin toh tikob cebou na tikob bibei tomange wucakkeu.
ACT 7:1 Kambo nii wabe dur tokki mi digenwuri na ken bicom ka?
ACT 7:2 Stephen toki yimi kange Teemi, kom nuwaye. Dukum kwamaro wo kange Abraham ki kwama me sopotamia, na nyimde ciyi firen Haran.
ACT 7:3 Ci nyico ki, dubom bitine mwe kange tengwanim mwembo na yaken biti wuro ma nungmeven tiye.
ACT 7:4 Dila chon dubom biten chaidean la yim mwor Haran, di wiri bwiyaka tee cekkori kwama bou ki cho mwor takke wo, fiye mu yimwi naweu.
ACT 7:5 Chon necho kangem nob wuro wari kange ce na Tikange cho. mani bi duware ce, bwen wo mwa fuwam natiye dor cere, la chon tum fou ner bwentano Abraham manki bweri kon matin necho takke wo ca nyimtiye gwam kange ten gwanim cero bwan tano con bwiyam di
ACT 7:6 kwama yico kerti na wuro nubo loca ciya yi bidom bitine nubo kange. Nyo fiyeyinu cho limbo dige bwiye atin bou chinen ki yera na bibei canga catin nuwa dotange na choro kwini kwob naar.
ACT 7:7 La man ma bolang kale kowo neci dotange tiye kwama ki ciya cheruw nacin wab ye fiye wo nen.
ACT 7:8 La kwama ne Abraham diker wabka, di la Abraham yi lam tee Ishaku lan wabum cho ki. kume narube, Ishaku yilam Tee, la Jacob yilam tee bibei yo wab culom bo yobe
ACT 7:9 Kambo yitub cebu ciyabo kange Joseph la cin miyem cho nab yamembo Egypt La kwama kange cho.
ACT 7:10 La cercho mor dotange cenen. La neeh Joseph fofka kange yomka kabum Pharaoh liya Egypt wo yocho dur nubero gwam mor Egypt kange mor lowenen gwam.
ACT 7:11 Kambo ci ma wura dure di titen macar kange kan ana kange dotange durko tebbebbo nuwa la ci fiyabo cari.
ACT 7:12 La Jacob wo nuwa carito wini masar di cho ci tom tomange ciya bou ki bwo kabo.
ACT 7:13 kambo chiya boka na yobe ceri, la Yusufu fweltang keb cebonen dor cer ki kwa curo fir auna nyimom yitub Yusufu.
ACT 7:14 Yusufu yi yitub cebo chiya bou ki tee che Yakubu kange diker ciyero kange bibei yo locheu firen Masar, gwam ciye nubo cibi kwini niber culombou nung.
ACT 7:15 Yakubu choken yim firen biten Masar la chon bwiyam kange Tee ce.
ACT 7:16 Chin tucho mor Shechem la chin yoken cho mor tuwi wo Abraham Teni ki kyemer bibwe Hamor nen Shechem.
ACT 7:17 La ki kwama bi bwiyer kwamaro bidomeri Kwama yi Abraham nubo an duwi mor Egypt be.
ACT 7:18 La chin yoh kange liya wi Masar wuro yumbo Yakubu.
ACT 7:19 Liya chiro bol nubo ne tebyebbo dotange kambou ken chin dukchi tebyebo ki ciya cukou dor cero fiye dotange mani ciya dobchiti.
ACT 7:20 Ki kwama wo chi bou Musa, Cho yori kabo nanimde kwama na yocho chuwakko taar mor loh tee ce.
ACT 7:21 kambo chi yoken cho kaleri bwebubya Pharaoh's tumcho kung cho na yilam bibwe che.
ACT 7:22 Musa wiki yulang merang biten Egypt kange bikwan keret kange nangen.
ACT 7:23 kambo cho dou choroti kwini naar re ri chin kwabi mor nere ce ki cha tou yice bibei Israila.
ACT 7:24 La chon to nii kange ti Musa tikaan niwa ci nuwa dotange ki twalka bama care.
ACT 7:25 Kwaneri Musa na ci ciya takali kwama bou cinenne di la mani nyo. Chin yombo Kwamaki kancak cha chok chi la chi yombo.
ACT 7:26 Chelfini chin bou irsailawa kangumbo ki kwalkangi bwiti chi la chin mani nacho bouchinen ki filang bwiti yichi ki yebwi kom kwerkanti bwitikume?
ACT 7:27 Dila nii wo ter keceu tuken cho firen yi ki necho liyar do wo more che?
ACT 7:28 Muki cwi muki namun twalum yoh kambo mwa twalum Israilawa wure ka?
ACT 7:29 Musa chawaken kambo cha nuwa wori chon yilachinendiker yumankar biten Midian, wo cha yilam Tee bibeiyo yobou.
ACT 7:30 Kambo choro kwini naare chum meri bibei tomange cher cenen mor Yeri bang sinai ki biyen kiret mor yere.
ACT 7:31 Kambo Musa toh kirak keri yimanka lan fiyacho, lan chi kutau ten bidom na chi toh yora, chin nuwa dir kwama tok ti ki, Mo mi kwama tee mwe, Ibrahim kange Ishaku, kange Yakubu, kange Masu cwam tai fwe ki kungka dor nacir to.
ACT 7:32 kwama yi cho ki chukom tai mweu fiyemin tim wiyeu. liyar kwama.
ACT 7:33 Kwama yi cho ki chukom taa mweu namwek fiye mun tim wiyeu nku wabe.
ACT 7:34 Kebo koni nubo lomi nuwa dotangeti masar la min nuwa fubom ciyembo, no nyori manya na chukom chi sanakowo, bou na twom nen Masar.
ACT 7:35 wuro cho Musa chi kuwe dila kom ki we doknen ni warka dor nyere cho niwo kwama tomou na yilam ni dure kange ni cerka kwama ni bwirer kambo cho tou mor kiye.
ACT 7:36 Musa yaki chi mor masar kambo cha madukum mor chachi ki kume kwini naar.
ACT 7:37 Musa yi nubo Israilawa ki kwaka an yoh kumen nyi wabe dur bitine kume, yotob kumeb na mou.
ACT 7:38 Won cho nii wo wari kange nobe mwor kiye ki no tob kange nob dukkumen wuro bwangten ka cho chi mane tokkang ker dor ter Sinail cho wo wari kange teb yebbo wuro cho ni wuro ne nyo ker kwama.
ACT 7:39 Won cho niwuro tebyebbo ko neka ko bidwiyere ci chikom cho more ciye, chin ne birum neri chiki yang masar.
ACT 7:40 Ki kwama chi tokti ki Aruna na ywel chimen kwama wo a yati ki chi mor masar reu. diker Musa ro churou firen masare nya nyombo diker bwikange ceu.
ACT 7:41 La chin ywel be kwame chi bo bi bwitin chukko na ywel kako koce, chin bilangi diker chi mani ki kang chekeu.
ACT 7:42 Kwama kangum chi la chin ya bilang bitenrendo diye kambo mu langum bifumer nob duktanka kom neye twimen kundo fichangeu. firen ki choro kwini naar wuro kom Israilawa?
ACT 7:43 Kom ciya kange kwama Molech kange kwama biteiren wo Rephan, kange wolo kom yulange. na kom wabci, man yi kikom firen kah Babila ki den canga.
ACT 7:44 Tuka kume kibi kur fulen firen ki na nungi chin wi. kambo kwama ma nagen ki Musa ki cha mani na wuro chi nung chineneu.
ACT 7:45 Wo cho bikur fulendo tuka kume bou chike ki kwama Joshua wuro bou ki kwama chi yo bitine kange wo nubo kange ce wo kwama ywachiye wi kabum tuka kume nen na choro nyo yaken ki kwama Dauda.
ACT 7:46 Wo fiya bilangka kwama nen diker bwiyeu chin ywel ku wabka kwama ki kwama yakubu ce.
ACT 7:47 La Suleimanu ywel ku kwama.
ACT 7:48 Di la nii liyare mani yi fiye nubo yulangi ki kange na wuro nii dukkome tokke.
ACT 7:49 Di kwama na liyar ce kalewuro ceu na yoka nanice di la luwe wini ka mumentiye? kwama toki nyowe, kakka fiye wuni wo ma fubomtiye?
ACT 7:50 Kebo nuremi kom manag diwura?
ACT 7:51 kom nubo ki kwichi duweu, wo nero biyebe kange wuro tuni mani nuware, nachuro nyo kom cwibo bibwiyer bifumero kom mati dike tuka kume mane.
ACT 7:52 Nob dukkomen wuni tuka kume nebo dotange chin twalangum nob dukommeb wuro baurangu ki kabawuro ki liayre kom yilam nob kange ceb kange nubo twalang chiye.
ACT 7:53 Kom nob mulang kako, kom yuwou bolange wo nob bi bwiyeror bouchike di kom mabo nangen chiko.
ACT 7:54 Kambo bibei tomange nuwa nyori nar chero kayam kambo ken, di chin ku mum chiyero ti chi ciyabo ki Istifanus.
ACT 7:55 Di la Chi dim ki yuwa tangbek chin kung nuwe ce di kwama, chin duktang kwama mati chin taou kiriti timye kango catiyet wo kwama ce.
ACT 7:56 Istifanus toki to mitodi kwama wumom, fou bibwe nifirenen tim tiye foh kang ko chatiyer kwama ce.
ACT 7:57 La nob tareu chin kungi chin kwa diro kibi kwan, la chin kumo tuniciye chu ki keciye win chin kwencinenten.
ACT 7:58 Chin chukom cinar lower choci mubang ce ki ter, na nung dike bwiye, la chin cikangum bellen cero durko chi yoti kabum bwe kange chi chuwoti ki Sawulu
ACT 7:59 Ki kwama mubang Istifanus cho yila chuwoti chi tokti teluwe me Kiriti yo bibwiyer miro.
ACT 7:60 Chon chungi chon kwa diro kibi kwan choki Tee me kwama tare bwirang kero dor cher kambbo toki nyeri la chin damdum.
ACT 8:1 Bulus ciya kange buwero. Kikwamacho dotange chilendo kwenu dor nob kwama miro wursalima, di la nubo nebilenkertiyeu ciin yalam gwamm mor bitine Yahudiya kange samariya, cii dob ka nob tomangeb.
ACT 8:2 Nabarubbo kibilenke chin furum Stephen laciyi yim kang buwam dorcer.
ACT 8:3 Di la Sawulu ma nob kwamabo nen diker kambo ken chiti doi luwe-luwe chi cikangum nabarobboti kange natubo, kumcitak furcina.
ACT 8:4 Duwa nubo neken bilenke birombo yalamem, chinen ya chine ker kwamaro.
ACT 8:5 Filibus yaken firen Samariya toker Yesuroti.
ACT 8:6 Kambo nubo nuwa lacitoten dikero Filibus matiyeri, lachin yilaken ki ner chero gwam na nuwau dike chitoktiyeu.
ACT 8:7 Won kelkeliyo bwirko chiranyu bwinubo ducce no nuweceu chin ciwiyeti kidir nubowo kwamang be kange kilentinimbo fiya twaka.
ACT 8:8 La chin ma fuwor nerer ducce bitinecho.
ACT 8:9 Nii kange wi bitinecho choti ki Siman. wo kikabe chin nikuye latakri chima nubo Samariyamin diker nyimanti nawo chi cho dorceriti ki chin diro kange.
ACT 8:10 Kwrub Samariya nubo dur kange bibei nuwa choti cikinyi ki “Niwo cho bikwan duret kwamaro wocii choti ki dureu.
ACT 8:11 Chi nuwa choti wori kutangnyi machinen diker nyimankati ki kwomje- kwomjece.
ACT 8:12 La kambo chi ne bilenke kange ker waber Filibus ceri, wo chi mati ker liya kwama kiden Yesu kriti lachin yuchinen mwem kwamambo gwamce nabarub kange natub.
ACT 8:13 Cho siman kibwicho ne bilenke kambo ciyu cinen mwem kwamamberi la chin mwerkang kange Filibus kambo chito cii ma diker nyimanka ti kange nanyendo dureri, la kwomchoti.
ACT 8:14 kambo nob tomangeb wursalima nuwa fulende samariyau yo kerkwamareri cii tuncinen Bitrus kange Yahaya.
ACT 8:15 kacilauweri, ciin kwobcinen dilo naci yo yuwatangbe kwamako.
ACT 8:16 Wori bwiri yuwatangbe kwamako yiraubo dorcher bwiri, chin yucinen ka mwem kwamambo kiden Tee kwama Yesu.
ACT 8:17 La Bitrus kange Yahaya cin yo cinenten kanceu dorcer lachin yo yuwa tangbe kwama.
ACT 8:18 Kambo siman to cii yuwatangbe kwama koti kiyeka kange nob tomangeb dorcerdi lanne chi kyemer.
ACT 8:19 Yici, ki “kom neye bikwandowo ken, lawo niwo miyo yo cinenti kanko dorcerei na yo yuwatangbe kwamako.
ACT 8:20 Di la Bitrus yicho ki, nawori mweu a yanchang kange mwo. wori muti kwain mwan fiya yuwatangbe kwamake ki chuweka mwek.
ACT 8:21 Mu manki chuner fou dikero wuronen, wori mor nere mweu kebo dong-dong kwama nen.
ACT 8:22 Nyori ywelum bwirang ker mwero, di la kwob dilo kwama nen kangeri an dob mwen bwirang ker mwero muyo ner mwereu.
ACT 8:23 Wori min nyimom mumor kanka nerek tak ri, mor bwaka nerek.
ACT 8:24 Siman ciya yiki “kwobka dilo kwama nen kermir, dike kange mor dikerwo mtokeu, a abwire kange mwo.
ACT 8:25 Kambo Bitrus kange cidim ne kaker kwamareri, chin yilaken wursalima, ciyakenti dor nurer di, cin wab ker kwamaro chinar lor Samariya ducce.
ACT 8:26 naweu bwe tomange kwama yi Filibus ker ki Kweri yaken chunyako bang nure yirau tob kange wursalima yaken Gaza (Nure wo ki no kwechane.
ACT 8:27 Kweri yaken nikange wo ciro Abaca, in Liyar dur Chunya kandu katu, liya Abaca. cho cima liyar kulen choro tiye gwamme Bou wursalima cama wabkerwi.
ACT 8:28 Yikenti yimyie diker yamercer kiye, bifumer Ishaya niker dukumer.
ACT 8:29 Yuwatangbe ko yi Filibus ki “yaten bidom kange kulend kwikarowo”.
ACT 8:30 Filibus cwa yanfiyacho nuwa ci kiye bifumer Ishaya ne ker dukkumerti la ciki mum nyimom dike me kiyetiyeu?”
ACT 8:31 Bahabashe yiki “amanye manyumantiye caro kange fwetang membori? ken Filibus adou mor diker kwika ceronen nayi kange cho.
ACT 8:32 Won cho dikero Bahabashe kiyeti “Ciin yaken kicho mu kwame fiye biyeka bir-bir tak na be kwame kom nob cangkab, wombo nyi.
ACT 8:33 Dor yiber dorer cer ci macinen bolang kebo mor luma we ane kercero car kotiye? wor cii tum dukumece dorbitiner.
ACT 8:34 La Tee me filibus yiki, “min kennen yiye we niker dukumerowo tok kero wotiye? kidor cer kaka'a nikange kidumenka?
ACT 8:35 Filibus Teer kero dor bifumer Ishaya Lan ma cinen ker kwamaro.
ACT 8:36 Kambo ciyaken nureri, cin lam kong caji kange Tee wuro yiki “To, mwambo wofo, yebwi mani a yumen mwem kwamam botiye?
ACT 8:37 Filibus yiki “No mun ne bilenke win mor nerer mweri, cin yumwen mwem kwamambo. Dila Bahabashe yiki minne bileke.
ACT 8:38 La Bahabashe yiki atim kidiker kwikaro. Lachin yuchinenmwembo.
ACT 8:39 Kambo chi cherum mwembo nenneri yuwatangbe kwamako dum Filibus Teeu totensobo tak, la yakenti naken bilang tumboti.
ACT 8:40 Dila filibus cerkangeu Azotus. Tiyangem bitinecho token ker kwamamaroti bitine cho nen yacin lamciko kaisariya.
ACT 9:1 Di la Shawulu yoti kantni tikanka kerek tayek kange twalangka nob bwangka Yesu chere ni wabe durkonen.
ACT 9:2 Kentencho bifumer naci yaciko kuwabe kwamamu Dimaskus, wori no fiya ni nanure woceri Bwayile kange nawiye, naci bou kici wursalima naci bwamci.
ACT 9:3 kambo liyakentiyeri chin dadom kange Dimaskus dang jang, dang jang filango yirau di kwama kangtangumcho.
ACT 9:4 lachin yarken bitineri cin nuwa diro kange yichoti “Shawulu, Shawulu yebwi mu neye dotange tiye?
ACT 9:5 Shawulu ciyi toki kii we mwo kwama?” kwama yicho “mo Yesu wuro mune dotange tiyeu.”
ACT 9:6 Di la kweni doken mor cinar lorcho ciyam yinen dikerowa tamyo maneu.
ACT 9:7 Nubowo yakenti kange shawulu tirangum bir-bir cin lem diker tok kar, chi nuwa dirti, dila citobo nii wii.
ACT 9:8 Shawulu kweni bitine kambo chi wom nuwe ceri, mani ci toh dikerti, lacin tacinen kango cinbouki cho mor cinar lor Dimaskus.
ACT 9:9 lam kume taar manici toti manici cati, manici noti.
ACT 9:10 Nii tomange kange wi Dimaskus dencero Hannaniya, dila kwama tok ker kange cho mor dukumer yicho ki “Hannaniya” ciki To, minwo kwama”
ACT 9:11 Kwama yicho, Kweni yaken cinarloro choti ki Mikakke, lo niwo choti ki Yahuza me ni bou Tarsus dencero Shawulu, ci kwob diloti.
ACT 9:12 Chinto mo dukume nikange douti dendo Hannaniya wi douti dila kun kang yocinenti wori nuweceu na wumom.
ACT 9:13 Di la Hannaniya ciya kwama min nuwa fulen nubowin ducce dor niwon kange dara bwiram nanye net cero cima nubo lomwennen wucakeu yim wursalima.
ACT 9:14 Liya wabe durko necho nyal naci tam gwamm nubowo chodencerotiyeu.”
ACT 9:15 Dila kwama yicho ya cho cin kulen nangenner minr min chokum cho choke wo awaden miroti nubo nenneu kange liyabtinib kange Israila.
ACT 9:16 Wori man dancinen dotange ca nuwati ker denerer miu.”
ACT 9:17 la Hannaniya yaken doken luwecho. yocinenti kanko dor, yiki “kemi shawulu Yesu toki wo dandorcer munen nure kikwama mu boutiyeu, toh muye nati fiya toka fiyek nadimki yuwa tangbeko wucakeu.
ACT 9:18 dang jang dikero kange no wulom dikem nuwe shawulu, la fiyam toka fiyek kwene cin yucinen mwem kwamambo.
ACT 9:19 La chamcharito cho ci necho bikwam neret yi wari kange nob bwangkab wi Dimaskus kumeni kila.
ACT 9:20 Wi danjang neker Yesurti mor kuwabe yitki incho bibkwe kwama.
ACT 9:21 kwarub nubo nuwa cho tiyeu cin yimangti ciki “wo kebo niwo twalang nubo wursalimatiya choden do wotiyeu ba? ciboufota natamci cineken liya wabe durko.”
ACT 9:22 Di la shawulu fiyam bikwan kambo ken ci bouti ki kwamka kange bolka tiber Yafudawar kange nubo yim Dimaskus ki nurewo ci dancimen Yesu incho Kristi.
ACT 9:23 Ki kumeni kila nawo chumeu, Yafudawa mwer kangi nacin twallum cho.
ACT 9:24 Di la Nyomom dike mwertiyeu. Cii chirou choti nyilo kalek cinar lorocho nacin twallum cho.
ACT 9:25 Di la ki cin kumeri nob bwankabo tuh cho mor bulene chin dokken cho tiyak.
ACT 9:26 Kambo chi bou wursalimari, shawulu cwinaci mwerkandor kange nob bwangkab. Di la kwarub ce ci cwachoti wori ci ciyabo chokeneu cin yilam nii bwangkaba.
ACT 9:27 La Barnabas tuh cho bouchiko nob tomangebo nen. yici kambo Shawulu wabkan kange kwama nureu. Di la kwama tok kero kange cho, shawulu ma tok ker Yesu nyang lang Dimaskus.
ACT 9:28 Wabkanci kwama dotacek kange cerkacek wursalima. In tok ker kwamar nyanglang mor den Yesu.
ACT 9:29 Chin ma kwobkanke kange Yafudawa Helenawa, dila cinti naci to chi twallumcho.
ACT 9:30 Kambo kebbebo nyimom nyeri, cho ci beken kicho Kaisariya. ci tunkencho Tarsus.
ACT 9:31 Lana nyime Ekilisiya gwam biten Yafudiya. Galili kange Samariya ci fiya luma kange muka lachi yi yim cimbo ti mor tai kwama, kange birim nerem Yuwatangbe kwamak, nob kwamabo kila chiko chob ten.
ACT 9:32 Yilam kambo Bitrus buyelangum chunka bitinen kocho gwam, yilam nob bwanka kwamake yim biten Lydda.
ACT 9:33 Cin fiya nii kange dendo Aeneas, wur bwiyo nom nowe, dim choro narub dor kwangnid.
ACT 9:34 Birtus yicoki Aeneas, Yesu kiristi twamnen. kweni kun diker damer mwero. nawonyo kweninti.
ACT 9:35 La gwamm nubo biten Lydda kange biten sarona cinto niiwo, dila cin yilau fiye kwama wiyeu.
ACT 9:36 Naweu ni kwama kange wi yafe dendo tabita, dendo Kinug “Dorcas” Nawiye wo dimki mana nangen do ken cii bwini nubo manki dikereti.
ACT 9:37 In lam kwama wo ci daken twira la cin buyam, kambo ci Yuchinen mwembo ci yokencho luwe diyeu.
ACT 9:38 Dila Lydda bidom kange yafa nob bwanka be nuwa Bitrus kinon firen cin twom nubo yob cinen. Cii kenchoti, “Tabre bwi bou nyinen”.
ACT 9:39 Bitrus kweni yaken kange ci, danjang ci bouri, cho ci yaken kicho luwe diye. La natub bunebo bouti ti bidom chiwiyeti, la chin tuh belendo kange kulendo Dorcas churcineneu ki kwama ciwariyeu.
ACT 9:40 Bitrus cho kumai gwamm mor kuwe, chunken kwob dilo, dila yila chunya twarek, kii, “Tabita kwenuu”. ci wom nuweceu, cito Bitrus ri chin yiken.
ACT 9:41 Bitrus tar kanceko kunnyu cho lana nyime chou bwanka kwamako kange natub bunebo, cin neci Tabita ki dume.
ACT 9:42 Dikerowo yilam nubo nyimom gwamm yafa, la nyori nubo ducce ne bilenke kwama nen.
ACT 9:43 La yilam Bitrus yi kumeni kila kange Yafa kange ni kange dendo saminu Majemi
ACT 10:1 Nii kange nowi biten Kaisariya dendo karnilious cin dur nob kwenebo cii choti ki Istifanus.
ACT 10:2 Inni wabe, wo neken dorcero kange loceu bwanka kwamak; ne tikali kemerti ducce Yafudawa nen kwob dilo fiye kwama wiyeu, kir-kir.
ACT 10:3 Ki kang keneko taar na yimkakumbo ce cin bou cinen mor dukumer bwe tomange kwama bouti cinen dila bwetomange kwama toki ki, “Karnilious”.
ACT 10:4 karnilous cin cii bwetomange kwama ninten nuwe mortaye. inye ni luwe?” Bwe tomange kwama yicho ki “dilo mweu luma nere mweko nune nubo bwinibotiyeu, lam di kwama nan luma nerer diker kwama kabum kwama.
ACT 10:5 Naweu, twom nubo aya biten Joppa ciya bou ki nii chuwoti Saminu woci choti ki Bitrus ceu.
ACT 10:6 Yim kange Saminu nitu tiye, wolocen kino kon chachi.
ACT 10:7 kambo nii to mange wo tok kero ceu yilanken di, Karnilious Chuwo yob mor bibei changa loceu, kange nii kwene win mor tangne cenen wuro bwanten kwama tiyeu.
ACT 10:8 Karnilious yici dikero bweuwe gwamm la twomei Jappa.
ACT 10:9 Celfinice ki kan keneko nukkune (Kikakuk) ci yakenti kambo cidadom kange cinar loreri Bitrus kwiken luweu diyeu naci kwob dilo.
ACT 10:10 La cin nuwa wura lacin cwiti diker cakarti, lakambo nubo macaritiyeu dila cin toh dukum.
ACT 10:11 La cin toh dikwama wumom dila kangum cembo yirauti, kange diker na lalango dur yirauti dor bitiner, ci chorumti chunga ceko nareuniu.
ACT 10:12 Morece biciro fwelfwele nako narreu gwamm wi kange nubo kongti kongeu, dorbitiner kange bilibe tinim dii kwama.
ACT 10:13 Di la diro tok ker kange cho Kweni Bitrus, biyeucho.
ACT 10:14 Di la Bitrus yike, kebongo kwama wori, micambo dike wucakke wi kange dike yeinyeu”.
ACT 10:15 Di la diro bou chinen yobeceutak, “dike kwama mamco wucakkeri chore muki yeikabo.
ACT 10:16 Wuro bwiu kinti taar, dila ciin tum kwelen yaken dii kwama.
ACT 10:17 Kambo Bitrus mor kwomka ki danke dukumembo citoweri, dila nubo Karnilious twomou bou tiran gum nyilok locho, kambo ci mem nureri.
ACT 10:18 Dila cin ma attifolo cimen nii chuwoti ki Saminu Bitrus ceu yiraufoka.
ACT 10:19 Kambo Bitrus mor kwakakerek dor dukumer yuwa tangbe kwamako yicho ki “To, nubo yoh donenti.
ACT 10:20 Kwani yirau yaken kange cii mare bwi yambo nenkange ciyeu wori mo mi twom che”.
ACT 10:21 Bitrus yirau nubonen yice ki mo komdo tiya. yebwi kom bowe?
ACT 10:22 Ki dur nub kwenebo ceroti ki karnilious niken wo bwangten kwamatiyeu, nubo Yafuda nyumom cho choniwo bwe tomange kwama wucakkeyeu twomuu na mu bou loche, nuwa tomange munen.
ACT 10:23 La Bitrus chouci ciya dou mor naci yiken kange cho. celfiniceri yaken wari kange ci la kangem bo Yafa yoci nure.
ACT 10:24 Celfiniceri cin doken kaisariya Karnilious ningtsng citi, chou kebcebo kange farub cebo bidomeu.
ACT 10:25 kambo Bitrus doweri karnilious takange nuwe kange cho chungi necho dur.
ACT 10:26 Di la Bitrus kuncho yichoti kweni ti mo keneu niffir.
ACT 10:27 Ki kwama Bitrus tokkankerti kangeceu, doken mordi kwabti nubo ducce mwerum fiye win.
ACT 10:28 Yi ciki “Komki bwikom kom nyimom nii Yafuda mani mma naniyak kaka'a na ya kange nen, kaka'a bitine kange. Dila kwama yiye ki chokeni manki wucakke.
ACT 10:29 Wo dike bwi mabou nyimanka maniye, kikwama kacou Yereu. la yori minne yebwi kom twomi komkin bowe”.
ACT 10:30 Karnilious yiki kumeni naar wo chumeu dong dong kwama wo, mi kwob diloti ki kwama Tee rou, (kang keno taareu) mor luwemi, mintori tinkani ki kulendo fuwor.
ACT 10:31 Yiki Karnilious kwama nuwam dilomweu tikali mweu nubonen i nkwa kwamanen ki mwo.
ACT 10:32 La nyori twomkange yafa, two min a chomwen nii kangewi dendo Saminu wo ci chotiki Bitrus. kiyi cho saminu ni chu tee tiyeu, yim kong caji.
ACT 10:33 Na weu cin twom cinen cha bou gwam ce na cin mwerkange wi kabom chem kwama na chi nuwa dikero gwam wo cha yici ki ciya maneu ki dencer Teluwe.
ACT 10:34 La Bitrus karcinen ki Biling ke miu nyimom kwama mani nuwo ki dimen.
ACT 10:35 Lan nyori mor nubo gwamm niwo wab chotiyeu kange ni madiker yoryoreu kwama yochoti.
ACT 10:36 kom nyimom tomange cinen Israila ki kwamawo ci yici kero lumer fiye Yesu Kristi wiyeu woncho kwama wucakakeu.
ACT 10:37 Kom ki bwikom kom nyimom dikero birombo bwiuweu, wo bwiu mor Yafuda terti Galili kambo tomangeYukan munnyek kwama wo Yahaya maneu.
ACT 10:38 Nannyeng tinim Yesu nii Nazaret kambo kwama yomcho ki yuwa tangbe ceko wucakkeu. kange bikwan duret. Dila yoti kanwi ma nangen lumarti kange twaka nubeko gwamm brombo bwe kelkele bwomeu, wori kwama kange cho.
ACT 10:39 Nobu tom dikero camaneu gwamm biten Yafudawa kange mor wursalima wuro Yesu wo citwallume, kiyeika dor chilom bwatiyeu.
ACT 10:40 Ni wuro kwama kungum cho kikume taare dila yilam nubo nyumom cho.
ACT 10:41 Kebo nubonen kwarub, dila nubowo kwama choci ki kaba-biki bwibo nubo ba cha bano wari kannge cho kambo kwama kuncho mor tuweu.
ACT 10:42 Yibo bi yi nubo ker kwamaro biyitenci wocho wuro kwama yo a ma dumeti kange bwar bolang tiyeu.
ACT 10:43 Nob dukum kerem gwamm dokker cero, wuyak, birom ne bilinke tiyeri nafiyam cherka mor deneche.
ACT 10:44 Kambo Bitrus tok keroti dor dikero biromberi, yuwa tanbge kwamako yirau dor kwarub nubo yirom wi nuwa ker kwama roti cinen.
ACT 10:45 Nubo wuro mor mwerkangka nob bangka kwamakeu, cin ciya ki mwati ka lareko, kwarub nubo bou kange Bitrus ceu nuwa nyimanka wori yuwa tangbe kwamako yirau dor nuber.
ACT 10:46 Wori cin nuwa nubo biro tok keroti ki nyini kange chicaklang kwamati. Dila Bitrus ciya.
ACT 10:47 Kange wi wuro aywam nubowoti yuka mwem kwama keu nabeu?
ACT 10:48 Lan toki a yucinen mwembo kiden Yesu Kristi Lacin kencho ayi wari kange ci na kumewo.
ACT 11:1 Nawo nob nangenbo kange kebcebo wo Yahudiya nuwa ki nobo kumtacele ciken cin yo ker kwamaro.
ACT 11:2 La Bitrus bo Ursalima, boro mor nobo mwatum bwi nabarube torang choti.
ACT 11:3 Mo mwerkan dor kange nobo biye bo bwi nabarube, mon cha chari kange ci.
ACT 11:4 Bitrus teri fwetancinen keroti ki.
ACT 11:5 maki kwob dilo mor cinan lor yafa man to dukum bulen do yiraw nyona yilang ko dur wo ci cuku kwama culangko nare yirau kabum mim.
ACT 11:6 Man nyo cimenti nuwe wi, take man bulange durcer, man to bi yuwaro nako nwar na dorbitinero ce, biyuwaro bwirko, kange buro kongti konge, kange bilibetinim bo dii kwama.
ACT 11:7 Min nuwa diro yiyeti kwemi, Bitrus biyem wom.
ACT 11:8 Miki kebo nyo teluwe dike kange mani wo kebo na wucake ce kange wo yai nye do nyi miye.
ACT 11:9 Diro ciya firen dii kwama, ki dike kwama chuwo ki wucakke, chuwo moki kebo wucakke.
ACT 11:10 dike bwi Kiriti taar nimde tuh yilanken ciko kwama.
ACT 11:11 Can nawo nobo, taar tirangum kabum luwem bo nyo more ceu, ci tom ci firen kaisariya fiye ma wuye.
ACT 11:12 Yuwa tangbe ko yiye nyo ya ware kange ci, nungka demene men. kebbebo wuro nukken ciya wari kange mo la nyo doken lo nii cuwo.
ACT 11:13 Yi nyo kambo cho to nii tomange kwama tim mor luwece, yiti ki twom nob taar Yafa, ya ciya cho Saminu wo cuwoti ki Bitrus.
ACT 11:14 Chan yi kom tomange wo ka fiya fulokati mo kange lomwe.
ACT 11:15 Man ter kiro kange ci, yuwa tangbeko yirau dor cer nawo yira bineneu ki kaba.
ACT 11:16 La man bulangi kange ker Teluwe, nawo cho toke, “Bilenke Yuwanna ma Yuu nub nen mwemti ki kume a ma kumen ki yuwa tangbe.
ACT 11:17 Tano kwama neci nyomka nawo ne beri, fiya bo ne bilenke fiye teluwe Yesu Almasihu, man we ma kobkanti kange kwama?
ACT 11:18 Ci nuwe dike wo ri lan bwayum diker tokkaker dila cin duktan kwama cike nobo kumtaceleu kwama neci yiloka ko ciya fiya dume tiye.
ACT 11:19 Buro yila, ki ker dotange bwanten bwiko bwar Istifanus, cin kwiya ya lam finikiya, kuburus, kange kuranne, ci ba Antakiya, dila cin tok ker fulener, yesu Yahudawa nen ki kwaci.
ACT 11:20 Di la kangem ciyembo nob bo kuburus kange kuranne, kurane, ci, bo Antakiya ci tok ker kange Helenawa, cin yi ci fulenker Teluwe Yesu.
ACT 11:21 Take bikwan Teluwe (Ubangiji) wari kange ci, nobo dutce ne bilenker, cin yilau Teluwe nen.
ACT 11:22 Fulen ciyero lam tii nob kwama bo Ursalima so ci tung Barnabas nob kwamabo, cin merang nobo dutce. Wi Antakiya ci ter cho ka nob tomangebo kritta.
ACT 11:23 Di cho lau con to luma kwama co ma fuwor neret, chon nece bikwan gwam, ciya tim mor Teluwe, ki nerciyero gwam.
ACT 11:24 Wuri chon niken dim ki yuwa tangbe kange bilenke, nobo kila cin yokten Teluwe nen.
ACT 11:25 Barnabas cu Tarsus na cho do Shawulu.
ACT 11:26 Fiyacho, chola bou ki cho Antakiya. cho yi wi Antakiya choro win ci mwerkanti kange nob kwama bo, cin merang nobo dutce. Wi Antakiya ci ter cho ka nob tomangebo Krista.
ACT 11:27 Mor Kumeni rowo kangem nob nuwa ka dukume, bo Antakiya.
ACT 11:28 Win more ciye dencero Agabus Kwini titiye tok ker ki bi kwan yuwa tange ki, an ma tik ka kanga kambo ken dor bitinero nin gwam. Wuro biwi kal Kalaudiya.
ACT 11:29 La nob tomagebo tuki kor neret, wo ni ki ma nyi bi kwane ce, cin tun kebciyebo nin feren yahudiya ki tikali.
ACT 11:30 Cin mani nyo, cin tung nobo durko nin ki kyemer, do kan Barnabas kange Shawulu.
ACT 12:1 ki kwama wo Hiridus dok kangem nob bwankabo nin kan na co nuwa cinen.
ACT 12:2 Chon twallum Yakubu kange Yuwana ki kulen.
ACT 12:3 Bwiko cho to nyo, lom yahudawa nin con ta Bitrus.
ACT 12:4 Bwiko cho ta bitrus di chon kum cho Furcuna, chon yoti nobo tee kwentiyeu na a to co ti chon wii ner boka ki cho dukume yabka.
ACT 12:5 La Bitrus kumkume furcuna, kange num kebcebo bwang ten kwamatiye kwob dilo ti kwama nen dor cer.
ACT 12:6 nyo na fini Hiridus a chok cho fiye, mor kume wo, Bitrus dadumti tiber nobo te kwentiye yob, bwambwambe ki gwelmar yab, nob te kwentiyeu tirangum nyilo furcuna.
ACT 12:7 Nyomka man di la ka nob tomange kwama wucakke cerkangu cinen filan ko tiba kuwe cho, ke Bitrus cungakin kuncho tak ki, Kweni wulom' di la gwelmaro kan ceke cherum.
ACT 12:8 Ni tomange kwama wucakke yi cho ki, cakkangum kulen mwero dum tameu, Bitrus mani nyo yeyum yilam mweko, bwan men ten.
ACT 12:9 Bitrus bwanten nii tomange wucakke, cin cerken kale, nyom bo dike nii tomange wucakke matiye, bilenke, ce ki ke dukum.
ACT 12:10 Di la cin cum nobo to yiloko wine kange yobe, cin lam yiloko ci ma kyemere, wo to cinanloro tiye; wum cinen ki bwici, cin cerum, ci bwangten nure, wi dangjang nii tomange wucakke dobomcho.
ACT 12:11 Bitrus yilau mor bwiyece, yiki bilenke man nyom naweu teluwe, tungu nii tomange ce wucakke bo na cok ye kan Hiridus kange dike yahudawa kwatiye.
ACT 12:12 Cho nyomom yori, cho bou la Maryamu wo bou Yahaya, den Teecero Markus wobo bwanten Yesu tiye mwerkange wi dutce ci kwob dilo ti.
ACT 12:13 Di chon kwa yiloko luweko la bubiya mor luwe chou bo na wom yiloko.
ACT 12:14 Chon nuwa dir Bitrus bubiya ka timi bilangtum dolbo womka, yila cwa chu kuh na cho ne ci fulen Bitrus tim nyilo.
ACT 12:15 Cin cho ki mo twelum twele, bubiya cinti, ki nyo. cike nii tomange ce wucakke ka.
ACT 12:16 Bitrus titen kwaka yiloko la cin wom nyilokori, ci ton cho la dike nyomankar tamci.
ACT 12:17 Bitrus nung ciki kang maci nenti ki ciya kumom. cho ci yi ci fulendo kambo teluwe cokce furcuna. coki kom yi Yakub kange kebbcebbo gwam. dike bwiye. cho dob ciye, chu fiye kange.
ACT 12:18 Fini celi, kebo be kwalkanka kweni tiber nobo tekwentiye di bwi kange Bitrus.
ACT 12:19 Bwiko Hiridus do cho fiya cho bo la chon me nobo totiye chon neci nyaldo a twallum ci, la cho yirau yahudiya yaken kaisariya, yi yim cem wi.
ACT 12:20 Naweu Hiridus mam funer kange nobo Taya kange Sidon, cin chu fiye cho wiye wari, cinken Bilatus, ni tikali liya, a tikanci, dila cindo ywelka, wori ciki fiya carito bitine ce.
ACT 12:21 bi diye wo ci yomom Hiridus cakkangum ki kulen liyare take yiken dor kuttile liyare, chon ma yiranci ker.
ACT 12:22 Nobo kwa kiyange, ki wo dir kwamar, kebo na nifiroce.
ACT 12:23 Wi dangcang nii tomange kwama wucakke kwa cho, wuri co ne bo kwama duktangka wi dangcang na yuwe cam co chon bwiyam.
ACT 12:24 Ker kwamaro, ti kuyai yoktenti.
ACT 12:25 Bwiko Barnabas kange Shawulu dim nagen ciyero Ursalima, ci yilauti, ci bo wari, kan Yahaya, woro din te cero markus (Barnabas kange Shawulu) cin yilaken Ursalima.
ACT 13:1 mor nob bwanka kwamanko Antakiya nob nuwaka dukumebo wi, kange nob merangka. ci bi Barnabas, Saminu woro ci (chuti ki Baki) kange lukiya Bakurane kange manayin woro ci (yo ci wari kange Liya Hiridus ni ca liyare) kange Shawulu.
ACT 13:2 Di la ci wab kwamati ki yim bo ngak-ngak kange dulomwe, di yuwa tangbeko ki kom cok men Barnabas kange Shawulu dor nangen do ma cu ciye.
ACT 13:3 Merka kwob dilo kange ngak-ngak kange dulomwe la ci yo cimenti kanko dur, ci yoci.
ACT 13:4 Shawulu kange Barnabas cin bwanten dir yuwa tangbeko wucakke cincu culukiya, wuri cin yabken diyele kuburus.
ACT 13:5 Fiya ci cinanlor salomi cin merang ker kwamaro mor kur bi waber Yahudawa, ci wari kange Yahaya Markus ni tikanci tiye.
ACT 13:6 Bwiko cho chi kentangum diyele gwam, yaken Bafusa, foh ci fiya kange bayahudiya dencero Bar Yesu. nima fulentiye take nii nuwaka dukume cwerke.
ACT 13:7 Ni fulene wo ci cuwo ti ki Makaddas, cho carju Bulus nii wo ki yilen ne. wuro cuwo co Bulus kange Barnabas co cwiti na cho nuwa ker kwama.
ACT 13:8 Di la elima ne fulen (Fwetanka dene ce) kwabkangi kange ci cwiti na co fwem makadda cin bilenke nen.
ACT 13:9 la Shawulu wo ci cho ti ki Bulus dimki yuwa tangbeko wucakke la yo cimen ten nuwe.
ACT 13:10 La chon yiki mo bi bwe bwekelkele mo dimki bibolero kange cil. mo nii kiye dike ken. mani mwa dob werkanka nor Teluwe kwama tim cere tiya? naweu.
ACT 13:11 kang teluwe kwama wo dor mwer, naweu yilam fukma. mani mo to kakuk ti can can do wo. Wi danjang ka bikumta kume kange kumtacele cumom cho chon ter bwelankako do nobo a ti cimen kang ko tiye.
ACT 13:12 Bwiko Makaddaci to dike bwiri neken bilenke wurico ma nyomanka ki merangka ker kwama.
ACT 13:13 Bulus kange farce cin tok kangi cin yabken bafuca yaken firjiya kange Bamfiliya mor nabire mwenge.
ACT 13:14 Bulus kange farubcebo cin chu Firjiya kange Antakiya biten Bidiya fou ci do bikur wabe diye Asabaici cin yiken.
ACT 13:15 Bwiko kiyeranka werfunero kange nob nuwa ka dukume, nobo du bi kur wabero tun tomange, ki kebyebo na kon wiki tomange na neka bikwan ce di kom toki.
ACT 13:16 Bulus la kweni nunge ki kang, nobo Israila kange kom ki ne kwama durtiye kom nuwa.
ACT 13:17 Kwama Israila, chok tenkwanub bebbo, la cin bwi firen Masar, la ki bi kwancer na duktankako ce, ci cokuciye.
ACT 13:18 Bii ner kange ci kutantum curem kwini naar,
ACT 13:19 Kambo cho twallum bitine niber wi biten Kan ana. ni tenkwanub bebo kwali.
ACT 13:20 Dike wo gwam bwi curo kwini kwob na'ar tuddo kwini nung wo cume, kambo wuro kwama neci nob bolangeb, nimde nii dukume Samaila bou.
ACT 13:21 Nobo keni a ne ci liya, kwama ne ci Shawulu bibwe Kish, ni naniyak Benjamin yilam liya curo kwini na'ar.
ACT 13:22 Kwma kwmco dor kutile liyare nen, kum dauda yilam liya ciye. Dor Dauda kwama yiki man fiya Dauda bibwe Yesu niwo ner miro cwitiye an ma dike ma cwitiye gwam.
ACT 13:23 Fou mor naniya ni wo kwama ceru ki nii fuloka Yesu, na wo co ma noro can mane.
ACT 13:24 Wuro bwi nimde Yesu bou yahaya tok ker Yukwamwem kwamambo na yilokako ce wo nobo Israila.
ACT 13:25 WoroYahaya dim nagen cerori co tok ki we kom kwatiye? make bo cho.
ACT 13:26 Kebmibo bibei mor naniya Ibrahim, kange wo wab kwama ti more kume, ki bo ci tungu fulen folokako.
ACT 13:27 Ki ker nobo yirangum Ursalima kange nobo tanki ciye, ci nyom cho bou cin dim tok ka nob to dukumtiye wo ci kiyeranti kakuk Asabaici fiye twalka ceko.
ACT 13:28 bwen no dwalleu ci fiya dike bwi wo lam na bware ce dor cer cinken Bilatus a twallum cho.
ACT 13:29 Kambo ci dim kwarub dike ci mulange dor cere, la cin cukum cho dor bwatiye ci yoken cho mor tuwe.
ACT 13:30 Di kwama kum co mor bwiyare.
ACT 13:31 Nobo bou wari kange ce feren galili kange Ursalima la cin ta to co ti kume kila. Nobo wuro ci warke ce nobonin nawo.
ACT 13:32 Nyon bou kumen ki fulen wo lamlome, ker norowo ci ma tenkwanubebo neneu.
ACT 13:33 Teluwe dobbinen noro. Nyo chon kum Yesu mor tuwe, nawo mor bifumereu Zabura na yobe cemo bi bwemi dwen ma yilam Tee mwe.
ACT 13:34 Tak dike bwici kun cho tuwe co wo kari, bwi ceu fuyem tok ker nyo, man ne kom bibwiyer dauda wo wucaake bichom.
ACT 13:35 Wo cho dike bwi co tok ker mor kange Zabura mani mwa dob nii wucakke mweti fuyem.
ACT 13:36 kambo Dauda ma kwama ni wabe mor nire ce dike kwama cwitikye, ca bwiyam, cin furumco wari kange tenkwanubcebo, con fuyem.
ACT 13:37 Di la nii wo kwama kunge to bo fuyeka.
ACT 13:38 Kebmebo kom yomom fiye niwo wiyeu ci makumen fulen kere cutangka bwirang ke.
ACT 13:39 Fiye co wiye gwam nii neken bilenke an fulom mor dike werfener Musa ko mani cokkom ti dor cereu.
ACT 13:40 Na wo nyori kom yila ki cini kange dike nob nuwaka dukumeko toke kari bwi dor kumer.
ACT 13:41 Kom nob cwikanka, kan lentanginker nyomankar take kan dim. wori mama nagen ti morkumeni kume, nangen do maka ciyati bwen ci yi komdi.
ACT 13:42 Bulus kange Barnabas certiri nobo kenci ciya tok ten kerowo bidiye Asabaici wo botiye.
ACT 13:43 Kambo wabe dime, Yahudawa kila kange wuro do bwanka Yahudawa co ci ne danne, ciya ma nangen luma kwama.
ACT 13:44 Asabaici yilakangu cunnukuru bwirum na ci nuwa ker kwamaro.
ACT 13:45 Di la yahudawa to mwer ka nobe ko, la cin dinki kor ci wengngum dike Bulus toke take cin ko.
ACT 13:46 Dila Bulus kange Barnabas cin tok ker ki bi kwan manki gtai, ciki tamyo a ter yika kume ko ker kwamaro, Dauda kom tungume, kom nungi kom datenbo dume wo diriye na wo Nyori, nyan yilaken nobo kunmtacele nen.
ACT 13:47 Nyo Teluwe dok nyo ki, man yo kom filang wiye nobo kuntacele wiye, na kom boki fulonka cwika dorbitinero nen.
ACT 13:48 Nobo kumtacele nuwa nyori la cin ma bilantum, cin wab ker kwamaro gwam wuro ci ne fiyaka dume diri yiloten.
ACT 13:49 Ker Teluwe wabi wi yare tinin bo cuwo.
ACT 13:50 Dila Yahudawa cuk natubo kange ma wabe, nobo ken, kange nobo durtinim nabarubb wi cinanlore.
ACT 13:51 Dila Bulus kange Barnabas fercinen ti kwero naci ke wi. cin cu cinanlor koniya.
ACT 13:52 Nob bwankabo cin dim ki fuwor neret kange yuwa tangbe.
ACT 14:1 Ki kwama wo Bulus kange Barnabas doken bikur wabe yahudawa ri cin tok kero kambo numbo duce wo yahudawa kange Helinawa ne bilenke.
ACT 14:2 La yahudawa buro nebo dureu cuuk nubo wo kumceleu ri dukci cin man funer kange keb cebo.
ACT 14:3 La cin yi wi kumeni kila, ci tok ker cero ti kibi kwan neret wori bikwan kwamaro wi kange la cin ne yirome dor luma cero. Cin ma wuro ki yirome diker nyimang katini wo a mati kang Bulus kange Barnabas.
ACT 14:4 Di la nubo cinan loreu kitangum kangen bo bwangten yahudawa kangumbo bwnagten nob tomangebo.
ACT 14:5 Kambo nubo kunta cileu kange Yahudawa (wari kange dubo durtiniceu) cuwa naci neci dotange la naci mubang ci ki ter.
ACT 14:6 Dila kambo ci nyumom nyeri, ciin cuwa cin cu cinanlor Likoniya, Listira kange Derbe, kange biten tini kentangum ciyeu.
ACT 14:7 Fiye cii yoti kang tok ker kwamako nine.
ACT 14:8 wi Listira, nii kange yim, manki bi kwan nace ko nin wori cin kilen cikko nee ce bou ceu ci yabo yam wi.
ACT 14:9 Nii wo nuwam Bulus tok ker ti, Bbulus dok ti nuwece wi morece. Bulus fwel cenen ten nu la ci tori ciin bilenke naci fiya luma.
ACT 14:10 La cin yi cho ki diro dur, kwenti dor na mwek.” La cho mwabiri ter yambo
ACT 14:11 Kambo nubo mwerum duceuto dikero Bulus maneri, cin kung diro kiny Likoniya ciki, “Bweltimbo bou na noob lacin bow binen”.
ACT 14:12 Ci cuo Barnabas ki “Zafsa” la bulus Hamisa wori co nii ci tok ker tii duceu.
ACT 14:13 Liya wabe Zafsa wo bikur wabeer cero kino bwinko cinan loreu bou ti nenne kange funtini cibwati na latereu nyilo, co, kange nubo mwenim neu cui naci twi ciilen dikero ficange.
ACT 14:14 Di la kambo nob tomangebo nuwa nyeri, ciinm worum kwilen cero, ri cin cerum mor mwerkanga nube ko nen wulom, ci kwa diroti.
ACT 14:15 Ki “nubo ye bwi kom ma dikeroburo tiye? nyin nob ken, ki bwiyo dong-dong kange kumeu. Nyiki yi kom kero ken ri nako yilau bwanka dikeertinimbo bwirko buro ri nakom bwang ten kwama wo ki dumeu.
ACT 14:16 Wo ywel dii kwama, dor bitiner wima kange dikero more ce gwam.
ACT 14:17 Gwam kange wuro ci dob bo dor cero warka mani, ki co min mani yora ki mwem bo cine kom dii kwamau kange melako ki bi bwereu cin dim neer kumero ki cari kange bilangtum.
ACT 14:18 La ki kero wo duwal Bulus kange Barnabas fiye bwei nyimde ci tim ki ci twika cinenek nuwanko ficange.
ACT 14:19 Di la Yahudawa kangembo Antakiya kange Ikoniya bou la cin kwom neer nubero. ciin nubang Bulus ki ter ri la ciin kwob co ciin yaken kicho bwiko cinarlor, cii kwatiri cin bwiyam.
ACT 14:20 Duwal kambo nob bwangka ko tirangum cunga ceke ri cin kwanum la cin doken cinan lor cel finiri cin chu darba kange Barnabas.
ACT 14:21 Kambo tokka fullen kerero cinan loro curo kange fiya ka nob bwangka ceko ducceri, cin yilaken Listira, kange Ikoniya kange Antakiya.
ACT 14:22 Ciin ti neka neer nob bwangkako bikwan ti naci ya yam mor bilenke, ki “Tam ban doken mor liyar kwama ki dotange duce.
ACT 14:23 Kambo ci cikang nubo a bwangtenti kici mor ku wabe gwammeri, la cin kwobcinen dilo ki ngak-ngak ciin neken cii kang kwama, wo cii ne bilelnke cineneu.
ACT 14:24 La cin cuken mor Bicidiya ci lam Bamfiliya.
ACT 14:25 Kambo ci tokker cero Biriya, cin yira ken Italiya.
ACT 14:26 Ci dob fiye co tiri, ciin yabken Antakiya mor mwege, fiye wo cii duk cii kang luma kwamak ki nangen do wo cii dim naweu.
ACT 14:27 Ki kwamawo ci lam Antakiya ri cin mweer nubo ku wabe wariyeu, ciin yici dikero gwam wo kwama mani ki ciyeu, kange kambo ci wumom nure bilenke nubo kumtacileu ni neu.
ACT 14:28 Cin yi wi kwitange kange nob bwangkabo.
ACT 15:1 nubo kangembo yirau yahudiya cin bou Antakiya ri, ciin merang kebcebo nen, ki “Tano kom biye bo laro nawo werfun Musa ro tokkeri, mani ko fiya cerkati.”
ACT 15:2 Wo dok Bulus kange Barnabas mor kobkangka kane ci. la cin cok Bulus kange Barnabas kange kangembo mre ce na cin ya Ursalima, cin wabkangi kange nobtomange bo, kange nubo durtinimbo dor meke wo.
ACT 15:3 La nubo ku wabeu tom ci, cin cu mor finikiya kange Samariya la ciin yi cii yioka nubeko kumtacileu. ciin bou ki fuwor nerero dur fiye kebcebo wiye.
ACT 15:4 Ki kwama wo ci bou mor Ursalima, nubo bi kurwabereu yoci kange nob tomangeebo, kange nubo durtinimbo, la cin yici dikero gwam wo kwama mani ki ci yeu.
ACT 15:5 Di la nubo kangembo wone bilenke, wo ki more nob ding lingebeu, kweni tiri ciki, “Tamnyo a biye cinan lor, rina neci nyal ri naci bwangten werfuner Musa ro”.
ACT 15:6 La nob bwangkabo kange nubo durko mweri wari naci to dike wor.
ACT 15:7 Bwiko kwob kanka ko duce ri, Bitrus kweni tii ri, la yi ciki “Kem bibo, kom nyimom ki kwama duce cumeu, kwama ck ni more kume, la nyimi nubo kumtacileu a nuwa fulen kerer certiye, naci ne bilenke.
ACT 15:8 kwama wo nyimom mor nereu, la yici ki yuwa tangbe co wucakke ci nee cii na wo ci ne beu.
ACT 15:9 Ci tu bobo ki dimen kange ci la cin nirom ner cero ki belinke.
ACT 15:10 La nyori, ye bwi ko cuwa kwama, la kom yo nob bwanka bonen ten tu tum ti, wo tebbeb kaka'a bo dolbo tu kake?
ACT 15:11 Dila bin ne bilenke ban fiya fuloka ki luma nere kwama na ci ken.
ACT 15:12 Nubo gwam tam cinge kambo ci nuwa Barnabas ti kange Bulus yici yirom boti kange diker nyimankako wo kwama mani tiber nubo kumtancileu kange ceke.
ACT 15:13 kambo diim tokka kere kori, Yakubu ciya ki “Kebmibo, ko nuwa ye.
ACT 15:14 Simon tok kambo kwama ki kaba ki lumanek tiikam nubo wo yim kumtacileu ri naci to dorcero nin nob more ce.
ACT 15:15 Ke tinim nob tomangeb dukumero ciya kange wo, nawo mulangum meu.
ACT 15:16 Bwiko dikero wo man yilau, ri man mutilo Dauda wi tak, wo yuram bitineu, man yila muti tiyak cekowi, nabi tiken ki cho.
ACT 15:17 La nubo kumeu atin do kwama kange nubo kumta cileu gwam wo cico tiki dem mire.
ACT 15:18 wo cho dike kwama tokkeu, wo ma dikero buro nyumom nanduweu.
ACT 15:19 Nyori, mi tori bi nere nubo kumta cileu wo yilam kwama nineu dotange.
ACT 15:20 Dila kange cinen tam nyo ciya dubom fulendo kange buro tumbo, kange wo ka biciro bwiyam bwiya.
ACT 15:21 Wori ci tok ker ti mor werfun Musa mor cinan lor gwam ki kaltiro nanduweu la ciki kiyei mor bikur waber diye fobka gwam.
ACT 15:22 La yor nob tomnagebonen kange nubo durko kange nubo bikur wabe ro nen gwammeu na ci chok Yahuza cwoti ki Barsabbas kange cila buro no nubo dor kebcebeu. la cin tom Antakiya kange Bulus Barnabas.
ACT 15:23 cin mulangi ki kangcek fiye nob tomangebo, kange nubo durko, keb kumebo, ki kebnyebo wo no kumtacileu mor Antakiya, Siriya, Ciliciya, Yarume.
ACT 15:24 wori nyim nuwa kangem nubo ceri fou nyinen, kebo ki yomka nyek, la cin kwomcang kom ki keti ro kange kumen nereu.
ACT 15:25 Nyitori yori kabo nyo wo nyane dume ne wine nanyi cok nubo kangem ri nanyi tomci kumen kange nubo nyi cui cuiyeu Barnabas kange Bulus.
ACT 15:26 Nubo wo neken dume ceu ki Teluwer bek Yesu Kiriti.
ACT 15:27 La nyin tom yakubu kange Silas wo, ayikom dike coti win ken ki mor kere ce.
ACT 15:28 Wori yori kabo yuwa tangbe kwamakonen kang nyo ri, nyi yo kumen deben do dur wo la dikero wo tam a bwang tenneu.
ACT 15:29 Di kom dubom dike cii neken bibwiteu, noka bwiyale, woka biciro bwiyam bwiyau, kange buroka. No kom dubom dikero buro ri, kan yi kwamer.
ACT 15:30 La ciin kambo ci yalammeri, yirau antakiya, kambo ci mweru nubo duce wariyeri, ciin neken cii mulangkako.
ACT 15:31 Ki bwikob kiyekako ri, ciin bilangi ki bikwan nere ro.
ACT 15:32 yahuza kange wo nob tomangeb dukumek takeu ne nubo bi kwan neret ki keti duce, ri la cin fiya bi kwan.
ACT 15:33 kambo ci darang kume tini wiyeri, ciin yoken cii ki fuwor neret nubo co nen, na ci yilaken nubo tomou ciye nen.
ACT 15:34 Dila cila tori yori kabo ci tim wi.
ACT 15:35 Dila Bulus kange Barnabas tim Antakiya (kang tangum kebcebo duce) ci ki merang cinen ti ri, ci tok ker kwamaro ti.
ACT 15:36 Kambo kume tini ri Bulus yi Barnabas ki' na weu “bi yila nabi yarum kebbebo mor Cinanloro gwam wo ni tok ker kwamareu, nabi to keno ci mati nyi ri”.
ACT 15:37 Barnabas cui naci tu Yahaya cii cuo ti ki Markus ce kange ci.
ACT 15:38 Dila Bulus kwabi ri, ki yorbo cia tu Markus, wo dubom cii mor Bamfiliya ri yabo kab tak kange ci nagen do nineu.
ACT 15:39 La kwob kangkako dou tiber cer, la bou ki yal kanka bwitici, Barnabas tu Markus kane co la yab mwmbo ciin yaken kuburus.
ACT 15:40 Dila Bulus cok cica can ciin cu, bwiko dulo ko kebcebo kwocinen, neken cii kang luma kwama.
ACT 15:41 La cin yaken mor Syria kange Cilicia, ci nee nubo bikur wabere bikwan neret ti.
ACT 16:1 Bulus tak bou Darbe kange listira, la nii bwankako kange co ti ki Timoti wiwi, bibwe nawiye Yahuda wo nii bilenke, dila Tee ce Baheline.
ACT 16:2 Cii tok dikero kenti dorcer nyi nubo wo Listira kange Ikoniya.
ACT 16:3 Bulus cui naci ya yam kange co, la cin to cho, cin biye cinen laro ker yahudawa wo fiye tini curo nineu. wori gwamce nyimom ki tece nii heline.
ACT 16:4 Kambo ci cukenti mor cinanlore, ciin nerang nyal tinimbo nob tomangebo wo kange. nubo dur tinimbo wo mor Ursalima ciya cike ri, naci bwangten.
ACT 16:5 La nubo bikur wabereu fiya bikwan neret mor bilenke la ciin kila cii cobten ti diye ki diye.
ACT 16:6 Bulus kange nubo tikan co tiyeu ya mor cungko Phrygia kange Galatiaya, wori yuwa tangbe kwamako ywanmci tokka ker cero cunga ko Asia.
ACT 16:7 Ki kwama wo cii bow bidom kange Misiyari, cii cuwa na ci do mor Bitiniya, dila yuwa tangbe Yesu ywamci.
ACT 16:8 Kambo ci dou Mysia ri, ciin yirau mor cinanlor Troas.
ACT 16:9 Bulus ma dukumbo ki kume; nii Makidoniya tiim wi, kinong coti ki, “Bou fou Makidoniya na mwi tikang nyo”.
ACT 16:10 Kambo Bulus to dumeri, dangjang do naci yaken Makidoniya, cin kwabi nercer ki kwama cuo nyo nyi tok ker cero Makidoniya.
ACT 16:11 Kambo ci dob mor Troas ri, nyin yaken ciyer nyin yaken Samothrace, la cel fini ceri nyin bow Neapolis.
ACT 16:12 La nyi kwen wiri nyin cuo Philippi, wo co cinan lor Makidoniya, cinan lor la tangnumbo mor biten Roma; La nyin cerum wi cinan lor nen kume ni kila.
ACT 16:13 Ki diye fobka Yahudawa ri nyin cer ken nyilo cinan lor kong chaci ki kwa nere ki nysn fiya fiye kwobka dilo wi. La nyin yiken ri, nyon tok ker. kange natubo wo mwerum wiyeu.
ACT 16:14 Nawiye kange dendo ki Lidiya, wo wiye kwilen tiyeu, ci ceru cinan lor Tiyatira, wo wab kwamatiyeu, cuwa tu nuwa nyo. La Teluwe wumom neer cero cin cuwa tu ki dike Bulus tok tiyeu nen.
ACT 16:15 Kambo co kange nubo loceri, cin kenyo ciki, no kom ciya komki min yilam ki bilenke kwama nin di kom bou ko cerum lomi. “La cin dok nyo nyin ciya.
ACT 16:16 Nyori, ki kwamawo nyin yaken ti fiye kwob ka diloke, bibuya canga kange woki ninga tokake wab kang nyo. Ci bou teluwe ce nen ti ki kyemer ducce ki to kako ci totiyeu.
ACT 16:17 La bubiya wo bwnag ten Bulus ti kange nyo la ci kwabang dir, ti ki “Nubo buro cangab kwama dureb. ciki yi kom nure fuloka”.
ACT 16:18 Ciki mai nyo ki kume tini kila. Dila kambo Bulus kangum neer cero kayam meri, yi kangi la yico “mi nyal nenti ki den Yesu Kiristi, ceru cinen”. La ciin cerum ki kwama co.
ACT 16:19 Kambo teb teluweb cebo tori yoka neerek fiya ka mweb kemerceu cuwe ri, ciin tam Bulus kange cila kwob kanci yaken ki cii fiye tubo miyem diker tiye kabum nob bolangeb.
ACT 16:20 kambo ci bou ki ci ka bum nob bolangebri, cii ki “Nubo buro kum cnag cinan lor beroti. ciin yahudawa.
ACT 16:21 Cii merang nure ti wo kebo dong-dong kange dike nubo Roma ciye ciya cuko naci bwang tenneu.
ACT 16:22 La mwerkan nubo ko gwam kwinang Bulus ce kange Silas, nob bolangebo wob rangum kwilen cero cii nen ri ne nyallo naci makanci ki Belyange kwamangi nyeu.
ACT 16:23 Kambo malli ciyeri? Ciin dokken cii mor Furcina, ri ciin yi nii to furcina tiyeu na kii ca kum cii yorak.
ACT 16:24 kambo ci yo nyallo weri, nii to ka Furcinako dokken cii kuwe more ri cin kum na tini ceko.
ACT 16:25 Kina ciinkume Bulus kange Silas, kwob dilo rila cii ka nuwe wabka kwama tii la tangnum nubo furcinau cuwa tuu nuwa ciiti.
ACT 16:26 Dang jangri ka mikanka dor bitiner wo dok kwar kur furcinau mikangume la danjang nyilok tininmbo gwam womangum kang nubo bwambwabeu kwiya.
ACT 16:27 Nii to furcinatiyeu yuram dumbo ri, cin to nyiloko wumom, la cin co ku kulen cero ri, cin cui naci twallum dor cero, wori cin kwabi ki nubo furcinau cirangum.
ACT 16:28 La Bulus kwa cinen dir kibi kwan ki, “Nuware dor mwe ro nen twirak, wori nyin wi fou gwam nye.
ACT 16:29 Nii to furcina tiyeu me naci bo cinen ki kirak, la cin doken mor wulom mor taiye, ciin cungi kabum Bulus kange Silas.
ACT 16:30 La ciin coku ci kaleri, ciki “Nubo dur miik nye ma mati nami fiya fuloka?
ACT 16:31 Ciin yico ki “Neken bilenke teluwe Yesu nen, namwi fiya fuloka mo kang nubo lomeu gwam.
ACT 16:32 Ciin yico ker Teluwero, kange nubo loceu gwam.
ACT 16:33 La nii yo furcina tiyeu tu ci ki kume cuo, la cin nirom dercero, ri co loce gwam cin yum mwem kwamam bo dang jang.
ACT 16:34 la kambo ci bou ti Bulus kange Silas loco ri, ci tik cinen carito kaciye, cin bilangi ducce kange nubo mor luwe ceu, wori cin ne bilenke kwama nen.
ACT 16:35 La kambo fini celumeri, nob bolangebo tom nobo to cinanlor tiye nen ker, ciki “Dob nubo co a yaken ti”.
ACT 16:36 nii to furcinan tiyeu yi Bulus kero couki “Nob bolangebo tunguo tomange minen na dob kom ko yakenti. na weu dila kom ceru ri nako yakenti ki luma.
ACT 16:37 Dila Bulus kane silas ciya cinen ki “Cii malli nyo nyanglang bolang mani, ri nyi nubo Roma keneu- la ciin mer ken nyo mor furcina. La ciki cui wona weu naci yoken ki yurangka ka? mani nyo! Ciya bou ki bwici naci cok nyo kale”.
ACT 16:38 La nii to kakkawo ya yi nob bolangebo kereburo. Kambo ci nuwa ki Bulus kange Silas nubo Roam ri cin cuwam tai.
ACT 16:39 Nob bolangebo bou la ciin ken ci rila cii cokangum kale, la cin yici ki ciya cerum mor cinan loro nen.
ACT 16:40 La Bulus kange Silas cerangum furcina ri cin bou to Lidiya. Kambo Bulus kange Silas to nuberi, ciin neci bikwan neret, cin dubom cinan loro.
ACT 17:1 Kambo cin cum biten Amfibolis kange Aboloniya, cin lam biten Tasaloniya ka, fiye lo kwama yahudawa wiyeu.
ACT 17:2 Bulus, kambo cilerumeu yakenti cinen tokanti kange ci kume nukune kiriti taar, mor bifumer tinim.
ACT 17:3 Bulus wumom bifumero yici ki, “Atam nyo Kiristi anuwa dotange, an kunum mor tuwe yici ki “inco Yesu miyikom ti inco kiristi.
ACT 17:4 Kangum Yahudawa ciya cin bwangten Bulus kange Silas, kange Helinawa, Kange nubo kumtacile neken dor cereu duce kange natubo dur tinim kebo bi duwar.
ACT 17:5 yahudawa biro nebo bilenke cin dim ki kurom, cin tokangum nob kutumebo fiye mi yeka kange tenka, cin kum kutumeu mor cinan lor, nubo ducce bwang ten citi. yacin ter kiyando lo Yesu nen, cin cokum Bulus kange Silas kabum nubem.
ACT 17:6 Dila citobo Bulus kange Silas cin kwob kangum Yason kange nob bwanka kwamam ko kange yaken kici kabum nob bolonageb mor bitinenceu, ciyiti ki, Birombo nubo kunene nubertiye, wo cin bou binen.
ACT 17:7 Nubo wuro Yason yociyeu cin fuwam werfun Kaisar, ciyiti liyakange wi dendo Yesu.
ACT 17:8 Kambo nubo kange nob bolnagebo nuwa nyeri, lan kwomci.
ACT 17:9 kambo ciyo kenero Yason nir kange tangne nubori, lacin nyamkan cinen.
ACT 17:10 Mor kumewo nob kwamabo cokum Bulus kang. Silas, cin twomci biten Biriya. kambo ci lameri, cin doken mor lo kwama yahuda.
ACT 17:11 Nubo Biriya kidimen kange nubo Tasuliska, cin ciya kange ker Bulus cero kinero win. Cifuwa bifumer kwamaro ti kumeni kumeni, wori na cin yimon ker Bulus. Yora. keno bilenkeri.
ACT 17:12 Naweu la nubo ducce morece cin ne bilenke wari, kange natub helinawa wo, cin yimom kange nabarubo ducce.
ACT 17:13 kambo yahudawa wo tasaloniyawa cinuwa ki Bulus tok ker kwamaroti Biriya cin yaken wi firen, cin kun ner nubero.
ACT 17:14 Dang jang nob kwamabo Biriya to Bulus twam ken caji cin dubo silas kange Timoti bwiri.
ACT 17:15 Birombo wo yati ki Bulus tuu co kutan biten Antina. kambo ci dob Bulus wiyeri, cin yo tomange, cinen wo Silas ce kange Timoti na cin bou cinen wolum no nure wiri.
ACT 17:16 kambo Bulus ningtan boka Silas koti kange Timoti Atina kangum ner mor nerece, kambo cito bitineco dimki bibwiti tinim.
ACT 17:17 Cin fuwanangi kange yahudawa lo kwama kange nubo wab kwamamtiyeu, kange birombo citiye kirkireu, fiye miyake kange tenka.
ACT 17:18 Dila kange Abikuriyawam nob nyomkab wabkang kange co. Kangumbo yiki “Nyewo niwo tokker nyeu ki tok kiye?” kangembo yiki “Cin cerkan ni kange wo co nubo ti na bwang ten fulendo fwereu,” Wori ci tok ker Yeesu roti kange kwenka ceko tuweu.
ACT 17:19 Cin Bulus cin yaken ciko diko Arassa, ciyitiki, mwo nyin yo merangka ko wo mwe fwerko woka?
ACT 17:20 Kertinimbo mutikan tiyeu, fiye nyinen. Nyi cwiti na nyimom dike kerowo dan tiyeu”.
ACT 17:21 (Antimiyawa) kange fabubo more ceu, cine dor ciro kang tikangka dikero fwirtinim kange tangnim cem.
ACT 17:22 Bulus tiken tiber dii Arasa yiki, “Kom nubo Aniniyawa min nyimom kom nob bikwaneb fuleneb.
ACT 17:23 Min ynimom kambo kom ki wabre kwama kimeu min bwelangtiyeu, dila minto tang lando kange dikero mulangum wi dorce tokktiki, “Kwama wo wuro cin nyombeu.” Miki tok dike kom wabti mor bwininyomkau.
ACT 17:24 kwama ywel dor bitinero kange dike moreceu, kambi cin co kwamam diyeu kange bitineu, mani yi lo kwama wuro nubo mu ki kang cikeu.
ACT 17:25 Mani do tikaliti kange wo labou a neco tiyeu, kange fubom kange dikero wuyak.
ACT 17:26 Nii win nin ci fwel nubo dor bitinere gwam, naci yi dor bitiner, co ci nung kume ciya mati dor bitinere kange yika tini fiye ciya yim tiye.
ACT 17:27 Naci do kwama, tano ciya do cori, naci fiya co. Bwenno ci kutangbo beneneu.
ACT 17:28 Biyim morece binuwa luma bekti, kambo kange mi nyomka more kume toke. “Bo bibyo loce.
ACT 17:29 Nno bi bei kwama ri, datenbo bi mwer kang kwama kange mwin kaka no kokaa banatini, kange tini wo ci ywirangeu.
ACT 17:30 Dila nyori, kwama turingum kumeni bwini nyom ka, dila cin tokker nubokwarub adubom bwinraka kereko.
ACT 17:31 Kuniwi wo ciyo ca ma dorbitinenereu win bolang tiyeu mor bilenke, ki niiwo ci cokeu. Kwama dang nii co ki kunka ceko tuwe.
ACT 17:32 kambo nubo Atina nuwa ker kwenka tuweri, kangem bo buo Bulus kangem bo ki. “Nyan nuwa tenen tak, dor kerero wonen.
ACT 17:33 Lanyori Bulus dubomci.
ACT 17:34 Dila nabarubo kangum bo morece ciya ki ker kwamaro, cin ne bilenke, mworum kange diyoni Siyus in ni durlor. Dii Arasa kange nawiye kange deudo damaris kangum bo wari, kange ci.
ACT 18:1 Bwiko dike buro ko gwam di Bulus dubom Antakiya yaken Koranti.
ACT 18:2 La wi ca wab kan kange bayafude kange dendo Akila, bwe bitine Buntus bou ti bowe Italiya kange wice Balkisu. wori kalaudiya tok kero ki nyial Yafudawa a dubom Romawu. Bulus ya cinen.
ACT 18:3 la wori nangen ciro win con yi kange ci co managen. wori cin nob yuwel ka teneb.
ACT 18:4 La nyo Bulus ti yai ku wabe kakuk fobka co cuiti na co fiya ciya Yahudawa kange Elenawa.
ACT 18:5 kambo Silas kang Timoti lam Makidoniya ri, Bulus neken dorcero kero min, warker Yafudawa nen Yesu co Kristi.
ACT 18:6 La kambo Yafudawa kunang cinenten, ci to coti Bulus chokum belle ceu kaci la yii cia bwiyale kumeu a yila dor kumer. Man cerum nawo kange kab maki yan nob kumta cilenen.
ACT 18:7 La chon dobum ci con cu lo Titus, Justus nii wo wab kwamam tiye. Loceu bidom kange ku wabeu.
ACT 18:8 Ki pu nii dur wuu wabero ne bilenker Teluwe nen, kange nubo loceu, la korangtiyawa dorcereu ne bilenker la cin yuu cinen mwem kwamambo.
ACT 18:9 Kwma yii Bulus ki kume mor dukume cuwa re tai, tokkero kendo.
ACT 18:10 La min wi kange mo, kange nii mani a nuwa mwen twirak tiye wori min wi ki nob ducce fou mor cinan loro wo.
ACT 18:11 Bulus da wi na coro win kange cuiyakko nukkun, merang ker kwamamroti more ciye.
ACT 18:12 kambo Galiyo yilam nii tamki Akaya, Yafudawa kwenang Bulus nin ten wo llam ci yaken ki co kabum bolangeu.
ACT 18:13 Niwo bolum nubo ti na wab kwama, kidimen kange werfun do.
ACT 18:14 La kambo Bulus ki naco tok keredi, Galiyo toki, yi Yafudawa kom “Yafudawa na ki kero bwirko ca maneu na dur di mitin warkero.
ACT 18:15 la buro kan me ke dor kered kange denti kange wer fun kumer, ko tokkan wo bwitikom. Ma cuibo yila nii bolange dor ketitowo.
ACT 18:16 Galiyo dok ci a kwenum fiye boulange nen.
ACT 18:17 la nyeu ci ta sactanicu inya bi kur wabero ci buk co kabum kutile buolange. La galiyo karbo diker ci maneu.
ACT 18:18 Bulus kambo yiwi kumeni kila nyeu lan dubom kebcebo yaken Suriya. Mor nabire mwenge kange Balkisu kange Akila la na co dob fiye nabire mwenge tum nob ti cankuriyari, con cerum yiri doreceu. wori con tuu nor Banazare.
ACT 18:19 Kambo ci bou Aficari, Bulus dubom Balkisu kange Akila wi, la ceu bwicui con yaken mor bi kur waber Yafudawar con fuwakangi wari.
ACT 18:20 La cin me Bulus na yim kange ci kumtinidi, la ciyabo.
ACT 18:21 Ta nure ce dob ci lam yi ci man yila ten kumen na kwama ciyari. La con doken nabire mwenge wi Afisa.
ACT 18:22 Kambo Bulus Yiram kai cariyari, la con kwi con yarum ku wabeu wursalima la con yira ken Antakiya.
ACT 18:23 Bwiko co yim wi kumeni kilamri, Bulus taa nure ce yaken cinan loro Galatiyawa kange Firjiya la ne bi bei tomangeu bikwan nerer.
ACT 18:24 La wi kange bayafude dendo Afolos wo ci bou ce Iskandariya bou Afica, chon nii nyomka ker kwamar.
ACT 18:25 Afolos Cin ne merangka wo teluwe ceu. Nii bikwan yuwa tangbek. coki tok dong dong dikero dor Yesu reu. la chon nyomom ka yuu ka mwenge yuwanak.
ACT 18:26 Afolos ter tok ka kere ki kibi kwan mor bikur waber. La kambo Balkisu, kange Akila nuwa ceri, cin cou cho chunga la cin fwetang cinen nure kwama kambo ken.
ACT 18:27 La kambo cho cwui na cho cuken Akaya la kebcebo ne bo bi kwan neerer, la ci mu lang bibei tomange wo Akaya na ci yoco, kambo ca yiram meri, con Tikan nubo buro ne bilenker ki luma ducce.
ACT 18:28 Afolos Yafudawa diker nyumanka kange bikwan do cho cikeu nungi kero nin la Yesu co Kristi
ACT 19:1 Afolos firen koranti, Bulus kentangum bitine diyele con bo cinanr lor Afisa. fou tak co fiya kangem nob bwanka.
ACT 19:2 Bulus yici kom yo yuwa tangbe ka fiya kom ni bilenke cin ciya, o-ong nyo nuwambo fulen yuwa tangbeko wucakke wi.
ACT 19:3 Bulus la ki yuka mwenge ko wini kom mane, ciki yuka mwenge Yahaya.
ACT 19:4 Bulus ciya ki yahaya ma nubo nen yuka mwenge yiloka, yiki kom ne bilenke wo a boti bwiti bwiko cek, Yesu.
ACT 19:5 Nubo nuwa nyori, co ci yu cinen mwembo ki den teluwe Yesu.
ACT 19:6 Di la Bulus yoti kanko dor cer dila yuwa tangbeko wucakke, yirau dor cer, cin tok ker kange nyitin kange to ka dukume.
ACT 19:7 Cin dim bi kate kwob shilombo yob.
ACT 19:8 Bulus doken kor bi waber co merangti ki bi kwan bwiyer na cuka taar ce. bwantenti ci mor fowaka keret, co fwetang nubonenti ciya ne bilenke, dor dike tabi na liyar kwamaro ce.
ACT 19:9 Dila kangem yahudawa bongum, cin ko bwankako, di cin yoten kanka nure Almasiya kabum mwerka nobek. Nyori Bulus kwab cinen wari kange nubo ne bilenke, yoten merangkako mor merangka Tyrannus.
ACT 19:10 Nyo co matiye dim curo yob, yaken biten Asia nuwan ker kwamaro, yahudawa kange Helinawa.
ACT 19:11 Kwama ma nangen do dur kan Bulus.
ACT 19:12 Wo nubo nuwa bo luma fiya luma twirak ciyeko dim. yowako bwiko ciru nubo nen, ninga, kange kelkelito, yuwako bwirko ci cerangum bwi nobe. La cin yo lalang kwabka bwi Bulus ce.
ACT 19:13 Yahudawa kangem nub bowab wi cin dob fiye co neneu, cin tu dor cero nin na cin ma nange ki den Yesu, ciki nyo dokkom mor den Yesu wo Bulus ma biwerer cerotiye, kom cerum”.
ACT 19:14 Nubo ma dike wo ci bi neber, bibeyo lo nii wabe durko kange bweyude dendo Sceva wii kibi bei niber wo ma dikero wo tieyu.
ACT 19:15 Yuwako bwirko kari ki ma nyomom Yesu, ma nyomom bulus la kumeu, bi we?
ACT 19:16 La yuwako bwirko bwirko mor nii kwenancinenten lam ci cok, ci cer wi ku we cuwo kwancer ki deti.
ACT 19:17 Wuro yilam dike nyomom nyome fiye nubo wiye gwam, Yahudawa kange Helenawa nubo yim Afisa. Cin nuwa tai kambo ken, den teluwwe Yesu fiya duktangka.
ACT 19:18 Nob bwankabo dutce tak, ci bo ci kiye nangendo bwirko ci mane.
ACT 19:19 Nob buwabo cin bo ki bifumer ciyero cin twirangum kabum nobem wo ci kiye dike a tatiye, Lam bikate kwini nung na mwindo ce.
ACT 19:20 La ker kwamaro yalati kibi kwan nure dutce.
ACT 19:21 Kambo Bulus dim nangen cero na bibweret kwamaroce Afisa, yuwa tanbgeko bwanten ki co nure Makidoniya kange Akiya dor nuret, cin yaken Ursalima, co ki, Bwiko ma ferenne, tamyo ya Roma.
ACT 19:22 Bulus twom bibei tomange ce yob, Timoti, kange Erastus, firen Makidoniya, nobuwo tikan ceu.
ACT 19:23 Di la co ki bwici con nintanci firen Asiya nyobi dob. Dila kobkankako dur kweni afisa ker dor nure do wo.
ACT 19:24 Knage nii kwabi dendo Dimatrayus wuro Tuu fulen bwiner tiye wo Diyana ce, wo nangendo bo nob kwabi to nin ti fiya ka kambo ken.
ACT 19:25 La cin mwer nub kwabiyo yici ki, kom nyomom ki kwabiyo wo bo fiya kiyemer doka ti dutce.
ACT 19:26 Kom to, kom nuwa ki kebo ka afisa, dila gwam biten asiya Bulus wo bolom nubo dutce. Yiti ki “Fulen da kange mani ci yweltiki kange”.
ACT 19:27 Kebo kwabi beto a fiyakomkati ki kwace, dila bikur fulen bero Diyana durku a yilam manki nangen. Nyon ca lem dur cero. Co kange biten Asiya gwam, Kange dorbitiner wabko tiye.
ACT 19:28 Di cin nuwa nyori, ci mam funer kambo ken, cin co bi cor ki diro kwamer “Nii dur co Diyana wo Afisa”.
ACT 19:29 Cinan loro gwam dim ka bwali, nubo tibranbo yaka fiye mwerka. Fiya cuwo cin tam far yame ce Bulus, Gayus, kange Aristarchus, borombo bou Makidoniya.
ACT 19:30 Bulus mani naco do mor nobe, di nob bwanka cebo yuwanco.
ACT 19:31 Nyo farub Bulus cebo kangembo wo nubo durtinim yare Asiya cin tom cinen ki kemi kwam kwame ca dore tare.
ACT 19:32 Kange nob cuk kange dikerti, kangem ken cuk kange dikerti, wori nobe kweri nero kayam. Dutce more ce nyombo ye bwi ci mwere.
ACT 19:33 Kangem mor nubo yi Iskandari wo Yahudawa cin tung ti kabbeu, dila Iskandari cerou kung kang ceko ki ciya kumom, cwiti na ci yi nubo mwerom meu ker.
ACT 19:34 Di la kambo ci nyomom co Bayahude di gwam ciye cin kun kiyange na kang keneko yobece ci tok ti ki, “Dur ki no fiye Artimas wo Afisa.”
ACT 19:35 Di nii mulankako cinanloro cwo nou dor nobere, la co ki, kom nubo Afisa, we nyombo ki Afisa tiberowo fulen (Allaliri) nii dur kange fulen do yaru firen dii kwama?
ACT 19:36 Di la ci kanang bo dike weu, daten kom kumom, kom mare kange diker kutti kutti.
ACT 19:37 Kom bo ki nubo wuro fou ku bolange, kebo dur cin nob kob, na mor bi kur wabe, kaka nob dilakab fiye kwama be wiye.
ACT 19:38 Tano Damatriyas kange nob kwabito wari kange ciye nan wiki kange ker dor kange ku bolange wi wumom wume, nob bolange bo wiranagi, ci a ya ki kiyange bwitici.
ACT 19:39 Tano kero kange wi na toka ko ceri an do tiber ciro fou mwerka beko, bo yiti dok-doke.
ACT 19:40 Bilenke boki no mor bitore kange kwalkanke wo bwi duweneu. bo manki dike ba torti dor dike wo bwiye, co tok nyori co, ci yo nobe.
ACT 19:41 Kambo ca nuwa nyori la con dob nubo yalkange.
ACT 20:1 kambo kwalkake dimeri Bulus twomi a cou bibei tomange, la con neci bikwan nerer. La con ne ci nacume can dubom ci coki, Makidoniya.
ACT 20:2 kambo co ya bitene ceri, con yi nob bwanka bo ker bikwaner, La con biyeken biten Helenawa.
ACT 20:3 kambo ca mam cuikko taar wiyeri, yafudawa ma cinen biciren kambo co dadom ca kwina bire mwenge tiye na co yaken Suriya. la con fulogum neer cero yila ken Makidoniya.
ACT 20:4 Nubo yuo cho Asiau, mwerkange Sabatarus, bibwe Buru, Biriya gayus, bibwe Derbi, Timoti kange Antakus, kange Sakundu, gwam ciye nob bwankab Tasalonika, Kange Tikikus, kange Trophimus wo Asia.
ACT 20:5 La nubo buro cuken ten nyinen la ci nintang nyo Taruwasa.
ACT 20:6 kambo na do nabire mwenge Filippi bwiko kumerek carito man ki cam fuwam meu. La cin yii wi kume niber.
ACT 20:7 Kume kaba kumeni kiyang cari teri, Bulus yi nob bwanka bo ker, co cuiti na kubo celfini, la con kwob kercero cuwemje lam cin kume.
ACT 20:8 Kirako wi kila kuwe diyewo nyo mwerkangum wiyeu.
ACT 20:9 La cerangeu bwe kange yimwi dendo Eutychus, wuro yarken dumbo tu'u cou, kambo Bulus tok keroti cuwemi bwe bwayile wo dam dumeu, yuram, bitine con bwiyam.
ACT 20:10 La Bulus yirau ri toki ki, kange nii akwomde dor cer, dume wi bwiyabo.
ACT 20:11 lacon kwiken luwediyeu tak, cinkabkanghum ci cam.'
ACT 20:12 chin bou ki bweu ki dume lachin fiya birom nere kebo bi duwar.
ACT 20:13 la nyo yakenten Bulus nin kina bire munghe nyon doken Assos, nyon cwi na nyo tum Bulus kina bire. wonco dike cocwi maka, con cwi naco yakina.
ACT 20:14 kambo ci fiya nyo Assos ri nyon tumco mor nabire mwenghe nyin yaken metelina.
ACT 20:15 Bwiko kwenka nyeko firen celfini ce nyo bou diyele kiyo celfini tak nyon bou cinanloro militu.
ACT 20:16 La Bulus tuken cuu kako Afisa mor na bire mwenghe. kati yilo co tengum dorcer Asiya, wori co kayamti. na mam di bi dii kakuk fenticon na fiya co wursalima.
ACT 20:17 Wi militu con tom nabarub ya afisa na cou cinen nubo durko ku wabe.
ACT 20:18 Kambo ci bou cinenri, con yi ci ki “Kom ki bwikom kom nyumom, Tabti ki diye kaba ma dokum na'a Asiyau, kambo ma twal kumeti kange komeu.
ACT 20:19 Min bwang teluwe ninenten ki lomjume nee kange mwem, mor boulange wo fiya yero ki biciren, Yafudawa bou.
ACT 20:20 Kom nyumom ma nuwa bou tuu ka nan yikom dike a ma kumen tiye, min bwang kumenten luwe ma merang kumen dikero ti yanglang.
ACT 20:21 Kom nyumom kambo ma werang Yafudawa ti kange Helenawa dor yiloka kwama, kange biten ker fiye teluwe Yesu.
ACT 20:22 La na weu miki yang wursalima yuwa tangbe kwamako mung men ti nyang lang tam in ya, ma nyombo dike a fiyayeti fireneu.
ACT 20:23 La Yuwa tangbeko nung menti cinan loro gwam bwanka kange dotange nintang ye ti.
ACT 20:24 La ma tubo dumemi wiki kange nangen minen, nan dim cuak ko knage nangen do ma yo fiye teluwe Yesu, na tokka fulen ker luma.
ACT 20:25 Na weu kom to, min nyumom kom gwam, bouro ma yiciker liyar kwamareu, mani ka toyeti tak.
ACT 20:26 la min yimkom ki diye no, miman ki bwiyale ni dur mir.
ACT 20:27 Wori ma nuwa tutum nan yikom kange dike kwama cuiti kumeneu.
ACT 20:28 Na cori ko ta dor kumero kange nob bwangkabo wo yuwa tangbe kwama yokom nubo dur cereu. beko cobi, ko to kuu wabe kwamau, wo ca ten ki bwiyale ceu.
ACT 20:29 man nyumom bwiko ma kubomtiyeu, Bifumeru me kangem an dou (Nob yulaneb) more kume mani cia dob kwama ten do ti.
ACT 20:30 Man nyumom bwen no more kumeri kangum nob an kweri an toker kerti to bwirangi nyeu na kom bibei tomange bwiyocik.
ACT 20:31 Na ceu ko yi yim cobkam, ko kwabi ki coro taar man dobbo yika kumek kererk. kange mwem kume kange kakuk.
ACT 20:32 Na wonyeu ma dob komti kange kwama kange ker luma cero, wo bi kwan mu ka kumekeu, lana ne ten kom kwali wari kange nuboburo wi mor kwama cokum gwammeu.
ACT 20:33 Ma dillanbo nuwe ki kanan mwin kange kulen.
ACT 20:34 Mo ki bwimo mom nyumom kanko wo ki ma diker min cuiti mani kange nubo wo kange meu.
ACT 20:35 Dikero gwam min yikom dikero ka ma tikaliti cikeu, kange dike ka mam nangen do ti cikeu, na kom kwa ki ner kerero wo Teluwe Yesu kibwki cho tokeu, wi ki fiyaka dutce.
ACT 20:36 kambo ca dim tokakeri, chon chungi dor nurer chin kwob dilo ti.
ACT 20:37 Nub ciwiye wi kila, cin ne Bulus kwendowe kange cwika cek.
ACT 20:38 La cin kangum ner ki dikero wo cha tikeu, ki mani ciya tou choti tak. La chin yo cho mor na bire.
ACT 21:1 kambo nya yalkang kange ciyeri nyon doken mor nabire mwenge nyon ta nure cinanlor koceu. Celfini la nyon lam Rodusa, wi la nyon yaken cinan loro Batara.
ACT 21:2 Kambo nyo fiya nabire mwenge yab ken ti Phoenicia, la nyon doken.
ACT 21:3 Kambo nyon tou kibru tiyeu, nyon dubom kan ko mokenyeu, nyon mer dor Suriya, nyo yira cinan lorp Taya, wori nabire mwenge a cer kulen cero wi.
ACT 21:4 Kambo nyo fiya bibei tomange, la nyo yiwi kume niber, la bibei tomange yii Bulus, ki yuwa tangbe yare wursalima.
ACT 21:5 Bwiko kumetinen nyon yoten kang yam nyon bo min. gwam ciye kange natub ci bo kange bibeiyo lociyeu cin yo nyo bwim cinan lor. Co la nya cung cungi kong caji nyo kwob dilo.
ACT 21:6 Nya ne kang na cungme kange ci. La nyon doken nabire mwenge, ci kange natub cibo cin yilaken lo.
ACT 21:7 Kambo nyo dim yim nyembo taya di nyon lam talamaya. La wi, nyo yar kan kange kebnyebo nya da kume win kange ci.
ACT 21:8 Celfini nyon kweni nyon cuu kaisariya. nyo donken lo Philip be nine fulen ker tiye, win mor nobe nibereu, nyon yii kange co.
ACT 21:9 La nii wo wiki bibeyo na'ar, bibutob wo tok ker dukumer tiyeu.
ACT 21:10 Kambo nyo yii wi kumeni biduwareri, kange nii dukume bou mor Yahudawa den cero Agabus.
ACT 21:11 Bou nyi nen tuu dak Bulus ko, la bwam nace kange kange ceko, la co toki, yuwa tangbe kwamako toki, nyo Yahudawa a bwa nii dakkewo tiye, la ci an neken cho kang nob kumtacile.
ACT 21:12 Kambo nya nuwa dikero buro di, nyo kange nubo yim wiyeu ken Bulus a yare wursalima.
ACT 21:13 La Bulus yici, ye kom matiye, ko ci wuyeti kom kimen bikwan nertiye? La min ciya kebo ka bwaka, la nan bwiyam wursalima, ki den “Teluwe” Yesu.
ACT 21:14 Kambo Bulus mani a ciyatiyeri, nyon dubom ci ka wiyeko, la nyon toki, dike Teluwe cuitiye a ma nyo.
ACT 21:15 Kambo kumeni wo nyon tu cuayelyeu, nyon kwiker wursalima.
ACT 21:16 Kangem bibei tomange kaisariya cin bou kange nii ci choti ki Mnason, nii kubru, ni yuloka kabo, wuri nya yiiti kange ceu.
ACT 21:17 Kambo nya lam wursalima di, kebyebo nyo ki fuwor nerer.
ACT 21:18 Celfini ceri, Bulus ya kange nyo fintano Bitrus wiyeu, nubo durco wi gwam.
ACT 21:19 Kambo cha yarum ciyeri, la con yii ki winti dike kwama mani mor nubo yim kumtacileu, ki nangen cero.
ACT 21:20 Kambo ci nuwa di cin duktang kwama la cin yii co mon to yii be mbo bikaten kilam wo ne bilenker kange Yesu mor Yafudawa, na cin bwangten werfunero.
ACT 21:21 La cin yii dor mwer, mo merang yahudaa yim tiber nob kumtacileu ci cutang ker Musa ro wi, la mun yi ci abiyetende lar bibeyero, ci a bwangten de dambo carko.
ACT 21:22 Ye bama tiye? bicom ci an nuwa mon bou.
ACT 21:23 Na cori ma dike nyo yi nentiyeu, nubo na'ar wi yinen wo tum nure.
ACT 21:24 Yaken kange nubo buro na nirum dor mwero kange ci na ya cinen dike a ta'a tiyeu, na ci carum dor cero. La nubo gwam an nyimom kero ci tok ti dor mwerue cierke. Ci an nyumom mon nii mo bwangten werfuner tiye.
ACT 21:25 Dor nubo kumtacileu buro ne bilenkereu, nyon mulang cinen, nyon yici kero ki nyial, cia cokum dor cero, ki kulen do ci wab fulen do wiyeu. kange bwiyale, kange dike kwamiye, kange burotum.
ACT 21:26 la Bulus tuu nubo, celfini con nirum dor cero kange ci, la cin yaken kuu wabe, na co yici dii ka kume nirka ciyeko. Co diye neka luma ko a ne ci tieyu.
ACT 21:27 Kambo kumeni niber kiyan dimeu, Yhudawa buro Asiya to Bulus ku wabe, la cin bol nubo mwerkangum meu na tamco.
ACT 21:28 Ci kwabang diroti nubo Israila ki tikang nyo won co nii wo merang nubo minti fiye gwammeu, dike ma kiyeti kange nubeu. werfuner, kange fiye wuro kebo kawo, la con bou ki Helenawa mor kuu wabe, la con yayamfiye cakcake wo.
ACT 21:29 wori cin to Bulus wi kange Tarifima kange Bulus mor cinan lor ci kwati ki neer kange con bou ciko mor kuu wabe.
ACT 21:30 La cinan loro a yilam ki dike, la nubo cwakang wari ya cin tam Bulus. cin kuuken co kuu wabe kale, la cin mangang yilokoti.
ACT 21:31 Kambo ci cuiti na ci twalum ceri, fulen kwi lam niin dur nob kwenebo yico wursalima nubo cua tai ki kwalkanka ke.
ACT 21:32 La Con tuu nenkwanebo kange nob bikwanebo cin cuu yiranken fiye nubo wiyeu. Kambo nubo to ni dur kwenebori, la cin dubom buka Bulus ce ko.
ACT 21:33 La nii dur nob kwenebo yan lam tau Bulus, ki kom bwanco ki dukako yob. la cin me co ye mwa mane.
ACT 21:34 Kangem mor nubo mwerumeu, tok keroti ki dimen. kambo nii durko kwenebo mani nyom bilenker tiyeri, la con toki ki a yaken ki Bulus fiye nangene.
ACT 21:35 Kambo ci lam kwikari nob kwenebo tum co ker kwalkikwalki.
ACT 21:36 La nubo ducce bwangten kwabang tiki dir a twalum co.
ACT 21:37 Kambo Bulus darom na lam fiye nangeneri con yi nii dur cero ki man fiya nure nan yii nen ker ka? nii dur ko me co, moki tokum ki Helenaciya ka?
ACT 21:38 Mwa kebo bwe masare wo kuma cum bwiye mo ter mwer kanka duwek nobek, mo tu nubo bikate na'ar mwa cuu ciko kiya?
ACT 21:39 La Bulus ki min BaIsraile cinan loro Tarsus mor Cilicia min bwe bitine cinan loro dur. Ciyamen nan tokker kange nubowo.
ACT 21:40 Kambo nii dur ko neco nure di, Bulus kenti dor fiye fuwa naa kung ken kang ceko dii wo nung ti cia kumangumeu, kambo fiye tam cineri, Bulus yi ci kero ki Ibraniyanci.
ACT 22:1 Kebmibo kange tebmibo, kom nuwa kaka batiyo wo ma ka ti kumeneu.
ACT 22:2 La kambo nubo mwerume nuwa Bulus yici kero ki nyi Ibraniyanci ri, la cin tam cinen, con toki.
ACT 22:3 Min Ba Ibraniya ci bo Tarcus wo cili kili, kiya, la ma ma kiye kako fou mor cinanloro wo naar Gamaniel. Min fiya mwerum kambo ken dor bwangka mor bifumer tebbebo. min wiki ker bwangka kwamak, nawo gwam kumen ko nyo duweneu.
ACT 22:4 Min ne dotange ki nure wo yaken ciko bwar, bwaka kange tunka lokuka, nabarub kange natub.
ACT 22:5 Kambo wabe durko kange nubo durko a ne warketiye. Min yo mulang ka cinen dor kebbebo Dimascus, nan bwauci na bou ciko wursalima.
ACT 22:6 La ki cin kakuke can nawofilanko dur lo kwama yoten nefilang ti.
ACT 22:7 La man yarken bitine, la man nuwa diro yiye, Shawulu, Shawulu, ye bwi mwa neye dotangetiye?
ACT 22:8 La man kari, “we mo Teluwe? la con yiye, co Yesu nazaret, wo mo ne dotange tiyeu.
ACT 22:9 Nubo kange meu tom filanko, la ci nyombo dir nii woro yiye kereu.
ACT 22:10 la min meco ye ma matiye Teluwe/ teluwse yiye kweni do ken mor Dimascus.
ACT 22:11 La mani ma toti wori filanko wo yem nuwe miu. La nubo wari kange meu tamen kang ko ya kiye Dimascus.
ACT 22:12 Wi ma nii dendo Anaiya, nii cwa tai kwama tifiye wer funer nii ken wo Ibraniyawa dam wiyeu gwam tok coti.
ACT 22:13 Con bou minen, tii minen, la con man to co.
ACT 22:14 La con yiye, kwama wo tebbebo ciyeu coknen na mo nyumom diker co cuitiyeu. Na tom nubo cak-cak, na nuwam diro ceruti nyiceu.
ACT 22:15 wori mwan yikan nii warke ce nubo nin gwam ki dike mwa toweu kange wo mo nuwau.
ACT 22:16 Na weu ye bwi mo ning tang tiye?
ACT 22:17 Kambo ma yilaken wursalima la ma kwob diloti mor kuu waberi, la man yo dukum.
ACT 22:18 Min to yi teti kwer wolum na dobum wursalima can candowu, wori mani cia ciya warker mwe dor minreti.
ACT 22:19 La man toki Teluwe, ciki bwici nyumom kuwo man kurangi, man buk nubo buro ne bilenker dor mwerue mor bi kur wabero gwam.
ACT 22:20 kambo bwiyale ni warke mweu Istifanus coreu, ma tim wi mati ciyai ma con kulen nubo buro do twalceu.
ACT 22:21 La con yiye, ya wori man toum nen kutanfiye nubo kumtacile wiyeu.
ACT 22:22 Cin cuwa tuu cinen lamna wo. la cin kung dir ciyero citi toki, atwalum wang nubeko wo dor bitiner la kebo dong-dong ca dam wi.
ACT 22:23 Kambo ci kwabang diroti, ci mobang kuleng ciroti kange kung ka kwerek.
ACT 22:24 Nii dur nob kwenibou, toki a dom ki Bulus fiye nangen nob kwenebo. La con toki a me coti ki mallika balyakye, wori co ki bwici na co nyumom ye bwi ci kwabnag dirtikercere.
ACT 22:25 Kambo ci bwam co dii ki dukkari, Bulus yini bi kwane wo tim cinen, yori kabo werfun na tom nii wo barome wuro bulanko tacobeu?
ACT 22:26 La kambo nii bikwaneu nuwa weri, la con yaken ni dur nob kwenebo nen yico ki “ye ko do ma ka tiye?” la nii wo Romaneu.
ACT 22:27 La ni dur nob kwenebo bou la meci yiye mon Romanka bulus ciyaco, ki “Ong”.
ACT 22:28 Nii dur nob kwenebo yi coki, kiyemero ducce matiyen yim bwebitineme. La Bulus yico, ci bou ye bwe roma.
ACT 22:29 La nubo buro a meco kerti yeu dubangum co dang jang nii dur nob kwenebo cwam tai ken, kambo co nuwa Bulus bwe Ramon di, wori con bwam co di.
ACT 22:30 Celfiniceri nii dur nob kwenebo cuiti na co nyumom bilenker dor dike yafudawa fi Bulus ti cikeu. La con kwim bwaka cko la con yi liya wabeu kange nob dir loro gwam na cin mwerkangi. la con yirau ki abulus yoken co tiber ciyer.
ACT 23:1 Paul to nubo mwerume ri ki, minya yam kange kwam.
ACT 23:2 Nii dur wabero wo coti ki Ananiya ne nubo bikwan gwam ciya kwanice.
ACT 23:3 Dila Paul yi co ki, “Kwama an kwanne mo nii bwir moyim namo mamen warke ki bolang ka, dila moki ciya kwaye ki kang wo kebo dong-dong kange bolang?”.
ACT 23:4 Nubo tirangum wiyeu ki ye bwi mon torang nii dur nob waber kwama ro tiye?
ACT 23:5 Paul yiki, Yimi ma yombo miki nii dur, molangum molange ki, mani mwa tok bwirang kerti nii dur nubo lokume.
ACT 23:6 La kambo Bulus nyomom kange win bwe Saduciyawa, la con tok kero ki luma wi ki, kebmibbo min nii Farisawa, bibwe farisawa kambo min cuiti na nyomom kwenka ceko tuwe wo man ma bolang cekeu.
ACT 23:7 kambo ca tok nye ri, kwabkang ka bwi bwitici. Farisawa kange Sadukawa kange, mwerenkang kako wo.
ACT 23:8 Sadukawa toki ki, Kwenka mani, bibei tomange mani, yuwatangbeko mani, La nii farisawa nyom gwam.
ACT 23:9 Kwobkang kako kweni wi bwiti cii, la Farisawa ki ciya to bo dikero bwir fou nii wo nen. Ye a bwiti no yuwa tangbeko toker kange co kaka no Bibei tomangeceu toker kange cori.
ACT 23:10 Kambo kwobkang kako dur kweni tiber cereri, nii dur nob kwenebbo cwam tai ki kari ci wobrangum Bulus, ki fiti kang cek, la cin dok kwenebo na yira tou co ki bikwan tiber nob durembo na bou ki co fiye ca fiyam corka tiyeu.
ACT 23:11 Kambo kume kange lauweri, kwama tii cungya cek toki ki, “cware tai cin cuwa nen firen Ursalima naweu. Mwan nii kange fou Roman.
ACT 23:12 kambo fini celum ri, kangum yahudawa ma nero bwir laci nacin co dor ciyero nin chilka ki weri, naci chare kaka, ci no diker no ci twalum Bulus ri, nimde.
ACT 23:13 Nubo cum kwini na'ar wo yi yimbo bwirko weu.
ACT 23:14 La cin ya ni dur wabero nen kange nubo durko ki, Bin yo dorbero fiye chilka no ba twalbo Bulus diker mani wo ba matiye.
ACT 23:15 Na weu bi yi Liya wabero na bou ki co fou bitine na bin fiya co ki dikero bwir ka ceri, cin ciya na twalum co.
ACT 23:16 kambo bibwe hadace bwe bubiya nuwa na weri la ya yi Bulus ki,
ACT 23:17 “Bulus cho kange nii win na ya ki nii wo dur bero nen cin wi ki dike ca toktiye.
ACT 23:18 Nii wo tim wiyeu tuu bwewo yaciko fiye dur nub wabero wiyeu ki Bulus wo fou mor furcina, cin yiki ki nyon bou ki co monen cin wiki dike ca toktiye.
ACT 23:19 La nii dur nub waber tou co doken mor, la me co ki “Ye mon cuiti namon yi yere?”
ACT 23:20 Bwewo yi ki, “Yahudawa ciya ki bouki Bulus fine fiye mwerkangka, cin cuiti na me co diker dor bolnag ceko nen.
ACT 23:21 Dila necire cou, nubo wi cum kwini naar wo ci cwiti nacin twallum ceu. Cin yiyim bou wo ciki mani ciya chati, mani ciya noti, kambo ci twalum ceri nimde ci chachari. Bwen naweu, ciki bati ci ning tang diker mwa tok tiyeti.”
ACT 23:22 La nii dur wabero yici ki kom manki kange diker wo ka yii nii wo tiyeu, nii wo yimco dikero gwam.
ACT 23:23 La con cou nob bikwanebo yob ki, ciya cok nob bikwanebo bikwate yob nacin yaken ki co Caesarea, kange nub tuwabbo kwini niber, kange nubo bikate kwini yob, ciya kwenum ki kume taar rewo.
ACT 23:24 Con yici ki ciya dou bicirdo wo Bulus a fuhtiye na yaken ki con loh kwarer.
ACT 23:25 La con mulang bifumer nawo ki.
ACT 23:26 Claudius Lysias kimo liyar kalero nen Felix, yarum nen ti.
ACT 23:27 Nii wo Yahudawa tam co, la cin cuiti nacin twalum co. kambo bou cinen ki nub bikwaneb, la man cokceu. min yumom ciki no biten Romane.
ACT 23:28 Min cuiti na yunmom diker wo ci tok ti dor cereu. La min ya ki con fiye mwerkang ka.
ACT 23:29 Min nyom ci merang co kerti wo yilam na doka ceu. La cin manki diker wo yilam ciya twalum coti, ko ciya tung coti furcina.
ACT 23:30 Di la cin yiye ciki, dikero bwirko wi wo ci cwiti na cin ma nii wo nineu, la dangjang min tung kenco monen min toki diker ci ficoti cikeu ciya bou ciko fiye mou wiyeu. Ya kwamer.
ACT 23:31 La nob bikwanebo bwang ten diker cha tikeu. Cin bou ki Bulus ki bikume fou Antipatris.
ACT 23:32 Kambo kume lauweri nub bkwanebo dubom nob tuwab bo kange cou. lan cin yilanken ce loh.
ACT 23:33 Kambo nub tuwabbo lam Caesarea ri, cin nee takada wii liyar bitinenen, Cin neken ten Bulus cinen.
ACT 23:34 Kambo liya bitine tou takada ri, Ye bouki Bulus feh? coki no biten Cilicia.
ACT 23:35 Con yiki “Man nuwa nen gwam kambo nubo wo toker tidor mwereu bouri, Con toki ki, ciya yaken ki co kan Liya dur bitenero nen Hiridus firen wabkang ka.
ACT 24:1 Ki kume nundi, Nii kange wii ciyi cotike ananiya nii dur wabe, kangum nubo dur kange nob yob ka bolange decero, Tertullus yaken wi ki kiyange Bulus ce. kabum nii dur bitineronen.
ACT 24:2 Ki kwama wo Bulus tim kabum nii liyar Tertullus yoten torank coti kiwe gwamna “Ker mwer nyo fiya, yiblume to kaba, bo ki yulka bitine ben.
ACT 24:3 Dike mo maneri nyo ki bukan kangen, nii dur Felis.
ACT 24:4 Kali nene do tange, miki nanneti nuyen bi dom nan yinen ker.
ACT 24:5 Cin fiyam nii wo kan dikeroti kilanye yila cuk nubo Yahudawa kalenen gwam. ciya terkutumeti.
ACT 24:6 Mani naco fuyatamin kuwaber, co dike nyo teuce (Nyo cuiti na nyo warcinen wo dong dong kange funereu.
ACT 24:7 Dila Lysias boyoco win kibi gwan kanciyen.
ACT 24:8 Na mume Bulus dikero wo gwam di mwan yumom dike nyi tok ti dorcereu.
ACT 24:9 Yahudawa ciya bwanten ci, chin ciya chiko ki dong dong.
ACT 24:10 Ki kwama wo nii dur ko ne Bulus filanko na tok kereri, Bulus ciya, “Miyumom ki coti kila mwin nii warke bitinewo nen, ki bilangtum mi nung dor miro ti munen.
ACT 24:11 Mon yumom cubo kumeni kwob cillombo yob ciko min kwi nami ma wabka mor Ursalima.
