ACT 24:12 Kambo ci fiyaye mor bikur wabereu, ma kwobkang bo kange nii kange, ma kung bo kiyan tiber nuber mor bi kur wabe, kaka, cinan lor.
ACT 24:13 Mani ciya nung mwen bilenke dike ci toyeti cikeu.
ACT 24:14 Dila miyinen, mor dikerowo ci toki kuwabe nyoken mi bwangten kwama nen kwanimin. mine dur mor dike ci mulang mor bifumer durko.
ACT 24:15 Min wiki bi kwan nener naceu ken Kwama nen, na nubo buro, fuloka ko bwareu wi, ki nubo cak-cakeu kange nubo bwir gwam.
ACT 24:16 La kang-kang miki mani nami to nermiro kuwayebo, kabum Kwamam, kange niffir.
ACT 24:17 kangum cotinim mi bou nan tinkan kume diker cike kange lumanerer.
ACT 24:18 Min tu nyo ner mir mani nyo la yahudawa biten asiay dikero moten wo cenge ku wabe kebo ki mwer kanka ki kutume.
ACT 24:19 daten nubo bulum ciye bo fiye mo wiyeu duwen naci wiki diker tokka dor mwer.
ACT 24:20 na kebo nyori nubo lominbo ciya togki na ci fiye kidire kikwamawo matogti kabum nob mwerkanka Yahudawa.
ACT 24:21 No dor dikewo mi tokki ki dir kabum ciyeu, wori gwamka nob Bwerem. cimen coti ci doti naci moten bolanko.
ACT 24:22 Felis, wo ci yimco ker dor nureroweu, kungum nuwa kako. Cin yi ki, “No Lysias nii dor, nub kwenebo, yirau Ursalimari, man tok diker amati ki bolang mweko neneu.
ACT 24:23 La co yi nii bikwan ne nob kwenebbo ayoken Bulus kan nob corkab, la co fiya cerka biduwar kati kange mor ferubceb fiyabo nure aneco diker ci cwitiyeti.
ACT 24:24 Kambo Kumeni kange cumeri, Filibus kange wice Duruskila, wo Bayahudiya La cin twomi na cin bouki Bulus di naci nuwa cinen ker bilenker dor Almasiya Yeesu.
ACT 24:25 Di la kambo Bulus bulangi kange co, dor cak-cake, taka dorek, kange bolang ko boutiyeu, Felis cwam tai, La yiki, “Muyaken ti naweu. Dila non fiya filang ki bwiri, min twom mwen.”
ACT 24:26 Ki kwama wo cun nyoti nerwi ki Bulus a neco kemer ducce kir-kir naco tok ker kange co.
ACT 24:27 Ki cwuro yob Borkiyas Festas yilam nii dur buwab Filibus, wori ciki do fuwor bwiyat fiye Yahudawa yoten to Bulus ki toka.
ACT 25:1 La Festus do ki kume taar gwam kaisariya yaken Ursalima.
ACT 25:2 La nii dur wabe kange nubo dur yahudawa cin bo ki kwanere dor Bulus cer, la cin kenco.
ACT 25:3 Cin me tikali cinen na ci doken Bulus mor dotange - di Festus na cou Bulus Ursalima ri na cin twalumco dor nure
ACT 25:4 Dila Festus ciya ciki, Bulus bou firen kaisariya, kutakni coki bweco aniylareken firen.
ACT 25:5 Nyori wo Ayumom bwikan gekotiyeri. Na bwirank ke kange we kange nii wori ciya toco.
ACT 25:6 Dila ki kume narub kaka kwob la nyilake kaisariya. Celfini ceri Nyiken fiye bworange ki ciya bwoki Bulus kabum cem.
ACT 25:7 Kambo Bulus boweri Yahudawa wo Ursalima tirangum bidom ci yoten ci bwerauti ki kiyage laci fiyabo ken wi.
ACT 25:8 Bulus cokum dorcero ki, ma mabo nii nen bwiranke, kaka Yahudawa, kaka kuwabe kaka kaisar.”
ACT 25:9 Dila Festus ki do fuwor bwiyarade fiye Yahudawa wiye, Dila nyori co me Bulus ki mo cuiti namo ya Ursalima.
ACT 25:10 Bulus yiki co tim fiye maka borank kaisar fiye tam ceu. Min ma dike yorbei kom nyumom gwam.
ACT 25:11 Na bicom mima burankge mima dike dateng bwerangke mikobo in bwiyam. dila na dike lam na bitoren cwerke nin, nikange cunkange. mi tuwciurkumeti fiye kaisar.”
ACT 25:12 kambo Festus dim fuwakangkako kange nobe ri La ciya ki, mo cu kaisar monyanken kaisar”.
ACT 25:13 Ki kume kange, liya Agrippa kange Bernice cin yirau Caeserea na cin yacuner Festus ki diker.
ACT 25:14 La lam kumeni, kila Festus nyi liya keti bidarange wo Filibus domti mur kuu kuka.
ACT 25:15 Ki kwamawo mi Ursalima, kange dur ni wabka kange nubo dur Yahudawa ci boki kiyange ce fiye miwiyeu, cin keni naci twalumco.
ACT 25:16 Ki woro yi ciki, ke dam Romawa yibo ki aneken bibei nii bibwiyer, La wo ci kwakiyagece cin neco firank naco congum dorcero nob kiyagecenen, naco kiye ker kiyangece.
ACT 25:17 La ciin mwelim kebo ki tiranka kene, celfiniceri miyiken fiye maka bolange minyici ciya boki nii co.
ACT 25:18 Kambo nob kiyangebo boki kyangeceri, kero ken mani morece.
ACT 25:19 Miyumom kwaka kaciyeko na kuwaabece dor Yesu wo bwiyamdi Bulus ki wuki dume.
ACT 25:20 Mi fwiki kambo ma fuma kerowo matongti lami meco miki monyaken Ursalima na walum kero.
ACT 25:21 Dila Bulus do ciya toco, Kaisar walum kero lamitoki ciya yobco men tukco kaisar nen.
ACT 25:22 Agrippa yi Festus, Min cuiti na nuwa nii wo.” “Fini,” Festus yiki, “Mwan nuwa co.”
ACT 25:23 La ki celfiniceri Agrippa kange Bernice cin bou ki diker chaklang ka, kange nubo durko bitineceu. La Festus toki, ki ciya cokum Bulus fiye ciweyeu.
ACT 25:24 Festus yiki Liya Agrippa kange nubo wi kange ciyeu cin toh nii wo kange nubo mwerum feu nub Yahudawa kange coh Ursalima gwam ci werang coti ki daten bo co yim ki dume.
ACT 25:25 ma nyumom mabo bwirang ke daten bwere, Dila wori co twalum kero cou yaken cuko fiye kaisar wiyeu. Nyori ma motum intomken co.
ACT 25:26 Di miman ki Kerokange mitontiye miki murank kaisar nen. tomange, ki kerowo mibocuko kakumeu, nawonyon mitonentiyeu mo liya Agrippa. nan fiyam dike mayuktanti muranka mikonen dorcer.
ACT 25:27 Fiye miwiyeu Bwira kabo intunin bwiranke mi murankbo bwirang ke co.
ACT 26:1 La agrippa yi Bulus, “Mon nyam coka doremwei la Bulus kunkan ceko yoten condorceroti.”
ACT 26:2 Miki Fuwor nerer, liya Agrippa, ki kerowo yahudawa bouti cuko dor mireu.
ACT 26:3 Nyori mo nii yumka mor den Yahudawa kange yabciebo. Nyori mikenenti. Nyoli bob nermwero kange bwewo.
ACT 26:4 Miyi komti gwam yahudawa yubram fiye yim kallemibo fiye wucakke kange Ursalima.
ACT 26:5 Cin yubrangum ye ki kaba, daten ciya yumom miyiyen na bafarasawa.
ACT 26:6 Naweu miki naci mamen bolang nawo wori nor wa kwama tu tebbyebbo ni nen.
ACT 26:7 Wo cou nure ber gero kwab curomboyo yoti ner wiye. ciya wou ki kwamawo ci wabkwamati ki nero win fiye kwama wiyeu kakum kange kume. Ki yoka nerewa, Liya agrippa, yahudawa buranti.
ACT 26:8 Ye bwikange aburank ti ki diker yumanko kwama akun nob bweyame?
ACT 26:9 La mi burankge ki maka dikero kiden Yesu bana zaret.
ACT 26:10 Min ma buranka mor Ursalima, mi ku nob bwika kwamako duce mor Fursuna. Ki bikwan do wo mifiya fiye nob dur wabero wiyeu, kange wo ci twerciti mineci mwerka duwen.
ACT 26:11 neci dotange duce kwab kuh wabe mi cuti nan dongcinen naci ma burkane. Ma ma kiye ciren kangeci minaci dotange yaken cuka bitiye tim bokage.
ACT 26:12 Ki kwamawo mima buroka boti mi yaken Dimaskus ki ciyaka dur nob wabe.
ACT 26:13 Mor yame mi, ki kaku, mo liya mito firen dikawama wo la kaku filanken filanko ketenye, kange nubo nyo yakenti wari.
ACT 26:14 Kabom kwaob nyo yarken bitine, minuwa diro kange tok keroti kange mwoh ki nye Ibranciyawa yiti ki, shawulu, Shawulu ye bwi mon neye dotange tiye? bwikabo na kundike cucuwe.
ACT 26:15 La miki webo teluwe? Teluwe ciya mo Yesu wo mone dotange.
ACT 26:16 Naweu kwen titiye ki co kerowo manun dor miro munenen nan yome? na yilam canga kange nii warkere dor dike moyume dormireu nawo kange wuro miyinentiye. fokab.
ACT 26:17 Man cuken fiye nobo wiye kange nubo ma to ci fiye mowiyeu.
ACT 26:18 Na mo wumom nuwage ciyeu yilau ki ci kumtacile yilau ki ci filank. na cin fiya cerka fiye yuwako bwirko wiyeu na ci you yuwa kwama, kange fuloka dikero bwir nen wo cha ne nubo bwang ten co tiyeu.
ACT 26:19 La nyori, liya Agrippa miken kom kangumbo ki dukumbo wamito dikwamau.
ACT 26:20 Dila, kabokoce buro mor Dimaskus. kange Ursalima kange biten Yahudawa gwam, kange nob furenebo, mima cinen bwiranke naci yiloten fiye kwama wiyeu, cin ma dike daten yilokau.
ACT 26:21 Co dike bwi yahudawa ci tamce mor kuh wabe ci cuiti naci twalum co.
ACT 26:22 Kwama tikang wo duwin mi tim kabum bibei kange nubo dur, warke dor dike annabawa kange Musa toki abwitiye.
ACT 26:23 Dong dong Almasiya a nuwa dotange anyi lam kaba wociyar komti bwere an tok filang fiye yahudawa kange nubo yumbo kwama.
ACT 26:24 Kambo Bulus dim coka duwek cekori, Festus tok kero ki dir, ki Bulus twaka mani ki nyomka mweka donen twalka.
ACT 26:25 Dila Bulus yico, “mitwalbo nii dur Festus kibi kwan nerer mi tok bilenke tiye kange cinen.
ACT 26:26 Wori liya yum bo dike burombo gwam, co dike bwi mitok keroti kibi kwane, wori miyom dike kange mani wo yurangum yurange.
ACT 26:27 Mo ne bilenke kange nob tomange dukumbo, ko liya agrippa? mi nyomom mo ne bilenke.
ACT 26:28 Agrippa ni yi Bulus mor kere biduware muki cui namo bwolye na yilam nii bwanka kwama ka?
ACT 26:29 Bulus yiki “miki nanenti kwama, mor kene bi dure kange kene dur, kebo mo ki kwama, gwam kange nubo nuwa yilam na mo.
ACT 26:30 Liya kweni ti kange nubo dur kange Bernice, kange nubo gwam yilamom kange.
ACT 26:31 kambo ci dubom ku wabe ri cin ter tok kako kere ko bwiti ci ciki, “Nii wo mabo dike dotange borom kange bwika.”
ACT 26:32 Agrippa yi Festus ki naki niwo tumbo kiyage yakenbo cuko kaisar nadi noci yamkancinen.
ACT 27:1 Bwiko ciyaka ko ki nyiki yang italiya ciin neken kange nubo kangembo furcina kang nii dur nub kwenebo ci co ti yuliya wo mor mwan Agustus ke.
ACT 27:2 Nyin doken nabire mwenge mor Adramatiya, wo ywel bwiti na cii ya bidom kange cunga wima ko Anciya. La nyi yaken mor wima Aristakus wo Tasalonika mor Makidoniya cin yaken kange nyo.
ACT 27:3 Cel fini ceri nyi yiram cinanlor sidom, fiye wo Yuliyas nung Bulus nin neer lumare la cin dobco naci ya farub cebo nen di naci yo toka ceko.
ACT 27:4 Nyi kweni wiri nyin doken mor Wima ri nyon yaken kong mwenge kubruce, wori yuwa ko ne nyo dotange ti.
ACT 27:5 Ki kwama nyi yabken wima nyi yabken dinge kilikiya kange Bamfiliya nyim la mira, cinan loro Liciya.
ACT 27:6 Wii niii nabire nob kwenebo fiya nabire mwenge wo bou Takendariya ri, a yaken ti Italiya cin more ce.
ACT 27:7 Kambo nyi yakenti kumeni kila nyi yaken biluma, la ki cuile gwam ri nyin lam ki dotange bidom kange cinindu ri la yuwa ko dob nyo bo tak nanyi bwangten cunga ko cou, nyin yaken cunga ko ci kicimkice bidom kange karita bidom kange Salmani.
ACT 27:8 Nyi yaken cunga konge ki dotange, nyimde nyi bow fiye kange cou ti ki fiye turangka ko ken, wo bidom kange la ciya.
ACT 27:9 na weu nyin tu kumeni kila, la kwama ngag ngake Yuahadwa cum, la naweu yambo yilam ki tai la Bulus werang ci
ACT 27:10 Ciki, Nubo matori yambo wo bi ter tiyeu atin yilam ki nuwa ka twirak kange le-ka dikerek duce, kebo kawo kwilendo ceu kange nabire mwenge, dila kange dume beuken.
ACT 27:11 La nii na bire nub kwenebo cuwa tu ka diiir teluwe kange nuu nabire mwengeko nin la cuwa bo ker Bulus cero nin.
ACT 27:12 Wori fiye tuka kwilenek na bire mwenge ko bwei yim wiki cukakiya ri nob kwobka nabire mwengeko duce tok ki ciya dubom fiye cou la tano cwika fiyaka ri bi lam cinar lo finikiya, nabi yim (wa kiyauwi). La finikiya co fiye tii mwe nabire mwnege mor karita, wo to kwasalmen ti kange mar to me tiye.
ACT 27:13 Kambo yuwa bange ko ter cu kako kibi luma ri, nubo kwob nabire mwenge ko tiyeu kwabi neer cer ki ciin fiyam dikero cii cwi tiyeu. Dila ciin cukum duka nabirek mwnegeko la ciin bwangten cunga ko karita bidom kange kong mwenge ko
ACT 27:14 La fiyaco bi duwar di yuwako kwani nyeu wo cii cuwa tiki yuro kilidom yoten buk nyo ti diyelenen.
ACT 27:15 kambo nabire mwengeu fweki cukako fiye ki yuwa wori yuwa ko lambi kwan ceredi, nyin bwang ten nur yuwau.
ACT 27:16 La nyin bwnagten fiye nyi fiyam cerka ko diyele bi duware coti ki kauda, la ki dotange nyi bwam nabire bi duware bwi durko nen.
ACT 27:17 Kambo cii kongum nabire mwenge bi duware dii yeri, ciin ma nangen ki duka ceko ri ciin bwam bwi nabireko durko cuko. Taito tamci ki cukum dikero a tam nabire ti dor mwengere dila nyin bwang tenti.
ACT 27:18 Nyin nuwa dotange ducce ki yuwa mwengek wo ki celfiniceri ciin ter cutangka kwileneko wo mor nabire mwengenen wii.
ACT 27:19 Ki kume taar ri nob nangenebo mor nabire mwengeu cutang kwilendo mor mnabire wi ki kang cek.
ACT 27:20 kambo nyi to bo filang kakukek kaka bitiren kume taare ri, yoka nereko ki nyan fiya ceer kau cerum nyinen.
ACT 27:21 kambo cii ya yambo kwitan cari mani yeri, Bulus kweni tiber nob nangeneb nabire mwengeko ri ciki, “nubo, nakin kom cuwa tu kermiro nen, bi kwenu bo karitari no biki fiyabo twirako buro kange leka kwileko.
ACT 27:22 Na weu miyi komnti ko yilam ki birom nerem wori nii mania bwiyati more kume dila ka nabire mwenge bi lem tiye.
ACT 27:23 wori wo min naceu, wo mi wabti takeu bwe tomange ceu tii cunga miik.
ACT 27:24 La ciki cware tai, Bulus tam nyo mwanti kabum kaisar re. la to, kwama mor jire duwece neken gwam nubo wo yaken wari kange mweu.
ACT 27:25 La nyori ko yilam k bikwan neeret nubo, wori min ne bilenke kwama nen atin yilam nawo ci yiyereu.
ACT 27:26 La batin cwa bi kangtangi kange Island.
ACT 27:27 Kambo kume kwobcilombo naareu dimeri, la cii tung nyo fou kange firen mor wima ko adriyate, ki ciin kume ri nubo fu nabire mwenge tiyeu kwabi ki ciin dadum kange bitine Kange.
ACT 27:28 Kambo cii cuwa ri, cii fiya nako kwini yob kambo kakten biduwar di ci cuwa ten di nako kwob cilumbo nung.
ACT 27:29 Cin tum tai ki kangeri ciyan kwiti teer, la ciin curken duka ko ciin komti cikeu naar cwile nabire mwenge nen, cin kwob dilo fini a celum wulom.
ACT 27:30 Nob nangeneb nabire mwengebo do nure ciya dubom nabire tiye ri ciin merken nabire mwengeu biduwareu mor wima. ciin mani namwi ci yan merangken duka ko kangembo wo mor nabire mwenge kabum nabire ko nen.
ACT 27:31 Dila Bulus yi nii dur nob kwenebo kange tangum cembo “No nubo buro mani a tim ti mor nabire, msni ciys fiya cerka ti.”
ACT 27:32 Dila nob kwenebo mwatum dukako cinn dubti yuram.
ACT 27:33 Kambo fini ter celkakeri Bulus kenci gwam cia can carito. ciki Diye wo co diye kwobcillumbo naareu wo kom mor curka, la kom cabo cari.
ACT 27:34 La mi kinong komti, kom cam carito wori cerka kume ko lam, kange kume mani wiin wo a le yere dore cetiye”.
ACT 27:35 Bwiko ci tok kero wari ciin tu carito la ciin bu kwama nen kang, ciin duwa carito cin yo cakako.
ACT 27:36 Dila gwam ce ciin fiya bikwan neret ri ciin tu carito ken.
ACT 27:37 Nubo kwini kwob yob turdo kwini niber cilumbo nuukkun ki dume tini nabire mwenge nen.
ACT 27:38 Kambo cica ci bwameri, cin filam ten ki nabire mwengeu,
ACT 27:39 Kambo fini celumeri ci nyombo bitineu dila ciin to kum ki konge la ciin tokkangi bwiti no ci yan yila ki nabire mwengeu wiri.
ACT 27:40 La ciin mwatum duka ceko ri ciin dobti mor wima. ki kwama co wiin ciin kwim dukako, yila nabire tiyeu. Dila nabire mwengeu kwiti dor yabum cerum cereu. kambum cembo ywiken wi, la mor kwita kako mani la bi kwan mwelka mani.
ACT 27:41 cin bou fiye wo cajiyo yob mwerkangummeu, la na bire mwenge doken mor yabume. Tangum nabire mwengeu ywiken wi la mani yayamti, La cunga ko ki kyarangi ki mwembo mwelangtieu.
ACT 27:42 La nob kwenebo ci naci twallum nob furcinabo kari kange kwa mwembo cwalem.
ACT 27:43 dila nii dur cero cwi naci cer ki Bulus la cin tim ki dikero cii cui makau, nubo nyumom kwaka mwengek la cin mwabken mor mwenge cin yabken konge.
ACT 27:44 Dila tangnum bayilobo na bwangten kange dor bwatiyer kangembo dor nabire nen. Ki nurewo, la gwam nye nyin beken kwamer bitine.
ACT 28:1 Fiya cuwo nya yilau kwamere, nyan nuwa den diiyele cuwa ki malta.
ACT 28:2 Nubo mwan loro cuwa nung yinen luma nerek cin nuwa nyinen kira, cin yuwo nyo gwam ker mwemer kange cwuii ngir-ngireu.
ACT 28:3 La Bulus mwer bwatiye yo ti kirari, kwentibe ceru, wori kirako cwillen cakkan cinen ti kang.
ACT 28:4 La nubo mwan loro cuwo to na cuwe yayim kang cek ri, ci tokkangti bwitici ki, “Nii wo nii twal nob ti ci cuku mor bware caji. Kero dong dongeu ciyabo nii a buuti.”
ACT 28:5 La con waciken na cuwe kira, kii cobo.
ACT 28:6 Ci nintanti na ci to bwici fum, ki kwirum bwi na yarke bitine na bwiyam. La cin to co fiya kutangi, cin tobo diker fiya cobo di, cin fulongum ner cero, cin yi ki con bwel.
ACT 28:7 La bi dom kange fiye cuwe, take kange wi na nii durece diiyele cuwa, wo ci cuwo ti Babiliya yuwo nyo, ki luma nerek, tam nyo na kume taar ce.
ACT 28:8 La te Babiliya cokkati kiwirum bwi kange teka fiya cuwa Bulus ya cinnen kwob cinen dilo, cin yoti kang dor cer con twam co.
ACT 28:9 Bwiko dike woro bwiyeu tangne nube yim diile diile wuro nen nuba. Luma cin bou ken cin twam ci.
ACT 28:10 Nubo wuro ne nyo dur ti ki dur. La nyon ka bati yamtiri, cin ne nyo dike nyo cwitiyeu.
ACT 28:11 Bwiko cwak ko taare nyong kwen yambo ki nabire mwenge wo ma tirako wiiye, nsbire Alexandriya, ki bwel do yob ci ywellum tikab dore cike.
ACT 28:12 Bwiko nya yiram cinanr lor ciranku nyon yim wii kume taar.
ACT 28:13 Wii ri nyon yaken cinan lor Rigiyum ki kume wiin di, yuwa ko bangeu kwenu, la mor kume yobeu nyin lam cinan lor, Butiyoli,
ACT 28:14 Nyon fiya yitub nyebo kange wii, cin cuwo nyong yii kange ci kume niber, nure wo nya yaken Roma.
ACT 28:15 Nyo firen di yitub nyebo nuwa fulen nyero cin ceru cin yuwo nyo, tati fiye miyeka dike Abiya kange bituk taar. La Bitrus to yitubori, con fiya bikwan neret.
ACT 28:16 Kambo nya doken Roma ri, cin dob Bitrus na yi ki kwace kange nii kwene wo to co tiye.
ACT 28:17 Ki kume taar di Bulus cuwo nubo wuro na dur mor Yahudawa. La cin bou ri, con yiki, “yitub me, ma mabo nob nen dikero bwir kaka, dike ka ciya cike wo tembebo ceu, cin taye. Bwiko cin me ya, ci cwiti naci nyam kang minen ci fiya yebo ki bwirangke wo lam twalka.
ACT 28:18 Kambo cii merang ye kereri, cin cwi na cin nyemkan minen, wori ci fiya yebo ki bwirang ker wo lam ciya twalye tiye.
ACT 28:19 La Yahudawa tok diker cwika nerek ciyeu, cin dok ye, ya ki kiyange kaisar nin, muni bou ki kiyange bitineu.
ACT 28:20 Dor kerero wo ma cuwo kom na to kom na yi kom. Nyo neri Israila ci bwam yere.
ACT 28:21 La cin yi co “nya yuwobo tomange kange Yahudawa dor mwer kaka kange yitubo bou bo nyi nyo dikero bwir dor mwer.
ACT 28:22 Nyo wcii na yi nuwa muneng ye mo kwatiye dor mwan nibero wo, wori nyon nyimom dike wuro cin toki fiye gwam.
ACT 28:23 cin yo cinen kakuko, nubo ducce bou fiye ci yim wiye con yi ci dikero gwam, con yi cerka liyar kwama, con ken ci dor Yesu ter ti ki Musa ya ciko nob tomangeb ki buri mee doti.
ACT 28:24 Kangum bo ciya dike co tokkeu, kangumbo ne bo bilenke.
ACT 28:25 La cin ciya kambo kange butici, Bwiko Bulus dim kere di cin cu. “Yuwa tangbeko wusakke tok ker nyii Ishaya nii tomange teb kimeb bo nin.
ACT 28:26 Yi ki “ya nubo wuro nen, na yi ci,” ki nuwaka, kan nuwa, la ma ka nyomti, ki toka kan to, maka nyomti.
ACT 28:27 wori ner nibero wuro kuci, ki tuci, bwai naci nuwa, cin kumom nuwe ciye, naci tore ki nuwe ciye, ci nuwa ki tu ci nyimom ki ner cer, na ci yilau na twam ci.
ACT 28:28 Nyori kon nyimom fuloka kwamako, cin ya nubo nyumbo kwama, ciya nuwa.
ACT 28:29 La co tokum dike buro di yahudawau kweni, cu lor ki kwobkanka ko dur more ciye.
ACT 28:30 Bulus yii wi ki chor kambo co co yim loh Aya, cin wab nubo gwam wo bou cineneu.
ACT 28:31 La ci tok liyar kwamaro ti, ci meran dikero dor Yesu ti kibi kwamer neret ci ywa cobo wii.
ROM 1:1 Bulu canga Yesu Almasiya co na yilam nii tomange, take cokom coke na fulen kert Kwama.
ROM 1:2 Won co fulen kere do co ma nore ki kining nob tomangeb dukume ce more bifumero wucakke.
ROM 1:3 Dor bi bwece wo bo bowe naniya Dauda mor bwiye.
ROM 1:4 Fuye kwenka cek mor nobo tuwe, cin yo co a yilam bi Bwe Kwama bi Kwane ki yuwa tangbe ko wo wucakke- Yesu Almasiya.
ROM 1:5 Fiye wo co wiye bin nyo luma kange tomange ker ciyaka bilnke mor nobo kumtacili, ker dene ce.
ROM 1:6 Mor nobo wuro kumtacili, kom ken cin cuwo kom, kom yilam na Yesu Almasiya ce.
ROM 1:7 Bifumero wo ki nobo mor Rome gwam, kom nobo ma cwitiye wo Kwama ce, nobo wo cuwo cowe na yilam wucakke. Di luma ayi wari kange kom, kange fuwor nere Te be Kwama nin kange Teluwe be Yesu Almasiya.
ROM 1:8 Ki kiba ma bu` Kwama nin kang ti fiye Yesu Almasiya wiye ker kimer gwam wori cii tok fulen bilen ke kumero ti dor bitiner gwam.
ROM 1:9 Kwama wo ma wabti mor dume mi, mor fulen kerer Bi bweceu co warke mi, wo bwen fiyang di ma tok kom tiye.
ROM 1:10 Kang-kang ma ken ti mor dilo mi bwen ki ma nyi ri ki bwiri nan fiya caka kaba boka fiye kom wiye ki ciyaka Kwama.
ROM 1:11 Ma cwiti nan to kom nan ne kom ne kako kange na yuwa tangbeko ce, nan ne kom bikwan.
ROM 1:12 Mi ki nin tangi nan fiya neka bikwanek more kume, fiye bilenke bwiti be, wo kumeu kange miu.
ROM 1:13 Na weu ma cwibo kom yilam ki bwini yomka, keb mibo, ma cwi na bou kumen kang-kang, [dila no kebo na wori' no cii dob yebo], nami yilam ki bibei wo yuwa tangbe ko ce more kume, kambo ma fiya tangnum nubembo nineu.
ROM 1:14 Ma tum ki tutum nobo Helina kange tangnum nobembo, wuro ki yilene kange wo manki yilene.
ROM 1:15 Ma yim ki bati nan tok fulen keret cero kumen kom wuro mor Roma.
ROM 1:16 Mani ma nuwa kwenduwe tok fullen keret cet ti, bi kwan Kwama wo fulokakoce ki gwam nii wuro ne bilenkere, ki kaba Yahudawa, nimde Helinawa.
ROM 1:17 Wuro more ce cak-cake Kwama ceru yanglang fiye bilenke yaciko bilenke, nawo ci mulangeu,” Nii wo cak-cakeu an bu ker bilenke.
ROM 1:18 Kwama nung funer cero firen dii Kwama dor bwini wabka, kange bwini cak-cake na bi bwe nifiroce, wo bimum bilenke ki fiye bwini wucakke ciye.
ROM 1:19 wori dikero daten cii nyimom dor Kwama re yanglang fiye cii wiye. Wori Kwama fwetang cii nen bilenke.
ROM 1:20 Wori kabal cero wo twelum meu, bi kan cero bak-ni-bakeu wi fiya fwelka kale, mor fwelka kwilenti. Nobo buro ci man ki tabanka fiti.
ROM 1:21 Dike bwiye, bwentano cii nuwa ti ciin nyumom Kwama, dila cii nebo dur a nyo con Kwama. Kaka cii nung cinen buka kangek. Nyo, lacin ciin yilam kule, mor nere ciye, neer cero manki bulanka kumta cili tam ci.
ROM 1:22 Cii tu dor cero ti na nobo ki nyomka, dila ciin yilam kule tini.
ROM 1:23 Ciin fulongum duktonka Kwama nii diriye ki cer kanka dikero wo mani da diriye, na nii fir, bilibetinim, biyuwaro wo nako na'are kange wo kwob ti ki fwere.
ROM 1:24 Last nyo Kwama nekenci fiye dilanka, yeika nerek, cii ne bwiti dotange bwiti cii.
ROM 1:25 Ciin fulongum bilenke Kwama ki cwerke, take Ciin ma wabka kange bwanka dike wo fwelfwele, nyi Nii Fweli wo diker bilanka diri. A ti nyo.
ROM 1:26 Dor dikero wo, Kwama neken cii fite kayaka kange dotange, la natum ciyebo fulongum dam kurambo wo lerumme, la nwiye ki da kange nawiye
ROM 1:27 La nabarum ciyebo ken fulongum dam kurambo lerum nawiye kange bwayile, yilam bwayile kange bwayile cima kayaka ti. Wo co nabarubo dati kange nabarube cii ma nangen yeitumer ti, cii biye dike ci fiye ti.
ROM 1:28 Wori cii ciyabo kange Kwama mor yime ciye, Kwama neken cii fiye litanka nerek naci ma dikewo bwira bwira.
ROM 1:29 Cii diim ki bwini wucakke, Cil, nung-nung, biciren, kange kiye. Ciin nob koreb, twalkanka, bolkanka kange bwiran neret.
ROM 1:30 Ciin nob cuwarumeb, kange mwelka, nob kiyeb Kwama, wo kung kiyan tiye, nob kwici duwe, kange nob mwelka dikero bwir, nobo ko bwangka tebcibe.
ROM 1:31 Nobo man ki nyomka, cii kebo diker ciyaka, wo mani cwi bwiti, man ki cika bwine.
ROM 1:32 Ki nyoka cik dike Kwama ki nobo ma dikewo tiye ciin daten warke bwarek. Kebo ka maka dike wo, ciin ti bwaka bwiko nobo matiyeu.
ROM 2:1 Na weu mwi manki taka fiti mo nii fir, mo nii wo ma bolang tiye, dirkero mwi ma warke dor kangere, kuwa nen mwki bwimo. Wori mo nii bolangeu mo ma dii ke cuwo ti.
ROM 2:2 Dila bin nyumom bolang kwamako bilenke, an bou yaru dor nobo marang dike wo tiye.
ROM 2:3 Dila ti yora, mo nii, wo ma bolang ti dor nobo ma dike wo tiye bwenno mo ki mai ken duwaleu. Mo toti ri mwan kam funer Kwamara?
ROM 2:4 Kakaa mwiki cuwekang luma ceko, wo bou ki tibranka warke ce, kange birom ne ce? Mo nyombo mwiki luma neceu ki nung na ya kinnen yiloka ka?
ROM 2:5 Wori kwici ka duwe mweko kange ner mwero man ki yiloka mo ki tang dor mwero nin funer, bi diye funere, kakuk cerkangka bolang wucakke Kwama.
ROM 2:6 Can ya nobo dong dong dike nii mane.
ROM 2:7 ki nobo wuro ma nangen luma man ki kurongka, ciin fiya dor ciyero nin caklangka, bwayilen kange wucake, can ne ci dume diri.
ROM 2:8 Dila nobo cwi dor tiye, wuro ko ciyaka bilenke, ri la ciya kange bwini bilenkeu, funer kange kwenanka wo cilong cilonge an bo cii nen.
ROM 2:9 Kwama an yirau ki dikero bwir kange fir neret ki dume wo ma cile, ater ki Yahudawa ri nimde Helinawa.
ROM 2:10 Dila caklanka kange bwayilen, kange fuwor neret ciyan yi kange nobo gwam wo ma nangen do keneu, ater ki Yahudawa nimde Helinawa.
ROM 2:11 Wori Kwama kebo nii nanne.
ROM 2:12 Ki nobo gwam wo ma bwiranke kebo ki bolangeu, ciyan bwiya kebo ki bolang, ki nobo wuro ma bwiranke mor bolage a war cinen ki bolang
ROM 2:13 Di kebo nobo nuwa bolangti nobo wucak kabum Kwama me, dila nobo ma dikero bolanka tokke ti ciya kaaka tiye.
ROM 2:14 Dila no nobo kumtacili wo nyombo bolange, dila ciin ma dike dong dong daten bolange ce nur yime ce, ciin kwom bolangko dorcer, bwen duwal bolang man dor cireu.
ROM 2:15 Ki wo, ciin nungi dikero bolanko cwi tiyeu mulangum mulange mor nere ce. Diker mor nere ciye macinen warke ti, dume ne ceu ken neci warketi kange kwa nere ciyeko kua cii kaka tikang ci dor cero nin
ROM 2:16 kange Kwama nin. Wuro an bwi bidiye Kwama a ma bolang dike yurangum yurange wo nobo ce gwam, dor fulen keret Yecu Almasiya.
ROM 2:17 Bwen duwal mo co dor mweroti Bayahude la mo yim dor bolange mwi kwilangti ki ki Kwama,
ROM 2:18 ri mo nyumom dike co cwitiye, di mon ciya kange dike dong donge wori cin merang mwen mor bolange;
ROM 2:19 Bwen no mon ciya moki bwimwi mo nii tika kabak fugmanin ri, filang fiye nobo wo mor kumtacili,
ROM 2:20 wo ywel kule tini tiye, nii merangka bi beiyo bi duwatini, la kom wi ki nyomka kange wo bilenke ce mor bolange la wo ke yim kimem bo nyi?
ROM 2:21 Kom nobo merang kangembo nin tiyeu, kom merangbo dor kimero nina? kom wo kom ma bi weretti kom ki a kure kwiyeu, kom ku kui tiya?
ROM 2:22 Kom wo ko tokti kom ki kange a mare kayaka, kom ma kayatum tiya? Kom wo kom ko fulen neu, kom ku kui ti bikur wabe ra?
ROM 2:23 Kom nubo wo ma bilangtum ti kange kungka duwe ki bolangeu, kom ma Kwama nin bangtu ti ki bwini bwanka bolange ka?
ROM 2:24 La “den Kwama ro fiyabo neka durek nubo kumtacili nin ki ker kumer,” nawo kweri cii mulange.
ROM 2:25 Nyo biyeka te lareu wiki mwem fiye kom wiye tano kom bwangten bolangko ri, tano kom yilam nobo mani bwangten bolangko tiyeri, biyeka te lau yilam bwini biyeka te larek.
ROM 2:26 Tano, nii biye bo te la'u bwangten dikero bolangko cwitiye ri, ma ni ba tuu nii biyebo te la ce ti na nii wo biyem te la ka?
ROM 2:27 Nii wo biyebo te la ce bwiyeu, di bwangten bolangeu mani a dolti makimen bolang kom nobo biyem te la ra? Wori kom wiki bolangko mulangum mulangeu kange biyeka te la, di duwal kom bwangten bo bolangko!
ROM 2:28 Wori ci kebo Bayahudi kale; kaka nii biyem te laak wo diker bwiyereu.
ROM 2:29 Dila cin Bayahudi mor, nyo tak ri biyeka te laa ceko nawo mor nere, kange yuwa tangbe ri kebo bifumer. Nii wo caklanka ceko mania bou fiye nubo wiye, dila abou fiye Kwama wiye.
ROM 3:1 La fe lakankawo Bayahude cike? lan fe yokka biyeka te lareko?
ROM 3:2 Yora ceko wiki nure kila kila. Ki kaba, Ciin ne Yahudawa dukum fiye Kwama wiye.
ROM 3:3 La no kangem Yahudawa nebo blenker di? Bwini bilenke ciro, an kicim bilenker Kwama ro nangen na?
ROM 3:4 Mania yila ti nyo. La nyeu, Kwama a yila nii bilenker, bwenno nubbo gwam nob cwerkeb di. Nawo mulangumeu,”na nung mwen nawi yilam nii cak-cake mor kere mwe, la na ma turani no mwi bou fiye bolange ri.
ROM 3:5 Dila no bwini cak-cake beu an nung cak-cake Kwama ri, la ba tok biki ye? Ban toki biki Kwama man ki cak-cake wo ca bouti ki funer cero bine na? (miki manangen ki kwobkanka nii firek).
ROM 3:6 La ayilare nyo, la no nyori Kwama a ma dor bitinero nin olang nyi?
ROM 3:7 Tano bilenker Kwamar ki cwerke miko yok ten caklanka ce ducce ri, la ye bwi ba men bolangti duwal na bwiranke?
ROM 3:8 La ye bwi ma ko tok ti nawo tokan keti cwerketi dor nyere, nawo kangembo tuken nyon toki nyo,” la nyo ma dikero bwir na kendo na bou wa? Bolang ciyeko dong-dong.
ROM 3:9 Lan nye? ban kaa dor bero nin bati ka? ki bi duware ce. Wori kweri bo tom Yahudawa kange Helinawa gwam ce ki yimbo mor bwirang kere.
ROM 3:10 Nawo mulangeu nii cak-cake mani, mani wiin wo.
ROM 3:11 Kange nii yomka mani. Kange nii do Kwama tiye mani.
ROM 3:12 Ciin tiyangum nure gwam ciye. Gwam ciye ciin yilarangum cii man ki nangen, kange nii mani wo madike dong-dongeu, mani wiin wo.
ROM 3:13 Miya ciko na tuwe wumom wume, biyenti ceu ka biboler, mwan nyinonger nacuwek kino nyici.
ROM 3:14 Biyen ciro diim ki cwilka kange tweika.
ROM 3:15 Na ni ceu ki wulom fiye corka bwiyalek
ROM 3:16 Nure ceu dotange kange kayaka.
ROM 3:17 Nubo buro ynombo nur fuwor nerer.
ROM 3:18 Tai Kwama mani nuwe ciye.
ROM 3:19 La na weu ban nyumom dikero bolangka tokeu, bolangko ki tok ker kange nubo buro mor bolange keu.
ROM 3:20 Wori kange mania fiya cerka ti kabum cer ki nangen bolangek, nuwe ce. La mor bolangek, cin bou ki nyomka bwirangke.
ROM 3:21 Na weu kebo kange werfunr, cin nung nyomka cak-ake Kwama. Wuro werfunero kange nob dukumembo warker ti dorcereu.
ROM 3:22 Cak-cake Kwama fiye bilenker mor Yecu Almasiya ki nobo wo ne bilenke. Wori cwika dorek man.
ROM 3:23 Nobo gwam ma bwirangke la cii fwe ki fiye cak-cake Kwama wiye,
ROM 3:24 La ciin fiya cokka ki luma ca mor fanka ko wo Almasiya Yecu nine.
ROM 3:25 La Kwama neken Yecu Almasiya twika nuwange ko ficangeu ki bilenke mor bwiyale ce. Can neken Almasiya na nung cokka cek, wori ci ciyabo kange bwiranke be wo bwiyeu
ROM 3:26 mor birom nere ceu. Buro mani nyo nung cak-cake ceu, mor kale naweu. Naco nung dorcero cin warke, naco nungi co nii cerka nubeko ki bilenker mor Yecu.
ROM 3:27 Lan fe kungka doreko? cin cokum co. Ki ye bwiye? kin nangen ka? o-ong, la kan ker bilenkerer.
ROM 3:28 Lan co wo nyo takti nyoki nii fiya cerka mor bilenkerer kebo ki nangen werfuner.
ROM 3:29 Kaka Kwama ka Kwama Yahudawa ki kwa ciye ka? La ci kebo Kwama nubo kumtacili kena? ong, ki nubo kumta cili ken.
ROM 3:30 No bicom Kwama wiin di, can cer nii biyem te la-u ki bilenke kange wo biyebeu ki bilenker.
ROM 3:31 Bon fulongum werfundo ki bilenkerer ka? La amare nyo! La nyeu, bi tamki werfundo.
ROM 4:1 La ba tok boki ye wo Ibraim, te be mor tebwiye fiya?
ROM 4:2 No Ibraim fiya cerka fiye nangene ri ci kin fiyam ker kungka duwek, la kebo kabum Kwama.
ROM 4:3 La tak ye bifumro tok tiye? Ibraim ne bilenke Kwama nin, lan kiyeken cak-cake fiye ci wiye.
ROM 4:4 Na weu nii wo ma nangen tiyeu, cuner cero mani a kiyeti na luma fiye ci wiye, la dike na ce.
ROM 4:5 La co wo manki nangeneu, lan ne bilenker nii wo cer no bwiran ker tiyeu, bilen ker cero kiye ken na cak-cake cinen.
ROM 4:6 Dauda tok ker bibwiyer dor nii wo Kwama kiye nii cak-cakeu, ki bwini nangene.
ROM 4:7 La con toki, nob bibwiyereb nobo ci tab ciinen kero bwir ciyereu, buro bwirankereciyeu cumom-cumeu.
ROM 4:8 Nii bibwiyere wo kibi duware ce Kwwama mani a kiye cinenke ce tiyeu.
ROM 4:9 La bibwiyero tokeu ki no dor nubo biyem te la'u ki kwa ci, kaka kange cii nubo biyebo te lareu? Wori bon tok kero, “bilenker Ibraim me kiye cak-cake dor cer.”
ROM 4:10 La ci kiye co nyi? Ki bwiko Ibraim biyem tē lāre ce kaka co biyebo ka? Kebo mor biyeka, dila mor bwini biyeka te larek.
ROM 4:11 Ibraim yo yirom biye kam bo wuro co dokka kangek bilenkere co cike fiya ca biye beu. Co bibwiyer yiromero wo, dok co ca yilam tee nubo ne bilenkereu gwam. Bwen duwal ci biyebeu. Nyori dike nungeu a kiye cinen cak-cake.
ROM 4:12 Wori nungi con yilam tee nubo biyemeu buro kebo ka tē lā ceu biye meu dila kange nubo buro fuwaten naa ciyeti nur bilenker wo tee be Ibraim fuwau na nimre cii biyem tē lā ceu.
ROM 4:13 Wori noro ma Ibraim min kange naniya ceko, can yilam nii kwali dor bitinero boubo werfuneronin la bou cak-cake wo wo bilenkerer mineu.
ROM 4:14 Nā nubo burona werfundo ceu nob kwalib di, bilenker manki diker, la noro dubangum.
ROM 4:15 La werfunero ki bom nyo ki funer, la fiye ki bwini werfunere di fuwa ka nyalek man.
ROM 4:16 Lawo kin bilenker na noro yi dor lumar ri na bwangten naniyak Ibraimek gwam, kebo ka nubo bwangten werfun tiye, dila kange nubo buro yilam ki bilenke Ibraime. Cin Tee be gwam,
ROM 4:17 Kambo mulangum mulangeu, “min yonen na yilam tee bi tenni, kila kila”. Ibraim kino kabum nii co wo ci ciya cikeu, con Kwama, wo ne nubo bwiya meu dume tiyeu, na cwo diker maniyeu, na bou na no wi.
ROM 4:18 Wi yak kange dike bwiti bwiyeu, Ibraim ciya kange Kwama ki bi kwan neret dor kāba cek. La con yilam tee bi tenni kila-kilau kambo yim ceu,”Nyo naniyak mweko a yila tiye.”
ROM 4:19 Kebo ki yobka mor bilenker. Ibraim nyumom ki bwiceu dolbo bōka bwek (wori cor cero kiyang kwini kwob) kange ciraka fiye borek wice ko.
ROM 4:20 La ker nore Kwamaro, Ibaim tintang bo mor bwini neke bilenker, lanyeu, con ma bikwan mor bilenker la con ne Kwama duktangka.
ROM 4:21 Co diim ki ciyaka Kwama ma cinen nor, la can di cinen.
ROM 4:22 Lan kiye wo cak-cake cinen.
ROM 4:23 La kero wo kiye ci ne neu, mukang bo nace na dor ceroce ki kwāce.
ROM 4:24 La mulangum ki bo ken. ki nii wo a kiye cinen tiye, bo nobo ba ne bilenker ki nii wo kung Yecu Tee luwe beu bwareu.
ROM 4:25 Won co wuro ci neken co ker bwiran kerebe, lan kung co na fang bo.
ROM 5:1 Kambo ba fiya fanka fiye Kwama wiye ki bilenke, bon fiya luma kange Tee luwebe Yecu Almaciya.
ROM 5:2 Ci nen bō ken ban fiya doka ki bilenke mor luma Kwamako wo bo tiim dor cereu, la ma kwilangka bwiyek mor yoka nereko duktanka Kwamake.
ROM 5:3 Kebo ka wuro, dila bo ma kwilangka bwiyek ki nuwaka dotangek beko. Bo nyimom bo dotange beu atin dok bo birom nere,
ROM 5:4 Birom nere atin bouki mulendo ken, mulendo kendo an bou ki yoka nerek ki ikero a bouti fo kabeu,
ROM 5:5 La yoka nereko wuro mani a nebo kwenduwe ti, wori Kwama cor binen cwika ceko mor nerebe ki yuwa tangbe Kwamako wo ci ne beu.
ROM 5:6 La ki fiyacuwo bo kwambeu, ki kwama dong-dongeu Kiritti bwiyam ker nubo wo man ki Kwama.
ROM 5:7 La bwei na fiya nii wo a bwiyamti ker nii wo cak-cake, bwen duwaleu kangeri kange nii an cwi naci bwam ker nii kener.
ROM 5:8 Dila Kwama nung cwika ceko fiye bo wiye, wori fiyaco bon nob bwirankeu Kiritti bwiyam ker ber.
ROM 5:9 La na weu bo fiya cire duwece ki bwiyale ce, batin fiya cerka funer Kwama ro cinen.
ROM 5:10 Dila no fiya cwuo bin nob kiyebeu, ywellum tiber bero kange Kwama ki bwar bi bwe cero, la naweu bo fiyam ywelkangka tibere be kange ceu batin fiya cerka ki dume ceu.
ROM 5:11 Kebo kawo, la bon bilangi tak Kwama ker Teebe Yecu Kiritti, wo ker cer bo fiya ywel kangka tiberek beko weu.
ROM 5:12 La, kambo nii wiin nin bwirangke dou dor bitinere, nyo bwaro dou ker bwirang ke. La bwaro yalati nubo nin gwam wori gwam ma bwirangke.
ROM 5:13 La nyimde bolangko dou dor biner di, bwirangke wi dor bitiner dila kiyeka bwiran kere ko mani no bolangko mani ri.
ROM 5:14 Kange wo ri duwaleu, bwaro ma liyar, terti dor Adamu nimde Muca, la kange dor buro mabo bwiran ke yabka diir nyalek nawo Adamu ce wo yilam dangke ce nii wo a bou tiyeu.
ROM 5:15 Dila luma nereko kebo na bwirangke. La no ki bwirangkee nii wiin nubo kila bwiya rangum ri, luma Kwamak duce kange nekako Kwama nebeu ki luma nii wiin, Yecu kiritti, a cuwe ki nubo ducce.
ROM 5:16 La numa nere ko kebo na dikero bwiranke nii wiine bou cike. Bolang bwareko bwangu bwiranke nii wiine. Dila luma nerek Kwama ko bwangu bwirangke ducce dila bouki cērka.
ROM 5:17 La no ki bwirangke wo wiine bwaro ma liyar kange curo wiine ri, la ayila nyi kange buro yo luma ko ducce kange luma nerek cak-cake ma liyar mor dume kange cuwo wiineu, Yecu Kiritti.
ROM 5:18 La kambo bwirangke nii wiin bou ki bwar dor nubero gwameu, la nyo ken nangen cak-cake nii wiineu, bou ki cer ka kange dume wo nubo gwame ce.
ROM 5:19 La kambo dor bwirangke nii wiineu dok nubo kila yilarangum nob bwirangkebeu, nyo ken dor ki cak-cake nii wiine ri nubo ducce atin yilam cak-cak.
ROM 5:20 La bolangko bou ri na cob ten bwiranke. Dila fiye bwiranke ducce ri, luma Kwama kon duce laco.
ROM 5:21 Wo bwi nyori la kambo bwiranke ma liyar ti mor bware, la nyo luma an ma liyar dor cak-cake wo dume diri ye, mor Kiritti Teluwe be.
ROM 6:1 Ye bo tok ti na we? La ban ti maka bwiran kerekori na luma Kwama ko duwiya?
ROM 6:2 O-ong, mani a mati bo wo bi bwiyam ki maka bwirankeu, ba ma nyi nabi ti yimbo more ce?
ROM 6:3 La ko nyombo kom ki gwam wo yum mwem Kwamam mor Kiritti Yecu cin yum mwembo mor bware ca?
ROM 6:4 Ciin fwerum bo, fiya cuwo, kange co ki yuka mwengek Kwama ko mor bware. Wo bwi nyori, na yilam kambo Kiritti kwenum mor tuwe ki dume kiriti wiin ki duktanka Tee keu la boken bon yayam ki mor dume fwir
ROM 6:5 wori no bi yilam wiin kange co mor cerkanka bware ceko nin di, ba yilam kange co tak ki kwen ka ceko nin mor tuwe.
ROM 6:6 Bi nyimom bo ki nii be car ko cin kulken co ri naci twalum bwiyo wo na bwiranke ce. Wo bwi nyori nabi yila canga bwirankeb.
ROM 6:7 Nii wo bwiyameu cin yilam co nii cak-cake fiye bwiranke wiye.
ROM 6:8 Dila no bi bwiya kange Kiritti ri, bon ne bilenke yila ban yi wari kange co tak.
ROM 6:9 Bon nyimom boki, cin kungum Kiritti mor nubo bwiyarangume, dila naweu cin wiki dume. Bwaro mani ma liyar ti dor cer tak.
ROM 6:10 La ki bwaro coa bwiyam fiye bwiranke wiyeu, co bwa kiriti wiin dor nubo gwam. La yimbo co yimeu, co ki yi ker Kwama.
ROM 6:11 Nyori, Kom ke neu, tam kom tu dor kumero nubo bwiyam bwiya bwiranke nin, ri kom ki dume Kwama nin mor Kiritti Yecu.
ROM 6:12 La nyori, kom dobre bwiranke a ma liyar dor cūren bwiye kumero nin wo a dok kom neka dilanka ceko nin dur tiyeu.
ROM 6:13 Kom ne kende mwanti bwi kimero ki maka bwiranke, wo ci a yilam kwilen nangen ti wo maka dikero man cak-cake ce. Dila kom neken dor kumero Kwama nin na buro cii coku bwar di cii bou ki cii dumeu, nakom neken mwantini bwi komeu Kwama nin na kwilen nangener ro cak-cakeu.
ROM 6:14 Kom dob re bwiranke a maliyar dor kumer, wori bolanko mani dor kimer la luma Kwamak dor kumere.
ROM 6:15 Ye tak? Ban ma bwiranke wori bolanko mani dorber, di luma Kwamak dorbera? O-ong, mani a bwiti nyo.
ROM 6:16 Ko nyombo kom ki no kom neken dorkumero na cangab ri, kom cangab nii wo kom neco dur tiya? La kom cangab bwiranke wo ayati ki nii bware kaka cangab ki neka durek wo ayati ki nii cak-cake
ROM 6:17 Dila buka kangek Kwama nin! Wori no kom cangab bwirankeb, dila kom ne dur mor nere kume nur merankako cii nekome.
ROM 6:18 Kom fiya cerka mor bwiranke la kom yilam cangeb cak-cakeb.
ROM 6:19 Ma tok kero ti kange kom na nii wori, kom man kii kwan bwi kom. la nawo kom neken mwanti bwiyer kumero na cangab diker mani wucake, kange bwini bwanka bolangek kange maka dikero bwira bwira, nyo tak kom neken mwanti bwiyer komero na cangab dikero cak-cake wo nir kako wucake ce.
ROM 6:20 Fiyaco kom cangab bwirankeu, cin cer kom ki cak-cake.
ROM 6:21 Ki kwama cuwo, ye kom fiya ki nangen kuro wo na weu kom nuwa kwenduwe tiye? Wori dikero kom fiya ti nangendo cuwo nineu bwar
ROM 6:22 La na weu kom fiya cērka mor bwiranke ri la kom yilam canga Kwamak, kom wiki dikero kom fiya ki nir ka kumeko wucakeu. Diker kom fita tiye dume diriye.
ROM 6:23 Cuner bwiran kerero bwar, dila luma nerek Kwama ko dume diriye Kiritti Yecu Teluwe be.
ROM 7:1 Kaka ko nyombo ka, yitub mib (miki tok kange nobo wuro nyomom werfun deu) ki, werfun ca liyar ti dor nii, ya ciko dika dume cek.
ROM 7:2 Werfundo bwam nawiye nam nau bwece nin, no bwece ki dume ri, no bwece bwiyam ri, ciin cokum co bwaka werfuner na-ka ceko.
ROM 7:3 La no bwece wi ki dume ri, no co yi kange nii kange ri, a cuwo co ki, “nii burotum.” Dila no bwece bwiyam ri, ciin cokum co werfun do nin, la co kebo nawiye ma burotum tiye no co yim kange nii kangeri.
ROM 7:4 Nyori yitub mib, cin dok kom kin bwiyam mor werfune nin ken, dor bwiyer Kiritti. Nyori naci mwer kangum kom kange kange, nyori nii wo cii kungum mor nubo bwiya meu nin na kom bō Kwama nin bi bei.
ROM 7:5 No bi mor bwiye ri, dilanka bwiye beko wo werfundo kungu tiyeu, ma nangen ti ki mwantini bwiyer bero nin, na ci bō bwaro nin bi bei.
ROM 7:6 Dila naweu, cin cokum kom werfundo nin. Bon bwiyam dor dikero cuwo bwam be. Wuro nyo, nabi bwang cinen ten mor yuwa tangbeko fwir, kebo mor bwite carko.
ROM 7:7 Ye ba tok ti take? werfundo ki bwici bwiranke ka? A yilare nyo, miki nyom bo bwiranke, nō kebo dor werfuner ri, nō miki nyom bo nung-nung, na kebo wo werfundo ki,” mare nung-nunge di.”
ROM 7:8 Bwiranke fiya nure mor werfune nin, la co bou ki nung-nungo gwam minen. No werfundo mani ri, bwirang keu bwiyam.
ROM 7:9 Fiya co mi ki dume la bolang ko man, la werfundo bou ri, bwiran ke kwenu ken, la min bwiyam.
ROM 7:10 Werfundo wo no a bou ti ki dume, yilam bwar minen.
ROM 7:11 Wori bwiranke fiya nure ker werfune ro nin bolye. Fiye Werfundo nin twalum ye.
ROM 7:12 Nyori bolangko wucak, werfundo wucak, cak-cak ri, yora tak.
ROM 7:13 La dike yilam na keneu bwar mi nen ka? Mani a mati nyo. Dila bwiranke, na nungi cin bwiran ke ki dike yorau, bou ki bwar mi nen. Wuro na nungi ki ker werfuner, bwiranke yi lam bwirankere cum bi kwane.
ROM 7:14 La dike ban nyumom bo ki bolanko ki yuwa tangba, dila mi na bwiye ce. Cin miyem ye bwiranke nin.
ROM 7:15 La dike mi matiye, ma nyombo, dike mi cwiti na maneu, mi mabo, la dike ma cwibeu cwo mi matiye.
ROM 7:16 dila no min ma dike ma cwibo mane ri, min ciya kange werfundo, miki werfundo yori kabo.
ROM 7:17 La caneu, kebo mo matiye, bwiran kere yim minene.
ROM 7:18 Min nyimom minen, bwimi, dikero ken yibo mi ne minen. Ner maka dikero ken wi minen, la mani ma mati.
ROM 7:19 Ken ko micwitiyeu mani mi mati, dila bwirko ma cwibeu co mi matiye.
ROM 7:20 Nomin ma dike ma cwibe ri, yilam kebo mo ma matiye, la co bwiranke wo yim mi neneu.
ROM 7:21 La min fiya ciyakako minen wo ma cwitin ma dikero keneu, dila dikero bwir ko wi minen.
ROM 7:22 Min ma bilangtum mor werfun Kwama kange mor nere nii.
ROM 7:23 La min fiya mor mwanti bwiye mik. Ci ma kiyan ti kange ciyakako fwir ko mor nere miyeu. Tamye na canga ki werfun bwiranke wo mwanti bwiyer mireu.
ROM 7:24 Min nii dotange, we a cok yeti bwi bware we?
ROM 7:25 Mi bū kwama nin kange mor Yecu Kiritti, Tēluwe be, mo ki bwimi min bwangten werfun Kwama ki ner mir, la ki te bwiye ri mo ki bwangten werfun bwiran ke.
ROM 8:1 Nyori caneu kuwaka Mani nobody would more Kiritti Yecu.
ROM 8:2 wori werfun yuwa dumeko more Yecu neneu cērka dor werfuner bwiranke kange bwar.
ROM 8:3 Dike werfundo dolbo maka wori ci man kibi kwan mor bwiyeu, Kwama mani. Con tuwomou bi bwece mor cerkangka bwiran bwiyeko ki bwiranke na yilam twika kira bwiran keret la con twalum bwaro mor bwiye.
ROM 8:4 Ca mawo na dim dike werfundo tok ti more be wuro mani a yayam ti mor bwiteu, di yati mor yuwa nere keu.
ROM 8:5 Nubo wuro yim mor bwiyeu, yo ner ciro dor dikero na bwiye ceu, wuro ya yamti mor yuwa nere keu, yo ner ciro mor dikero na yuwa nereko ceu.
ROM 8:6 Nero wuro yom bwiyeu, bwar, la nero wuro yom yuwa nerekeu dume kange fwor nerek.
ROM 8:7 Nero yom bwiyeu ma kiyeti kwama nin, wori mani ne durti werfun Kwamar, mani mati tak.
ROM 8:8 Nubo wo mor bwiyeu, mani a yo Kwama nin ner ti.
ROM 8:9 Nyori, kom mani mor bwiye, kom no mor yuwa nerek, no kibi cuwom yuwa tangbe yim kimen di. La nii wo manki yuwa tangbe ko wo Kiritti ce ri, co man kange co.
ROM 8:10 No Kiritti yim kimen di, bwiyo bwiyam fiye bwiran keret dumeu. La yuwa Kwama ko mune neu, ki dume fiye bilen kerero wiye.
ROM 8:11 No yuwa Kwama ko wo kung Yecu bwareu yim munen di, co wo co kung Kiritti bwareu, an ne bwi bware kime dume fiye yuwa Kwama ko ni ne, wo yim mune neu.
ROM 8:12 Nyori kom yitub mib, boki cēn, kebo nawo bwii yeu na bo yati mor bwiye.
ROM 8:13 No yim mor bwiyeri, mon dadum na bwiyam, la no yim mor yuwa Kwama ri, mon twalum nangen bwiyero ri mwa bum.
ROM 8:14 Gwam wo yuwa tangbe Kwama bwangten ti ki ciyw ri, cii be bei Kwama.
ROM 8:15 Ko yuwo bo yuwa tangbe canga, wo ka yiti mor tāi take. Nyori, kom yo yuwa tangbe yila ka bi beiyek, wo ka cuwo ti,” Abba, Tēe!”
ROM 8:16 YUwa tangbeko ki bwici ne warke kange yuwa tangbe beko ki bon bi bei kwama.
ROM 8:17 No bo bi bei Kwama ri, bo nob Kwalib, nob kwalib Kwama. Takeu nob Kwalib kange Kiritti, no bo nuwa dotange kange co ri, ban fiya duktonka kange co.
ROM 8:18 Mi toti dotange wuro kale wo caneu, labo wo ba mwerkan coti kange dukton kako wo ca nung binen tiyeu.
ROM 8:19 Wori kuru yoka nerek fwelkau nintang nungka bibei Kwam ti.
ROM 8:20 Wori cin yoken fwelkako dikero bwir, kebo ki cwika cek, la na nii wo dokken co ce. Dila yo nere wi duwal.
ROM 8:21 La fwileu ki bwici ciya can cokumco canga na fwiyem, la ciyan bou ki co cēr duktongka bi bei Kwama.
ROM 8:22 La bon nyimom fwel kako gwam, ki tii nangi, ki dotange bore yau ciko duwen.
ROM 8:23 Kebo ka cuwo, bo ki bwibi yeu, wo ter fiya ka yuwa tangbe ki ƙa bau- la bo biki bwibo tii nangi binen, bo nintang yila ka yila bi bei ye koti, cērka bwiye beko.
ROM 8:24 Mor yo neri yo wo ba fiya fuloka. Dila yo neri ba to canneu kebo yo neri. We yo ner dike ca tobe?
ROM 8:25 No bo yoner dike bato bwiri ye ri, ban ningtangi ki birum neri.
ROM 8:26 Nyo tak, yuwa tangbe Kwama ko tikanbo ti mor yiber bwiyer ber, wo ba nyom bo kambo ba kwob dilo tiye, yuwa tangbe ko ki bwici, ken kini ti dor ber ki tinang kako man ki kiyeka.
ROM 8:27 Co wuro to nero tiyeu, nyimom kwaka nerek yuwa tangbe Kwama, wo ri ci ken kini dor bi bei Kwama ro wucakke mor cwika Kwamak.
ROM 8:28 Dila a nyimom nubo cwi kwama tiyeu, can ma cinen diker gwam wo yor-yore, ki buro ci cuwo ki cwika cekeu
ROM 8:29 Nyori wuro ci nyimom cii wulomeu, cin dok cii nacii tū cerkanka bi Bwe ce, na co yilam Bwe kāba mor keb ceb ducce.
ROM 8:30 Buro ci dokke, cii buro co coweu. Cii buro ca coweu, cii co cokke, nobo co cokke, cii co duktange.
ROM 8:31 Ye ba tokti tak dikero buro we? No Kwama kange bori, we a ma kiyeti kange be?
ROM 8:32 Co wo dobbo bi bwece neken co ker ber gwam, a manyi mani a cēr boti na nebo dikero gwam me?
ROM 8:33 We a bou ti kiyange dor nubo Kwama coke? Kwam co nii wo ma cokka tiye.
ROM 8:34 We wo war ker tiye? Kiritti co nii wo bwiya ker bere. La lanyo, cin kwenum. Co wuro kangko cattiyer Kwama ke, ci ken kiniti dor ber.
ROM 8:35 We a yalkang bo ti ki cwika Kiritti ye? Dotange, kaka kālaka kaka wura, kaka kwancer, kaka diker taiyer kaka ƙulen ka?
ROM 8:36 Nawo ci mulangeu, “Ker mwer cii twalang nyo kica tech. Cii tuken nyo na kwame biye ka.
ROM 8:37 mor dikero wo gwam nyin la nob turanii mor nii wo cwi bo tiye.
ROM 8:38 Nyori min ciya mor bware, kaka dume, kaka nob tomangeb Kwama wucake, kaka liyar, kaka dikero caneu, kaka dikero a bou tiyeu, kaka bikwan neret,
ROM 8:39 kaka cwemmer, kaka cuwaka, kaka dikero ci fwel-fweleu, mani ciya dolti ci tikangbo ki cwika Kwamak, wo Tē luwebe Kiritti Yecu ni neu.
ROM 9:1 Ma tok bilenke mor Kiritti. Ma cwerbo cwerke, dume ner miro ne warke dor miir mor yuwa tangbe ko wucakke,
ROM 9:2 La man wiki fir nerero dur kange buwarum ne wo man ki dika mor nere mi.
ROM 9:3 Man cwi na ci cilim ye ri ri naci tikangum ye kange Almaciya ker keb mib bo bwiyeu buro nyi ceru bitine wiineu.
ROM 9:4 Cii Icrailawa, ciin wi ki yilaka bi bei Kwamak, duktangka, nor tini, luma nere bolangek, wabka Kwamak, kange diker co ciya con macineneu.
ROM 9:5 Tenkwanibbo na ce wo Kiritti ceru wi ki te bwi yeu- Co wo cin Kwama dor dikero gwameu. Cak lanka nace diri. A ti nyo.
ROM 9:6 Dila kebo ki nor Kwama ro dii be. Kebo nubo gwam mor Icraila wo nii Icraila bilenke.
ROM 9:7 Kaka naniya Ibraime ko gwam bibeiyo loce ken. Dila “Na niya mweko a cuwo Icaku nen”
ROM 9:8 Bi beiyo tebwiye kebo bi bei Kwamab. Dila be bei nore bo cii ci tuu cii ti bi bei naniya ke.
ROM 9:9 Wo co noro: “ki kwama wo bilang matin bou, Caratu an bō bwe.”
ROM 9:10 Kebo ka wo, Rifkatu tū fwer kange nii kange wiin, tee be Icaku-
ROM 9:11 la cii bō bo bi beiyo bwiri takeu cii mabo dikero ken kaka dikero bwir, na cwika Kwama ko ki cokka ceko atin dim, kebo ker nangen tini dila ker ker cer wo cuwo bi cuworeu.
ROM 9:12 Cin yi co ki “Durko atin yila canga bi duwareu.”
ROM 9:13 Kin na wo cii mulangeu: “Yakubu ma cwi ye, la Icuwa ma kowe.”
ROM 9:14 Ye ba tok tiye? bwini cak-cake wi Kwama nina? Mani nyo.
ROM 9:15 Con yi Muca coki,”Man nung cii duwe ki nii wo ma nung ten cii duwe tiye, ta keu man nung bwinang ka ki nii wo ma nung ten bunang ka tiye.”
ROM 9:16 La kebo cwii ka niik kaka ker nii wo cwa cwake, dila ker Kwama, wo nung cii duwe.
ROM 9:17 La bifumero yi Fir'auna, “Wo co diker bwi ma kung neneu, nyori nami nung bi Kwan liyare miu monen, tak ri na dor bitinero gwam nuwa den miro.
ROM 9:18 La Kwama nung cii duwe dor nii co cwi ye, tak ri ciki dok bongtu ki nubo co cwiye.
ROM 9:19 Mon yiye moki,” Ye bwi cito bwirake ti duwale? We ma kwobkanka wi kange dike co cwi tiye?”
ROM 9:20 Nii fir, we mo mwa kwobkang ti kange Kwama? Dike ci mu-muweu atin yi nii wo muu ceu,”Ye bwi mwa muuye nya?”
ROM 9:21 La nii muu kubar tiyeu man ki bi kwan liyare dor kubaro ci lūweu naci muu tilar wo nangendo ken nece kange tilar nangener kangkang lo ki kubaro cuwo wiin ci lūwe ka?
ROM 9:22 Nye no Kwama, wo cwiti naci nung funer cer tak ri naci nung bikwan liyare ceu, mwirumom ki biirom nere ducce dukum funero cii yo na twalangka ko ce ri?
ROM 9:23 La nye, noci ma wuro nyo naci nung cuweka duktangka cek dor nubo co nungten ciire duwe, wo ki ƙaba ci ywel bwice duktangka?
ROM 9:24 La ta keno ci mam dike wuro ki bo ken, wo co cuwo takeu, kebo ka Yahudawa ki kwaci, dila more nubo kumta cile ken?
ROM 9:25 Kambo co toki tak mor Hosea: “Ma tin cuwo cii nubo lo mii, buro kebo nubo lo miyeu, kange nii co wo no kebo wo ma cwiyeu matin cuwo co nawiye ma cwitiye.
ROM 9:26 La an yilam, fiye ci yicii ki, “kom kebo nubo lo mi, 'wi ci a cuwo cii ki 'bi bei Kwama ki dume.'”
ROM 9:27 Icaya kung diir ker Icraila, “Bwenno kila ka bi bei Icraila kino na yabum mor caji duwaleu, Cwab ce a fiya fulo tiye,
ROM 9:28 Wori Teeluwe atin ma warke dor bitiner, gwam mani a tab bwi ti.”
ROM 9:29 Nawo Icaya toki ki kabau, “Na no Teeluwe nob kwene dob nyi nen bo naniyatini ri, nyoki yilam na Caduma, takeu nyoki yilam na Gwamrata.”
ROM 9:30 Ye ba tokti kake? Ri nubo kumtaciliu, buro no tibo doka cak-cakeu, fiyam cak-cake, cak-cake fiye bilenke.
ROM 9:31 Dila Icrailawa, buro ti doka werfun cak-cakeu, cii fiya bo.
ROM 9:32 Ye bwiye? Wori cii dobo ki bilenke, dila ki nangentini. Ciin kottangi ki ter kottangkar.
ROM 9:33 Na wo mulangum mulangeu, To, ma yo ter kottangkati kange cwela ko dok ȳare tiye Cihiyona. Nii wo ne bilenke dorcere ri, mania nuwa kwen duwe ti.
ROM 10:1 Keb mibbo, cwika nere miko kange kini mito Kwama nineu ki cii, ki fuloka ciyek.
ROM 10:2 Man ne warke dor ciyer miki ciin wiki ner bwanka Kwama, dila keo dor nyom ka.
ROM 10:3 Wori cii nyombo cak-cake Kwama, takeu cii do naci bouki cak-cake dor cero ceu. Ciin ko bwanka cak-cake Kwamau.
ROM 10:4 La Almaciya co diika werfunero ki cak-cake ker nubo gwam wo ne bilenke.
ROM 10:5 La Muca mulangi dor cak-cake wo bou fiye werfunereu: “Nii wo ma cak-cake werfuneu atin fiya dume ki cak-cake wo.”
ROM 10:6 Dila cak-cake wo bou fiye bilenke yiki, “Tok re mor nere mwe, 'We a kwiti dii kwama?' (la, na yirau ki Almaciya);
ROM 10:7 takeu tok re mwiki,' We a yira ti mor bitine?”' (na kungu Almaciya mor nubo bwiyam bwiya),
ROM 10:8 La ye ci tokke? “Kero kino bi dom kange mo, mor nyi mo, mor nere mwe.” Co ker bilenkero, wo nyo tokkeu.
ROM 10:9 No mwin tokki ki nyimo moki Yecu Teluwe, ri mwi ne bilenke mor nere mwe moki Kwama kungum co mor nubo bwiyam bwaya ri, mwan fiya fulo ka.
ROM 10:10 Wori nii ki ne bilenke ki ner na fiya cak-cake, takeu nyi ciki tok re naci fiya fuloka.
ROM 10:11 La bifumero tok ki,” Gwam nii wo ne bilenke ci ne ne ri kani a fiya kwen duwe ti.”
ROM 10:12 Wori nii Yahudiya man ki dimen kange nii kumtacili. Wori Kwama co Kwama nubo gwame, la ci cuwe kabo ki gwam nii wo cuwo ce nin.
ROM 10:13 Gwam nii wo cuwo den Teluwe ri an fiya fuloka.
ROM 10:14 La cii a cuwo nii wo cii nebo bilenke ci ne ne nyi? Cii a ne bilenke nyi dor nii wo cii nuwam bo kercer wiye? Cii a nuwa nyi no nii tok ka nani ri?
ROM 10:15 La cii a tok ker cer nyi no ci tuwom cii bo ri? - kambo ci mulangeu, “Yorka ki naa nube ko wo tok ker lumar ti wo dikero kendo ceu!”
ROM 10:16 Dila kebo gwam ciye ciya kange fulen kere. Icaya tokker, “Teluwe, we ciya kange ker nyere?”
ROM 10:17 Bileke ki bou nuwa ka, tak keu nuwa ki ker Almaciya.
ROM 10:18 La moki, “Cii nuwa bo ka? o-ng, ciin nuwam. “Dir ciyero yake dor bitiner gwam, tak keu ker ciyero yaken cwile dor bitiner.”
ROM 10:19 Takeu, moki, “Icraila nyom bo ka? “ki kaba Muca yiki,”Mon dok kom kor dor buro kebo biten nobeu. Ker bitinero man ki nyomka, matin dok kom funer.”
ROM 10:20 La Icaya wiki bikwan neret fiya cuwo ci tok ki, “Nubo doye beu fiyam ye. Man cerkangu ki nubo mebo nyom ka miko nin.”
ROM 10:21 La dor Icraila ciki, “man tar kang miko kume del nubo wo man ki neka dur tak keu bongi nyeu nin.”
ROM 11:1 La man toki, Kwam ko ko nubo loca? mani a mati nyo. Wori mõ keneu, man Ba-Icraile, naniyak Ibraimek tuwe luwe Bilyaminu.
ROM 11:2 Kwama kobo nubo lo ceu wo ki kaba ca nyimo meu. La kom nyombo dike bifumero toki dor Iliyare, kambo co yaki kiyane Icraila kabum Kwama meu.
ROM 11:3 “Teeluwe, cii twalangum nob dukumeb mwebo, ciin bubam fiye wabe meu, miki kwami ma kume, la cii do dumeti.
ROM 11:4 La Kwama kar cinen kiye? Min wiki nubo bi kate niber buro cung bo Ba'al nin cngeu.”
ROM 11:5 Kebo nyori na weu kum kangembo wi buro ma cokkeu ker cokka lumau.
ROM 11:6 La naki luma, kebo ki nangen tak, na kebo nyorri luma mani a yila luma ti tak.
ROM 11:7 Lan ye tak? Dike Icraila do tiyeu cii fiyabo, la nubo cok-cokeu ciin fiya co, tangnumbo kwamum ner cero.
ROM 11:8 La nawo mulangum mulangeu, Kwama neci yuwa tangbe bwini nyomka. nuwe tini wo la nacia tore fiye, tu'u niu wo la mani ci a nuwati, yau ciko diye wo.
ROM 11:9 Dauda ki, “Bntilen cero ayilam biliyar, kange ciito, ayilam ter kwaka nāak kange cokka cunek.
ROM 11:10 La nuwe ce a fikongum kume naci tore. tarye ceu a kuro kure diri.
ROM 11:11 La man toki, cii kottang kottang naci yari ka? Diker nawo a bwire. La nyeu, yila ka bwiye ko cii yilau, yila fulokako bou nubo kumtacili nin, na dok cii maka korek.
ROM 11:12 No yila ka bwiyeko cii yilam cweka dorbitiner di, la yare ciyeu cuweka nubo kumtaili yeu, la duwi ka ceko ba cuwa nyi, no ci bou takka ri?
ROM 11:13 Naweu maki tok kero kange kom nubo kumtaciliyeu, wori man nii tomange nubo kumtaciliyeu, maki maka bwik mor nangene miu.
ROM 11:14 Man mani kangeri an dok keb mibbo kor, na nyo cek kange.
ROM 11:15 No koka ciyeko bouki ywelkangka dor bitinero nin di, yoka ciyeko la a yila nyi, ayila dume fiye bwaro nine.
ROM 11:16 No bituttui wucak ri, nyo mimbo fuu ri kumeu, no nuti to wucak ri, nyo katini ceu ken.
ROM 11:17 La no kange kangni tiyeu kangembo kiya rangum di, na kom, ƙani jeitune ken di, wo ci bwabti more ciyeu, la kom ki kwali kange ci, mor ti jeitune co.
ROM 11:18 Kom mare bi tē nam dor kanitini nin. La no kom ma bitenam di, kebo kom ko ne niye bikwan tiye, la niye nekom bikwan tiye.
ROM 11:19 Mwan toki moki, “cin kim kangko nan bwab tiye mor.
ROM 11:20 Wuro bilenker, ki bwini bilenker ciyero cin kim cii wi kanko nin, la mo, tim ki bikwan mor bilen kerer kumebo nin, ko ture dor kumero na kange diker, la ko nuwa tai.
ROM 11:21 Lano Kwama dobbo kani kendo ri, mani a dobkom ti.
ROM 11:22 Ko to, nangen kange dotange Kwama wo ki dimeneu, ki kangko wineu tak, dotangeu ki bou dor Yahudawa buro yaru meu. La ki kangko wineu, cini Kwama bou monen, no ko ca kaba mor luma ce ri. La no mo kori, an tom nen.
ROM 11:23 La nyo, na cii yi bo mor bwini bilenker ciyero ri, a yila ken ki cii bwi tini. Wori Kwama an yila ken kici tak.
ROM 11:24 No cin mwatu nen jigindo wo kiye nin, ri cin mwer kang nen kange tii jigindo luwe ri, la a ma nyi na Yahudawa wo cii kani kwattiyeu, a yilauti ki cii tak mor tii jigin ciyere?
ROM 11:25 Keb mibbo, ma cwibo kom yi mor kumtacili, dor yur kero wuro, kati yilo ki yilam ki yulan mor nere kime. Yur kere wo co kwamka duwek ko kebo nawo diriyeu mani Icraila, nimde nubo kumtacili ou more ce.
ROM 11:26 Nyo Icraila gwam ciyan fiya fuloka, nawo mulangum mulangeu: “Mor ciyona nii cēr kako an ceru. Can an nyinangum bwini cak-cakeu Yakubu nin,
ROM 11:27 Wo an yilam nor mir kange cii kambo ma tum bwiran ker ciyereu.
ROM 11:28 Cunga ko kange, ker fulen kerero, cii nob kiyeb nyi kom. Ki cungako kange ki cok ka Kwamak, nubo ca cwi cwiye ker teb ciyeb.
ROM 11:29 Wori nēka Kwamak, kange bi cor Kwama, mani fulonger.
ROM 11:30 La kom ken no mani kom ne Kwama dur, la naweu, kom fiya cire duwe ker bwini neka durek ciyek.
ROM 11:31 Ki nure wo tak keu, Yahudawa buro mani ne dur. Ki cire duwe ci nung kumeneu, naweu nacii yo cire duwe ken.
ROM 11:32 Wori Kwama nungum nubo gwam mor bwini neka durek, na ci nung cire duwe dor nubo gwam.
ROM 11:33 Cuwaka cuweka yilen kange nyoka Kwama! Warka bolangek ceko cum bi kwan fuwaka, nure ce cum kabum nyomkam.
ROM 11:34 We nyumom dike co kwati nercere kaka we yilam nii kiye kerti kange ce?
ROM 11:35 Kaka we ter neka kwamak dike kange, wo tam nyo Kwama yāa co nan do ce?”
ROM 11:36 La fiye co wiye kange morce, dikero gwam ceruwe na yilaken cinen. Cinen duktangka diri. Ati nyo.
ROM 12:1 Mi ken kom yi kebmibbo, ki cire duwe Kwama, ko neken bwikimeu na twika nuwange dumek, wucak, diker ciyaka Kwama nin. Wuro co nangen kumero yoryore.
ROM 12:2 Kom bwangten de kale wuro, dila kom fulongum ki bwangka ner kume ro fwir ko. Ko mawuro na kom nyimom ye yora, diker yokar kange yoryore wo Kwama ciya cikeu.
ROM 12:3 Ki lima nereko wo ci neyereu, mi yi kom ti, kange a tūu re dor cero a cure bi kwan, nyori, bi kwarum nere kumeu a yilam ki yilen, dong-dong nawo Kwama ne bo bilenke ki dimeneu.
ROM 12:4 Bon wiki mwantini ducce mor bwiye wiin, la kebo mwantini ro gwam ma nangenti ka wangko ce.
ROM 12:5 Nyo takeu, bo wo bi kila nyeu bi bwiyo wiin mor Kiritti, la bon mwantini keb-bebeb ki winti-wintiye.
ROM 12:6 Boki nē kako ki dimen dong-dong kange lumako ci nebeu. No nēka niik ker dukumer ri, ca mani na dong-dong bilenke ci cikeu.
ROM 12:7 No nē ka niik na nangene ceri, ca mani. No na merang kako ceri, ca merangi.
ROM 12:8 No na bika nereko ce ri, ka ma birom neti. No na luma nereko ce ri, ca ne nero wiin. No na bwangka ka ce kange nob ri, mani ki ɓati, No na nungka bunangka ri, bunangi ki nero bilangtum.
ROM 12:9 Nyori cwi kako a yila re toka nuweko ce. Kom ko dikero yilam na bwireu, ko tam dikero yilam na keneu.
ROM 12:10 Dor cwika keb-bebeb, Ko cwi buti kime nure dateneu. Dor neka durek, ki ne buti kime dur.
ROM 12:11 Dor kor neret, ki mare bwi maka. Dor yuwa tangbe Kwama, ki yalam ki kuru. Dor Teluwe, kom bwangten co.
ROM 12:12 Ko bilangi mor yōneri ko cikeu, ko mwirumom mor dotange kime, kom ti kwobka dilo.
ROM 12:13 Kom tikan nob Kwama bo wuccake man ki dikereu. Kom do nure kila-kila wo ka yilam ti ki tikaliyeu.
ROM 12:14 Kom yo nubo nekom dotange tiye nin bibwiyer; kom ne bi bwiyer, kom cil de nii.
ROM 12:15 Bilangi kange nubo bilang tiyeu, ki ciwiye kange nubo ciwiye tiyeu.
ROM 12:16 Ki yilam ki nero wiin bwiti kimi. Ki yilare ki kunka duwe, nyori, kom yo nubo ki lomjome, Ko yila re ki yile mor kwa neri kume ni.
ROM 12:17 Ki yare cuner dikero bwir. Kom ma dikero ken nuwe nobe gwam.
ROM 12:18 No an mani ri, kom yi kwamer kange nubo gwam.
ROM 12:19 Ki ya re dor kimero nin cuner, dila ko dob funer Kwamaro nin. Wori mulangum-mulange, '“Cunero ki mo; Matin yām,' nuwa Teluwe.”
ROM 12:20 “La no nii kiye kime nuwa wura tiri, cam ki co. No ci nuwa dilo mwe tiri, neco mwem na nom. No kom ma wuro tiri, kan yo cinen kor kiret dorcir.”
ROM 12:21 Dikero bwir ko a la kom re, la ko la-m dikero bwirko ki dikero ken.
ROM 13:1 Be gwam kume kob ne nob liyare ki bi kwan kere be dur, wori bikwan kerebe kange mani no boubo Kwama nin ri. Nob bikwan kereb bo foweu, Kwama yo ciye.
ROM 13:2 Nyori nii wo kwobkangi kange nob bikwan kere ri, ci ma kwobkangka kange werfun Kwama; La nob kwob kangka kowo atin yo warke dorcir.
ROM 13:3 Nyori, nob liyarebbo kebo diker cwaka ki nubo ma dikero kentiye nin. La nubo ma dikero bwir tiyeu cwa citi. Mo cwiti na kom cware nii wo do liyare? Kom ma dikero yora, la mon nyo ciyaka ceko.
ROM 13:4 Wori cin canga Kwama fiye mo wiye ker bilenker. Dila no mo ma dike yorbe ri, cwa tai; Wori ci tābo kulen do kang cek koni. Wori cin canga Kwama, nii a yaa cuner ki funer dor nii wo ma dikero bwirreu.
ROM 13:5 Nyori tam ne dur, kebo ka ker funere, dila ker kwa neri kimeu.
ROM 13:6 Co dike bwi kom yā kyemer dore ti take. Wori nob bikwan kere bo cangab Kwama, cii ma nangen do wuro ti kang-kang
ROM 13:7 Kom yam nubo gwam nando cii bwag kimenten tiyeu: Kyemer doret ki nubo yo kyemer doret tiyeu, kyemer cokker ki nubo dateneu, tai ki nii wo daten taiyeu, ne dur ki nii wo daten neka dureke.
ROM 13:8 Dikero yilam nii kange ceu a yire dor mwer no cum cwika keb mwebe ri. Wori wo cwi nii bi dom kange ceri dim bolangko.
ROM 13:9 Werfundo ki: “Mare burotum, twal de nii, kure kui, mare cwilangka,” no werfundo kange wi tak ri, cin mwerken cii mor kero wo; “Cwi nii bi dom kange mweu na dor mwer.
ROM 13:10 Cwika mani a nuwa nii bidome nin ti, nyori cwikako co diika bolangeko.
ROM 13:11 Nyori, kom nyumom kange kene ko, kang kenko daten ko ywiram ti dumeu kiyang dim. Wori naweu fuloka kimeko mani bidom lāwo no kom ne bilenke ki ƙabau
ROM 13:12 Kumeu kwitangi, ls finiu dadum celka. Nyori bo dubom nangen kumtacili ro, la bi dum kwilen kwener filangero.
ROM 13:13 Bo ya yambo daten neu, namwi ki kakuk, kebo mor bilengtum bo bwir kaka mor norangka dikek; Bo yare yam mor burotum kaka mor cwilanka, bo yare mor kiye kange kwobkangka.
ROM 13:14 La kom yilam ki mulen Teluwe Yecu Kiritti, takeu kom yore mulen te bwiyer, kari ko bwangten mulem cero ti.
ROM 14:1 Kom yo nubo wo kwambo mor bilenkeu, kom mare kwarke dor kwob kangka.
ROM 14:2 Kange wiki bilenke co cam bwenno nyeri, la kange wo bilenke ceu kwambeu ki ca ce ka lalutini.
ROM 14:3 Nii wo ca rang dike gwam a kore wo mani careu; La nii wo mani carang dike gwameu a mare warke dor nii wo ro carangti gwameu. Wori Kwama ciya kange co.
ROM 14:4 Mon we, mo wo mo ma warke ti dor canga nii kangere? Tika ceko kange yàre ceu kino ka bum tēluwe ce. Dila atin dok c o naco tim, wori Tēluwe lam a tim ki co.
ROM 14:5 Kange nii duktang kakuko kange la tangnumbo. Kange ce tú kumeni gwam dong-dong. La nii a yi mor ciyaka nere ce.
ROM 14:6 Wo tū kakuko kange wucake, co tūm ki Teluwe, wo caa bicar tiyeu, ciki caa ker Teluwe, wori cin ne buka kange Kwama nin. Wo caa be ri, co dob cakako ker Teluwe, cin ne buka kange ken Kwama nin.
ROM 14:7 Wori nii kange mani wo yi yim dore ce tiye, takke, kange mani bwiya bwar ker dore ce.
ROM 14:8 No bo yim ki dume ri, bo ki yi ker Teluwer, bwenno bin bwiyam ri, bo bwiya bwar ker Kwamak. La bwenno boki dume kaka bon bwiyam ri, bona Kwama ce.
ROM 14:9 Wo co dike bwi Almaciya bwiya. takeu, kenum ki dumetak, na co yilam Teluwe dur wo nubo bwiyam me ce kange nubo wo ki dume.
ROM 14:10 La mo, ye bwi ko ma kebmwemo bo nin bolang tiye? mo keneu, ye bwi mo cwekang kemwe tiye? La gwabe be ban ti kabum kutile bolange Kwama.
ROM 14:11 Wori mulangum mulange, “Min werum,” nuwa Teluwe,”duwendo gwam atin cunge men, takeu, biyen do wiyak atin ne Kwama caklangka.”
ROM 14:12 Wori, gwam be bon tok dike ba maneu Kwama nin.
ROM 14:13 Nyori, bi dumen to ka bwiranke keb-bebbo, dila kom ma wuro, kange be ayila re kece nin diker kottanka kaka yila kece nin cito yare.
ROM 14:14 Min nyimom, min ciya cuko tak Teluwe Yecu nin, dike kanke man wo kebo wucak ki bwico. La nii wo tūken dike kange ner cer ki mani wucak di, cinen dike cuwo mani wucak.
ROM 14:15 Tano ker carit kemwe nuwa nin luma ri, mani kom ya yamti mor cwi kanka bwiti tak. Kom twalde keb kimebo wo Almaci bwiya ker ciyereu ker bicaret.
ROM 14:16 Nyori dob re dike mwa to tiri na keneu ayilam diker bitoret kangem bo nin.
ROM 14:17 Wori liyar Kwama ro kebo dor carit kange diker nōkar, dila cak-cake, kange, dam nerem, kange fwor neret mor Yuwa tangbe ko wucakke.
ROM 14:18 Nii wo bwanten Kwama ki nure weri, diker yokar Kwama nin takeu, nubo ciya cuko.
ROM 14:19 Nyori, bo bwangten diketini a bouti ki dam neremeu, kange wuro a bouti ki mūka bwiti be keu.
ROM 14:20 Kom kangum de nangen Kwama ro ki ker carit. Dikero gwam wucak, dila an yilam dikero bwir no nii an ca câri to a dok co yāre tiye ri.
ROM 14:21 Yori kabo wore nange kaka mwem inabim, kaka mare dike kange wo a dok kemwe ti mani a nuwa luma tiyeu.
ROM 14:22 Bilenke wo mo cikeu, tam co tiber mwer kange Kwama. Bi bwiyer ki nii wo ner cero kuwa cobo ki dikero co ciya cike.
ROM 14:23 Nii wo ner cero yob-yob dor diker di ca'u, ma bwiranke. Wori kebo ki bilenke ci cā. La dike kebo bilenke ceu bwiranke.
ROM 15:1 Naweu bo biki bikwaneu daten bi cii bwini kebbebo buro kwam beu, yorbo bi nung cwika durek.
ROM 15:2 Bi fuwo nubo bi dom kange be nin ner ki dikero ken, na mum co.
ROM 15:3 Wori Almaciya ki bwico cwibo dorcer. Nawo ci mulangeu,” Bitor nubero tō neneu yilau dormiir.”
ROM 15:4 Wori dike kweri cii mulangi ki kābau ci mulangi naci kwob tūbe, mor birom nere kange dangne wo bifumero nebo tiyeu bon yilam ki bikwan.
ROM 15:5 Naweu, Kwama wo ki birom nere, kange dangneu a nekom nero wiin wo yimbo wariye ce kange keb kimebo kam Kiritti Yecu.
ROM 15:6 Ca ma wuro ri nakom caklange Kwama kange Tee Teluwebe Yecu Kiritti ki nero wiin.
ROM 15:7 Nyori kom yo bwiti kime, nawo Kiritti yo kom neke, ki caklangka Kwamak.
ROM 15:8 Wori man yi miki Kiritti yilam canga biyeka tê larek nyi bilenke Kwama, co mawuro na dim noro ci ne teb-be
ROM 15:9 kange nubo kumtacili naci duktang Kwama ker cire duwe ceu. Kino nawo mulangum-mulangeu, “Naweu matin ne nen caklangka mor nubo yim kumtacile takeu man ƙa nuwe caklangka den mwerek.
ROM 15:10 Cin toki tak, “Kom ma fuwor nerer kom nubo kumtacile gwam, kange nubo loce.”
ROM 15:11 La tak ri, “Caklang Kwama, kom nubo kumtacile gwam; nubo gwam a caklang co.”
ROM 15:12 Takkeu, Icaiah yiki, “Nii kwali Yesse atin cerkangu, kange wuro a kwenti na ma liyar dor nubo kumtacile. Nubo kumtaciliu an fiya bi kwan nerer ci nen.”
ROM 15:13 Naweu Kwama nii ne bikwan nerer tiyeu a dim kom ki fuwor nerer ducce, kange dam nerem, di na bikwan nerero dim kom fiye bikwan yuwa tangbe ko wucakke.
ROM 15:14 Mo miki bwimi mon ciya kange kom, keb mibbo. Min ciya miki kom kom ki bwikom ko dim ki luma nerek ken, ko dim ki nyomka gwam. Min ciya miki kom lam kom ma bwiti kime nin bimwerum.
ROM 15:15 Dila ma mulang kimen ti kibi kwan neret dor dikero kangem nami kulom kimen tak, ker luma ko wo Kwama neye reu.
ROM 15:16 Luma nereko wo ci neyeri nami yilam canga Kiritti Yecu twòmi mor nubo kumtacile. Nami neci fulen ker Kwama ro na nii wābe. Nami ma wuro di na neka nubo kumtaciliko fiya yoka, wucak Yuwa tangbeko wucakke nin.
ROM 15:17 Luma miko kino Kiritti Yecu nin kange dor dike yilam Kwama ceu.
ROM 15:18 Wori mani ma tok dike kangeti no kebo dike Kiritti māni kang mik ki neka durêk nubo kumtacile ri. Buro co diketini cii maneki ker kange makakeu,
ROM 15:19 Ki bi Kwan yiromer kange diker nyimangkar, kange bi kwan Yuwa tangbeko wucakke. Wo yilam nyo tabti Urucalima, yaken cungako Ilirikum, mon ma nangen fulen keret Kiritti.
ROM 15:20 Ki nure wo, dike ma tu mor nere miyeu tokka fulen kerer, dila kebo fiye cii nyimom Kiritti ki deneu, kari yilo ter muuka fiye kange nii yom kwareu.
ROM 15:21 Kino nawo mulangum-mulangeu: “Buro ci yim cibo fulen kerer cero wiyeu an to co, kange buro nuwa beu, atin nyimom.”
ROM 15:22 La ciin yamye bou kako kimeneu kiriti kila-kila.
ROM 15:23 La naweu, mi man ki fiye kange yāre buro nin, mor cotito ducce mi cwiti nami bou kimen.
ROM 15:24 Mayo ner toka kimek ti, bwen fiya ma cuti nami ya Acbaniya ri na kom yo ye nure, bwiko ma nuwa luma yimeko kange kom bi duwareu.
ROM 15:25 La naweu yam mi Urucalima nami ma nob bilenkere bo nin nangen.
ROM 15:26 Wori lumang ner nubo Makidoniya kange buro Akaya, naci mwerkang diker tikalir na ne nob fuwabbo more nubo ne bilenke Urucalimau.
ROM 15:27 Ōng, luma nere ciyek, takkeu, kibi com, ciiki no na nod ceneb ciyeb. Wori no nubo kumtaciliu ma wer kanka mor diker yuwa tangbe ciyeko nin di, dāten ciken ciya tikang cii ki kwilen titi keen.
ROM 15:28 No ndim nangendo wo ri, takkeu, no cii yom kwilendo nubo mwerange ri, man cu Acbaniya nami yarum kom nure.
ROM 15:29 Min nyimom ki kwama wo ma bou ti kimeneu, man bou mor diika bi bwiyer Kiritti.
ROM 15:30 Naweu, mi ken kom ti, Kebmibbo, ker Teluwe be Yecu Kiritti, kange cwika ko tangbeko ki nereu, kom tii kange mo mor dilo kime Kwama nin dor mir.
ROM 15:31 Kom kwob dilo nami fiya cerka kang nubo buro ma kiye ti kange bilenke mor Yahudiyau, tak ri na nangen miro dor Urucalima fiya yoka nubo ne bilenke nin.
ROM 15:32 Kom kwob dilo nami fiya bo ka kimen mor fuwor nerer ki ciyaka Kwamak, takkeu namo, kange kom fiya fobka.
ROM 15:33 Kwama nii wo ne luma nerk tiyeu ayi wari kange kom gwam.
ROM 16:1 Min caklang Fibi korya nye kimen, cin canga bikur wābero mor Kankiriya,
ROM 16:2 na kom yo co mor Kwama. Kom ma wuro ki nure daten wo nob neka bilenkere ce, kom ti kange co, mor dikero ca do kom tiye nin. Wori co ciki bwici yilam nii tikali nube ducce, ki mo ce ken.
ROM 16:3 Kom yarum Bilki kange Akila, nob nangeneb kange mo mor Kiritti Yecu.
ROM 16:4 Buro neken dume ce ker dume mireu. Ma bucinen kang ti, dila kebo ka mo, la kange mwer kangka nob Kwama ko wo nubo kumtacili ceu.
ROM 16:5 Ko yarum nob Kwama bo wo lociyeu. Yarum Abainitas nii mi cwi tiyeu, wuro yilam co nii ter neka bilenke Kiritti nin Asiya.
ROM 16:6 Ko yarum Maryamu, wo manangen kibi kwan ker kimereu.
ROM 16:7 Kom yarum Andranikus, kange Yuniyas, kebmibbo, kange farum fucina mik. Ciin nubo ko nyumangum cii nyumange mor nob tomangeb, buro nyimangum ten Kiritti mineneu.
ROM 16:8 Ko yarum Amfiliyas, wo ma cwi mor Teluwe.
ROM 16:9 Ko yarum Urbanas, far nangene mi mor Kiritti, kange Istakis, nii ma cwiyeu.
ROM 16:10 Ko yarum ten Abalis, nii ken mor Kiritti. Ko yaru buro mor luwe Aristobulus ce.
ROM 16:11 Ko yarum Hirudiyan, kemi. Ko yarum nubo lo Narkiss, buro Teluwe nine.
ROM 16:12 Ko yarum Tarafina kange Tarafusa, buro manangen kibi kwan neret Kwama nineu. Ko yarum Barsisa nawiye ken, wo manangen do ducce Kwama nine.
ROM 16:13 Ko yarum Rufus, wuro Kwama cokkeu, kange nee ce kange wo miu.
ROM 16:14 Ko yarum Asinkiritas, Filiguna, Hamisa, Baturabas, Hamas, kange keb-bebbo buro kange ciyeu.
ROM 16:15 Ko yarum, Filulugusa, kange Yuliya, Niriyas kange korya ceu, kange Ulumfas, kange nob Kwama buro wari kange ciyeu.
ROM 16:16 Ko yarum bwiti kimeu ki kor-kang kako wucakke. Mwer kangka nob Kwama ko gwam yarum kom ti.
ROM 16:17 Naweu mi ken komti, keb-mibbo, na kom kwa nubo buro bouti ki yalkangka kange kottangkau ki ner. Cii tou dikero cum bikwan dike kom merange ti. Kom yila bwim cinen.
ROM 16:18 Wori wang nobeko buro mani cii bwang ten Teluwe be Yeecu Kiritti ti, la mor fwiye ciye. Ki luma nyiye ceko cii bolang nubo ki lom jome duwe ti.
ROM 16:19 Wori dangke neka dure kimeko lam fiye gwam. Min ma bilangtum, dor kimer, dila ma cwiti na kom yilam ki yilen dor dikero yilam na kenneu, kange wucakke ki dikero yilam na bwireu.
ROM 16:20 Kwama wo ne fuwor nerer tiyeu an dok kom nako fuwarangum bwekel-keleu wulom mor na kimek. Luma Teluwe be Yecu Kiritti ati kange kom.
ROM 16:21 Timoti, far nangene mi, yarum kom ti, kange Lukiyas, kange Yason, kange Susibataras, keb mibbo.
ROM 16:22 Mo Tartiyas nii wo mulang bifumero weu, ma yarum kom ti Kwama nin.
ROM 16:23 Gayus nii ciyerka miik kange nob Kwama bo gwam, yarum kom ti. Arastas wo co tinger yoka cinan loro ceu, yarum komti kange ke nye Kawartas, cii yarum kom ti.
ROM 16:24 Luma Teluwe be Yecu Kiritti ati kange kom gwam. Ati nyo.
ROM 16:25 Naweu duktangka nace wo lami na dok kom tim nawo fulen kere miro kange fulen ker Yecu Kiritti, Wo ker nung ka dukumeko wo no kwitangi yurangum-yurangeu,
ROM 16:26 Dila naweu cin wumom, ki mulangka nob tomangeb dukume ko cin yi ber biten tini gwam, ki tokka Kwama diriyeu, ker bwangka bilenker.
ROM 16:27 Ki Kwama wiin cwar ki yileneu, fiye Yecu Kiritti wiye, duktangka bak-ni-bak. Ati nyo.
1CO 1:1 Bulus Kwama cho che na ci yilam bwetomange ki chiyaka kwama kange yibe Sosthenes.
1CO 1:2 Fiye nob bwangka kwamako wiye mor Korontiya buro fiya chobka Kiristi Yesu ninneu kange burombo bi cho ki nubo wuchak gwam kange burombo fiye tinin wo chi choti ki den Kiristi Yesu wo yilam Teluwe che kange bou.
1CO 1:3 Nyo fwor nenert kange luma nakume fiye kwama tebe kange tehluwebe Yesu Kiristi.
1CO 1:4 Kang kang mi ne kwama buka kangeti dor kumer kange luma wo Kiristi Yesu ne kommeu.
1CO 1:5 Chon dokkom, kom yilam nub chweka mor fiye gwam, kange mor kere kange nyomanka diker gwam.
1CO 1:6 nyo nawo tokki dur Kiristi yilam ki bichom bilenkeh more kume.
1CO 1:7 Tano nyori buni neka yuwa tangbeko wuchak kumeneu, kwakkombo nawo kom chen yilaka tehbe Yesu almasiyatie.
1CO 1:8 La nyori cham chukkom na kom ne bilenke yila na kom tim ki dika kale. Na kom yilam nubo man ki di tor bini cheu ki kakuk bouka tebe Yesu
1CO 1:9 Kwama nii bilenke, wo cho kom mwor mwarkakka bi bweche Yesu Kiristi Teluwe be.
1CO 1:10 Naweu mi kenkomti kebmi mwor den Yesu Kiristi wo gwam kume kom chiya chikeu nyo yaklangka dure a fiyare kumen min kenkomti kom mwer dur kume dume ner kumero a yilam win. ki dikero kom kwatiye. lo kulowi bou ki ker kume ki yalkangka dure wi mure kume.
1CO 1:12 Miki yi kange kume yiti ki mi na Bulus cheche kange ki mina Afolos che che, kange ken ki mina Kefas che che kakka mina Alamsiya che.
1CO 1:13 Almasiya yalkang nyika? chin kul Bulus ker kumerka? kakka chi yu kumen mwembo ki den Bulus che ka?
1CO 1:14 Min bukang kwama ma yubo kange kumenin mwem la Istifanus kange Gayus.
1CO 1:15 Mi ma wo Katti kange yiki chi yu chinen mwembo mwor den mir.
1CO 1:16 Min yu mwor luwe Istifanus chenin mwem kebo nyori ma nyombo keno min yu kange nin mwem di.
1CO 1:17 Nyo Almasiya tomyebo nan yu kumen mwem dila nan yi kom fulen keret be tomyebo na tok fulen kere ki nyomka bi bwe nifirek. La nyori katti kulka Almasiyako le liyar Bikwaner chero.
1CO 1:18 Dila nyori fulen kulka bwatiyeko kulum fiye nubo bwiyarangum me. La mwor brombo kwama cherchiye bikwan kwamar.
1CO 1:19 Nyo mulangum -mulange matan chitang nyomka nob nyomkawi man wom nyomka chiko, chi nob nyomkabo.
1CO 1:20 Ni Nyomka ki nofe? ni merangka ki nofe? ni bokake ki nofe? wo kale wo ninen. Kwama yilabo nyomka kalekowo na yilare kulendo che.
1CO 1:21 No nyori kalewo mwor nyomka cheko nyombo kwama. La cho nyom kwama fiye kulen keret na cher nubo ne bilenkereu.
1CO 1:22 Nyori Yahudawa ki do diker nyimangka Helenawa ki do diker nyomka.
1CO 1:23 La nyori nyo ki tok fulen keret Almasiya wo chi kulken bwatiye bware. Ter kottangka fiye Yahudawa wiye lan kulen fiye Helenawawiye.
1CO 1:24 La brombo kwama chowe yahudawa kange helenawa nyo ki tok ker almasiya ki bi kwan nyomka kwama.
1CO 1:25 Kulen kwama ro la nyomka bibwe nifire kange buni bikwan kwamar la nifir ki bi kwan.
1CO 1:26 Kom to Bichor kumero kebmibo, ke bo gwam kume ki nyomka mor nube, ke gwam kume wi ki bikwan liyare, kebo gwam kume chi bou na cha liyare.
1CO 1:27 La nyo kwama chok dike yorbe fou kalewo, na ne nob nyomka kwenduwe kwama chok dike wo man ki kwanne fou kaleweu.
1CO 1:28 Kwama chok dike bwiranye kange chinekangume fou kale wo chok dike chi tu kebo dikereu na cho chwikangum dike chiyi na kenne.
1CO 1:29 Cho maworo katti kange fiya kung dur chero kabum chem.
1CO 1:30 La diker kwama ma nawonnyeu koom ki no mor almasiya Yesu wo yilam benen nyomka fiye kwama wiyeu.
1CO 1:31 Yilam nawo bifumero tokke, di nuwo chuk dor chertiye cha chuk dor chero mor Teh be
1CO 2:1 Ki kwama ma bou kumeneu kebmibo ma bouki nyomka ker kakka yulan nyomka nawo ma fwetangum dike yurangum dor kwamare. Nawo ma tok ker do kwamareu.
1CO 2:2 Dike bwiyeu min tum fou ner mir na nyomre diker ki kwama Yesu Almasiya wo chi kuli dor bwatiye bwareu.
1CO 2:3 Mi wari kange kom mor kambo tai kange yarka ne duche.
1CO 2:4 Dila tomangemi kange ker miro chi mani wari kange ker nyomkaro wo tu dume ter tiyeu. tano nyori, chin bouki fwetangka yuwa tangbeko kange bikwan liyaret.
1CO 2:5 Tano nyori bilenker kume ayilam de yulan nyomaka nubek la mor bikwan liyare kwama.
1CO 2:6 Nawo nyeu bou kin tokker nyomka yulaner fiye nubo tim yora, la kebo nyomka yulane kalewo kakka kebo nub liyar kalewo brombo chuken tiye.
1CO 2:7 No nyori bou ki tok nyomka kwama mor bilenker wo yurangum mani ki duktangka kallowe.
1CO 2:8 Kange nii liyar mani wo kallowo nyimom nyomka yulanero wo, na ki chin nyimom ki kwama chori no chi kulbo tehluwe duktangka.
1CO 2:9 na wuro mulangum diker kange mani wu nuwe to weh tuwo kange nuwa bo, nero kange mani kwabe dike wuro kwama ywel nubo wuro chwi cho tiye.
1CO 2:10 wuro cho dike yuwatangbe kwama fwetang nubo chwi cho tiye. La yuwatangbeko fiu diker gwam wo chuwa kwama maneh.
1CO 2:11 La we nyiwo kwaka bibwe nifire? lan cho yuwatangbeko yim mor dume nere che? Lan yuwatangbe kwama.
1CO 2:12 Nyor yobo yuwa tangbe kale, Lan yuwa tangbe ko bou fiye kwama wiye la na bi nyimom dikero nebo koniyeu.
1CO 2:13 Nyo ki tok ker dor diker yulando wo nifir mani a nyom tiye, Lan cho dike wo yuwa tangbeko merang nyineneu. kange yulan nyomka cheko.
1CO 2:14 Nii wo mani ki nyomka bifumer kwamake mani nyom dike wuro kebo yuwatangbek kwamake. Dila yilam kulen chinen mani cha nyom chiti dike bwiyeu yuwa tang be kwama a fwetang tiye.
1CO 2:15 Cho nii wo ki nyomka kwamake cho kinwar bolang dor diker gwam. Lan cho mani mor bolang tangnum nubem.
1CO 2:16 We nyimom mor nere teh re. La cha ma Liyar dor chere? La nye nyon wiki ner nawo Almasiya che.
1CO 3:1 Kebmibo ma nyombo tonka ke na nubo wo ki ker kwamare. Dila na nubo wo nyombo kere na bi bai yo fiyer mor almasiya.
1CO 3:2 Ma nekom mwem yirem kebo nage dila kom labo woka nage nawo kom labe.
1CO 3:3 Na wo nyo kom nobbwiyeb ta no kurom kange komkangkang tiber kumer no nyori kom kebo nobbwireb chano kom yaken tii dor chuka no bek.
1CO 3:4 no chano kange yiki mi no bwokob Bulus mi ki no bwikob Afolos chano nyori keb yim nii firem kom yitiyeka.
1CO 3:5 La we Afolos kaka we Bulus chi changa wo kom ne bilenke fiye chinen. Gwamchiye kwama nechi nagen ne.
1CO 3:6 Miu fiye. Afolos ne mwem kwama tiki dwiyom me.
1CO 3:7 La kange nii fiye kange nii neka mwemek kebo diker. La gwam dike dwiyom me.
1CO 3:8 kange nii fiye kwnag nii neka mwemek gwam chi win. Gwam chiye yo luma nagen da cho mane.
1CO 3:9 Yori bou farum nangen kwama kom take kwama muka kwama tok.
1CO 3:10 La luma neneng kwama neye liyar nii yomka muka ma kwar kange nii yoti muka wi la yori ki win ti winti nubo chi ya bii kambo yo mukakko.
1CO 3:11 kange man wou a kul kwarti ki dime ne kange wo kwari kulum me la yeesu almasiya.
1CO 3:12 nawe nyo kange kunti muka kwar do yori kakka ter waki wakerer kakka tero yori nye kakka bwatiye kakka yerang ka.
1CO 3:13 nagen chero yilam yanglang ki kakuko cho anto wom chi ata nung cho mor kira ko ata nang yorka nagenek chin ki dimen ki dimen mane.
1CO 3:14 no wo nagen chero timfrinati yo luma nagen chero.
1CO 3:15 Chano gwam yo nagen mwero twimo mwan lem luma la cho ki bwichi chan fiya chera dila tamwi tiber kerek.
1CO 3:16 La kom nyombo kom ku'u kwama ka yuwa tangbe yim more kima ka?
1CO 3:17 No kange kangum ku'u kwama, kwama ati kangum cho di louh kwama fiye wuchake kom ko nyo ken.
1CO 3:18 Be kange a bo de dor cher chano kange more kume chon nii nyomka yulanne ko wo kaldowo la cho yilam kule, wori chon yilam nii nyomka yulannek.
1CO 3:19 La yomka yualannek kale ko wo kulen fiye kwama wiye wori mulangum mulange nyo. Cho ki taa nob yomka yulannek mor kulenke chiye.
1CO 3:20 Nyo kwama nyumom yulan maka kulenek ko.
1CO 3:21 Nyo kange kungka dorek man ki no ber wori dikero na kume.
1CO 3:22 Bwen no Bulus ko Afolos, ko Kefas, ko Kale ri, dume kange bwar dikero chanawe, dikero bwiti gwam na kume.
1CO 3:23 Kom neken na Almasiya che, Almasiya neken na kwama che.
1CO 4:1 Wo cho kambo ka tunyo tiye, tami canga Almasiya kange nob taka yulan kwama.
1CO 4:2 Mwerum kange wuro, ciki cwi nob tomange na yilam nuboken.
1CO 4:3 La fiye mi wiyeu diker biduware nakom mamen bolang, na kange ku'u bolange wuro na nuboce. Nyori mani ma, mador miro nen bolangti.
1CO 4:4 Ma nyombo tano kange kwaneri wi dor mirdi, dila wuro mungbo na dike mi manki bwirangkerer. Kwama niwo amamen bolangtiye.
1CO 4:5 Nawori kom mwatire bolang na nyimde diye ce lam, na kwama yilau, an fwetangum gwam dike yurangum nangen kumtacileu, na yilo chi wubangi kwaner niri na nerece. na nimde nubo kwarub winti-winti na fiya chunenr cehro kwama nen.
