1CO 4:6 Kebmibo, mi ki cob deije wuro wi dor mir kange Afolos ki dor kimer, kambo nyo wi nyo chungayek kang merang dikero no tokki kom kumde diker na wo mulangum me. nayilam nyo kati yilo kange tiber kimer ta fwinti ki cin la kange dor kange.
1CO 4:7 nacho we wo to buni cqika tiber kumer kanhe kangem be? nye kom cike nawo kebo wo ci nekom koni ye? no koniri kom yoweri nyebwi kom kung dorti na dike kebo nye?
1CO 4:8 kweri kom fiyam diker kom dotiye, kom terum nagen liyaro yilo kebo kange nyo! dong dong bilangtum mimbo nakom fiya liyar, dike bwiye nabi ma liyar warikange kom.
1CO 4:9 ki nung nerermi? nyo nob nangen kwma na dong dong wi tikako cuwam bwire tami na nuboburo na nawo ci mwaticinan bolang bware. chin yilam diker toka fou kalewo, fou nob tomangenin, kange niffir.
1CO 4:10 Bin yilam nubo mani ki yulanne nyo ki almasiya. La kom nob nyomka mwor almasiya. Nyo nob yaretinim wi, La kom nob bi kwaneb, kebo nob yarang ka.
1CO 4:11 Yaken na wruo yeu bika nob wurab kange dulomwe nubo manki belle wuro yoriyeu, min nuwa bibukero bwira bwirau mor luwe.
1CO 4:12 Dotange fiya nyo kambo ken, nyoki manang nangen ki kang yek no ci ko nyori nyo bilangci kambo ci neyo dotange di, nya mwirumbo.
1CO 4:13 Ta no ci kwanyo kineredi, nyo ki tok ken nungi. yon yilam, di nawo ci yilam ki nyo nob. nyimangka fou kalewo kange chinge bowo la dwitiye gwam.
1CO 4:14 mi mulangbo dike buro nan dokkom kwenduwenen, wori nan makimen ywelka tami nob cwikako bibeiyo lomi.
1CO 4:15 Bwentano kom wi ki nib takako bikate kwob mwor almasiya, kom man ki teb ducce. dikebwieyu min yilam teh kume mwor almasiya Yesu wi wabbero nen.
1CO 4:16 Na weu min dubkom, kom ma namiu.
1CO 4:17 Cho diker bwii man twom nen Timoti bwe ma chwitiye kange ciyaka mik na bi bwenan co Teluwe na nung kumen nure kambo ma merang cinen ku wabeu.
1CO 4:18 Na weu kangum kumenbo yilam nob kunga dorek, ci mati tani mani ma bouti kumen.
1CO 4:19 Dila man bou kumen kebo wuro a kutang tiye. Na teluwe nungi nyori, na nimde kom yumom kange ker nub kung ka doreko.
1CO 4:20 Liyar kwama ro kebo ki tokka la ki filang.
1CO 4:21 Ye mon cwitiye, nbou kimen ka? ki dang ka kaka limer kaka bweldo limer.
1CO 5:1 Nyim nuwaki burotum wi tiber kume, twati burotumero wore chi ciyabo ciko mor nubo nyombo kwama nen. Fulen kerero minuweu incho, kange more kume dati ki wi kece.
1CO 5:2 Kom kundorti kambo tak! kebo firnerer daten komatiya? Co nii wo maniyeu, in tamnyo atin cokumco more kume.
1CO 5:3 Ta bwen no mi mani kange kom mor bwiye duwaleu, dila mi wari kange kom yuwa tanbagek, kweri min warum wuro, tamnyo miki nowi.
1CO 5:4 Ki kiini kom mwerkangi kiden Te kwama be Yesu di, Yesu tangbe miko wi wari kange kom mor Tekwama Yesu, kweri minma niiwonin bolang.
1CO 5:5 Mi ma nyo natin neken bwe kelkele niiwo twalum bwiyo, na yuwa tangbe ceko fulom ki dume te kwama.
1CO 5:6 Kung ka dorek kumeko yorbo. Ka nyombo kambo cham fuwambo nyo bi duwar ki kanghun mimbo gwam?
1CO 5:7 Kom nirom dor kumero wucak fiye can fuwambo wiyeu, wori nakom yilam na cwen, dila tiilita wuro mani ki ca fuwam. wori Kiristi kwame duklemu yabka beko chin twim fiang kico.
1CO 5:8 La nyori dila bi more duklumebeu ki camfuwam car, cam fuwambo wuro no ki dambo bwireu. Naweu, bi ma duklume be ki Tiilita mani ki chamfuwam chari bilenkeret.
1CO 5:9 Min mulang kumen mor bifumer tomanger mir mi ki kom mwerkang re dor kange nubo ma kayaka tiye.
1CO 5:10 Kebo nubo ma kayakati dor bitiner mitok tiye, kaka nob nungumgeb, kaka nob kub, kaka nubo bwangten fulen tiye, tam katim dubom biro dorbitinenreru.
1CO 5:11 Dila naweu mi mulang kumenti kom mwerkan dor kange nubo yim mor kayaka, kange nung nung, kange bwanka fulenek, kange nunger, kange norangka. kom care cari kange dwam do wuro.
1CO 5:12 Tala ma manyi naman nubo biro mani lokwama ni bolang? La nyori ke kambo ka ma nubo wabe kwama nin bolang tiya?
1CO 5:13 Dila kwama manubo wuro kaleneu bolang tiye. Ko cokum nii bwirko more kume.”
1CO 6:1 Tano kange more kume kwabkang ti kange ri, dila labo diker cayaken kabum nob bolangeb kange yambo kabum nubo bwangten kwamatiya? kaka kanyombo nubo bwangten kwamatiye ama dor bitinerro nen bolang tiya?
1CO 6:2 Tano ko kama dor bitinero nen bolangtiye ri, dila kamfweki fuwakangka kereko bidumeka?
1CO 6:3 Ka nyomba nibo bama nob tomangeb kwamabonin bolang tiya? la ano nyo mami bama keti yim kalem bo wonin bolangtiye?
1CO 6:4 Tano kom ma ketito duwen kange finiyenin bolangtiri, yebwi kom yakenti ki dwan kerer fiye nubo yumbo kwama wiye?
1CO 6:5 Ma to wuro kom nuwa kwenduwe. kange win mani more kume wuro kiyilen a dol fuwakangka kereti tiber kumera?
1CO 6:6 Dila nii bwangka kwama yakenti ki kiyange kice nii bwangka kwama mubolange kabum, niiwo nyombo kwama.
1CO 6:7 Bwini lomkangkako noti tiber kiristareu dangi fwefwe ciko. Yebwi manikom ciya dotange tiye? Yebwi mani mwa ciya wung likatiye?
1CO 6:8 Komki bwikom komma nninin yorbo kom wunglichiti tak.
1CO 6:9 Ka nyombo nubo mani ki cakcakeu mani fiya kwali lokwamatiya? kom nere bilenke dor cwerker. kange nob kayaka, kange nubo bwnagten fulentiyeu, kange nob burokab, kange nabarubbo burotumer, kange nubo merang buroka tiye.
1CO 6:10 nob kub, nung-nung, fule, buroka, nabarubo ma buroka tiyeu, nii kange mani morece afiya liyar kwamarti.
1CO 6:11 kangem kumenbo kino nyo dila chin nirimkom wucak, chin neken kom kwama nen. fiye yuwa tangbe kwama beko wiyeu.
1CO 6:12 Dikero gwam dong dong fiye mi wiyeu, dila kebo dikero wucake, diker nagener. Dikero gwam dong dong fiye mi wiye, dila mani maciya dike kange a cumomye tiye.
1CO 6:13 Carito kin morefuye, morfuye kin cariak, Dila kwama an cutang chiwigam. Chi ywelbo bwiyo nama kayaka. Dila nyori ki Tekwama an ne bwiyo diker.
1CO 6:14 Kwama a kung Teh mwe kange kange bo kibikwan dorek cek.
1CO 6:15 Ka nyom bwikumeu kutelti Almasiya? Mantu kutelti kwma ro nan mwerco kange burotuma? kwama a cukum.
1CO 6:16 Ka nyomba wuro murom kange burotumeri, yilam mwerum bwi kange ca?
1CO 6:17 Kambo bifumero tokeu, Chi yobeu chiyan knage yilam nagen win. Dila wuro mwerum kange tekwamari, cin yilam yuwa tangbe ko win ka co.
1CO 6:18 Ko cwam kayakako min, bwiraka kere wuyak niifir mati ki bwice, dila niifiro ma kayaka kotiyeu kima bwiranka lama bwiceu.
1CO 6:19 Ka nyom bwikumeu yime yuwa tangbe kwamako wucake, wuro yim more kume, wuro ka fiya kwama nina? ka nyombo kom kebo na dor kumeroce?
1CO 6:20 Chi ten kom ki fene. La nyori, kom duktang kwama ki bwikumeu.
1CO 7:1 La dor dikero wo kom mulnag meneu, “Yori kabo nii a kere nawiye.”
1CO 7:2 Dila ker cuwakatini dor bwiratum, daten nii a yilam ki wice ri nawiye ken a yilam ki bwece.
1CO 7:3 Bwayileu daten a ne wice dikero wo yilam na wice ceu nyo nawiye ama bwecenen tiye ken.
1CO 7:4 Na wiyeu man ki bikwan keret dor bwiceronen, la bwece cike. Nyo ken nii luweu mani ki bikwan keret dor bwicero nin. dila wice cike.
1CO 7:5 Kom kwak re bwiti wabkanka, no kebo wo kom ciya cuko bwiti kom nawo kumenin bi duware. kom ma wuro na kom neken dor kumero duloh. la nakom wab kangi wari tak, kati tila bwe kelkeleu cuwa komti bwini taka dorek kumeko.
1CO 7:6 Dila mi yikom wuro na neka yulanek kebo na werfun ni ce.
1CO 7:7 Man cwi nubo gwam yilam na mo. Dila kwama nerangbo luma nereko kidimen-kidimen. kange ki wang luma nereko wo kange ce wang ko wurendo.
1CO 7:8 Ki nubo buro nabeu kange natubo nabarub cebo bwiyameu, miki an yor cinen ciya nare na mo.
1CO 7:9 Dila no mani ci ya dol taka dorek tiri, ciya narangum. An la cinen diker ciya narangum kange wo kuruu a tum ci tiyeu.
1CO 7:10 ki nubo wo narangumeu ma neci werfundo woti kebo mo, la Tee kwama- Na wiye a kubo kubore lo bwece.
1CO 7:11 Dila no cin kubo bwece nin ri, ca nare kange nii kebo nyori, ca ywel kangum tibercero kange bwece, Nii nabareu a yware wice.
1CO 7:12 La ki tangnumbo miki, mo kebo Tee kwama no kange nii wi ki nawiye wo nebo bilenkeri, no nawiyeu co ciya can yim kange cori, ca ywaco re.
1CO 7:13 no nawiye wiki bwece wo nebo bilenkeri no bwece co ciya can yim kange cori ca dob core.
1CO 7:14 wori, Nii nabareu wo nebo bilenkeu yilam wo cii cokcokeu ker wicer, la nawiye wo nebo bilenkeu yilam wo cii cokcokeu ker bwecer. kebo nyori, bibeyo lokumeu mani a yila ti wucak. Dila kibi com ciin cokumcii coke.
1CO 7:15 Dila no buro bilenkeu curi, dom co a yaken ti no bwi nawori, noro wo nii nabareu teweu kaka nawiyeu, mani dor cer kwama cobo nabi yi mor fuwor neret.
1CO 7:16 Mwa nyom nyi, mo nawiye keno mwan ceer bwe meri? kaka mwa nyom nyi bwayile keno mwan ceer wimweri?
1CO 7:17 Bwenno nyiri, kambo kwama nerangbo dikeor yilam be ki dimeneu, nii a ma nangen do kambo kwama cou cew. wuro werfun miir ki bi kurwabero nin gwam.
1CO 7:18 Kange wi wo biyen biye lar fiya co cii cwo cou naci ne belenke? ca dore naci yilam na nii biye bo lareu. kamnge wi wo biye bo lar ki kwamawo cicwo co mor bilenke? ca biye re lar cero.
1CO 7:19 Biye ka larek kange bwini biyeka larek keb diker kwomkak. Dikero dateneu neak durek ki werfun
1CO 7:20 Nii a titi mor bicoro cii couceu. Fiyaco kwama cwo co naci ne bilenkeu.
1CO 7:21 Mwin changa fiyaco kwama cwo nena? kwom de dor mwer dor cer. Dila no mwan fiya nure ceer kari, mani nyo.
1CO 7:22 Wori nii wo kwama cuo co fiyaco cin cangau fiya ceerka kwama nin. Nyo tak, nii wo kebo canga fiyaco kwama cuo co nanci ne bilenkeu, canga Almasiya.
1CO 7:23 Cii teen kum ki kener ducce, nyori kom yilam de canga nobeb.
1CO 7:24 Kebmibo, bwenno nii fiya dor cero mor ye fiyaco ci cuo co naci ne bilenke ri, bi yilare kwama nen bwin.
1CO 7:25 dor nubo buro narangum bo wiyeu, ma mamni ki werfun kwama nen. Dila maki tok dikero mato daten ne na nii wo ki cii bwini kwamak, lan ciya ka.
1CO 7:26 Matori ker kungka nerek ko you tiyeu, yori kabo nii a yilam nawo ci yimeu.
1CO 7:27 Mwi bwam ki duka naka nawiye? dore ywaka cek. No mwi manki nawiyeri, dore naka nawiyek.
1CO 7:28 Dila no mwin nam ri, mwi mabo bwirang ke, no bubiya wo nambo wiyeu nam di, ci mabo bwirang ke. Dila buro narangumeu an nuwarang dotange tini ki denmwer-Kidemen, la ma cwiti nami cok kom more ce.
1CO 7:29 Dila wo miki, kembibo kang kene ko da dum cuka, tabti na wo, yaken cuko kab, nubo ki natubeu a yi namwi cii man cuko.
1CO 7:30 Nubo ci wiye tiyeu a mani namwi kebo nubo ci wiye, kange buro ma bilangtum tiyeu namwi kebo nubo ma bilang tum tiye, Nubo tenang diker tiyeu namwi cii man ki diker.
1CO 7:31 nubo buro ma nangenti ki kale weu a mare namwi ciin neken bikwan ceer maka nangenek ki kaleu, wori wank kale kowo atii dim.
1CO 7:32 Ma cwi nakom fiya ceerka ki komka tini. Nii wo na beu, ki bulnag ki diker yilam Tee kwama ce, kambo a ciya ti kange ce.
1CO 7:33 Dila nii wo na meu ki kwama dikero dor bitinenereu kambo ci lunga neer wicero tiyeu.
1CO 7:34 Neer cero tikangum. Nawiye wo nabeu kaka'a bubiya ki kwa'a diker yilam kwama ce, kambo ca neken dorceroti bwi kange yuwa tangbe. Dila nawiye nameu ki kwom dor dikero kale neu, kambo bwece a nuwa luma cek tiyeu.
1CO 7:35 Ma tok wuro na tikang kom, kemi nan dok kom totange. ma tok wuro ki dikero yor-yore, na kom neken dor kumero Tee kwama nin kambo diker kange mani a kwom kom tiye.
1CO 7:36 Dila no kange kwati ki mani ci ma bubiya conin dikero dateneri, no bubiyau cum cor nakar, takeu no tam nyori, ca ma dike ci cwi tiyeu. Kebo bwirangke ca matiye. Cii ya kangum.
1CO 7:37 Dila no cin tiim kibi kwan ner cerdi no kwom cobo catin tom dor cerori, no cin tum mor nenerce can ma wuro ri, na ci yomre bubiyace ri, can mani yora.
1CO 7:38 La co nii wo nam bubiyaceu mani dong dong, tak ri, wuro ciya ki mani ca na'a bubiya cetiyeu mani la kece ceu yorak.
1CO 7:39 Bolangko bwam na wiyeu ki kwama wo bwece ki dumeu, Dila no bwece bwiyamri, cin tin nam kange nii wo ca cwitiyeu, la a yilam mor nubo lo Tee kwama.
1CO 7:40 Duwal mor warkemiu, catin nuwa luma duce no ci yiken kambo ci yimmeri, takeu mi kwatiri mo ken man wiki yuwa tangbe kwama.
1CO 8:1 Naweu, dor caritowo bibwitinineu, bin nyumom biki gwam be bin wirangi ki nyomkak. Nyori kako bouti kurka taryek dila cwiuka wi ki muka.
1CO 8:2 Yomkako kwabi ki cii nyumom diker ri, nii cuo nyombo kambo daten ca nyumom tiyeu.
1CO 8:3 Dila no kange cwii kwamari, cin nyumom ni cwo.
1CO 8:4 la ker caka caritoko ca neken ne bi bwititiyeu, Bin nyumom biki bibwiti kalewo kebo dike kane tak ri, kwama kange man cum wo wiineu.
1CO 8:5 Bwenno dike cii cwo tiki bibwiti ni wi dii kwama kaka dor bitiner, (Kambo bibwitini kange teluwe tinim wi rangi kila nyeu.
1CO 8:6 Dila kwama win cwar fiye bi wiyeu wo dikero gwam ceru cineneu, wo kercer bi yimcu, kange Teluwe Yesu Almasiya wiin, wo cinen dikero gwam fiya fwelka, cinen tak bifiya fwelka.
1CO 8:7 La nyom kakawo kebo nubo gwam cike. Nyori kangembo, fiya co wab fulen, La cin ca carito wo na dikero cii neken bibwitiyeu. La kwarum nere ceu, yilam ki duti wori kwambo.
1CO 8:8 Dila cari mani a yatiki bo kwama nin. Ba bwirabo nobi cabori kaka bi cob co diker nobi caari.
1CO 8:9 Dila ko nhyumom ceerka kume ko yilam bo dikero a dok kangeti wo kwambo mor bilenke kottang ka tiye.
1CO 8:10 Ki dangne no yilam nii kange wo bilenke ceu kwambeu to nen mo nii mwiki nyom kau mwin ca cariti mor bikur waber bibwititi mwa dok kwarum nere ceu kwambeu bikwan caka dikero cii neken bibwiti ya?
1CO 8:11 La ker nyoka ko mwiciko dor bibwitireu nii wo kwambeu, keebe wo Almasiya bwiya kercereu, fiya bwari.
1CO 8:12 Nyori, no mwi ma kebmwebo nin bwerang ke, mwi dok ner cero kwambeu fiya der di, mwin ma Almasiya nin bwirang ke.
1CO 8:13 No cari atin dok kemi kot tangkari, mani ma wo nange ti tak, kati yila in kwob kebmibo nin yare.
1CO 9:1 ma man ki ceerka ka/ ma kebo nii tomange? Ma to bo Yesu Teluwe ba? Kom kerangbo nangen kaner Tee kwama nina?
1CO 9:2 No ma kebo nii tomange tangaum nobebo nin di, min co kumen. Wori kom warke nangen tomanger miro Tee kwama nin.
1CO 9:3 Wo co kwicank miko nubo buro cuwaye tiye nin.
1CO 9:4 Ba manki ceerka bi ca bi noo ka?
1CO 9:5 Bi mani ki ceerka na tuu dor bero nin natubo ne bilenke kambo tangnum nob tomangebo kange yitub Tee kwama, kange kefas ca?
1CO 9:6 Kaka ka Barnabas kange mo wo manki bikwan neret naci mare nangen na?
1CO 9:7 We yilam nii kwene ki kemercer bila ce? we co tola bi tuttuiri cabo bi tutti yo more ce? kaka we yuwa bicir di nobo yir cere?
1CO 9:8 ma tok dikeniti buro kibi kwan neret nii fira? Werfundo tok bo nyo kena?
1CO 9:9 Mulangum mulange mor werfun Musar “Kom dok tende Muzzle nyi nenner ki kwama wo ci fuwa range cam tiyeu.” La nenne kibi com kwama tok ker to dorcere?
1CO 9:10 kebo dorber ci tok kera? ci mulangum kibo wori nii wo kaka tom tiye ki kaka ki yoka nererk, rila wo fuwarange cam tiyeu a fuwarangi ki yoka nererk can fiya wi.
1CO 9:11 No nyi fii diker yuwa tangbe more kume ri, la diker bwei bweiye, fiye nyi wiye na nyi fiya kwilen kumena?
1CO 9:12 No kangem bo ca luma cerka kume ko wuro ri, nyi man ki wo laa wo ceu ka? kawo nyi mabo nangen ki ceerka kowuri la nyori nyim bim ner ki dikero gwam kange. wo nya bou tiki tii ka fulenYesu Almasiya.
1CO 9:13 Kom nyombo komki nubo buro ma nangen do wucakketi mor bikur wabe reu ki fiya cari bikur wabe ra? ko nyom bo nubo ma wabe ti tancilan do wuccake ki fiya carito mor diker ci bouti cuko tancilando wuccaka?
1CO 9:14 La nyo tak Teluwe kwma tokke ki nubo buro tok fulen kerer cero tiyeu a fiya cari cero ki fulen kerero nin.
1CO 9:15 Dila ma mabo nangen ki ceerka kowo. Takeu ma mulang bo wuro ri nakom ma men diker dor cer. an lamen diker in bwiyam kange wo kange man wo a ywamye bitenan bo wo tiye?
1CO 9:16 wuri no mi tok fule kerero tiri, ma manki dikero a dok ye bitenam tiye, wori min mawo. A kwann ye no ma tok bo fulen kerer di.
1CO 9:17 La no mawuro ki cwika miik ri man wiki cuner. Dila no kebo ki cwika mik ri, duwal man wiki nangen do kwama neyereu dor mir.
1CO 9:18 Nye cuner miro? ri kambo ma tok fulen kere ri, matin ne nubo fulen kerero ki luma nerek kebo ki kemer nyori mani ma manengen ti ki ceerka mor fulen kereo nineu.
1CO 9:19 Bwenno min fiya ceerka fiye gwammeu, min yilam canga nubo gwamme ri, nami fiyau ten kangem nubo.
1CO 9:20 Fiye Yahudawa wiyeu, min yilam nii Yahudawa na min fiya ciya ka Yahudawa wak gwam. Ki nubo bolangko ma liyar ceer tiyeu min yilam na ni bolang ma liyar ceertiye nami fiya ciyaka nub bolange.
1CO 9:21 Ki nubo mani mor liyar bolanger reu, min yilam na ni wo mani mor liyar bolangere. bwenno ba cer bo mor bolang kwamak miki bwimiyeu, dila miki no mor bolang Almasiya. Mi ma wuro nami fiya liyarka nubo mani mor bolangekeu.
1CO 9:22 Ki nubo wo kwamang beu, min yilam mi manki bikwan nami fiya ciyaka nubo kwamang beu. min yilam dikeni buro gwam ri bwenno a manyi ri, matin ceer kangembo.
1CO 9:23 Kom nyombo cwaka cwokek.
1CO 9:24 Nubo cwatiyeu ki cwa gwamce, dila nii wi ki yore nan cwake ra? cwa namwi cam nando.
1CO 9:25 Nii lore ki merang taka dorek mor dikero gwam. cii ki ma nyo naci fiya nando kayati kayau, dila beu biki mani nabi yo wuro mani kaya reu.
1CO 9:26 Wo co kando mi cwam tiyeu. kebo na nii wo cwacwak ti koniyeu. Won co kambo ma kwam kang tiye kebo na ni wokwa yuwatiye.
1CO 9:27 La man dok bwimiu yilam canga, ri kati yilo kambo mi yi kangembo fulen keredi, ki bwiri ci cokum ye.
1CO 10:1 Ma chwibo ki yilam kebo ki nyomka kebmibo tebbebo gwam ki no tob bilorem kange chuu mor wima.
1CO 10:2 Gwam cin yuchinen mwem Musambo more bilore kange wima.
1CO 10:3 Gwam chiye ci cha ti yuwa tangbe wucake win.
1CO 10:4 Gwam chiye chin noo yuwa tangbe wucake nyo wo ci no chwela yuwa tangbe ko bwanchinenten teyeu, chwelaka churo kiristi.
1CO 10:5 La kwama nuwabo lima ki ducce more ciye la bitenti chiro watangum wi yera.
1CO 10:6 Na weu dike buro yilam nungka binen, na bi yilare nob dilanka bwiyek dor dikero bwir wo bi dilantiye.
1CO 10:7 Bi yilare nob wabe fulene na wo more chiyeci matiye. na wo mulangum mulange, “Nubbo yiken cha, noo la kwen loro”.
1CO 10:8 Bi yilare kayaka, na wo ducce more che mane. Mor kume win nubo bikate kwini yob chilombo taar bwiyam dor cher.
1CO 10:9 Bi chuware Kiristi na wo ducce more chiye mane, La nachuwe twalangum chi.
1CO 10:10 Ki mare fwenna na wo ducce more che mane, cin bwiya bwar kang ni tomange kwama wucake.
1CO 10:11 Na weu dike buro machineneu na yilam nungka binen. Mullangum Mulange na yilam werangka, binen wo chile kale wo bo bineneu.
1CO 10:12 Nyori ni wuro toti chin timeri cha ma nyora kari cho yari.
1CO 10:13 chuwakakako kange mani wo bo kimen mani nubo nin gwamme, wori kwama ni bilenke. mani a dobti ci chuwakom wo a lam bikwan kumero tiye. Ki chuwaka chan ma kumen nure cherka, wo ka mwirumum tie.
1CO 10:14 Nyori kom mi cwiti-cwiyeu, kom cwam fiye fulene.
1CO 10:15 Miki yi kom na nubbo wuro ki nyomka, na kom warker dor dike ma tokkeu.
1CO 10:16 Kwele bibwiyere wo nyoten bibwiyer tiyeu, kebo wo ki chike gwam mor bwiyale kiristi ka? Charito wo nya wulangeu, kebo wo bi chiko win mor bwiye Kiristi ka?
1CO 10:17 Wori charito wiin, bo keneu bi ducce bwiyo wiin. Bin cha chari wiin gwam be.
1CO 10:18 ki too israila mor bwiye, kebo nubbo buro twi nuwang tiye cha dikero tangjilanko wucake tiye ka?
1CO 10:19 Ye mi toktiye, ki fulen diker ka? kaka charito ci ne fulen neu diker ka?
1CO 10:20 La miki tok dike buro nubbo nyombo kwama, nob fulenneb ki ne ninga dike buro, kebo kwama. ma chwibo ki mwerkang dor kange ninga.
1CO 10:21 ma ka noo kwele teluwe ti kange kwele ninga.
1CO 10:22 Kaka biki kang teluwe nin ner mor kiye ka? bin kwami bin lacho ka?
1CO 10:23 dikero gwam na wo yor yore, la kebo dikero gwam ki tikaliye. “Dikero gwam na wo yor. yore,” La kebo dikero gwam wo muu ni tiye.
1CO 10:24 Kange nii a dore dike yor yore dor chero che komi, nyori cha do dike yori ni chi wariye.
1CO 10:25 Kom cha dikero gwam ci miti fiye miyaka, kom mere bi mer more nere.
1CO 10:26 Wori “Kalewo na Teluwe che kange dike more che”.
1CO 10:27 No nii nyombo kwama chuwo nen chaka chari di, mwen chiya mo yari, cha dike cho ne nenneu, mere bi mer mor nere.
1CO 10:28 La no kange yinen ki “wo chin wabum fulen chiko di” chare, ki ker nii wo yi neneu kange ker meka nererk.
1CO 10:29 Meka nerek ni wineu, kebo mweu. Ye a bwiti war neri kange a warkerti dor cherka mike?
1CO 10:30 No min cha charito ki buka kangek ri, ye bwi chiya toyeti dor dikero wo ma ne buka kangekeu?
1CO 10:31 Nyori, no mo cha kaka noo, kaka dike mo maneu ri, mani gwam dike a bouti ki duktangka kwama ke.
1CO 10:32 Kom yilam dikero manki diker yaret Yahudawa nin, helenawa nin kange mwerkangka nubbo bwan kwama nin tiyeu.
1CO 10:33 Nyo tak kom ma dike wuro nubbo gwam a bilangtiye. Ma dobo yokka dor mirek kini, miki do nubbo nin ducce. Ma wuro mna fiya fuloka.
1CO 11:1 Yi yilam nob merangka ki mo, na wo min nii merangka ki Kiristi Yesu.
1CO 11:2 Na weu min chaklang kom wori mor dikero gwam kom kwayeti. Mi chaklang komti wori kom tam kibi kwan dikero ka chiya chikeu dong-dong na wo ma nekome.
1CO 11:3 Teluwe nubbe gwam, teluwe nawiye nii nabare, kwama cho teluwe Kiristi.
1CO 11:4 Nii nabare wo kwob dilo kaka ker dukumer, dor chero chumom chumeri nebo teluwe dur.
1CO 11:5 La nawiye wo kwob dilo kaka tok ker dukumer dor chero chombo chomeri, nebo teluwe che dur. Won yila na dikero namwi dor chero charum-chare.
1CO 11:6 No nawiye mani a chwom dor certiri, cha mwatum yiri cheto bi kwenje. No diker kwenduwer nawiye na mwatum yiri duwe cheri kaka charum di, cha chumom dor chero.
1CO 11:7 nii nabare mani a chumom dor cherti, wori chon cherken kange duktonka kwama, La nawiye duktongka nii nabarek.
1CO 11:8 wori nii nabare chi fwellu bo nawiye nin, nyori, nawiye chi fwellu nu nabare nine.
1CO 11:9 Chi fwelbo nawiye nin nii nabare, nawiye chi fwellu ki nii nabare.
1CO 11:10 wuro cho dike bwi nawiye a yilamti ki yirom bikwan keret dor chere ker nobb tomange wuccake.
1CO 11:11 kebo nyo tak ri, mor teluwe nawiye yibo dor cher fiye nii nabare wiye, nyo nii nabare keneu yibo dor cherfiye nawiye nine.
1CO 11:12 na wo nawiye bou nii nabare, Nyo nii nabare bou nawiye nin, dikero gwam bou kwamam nin.
1CO 11:13 Kom warkero ki bwikimi, yori kabo nawiye a kwob dilo kwama nin dor chero wumom-wume ka?
1CO 11:14 Kebo nyo yim bembo ki bwichi merang kimen ki no yiri nii nabare chwiyemi ri diker kwenduwer chinene ka?
1CO 11:15 Kebo nyo yim bembo ki bwichi merang kimen, no nawiye ki yirito chwiyem chwiyemeri, duktongka che ka? wori chi necho yirito na yilam diker chomkar.
1CO 11:16 No kange wi ki kwalkan ke dor dikero wori nyo manki dike kange nyo bwanten kwama.
1CO 11:17 la mor dike bwangu kero weu, mani ma chaklang komti, wori no kom mwerye kangi ri mani kom ma dikero ken kom ki maka dikero bwir.
1CO 11:18 Ki terka, min nuwa no kom nob kwamab ki mwerkangi ri, yalkanka wi more kume, mor kange min chiya chiko.
1CO 11:19 Wo an tam yalkangka wi muwore kume, na nnyori nubbo chiya chikeu na cheru more kume.
1CO 11:20 wo no kom mwerkangi ri kebo chari kwaka ki teluwe be kom chatiye.
1CO 11:21 No kom chatiri, wo ki cha na che na tannebo cha chiye, kangumbo cham. kange nuwa wurati, kange nom ducce.
1CO 11:22 kom manki luwe ka chati, ka notiwiye ka? kom chweye kangum mwerkangka nob kwamab takeu kom ne nubbo manchike dotange. Ye ma yikom tiye? chaklang kom ka? mani ma chaklang komti wonin.
1CO 11:23 Wori dike ma ywou teluwe be nine cho mi ne kom tiye, teluwe be Yesu kume chi miyem cheu tuu tii Liita.
1CO 11:24 Bwiko cho bu kangeri, cheom wulangi chon yi ki, “Wo bwini chi ne komme, kom mawo na kwakako che kange mo.”
1CO 11:25 Nure wo tak chon tuu kwele bwiko tii llitau, chon yi ki kwelewo na norro fwirko che chi chiya chike mor bwiyale mi. Kom ma wo kir-kir na kwaka miko che.
1CO 11:26 Dike ka cha tii liita we, ka no kwele kom ki kwadir bwaret teluwe be ya chiko bi diye cha boutiye.
1CO 11:27 Nyori nii wo cha tiyowe, noo mor kwele teluwe be ki dike datenbe ri, chin ne dikero doatnge bwir bwi kange bwiyale teluwe be.
1CO 11:28 Nyori kom ter chuwaka dorek kumeko nimre kom cha tii liita, na kom noo mor kwele wo.
1CO 11:29 Wo no cha noo, tikambo bwiyeu, cha noo dor chero nin bolang.
1CO 11:30 Cho muwore kume kangumbo manki bikwan, nuwabo luma, kangum kimembo dam dum.
1CO 11:31 La no bi chuwa dor bero tiri mani chiya ma binen bolangti.
1CO 11:32 La no teluwe be ma binen bolangri, biki mwekan, nyori na chi kuwa bore kange kale wo.
1CO 11:33 Nyori kom yitub mibo no kom ningtang bwiti.
1CO 11:34 No nii wo nuwa wura tiyeri, cha cham lo, la no kom mwerkangi ri, kebo bolang che. dor tanne dikero ka mulangu weu, non bou ri man nung kume nure.
1CO 12:1 Dor neka diker na yuwatangbeko ceu kebmibo, ma cwibo kom manki nyomka.
1CO 12:2 Kom nyimom fiya cuwo kom nyombo kwama, cin bolkom kulen fulenero mani tokkereu, ki nure kila-kila chi yaaki kome.
1CO 12:3 Nyori mi cwiti kom nyimom kange nii mani wo a tok ker yuwatangbe kwama ri, ayitiki,”yesu chilum-chile”, nii mani wo a tok ki,”yesu teluwe, kange yuwa tangbe wuchake ri.”
1CO 12:4 Na weu neka dikero ki dimenti la yuwa tangbeko wiin.
1CO 12:5 Wabe wii ki dimen-ki-dimen la teluwe wiin.
1CO 12:6 nangen wii ki dimen, la kwama wiin wo na ma nagendo ti gwam mor gwamme.
1CO 12:7 Nubbo nin gwam chin ne bikwan nungka yuwa tangbe nyanglang wo a yilamti ki nangen nubbo nin gwamme.
1CO 12:8 Kange yuwa nyomkar, yuwa tangbeko wiin.
1CO 12:9 Kange nin, chin ne cho bilenke, chon yuwa tangbeko chuwo wiin, kange nin, chin ne cho twaka cho yuwa tangbeko chuwo wiin.
1CO 12:10 Kange nin chin ne nangen nyimantum, kange ker dukumer. kange nin chin ne cho nyomka, yalkangka yuwa tangbetini, kange nin, nyomka nyiini ki dimen-ki-dimen, kange nin fwetanka nyiini ki dimen-ki-dimen.
1CO 12:11 Gwam wuro nangen yuwa tangbe wiin, tikan nubbo nen ti ki winti-winti na wo cha chwiyeu.
1CO 12:12 Na wo bwiyo wiin, la ki mwantiyeu, mwantiyo buro cho bwiyo cho wiinneu, nyo Kiristi nin.
1CO 12:13 Nyo yuwa tangbeko wiin chi bo gwam chi yubinen mwembo gwam mor bwiyo wiin. Yafudawa kaka Heleniyawa, chnaga kaka nii chokkum-choke, gwam chi mabo ba no yuwa tangbeko wiin.
1CO 12:14 Wo bwiyo kebo mwan wiin, kila kabo.
1CO 12:15 No nako yii ki, “Wori na kebo kang, mi mani mwan bwiyer”. Wo mani ywacho yilaka mwan bwiye.
1CO 12:16 No tuuwo yi ki, “Wori ma kebo nuwe, ma kebo mwan,” Wo mani a ywacho yilaka mwan bwiyeti.
1CO 12:17 No bwiyo gwam nuwari, a nuwa kero ki ye? No bwiyo gwam tuu ri, a twi diker kiye?
1CO 12:18 La kwama ywel manwti bwiyero winti-winti mor bwiye na wo cho chwiyeu.
1CO 12:19 No chi gwam mwanti wiin di, la bwiyo ki nofe?
1CO 12:20 Wo mwanti bwiye kila, la bwiyo wiin.
1CO 12:21 Nuwe mani a yii kangko ti “ma cwinenbo” kaka doro yii naako, “Machwinenbo”.
1CO 12:22 La mwanti bwiye toti namwi bukkeu, chi yoryore.
1CO 12:23 Kange mwanti bwiye, yorbo toka, bi nechi durti duche, mwanti bwiyero yoryore wi ki. dur wo la ciye.
1CO 12:24 Channeu mwanti bwiye chwibo dike buro, kwama mwerkang bwiye, ne durti duche mwanti bwiye man chike.
1CO 12:25 Cha ma wo na yilam yalkangka mani mor bwiye, la na mwantiyo tokan bwiti ti kambo keng.
1CO 12:26 La no mwando wiin nuwa dotange ri, mwantito gwam nuwa dotange wari kaka mwando wiin no chin ne dur di, gwam mwantito bilangi wari.
1CO 12:27 Channeu kom bwi Kiristi kange mwantito bwichiyeu.
1CO 12:28 Kwama yo mor nob mwerkanka chek, wiineu nob tomangeb, yobeu nob dukumeb, taareu nob merangkab, bwanteneu nob maka diker nyimankar, neka twaka, buro ma tikali tiyeu, buro ma nangen kale tiyeu, kange buro nyimom nyiini ki dimen-ki-dimeneu.
1CO 12:29 Gwam che nub tomangeb ka? Gwam che nob dukumeb ka? Gwam che nob merangka ka? Gwam che ki name twaka ka?
1CO 12:30 Gwam che chi tokerti ki nyiini ka? Gwam che fwetang nyiini tiye ka?
1CO 12:31 Do nekako dur ki kor neret. La man nange kimen nure datenneu.
1CO 13:1 Ta bwenno yilam miki tok kero ki biyendi nuber, kange wo nob tomangeb kwama bo cori cano mimanki chwikari, min yilam na dinglinge ki dikereu, kaka nyorako kidineru.
1CO 13:2 Ca bwenno yilam minwiki ker neka dukumeri, dila min nyumom bilenke yurangum yurange, kange nyomka gwamm, cano miki bilenker tenang tenangeu nawuro matungum cwelaktiyero. Tano mi manki cwikari, mi kebo dike kange.
1CO 13:3 Ta bwenno min neken dike micike gwam nacin nob buneberi, nan neten bwimiu naci twime.
1CO 13:4 Cwika wiki yobka nerek kange dikero ken, cwika mani ma kurom kaka cukka dorek. Cwika mani dang kunka dorek.
1CO 13:5 Kaka mani wab dorcer. Mani kang ner wulom, mani kiye tenanka kereko bwir.
1CO 13:6 Mani nyori, ci ma bilangtumti, ki bilinkerer.
1CO 13:7 Cwika binerti mor diker gwam ne bilenketi. diker gwam, we ki ciyaka dikerek gwam, bwa nerti ki diker gwam.
1CO 13:8 Cwika mani dir, Tano tomange dukum tinim wiri, anbou ya cum. Tano biyentinim wiri, ciyan lerangum. Tona nyomka wiri ciya kom.
1CO 13:9 Wori biki nyomka dii-dii takri biki dii-dil.
1CO 13:10 Kambo wuro dimdiyeu boweri ciro dibeu ancum.
1CO 13:11 Min bi bweu, miki tok kero na bwe, miki kwadikero na bwe, miki hujo na bwe. kambo malam niiyeri min cutang bibwetiwowi.
1CO 13:12 Naweu bititoi mwin mor nuwe tirome, dila diye tikob kange tikobe, naweu min nyimom biduwar, dila diyecori man fiya nyomkako dimdiyeu kambbo cii mameu nyumkako dimdiyeu.
1CO 13:13 lawnaweu dikerewo taareu inwi. neka bilingkek, yoka nerek kange cwika, dila wo teneg moere ceu cwika.
1CO 14:1 Kom bwan cwikako takri kom citi dor dikerowo yuwa tangbe kwamamko nenin nobo, na ker dukumer.
1CO 14:2 La niwo tokker kibiyenneu tokbo kange nob la konga kwama Dila nii kange mani nuwa coti wori ciki tok kero yurangum yurange mor yuwa tangbe kwama ke.
1CO 14:3 Dila wo tok ker dukumer tiyeu ki tok kange nob naci mumci, naci bikwaneret, naci neci birim nerem tak.
1CO 14:4 Wuro tok keroti kibiyondo kange ki mudorcer, dila nii tok ker dukumertiyeu, ki mu wabe kwama.
1CO 14:5 Naweu mincwi kom tok kerti ki biyentinim. Mincwi kom tok ker dukumero laweu. Wuro tok ker dukumer tiyeu la wuro tok kerti kibiyentiyeu, (No kange fwetangi dob kwama bo nyimiri nanyime).
1CO 14:6 Naweu keb mibo tannonbou kumer mitok kerti ki biyen tinim diri, kafiya dwika nyi kime? mani mati non nyikom ki dukumeri, kaka nyomka kaka ker dukumer, kaka merangka na nyime.
1CO 14:7 Tano kulen kwabanka koworo manag ki dumeu na lirak kange bilifwiyen atin nedir dila mani cenin dirti kidimen kidimenri, kange anyem nyi ki wonco diro lirako kange bilifwiyen netiya?
1CO 14:8 Lano ci cu cumen kidiro datenberi, kange a nyomomtiye? ki nangyo kange kom.
1CO 14:9 Tano kom tokkaero manki nureceri, kange a nyomnyi kiwonco dike kom toke? ka an tokker, dila kange mani nyomti.
1CO 14:10 Nyimanka man biyentito wi dorbitiner kidimen kidimen, dila mani winwo morecer nawo manki dike tokkiye.
1CO 14:11 Tano ni nyombo diki tokkiyeu, mati yilam fabe fiye nii kere wiyeu, ni kereu an yilam fabe mintilak.
1CO 14:12 Kinonyo kumen Dila kambo kom cen boka yuwatangbekotiyeu, kom cidor mor dwika muka lokwamak.
1CO 14:13 Lawo tokkerti ki biyenneu ciya kwob dilo nabe ci fwetangi.
1CO 14:14 Tawo kwob dila ki biyendi, yuwa tangbemiki kwob dilo dila nyomkamika yoktenbo.
1CO 14:15 La, ye mamatiye? man kwob dilo kiyuwa tangbemik, nan kwobten dilo kinyomka mik. manko nure ki yuwa tangbe mik, nan katen nuwe kinyom ka mik tak.
1CO 14:16 No nobonyori, tano mu caklang kwama kiyuwatangbe koniri, amangi niiwo kaleu attokki “atiye” dor buka kangko mu dontantiyeu noci nyombo dike mu toktiyeuri?
1CO 14:17 Kom dang buka kangek nyimanka mani, dila kange dwibo ciko.
1CO 14:18 Mibu kwamanin kang ti mi tokkerti, ki biyenim lawo kumen gwamm.
1CO 14:19 Dilanawo min cwi na tokker mor lo wabe kwama nyiyo nung wuri ma nyimommeu na mu kangembo kange ker bikate kwob mor biyenne.
1CO 14:20 Kebmibo, kom yilare bibei bikwanere, nyori kom yilam bibei fiye maka dikero bwir. Dila kwama kume a yilam nubo durece.
1CO 14:21 Mulangum mor bwolange kii man tokker kange nubo biro fiye nob fabub biyenebbo wiyeu, kange toknyireyer fabuber. Kangewo gwam maniciya cuwa tuuti,” in nuwa kwama.
1CO 14:22 biyentinimbo yirom kebo, fiye nubowo nebilinker tiyenin dila fiye nuboro nebo biling kenin. ker dukumer yirom fiye nubowo nebiling ketiyening kebo fiye nubowuro nebo biling kenin.
1CO 14:23 Dilano lo wabe kwamma atin mwerum fiye win natokker kibiyentinim, birombo kaleu kange birombo nebo bilingke dou mordi nami yiti kimon twelum twele?
1CO 14:24 Tano kom tokker dukumertiri, niwo nebo bilingke douri, kero atin kece ciyatin warcinen warke dor kerero conin.
1CO 14:25 Yurka nerek ceko atin ceru kale, la niyeco catin yarken bitinen ci wab kwama, atim toki kibocom kwama wikange kom.
1CO 14:26 Dila yotak kebmibo? tano kom mwer kang nyiri, kange wiki zabura, merangka dukum biyem tinim, kaka fwetangka. Tokker diker muka lowaber kwamak.
1CO 14:27 Tano kange tokker tokker kibiyendi kilaka ciko afiya nob yob kaka taar, dila ciya toktti kiwinti kiwinti, la kange na a fwetang dikero ciitoketi.
1CO 14:28 Tano wuro a fwetangtiyeu maniri, gwammce ciya kumom lowabe. Dila kwarube ciya yidorciro keroco ki kwace kange kwama.
1CO 14:29 Nyori nobker dukumero yob kaka tarr atokero, tangne ce a cwutuu warii nyomka dikeci toktiyeu.
1CO 14:30 Tano cin nekange nyomka yimwi mor waberi, niwo ki kabau a kumom.
1CO 14:31 Kwarub kume kan tokker dukumer kiwinti kiwinti, na wuyakkume kom merang dikerwi nafiyaen bikwan nerertak.
1CO 14:32 Wori yuwa tangbek nob ker dukumeroo kino wari kange nob ker dukumero,
1CO 14:33 Wori kwama kebo kwama kulomka na nero fuworece.
1CO 14:34 Natubo akumom nyici mor lo wabe kwama wori, cii necibo ciyaka tokka kerek. nyiyeceu ciya neken dor ciro kambo bolang werfundo tokeu.
1CO 14:35 No dikero kangewi cii cwiti na cii merangeri, ciya me bwetubcibo lo diker kwenduwer, nawiye natok ker mor lo wabe.
1CO 14:36 Ker kwama ro bou kumena? laukumen kom ki kwama?
1CO 14:37 No kange kwati kicinin tomange dukumeri, kaka cin nii ki dike wuro nyi mulangka cinentiyeu nyal bou fiye teluwe wiyeu.
1CO 14:38 Tano wuro ko nuwaka diker kowori, cekeneu a nuwa core.
1CO 14:39 naweu, kebmibo kom yilam kikuru tokka ker dukumer kambo ken, kom kore tokka.
1CO 14:40 Dila a ma dikero wuyak nure datene.
1CO 15:1 La naweu kebmibo mi kulomkumen ker kwamaro wuro mu yikom komyo kom manangen cikeno.
1CO 15:2 Won cho ker kwamaro cii ma kumen dumecike no kom tam kero miyi komeu kibi kwana tim yilam nokom nebo bilingke ken dor cerdi nayime.
1CO 15:3 Wori mane kom kwamage dike ro ken wuro ma yoki kaba lamti almasiya bwiya ker bwirang kerber, kambo bifumer cero tokeu.
1CO 15:4 Ciin fwerum co tak, dila kwenum ki kume taare kambo bifumero tokeu.
1CO 15:5 Dila dang jang dor cero kefas nin na nyime kwobcilombo yobe nin.
1CO 15:6 Kambo nyeri lam dan dor cero nubo kwini nungin cikowin. Biro kangum cimbo wiki dume diduweno koweu, dila kangem cembo damdum.
1CO 15:7 Dila kambo nyeri ya dang dorcero Yakubu nen kange nubo kwarub.
1CO 15:8 Kibwiri, dangu dorcero minen na bwecibo dibe.
1CO 15:9 Wori, mo mi dwel dwel mor nob tomangeb cebo nen. Midatenbo a coye ki nii tomange, wori mine lo wabe kwama dotange.
1CO 15:10 Dila luma nerek teluwe toki ni fiyewo miwi nanweu, luma nere cero moremiyeu kebo koni dilan luma kwama wari kange mo.
1CO 15:11 Dila naweu, mo kaka cii nya tok ker kwamaro nyo ka ne bilenke nyotak.
1CO 15:12 tano ciin toki ki Yesu kwenum tuweri, cimanyi kangem kumembo tokti ki “Kwenka tuwek maniye?”
1CO 15:13 Tano kwenka tuwek maniri cii kunbo Almasiya ken.
1CO 15:14 Tano almasiya kwenbori ker nyero yilam dikero bwi koni yotak biling keret kumero yilam dikero bwir koni.
1CO 15:15 Nyin yilam nob warkeb cwerkeb dikero kwamab, nyinti nyiki kungum Almasiya tuwe wendi kuncobo.
1CO 15:16 Tano yilam kwenka tuwek maniri, Almasiya keneu ci kuncobo.
1CO 15:17 Tano cii kunbo Almasiya ri, bilinkere kume na bwir komi nawotakeu kom mor bwirang kerer kumer.
1CO 15:18 La birombo bwiya mor Almasiya yakcamce naweu.
1CO 15:19 Tano kin cho yimbo win cwar biyo neroti Almasiya ninneri, la mor nube gwam bilanci diker cibwinir.
1CO 15:20 Dila naweu, Almasiya kwenum tuwe, wuro dok cho ciyilam bika kabak mor kwenka tuwek.
1CO 15:21 Kambo buwaro dou dor bitiner dor nii wineu kwenka tuweko kino nyoken.
1CO 15:22 Kambo mor Adamu gwam cii buyameu, an fulo cii mor almasiya gwamken.
1CO 15:23 Dila kwarubce wiki nurece; Almasiya, bika kabak, nayime birombo na Almasiya ceu ciyan fulou ki kume bokacek.
1CO 15:24 na nyime bwiyeko an bwangu, ki kwama Almasiya a neken Tee kwama liyarotiyeu. la na nyime an tungum liyaro gwam, bikwan kerert bikwan duret.
1CO 15:25 An ma liyar cero na wuro catin yoken nob kurombe cebo fou na tacok bitine.
1CO 15:26 Buwaro co nii kiye bwiko wo ciya twaltiyeu.
1CO 15:27 Dila “naci yoken dikero gwam fou natacok bitine.” Kambo ciyi ciki cinyoken dikero gwam wuro dangum nyanglang mo mwerbo kange wo yoken dikero gwam cineneu.
1CO 15:28 Tano dikero gwam kino kang cari, dila bwe keneu kino kang bikwan Liyare co nii neken dikero gwam kang liyaroken. Wo atim yilam nyo na Tee kwama yilam diker gwam mor diker gwam.
1CO 15:29 Kaka'a ye abwiti kange birombo ci yucinen mwem burweremtiyeu? kwenka tuwek maniri, in yeyorak mungeko yucinentiyeu?
1CO 15:30 Ye bwi bi mor chito kir-kire.
1CO 15:31 Miti buyai kirkir. wuri cowo mitokti kicwikka dorekeu, kebmibo, wuro miciko mor Almasiya Yesu Teluwebe.
1CO 15:32 Ye atikang yetiye nuwe nube, tano bukkani kange Afisari, tano kwenka tuwek maniri, “Naweu bica bino, wori fini ban buyam”.
1CO 15:33 Ciyabol komre wori “mwerka dorek kange nubo bwir kange yimbo kenti”.
1CO 15:34 Ko yi cooki! kom yiyim Cakcakem; kom care kaba ki bwirankeret. wori kangem kumembo manki nomka kwama. Miki tok wuro nan nekom kwenduwe.
1CO 15:35 Dila kange an toki kii kwenka tuweko a manye? Co bwiyo wini ciya kwenti cike?
1CO 15:36 Kom nubo nyombo diker kambo kenei dike mwa fiyeu mani ter dwikati an buyam bwiri.
1CO 15:37 Dike mwe fiyeu kebo bwico a ceruutiye, in nunice komi. Wuro yilabo bikateri ayila dike kange kidimen.
1CO 15:38 Dila kwama amnuce bwiyo kambo ci cwiyeu, wuyak nun diketininmbo kice bwice.
1CO 15:39 Biyo kwarub kebo win. nawori bwiyo wi dwantibo wo bicireceu witak, bwi bilibeu witak, kange bwi jingeu.
1CO 15:40 bwiyolak nawo dii kwama kange bwiyewo dorbitineroceu. Dila duktangka bwidikwako kidimen duktangka bwidorbitinero ceu, kidimen.
1CO 15:41 Wori, bitirendo kange yilam kidimen fiye duktangka bitirendo wiyeu.
1CO 15:42 Kwenka tuweko kinonyo dike cifiyeu diker yakcaker, wuro ci kungeu kebo diker yakcaker.
1CO 15:43 Cii ficobo kiyoracek, ciin kungum cho dotangeka. cii fico mor deti, ciin kungum co mor bikwandoret.
1CO 15:44 Cii fico kibwiyo kendo, cii kung cho mor bwidumer. Ta No bwiye kendo wowiri, bwidume wiken.
1CO 15:45 nyo ci mulange, Adamu nii kaba yilam nii dume”. Adamu bwiko yilam yuwa tangbe ne dumetiye.
1CO 15:46 Kebo yuwa tangbe ko cou ter boka co bwiyo kendowo, na niyme yuwa tangbeko ceu.
1CO 15:47 Nii kaba cirou bitine, fou dor bitiner. Dila cho nii yobe cirou kwama.
1CO 15:48 kambo nii cho cirou bitneu kino nyo birombo ci fweleu kinbitine. kambo nii cho kino kwama birombo naceu nyoken.
1CO 15:49 Kambo bikumki bwiyowuro cerkang bitineceu, nyoken bayila niiwo dii kwama tiyeu.
1CO 15:50 Ma tok nawuro kebmibo miki nage kange bwiyale mani ciya to liyar kwamaroti. Nyotak, wuro yakcamti yakcau mani ca kwati wuro mani yakcareti.
1CO 15:51 To, miyikom yurka bilinketi: mani ba buyati gwam dila ciya fulogumbo.
1CO 15:52 Ciya fulongum bo nawo nawo, mor lifranka nuwek, ki cume bwiko. wori ciyan cuu cumeu, nubo bwyameu an kweni ki dume, ciyan fulongum bo tak.
1CO 15:53 Dila wuro kayati kayau in tamnyo can yoti bwiyowuro manki kayakau, bwiyo wuro buyati buya takeu can yoti wuro manki buyakau.
1CO 15:54 Tano bwiyowo kayati kayau ci yoti wuro manki kayakau bwiyati buyau ciyoti wuro manki buyaka wiri, dila dike ci munlangeu andim “Min buwaro mor caka kaba”.
1CO 15:55 Buwar, fe caka kaba mweko? buwar fe mwan mwero.
1CO 15:56 La mwan mwero bwirankerer, bikwan bwirankerero in bolang.
1CO 15:57 Dila bua kangek ki kwama wo nebo caka kabak fiye teluwe Yesu Almasiya!
1CO 15:58 La na weu, kom kebmibo komti yora kom mikanger. Kom titi nangen Tee ronin, kom nyimom nangen kumero fiye Teluwe wiyeu mani bwangten mwemti.
1CO 16:1 La naweu ker merangka nob kwamabo wucakeu, kambo mayi ku wabiti kwama Galatiya kom manyo.
1CO 16:2 Ki kume kaba wo kume nibereceu. Kwarub kume kayo dikerti, a tiyoi dong dong dolka kumek. kom manyo dila tano bouri kabita murang dikerti
1CO 16:3 tawon bouri birombo kom ciya kange cheu man neci tomange bifumer naci yaken chiko wursalima.
1CO 16:4 Na nyi non daten mokeneu in yakendi, laci yaken wari kange mo.
1CO 16:5 Manbou kumen kambo matiyangi Makidoniyari, wori mantinyagi Makidoniya.
1CO 16:6 kangeri matin yim wi biduwar kangeri manten miyelak wi kange kom nakom tikang ye kange yammimbo, fiye mi yakenti wiyeu, gwam.
1CO 16:7 Ma cwibon tokom kumeni biduwar. Micwitin tuu kumeni kange kom tano Tee kwama ciyari.
1CO 16:8 Dila manti Afisus in lam kume fentakos.
1CO 16:9 La cin wommen nyiloko kuyakuyau nob kiyebo wi ducce tak.
1CO 16:10 Kambo Timoti ou yafi fulang ka more kumeri, kambo nagen Teluwe cimati nawo ni matiyeu.
1CO 16:11 Kange a cwekancore. Komti kanco mor yamece kinero fuwor, naci yilam minen Wori minto nure bokacekti kange kebceb.
1CO 16:12 kange ker kebo Afolosero, Min neco bikwanerer a yakumen kange kangneu. Dila manici ciya bokakoti nawo. Atim bou kumen tano kwama bokaceko lauri.
1CO 16:13 Kom yiki bati ko ti yora mor bilenke, komma na nabarub, kom yilam kibi kwan.
1CO 16:14 Kom madikero kom matiyeu kwarub mor cwika
1CO 16:15 Kom nyimom nubo lo Sitefanas ce ter yiloko Akaya, lacin neken dor cero cima nob kwamabo wucakke nangenti. Naweu mikenkomti, kebmibo.
1CO 16:16 Kom bwangten dir ubo wuro kange birombo matikaliti mor nangenne cokkangti wari kange komtakeu.
1CO 16:17 Min ma nero fuwor kiboka Stephanas, kange Fortunatus, kange Achaicus. cin titi nyi yowo kom manifeu.
1CO 16:18 La cin yobmen yuwa tangbe miko kange kumeu. Naweu, kom nyom nob na birombo.
1CO 16:19 Ki kwama Asiya yarumkomti. Akila kange Bilkisu, wari kange ku kwama lociyeu yarumkomti kiden teluwer.
1CO 16:20 Kebbeb nob kwamabo gwam arumkomti kom yarum bwiti ki korkankako wucakkeu.
1CO 16:21 Mo Bulus, mi mulang wuro ki kang mik.
1CO 16:22 Tano kange cwibo Tee kwamari a yilam cilumcile. Teluwebe, bou!
1CO 16:23 Luma teluwa Yesu ko ati kange kom.
1CO 16:24 Na weu cwika miko ati kange kom gwam mor Almasiya Yesu. (Ati nyo)
2CO 1:1 Bulus nii tomange Yesu Almasiya ki maka kwamak kange yii be Timoti, a ne bikur waber kwamaro wo korintiyawa, kange nubo bwang kwama nin tiyeu gwam mor cinan loro Akayau.
2CO 1:2 Luma kange yim fuwor nerem fiye kwama Tebe kange Teluwe be Yesu Kristi.
2CO 1:3 Kwama Tee Teluwe Yesu a fiya duktang ka, cho kwama cini, kange dangne.
2CO 1:4 Kwama ne bo dangne mor kalaka beko nen gwam, na bo ne nubo buro mor kalaka dangne gwam ciye. Bo ki ne tangnim bo dangne ki dangne wo kwama nebeu.
2CO 1:5 No kambo dotange Kristi yokten kerbereu, la nyo bii neeri beu an yokten mor Yesu.
2CO 1:6 La bwentano bo nuwa dotange tiri, na birom neeren bem bo ce kange cerka bek, la nyo na yo bim neeri ker birom nee kumen. dangne kume ma nangen ti na ko bim neer ki dotange wo nya nuwau.
2CO 1:7 Yoneeri yeu, kumeneu man ki mokka wori nyon nyumom kambo bi wari kala kako nineu nyo ba yii ti wari mor birom neerem nyemtiye.
2CO 1:8 Nyo cwi kombo ki bwini nyomka, kebmibo ki dotange wo fiya nyo Asiyau. Chin furankam nyo, wo cum bikwan nyere, wo nyo cokum neer nyan ma dumeu.
2CO 1:9 Bicom nyon nuwa warker bwarer dor nyer bwi nyo katiyico nyo kin nyo. La nyeu kwama nin niwo kung nubo bwiyarangumeu.
2CO 1:10 Con ckumbo nyi bware bwirko nin, con cokten bo tak. yoneri be kino cinen ayila cokten bo.
2CO 1:11 Can ma wo kambo ko tikang nyo ti mor dilou. nubo ducce an ne buka kangek ker nyer, ki luma nee kaka ko nee nyeu mor dilo nubo kila-kilau.
2CO 1:12 Dike bwi nyo cukti yeu co wo: War ke dume neeyeu nyoki ya wucak kange yimbo ken mor kwama, fou dor bitinerowo. Nyo ma wo kange kom kebo mor nyom ka ko dor bitinenrowo.
2CO 1:13 Nya mulang ki membo dike mani ka kiyeti kaka ka nyomtiye, miki yoneri mwan nyumom gwam.
2CO 1:14 Na wo ka nyumom nyo bi duwareu, kan ma bwi ki nyo ki diye bouka Teluwe bek Yesu, Na- wo ma tiki komeu.
2CO 1:15 Ki ciyaka kowo mi ciko nhyeu, min curi nan bou kumen ki kabak, na yarume yobeu na makumen nangen.
2CO 1:16 Ma ywabwiti nan yarumkom na ma yaken ti- Makidoniya ri, nan yarum ten kom nan yilau Makidoniya ri, na ko toum ye na ma yilaketi yahudiyari.
2CO 1:17 Kambo ma kwati na weri, kwa neeri ka? ma ki ywel diker cuwaka nifirek, kambo ma yiti ong-di- ong o-ong di -o-ong, ciko win?
2CO 1:18 Na wo kwama nii bilelnkeu, ker nyero kumeneu ke bo ong kange o-ong.
2CO 1:19 Wori bi bwe kwama Yesu Kristi wo Silbama, Timoti kange mo nyo yi kom ker cer tiyeu, kebo ong kange o-ong.
2CO 1:20 Wori mor kwama cinen gwam ong- more ce, nyori fiye co wiye bo touti ati nyo mor duktangka kwamak.
2CO 1:21 Na weu kwama nyumom bo nye kange kom mor Kristi, con cokum bo.
2CO 1:22 Con kwa kang bek dor ber ne bo yuwa tangbe kwamak mor neere be nyi dike wo a ne bo tiki bwiyeu.
2CO 1:23 La man co kwama na nii warker mi, dike bwi ma bou bo koritiya na cier kom.
2CO 1:24 Wuro kebo na nyi yilam teluwe bilenkerer kumer, la nyeu bon biyitob kange kom, bilanka kume ko, kambo ka tii mor bilenker kumero nineu.
2CO 2:1 Co nyori man warum ki bwimi, mani ma yati kumen tak, ki dariko wo bwai bwayeu.
2CO 2:2 nan kang kumen neer di, we a ne ye bikwan neerer tiye, na kebo co wo ma kang ten neeredi?
2CO 2:3 Ma mulang kumen na wo ma maneu, nan bou kumen di in fiya kang ka neerer fiye nubo wo a fou men neer tiyeu, man wi kibi kwan nerer kumen gwam, fou neerer do ma cikeu, cokumeu gwam.
2CO 2:4 Ma mulang kumen mor kalaka kange kang ka neerek, kange mwem nuwem ducce. mani ma cwiti kang kumen neer tak, La nyeu na kom nyumom cuwaka cwika kume min cikeu.
2CO 2:5 Na kange bou ki diker kangka neerek di kebo ka mo ki kwami co maten tike we, la cnga ko kange ri na kang kumen degwam.
2CO 2:6 Mwerum bou ka ma nii wo nineu, cuwati.
2CO 2:7 La naweu kebo mwerum, kom cutang cinen wi. kom bi cinen neer ko mani nhyo katiyilo fir neerer dur cengem co.
2CO 2:8 Ma yii komti ko nung cinen cwika kume ko nyang lang.
2CO 2:9 on co dike bwi ma mulang kumeneu nan cuwa kom, nan nyumom keno kom nob bwangkab di.
2CO 2:10 Na nii ka cutang cinen wiyeri, mi keneu man cutang cinen wi, dike ma cutang wiyeu, na man cutang kange diker wiri ker kumer kabum Kristim.
2CO 2:11 Won yilam nyo kati bwekelkele bolbo, wori ba man ki kwomtom ki yulsn cero.
2CO 2:12 Kwama wom men nyoliko kambo ma bou taru wasa ma ne fulen ker Kristi wiyeu.
2CO 2:13 Ki curo gwam neer miro dabo, wori ma tobo yimi Titus wi. La min dobum ci min yilaken Makidoniya.
2CO 2:14 La buka kangek fiye kwama wiyeu wo nebo turani ti mor Kristi kir kir ker nyer ca wa kun finager nyom ka ce fiye gwameu.
2CO 2:15 Bo kun do ficangeu kwama nin mor Yesu. mor nubo buro fulociyeu, kange biro bwiya ti bwiyau.
2CO 2:16 Nubo biro bwiya ti bwiyau kunficanger bwarer yang ciko bwar. Buro fulo-ci ti fuloweu kun ficanger dume yang ciko dume. wedaten dike burowe?
2CO 2:17 Bo kebo na tangnin nubembo buro miyeker kwamar ti na ci fiya ki mwemeu, la nyeu ki neero wucakey bo tou ti mor Yesu na wo kwama toum beu nuwe kwama.
2CO 3:1 Ba ter wabka dor berek tak ka? nyo cqwi bo warke kumen kaka nyinen na mo tangim nobembo matiyeu, kebo nya?
2CO 3:2 Kom ki bwikom kom warke nyeu mulangum mulange mor neere nye, wo nubo gwam nyumom la ti kiyei.
2CO 3:3 kom nungi kom warke fiye kristi wiyeu nan nangene nyero, mulangbo ki kwekwe, la mulangum ki yuwa tangbe kwamako ki dumeu. mulangbo dor teret, la dor neere nifirer.
2CO 3:4 Won cho bikwan neerero nyo ciko mor Yesu kabum kwamam.
2CO 3:5 Nya manki kange nyumanka dor nyere wo nay yi ti nyoka kange diker bou nyineneu nyomka nyeko ki na kwama nen.
2CO 3:6 Kwama mani nyo yilam canga nyumangum nyumange, wo noro fwirko ce. Noro wo kebo mulangkako ce, la na yuwa tangbe ko ce ne dume tiye.
2CO 3:7 nangen do wo bou ki bware, mulang kin kwekwe dor terer. Bouki duktangkako wo Israilawa mania to Musa ti tikob cerue, won cho duktangkako diti diyeu.
2CO 3:8 La nagen duktangkako yuwa tangbe ko a yilam nyi?
2CO 3:9 Na naweu do diti diyeu wiki duktangka ri, La nyi wo bilenkeroceu, a fiya duktangks tiye?
2CO 3:10 Kwa neere man ki dike wo kwati bo to cho ki duktangka, la man ciko wuro nineu co duktangkako wo cum ceu.
2CO 3:11 La no wo cukeneu wiki duktangkari, la a fiya nyi wo naceu ki duktangka keu?
2CO 3:12 La bon wiki yorneri weu bo wi ki bikwan bwir.
2CO 3:13 Bo kebo na Musa wo cumom tikob ceb ki lalan kati israilawa to tikob cebo miblangti miblangeu. duktangkako wo cuti cuweu.
2CO 3:14 La neer ciyero kwamangum duwal na ci kiye noro carko ri yilam ko ciyam tikobeu, wi duwal kwalbo, la fiye Yesu ninen ki kwace a kwaltiye.
2CO 3:15 Bwentano duwen na cin kiye Musa ri, yilan ko cumon neer ciyero.
2CO 3:16 La nii yilaken teluwe nindi, yilanko cuwon kwalum.
2CO 3:17 Teluweu co yuwa tangbeko fiye yuwa tangbeko wiyeu cerkawi.
2CO 3:18 Na wo gwam be, tikobo combo comeu bo to duktangka teluwe ko ti. Fulongum bo mor duktangkako cho win, ki yim duktangka kabako yaken ciko wuronin. na wo Teluwe nin co yuwa tangbekeu.
2CO 4:1 Wori bo wiki nangen take kambo nyo yom yireduwe nyo cat bo.
2CO 4:2 Nyeu nyo dubom nure na kwenduwe ce gwam, kange wo yurangum, yurangeu, mani nyo yi yim bicirenne, take nyo tabo ker kwamaro ki bilangiya, fiye tokka bilenker, nyo ne dor nyero fiye nobo wuyenin gwam kabum kwama.
2CO 4:3 Di tano fulen keret kwamaro nyero cumom cumeri, cumom cume fiye nubo bwiyati bwiya nine.
2CO 4:4 kabal ciyero, kwama dor bitinenrowo ciyam nerciyero bwini neka bilenke.
2CO 4:5 Ma nyo tok ker dorcer nyer, ka Yesu, Almasiya ni Teluwe, nyo keneu canga kumek ki ker Yesu.
2CO 4:6 Kwama co nii yiki, Filangko an tiba mor kumtacile! an tiba mor neretbe na ne filang nyomka duktangka kwama kabum Yesu Almasiya.
2CO 4:7 Di la bo wiki cweka cer more ronin, wo a yilamti nyanklang yiti wo la dure bi kwan na kwama ce, kebo nabe.
2CO 4:8 bo nuwa dotangeti nure nin gwam, ci woo nyobo gwam. Nyon cwam tai di la nyo cok bo ner. cin ne nyo dotange, dila ci yal nyo bo.
2CO 4:9 Ci ne nyo dotange, di la ci merang nyobowi, cin buk nyo di la nyo kayabo.
2CO 4:10 Nyeu kicatec nyo tum ki bwar Yesu mor bwiye nye, na fwetang yim Yesumbo mor bwiye nye tak.
2CO 4:11 Nyo wo kwace ki catec ci neken nyo ti bwar kiker Yesu, na Yesu yilam nyanglang mor bwiye nye, na nii firoce.
2CO 4:12 Bwaro ma nangenti more nye, di la dume ma nangenti more kume.
2CO 4:13 Di la nyo wiki yumatangbe ko wucakke na bilenkerer ce na wo ci mulangge. ma ne bilenke, ma tokki, nyo ken nyom ne bilenke, nyo nya toke.
2CO 4:14 nyo nyimom nii wo ya kun teluwe Yesu kristi mor tuwe, a yila kun nyo wari kange Yesu. Nyo nyimom an yobe wari kabum cem.
2CO 4:15 dikero gwam ker kumer bwiye, fiya co wa lumako nubo nin kila, neka buka kangek yokten duktanka kwama konin.
2CO 4:16 Nyo dila nyo cwa bo, duwale kale nyo kayatiye, mor co fulong nyoti kicatec.
2CO 4:17 Di la na wori dotange bi dobe ywelnyoti na tutum duktangka wo bakni bakece wo cum cuwaka.
2CO 4:18 wori ma nyo to dikero wo bo totiye ti, dila dikero ma bo tiye mani bakni bak, wo mani bo totiye co banki bako ce.
2CO 5:1 Nyo nhyimum tano buwe wo bbo yim wiye wurom di, bo wi ki mukako kange kwama nin. Luwe wuro kebo kange muwe, luwe bakni bake mor di kwama.
2CO 5:2 Wori mor bwiye wo boti tinangi, bo ningtangti a du binen ki fiye yime be wo dii kwama.
2CO 5:3 Bo nintang woti, ki fiye bi duro mani a fiya boti kwancer.
2CO 5:4 Di la nyomanka man kambo bo mor bi kure, bo tinanti, bo ki tutum. ma nyo cwi yim fobka. Nyo co nyo cwi a dum nyo, na dume mim dike bwiya tiye.
2CO 5:5 Ni wo ywel nyoti na dikece kwma. nii wo nyo yuwa tangbeko wucak na nor dike botiye.
2CO 5:6 Di la na nyo yilam kibi kwan bwen fiyandi, Bo cubi kambo bo lika mor bwiyeri, bo kutan kange Teluwe.
2CO 5:7 Di dor bilenke bo yakentiye, ke bo na toka nuwekoce.
2CO 5:8 Nyo bo wiki bikwan na bo yalkangum kange bwiyo, be na bo yi wari kange bwiyo, be na bo yii wari kange Teluwe.
2CO 5:9 Nyo tii nyo yilam tennaka, bwen nyo mor bwiye kaka, kutarn na nyo lomco.
2CO 5:10 Wori tamyo gwambe bo mwerkangi kabum fiye yim liyare bulange Almasiya, be na gwam bo yo nyi cha mane mor bwiye, bwen na ken kaka na bwir.
2CO 5:11 Wo nyori, ba nyomom tai Teluwe bo kwou noboti. Kwama to boti twelum. mi kwati nyo ken twelum mor nere kume.
2CO 5:12 Nyo kwob kombo be na kom to nyo na nobo ken, nyo nyokin yi la kumen fiye firka, be kom fiya dike ka kar nubo wuro tuu dor chiyero na kange diker, dila kebo nyo mor nere.
2CO 5:13 Tano nyo cherum mor nyomka nyeri, kwama bwi nyo mane. Tano tak nyo mor nyomka nyeri, ker kumer bwiye.
2CO 5:14 Wori chika Almasiya dok nyo, be na nyo nyomom wo, nii win wor nubo gwam byiya.
2CO 5:15 Tak Almasiya biya dor nubo gwam, na wuro kwar cheu, a yire yila chiya yire na dorchero che. nyeu chiya yi yimbo daten na cheu wo bwiya yila chi kungum che.
2CO 5:16 Ki kero wo, naweu ma nya ma kange nin bulmag ti ki chuwa bi bwe nifire nin, bwen dwal biye nyo to Almasiya nyeu na weu nyo yiloten maka kange nin bolange nyo.
2CO 5:17 nyori gwam wo mor Almasiya, nii fwir, dikero charko chum. To yilamk afwir,
2CO 5:18 Gwam dike buro ki no kwama nin cho ci fuwa ywelbo ki bwichi fiye Almasiya nine, yila ne bo nangen ywelka.
2CO 5:19 Mor Almasiya kwama fuwa ywel kale fiye chine neu, mani ki kiyeka bwiranke chiye dor chir. Dob binen tomange ywelka.
2CO 5:20 Nyo cin chokbo nob tomange Almasiya, nyo mwini kwama cho nuboti fiye bineneu. nyo ken komti ki ker Almasiya kom ywelum yimkumenbo kange kwama.
2CO 5:21 Cho chi fo Almasiya na yilam twika kunek ker bwiranker ber. cho nii mambo bwirangke wiye. Ma nyo na bo yilam wucak na kwama.
2CO 6:1 Bo man nangen do ti wari, maken kom yore, luma kwamako ki bilangiya.
2CO 6:2 Chon toki, ma nuwa fiya luma nawo neyu fuloka man tikankom, nawo luma, to na weu kakuk fuloka.
2CO 6:3 Nyo yobo ter kotangka nure kange nyo cwibo nangen nyero a yilamn abwir.
2CO 6:4 Nyori nyon nung dor nyero nangen nyeronin, nyo channgha kwma. nyon changa che fiye mwirumka, kalaka chotaka, dotange.
2CO 6:5 Bibukar, furcuna, kyan mor nangen kamboken, mor bwini dume kangem kumentin, mor wura.
2CO 6:6 Mor wucakke nyomka, birumne, ken mor yuwa tangbe wucakke, kange cwika na bilenkerce.
2CO 6:7 Nyon canga che mor bilenke, mor ciya kwama, nyo wiki kulen kwener na wucakke che kan nyek chatiyer kange mok.
2CO 6:8 Nyo ma nangenti mor bwayilene kange bwini bwayilene, koka, kange chaklangka. chi torang nyoti ki nyo nob bi bolere nyo gwam nyom nob bilenke.
2CO 6:9 Nyo ma nangen do ti tamwi chi nyom nyobo, wo nyo nyomom nyome, chine nyo ma nangenti na nubo bwiyam me, di wo nyo kwarche, nyo manangenti na nobo chi mwatiten bwolnage, dilakebo mwatika bwokang twalka.
2CO 6:10 nyo managenti na nubo ki fir nenerede, nyo ki fwor neret kangkang, nyo ma nangenti na no nob fuwayeb, wiki diker gwam.
2CO 6:11 Nyon yikom bilenke gwam korintiya ner nyero wumom wome.
2CO 6:12 Nyo kwarbo ner kumero, kom ko kwaryinen nerkumero.
2CO 6:13 Naweu mor cheltangka ko nyeu, ma tok kerti kange kom nyo nabi bei kom womyinen ner kumero.
2CO 6:14 Kom yiire wari kange nubo nebo bilenke, naniyak ye tiber wucakke kange bulange? kaka takeu naniyak yee tiber filanger kange kumtacile?
2CO 6:15 Chiyakankako wini tiber Almasiya kange bwekelkele? Yee mwerkang nubo ne bilenke kange nubo nebo bilenke?
2CO 6:16 Takeu, chiyakankako wini cheu. bonbikur waber kwamaro ki dume, nawo kwama tokeu, “Ma yii more chiye nan ya yam tiber chiyer.” ma yilam kwama chiye, chiyan yilam nobmib.
2CO 6:17 Nyori kom cheru fiye chinene kom chokum bwiko, “Nuwa teluwe kom teire diker kange mani wucakke, man yoo kom.
2CO 6:18 Man yilam Tee kumen, kom keneu kan yilam bibei bayilobe kange bibutob mi nen, nuwa Teluwe nii bi kwane gwam.
2CO 7:1 Cwika buti kambo bin wiki bilenkeu, nyori bi yulangum bwibeu ki dike wuro a knag binen bwibe tiyeu, kange bilenkebeu. Bido wucakeu mor tai kwama.
2CO 7:2 Kom nebo filang nyo kange bo ni kane nin ner nyo yobo kange min diker na bwirace kakka nyi ma kange min bwiran ker.
2CO 7:3 Kebo kiden yarka kumek mi tokki nyowo dike bwiyeu kweri min yikom miki komti wi neryer, nabi bwiya wari, nabi kweni wari.
2CO 7:4 Min wi ki tikali tiber kumer miki fuwor nerer kange kom.
2CO 7:5 Kom bo bi makidoniya bwibeu fiyabo fobka no tomo nyori, bin do mwar dotange ki nure mwanti kange kayaka nerek kace tai to yoyi nwi mor.
2CO 7:6 La kwama, ni dang neri kange tikali, cinnung dangne binen ki boka Titus.
2CO 7:7 kebo ki den boka cek koni kwam nung dangne ceu la ki boka Titus co nung dangne ce kimen. con nyinyo dotange cwika kimeko, fir nerer, cwemwer tikali kumero dormir. mo min ma fuwor nerer kambo ken.
2CO 7:8 Tano nyori tomange miyu, wo kange kimen ner, mi mabo naki min nyimin morece. La kambo mi nyimom tomange kang kimen nereu min ma naki min nyimi. di la kayaka ner kumro yabo kutam.
2CO 7:9 La Caneu miki fuwor nerer kebo kiden kayaka ner kimenro dila ki kayaka ner ner kumero bou kimen fuloka. kom fiyador kumer mwar tomange na wabice, dila kom yar bo ki den nyer.
2CO 7:10 Kambo kayaka nener fiye kwama wiyeu bouti ki fuloka wuro bouti nure na mani mwa tok nakimin nyimi morece.
2CO 7:11 Ki to kambo dotange fiye kwama wiyeu bokimen cuko more kume, Miki nung dike ner kumere kom mane kom manki bwirang ke. Miki nung biduyer funer kumero, tai kumero ki dokka ner kumero kange maka diker kumero, kange bilangka kom cwiti na makuman dikero kan! wi mor diker kom manti bwirang ke wiye.
2CO 7:12 Tano nyori mi mulang kumeneu mi mulangbo ki den nii bwirang ke. kaka ki den niwo ci manten bwirangkeu? ma mulang diker ner kumereu na fiyam fiye kwama nen.
2CO 7:13 Won cho dike bwiye nyo firkome, kebo mor nangeri nye, yila nyo ma Bilang ka kambo ken ki boka Titus ce ko.
2CO 7:14 Tano nyori mi kung dorti ki kabum cori, mi nuwabo kwenduwe. Wi nyo na cho dike wuro nyo yikome bilenke. Bilangka nyeka na kom to Titus yilam bilenke.
2CO 7:15 Cwika ceko kumen wiki bidwiyer kambo cho yo nerti ker bilenke kumenko gwameu, kambo kom nyocho ki tai kange mukangka bwiyeu, fuwor nerer mi dike bwiyeu fuwor nerer miyu nyoweu.
2CO 7:16 Min wiki bilenke kambo ken, nero win tai mani kange kom.
2CO 8:1 Bi cwiti bwibe na kom nyimom kebmibbo ki tikali kwama wo ci mane mor kuu wabee kwama Makidoniya.
2CO 8:2 Ki kwama dotange dur wo bouwe, filang fuwor nerer kange dotange bwini ciyeu wo bouki filang nake ki kang mor bilangkako
2CO 8:3 Kambo mi ne bilenke kom ne ki cwika kumek fiye fiyaka kume lame, kom ne cwika ko ki ciyaka mor nere kume.
2CO 8:4 Ki kinong ka ducce na fii nako noci neci filang wuro ciya yayamti mor bwangka kwama nubo manki dwikau.
2CO 8:5 Nyo bwiye kebo nawo nyo kwatiyeu, no tano nyori la cin ter neka dor cero wi Teluwe nen.
2CO 8:6 Di la nyon bwa bwiko Titus ce ko wuro kweri terum maka nange do kiden dii ka, nangendo wo mi neken biyare cunga kume.
2CO 8:7 Dila kom calam mwer diker kwarub, mor bilenke, mor kerer, mor nyumka, mor nangen manki luwaka mor cwika ki mek ki denyer. Tano nyori kom fiya saka kaba mor neka kumek.
2CO 8:8 Mi tok nyo kebo ki den mir kom ki, “bikwan” Tano ynori mi tok nyo nan cuwa bikwan cwika kumeko mi cuwati kange tanin yorka nubembo.
2CO 8:9 Dike bwiyeu kom nyimom ta kila Teluwe kristi Almasiya kambo nyeu ci ni cwika
2CO 8:10 Wi mor dikero wuro man neken yulando wo a tikan kom tiyeu. ki coru wo cumeu, kebo diker koni kom terer dila kom ma kuru na kom mani.
2CO 8:11 Can naweu kom takum kambo ki kaba kom nyoner kom mane ki kwama cure, dila kom ma kibwikom takum ki yulan birim maka kumeko.
2CO 8:12 Non wi nerkumer di, maka nangen do wori dikero ken yuk kumen tak tamnyo dong-dong dike nii cike kebo ki dike ci mani cikeu.
2CO 8:13 Ki den nangen dowo na tuu kumen na kangumbo na fiya yiber. Dila tano nyori na fiya yulang wi.
2CO 8:14 Cwika kumeko ki kwama wo caneu na fiya corka bwini. nyo tak cwika ciyeko na dol corka bwini ciyeko dike bwiyeu na fiya yulang ka?
2CO 8:15 Wii mulangum mulange ki wuro ciko ducce fiya bo dilka wi dikerwi yilo wuro cuka bi duware kebo diker wiin.
2CO 8:16 Dila buka kange fiye kwama wiye, na wii mor nere Titus ceu neneu Bilangka toka kumeko na yilam minen kumenen.
2CO 8:17 Nyo la kebo ka kinongka beko koni ci yowe dila ca ma kibi com dor cer. ki cwika nere cek.
2CO 8:18 Nyo tano kange yice wuro ci bilang chotiye mor tiber bikur wabe kwama kiden nangen cero wo mor ker bifumer cereu.
2CO 8:19 Kebo kiden do wuro ki kwacho, kiden nubo bikur wabe kwama, na cin ya kange ci fiye dike cho bwi wiyeu. Won cho durko chi ne kwama kange cwika beko.
2CO 8:20 Nyo ki cwa kati yilo kange ni dok nyenti bwirang ke wi mor tikali kume nen.
2CO 8:21 Won cwika yek na nyo ma diker kebo kabum Teluwe ki kwaco, Dila kabum nubem bo ken.
2CO 8:22 Nyo yila nyo tom yii ye wari kange cii kutangi ki cuwaka cek. tak nyo fiya co ki tikali kambo ken. can neu tak cin wiki bikwan fiye mo wiyeu.
2CO 8:23 Dila Titus far nangenne mi, kange nii nangene mwe. Chi bibei tomange chi twom che.
2CO 8:24 Tano nyoriKom nug cinen cwika kumeko kati yilo tak nakom nung bikur wabero dike bwi fuwor nerer kumeu wari kange kumeu
2CO 9:1 Kiden nangen kwama na nubo buro manki dwitiye kebo na cho minen na mulang mwen.
2CO 9:2 Min nyumom kuru kume wuro mi ma kungka dor cike kabum nubo Makidoniya. Min nyikom ki choro wo cumeu kweri chi yim ki bati kero. Bikwan kumero kangem kumembo doo maka nangen.
2CO 9:3 Di naweu min twom kumen kebbebo na kati yilo kung ka dorek kumeko kati yilam manki tuwerker cer. dike bwiyeu nakom yim ki bati kambo ma yi kom noo ka matiye.
2CO 9:4 No tano mani nyori, no kange mor Makidoniya bwangum ten con yumom kom yibo ki batiri, mani nya nuwa kwenduweti na kange kume dike bwiyeu.
2CO 9:5 Dila ma to nyori daten di tung kebmibbo ciya bo kumen kati yilo kwama kene lam. Kom yulangum ki den dike kom yoo nerkumereu. Yilam nyo dike bwiyeu na ywelum kiden neka diker na chaka kabace kebo diker charikar kibikwan.
2CO 9:6 Kero wuro niwo fii -fik ki cwika chekeri a biye ki cwika cek, Niwo fii-fik nero keneri a biye ki caklangka.
2CO 9:7 Gwam kume ka merang kambo kom cwi mor nere kumeu. Mani mwa neti ki kangka nererk yilo tamwi ci dok nen ki bikwan, La nyo kwama ki cwi niwo ne ki nero fuwor.
2CO 9:8 Kwama wi ki bikwan dog ka dike kom nerangeu, na bwiki den kumer, dikero bwiyeu mwo dikero nin gwam, kom fiya na yilam kiden kumer kange nangen kumer.
2CO 9:9 Nyo na wuro ci mulange, ti kan cwika ceko, ne kiden nubo mani cekeu, liyaro wi man ki diker.
2CO 9:10 Ki nii wo doh dum diker na fiiyeu chati fiya chari, la chan fiya dum dikembo ducce wo cha fiitiye. chati yuk nubo ki bilenke nenten ki kwama biyeka kange nubo manki bwarangkeu.
2CO 9:11 Mwan fiya diker kangek fiyentano mwa ma diker wiyeu, wuro a yilam ki buka kangek kwama fiye nyo wiyeu.
2CO 9:12 Maka nangen nebo kebo ka wo mwa ma nubo wo cwitiyeu, kange nubo ne bilenke tiyeu. Manten ki nure wo mwa buo kwama nen kang tiyeu.
2CO 9:13 Dike bwiyeu chin cuwam nen, chin ciya kange nangen mwero mwan fiya chalangka kwama ki bilenke mweu kange yiloka mweko fiye wabe kiristi. mwan chaklang kwama tak.
2CO 9:14 Chiya kwob kumen dilo kange bilangtum dikero kom maneu.
2CO 9:15 Buka kangek kwama nen ki dike bwiyeu neka cheko kabum chem kange fwetang ka cheko.
2CO 10:1 Mo Bulus ki bwimi ma kenan komti ki lomchome kange dangne Alamsiya. man wii ki tiber duwe fiya ma wari kange komme. Di ma ki bikwan bwiyer kumen fiya ma man wari kange kom me.
2CO 10:2 Ma ken komti fiya ma wari kange kom me, ma chwibo yilam ki kun ka duwek, Di ma toti man do na yilam nii kibikwan bwiyer, fiya ma kwabkanti kange nubo wo kwati tamwi nyo yim mor bwiye.
2CO 10:3 Bwen duwal boki yaa mor bwiye, kwen bero kebo na bwiye che bo matiye.
2CO 10:4 Kulen kwenero bwo timti chikeu kebo na bwiyale che, nyiyo chuwa, kulen kwener kwamar kibi kwan bukchanka bikwanti bwekelkele, chi tungum kwobkanka wo bouti ki tiyanka.
2CO 10:5 Bo bukchangum dikero ti gwam, wo ma kiyeti kange nyomka kwama. Bota bulanka kowo boti ki nuwaka Almasiya.
2CO 10:6 Bo yimki bati na bo warum nagen na kwenduwe ce,
2CO 10:7 To dike chi yo kabum kume twelume. Tano kange cho nyomom na Almasiya che cha kulom dorcero nin kambo cho na Almasiya che, kambo nyo, nyokene.
2CO 10:8 Bwen man kwila-nge ki bikwando nyo chike, wo Teluwe nee nye be na nyo firkom, kebo na nyo werum kom chiko, mani ma nuwa kwenduweti.
2CO 10:9 Ma chwibo tamwi maki nekom tai kibi fumer miro.
2CO 10:10 Ka-ngem nob yiti ki, bifumer chero kibikwan kange neeka taiyek, di mo too chori mwini man kibi kwan, ker chero kebo na nuwaka che.
2CO 10:11 Nubo chuwo na nyimom, kero nyo tokti morbifumer fiya nyo maniye, nyo nya matiye tano nyo wiri.
2CO 10:12 Nyeu nyo mwerbo dor nyer kan-nge niikan-nge chaklang dor chertiye, dila chi nungkan dor cherti bwiti chi, chi manki nyomka.
2CO 10:13 Di la ma nyo kwilang bwiti chum bikwane, nyo cho nya ma chwati dike kwama yo nyo mane, kambo a lamti kume neu.
2CO 10:14 Di la nyo chubo kambo nyo lam kumene. Nyo kabako nyo lam kumen ki fulen keret Almasiya.
2CO 10:15 nyo kwilang bo bwi wo chum bikwane ki nagen ka-ngem nob nyeu nyo chwiti bilenke kume na yokten, na chunga nangen nyero womten kamboken, dong dong yika cheko nin.
2CO 10:16 Nyo chwiti na chuwo na nyo yaken ki fulen keretdo, yarentinimbo kab kan-nge kommeu, mani nya kwilan bwiti beti ki nangen do ma fiye nii kan-nge che.
2CO 10:17 Di gwam wo na a kwilang bwitiyeri, cha ma mor Teluwe.
2CO 10:18 Kan -nge nii man wo a war dor chero ninti cho chiya-chiya. Di na wori, la kawo Teluwe warker dor chereu.
2CO 11:1 ma cwiti kom bwam neerkumer kange mo mor kulene bidom bwentano duwal kom bwaneer ti kange meu.
2CO 11:2 Wori min ma korti ker kumer, kor miro na kwama ce kumeno na korti ker tu kumen mor naka nii na baroko wiyeu. Man tum nor na nung kom na bubiya cak-cak kabum Yesu.
2CO 11:3 La ma cha tai kumeti kangeri nawo nasuwe boul hauwau weu, ki yulan cereu, yilo neer kumero yilam neka duweko kendo Alamsiya nin.
2CO 11:4 kangeri, nii kange bouki fulen Yesuro kange kebo wo yi komker dor cereri, kaka kom yo yuwa tangbe kange ki dimen kange wo ka yo kabari, kangeri, kom yo fulen kero kange ki dimen kange wo ka yo ki kabau, ciyakako ma dike biro ninenu lam.
2CO 11:5 Min kwatiri, min kebo bwiko wo mor nubo biro choti ki nob tomangebo dure.
2CO 11:6 Bwen tano ci merang bo tokka keret di, ma manki bwini mwerum mor kiyeka. Ki nure gwam la dike bro gwam nyon kwulum kumen.
2CO 11:7 Mama bwirang ke ka wori man cwuwe kangum dor miro na ko fiya duktangka? wori man yi kom ker kwamaro koni.
2CO 11:8 Man ma tangnim kumenbo kuwabembo nin kwi kiyoka tikali ko cinen nan makumen nangen chiko.
2CO 11:9 Fiya co mikange komeu min fiya dor miro cwika ma yobo kange nii nin tuuka. wori kebbebo bou Makidoniya cor min bwini mito mor die gwam nin cokum dor mir katinyila kumen tu'u tum. Man ca kaba ki makanyo.
2CO 11:10 Na wo bilenke Almasiya more miyeu, mani ma kwomti ki tokka kowo mor biten Akaya gwam.
2CO 11:11 Ye bwiye? wori ma cwikomba? kwama yumom.
2CO 11:12 dike ma maneu, ma makan co cuwo. Man ma nyo na kisim nubo bro cwiti na cin fiya filang na ci yilam na nyo mor dike bro ci kung dor ti cikeu.
2CO 11:13 Nubo bro nob tomange cwerke, nob bibouler, ci tu dor cero ti na nob tomange Almasiya.
2CO 11:14 Won diker nyuman kar wori bwikelkele tu dor cer na nii tomange wucake filang.
2CO 11:15 Kebo diker nyumankaro dur na canga ce an tu dor cer na canga cak-cakeri, bwiko ciko a yila dong dong kange dike ci maneu.
2CO 11:16 man yokten tokkako. Kange a tuyere na kule, na kom kwa neer nyori, ko tuye min kule nan kungum dor ciko bi dob.
2CO 11:17 Dike ma tokti dor woreu kab-kab ni kung dor tiyeu kebo ki ciya Teluwek, la maki tok kero na kule.
2CO 11:18 Nubo ducce kung dor ti mor bwiye, man kungi ken.
2CO 11:19 Ko bilangti na ko mwerkang kange kuletini, kom nob yileneb.
2CO 11:20 Kom ma dangne ti kange wo a yilam komti cangau, naco yilakangum komri, coki ma nangen ki kom na co fiya, na co kung dor cer di, kaka co kwa kom ki kang ka tikob.
2CO 11:21 man nii tok ka nyon nuwa kwenduwe wo nya fiya bo bi kwan na nyo kumen nyeu.
2CO 11:22 Cin Yahudawa ka? mo kenenu nyo. cin Israilawaka? mo keneu nyo. Cin Naniyak Ibraniyawak ka? mou keneu nyo.
2CO 11:23 Cin canga Almasiyak ka? man tok kero ti mwini ma man mor nee mi. man la ci. man ma nangen kibi kwan ki Fusuna, kibi buker man ki kiyeka, ki toka bwarek ko wo kila kilau.
2CO 11:24 Kom yahudawa Kristi to nung ci malliye kwini naar win mani.
2CO 11:25 Kiristi ta'ar ci mwek kangeye ki dange. kirito win ci mobang ye ki tere, kiriti ta'ar nabire mwenge win mor ki me. man dam kume win kan diye win mor wima.
2CO 11:26 Man nuwa ki yarang ka yamek, mor dotange caji mor kishika nob kubek. Mor dotange fiye nob mibo wiyeu, kange dotange fiye nob kumtacille neneu, dotange mor cinan lore, dotange mor yerake, mor dotange wima, dotange yitob cwerkebe nin.
2CO 11:27 Man fiya dorminro nagen do bwaiye ki mukki mor kume ni kila manki dum, mor wura kange dilo mwe, mor yim dilomwem, mor dula kange bwini kulen tukar.
2CO 11:28 Kebo kawo tukako wi dor mir kito tes ki kwomka duwemiko dor ku wabetini.
2CO 11:29 We yibere, lami ma yilabo yiber dor cere? we ci dokco yare di, buwa yebe?
2CO 11:30 Na man kun dor di ma kung dor ki dike nung bwini bikwane mitiyeu.
2CO 11:31 Kwama kange Teluwe Yesu Kristi wo chin wab bakeu, nyumom kebo cwerke ma cwere.
2CO 11:32 Mor Dimaskus nii durko tam ciko tob kange liya Aistas doki a to cinan loro Aristaseti na ci tamye.
2CO 11:33 La ci do kuye cerange mor bulene ci meru ye bwilom cinan loro, nimre ma ceri kange ceke.
2CO 12:1 man kung dor miro bwenno manki yokka dikereu, la man ca kaba ki dukum bo yau Teluwe wemineneu.
2CO 12:2 man nyumom kange mor kiristi, coti to kwob cilombo na'ar cumeu, keno mor bwiyeri, keno kebo mor bwiye ri, ma nyombo, kwama nyome. Cin tum co yaken chiko dii no bwiri keno mani bwiri, kwama nyumom.
2CO 12:3 La man nyumom niiwo, keno kino bwiri keno mani bwiri, kwama nyumom.
2CO 12:4 Cin tum co yaken kico firen kwechang la con nuwa duktangka dikero brombo nii dol min tokka.
2CO 12:5 Ki ker nii wo man kung dor, la ki ker mir mani ma kung dor ti. Na kebo ker cune mirdi.
2CO 12:6 Na ma cwiti na kung dor di, mani ma yila kule ti, wori ma tokka bilenke. La man dubom kung ka duweko, na kange nii kware ki mo cum dike co tomineneu kange wo ca nuwa mineu.
2CO 12:7 Man cwam kung ka duwenin ki dukumbo kwamero bro. cwiyak mor bwiye neye, nii tomange bwekelkele nin na neye dotange, nan kung re dor minro.
2CO 12:8 Kirito ta'ar ma ken Teluwe ti dor wuro na co tum wo minen.
2CO 12:9 La yiye, luma miko cuwa mwenti la mor cune bikwan ki dire. la ma tum kungka duwek mor cunermi. Na bikwan Kristi ro na yiti minen.
2CO 12:10 La nyeu, cuwamenti mor cune, mor cuwe kangka mor dotange kuka kange bwentano fiyang ma kwaberi, ma kwamer.
2CO 12:11 man yilam kule kom ko dok ye nye. na daten fiya caklangka kumeen. Wori ma kebo bwiko mor nob tomange bo, bwentano ma kebo diker duwaleu.
2CO 12:12 nangen nob tomangebo mani more kume, ki dangne, yirom kange nyumanka.
2CO 12:13 Ma nyi ka yila kwame mor kuni wabeninen, wori ma tu'u kumenbo ka?
2CO 12:14 Ko to man ywelbwi nan bou kumen kiriti ta'areu, mani ma tuu kumenti, la ma dike kange wo na kumeu, kom ma cwitiye, la kebo bibei ayo tebbonin tiye, teb anyo bibeiyo nin tiye.
2CO 12:15 Man bilangi tikangkom bwen tam neken dume miri, na man cwikomdi. mo ka cwiti bi dobeka?
2CO 12:16 La na wo nyeu, ma tuu kumenbo kambo man nii yulaneu, mo ma buol kome.
2CO 12:17 La man tuu kumen ki kange yibe ma tunguwe?
2CO 12:18 man ken Titus na ya kumen, La man twom kebe wine na ya kange co. Titus tuu kumena? kebo mor yuwa tangbe ko win bo yati kange kome? kebo mor na win bo yati kange kome?
2CO 12:19 Kom kwa tiri na kwome wo nyoki wengang dor nyer kumena? kabum kwamam, mor Kristi nyo yikom dikero ti gwam na ko fiya bikwan.
2CO 12:20 Man cwa kati yilo yari ma fiya kom bo nawo ma cwitiyeu. Ma cwati mani ka fiya yeti na wo ko cwitiyeu. man cwa kwalkange an no wi, kange kor, kungka funerek, cwika duwek, cuwarum, kungka duwek, kange bwini nuwa kangka.
2CO 12:21 Mati cwai bwikowo na yilameri, kwama ni an cukumye kabum kumeu. maticwai man ma fir neerer wori, nubo ducce ma bwiran ke nimre nawo. brombo yilo ten bo bwini wucakeu kange burotum kange kayatum kange nangen dilaka wo ci manue.
2CO 13:1 Won cho kero to ta'areu ma yati kumeneu boki, ciya doka nak nyi nob warkeb yob kaka ta'ar.
2CO 13:2 Kweri man tolum kero bwi dor nobero ma bwiran keu kange tangimbo fiya fiya ce mi kange kom ki yanminbo yobeu, yila ma tokten ti. Nan yilatendi mani ma kwob cinen.
2CO 13:3 ma yi kom woti wori, kom do warke ti, kerenkrsiti tok ker ti ki nyini yeri. Co kebo nii dilime fiye ko wiye. la nyeu con nii bikwane more Kume.
2CO 13:4 Wori ci kulkenco mor dilimka, la co ki dume ki bi kwan kwamar. Bo keneu bo nob dilimeb more ce, la ban yi ki dume kange co mor bikwan kwamar wo more kumeu.
2CO 13:5 Ko cuwa kumero na ko to kano kom ki no mor bilenkerer di. ko ma dor kumero min cuwaka. Ka to bo ki bati Yesu wi more kume ka? wi more kume ati kawo na ci ciya kange kom di.
2CO 13:6 Beri min wi ki bi kwan neerer ko fiya cin ciya nyo.
2CO 13:7 Ma kwob dilo kwama min mani ci a fiya kom ti ki bwireanke. Ma kenbo na fwetangum ki bon cam cuwakako wo. La nyeu ma ki kwob dilo ko ma dike dong dongeu. Na duwal mani mwini nyo to kum cuwakakeu.
2CO 13:8 Wori nyo nyombo maka kange diker yilam kwob kang ka kange bilen kere. La nyo ki ma na bilenkero ce.
2CO 13:9 Nyoki fuwor neerer na yokomdi kom wi kibi kwan, nyo kwob diloti na kom takom.
2CO 13:10 Ma mulange dike buro fiya cho ma man kange komeu, kambo na makange komeri, mani yila kumen nii tokka ti. Ma cwibo ma nangen ki bikwan do wo kwama neyereu nan yalkangum, la ma mukom muu.
2CO 13:11 Cuwa bwir tiyeu yitobmibo kom ma fuwor neerer kom ma nangen wo fwinno ceu, ko na ma bikwan, ko ciya ki bwiti ko yi yim mor fuwor neere, La kwama cwika kange fuwor neerer an yi kange kom.
2CO 13:12 Kom yarum bwiti ki neero wucakeu.
2CO 13:13 Nubo bwang kwama nin tiyeu yarum komti gwam.
2CO 13:14 Luma Teluwe be Yesu, kange cwika kwamak, kange mwerkanka duwek yuwa tangbe cek, ciya yi kange kom gwam.
GAL 1:1 Bulus nii tomange-kebo nii tomange nobbe kaka tomange ceu bou bo nii kange nin, dila bou Yecu kiritti nin kange Kwama Tee, wo kungum co bwareu-
GAL 1:2 Kange yitubbo mine neu gwam, ki bi kur wabero Galatiya:
GAL 1:3 Luma Kwamako kumeneu kange dam nerem bo Kwama nin Tēe Teluwe be Yecu Kiritti,
GAL 1:4 wo neken neken dorcero ker bwirang kere be ri na ci cēer bo fo ki kaldo bwirko ko wo nineu, ki cwika Kwama kange Teebe,
GAL 1:5 duktangka na ca diri. Ati nyo.
GAL 1:6 Min nyimang ki dob kako wulom-wulom ko dubom co, wo cuwo kom ki luma nere Yesu. Min nyimangi kambo ko yilaken ti fulen kerero kangeu,
GAL 1:7 Kebo wori fullen kere ro kange wiki dimen dila nubo kangenbo wii buro cwiti naci kungkumen nere di ci cwiti naci kangum fullen kerer Kiritti.
GAL 1:8 Dila bwenno nyo kaka nob tomangebo dii Kwamau yikom fullen kerero kangeti kebo wo nyi yikome ri cilkako a bwang cinen ten.
GAL 1:9 Nawo nyi yi kom fiya ceu, yila ma yikom ti nawo tak, “Tano kange yikom fullen kerer Kwamar ki dimen kange wo kom yowe ri ca yilam wo cilim cileu.”
GAL 1:10 La miki do nan fiya ciyaka fiye nubo wiye kakaa Kwama nin ka? La miki do ciyaka fiye nubo wiye ka? No naeu duwal mado nami fiya ciyaka fiye nubo wiyeri, mike bo bwe canga Kiristi.
GAL 1:11 Wori ma cwiti ko nyimom, keb-mibbo, kom ki fulen kerero wo ma tok tiyeu kebo fulen kerer niir.
GAL 1:12 Ma yobo kange nii nin, kakaa cii merang men merang. Nyori, mor dukume Yecu Kiritti bou minene.
GAL 1:13 Kom nuwam ker dor yime miu fiya cuwo ma bwangten dām Yahudawam bo tiyeu, kambo mane nob bwangka Kwama dotange ti cum bi kwaneu kange kambo ma cwi nami yālangum cii yeu.
GAL 1:14 Min ya kaba mor yim Yahudawam bo nin min la kalti miro, duce mor nubo lomeu. Min wiki kor nere ro Cuum bi kwaneu ker bwangka yimer teb mibo.
GAL 1:15 Dila kambo Kwama, wo cok ye fiyaco mi fwer nee mireu, kange co wo cuwo ye mor luma nere ceke,
GAL 1:16 Cin ciya cin nung men bibwece nami yi nubo kumtacilieu ker cer, fiyaco dangcang ma dobo nyomka nii ki nange kange bwiyale nin.
GAL 1:17 Ma yabo Urusalima nubo buro yilam ten nob tomangeb Kwama minene nin. Nyori min yaken Arabia nimde ma yila ken Dimaska.
GAL 1:18 La kambo coro ta'ar cumeri min yaken Urusalima nami fiya nyomka Kefas se, min yi kange co kume Kwob cilombo nung.
GAL 1:19 La ma tobo kange wiin wo mor tangnum nob tomange no kebo ka Yakubu, yi Tee-luwebe Yecu ri.
GAL 1:20 Mor dikero ma mulang kime neu, mayi kom ti kabum Kwama kebo cwerke ma cwer tiye.
GAL 1:21 Dila min yaken biten Suriya kange Kilikiya.
GAL 1:22 Duwal kange ci nyom ye bo tikom mor nubo nebilenke Kiritti nin Yahudiya.
GAL 1:23 Ciki nuwa nubo ki toki,”nii wo no fiyaco nēbo dotange nyeu, naweu yila ne fullen ker bilenkero no fiyaco ci cwi naci kangum me ti.”
GAL 1:24 La ciin duktang kwama ker miir.
GAL 2:1 La bwiko coro kwob cilombo na'ar di min yaken tak Urusalima kange Barnabas, min tuten Titus kange mo.
GAL 2:2 Ma kwiwi ker dukumero Kwama nung men neu, la man yi cii fullen kerero ma tok ti more nubo kumtacili yeu. miin tok yuuke kange buro cii toti nubo dur more ciyeu, nami nung cii nen ma cwabo-kakaa ma cwabo koni.
GAL 2:3 Dila ki Titus ce wo wari kange meu, wo Baheline, ma dok cobo biyeka tē- lāk ki bi kwan.
GAL 2:4 Keb bebo cwerke ceu dou binen kebo ki nyomka bek naci tō fang kakowo ba fiya Yesu Kiritti nineu. Ciin cwi naci yilam ki bo cangab,
GAL 2:5 Dila nyi cuwabo tuu cinen ki biduware ce na bilenke fulen kerero fiya yim kimen.
GAL 2:6 La buro yilam nubo dur reu (bwenno ciin yē ri kwom ye bo, Kwama mani nung cwika dorek)- buro, miki, wo toti ciin nubo dureu, cobmen ten bo dikero kange.
GAL 2:7 Nyori, ciin tori Kwama neye fulen ker cero nan yi nubo wo biyebo tē lareu, nawo ci ne Bitrus fuien kerero naci ne nubo biyem tē lareu.
GAL 2:8 Wori Kwama, wo manangen ki Bitrus na yilam nii tomange nubo biyem tē lareu, manangen minen ken ki nubo kubtacili nin.
GAL 2:9 Ki Kwama wo Yakubu, Kefas, kange Yohanna wo cii tociti na nubo wo bou ki duwika mor nob bilenkerebo nineu, nyumom luma Kwamako wo cii neyere ri, ciin mwerkan kang, kange Barnabas kange mo. Cii ma wuro ri nanyi yaken nye nubo kumtacili nin ri naci yaken ciye ki nubo biyem tē lare ce nin.
GAL 2:10 Ciin ken nyo na nyi ƙwa nob fuwabbo ki ner, dikero no ma cwiti maneu.
GAL 2:11 Dila fiyaco Bitrus bou Antakiyau, Miin kwinang ci nenten wori ci mabo dong-dong.
GAL 2:12 Nimde nubo kangem bo bou Yakubu nin di, Kefas ca cariti kange nubo kumtacileu. Dila kambo nubo cuwo dou weri, cin dubom, ri cin cerum wi nubo kumtacili nen. Ciki nuwa tai nubo wo cwi biyeka te lare tiyeu.
GAL 2:13 Tangni Yahudawa buro wāri kangeceu bwangten nero bwir ko wuro ken.
GAL 2:14 La kambo ma to dikero ci maneu bwangtenbo bilenke fulen kere reri, mnyi Kefas kabum ciyem gwam,” No mwin nii Yahudiya dila mwi yi yim mwemboti na nii kumtacile, la kebo na nii Yahudiya ri, mwa dok nubo kumtacile nyi kibi kwan na cii yi na Yahudawa?
GAL 2:15 Bo biki bwibo bin Yahudawa ki bor, la bi kebo nubo kumtacili nob bwirang kebeu;
GAL 2:16 La bwanno bin nyimom nii mania fiya cērka ki nangen bolangere, dila a fiya ki neka bilenke Yesu Kiritti nin. Bo keneu bin ne bilenke Kiritti Yesu nin di nabi fiya ceerka ki bilenke Kiritti nin dila kebo ki nangen bolanger. Ki nangen bolanger nii kange mani wo a fiya ceerka tiye.
GAL 2:17 La no, kambo bi cwi nabi fiya cērka Kiritti nineu, bo keneu, bin fiya dor bero nob bwirangkeb ken, La Kiritti ki bwa bwiko bwirangke ra? O-ong, kebo nyo!
GAL 2:18 La tano nyila muuti dikero no ma wurongum ki ƙaba ri, min nung dormiro min nii bwirangke.
GAL 2:19 Wori kifiye bolangko wiyeu, ma bwiya bwar bolanger, ri nami yi yim Kwama.
GAL 2:20 Ciin kulken ye kange Kirist. Kebo mo ma yim me, la Kiristi yim mi nene. Yimbo ma yim mor curen bwiyer mireu ma yim ki bilenke bi Bwe Kwama nin, wo cwiye ri neken dorcero ker mireu.
GAL 2:21 Ma yoken bo luma Kwama ko cungaken, wori no atin fiya cak-cake ki bwangka bolangeri, Kiristi bwiya bwaro bwir
GAL 3:1 Kom Galatiyawa nubo man ki yulaneu! we tum yulan kimere? Kebo Yesu kiristi wo cii kulkene cii nungi kabum nuwe kima?
GAL 3:2 Wo co dikero wiin cwar macwiti merangi kimeneu: Kom yo yuwa tangbeko ki nangen bolanger kakaa ki nuwaka ker bilenkerer?
GAL 3:3 Bwini yulan kimero lam nya? Kom ter ki yuwa tangbe, la na weu kom cwi na kom takum ki bwiya?
GAL 3:4 Kom nuwa dotange dikero ducce koniya-no kibi com koni ri?
GAL 3:5 Co wo ne kom yuwa tangbe Kwamako ri yila marang diker nyimanka more kimeu ma nyo ki nangen bolanger kakaa ki nuwaka ki kibelenke?
