GAL 3:6 Nawo Ibraim “ne bilenke Kwama nin di cii kiye cinenti na cak-cakeu,”
GAL 3:7 Ki nure wo ken ko nyimom, komki buro ne bilenkeu, bi beyo lo Ibraim me.
GAL 3:8 Bifumero tom towe kabumbo Kwama atin ceer nubo kumtacileu ki bilenke, yi Ibraim fullen kere wulom, ciki,” Mwinen, dor bitinero gwam atin fiya bi bwiyer.”
GAL 3:9 La, buro ki bilenkeu, fiya bi bwiyer wari kange Ibraim, nii ki bilenke.
GAL 3:10 Gwam buro citen nuwe ti ki nangen bolangeri, ciki no mor cilka; la nyo mulangum-mulange, “Nii cii cilom cile wo bwangtenbo dikero gwam wo mulangum mor diker mulanka bolange, ri ci mā cii beu.
GAL 3:11 Na weu bin tom yanglang nii kange mani wo fiya ceerka kabum Kwama ki bwangka bolange ke, wori nii wo cak-cakeu atin fiya dume ki bilenke.
GAL 3:12 La bolanko kebo na neka bilenke ko ce la,”Nii wo manangen bolanger tiyeu tam ca yi ki cii.
GAL 3:13 Kiristi fang bo mor cilka bolange ki wo ci yilam wo cii cilim cileu ker ber-la mulangum-mulange, “Nii ci cilom cile wo cii kulken dor bwatiyere”-
GAL 3:14 La na bi bwiyer Ibrahim mero na bou nubo kumtacili nin Yecu Kiriti nin, di nayi lam ki bilenke batin yo nor yuwa tangbeko ceu.
GAL 3:15 Keb mibo, miki tok kero ki diro nii firo ciya cikeu. Bwenno nor nii tu naci mā ne ri, mani ci dobti kakaa ci cobten diker ti dorcer no cin dokum kang noro curo nin di.
GAL 3:16 Naweu noro ci mam ki Ibrahim kange naniya ciyek. Tokbo ki,” naniya tini”, wo nungti ki kila-kilau, dila wiin cwar, “La ki naniya mwek,” wo co Kiristi yeu.
GAL 3:17 Naweu dike ma tok tiyeu co wo: Bolankawo bou ki coro 430 cumeu, la dobbo noro wo Kwama tū ki ƙabau.
GAL 3:18 Na no kwalito bou binen ki bolang di, ci bou bo ki nor tak. Dila Kwama ne Ibrahim ki nor.
GAL 3:19 Nye dike bwi cii ne bolanke? Cii cob ten ki ker bwiranke kumeu nyimde naniyak Ibrahim meko bou, wo ker cer Kwama ne noreu. La bolanko cii neu kang nob tomangebo dii kwama kange nii wo tim tibereu. Naweeu, wo tim tibereu ki nung nii cuum wiin, dila Kwama wiin.
GAL 3:21 La bolangko ki ma kiye kange nor Kwamar ka? Kebo nyo, kibi duware ce! Nano ki ciin ne bolangko kange wo ane dume tiyeri, lano cak-cakeu an bou ki bolang ko wuro nin.
GAL 3:22 La bifumer Kwama ro ƙuken dikero gwam kang bwiran ke nin. Kwama ma wuro nyo ri naci nebo nor cēr ka beko ki neka bilenke Yecu Kiristi ninneu na neken nubo ne bilenkeu.
GAL 3:23 na nimde bilenke bou ri, ciin bwambo ki bolang, bi kum-kuwe, nimde bilenkeu cerkangu.
GAL 3:24 La bolangko yilam wo corbo tiye na nimde Kiristi bou, ri nabi fiya cerka ki bilenke.
GAL 3:25 Dila na weu bilenkeu bekenneu, bi mani kang nii corkak tak.
GAL 3:26 La kom gwam bi bei Kwamak ki bilenke ko ne Kiritti Yecu nineu.
GAL 3:27 Gwam buro cii yuten mwem Kwama ko mor Almasiyau, kom duum bwiki meu ki Kiristi yesu.
GAL 3:28 Bwe Yahudiya mani more kime kakaa Bwe Helene, canga mani kakaa wo kebo cangau, nii nabare mani kakaa nawiye, la kom gwam wiin mor Kiristi Yesu.
GAL 3:29 No kom na Kiristi ce ri, kom naniya Ibrahim mek, nob kwalib ki noro.
GAL 4:1 mikitok miki tano nii kwale bwe biduware, cimanki dimen kange can-nge, bweno kwalito gwam naceu.
GAL 4:2 Dila ciki no kange nob corkab kange nubo cii ciya cikeu na nyime kumewo tece dan-ngeu.
GAL 4:3 Boken, ki kwama bin bibeyeu ciintambo mor cangab kikulentini kaleweu.
GAL 4:4 Dila kambo kiini diim dong-dong ri, Kwama tomou bi bwece mor boka nawiye bo mor bola-nge.
GAL 4:5 cimawo naci yialamkibo bi beyo loce.
GAL 4:6 Lawori kom bibei, Kwama twomuu yuwatangbe bibweceko mor nere kume wocotiki,”Abba Te.”
GAL 4:7 La mukebo ca-nga tak, mu yilam bwe, lano mun bweri, munwi mor nubo acakwali kwama rotiyeu.
GAL 4:8 dila kikiinico, nokm nyombo kwamau, komyilam ca-ngab kibwanka fulenekowo kebo diker bwankareu.
GAL 4:9 Lanaweu kom nyimom kwamau, kakaa nawo kwama nyimom komeu, yebwi kom yilaken mor yikumembo ficeu mani atikangkomtiye? komki cwinakom yilam ca-ngab taka?
GAL 4:10 Ka nyimom kume kange cwakko fwir kange cwakiya kange cor!
GAL 4:11 Kom neye tai, katiyilo na-ngen miro more kumeu yilam dotange koni.
GAL 4:12 Mikenkomti kebmibo, kom yilam namo, wori mokeneu min yilam nakom. kom mamenbo bwiranke.
GAL 4:13 Dila kom nyimm kerbwini nuwaka luma bwiye dokye min yikom fulen kerero kikaba.
GAL 4:14 Bwenno bwini luma bwiye miko dokkom mor cuwaka duwaleu, kom dobyebo kakaa kom dobyebo. Nyiyoco komyoye na nii toma-nge kwama, na yesu kiristi kibwico.
GAL 4:15 Labibwiyer kumero kinofe naweu? minyikom miki, cwika fiyakari, komki cika-ngu nuwetin kumero koneye.
GAL 4:16 Lamiyilam nii kiye kume wori miyikom bilenke tiya?
GAL 4:17 Cii dotiki korneret na cii kwobken kom fiye cii wiye, dila kebo nalumace. Cii cwiti na cii cokumkom nyinen nakom yilanken cii nen.
GAL 4:18 Yori kabo nii ayilamkikor kang-kang dor diroken, ayilare nomiwari kange komri nyime.
GAL 4:19 Bibeyolomi bidwartinim, minuwa dotange bore bwetitak ker kumer, no kiristi fiyam yim kumendi nyime.
GAL 4:20 Mincwi nanno wari ka-nge kom naweu, nan fulo-ngumg diirmiro wori man fiya kwomka ducce kerkumer.
GAL 4:21 Komyiye komwo komcwiti na balango ma liyar dorkumereu, manikom cuwa tuuri bolango ninna?
GAL 4:22 Mula-ngum mula-nge Ibrahimwiki bibeyo yob wiin bubiya ca-nga nin la wiin nawiye ki cheerkanin.
GAL 4:23 Wineu nawiye ca-nga bo morbwiye, dila wineu na norece nawiye cheerka nin.
GAL 4:24 Nii atintokker dor dikero bironin na dangke, naweu natubo biro yobem kidang nor. Wiin morecee bou bang sinai labo bibeyo birombo ca-ngab be. Wo Hazaratu.
GAL 4:25 Hazaratu ki dang bang sinai wuro Arabiya; ciki dang wurusalima tak wori cikio mor ca-nga wari ka-nge bibwece
GAL 4:26 Dila wurusalima wo diyeu fiya ceerka, cin nebe tak.
GAL 4:27 Mula-ngum mula-nge,”Bila-ngi mwo cwombilome wo bombo bwe wiyeu. Kun diir namob biyalte, mwo wuro nuwambo buwarum bwem wiyeu. Wori bibei nawiye cii koweu la nawiyewo ki bwayile ceu kilaka.”
GAL 4:28 Dila kom, kebmibo, na Ishaku bibei nore.
GAL 4:29 fiyaco wo cii bo mor bwiyeu ne wuro cii bo mor yuwatangbekeu dota-nge. Kini nyo naweu.
GAL 4:30 Dila ye bifumer Kwama ro tokke?”Ywabken bubiya ca-nga ka-nge bibwece. Wori bibwe bubiya ca-nga mani a ca kwaliti ka-nge bibwe nawiye ceerkati.”Nyori, kebmibo, kebo bibei ca-ngab bubiyak, dila nawiye ki ceerka.
GAL 5:1 Ker ceerka kiristi in ceerbo. Ko tikibi kwan, kociyare komyilam de ca-ngab fiye bolango wiye tak.
GAL 5:2 Komto, mo Bulus miyikomti, nokom ciya cii biye kumen lardi, kiristi mani yilati ki tikali fiye kom wiyeu gwam.
GAL 5:3 Nyotak miyi nubo wiyak wociya cii biye cinen lareu tamco dor can bwangten bolango wiyak.
GAL 5:4 Lakom cerum kiristi nin, komwo ciiya ceerkomti ki bola-ngeu; manikom nuwa luwa Kwama koti tak.
GAL 5:5 Laki yuwatangb Kwama, ki bilenke, biningtang yoka nereko cakcaketi ki nero wiin.
GAL 5:6 Mor kiristi Yesu, wobiyem lar ka-nge wo biyebo lareu cii wiin, dila kan bilenke ma na-ngenti mor cwika
GAL 5:7 Fiyaco kom ca kabati dong-dong. We ywamkom bwangka bilenke?
GAL 5:8 Ciyakakowo boubo niio cokome nin!
GAL 5:9 camfuwambo biduwar ki dokre mimbo fuka ducce.
GAL 5:10 Min ciya ka-nge kom kabum Kwamam mani kom bwangteng nuri ka-nge ti ki dmen. Co wuro kung kumen nertiyeu can nuwa dota-nge bola-nge bwenno cin we duwal di
GAL 5:11 Kebmibo, tano miki tokker Kwamar dorbiyeka larekri duwal di, yebwi cii neye dota-nge tiye? Lanawori ter kottangkako kwoblom bwatiye kiristim bo kutam.
GAL 5:12 Lanubowo kwomcang komtiyeu, min cwi nacii yala-ngum dor ciiro!
GAL 5:13 Kebmibo, mi cokom ker ceerkar. dikm turo ceerka kumeko nayilam idker na-nger bwiyer.
GAL 5:14 wori bolango gwam diim kibolango win.”Cwi nii bidom ka-nge mweu na dormwer.”
GAL 5:15 dila nokom ca na-nge kebkumebe tiri komka bati kati yilo kom twalng bwiti kumeu.
GAL 5:16 Dila mikikom yayam mor yuawtangbe, dila mani kom bwangteng diki bwikume cwitiye ti.
GAL 5:17 wori dike bwiyo cwitiyeu makiyeti ka-nge dike yuwatangbeko cwitiyeu, dila dikero yuwatangbeko cwitiyeu ma kiyeti ka-nge dike bwiyo cwityeu.
GAL 5:18 Lano yuwatang bwangtenti kikomeri, bolango mani a ma liyarti dorkumer.
GAL 5:19 Na-ngen bwiyero kino ngang-lang: kayaka, duti, fwandiker, bwangka fulenek,
GAL 5:20 kiye, kwobkangka, kor, funer, bikuwen, kutume, yalkanka, kucuni,
GAL 5:21 norangka ka-nge tangne dikertinim na biro. Fiyco min werangkom miki, nubo madike birotiyeu mani a doti liyar Kwamar.
GAL 5:22 Dila bibwiyer yuwatngbeko cowo, cwika, fuwor nerek, luma nerek, birom nem, luma nero ken, bilenke,
GAL 5:23 lomjome, ka-nge taka dorek, bolang mani dor dikero biro.
GAL 5:24 Biro yilam yesu ceu kiristi ceu ciin fwerken kulen bwiyero ka-nge cwika ciiko.
GAL 5:25 No yimbembo nayutangbeko ceri, daten biyayam kiyutangbe.
GAL 5:26 Biyalamre nob kunka dorek, mwerka dor kebbeb ka-nge nung-nung.
GAL 6:1 Kebmibo, nokom tau nii bwirang keretiye, kom biro ki yuwatangbekeu, kom yilau kico mor yuwatangbeko lomcomeu. Dila ko nyom dorkumero, kati kom doken cuwaka.
GAL 6:2 Kom ci bwini bwitikumero, la-nyeu an diim bolang kiristi ko
GAL 6:3 Tano ka-nge antu dorcero kicin diker dila ci kebori, ci bol dorcer.
GAL 6:4 Nii acuwa na-ngen cero, lana nyime catin diker buulang mor bwiyece kebo ka-nge nii nin.
GAL 6:5 Nii atu na-ngen doret cer ki bwico.
GAL 6:6 Wuro cii merangten dikereu, ca caluma dikeroco ka-nge wo merang ci nen neu.
GAL 6:7 ciiya bol komde, nii mani ayi Kwama mwan kereti, dike nii fiyeu co dike ca biyeetiye.
GAL 6:8 Niiwo fii dum ki cwika bwiyekeri, cabiyee bubaka fiye bwiyo wiye. Nii wo fi dum yuwatangbekeri, ca biye dume fiye yuwatangbeko wiyi.
GAL 6:9 A luwabore maka dikero ko ken, tano kiini lam dong-dong ri ban biye bituwe, ta bi cokbo nerbero ri
GAL 6:10 Ki kiini biki keka-ngiyeu, bima nubonin dikero ken gwam, nobo nanubowo yilam akwama ce ki bilenke.
GAL 6:11 To bifumero durko mimukang kumen kikang mikeu.
GAL 6:12 Nubo cwiti nacii dang dang nym mor bwiyeceu, cii ciidokkomti kibikwan nakom biyem lareu. Cii ma-nyeu kati yilo cii ne cii dota-nge ker kwoblom bwatiyem kiristim.
GAL 6:13 La kebo kanubo biyem lereu bwangteng bolong tiye, dila ciiki cwi kom biyem laro nacii kung dorti mor bwiye kume.
GAL 6:14 La ayilam de mima bitenamti, nokebo ki kwoblom bwtiyem Teluwe be Yesu kiristi tiri, won co dike bwi cii kulken kalewo fiye mi wiye.
GAL 6:15 Biyeka lareko ka-nge wo biyebeu kebo dike ka-nge fiye miwiye. Kan boro fwir yilam dikero ken fiye miwiye.
GAL 6:16 Birombo yiyimbo ken tiyeu, yobka nerek ka-nge jire dume ayilam cee, ka-nge dor Israila Kwamar ken.
GAL 6:17 Tabti anwo yaken ciko ka-nge a kwomyere, wori mi tumki yirom Yesum bwimi.
GAL 6:18 Luma Teluwebe Yesu abwangten ka-nge yuwatangbe kume ko, kebmibo. Ati nyo.
EPH 1:1 Bulus ni tomange Yeecu Kiriti ki ci yaka fiye kwama, kii nubo coccoke na kwama yim Afisawa borom bo ma bilenketi mor Yeecu.
EPH 1:2 Naweu luma kwama ko ati kange kom kange fuwor nener fiye kwama Tee be kange Tee kwama Yeecu Kiriti.
EPH 1:3 Caklanka ki Tee kwama Yeecu Kiriti co ci nebo bibwiyere ki bibwiyer tinimbo wuyakiwo mor nenero lumako ceu mor dii kwama mor Kritti.
EPH 1:4 Nan yi me felka kaleko mor Yeecu. co kombo nabi yi yimbo wucakke kange yambo maniki duti kaceu.
EPH 1:5 Mor cwika kwama dangi ki naci tumbo nabi yilam bibwece fiye Yeecu Kirirti wiyeu. Ci ma wo kambo ci cwiti naci mane.
EPH 1:6 Cune inco kwama naci yo caklanka wo duktangka luma nererk ko ceu. won co dike nebo kang nyam aya fiya bwe nerece wiye.
EPH 1:7 La mor bwe nere ci ceerbi fiye bwiyale ce kange tabka bwiran kerer fiye luma nererce ko lalame.
EPH 1:8 Cin ne luma nererkowo, Lama nyo mor nyomka gwam.
EPH 1:9 Kwama yibo bilenke dikero wuro yurangum yurangeu. Ki nyomka ce kange dikero gwam dii kwama kange dor bintiner mor Yeecu.
EPH 1:10 Cin cokbo almasihu nabi yilam nob kwaleb na kwama ce.
EPH 1:11 Mor Kritti cin ma binen ywelka ko wo kika mor ywelka cek, cin ni ma dikeroti gwam nawo nerceroceu.
EPH 1:12 Kwama man yo wori nabi fulom na caklanka duktanka ceko cekoceu. inbo nob kababo bifiya yoka neroko weu mor almacihu.
EPH 1:13 Mor Almacihu kom fiya nuwaka kerbileng kerer, ker dumer ber fiya Yeecu wiye. morece kom nebilenker ci dokkume kang ki Yuwatanbe kwama ko wucakke woci ma kumen mor cereu.
EPH 1:14 Yuwatanbe ko inco ciyaka kwali beko na nyime yabi fiya. wuro na caklanka duktanka cek.
EPH 1:15 Naweu, ki kwama mi nuwau fulen bilenkerer kumero mor Ubangiji Yeecu kange cwikacek yaken ciko kwarub birombo cii cokci kercereu.
EPH 1:16 Ma kurong bo kwaka ki kom mi kwob kimen diloti mor dilotinim.
EPH 1:17 min kwob kumen dilo miki Tee bwe wo di kwama Yeecu Almasihu Tee wo wucake ane kom yuwa tangba ceko wo ba fiya bukati cikeu kange wo nyomka cek kwarub.
EPH 1:18 Mi kwob diloti na nuwe kume wumom nakom nyimom ciya bicore kumeko. Mikwob diloti nakom nyimom cuweka liyar kwaliero mor birombo ci cokunnaceu.
EPH 1:19 Mi kwob diloti kom yimom liyard cero wuro na dur wuro mankidi more benen wuri bine bilenker dwikako wuro kino fiye nanyer kwaner bikwan nerer cet.
EPH 1:20 Wonka bikwan durero ci mam nagen ciko mor Almasihu ki kwama wo kwama kunco tuweu yokenco kanko cacciyere mor di kwama.
EPH 1:21 Cin yo kenco dor birbishi kange Liyar, do ka, lo dako wannen irin liyar can yoken Almasihu kebo na kele wuro ce ki kwaco dila kange kalewo bouti yeu.
EPH 1:22 Kwama dokken dikero gwam mor Bibwe kwama cin yonco dur dor dikero nen gwam mor nub bwanka ceko.
EPH 1:23 Nub bwanka ko in bwico, dika niwo dim dikero gwam mor dikero gwam, gwameu.
EPH 2:1 Dila nan duwo kom bwambwa mor bwirang ker kumer kange kanke.
EPH 2:2 More ce kom yim yim kumem bo wo dor bitinerowo kom bwanten niwo ma yila bikwan tini diyok kwamak, won co yuwako ma nagenti, mor bibei bi kwan doret.
EPH 2:3 Nanduwo gwambe bi mor nubo birombo nebo bilenkere bibwang ten ka dikero bwirko bwibe cwitiyeu. bi matika nagen bwiyer kange dike nerbero katiyeu. fo bwiri bibei wuro daten funer kwamareu, na kangem.
EPH 2:4 Dila kwama nii ci bwini tenagi nye, ni ker wikaro ci cwibo manki dika.
EPH 2:5 Kambo bibwiyam bwiya mo bwirangke, bouki bo mor nero funer wari kange almasihu. ci fulobo kin luma nerer cek.
EPH 2:6 Kwama kunbo wari dila yobo biyi ari nawo, win mor Almasihu Yeecu.
EPH 2:7 Ci ma wuri ker kaldo wuro bouti yeu. na daang cuyeka luma nerer cko fiye Yeecu wiyeu. Kdang binen wuro kino luma neret cek.
EPH 2:8 Naweu ci ceerbo kin lumanerek wo bilenkeroceu wo kebo fiye kom wiye, luma nerek kwamak.
EPH 2:9 Kebo dor nagenent nawori kange kume a kunde dor.
EPH 2:10 Bin nagen kange kwamar, fwelfwele mor almasihu Yeecu nabima nagen do ken, birombo nanduwo kwama yowau nabi, yi yimbo moreceu.
EPH 2:11 Naweu kom kwabi nanduwo kom nubo yombo kwama ki yim bwiyeme. ci ki cuwoki “nubo biyebo Lave” dike ci coki biye Lave bwiyeu wuri kan nube ko matiyeu.
EPH 2:12 Dila ki kwama wo nacin kab kangum kuke da almasihu. kom fabub nubo Israila nin. ko fabub ker neret. Kom manki yomka dor finir. Kom manki kwama dor bitiner.
EPH 2:13 Di la na weu mor almasihu Yeecu kom wo nanduwo kutan kange kwama, cin bou ki kom bidom fiye buyale almasihu.
EPH 2:14 Cin co fuwor nener bero. La naci yilam win kiyobeu. Mor bwiyece cin bubam tiyak kiyeko wo kab kangum bo kange bwitibou.
EPH 2:15 La naci tungum warka kowo ki nyaleu kange werfuneu, dila naci fwel nii fwir win more ce. makako nyeu bou ki lumanerek.
EPH 2:16 Ci manyo naci mwer nubo yob mor bwiye wi kange kwama fiye yeikaka. Fiye kwoblom bwatiyeu cin twalum kiye tiber cereu
EPH 2:17 Yeecu bou makimen ker fuwor nener kom wo km kutan kange kom wo kom bidomeu.
EPH 2:18 Na fiye Yeecu wiyeu kwarubbe yobeu win mor yuwa tangbak cek biki nure yakenti Tee nenneu.
EPH 2:19 Naweu kom nubo yombo kwama wni wo, kebo fabub. nawori faub ari knage birombo cokcokeu wo kwama cer farub, nangeneb.
EPH 2:20 Birombo ci mu ci dor kwar nob tomangeb kange nob ker dukumeb. Almasihu Yeecu ki dorcer coci lanrang Tee mukare.
EPH 2:21 Mukako mwer morece kwarub, ci diti na lo kwama mor Ubangiji.
EPH 2:22 Morece ci mu kom tiye gwam kom yilam fiti yim kwama mor yuwa tangbecek.
EPH 3:1 Lana wori, mo Bulus bwe furcina ker almasihu ma kom nubo yombo kwama.
EPH 3:2 Mi kwati kom nuwam don nager do dur ko wo luma kwama ceu neken mor ker kumer.
EPH 3:3 Mi mulankumen dor dukumero ci yi yereu. won co bilnker yurangum yurangeu ma tokker dor cer mor bifumero kange.
EPH 3:4 Kambo ko fiye dor cereu, kan nyimom basira miu mor yuranka bilenker don amlsihu.
EPH 3:5 Wuro kaltiyo nanduwo i yi cibo nubo. la na weu cin dang nob tomangeb bo nen kange nob tomangeb dukumeb. cokum coke mor Yuwa tanbe.
EPH 3:6 Kero wo yurangum yurangeu, in co ker kwarowo dangi nubo nyombo kwama faub kwalib wari kange bo, kutelti mor bwiye win. Farub mwerkankab wari mor nortimin almasihu Yeecu fiye kerkwamari wiyeu.
EPH 3:7 Wonco dike bwi mi yilam canga fiye yomka luma kwama nekye nawo durbi kwaner cero.
EPH 3:8 Kwama neyi nyomka kowe. canno min coni dual duwale mor birombo cokeu na kwamace, nan tok ker kwama nubo nyom bo kwama nin don cuweko almasihu wuro manki dika.
EPH 3:9 Nan fetang nubomin gwam dike kwama ywelcinentiye bilenkero wuro yurangum yurangeu wo coti coti kwama yurangumeu, co cinnir fweldiko gwam.
EPH 3:10 Nawori fiye ku wabero nob bidweb kang nubo ma liyar diko kwama tiyeu, ciyan nyimom yomka kwama fiyeco ki dimen kidimen.
EPH 3:11 Wuro bwi nyo nawo co ci mani mor Almasihu Yecu Tee be kwama.
EPH 3:12 La mor bibwe kwama bin wiki bikwan nener ducce, kange ciyaka kiker bilenkerbe morece.
EPH 3:13 Naweu mi kenkomti kom cwaretai kiker dotange mi nuwa kerkumereu wo yilam duktang kumen keu.
EPH 3:14 Naweu min cunti ki duwenmir kabum Tee.
EPH 3:15 Wuro fiye ciwuye ci cuwanga nuboti wuro kwama kange bitineu.
EPH 3:16 Mi kwobdilo cin ciya kumn dor cuweka duktankace. kom biner kambo ken ki dur bikwanererowo yuwa tangbanko mineu wo more kumeu.
EPH 3:17 Min kwob diloti Almasihu ayi mor nener kume ki bilenker ke mi ker abdilo ti tak kom tim yora kom mum yora kambo kem mor cwika cek.
EPH 3:18 Kom yilam mor cwika cek wori na nyimom, kange nob bwanka kwama wari wuyak, in ye cuwaka, kange kuyaka, kange cuwemka cwiki almasihu.
EPH 3:19 Mi kwobdiloti na kom nyimom tenanka cwika almasihu wo cum nyonka. Kom mawo naci dimkom ki dika kwamak.
EPH 3:20 Naweu wo ki dur bi kwaner maka dikero bi kenu kaka kwanka nerer bisaga dur bi kwaner cer manangenti more beu.
EPH 3:21 duktangk a yilam nace mor fiye wabka fiye Yeecu wiyeu yaken ciko ki curom tinin diri diri Atinyo.
EPH 4:1 Nawo ri nawo min mi furcineu ker kwama mi kenkomti kom yi yimbo daten kange bi co kwama makemeneu.
EPH 4:2 Kom yilam ki dikero ken do wu a mati ki dikero ken kange birom nenerem. Kom yo kebkume bo mor cwika.
EPH 4:3 Kom yi yim mwerka dorek mor yuwa tangbek kom morum mor fuwor neret.
EPH 4:4 Bwiyo wi win kange yuwa tangbekko win, kam ci co kom dor yoka nerer ko wineu.
EPH 4:5 Kwama win bilenke win, kange yuka munge kwama win.
EPH 4:6 Kwama win kange Tee gwam. Co ci dor diker wuyake, fiye wuyake, kange mor wuyak.
EPH 4:7 Kwama ci nebo nyomka dong dong kange cuwaka nyka almasihu.
EPH 4:8 Nawo cin bwanten kange cannya mo dotange cin ma nubo ki yomka.
EPH 4:9 In ye tok tiye, “Cin kwiken” kiyi yiram, yaken bitine more cuwa cuwau.
EPH 4:10 Co ci yiraweu co ci kwiken dikwama ci mawu naci dim dikero gwam.
EPH 4:11 Yeecu Nii ne nub yomka nawuro nyo nob tomangeb, dukume nubo waker cero fiye nubo to kwamatiyeu, kange nob merangkatiyeu.
EPH 4:12 Cima nyo na ywellum nob kwama bo na maka nange neke ce, na mum bwi almaihu.
EPH 4:13 Ci manyo nabi lam yim bilnker bo ken bo kange nyoka bibwe kwama. ci manyo la bi lam dwika, na birombo lam dim dur cero lo Yeecu.
EPH 4:14 Yecu muu wuro nyo kati yelo bi yilam na bi bei. ka cita yilang boti. Wuro nyo kati yoli bi yuwa merangka binen kankak kange buyelangka nob maka cwerkeko.
EPH 4:15 Nyori ban tok bilenker mor cwika wori nabi dwi mor bi kwanner cer, co cin durken mor Yeecu.
EPH 4:16 Yeecu mwerum bwi nob neka bilenker. Bwiyo mwerum mwere fiye kulteltinim bo wiyeu, na bwiyo duyom na mum dencero mor cwika.
EPH 4:17 Naweu nii makumen be wereti mor kwama miki kom cwobtende yimbo na yim nubo nyombo kwama cimati yim azanci bang da wofi wo manki nageneu.
EPH 4:18 Cin fim kumti cile mor kwaka nerer ciko fabub ki dume nawo kwama ceu, fiyu bwin nyo ka cek wo more ceu kange wo kwamka nerer cekeu.
EPH 4:19 Ma ci nuwa kwenduwe ti cin neken dor ciro nagen mor bwiyer maka nangendo yeyeu kange la cin merang kenti ki dikero bwir.
EPH 4:20 La kebo nyo kom merang nage kwama re.
EPH 4:21 Min kwatiri kom kweri, kom nuwam dorcer. mikwatiri cin merang kumen morece, nawo bilenker Yeecu nyeu.
EPH 4:22 Yii nen ki tam dikero nanduwo mwa merangeu, kom yii yimkumenbo nanduwo, la nii cer nii carko yakcanti ki bwirankeret ceko.
EPH 4:23 Kom minang nii carkowo naci mirim kom fwice mor yuwa tangbe kumek.
EPH 4:24 Kom manyo nakom dum ni fwir wo cerkan kwama ci fwel mor bilenker nere, kange wucak kange bilenke.
EPH 4:25 Na wori kom cutan cwekewi, “Tok bilenke kange nii bidom kange mweu,” wori bin kuteltin bwitibo.
EPH 4:26 “Kom kanngum ner, dila mare bwiranke”. kom dob re ka kuko ayarum kom kang nerek.
EPH 4:27 Kom nere bwe kelkele nyilo.
EPH 4:28 Ni ku kumtiyeri adubom kuka kuyeko tak. La nyi co liya mananngen manangen ki kanice naci fiya dike catikan nubo kwambe ti cikeu.
EPH 4:29 Kero fwemfweu acirangum nyi kom. No nyori, kom ywelten dor kumero na ne luma nubo nuwatiye.
EPH 4:30 Kom kande yuwatangbe kwamako nin ner fo fiye ciweu ci dok kumen kange nawo kaku ceer kako ceu.
EPH 4:31 Kom cutan fur nerero win, da hasala. fush da tankiya da reny da dukan mugunta. kom ma bwiti kume nen dikiero ken, kom yilam ki nero yiber.
EPH 4:32 Kom dob keb kume bo bwirangker cero kambo kwama kume Yeecu dob kumen bwirang ker kumeru.
EPH 5:1 Nuweu Kom ma meranka ki kwama na be beyo cwitiye.
EPH 5:2 Kom yi yimbo mor cwika nawo Yeecu cwibeu latak neken dor cero dike luma neret kange diker ne kar fiye kwama wiyeu dorber, twika dikero fican fican diker yokar fiye kwama wiyeu.
EPH 5:3 Burotum kange kwarub kayaltum, kange kaya kaya kawowo yei nyeu ciya cuwo kome more ce, nyo daten kinob bwangka kwama.
EPH 5:4 ciya cuwo re batsa ker kulerner kange alfasa birombo daten bem. No nyori biyilam nob buka kangek.
EPH 5:5 Naweu kom nyi mom ni kayaka kange ni mani wucakeu.
EPH 5:6 Kangem abolkome kiketito bwir. in co dikero birom bo funer kwamaro boutiye dor bibeyo bonya nyi nyeu.
EPH 5:7 Kom mwerkan re dor wari kange ci.
EPH 5:8 Wori naduwo kom kunta cile dila naweu kom filan mo kwama. Dila kom yayambo nabibei filange.
EPH 5:9 Wori nange filange ro co lumako, luma nerek kange bilenke.
EPH 5:10 Kom do dike kwama ma funner nerer ti cikeu.
EPH 5:11 yorekan nange do wo manki yorako ken kange nagen do kumtacile dila yora a womci.
EPH 5:12 Diker kwenduwe kange duka diker ci mani yurangum yurangeu.
EPH 5:13 Diker gwam cano filang danciri ciki tom nyo.
EPH 5:14 Wori diker yilam ci to ti filange ri co diker bwi citoki wuram mo ni dume kwenum mor buware, Yeecu atim ne filang dor mwer.
EPH 5:15 La na weu kom mayora mor timbo kom tim kumentiye.
EPH 5:16 Kom tiyora kange maka nangenek ki kanka neret wori kume cwiku n bwi.
EPH 5:17 Na wori kom yakcare ki nyom wori kang yim nimti lanyori kom dim ki yuwa tangbe kwama wucakkeu.
EPH 5:18 Nyori kom nore dikero bwir wo a yokom ti mor dotangeu, daten di kom dim ki yuwatangbe kwama,
EPH 5:19 Kom ki tokkan kero ti bwiti kume kon ki zabura kange nuwe kange nuwetinim mor nerer kom, kanuwe cakkeu ki ner kumer fiye kwama wiyeu.
EPH 5:20 bak ni bak kom ne bilenker keti wori dikero gwam mor den Yeecu Tee be kwama.
EPH 5:21 Kom Ciya kom tum dotange bwiki kume mor neka kwama
EPH 5:22 Natub kom bwanten dir nabarub kumebo mun kom ki man ki kwama.
EPH 5:23 Wori bwayile co dur wicero nawo almasihu dur nub bwanka kwamak co ni fuloka bwiyeko.
EPH 5:24 Dila kambo nub bwanka kwama ko neken durcero tiye, tamyo natubo ciya bwece dur gwam.
EPH 5:25 Nabarub kom cwit natub kumebo kambo Yecu cwi nub bwanka cekeu. ya neken dor kercer.
EPH 5:26 Ci ma nawo na ciyim ci wucak. Naci nirimbo ki mwom nikam fiye kercero wiyeu.
EPH 5:27 Ci ma oyo naci neken dor cero nub bwanka kwama ko nen wo yoryoreu manki dike kece kulande mani na birombo na wuro dila ca yilam wucak mani ki dwiti.
EPH 5:28 Na woro nabarubo kom ci natub kumeb bo na bwikom wuro cwi wiceri cwi dorcer.
EPH 5:29 Ni mani wo kom bwice wiye. Dila neci raritoti cwiti na wo kwama cwiti nub bwanka cebo matiyeu.
EPH 5:30 Wori bin kutteli kebbeb.
EPH 5:31 Nyori ni nabare a dubom Tee ce dubo nece citab wice nin ci yob cin yilam nange win.
EPH 5:32 Dike wo yurangum yurangeu tenanin dila miki tok kange nub bwanka kwama.
EPH 5:33 Kange o wuya kom nabarobo mon cwi tatumubo nador kumer nawiye kang can can ne bwece durko.
EPH 6:1 Bibeyo kom bwanten tebkumebo mor kwama wuro dong dong.
EPH 6:2 Ne Tee mwe durko kange Ne mwe” won co werfun kabaro kange nore.
EPH 6:3 La nye ka ma bi buyer wori, na kumeri kumeu cuwemi dor bitiner”.
EPH 6:4 Nyo Tebbo kom kwomde bibeyo lokume a lamde kanka nerer, dila kom mweci mor mwerum mem kwama kange kwobka tuwek.
EPH 6:5 Kom cangab bo kom bwanten dir Tee luwer kumero wo dor bitinero ceu knage neka durek kange tai kiner bilenker. ma cinen na dimu ki mam ki Tee mwe wo dii kwama.
EPH 6:6 Kom neci durko nobo wori cito kom tiyeu na kom neci fuwor nerer Nyori kom macinen muni kom ki mam ki kwama kom a ker kwama ro mor nere.
EPH 6:7 Kom ma dikero kiner kumero wuyak. muni komti bwnate kwama kebo niffir.
EPH 6:8 Kom nyo diker nimane can fiya yokacek fiya kwama cin nannga ka kaka ci keba.
EPH 6:9 Kom Teeb Luwe bo kom ma cannga kume nen nyo kom necire dotange kom nyi mom co niwo cin Tee ciu kange kom win kino kwama kom nyi manici dong nyimanka.
EPH 6:10 Diker wuyak, kom ne bi kwan nerer mor kwama kange mor dur bi kwaner cer.
EPH 6:11 Kom tu kulen kwener kwamaro gwam na fiya na kom ca kaba dor yulan bwe kelkeler.
EPH 6:12 Wori kwenbero kebo na nangi ce kange buyale. Dila kange bikwan liyarero wo no warkabo dor bitinereu. wori kaldo kumta cile kange nob kweneb cibo fo mor kalewoninen.
EPH 6:13 Nyori kom tukulen kwener kwama gwam na ko do lum kom tim kibi kwan mor kwener wonen.
EPH 6:14 Naweu, kom tim kibi kwan kom bwam dak kumeko mor bilenker kom merumom sulke cak-cakeu.
EPH 6:15 Kom wuro kambo kom bwam nani kume nakom yaken ki ker kwama lumakoceu.
EPH 6:16 Mor dikero gwam kom tu kusanko bilenke ko, wuro katwalum bok tinim nii bwir ko cikeu.
EPH 6:17 Kom tu wambile ker dumero kange kulen yuwa tanbako, wuro ker kwamareu.
EPH 6:18 Wari kange dilo tinim kange kini kom kwob dilo ngir mor yuwatangbeko kin co nero wo kom kicom wuruti ki birim nerem kange kini ker nub kwama gwam.
EPH 6:19 Kom kwob dilona yitomange kambo min wumom yimeu. Kom kwob men dilo nan fiyam bi kwan nerer tok ka bilelnke yurangum yurangeu.
EPH 6:20 Dila na kom nyimom nyim minbo kange kambo mi yimmeu,
EPH 6:21 Tikikus, kemi macwiti cwiyeu, kange ciyaka cannga mor kwama anyikom co dike wiyeu.
EPH 6:22 Wonco dike bwi mi two mu co kumen ne wori nakom nyi mom dike nyi more ceu, na kom fiyam yobka nerer mor nerer kume.
EPH 6:23 Na weu fuwor nener kwama ati kange kom keb mibo ki bilenker wuro Tee kwama kange kwama Yeecu Kritti.
EPH 6:24 Luma kwama ati kange kom birombo cwi Tee kwama Yeecu Kritti wari kange cwika ko mani ki bwiyaka.
PHI 1:1 Bulus ka-nge Timoti cangab kiristi Yeesu yã ciko nob kwamab wucake wo Fillibi ka-nge nubo tam ki nubo bwanten kwama tiye, ka-nge nubo durku lo wabbeu. ka-nge nobo durko ku wabbe.
PHI 1:2 luma kimen ka-nge fuwor neret tebe kwama nin ka-nge Teluwe Yeesu kiristi.
PHI 1:3 mi bu kwama nin ka-ngeti diye no ma kwa kom ki nere di.
PHI 1:4 kir-kir mor dilo minin kimen gwam, mi kwob dilo miti ki nero fuwor.
PHI 1:5 mi bu ka-ngeti dor nangenero bi mati wari mor fulen kere ka cikko ba teruwe ya ciko na wo.
PHI 1:6 miki bi kwamer neret wo ter nangen ken kimeneu an yaken ciko cwobka di kakuk Yeesu kiristi.
PHI 1:7 won digero ken nuwa nyo nure wuro dor kimer gwan, nyori miki kom gwam ner mir. kom yilam far nangene mi mor luma, ki bwaka miko ka-nge cerka dorek mik ka-nge tika ki bi kwan bifumero nin.
PHI 1:8 kwama warke mi, kuru kime gwam mi ciko mor cwika dur wo Yeesu kiristi ce.
PHI 1:9 wo co dilo mi, cwika kime ko a yokten kab mor merangka ka-nge, ka-nge nyomko diger gwam.
PHI 1:10 nyori na ko ciye ki dige yor yore gwam na kom yilam nobo ki bilengke, digero bwir mani kimen ya cika dige kiristi.
PHI 1:11 dim ki bi tutti wucake wo bouti fiye Yeesu kiristi na duktangka ka-nge caklangka kwama.
PHI 1:12 mi cwi komti ki nyimi keb mibo, dige fiya yereu matikali fiye yokka fulen keret kwama.
PHI 1:13 bwaka miko mor kiristi bou ki filang nubo lo liya, nubo tõ nub tiyeu gwam, ka-nge kangum bo fiye ka-nge.
PHI 1:14 kangum yitub beb, ki kinin yilam ki bi kwan neret mor Teluwebe ker bwaka miko, ciki nero kwamer ciya miko keroti man ki taiye.
PHI 1:15 kangum bo tok ker kiristi ki kor neret ki kwilki-kwilkiye. kangum bo ki nero ken.
PHI 1:16 nubo ki biye wo ki ma ki cwika, ki nyomka ci bwayere na yilam kucang fulen keret.
PHI 1:17 nubo wo bwiye ki tok ker kiristi do mor cwika neret ciye, kebo dor bilen keret. ci kwatiri ciyan neye dotange ki fiya cuwo mi bwambwabe.
PHI 1:18 “la ye” diger win, mor digero gwam, bwen tano ciki ma ki cwerke kaka bilengke. cin tok fulen kwamaro, nyeu, min nuwa luma, ong min nuwa luma.
PHI 1:19 min nyimom wo a dok cerkamik mor dilo kime ka-nge tikali yuwa kwaman tangbe wo Yeesu kiristi.
PHI 1:20 miki kuru kang yo neri mani ma nuwa kwenduwe ti, ka-nge ti ka kibi kwang, can ka-nge kicatecc, kiristi an fiya dur kwimi, bwar kaka'a mor dume.
PHI 1:21 minen “mu ki dumeri, kiristi, no bwar di yokka.
PHI 1:22 mor bwiyeri, mi nintang wo ti gwam.
PHI 1:23 la yilam digero bwaibwaye tiber digero wo yobeu. cwika miko na kũbo na ya'a yi ka-nge Yeesu, wo dige yore gwam,
PHI 1:24 nyeu yilam ki dume, tam nyo ker kimer.
PHI 1:25 wo min ciya ciko, min nyimom man yim nan bwanten ka-nge kom gwam dor caka kaba ka-nge bilantum mor bilengke.
PHI 1:26 nyori fiye mi wiye na kom fiya yokka mor kiristi Yeesu no bou kimen takri.
PHI 1:27 ki ma digero daten fulen keret kiristi, na nyori. no bou mato komri kaka'a mi mani ri, nuwa kimen kom tim kibi kwamer mor yuwa tangbe wucake wiin ki nero wiin, kwilki-kwilki ker fulen keret kwama.
PHI 1:28 ki nuware tai nubo wuro yilam nob kiye kime. wuro yirom cinen na wuroka ciko ce, kime fuloka kime ko-wuro kwama nin ne.
PHI 1:29 cin nekom yiber ker kiristi, kebo ka neka bilengke cinen ka-nge nuwa ka dotangen ker cer,
PHI 1:30 na dontang wo ka to mine neu, la can ka tuwe.
PHI 2:1 no nekangka bi kwannek wiri no birum neri wiri wi wo cwika netiyeri, no mwer ka-ngka duwe mor yuwa tangbe wucake wiri, no cire duwe ka-nge bunangka wiri,
PHI 2:2 ko dok bilantum mini bo a dim, nawo ka yilam nero wiine, kom kicwika wiin, ko mwerka-ngum mor yuwako wucake kom ki dige ka yõ kabawiin.
PHI 2:3 kom mare diger ki cwika duwe kaka'a diger bi boler, nyori ki taka duwe, tu tang ne nube cin lã nen.
PHI 2:4 kom tore ka dike kom cwitiye koni, nyori kom to dige kangumbo cwitiyeu.
PHI 2:5 ki nyimom wori ki bwikimi, buro mor kiristi Yeesu.
PHI 2:6 wori yi yim na kwama dila tũbo dor cerowiin na kwama.
PHI 2:7 nyori cin tũ dor cero na cang. ci ki bwi nifire, cin tũ dor cero canga cin cerkangu na nifir.
PHI 2:8 con cukum dor ki co cero, cin yilam ki ne duri wo yo yaken ki co bware, bwaro wo dor bwatiye reu,
PHI 2:9 nyori kwama neco duktankaku dur, con neco dendo la den gwamme.
PHI 2:10 ci ma wureu, na nyori mor dene Yeesu dwendo gwam an cun-cunge, dwen nobo wo kwamau, ka-nge wo dor bitinereu ka-nge wo mor bitineu
PHI 2:11 ca mawo na biyendo gwam, na toki ki, “Yeesu co kiristi ka-nge Teluwe ker duktongka kwama Teu.
PHI 2:12 nyori kom keb mibo mi cwitiye, nawo ki ne durti ki ca tecceu nuwen, la can a lã nyo mi maniyeu. ki do fangka kime ko ki tai ka-nge, kwama bwiyek.
PHI 2:13 wo kwama ma nangen ti more kime ki cwika cek ka-nge nuwa ka luma ce ken.
PHI 2:14 kom ma diger gwam kebo ki fwenna kaka kwob kanka.
PHI 2:15 nyori na kom yilam kom man ki kwama man ki diger bitorek ka-nge bilengke, bi bei kwama man ki diger bitorektiber kaldo wo bwira nyonlangum-nyonlangeu, woro ka yilam kira tibati mor kale.
PHI 2:16 kom tam ker dume, na nyori ki bi diye kiristi na yilam ki nyial ma cwa bo cwak ka-ge nangen koni.
PHI 2:17 no mwenno ci yumyeti na nuwang twika ka-nge nangen bilen keret di, miki fwor nerek ka-nge bilengka kimen gwam.
PHI 2:18 nyo takeu, kom ken nuwa luma, naki bilangi ka-nge mo.
PHI 2:19 nyori muki nyo-neri Teluwe Yeesu nin in twom Timoti kimen kutang bo, na fiya bi kwamar neret no nuwa dige dor kimerdi.
PHI 2:20 mi mangki nii na co, wori ki bi cwom kwa kom ti ki neri.
PHI 2:21 wori digero dor cire koni ci nyime kebo digero wo na Yeesu kiristi.
PHI 2:22 ka nyimom yora ceko, wori na bwe te nin, con mamen nangen mor fulen kere.
PHI 2:23 nyori mi yo nerti na twom co kimen non to dige a yakenti fo ka-nge mer.
PHI 2:24 miki bi kwamer neret mor Teluwe, mo ki bwimi man bou kutang bo.
PHI 2:25 min tõ tam yo twom Abafaroditu a wajenku. con ka-nge far nangenne ka-nge far kwene ka-nge nii tome ka-nge canga kime dor dige mi cwitiye.
PHI 2:26 wori con kung ner dor kimer, na co ya kimen gwam, wori kom nuwa ki co nuwa bo luma.
PHI 2:27 ki cwom ca nuwabo luma, con dadom bwar, la kwama cii dor cero, kebo co ka-nge mo, nyori nan fiyare bwiraka nere dor bwiraka nerek.
PHI 2:28 nyori miki kuru ducce, twom co no komto co tak ri kan bilangi, mo keneu ner mure an daken.
PHI 2:29 ki yuwo Abafaraditu mor Teluwe ki for nerek gwam. kom ne dur nob na co.
PHI 2:30 kin ker nangen kiristi ca dadom ca bwiyetiye, con ciya leka dume cek naci mamen nangen do wuro no kom ka matiye.
PHI 3:1 diger wuyak kebmibo, kom ma fuwor nerer mor kwama nan yilam mulankumenten digero birombo kebo dige ka-nge minen. digero birombo an co kumkom.
PHI 3:2 kom nyimi kibi cuwentin do. kom nyimi ka-ngi nob nangen nebo bwirko. kom nyimi ka-nge nob wor man ka.
PHI 3:3 inbo nubo mwatum lare wori inbo bi wab kwamati ki yuwatangbe ceke. inbo nubo bulangti mor kiristi Yeesu, bi manki tai mor bwiye tak.
PHI 3:4 la duwaleu, mo miki dor mir minwi kibi kwannerer dor bwiyer no ka-nge atin kwabi cin wi ki bi kwannererdi, mo, min laco.
PHI 3:5 ci mwatimen laro ki kume narube, nubo Israila nin, wo duwet lor Biliyaminu, bayahuden Yafudawa, fiye bolange min Bafarisiye.
PHI 3:6 fiye nannge ne min ne Ikilisiyo dotangi kor luma nerer mor bolange min yilam mimanki diger bitoret.
PHI 3:7 dila dikero birombo gwam yilam fiyaka fiye miwiyeu, mintu tukenci diger yaret ker Almasihu.
PHI 3:8 nyo, mi kiyarangen digero woti cin diger yaret ker ni lala nyonka kiristi Yeesu Teebe. wori co mi cam kaba digero gwamme. min yoken ci digero manki nangen fiye miwiyeu wori nan don co ka kaba Almasihu.
PHI 3:9 ciya fiya ye merece. mi manki ka-nge luma doret min oblange. lanyori, min wiki lua fiye bilengke mor kiristi, lumakowo fiye kwama wuyeu wo bilengke wiyeu.
PHI 3:10 Naweu me cwiti nyumom kebi kwandur kwenkacek, ka-nge nuwaka dotangek ceko. nan nyilam naco tak fiye buwaree,
PHI 3:11 dila cano nyori nayan lam kwenka mor tuwe.
PHI 3:12 ma yibo miki min fiyau digero birom, manyo takri min kweri min yilam wo dim diyeu. dila miki tok miki ci dor nan lam yom wuro kiristi Yeesu couye ker cereu.
PHI 3:13 kebmibo, matok bo miki min kweri min yom wuro bwiririn dila diger wi win wo min matiye. matabunti kidige bwiyeu, midorti dige wuro kabe nin.
PHI 3:14 mi doken dorti dor digerowo ci cwoye dorcereu nan fiyam cuner caka kabak wo bi cor kwamaroce diri-diriyeu mor kiristi Yeesu.
PHI 3:15 gwammebe birombo tanmtabe dor cireu, bi kwaner nure wuro min cano bikwa dige ka-nge kidimendi, kwama atin dang kumen digero wo tak.
PHI 3:16 Dila fiye kweri balamlau, bitamo nyo.
PHI 3:17 kom yilam nob biltengar rebmib, keb mibo. konto yora birombo yakenti kambo nyi yilam diger meromkar fiye ci wiyeu.
PHI 3:18 nubo ducce yankenti, co nubo wo miyiki kom fulen cereu, na weu miyikomti tak lakila na nob kiyeb bentilen kiristi.
PHI 3:19 dila ciyan buyam. wori kwama ceu fwercer, bikwan nerer cere kino mor kwenduwece. nereiro kino kalendo dor bitiner.
PHI 3:20 labeu fiye yime beu kino dii kwama, fiye bi ningtongum dumetiyeu, kwama Yeesu kiristi.
PHI 3:21 An fulongum bwibeu wo fuyeti fuyeu na yilam na bwiyo wo yoryoreu, ywelywele kibi kwan duret cereu naci yoken digero gwamcinen.
PHI 4:1 Tano nyori nob neremi yitum mibbo ka-nge wo mi bilangtiyeu, fowor neremi na bilang duwe mi, wi nure curo kom ti yora mwor Teluwe nob nere farubmib.
PHI 4:2 mi kinong Afodiya, mi konong feneti, kom yilam ki yulando win mwor Teluwe.
PHI 4:3 manki kwane yila mi konong komi, farub yimem kwobka tuni na bilengke: kom tikan natubo wuro nin dige biwiyeu bin nuwa dotange wari ka-nge ci mwor keret bifumer wari ka-nge kilimas kange tangnim farub mi. wuro den ciyero wi mulan-gum mwor bifumer dume.
PHI 4:4 ma fuwor neri mwor Teluwe kang-kang. yila mi tokti, ma fuwor neri.
PHI 4:5 ki dobti nubo gwam na to-o birim niri kume. Teluwe dadom.
PHI 4:6 kom yaranda ki ka-nge diger na curoyeu, mwor diger gwam wari ki kwobka dul-lo ki keni-keni, ki buka ka-ngek, wori keni- keni kumen na fiya kwama.
PHI 4:7 luma kwama, Atin cum gwam nyomka na wo a ywel ner kumero ka-nge nang niri kume mwor Almaciya Yeesu.
PHI 4:8 ki bwiko keb mibbo, gwam dige wuro yilam na bilengke ceu, gwam dige yilam na neka ducce, gwam dige yilam na cakcakkece. gwam dige yilam na kene, gwam dige yilam wo yom yowe, gwam dige bouti ki luma, gwam dige ki digewo yor-yore ci toktiye, non wiki bilengkeri, kwa ki ner dor dige buro nin.
PHI 4:9 dige buro kom merangeu ki yoweu ki nuwau ki to-o mwor yim mimbo ninne, kom ma nangen ki dige buro. kwama ni luma an no-o wari ka-nge kom.
PHI 4:10 min ma fuwor neri kambo ken mwor Te-e dige bwiyeu canneu kom fwelum toka kumeko ki mo. kom toye ki nwo fuwor kibo com ki kaba cumeu, dila kom fiyabo filang na tika kali mi ce.
PHI 4:11 kebo na corka buni ce ma tok wure nan merang dang neri bwentano ki ma nyori.
PHI 4:12 min nyimom kambo ma yiiti min kambo ma fiyati ki ducce, bwentano ki nure wuni mwor digero gwam min merang yulan kambo ma cati ka-nge kambo ma yimti ki wuran, kambo yilamti ki digero yilo nan yim mwor doka.
PHI 4:13 man dol maka diger gwam wi cinnen co niwo ci bwamen na tiyeu.
PHI 4:14 gwam ki na co, kom yii yimbo datenne kange mo'o mwor dotange
PHI 4:15 yilo kom nyimom, kom Filibiyawa, ki kaba bifumer kere ki kwama ma dubom Makadoniya. ka-nge kurwabi mani wo bwamen na ker yoka ka-nge neka kar kom ki kwa kom.
PHI 4:16 kakka ki kwama mi Tassalonika, kon tomi ki tikali kumeu wo corka buni ce cum kiristi yob.
PHI 4:17 kebo ki den miki do na nero timero ba, la wo tano nyori, miki do tikali wuro ki boure ki la ka mwor yoka kumek.
PHI 4:18 min yo digero gwam, min wi kiki kila rang-ngi kom bwamen fuwer, min nyo wi kang Abafroditus digero kange wi kumen, kunka lima dige muri na ficang fican-nge, yom yowe neniri datenne fo kwama.
PHI 4:19 kwama mi an dim gwam dokabekko ki dor cer na cwika ceko kambo co ne wi nyo mwor Almaciya Yeesu.
PHI 4:20 na yeu dobti duktongka la nuwece fo kwama ki tebe in di diiri a tinyo.
PHI 4:21 yarum gwam nubo na bwangka kwama ce mwor Almasiya Yeesu. gwam yitub mi bbo ci wari ka-nge moweu ci ma yarumeti.
PHI 4:22 gwam nob bwangka kereko ci mayarumeti, tam in co nubo buro ci yim yiye Kaisare.
PHI 4:23 dobti luma Teluwe Yeesu Almasiya na yi wari ki yuwa tangbe kume ko. Atinyo.
COL 1:1 Bulus Nii ttomange Yeecu Kriritti ki maka kwama, kange Timoti yibe.
COL 1:2 Tom bo ne bilenker kange kebbebo mor Almacifu mor kolosiyawa ba, ciya ki ciyeu, Nyori luma kange fur nener ayi ari kange kom, fiya kwama tebe iyeu.
COL 1:3 Nyo min ma buka kangek kwama nen, Te teluwe be Yecu Kritti, nyo kwob kumen diloti, kir-kir,
COL 1:4 Nyon mwa ki bilelnker kume mor Kritti Yeecu, kange ciuka ko kom ciko dor nob kwama bo cak-cakeu.
COL 1:5 Kom wiki cuika ko wo, wori kom ki yoneri yom na kume lo kwama. Kon nuwa dor yoneriro wo, na nimre mor bilenker, fulen ker.
COL 1:6 Wuro bou kumeneu, fulen kero ti tui, la ti bui fiyemin gwam dor bitiner. mawo kumen kom ki diye wo ka nuwam co la ka merangum dor luma kwamak bicom.
COL 1:7 Won co fulenkero na wo mo merang Abafara canga be ba cui cuiyeu won canga kritti tum nyi be nii bilenker.
COL 1:8 Abafaras ni nyo cuika kume ko mor yuwatangbe kwama.
COL 1:9 Ker cuika ka ro wo diye nyo nuwameu, nyo dob bo kwob ka dilo dorkumer. Nyo ti mai na ko dim ki nyomka nerer cek, kange ne ka kwamak, kange nyomka yuwa tangbek.
COL 1:10 Nyo kwob diloti na ko ya yom bo daten kange Teluwe, ki mure wwo a fo cinen tiyeu. nyo kwob diloti nyo ki kan ne bbitutti mor nagenero ken, na ko ii mor nyomka cek.
COL 1:11 Nyo kwob diloti ko ma bi kwamer nerer mor nyomka ki bi kwan duktangka cek. kange birom nerer kange dange.
COL 1:12 Nyo kwob diloti kan ma buka kangek fur neerer Tee nin wo doki ka fiya mor kwali nob kwamar mor filang wucakkeu.
COL 1:13 Con yoo boliyar kumtaciler, yila ken ki bo liyar bi bwece co cui-cuiyeu.
COL 1:14 Fiye bwe nine bafiya fanka, tabka bwiran kerer.
COL 1:15 Bweu co cer kang na kwama wo mani fur reu. Bwe kaba dike fwele gwam.
COL 1:16 La cinen dikero gwam fwele, buro diyeu kange buro bitineu, wo toti toweu, kange dike wo mani to tiyeu, kaka kange liyar tinnim kange Bikwan kerer, dikero gwam co ca fwel ciye, lana ce.
COL 1:17 Con wi na nimre dikero gwam, more c la dikero mwerkangume.
COL 1:18 Lam co dor bwiyer ki wabero, co kabau, kange bwe kabau mor nubo bwiyarangumeu. La con wiki fiye kaba mor dikere gwam.
COL 1:19 La kwama ma fur neerer toki dika ceko gwam a yi morece.
COL 1:20 Na co yuwelkangum fiye bwe wiyeu, dikero gwam cinen. Kwama ma fur neerer, wo buyale ce cori dor koblom batiyem. Kwama yuwelkangum dikero gwam cinen ki bwici. kaka co dikero bitinereu kaka con wo diyeu,
COL 1:21 Fiya co kom fabub kwama nen nob kiyeb ceb mor neere, kange ma ka dikero bwir.
COL 1:22 La na weu, con yuwel kangum kom ki bwiciu fiye bwareu. Co mawo na co neken kom wucak man ki kurom.
COL 1:23 Na kom ca kaba ti mor bilenker di, kulumkue, Tim tiye buro mani kutar cunga fiye yoneri fulen kerero, a nuwu. Won co fulenkerero yi nubo fwelfwele tob kange lo kwamau, won co fulen kerero mo bulus ma yilam caga.
COL 1:24 Naweu, miti bilangi ki dotange miu dor kumer, mor bwiye min dim dikero kum mor dotange Almasihu, wo bwiciu, co ku wabeu.
COL 1:25 Ki woro kuwabeu yila canga, ki nagen do kwama ney dor kumereu, na dim tomange kwama.
COL 1:26 Wuro co yurke bicome wo yurangum yurange, coti kange kaltinum. La na weu, cin fweltangu nob kwama bo wucak nen.
COL 1:27 La cinen kwama cuiti na co fweltangu cuweka duktangka yurke bilenker tiber nob kumta cile. nungi Alamacifu more kume. Nyomka duktangkako botiyeu.
COL 1:28 Co nyo ne fulen cero tiye, ne ci biwerti kange merangka gwam ciyek ki nyomka gwam, la na bo ne nubo dim diye gwam mor Yeecu.
COL 1:29 Ki dor wor ma nangenti mi yokten bi kwanti ki bikwan cero wo managen ti minen ki bi kwaneu.
COL 2:1 Ma cuit na kon yumom kambo ma kala dor kumereu, wori nubo buro lawudi kaya kange burom bo ducce tom tikob mib wi nuwe kange teu.
COL 2:2 man ma nagen na neerciro fiya bikwan fiye mwerka ciyek mor cuika, ya ciko cweka ciyen gwam wo bicome kange nyomka yurke bilenker kwama mor Kritti.
COL 2:3 More ce fiye yoka Yulanek kange nyomka yukragume.
COL 2:4 Ma tok wo kati kange kwob kang kom ki keti bibolere.
COL 2:5 Bwenno ma man kange kom mor nageu, la man wi kange kom mor yuwa tangbe. Mati bilangi, to yimo kom more ceu na ken kange bikwan bilenkerer ero mor Almasifu.
COL 2:6 Kambo ka yom Almacifu Teluwe, kom ya yam kumem morece.
COL 2:7 Kom kulum more ce, ko mum morece, ko kulum bilenker na wo merang kumeneu, ko lerum buka kangek.
COL 2:8 Ko bii yora kati yilo kange kwobkom ki nyomka kange bi beiyo bwir wo dam nubom ki bwangka dikero wo kaleu, kebo na Almasifu ce.
COL 2:9 More ce dii ka kwama ko gwam mor bwiye nunge.
COL 2:10 Kom dim more ce, won co kaba bikwaneko gwam, kange liyar.
COL 2:11 Mor co ci biye kumen lare, ki biyekako wo kebo nubo fir mani mor cok ka tee bwiyek. La mor biyeka kriti.
COL 2:12 Fuwerum kom wari mor yuka mwegk kwamak. la more ce ci kung kom mor bilenker kibi kwan kwamar, wo kung co bwareu.
COL 2:13 kwatti kom bwiyam mor karika kerek kume kange bwinin biyeka bwikume ko, con yilam ki kom ki dume wari kange co la tab binen ki ketiro ba kangeu.
COL 2:14 Con nyinangu cen kumero mulangum mulangeu, kange bidoti ciyeu, con tum ciro nunge ki kulka ko koblom bwatiye meu.
COL 2:15 con kubangum bikwantini kange liyar tinim, con kwinm kercir nure nube, con turani dor cir ki kulka ko koblom batiyeu.
COL 2:16 Na nyori kange ama kumen bolang mor caka kange nokar kangeri, cuiyak ko fwir, kaka kakuk fobka.
COL 2:17 Won co kakilok diker buro boutiyeu. La kendo Almasifu.
COL 2:18 kange ni cui cukka duwekti ki wabka nb tomangebo wucakeu a m kumen bolang na ko fiyare cuner kwamaro. mwan nii ro wo ki do mor dike ca toweu, la yilam ni bikwan dorek ki kwaneri ce wo bwiyeu.
COL 2:19 Mani mwerkangum kange dor. Mor dore bwiyo gwam kange niyetimun ma nagentinye la ci mwerum wari. Tidui ki duikako kwama ne tiyeu.
COL 2:20 Na ko bwiyam kange Almasifu ki yuwa kelkeliyo dor bitinereri yebo ko da dan kumenti na mwi kom kino tuwer kalere.
COL 2:21 ko tare, ko twire, ko kere?
COL 2:22 Dikero burom bo dika ciyeko kayaka, nama nagen tiki ci ki bidoti kangemerang ka nifirek.
COL 2:23 Werfun d wo wi ki nyomka wo bwiyoceu, lan bwnakakoce, wo kin koni wo cuwe kanka kange ne ka bwiyek dotange. La ci man ki kange nangen dor diwo bwiyo cuiti yeu.
COL 3:1 na kwama kung kom kange Kritti di, ku dika wo diyeu, fiye Kritti yim wi kang ko ctiyer kwamareu.
COL 3:2 Kwa ki dike wo dii kwamau, kebo dike buro bitineu.
COL 3:3 La kom bwiyam dume kume yurangum yurange wari kange Almasifu mor kwama.
COL 3:4 kambo Almasifu cer knagu weu, worom co dume kume, la kom kenu kan cerkangi kange co mor duktangka cek.
COL 3:5 Kom twalum dikang ka nuwe kofo dor bitinereeu, burotum kane kayatum bwini wucake, dilangkako bwir. wuro bwirayeu kange wuro co wbka fulenku.
COL 3:6 Dor dike buro fumer kwama ro a bou ti dor bibei bongtuuwe.
COL 3:7 mor dikero buro ma dam kumenbe, kwatti ko yim more ciyeu.
COL 3:8 La caneu tam kom dubom buro, cilonka neererk, funer kwabaan ka ko bwir, torkanka, kange kettito yang-yange nyi kom.
COL 3:9 Kom ceur de bwiti nn cuirke wori kon cokum nii a, r ko kange naen cero.
COL 3:10 Kom merum ni fwir, wo fulonti mor anyo ka ki dimer wo ya felceu.
COL 3:11 Co fiye bacline man kange bayafude nii biyemeu, kange wo biyebeu. s faabub canga nii cerum cereu, baubawa kenon bacikitiye, La Almasifu co gwam, wi mr gwameu.
COL 3:12 Ki dur kumer na wa kwama cok cokeu, nubo wucakkeu, kange ma cuitiyeu, La kom merum cinin nagen do kentinim yiber duwer, taka kange dangeu.
COL 3:13 Ma dangne kange bwiti, kom ma bwitinin luma, n kange wi ki kwama ka duwek kange keceri, kom cutangwi nawo Teluwe cutang kume wiyeu.
COL 3:14 lam dike buro gwam, ko yilam ki cuika woron co dika nyomkake.
COL 3:15 luma Almasifuro a tun neer kumero, kiker lumaro wo cocokeu, me mor bwiyo wi. Kom bu'u kang.
COL 3:16 Ko dob ker Almasifuro a yi more kume bwimbwiye. Ki nyomka gwam kom merangi ko mwe bwiti ti ki jabure, kange nuwe caklang k, kana mwe yuwa tangbe. kom ti kabi wari ki buka kangek mor neere kume fiye kwama wiyeu.
COL 3:17 Dike ka ma gwam mor kere kange nagen ko mani gwam mor den Teluwe Yeecu. Kom bukanti kwama Tee more ce.
COL 3:18 Natubo ko ne nabarub kume bo dur kambo dateneu mor Teluwe.
COL 3:19 nabarubbo kon cui natub kumeb bo kom kulang cire.
COL 3:20 bibeyo ko ne Tebkumebo diker gwam teramde bibeiyo kati yilo ci cwam tai.
COL 3:21 Kom tebbo ko terande bibeiyo kati yilo ci cuwam tai.
COL 3:22 Cangab ko ne teluwe kume dur ko mor dikero gwam, kebo toka nuwe ko ce kebo na fur nob nin neer, La ki bilenker mor neere kume, ko ca tai teluwe kume.
COL 3:23 Dike ko matiyeu ko manangen wo mor neerer kume, wo teluwe ceu kebo na nobo ciye.
COL 3:24 Ko nyumom kiwo kan yo cuner wo kwalito ce fiye Teluweu. Wori Aasifu Yeecu ko bwangten tiye.
COL 3:25 Na niwo ma bwini cakcake di an yo cuner bwini cakcake camaneu. la cuika dorek mani.
COL 4:1 Kom teluweb, kon ne canga kumeu dike dong-dong wo daten kana ciyeu. Kom nyumom kom wi ki Teluwe dii.
COL 4:2 Kom Ca kaba mor kwama wom kobka dilok.
COL 4:3 Ko kob dilo wari dor nyer, na kwama wom nyilo wo kero ceu, natok yurke kritti la co ma kumkuwe.
COL 4:4 ko kwob dilo nan nyumom tok ka ceko dong dong, nawo daten tokeu.
COL 4:5 Ko ya yam ki yulan kange nubo o kaleu, ko ma nangen beri tungande.
COL 4:6 Ker kume ro kir kir a yilam ker lumar. la a yilam ki luma nuwaka, na ko nyumom kam kak kar nubo nen tiyeu.
COL 4:7 La kange dike buro ma more cou, Tikiku an yi fwetan kumen ci. co yimi ma cui cuiyeu, con far canga mi mor Teluwe. Matoum co kumenceu cowo na nyumom dike nyo more ceu, na ne kom bikwan neerer.
COL 4:9 Ma tuom co kange Onicimus wo ma ciya ciya yibe win more kume wo ma cui cuiye. Ci an yi kom gwam dike bwi feu.
COL 4:10 Arictakus far kuka miko yarum komti, kange Markus yii Barnaba (wuro dorcer ka fiya ker ki nyilae na bouri ko yoco).
COL 4:11 Kange Yeecu wo coti Yucteu, ci kwaci mor faru ngeneb mibo biyem lare farub nageneb wo liyar kwamaro ceu. cin yilam birom neerer fiye mi wiyeu.
COL 4:12 abafaras Yarum komti com win more kumenin la canga Almasifu Yeecu. Kir kiri kwob kumen diloti, na ko tim dimdiye na bilenkerero ceu mor dike kwama cuiye.
COL 4:13 Na wark ti dor cer la con ma nangenti ki bi kwan dor kumer, kange nubo wo lawudikiya kange nubo wo mafuliyeu.
COL 4:14 Luka nii Nyinonge wo ba cuiteu kange dimac. yarum kom ti.
COL 4:15 Kom yarum kebbebo wo lawudikiyau, kange nimf kange ku wabe loceu.
COL 4:16 kambo kiye kumen tomange wo tiber kumere di, La na kiye ten tak ku wabe wo lawudi kiyau, ko Nyumom kom kiye tomange wo lawudukiya.
COL 4:17 Ko yi Arkiba co ayo neerrcer nagen do ca yo mr Teluwe wori na ci dim.
COL 4:18 Yarume wo ki kang mik Bulus. Ko kwabi ki kuka miko luma ayi kange kom.
1TH 1:1 Bulus nin, ka-nge Sila ka-nge Timoti, na ne bikur wabero Tassabinka
1TH 1:2 ka-nge kang nyone buka ka-ngekti kwama nin ki kom gwam, nawo nyo dok komti mor dulo nyeu.
1TH 1:3 nyo bulangti man ki kurongka kabum kwama ben Teebe nangen kumero bilengke, nangen cwikaro, ka-nge birum nee, bikwan bwiyer wo kabeu mor Teluwe be Yeesu kiristi.
1TH 1:4 keb mi bo kwama cwiyeu, man nyumom con cok kom.
1TH 1:5 wori fulendo nya bo kumen cikeu kebo ker koni, mor bikwane, mor yuwa tangbe wucake, ka-nge mor ciyeka. nyo more kume, ker kumer.
1TH 1:6 kom yilam nob bitengar nyeb ka-nge wo Teluwe ceu na wuro kom nyo kere mwor datange ki for neered fiye yuwa
1TH 1:7 na ciro kom yilam danka cinin gwam mor makadoniya ka-nge Akaya wo ne bilengkeu.
1TH 1:8 dii kumen ker Teluwe ro ker kwamaro bwiye, kebo ka makadoniya ka-nge Akaya. nyeu fiye gwam bilengke kume kwama nineu yakane, na co nyeu, nyo cwibo nyo tok ka-nge diker.
1TH 1:9 ci ki bwici cin tok twati bokaka nyo bo kume nen, cin toki kambo ka yilaken kwama nineu, ka dubom fulenen, na ko bwanten kwama wo ki dumeu, ka-nge bilengke.
1TH 1:10 cin toki ki kom cen boka bi bwecekti dii kwama, wo a kung nubo bwiyameu wo con Yeesu wo cokbo mor funero bouti yeu.
1TH 2:1 dige bwi kom, nyimom yitub mibo boka nyeko ki menen kebo koni.
1TH 2:2 kom, kom nyimom kambo ci nekom datange kange birum neri mwor Almachiya. dige bwiyeu nan makimen ker kwamaro dotange ducce.
1TH 2:3 dige bwiyeu ker nyero yake fiye ki wiye kom kebo nubo bwit, bwentano mwor dwitiri. dii kebo na kani ce.
1TH 2:4 tano nyori kambo kwama ciya ka-nge be. nyila nebo kero na lume ce, dila nyo yi tok kertiye. nyo tok kerti kebo na na nubo bilangyo. la nyo ki na yi bilang kwama. dige bwiyeu co cuwa neryero tiye.
1TH 2:5 dige bwiyeu nyi Makimenbo lima yewi, bwentano windi na wuro ki nyome, ka-nge cungi ki yulang, na wuro kwama co ni nyom kabe
1TH 2:6 la nyo dobo dwiyingka wi nubo nin kakka wi kimen kakka nubo ka-nge nin naki nyin cwidi no nyitin ma nangen ki bi dwiyer nyero wo nyom ka Almachiya.
1TH 2:7 na curo nyori, nyon dubom bi dwir nyero tiber kumer na wuro nee ki mare bi beiyo locenin dangne wi nyo.
1TH 2:8 no nyori nyi wi ki cwika tiber kumer, kebo ker Almachiya ki kwaco nyo ma kumen tiye dila ka-nge ner nyero ki dor kimer, dige bwiyeu ki cwika nyinen.
1TH 2:9 kom kwa, kebmibo, ki nangen nyero ka-nge dotange nyeu. kakuk ka-nge kume nyo ma nangenti kati yilo nyi cub ka-ngen kumem mendo nin nangen. ki kwama wuro nyi makimen ker kwama tiye.
1TH 2:10 kom nob warkeb, la nyo wo kwama ce, kambo nyo yii-yim luma ka-nge liyer ka-nge. ka-nge ker digero bwir wi kumen wuro kom ne bilengke.
1TH 2:11 no nyori kom nyimom kambo nyo mati ka-nge kom me, kambo tee ka-nge bwe, kambo na wuro nyo nyi kom kere datenne ka-nge wuro fwetang kome nyon nyitin kom dige datenne.
1TH 2:12 na kom ya yambo daten ka-nge kwama, wuro cuwo kom mwor liyarcer ka-nge duktangka ceko.
1TH 2:13 co diye bwi nyi bwi kwama nin ti kangka. dige bwiye ki kwama kom yo ker kwamare wi nubo buro ka-nge nubo buro kom nuwa, na wuro yeu ker kwama, wo co kero wuro mannangti kumene wuro kom ne bilengke
1TH 2:14 na dor ma nangti ki bi kur kwama wuro Yafudiya ki den bi bwe kwama kiristi dige bwiyeu kom nuwa dotange na nawoyeu wi nubo bitinekume, kambo nob dinglinka.
1TH 2:15 Yafudawa ci twalum teluwe, kiristi ka-nge tange nin nob duk kume la Yafudawa tak yuwa ciye, ci mabo kwama nin. diri, ci kwakangti ka-nge tangenin nubo.
1TH 2:16 cin kwa kum nyo tokka keret ka-nge nubo kati yilo ci fiye fuloka na curo nyori kang-kang ci fiya kero bwiti la ki bwiri funero yilaken dor ciyer.
1TH 2:17 kom nuwa yitum mibo, nyon malang kimen kwama bidob, na bilengke ce, kebo mwor nere, nyin ma dige datene na wuro nya to tikob kumebo tiye.
1TH 2:18 dige bwiyeu neryer nyi cwi toka kimeboti, mo Bulus kebo kiristi win la bwekelkele ywa nyo.
1TH 2:19 la nye fuwor nere kume kabe, kaka kuru kakka yilang duwe liyare, wi kabum teluwe kiristi ki dige boka cek? kakka kebo ke kom ka, ka-nge tangnim nobom?
1TH 2:20 dige biyeu kom ki liyar nyero ka-nge fuwoka ner neyer.
1TH 3:1 Tano nyori, no nyiti dolbo mwiruka, la nyi to daten nyo tim Atina buridin.
1TH 3:2 co nyo tom Timoti, ka-nge yii nye ka-nge canga kwama ki ker Almachiya, na yilam tikabi ka-nge dange ka-nge kom fiye bilengke.
1TH 3:3 nyo mayo kati ka-nge tiber kumer na yarangi ki den dotange, dige biyeu kom ki bwi kimi kom nyom kambo ci cuwo kome.
1TH 3:4 bilengke, ki kwama nyo wari ka-nge kome, nyon yikom nyi kino bidom ka-nge dotange. la nyo tak yilame na wuro kom nyimome.
1TH 3:5 dige bwiyeu mi dolbo mwirum ka dige bwi mi tom ki men na kom nyimom fiye bilengke kume wiye. ka-ngeri bwekelkele boulum kom nure ka-nge dila dotange beu yilamnyo koni.
1TH 3:6 daten Timoti na yilau cunga kumek na ci bou nyinen ki tomange wo limi nyowe dor bilengke kume ka-nge cwika kume ko cin nyiyo ki ma dige dateneti doryer, la kom bilang cwika nyekti nawo nyi cwitoka kume tiye.
1TH 3:7 dige bwiyeu, yitob mibo, nyin fiya ker kumero fiye kom wiye na bilengke kume ce dige bwiyeu ki ker bwuwaka ner nyero ka-nge dotange nye.
1TH 3:8 can neu nyi ki fuloka, no kom ti ki bi kwandi mwor kwamari.
1TH 3:9 dila buka ka-nge ko wuni nya ma kwama nin tiye ki den kumer dige bwiye fuwor ner nyero gwam wo nyi cikeu wi ka bumkwama ki kom?
1TH 3:10 kume ka-nge kakuk nyi kwob ki men duloti na nyi to tikob kimebo. na nyo dim dige kom fiya be mwor bilengke kume.
1TH 3:11 nyo kwama ka-nge tee ka-nge bi bwece ka-nge Teluwe be kiristi na bwangten ki na nye ko fiye ki wiye
1TH 3:12 no nyori Teluwe na ti dobti kom bwii ki cwika yitub kumebo ka-nge nubo gwam, na wo nyi ma kumentiye
1TH 3:13 Tano nyori naco mani nyo tikalinnin mwor nere kume na yilam kero ke na wo yoryore kabum kwama ka-nge Teluwe ki kwama ka-nge boka Teluwe kiristi gwam ka-nge duktange cekko.
1TH 4:1 kambo cuwam bwireu, kebmibo nyo ne kom bikwan ka-nge nyo werang komti mwor tee kiristi. kambo kiyo kero nyinen kambo yilam koka mani morece na kom yayam yora ka-nge kwama, ki nure wuro kom cu, di na kom cu nyo.
1TH 4:2 dige bwiye kom nyimom kero yii yikome mwor Teluwe kiristi.
1TH 4:3 nyo co ner kwama cokum kom, coki kom yilam nure kayaka ka-nge kayatum.
1TH 4:4 buti kume ki tam wice mwor liyar ka-nge dugtongka
1TH 4:5 nuwa cinen dotange dige daten be, nawuro nubo nyombo kwama ki mare
1TH 4:6 ni ka-nge ca mara cabli daka yice, ce ki ker bilengka dige bwiyeu kwama atinma bwokang ker dige wuro fiya nubo tiye. nawo ki bwii nyo werangkome yilo nyi tokker dor cereu.
1TH 4:7 dige bwiye kwama cuwobo ki ker dwiti la ki ker yim twai kwama wo dwiti mani ye.
1TH 4:8 Tano nyori gwam niwo wureri kebo nob kweneb mib dila kwama niwo neken liyar cere duktangka cekeu nyo kumen.
1TH 4:9 nyo ka-nge cwika yitub kimebo, ka-nge ni mani cacub kumen mulangkati, la kom ki bwi kumi kwama nung kumen cwika keb kimeb.
1TH 4:10 kwaneri mani, kom mati nyo ki den keb kumeb gwam wo yim maki doniya dila nyo werang komti yitub mibo, kom nyo nawo ka-nge cubka.
1TH 4:11 kom ma dige datene kom yiken fiye kutan kom kwa ki kero nyi kome, kom ma nangen ki kang kumek, kambo nyo yi kom firen bwiyeu.
1TH 4:12 kom mayo na yam kumembo na ma dong-dong kabum nubo buro nebo bilengke dila atan yilam kom mani more maka dige kebo na kene.
1TH 4:13 nyo cwibo kom yilam manki nur fwetangka, ki nubo buro dam dume, kati yilo kom dam-dum na nubo buro no manki bilengker dige kabe.
1TH 4:14 Tano bi neken bilengkedi kiristi more ciye.
1TH 4:15 dige bwiye nyi yi kom bo wuro mworker Teluwe, bo wuro biwarce naweu na yaken di boka Teluwe, twai mani ba yulum nubo buro dam dometi.
1TH 4:16 dige bwiyeu kwama ce ki bwici an bou ki dir ni tomange dur la nubo bwiyam mwor Almachiya ci ter kwen kako.
1TH 4:17 la wuro ci dobe wari ka-nge beu bi kwar cer ciyeu ciyan tuken bo mwor bilortinim, bi wab kan ka-nge Teluwe mwor dii kwama na curo nyo ba kutatiye ka-nge wari ka-nge Teluwe
1TH 4:18 Tano nyori kom ne ki dangne wi ka-nge keb kime bo nin ki kero buro.
1TH 5:1 no woyeu, ki ker kwamawo ka-nge kalewo, kom mani ki cwi dige a mulang kumen tiye
1TH 5:2 dige bwiyeu kom ki bwi kumi kom nyom yora ki di boka kwama wi nyo na ni kuwe na kume,
1TH 5:3 kambo tok ker yim lumati ka-nge dam narem ken, di bwaro bou kin diye man ki kume an yilam na, nawiye boro, na, nawiye ki fwere man fi cerka.
1TH 5:4 la kom yi tobmib, ki mani mwor kumta cili, na kume wuro na bo kimen na ni kuwe.
1TH 5:5 gwam kume kom bi bei filang, ke bibei ka kuke, nyo kebo bibeikume.
1TH 5:6 nyo kom doredum na wuro ka-ngembo ki mare tano na curo nyori bi yim ki bati ka-nge yim fwetangka yora.
1TH 5:7 dige bwiyeu nubo dadum tiye ki da ki kume nyo nubo notiyeu ki no ki kume.
1TH 5:8 kaubo bibei ka kukeu la bi yim yora, nyo bi yo kwor bilengke ka-nge wo cwi kakko ce na bi ner bero firen dii kwama.
1TH 5:9 kwama yibo ki na bi to kayaka nercer la nabi fiya a fuloka ki den Teluwe be kiristi Almachiya ciya.
1TH 5:10 co niwo bwiya ki den bere, bwenta bi kwarce kakka bwiyam, bi wari ka-nge co
1TH 5:11 Tano nyori kom ne dangne ka-nge kebkime bo nakom cikang buti na wuro kom matiye.
1TH 5:12 nyo kinong komti kebmibo kom ne dur nubo buro ma nangen tiber kimere, wuro tam ka-nge kom makumen nangen tiye ki den Teluwe, nubo buro ki nang kome.
1TH 5:13 nyo konong komti tak, kom nunga cinen nure kom nung cinen cwika nyo na dige kendo wuro ci manangtiyeu na kom yii yim lumam ka-nge ci.
1TH 5:14 nyo maki men dige datenne ti na kero kom manang cuko macine neu. tano na curo ki kom matika digero ken wuro nubo nuwa luma kimen nubo kwarub kom ci kande ci ka-nge.
1TH 5:15 kom to ka-nge a ya'are kece nin cile ki cile nyeu kom do bwiti nin dikero ken na gwamece.
1TH 5:16 Bila-ngi kang-kang
1TH 5:17 Kwob dulo man ki yiloka.
1TH 5:18 Mor diger gwam nee buka ka-ngek wo co cwika kwama mor kiristi Yeesu ki kom.
1TH 5:19 Domde yuwa tangbeko wucake.
1TH 5:20 Cwekangde to'oka dukume.
1TH 5:21 cuwa digero gwam, ko tam dige yoryore.
1TH 5:22 co-ngum gwam cile more kume.
1TH 5:23 kwama wo lumace ca yilam ki kom nubo ken, la gwam kume kom yilam ki bwiyer kumero, ner kumero bwikume, na yilam muwerum mwere man ki dwiti kana ken na boka Teluwe be cuwo kiristi Almachiya.
1TH 5:24 niwo kome ni kendo ken.
1TH 5:25 kebmibbo kom dulo ki denyer.
1TH 5:26 kom yarum kebkimebo gwam ka-nge nubo kendo.
1TH 5:27 mi kinong komti ki den Teluwe kom cuwo bifumer na nubo ceye gwam ki kwobka dulo
1TH 5:28 dila luma kwama kiristi Almachiya na yilam wari ka-nge kom.
2TH 1:1 Bulus, Silbannus ka-nge Timothy, fiye ku wabe fiye Tasolonika mor kwama Tebe ka-nge Yeesu Almasihu.
2TH 1:2 dila luma abon monteng ka-nge furneret fiye kwama Tebe ka-nge Teluwe be Yeesu Almasihu.
2TH 1:3 nyo bi bukan kwama nen kankan wori kom bi yiteng. nyon dong-dong. na bikengke kumeko yuteng yora, kam cwika bwiti kumeko yutenti.
2TH 1:4 nyo ki dorger nyoki kurak bwi ki kom nob kwama. nyo tongker borum nere kimeti ka-nge bilengke kume mor dotangkom moreceu. nyo tongker ka-nge kale kom bimneret.
2TH 1:5 woco yurom burak kwama ko kendo. makako nyo co ciya to komti nobo ken na liyar wo kom duwa dotange ti dorceru.
2TH 1:6 wucak fiye kwama wiye wo a nyoken dotange fiye nobo cwilankome tiye.
2TH 1:7 yila ne kom fwoka nakom tum dotange wari ka-nge nyo. a manyo naci tok Teluwe Yeesu firen di kwama ka-nge nob tomangece ki bikwan cer.
2TH 1:8 mor kire mwen mwewa tum fange dor nobo nyoker Teluwe bei Yeesu Almasihu.
2TH 1:9 ciya nowa doktange dur waber diri-diri tikom Teluwe ka-nge duktangka bigwam co.
2TH 1:10 man ma wo ki kwama wo co bwitiye kiker nobe a duktangka co tiye, cin yarum yumanka fiye nobo gwam ne bilengke nako ne bilengke tomangkako more kume.
2TH 1:11 ki wolo nyo kom duroti kan, kang. ker kumer nyo gwam duro na kwama bei a toki komduwa bicorkimero. nyo gwam diroti cinyaki nankumero wo maka digero kendongceu ka-nge neken bilengke ka-nge bikwan.
2TH 1:12 nyo kwab dilo na den Teluwe bei Yeesu na fiya duktangka fiye kom wiye. dilo nyo co ciya duktangka kom ki luma kwama bei ka-nge Teluwe bei Yeesu Almasihu.
2TH 2:1 nawo kibo Teluwe bei Yeesu Almasihu ka-nge mwerkonge kabeka ki wabka wori ka-nge co, nyo ki nan ka bmibo.
2TH 2:2 kankatangde bwokanko ka-nge katangka kiker yuwako ka-nge murungka kowo cakange wo nyen, wotangti ki bwoko Teluwe wari lam.
2TH 2:3 ka-nge nii win a bolkomde ka-nge nure. wori kakuko ka-nge mani aboti na nii wo bwegige bo na nung nii bontu con bwe bwore.
2TH 2:4 wo co niwo kabe, cowo kungdor ceroti fiye kwab ci com kwama tiye ka-nge wo ci bwentang tiye. maka konyo an yeram fiye kwama wiye ki togki co kwama.
2TH 2:5 kom kwabo ki kwama wo mi wari ka-ngekom ye mi yi kom digero buro.
2TH 2:6 na wong kom nyumom dige timki coye, wori cin toki ki kwama wo datenen.
2TH 2:7 nawon yunka maborang tiye manageti.
2TH 2:8 najimde naci nung nii banktun, wo Teluwe Yeesu a menrangtiye ki fwobom nice. Teluwe anyakeng co kebo diger kebo kibo kacan.
2TH 2:9 ni bongtuwo an bou, ki nange bwekerkere ka-nge bikwang, yurom ka-nge diger yuka cwarke.
2TH 2:10 ka-nge gwam borkako na bwini wucak koce dige wo an yilam diger yarko, wori ci yobo cwika bilengke kebo ciya furonka.
2TH 2:11 ki dige wo bwinye kwama tuncinen cwerkanka na ci ciya curke.
2TH 2:12 nyori gwam ciye ciyan macine borangko, nubo buro ciyabo ki bilengkeu ci nuwa cworketi.
2TH 2:13 dila nyo bucinen kanti kang kom fiye kwama wiye wori kom bi yitang woro Teluwe conkom yilam bi bei kaba nakom fiya furonka mor wucakkeu yuwa ka-nge ciyaka ka-nge bilengke.
2TH 2:14 wo co dige co kwama fiye ker furankero wiye na kom fiya duktangka Teluwe Yeesu Almasihu.
2TH 2:15 na wo kebmibo kom tiki bilengke kom tam dige ci merang kumen, ka-nge ki ker ka-ngen ki murang.
2TH 2:16 na wo Teluwe Yeesu Almasihu ki dorcer, ka-nge kwama tebe wo cwibe anebo bwoniri womanki dige ka-nge bikwan don ker wori kabum fiye luma.
2TH 2:17 a bikumen ner ka-nge moner kumenro mor nanen kendoni.
2TH 3:1 nawo kebmibo kom kwob nyinen dilo ker Teluwe na ya wulom na fiya duktangka kambo warika-nge kome.
2TH 3:2 kom kwab dilo be na fiya cirka fiye nobo gwam ki bilengke.
2TH 3:3 dila Teluwe be, ni luma, co wo a ywikom tiye na cerkom fiye cile.
2TH 3:4 nyon ki bi kwan mor Teluwe dor kumer ki komti mani, take kom ca kaba maka digero nyo yi koe,
2TH 3:5 Teluwe a bwantenki ner kumero mor cwika kwama ka-nge birum ne Almasiya.
2TH 3:6 na wcu nyo ka-nge dokkomti mor dene Teluwe Yeesu Almasiya kom yeri ka-nge kebe wo yim koniye kebo dambo yuwa fiye nyo wiye.
2TH 3:7 wori kom ki bwi kom, kom nyimom yori kabo kom meranngi ki nyo, yibo more kume na wuro men ki mweka.
2TH 3:8 nyo ca bo cari ka-nge nii wo nyo yacebe, nyeu nyon ma nangen kume ka-nge kakuk mor dotange ka-nge kalaka, kari nyo kumen titum.
2TH 3:9 nyo ma nyo, nungbo nyo manki bikwam, na di nyo mane, bena nyo yilam chker merangka kumen.
2TH 3:11 fiya nyo wari ka-nge kome nyo dokkom nii wo mani cwi maka nangenneu, ca la ka doranka loni ka-ngen.
2TH 3:12 wank nobo wuro nyo dokriye, tak nyo ne ci kwanti mor Teluwe Yeesu Almaciya ci ma nangen yora, ciya ca cari citi.
2TH 3:13 di keb mibo kom dobre maka dige wo dong-dong.
2TH 3:14 Tano ka-nge ko ciya ka ka-nge ker nyero di mor bifumero wo, kom ma yora kom mare naniya ka-nge co, be na co nuwa kwenduwe.
2TH 3:15 kom to cori nyo na nii kiye, di komyi co ki lumer nyo na kekume.
2TH 3:16 di Teluwe daka ne ca nekum da ka neko kirkir bwen nure wini Teluwe a yi wari ka-nge kom. gwam
2TH 3:17 woro co yarume mi, mo Bulus ki ka-ngemik wo co yirum bo mor bifumer miro nin. nyo ma mulangtiye
2TH 3:18 di luma Teluwe be Yeesu Amaciya a yi wari ka-nge kom gwam.
1TI 1:1 Bulu, nii tomange Almaciya Yecu ki dokka Kwama nii fulo ka be, kange Almaciya yoka nere bek.
1TI 1:2 Mulangum ki Timoti, bi bwe mi bi com mor bilenke: Luma, jireduwe, kange fuwor neret fiye Kwama kange Almaciya Yecu Tee luwe be.
1TI 1:3 Kambo ma kinong nen na mwi mani fiyaco ma yaken ti Makidoniyau, tim mwe Afisa ri namo dok kangem nobem ciya merangde kange merang kako ki dimene, wi mwer kutume ti, nyi tikanka bati Kwama, mor bilenke.
1TI 1:4 ciya cuware tu nuwaka keti bi dange kange bwanka dike manki dika. wuro mwerkang kutume, nyi tikali bati Kwama fiye bilenke.
1TI 1:5 Dike bolangko nung tiyeu cwika mor nero wucakke kange dume wucakke kange bilenke.
1TI 1:6 Kangem nobo tiyangum ciin yilaken kelkelito bwir.
1TI 1:7 cii cwiti ciin yilam nob merangka bolange dila cii nyombo dike cii tok tiye kange dike cii ti dorcere.
1TI 1:8 Dila bon nyumom bolangko yorikabo tano manangen ciko nure datene ri.
1TI 1:9 Di bon nyumom wo, bolange kebo ki nii wucakke, dila ki nobo mani bwangten werfunner, nobo ki kungka duweke kange buro mani bwangten Kwama kange nob bwirangke, kange wo man ki Kwama, kange nob dilaka, ciin ne bolangko ki nobo twal teb tiye, kange wo twal neb tiye, kange nobo twal dor tiye.
1TI 1:10 Ki nob burotum, nabarubbo dati kange nabarub kakaa natubbo dati kange natubbe, ki nobo kuu nob tiye naci ya kici canga, ki nob cwerkeb kange nob warke cwerkeb, kange gwam dike ma kiyeti kange dikero wo na keneu.
1TI 1:11 Werfunne wo dor fullen kerer Kwama na bi bwiyerce, wo ci ne take.
1TI 1:12 Mi bukang ti Almaciya Yecu Teluwebe. Wo neye bikwane, wori cin ciya kange mo, yoye mor nangene ce.
1TI 1:13 Fiya co no min nii dilaka, nii ne dotange tiye, nii kwenang ka dila gwam kange wo cin ciyaye wori ma macwo mor kumtacili kange bwini neka bilenke.
1TI 1:14 Dila luma Teluwe beko coru minen duce kange bilenke, kange cwika kako wo mor Almaciya Yecu.
1TI 1:15 Fulendo wo bilenke, daten yoka gwam, wo yiki Almaciya bo dor bitiner na fulo nob bwirangke. Mo nii wo ceu bwira ki dariye.
1TI 1:16 Wo dike bwi mafiya cire duwe, di minen, nii kaba ki nungka birom nere Yecu Almaciya. Be ci mawo ri na yilam dangke ki nobo wo ane bilenke ti cinen nafiya dume diri.
1TI 1:17 Naweu ki liya kalewe, wo man ki bwar, yurangum yurange, Kwama wiin, Dur, duktangka nace bak ni bak. A tinyo.
1TI 1:18 Ma nenen werfunero woti munen, bi bwe mi, Timoti, dong-dong kange dugumbo ci mani dor mwereu be na mwi tem kwendo yora.
1TI 1:19 mawo be na yilam ki bilenke kange nero ken, kangem nob ciin ko cuwaka tu, ciin dubom bilenker ceu.
1TI 1:20 Nabi Himinawuc kange Ickandariya, wuro ma neken cii bwekelkele nin naci fiya mwerum kange dobka dilaka.
1TI 2:1 Nyo ki kaba, mi kenti a maken ka kange dilo, kange maka kini dor nober gwam kange neka buka kange dor nobo gwam.
1TI 2:2 Dor liyabe kange nobo tam ki nobe, dor yim lumam kange kwarce mor Kwama kange yorka.
1TI 2:3 Wuro yori kabo kange yoka kabum Kwama nii fuloka be.
1TI 2:4 Ci cwi ti na nobo gwam fiya fuloka naci nyimom bilenke.
1TI 2:5 Wori Kwama wiin kange wo tiber nii kange Kwama, nii wo Almaciya Yecu.
1TI 2:6 Cin neken dorcer fanka ki nobo gwam, dor warke ki dong donge kene.
1TI 2:7 Ki kero wo, cin dok ye moki bwimi, ma yilam nii tokka fulen kere kange nii tomange. Bilenke ma tok tiye. kebo cwerke ma tok tiye. Ma nii merangka ki nobo kumtacile mor bilenker kange ciyaka.
1TI 2:8 Nyo ma cwitiye, nabarubo fiye gwam ciya kwob dilo take ciya kung kang ceko wucake kebo ki funer kange kwobkanka.
1TI 2:9 Nyo tak ma cwiti natubo ciya du kwilendow datenne, kange bwayilendo datenne, kange taka duwe, ciya yilare nobo ma dorti ki mwine, kange kwilendo ki kyemere.
1TI 2:10 Ma cwiti ciya du kwilendo da natubo ya yamti mor Kwama be fiye nangendo ken.
1TI 2:11 Nawiye a merangi mor taka duwe kange yiber duwer mor diker gwam.
1TI 2:12 Ma ciyabo nawiye a merangi kaka ca nung bi kwan dor bwayile, di ca yii mor taka duwek.
1TI 2:13 Adamu cii ter fwelkake nyimde Hawwa'u.
1TI 2:14 Kebo Adamu cii bole dila nawiye cii bole, wo yarken bwirangke.
1TI 2:15 Nyo duwal ca tin fiya fuloka fiye boka bi beiyek, tano cii tam nur bilenke kange cwika, kange wucakke, kange nero yor yore ri.
1TI 3:1 kerwo dong dong, tano kange cwiti na co yilam dur bikur wabe di, coki cwi nangendo ken.
1TI 3:2 Nyo nii dur kur waber a yilam diker bitorer man dorcer, ca yilam nii ki nawiye wiine, nii tam dor cere, nii wo man ki kutume, nii yo fabubtiye. ca yilam nii nyimom merangka.
1TI 3:3 Ca yilare nii noka nyomek, ca yilare nii ki funere, nyeu a yilam ki fuwor neret, nii wo tam dore, kebo nii cwi kemer tiye.
1TI 3:4 Tam nyo ca tam loceu, bibeyo loceu ayilam wo nuwa co tiye kange neka biduyet.
1TI 3:5 Tano nii dolbo taka loceko di, ca ta nob Kwama bo nyi?
1TI 3:6 Ca yilare nii fwir wo fiya fiya fuloka tiye, kari co dii bwiyo ki cwika dorek, kari ci yarken mor warke wo cii ma bwekelkele nineu.
1TI 3:7 Tam nyo ca yila ki warke ken tak mor nobo buro mani more beu, kati ci yarken mor kwenduwe kange cito bwekelkele.
1TI 3:8 Nyo nobo ma nangen ti bi kur wabere, ken, cia yilam ki taka dorek, kebo nobo ki ni yobe dabo ci a yilam nob noka nyinek kange nob kucunu.
1TI 3:9 Ci a yilam nob nung bilenketi ki nero wucakke.
1TI 3:10 Daten a cuwa cii bwiri, no ciin wi ki warke ken di nimde cii ta nangendo wori cii man ki diker bitorer.
1TI 3:11 Nyo natubo ken a yilam nobo ken, dabo ciya yilam nob cuwarumeb, di nob taka doreb, kange yim ciyaka mor dikero gwam.
1TI 3:12 Tam nyo nobo dur bikur waber a yilam ki nawiye wiin. Ciya dolum mweka bibeyo loceu kange to ka loniciye.
1TI 3:13 Nobo wuro manangendo keneu ciiki fiya dorcero nin dendo ken kange bikwan neret mor bilenke wo Almaciya Yecu nine.
1TI 3:14 Ma mulang mwen dike buroti ki yoka nerek man bo mwinen fo kutangbo.
1TI 3:15 Tano ntabwiri, maki mulang mwen be na nyumom wang yimeko daten ayiti mor luwe Kwama, wo nob bwanka Kwama ki dume, bikwan, kange tikali bilenke.
1TI 3:16 Kani man, fwetangka bilenke bwangka beko teenangi kabo: Con nung dorcero mor bwiye, Yuwa tangbeko nungi cin nii ken, nob tomange Kwama wucakke tom co, cii tok ker fulene ce mor nobo kumtacili, ciin ne bilenke fo dorbitiner, nimde ciin tu co dii kwama mor duktonka.
1TI 4:1 Yuwa tangbeko toki nyanglang ki kaldo ccwile kangem nobo an tiyangum bilenke nin, ciyan yoken neer cero fiye yuwako bwirko wo bolange cii tiye, kange meranka kelkeli
1TI 4:2 mor cwerke kange biciren, dume ceu an mam bi kwa.
1TI 4:3 Ciyan ko na kako kange carito Kwama fweli naci kabkangi ki buka kangek mor nobo ne bilenke ri ciin nyimom bilenke.
1TI 4:4 Dike Kwama fwele yori kabo, dike ba yoki buka kange keu dabo bi ko co.
1TI 4:5 Di kweri cin nirom co fiye ker Kwama ro wiye kange dilo.
1TI 4:6 Tano mo kulom kebmwebonin diker wori, mwan yilam canga ken wo Almaciya Yecu ce, wori mo fiya muka ki ker bilenker kange ki merangkako wo mo bwangtene.
1TI 4:7 Di cwaa fulen cwerke wuro natubo carko cwi tiye, nyo mwe dor mwero mor bwangka Kwama.
1TI 4:8 Bi mwerum bwiyek yora bidob, dila mweka duwek mor bwangka Kwama yori kabo mor dikero gwam. Wori ci tam ker dumero wo naweu kange dume wo bouti kabeu.
1TI 4:9 Kero wo daten ciyaka, lam ayo co kwarub.
1TI 4:10 Co dike bwi ba nuwa dotange ri bama nangenti kambo kene. Wori ba yoten neer ti Kwama ki dume nin, nii fuloka nobo gwam, durcer ki nobo ne bilenke.
1TI 4:11 Kwa diro na merang dike wuro.
1TI 4:12 Ciyare kange a cwikangum bibweimweto. nyori, yilam dangne fiye nob bwangka Kwama ko wiye, mor kere, mwilen mwero, cwika, ciyaka kange wucakke.
1TI 4:13 Na nimde bou ri, ya kiye ranka nobe konin dike mulangum mulangeti, kange bi weret fumerer kange merangka.
1TI 4:14 Mare bilangiya ki nekako mo cike, wo cii nenen ki tokka dukume, ki yoka kangek nobo dureb.
1TI 4:15 Be cibi ki diketini buro. Ma yora more ce na caka kabak mweko yilam yanglang nuwe nobe gwam.
1TI 4:16 Ti ki bati ki dor mwero kange merangkako. Ca kaba more ce. No mwi ma nyori, mwan fulo dor mwero kange nobo nuwa nen tiye.
1TI 5:1 Ko care nii dur nin tor, nyori ki ken co namwi con tee. Bi beyo kom tuci na yitub kimeb
1TI 5:2 Natubo durko, namwi neb kimeb, natubo bi duwartini namwi kor biwutob kimeb, mor wucakke.
1TI 5:3 Ki ne dur natub kwalebo nin, wo ki cuwom natub kwalebeu.
1TI 5:4 No nawiye kwale wi ki bi bei kange tenkwanub ri, ciya merang neka durek mor luwe ce buri. Ciya yaa teb cibo, wori wo yori kabo Kwama nin.
1TI 5:5 Dila nawiye kwale ki bi cuwomeu ciin dob co ki kwace. Cin yo nercero Kwama nin. Ci ya ti ki kini dilo ceu kume kange kakuk.
1TI 5:6 La nawiye wo yim mor nuwaka lumakeu bwiyam, bwentano ciki dume ri.
1TI 5:7 Ki yi cii kero buro, naci yilare diker bi torek.
1TI 5:8 No nii nebo nebo naniyak cek dikero cii cwitiye kaka buro mor lo ceu ri kanangum bilenke, la cin la nii wo nyombo Kwama.
1TI 5:9 Ki tu nawiye, nawiye kwale no ci labo coro kwi nukkun di, nawiye bwece wiine.
1TI 5:10 Nawiye ka nyumom co ki maka dikero keneu, kangeri toka bi beyek, kaka ci yuwa fabub ti, kaka cin nirom na nob Kwamab, kaka cin tikang nubo nuwam twirau, kaka wo yo maka dikero ken kabeu.
1TI 5:11 La natub kwale bi duwartini, be ko kiye cire mor tangnum cem bo nin. No cii nuwa kuru bwiye lam Almaciya ri, ci cwiti naci nam.
1TI 5:12 Ki nure wuro di, ciin bo dorcero nin ki bwiran ke, wori ciin kurongum neka dorek ciko ki kabau.
1TI 5:13 Nyo takeu ciin merang twabwi, wori citi bwelangi luwe, luwe. Kebo ka twabwi takeu, cii tokang dikero wo datenbo cii tokeu.
1TI 5:14 Nyori mi witi natub kwalebo bi duwartini a nam naci bo bi bei, ciya tam lociyo, na ci nere nii kiye nure na kwobkangken bo bwi.
1TI 5:15 Kangembo yila ken bwe kelkele nin.
1TI 5:16 No nawiye kange bwangten Kwama tiye wi ki natub kwaleb di, ca tikang cii, nyori katin ciya tutum fiye nobo bwang Kwama nin tiye, nyori naci tikang buro natub kwaleb ki cuwo meu.
1TI 5:17 Ki ne nubo durko wo ma liyar yorau durko dacinen teneu, na nubo buro manangenti ki kere kange mor merangka.
1TI 5:18 Ker Kwamaro toki “dok re duka cur nen ner no manangen canger tiri,” nii manangenneu daten a neco mukti nangene ceu.
1TI 5:19 Ki ywore kiyange dor nii durek no nob warkeu labo yob kaka taar di.
1TI 5:20 Kom mwe nob bwirangke nuwe nube gwam, nyori tangni ceu an cwa tai.
1TI 5:21 Mi nekom werfun ti kabum Kwama kange Kiritti Yecu kange nob tomange Kwama wucake cii coke, kom tam dikero wo ma dok kimeneu kebo ki cwika duwe, kom ma diker kebo wo ma cwiti kone.
1TI 5:22 Kom yore kang wulom-wulom dor niir, kom tikan re bwirang ke kange nii kange. tam bwi mweu wucak.
1TI 5:23 Ma mwa no mwem tim tak, la no nyombo bi duwar ker fwerek mwek kange twira mweko kir-kireu.
1TI 5:24 Bwirangke kange nobe nyimom wumom yanglang, la an yaken kaa cii fiye warka. Dila Kangem bwira kerembo bwang ten ki bwi.
1TI 5:25 Nyo tak, kange nangedo kenko nyimom wumom-wume, la kangembo mani a yuranti.
1TI 6:1 Nubo buro ki bentilen bwatiyer na cangau cii a tu teluwetini ce na nubo lam neka dureke. Ciya mawo kati den Kwamaro kange merangka ko dilam.
1TI 6:2 Cangabo ki teb leuwebbo nyimom Kwama ci a nung ciinen de cwekanka wori ciin yitub. Nyori ci a yok ten bwanka ceyeko. Teluwebbo cii tikan cii ti ki nangen neu nobo nyumom Kwama la cii cwi cii tiye. Kom merangi, kom tok dike buro.
1TI 6:3 No kange nii merang werfundo kange ki cwerke, wo ciyabokange merangka Teluwe Yecu Almaciya, No ci ciya bo kange merangka ko a bou ti ki yimbo daten bwang ka Kwama.
1TI 6:4 Nii co wiki cwika dorek ca nyom bo diker. Ciki nero yorbe mor kanangka kange kwobkangkador kero wo a yilam kwerkangka, kwobkangka, bitor, kwaneriyo bwir.
1TI 6:5 Kange bukkanka tiber nobe wuro ki bi bwiyer nere. Ciin mirang bilenke wi cii kwa tiri yim bwanka Kwama dike ciyi fiya kiyemer tiye.
1TI 6:6 Bwangka Kwama kange birum ne mor fiyaka, fiyaka ko dur.
1TI 6:7 Ba boubo ki diker mor kale wo, nyori ma ba cer ti ki diker more ce.
1TI 6:8 Nyori, ti kange kulen la binen nyo.
1TI 6:9 Nyori buro cwiti na yilam nob kiyemereu, kiyarken mor cuwaka, mor ciito. Ciiki yar morkulene kange diker nuwaka twirak wo nercereu, kange mor dike wuro gwam nobo yarken ti mor kayaka kange bware.
1TI 6:10 Cwi ka kiyemerek necii dotange gwam. nobo do co tiye, ciin bo lumci fiye bilenke, ciin kwer bwoci ki tai to dur.
1TI 6:11 M o nii Kwama, cwam dike buro nin. Do yim wucakem, bwangka Kwamak, bilenke, mwerumka, kange yiber duwer.
1TI 6:12 Te kwen do ken bilenke ceu. Kom tam dume bak-nin bakeu wo cii cuwo kom cikeu, wuro dorcer ko ne warka ti nobo nin ducceu na dor dikero keneu.
1TI 6:13 Ma nekom werfuno wuro kabum Kwamam, wo ne dume dikero nin gwamme, kange kabum Kiritti wo ne warke ken ka Buntu Bilatu.
1TI 6:14 Na kom tam werfundo do wo manki tecanka kaka toka dikero bwir ya ciko boka Teluwe be Yecu Kiritti.
1TI 6:15 Kwama an nung bouka ceko fiya cuwo daten neu, Kwama nii duktongka kange wo lami nyo gwame Teluwe wo ca liyar tiye.
1TI 6:16 Ka co wo mani bwiya bwareu, yim ka filang ko nii yanin wiye. Nii kange man wo to ce, kaka wo an to ce. Cinen dur kange bikwan do bak-ni- bake. Ati nyo.
1TI 6:17 Yi nubo ki kiyemere ciya kungde dorciir, tak ri ci a yore ner dor kiyemer ciir wori man bak-ni-bakE, nyori ci a ciya ki yo neri mor Kwama. Can nebo kiyemero ken ko wo ba nuwa luma tiye.
1TI 6:18 Yi cii ci a ma dikero ken, naci fiya kiyemer mor nangene ken, na yilam ki luma neek, ri naci bilang tikanka dikerek wari.
1TI 6:19 Ki wori, ci yan yo dorcero ni kwaro ken ki diker a bou tiyeu, nyori naci tam dume ken.
1TI 6:20 Timoti, tam dike ci ne neneu yora. Ciyare ker kulener kange kwaneri wo makiyanti bwiticiye wo cii cuwo ti ki cwerke kii nyomkau.
1TI 6:21 Nubo kange tok dike wuro ti, nyori ciin lem fiyaka bilenke. Luma a yii kange mo.
2TI 1:1 Paul bwe tomange Yesu Almacifu ki maka kwamak, dor nored dumero Almacifu Yesu.
2TI 1:2 Timoti bwe ma cwi-cwi yeu, luma nuwa ka duwek kange, foor nerer fiye kwama Tee kange Almacifu Yesu telue beu.
2TI 1:3 Min buh kwama nen kang, wo ma bwang tenti fiye co tenkwanob mibwo wiye, ki dume nerer ken, kambo ma kwati ki mo mor dilo ma kwabti kir-kireu (kume kange kakok).
2TI 1:4 Kambo ma kwaki mwem nuwem be, la man cii na tonen, wori na dimki foor nerer.
2TI 1:5 Cin kuraye ki bilenker mwero cak-cakeu, wuro fyan dimero nuka mwe loyis nineu, kange neemwe Afiniki man nyumom co yim more mwe.
2TI 1:6 Won co dikero bwi ma kulom nenti miki fweli fuu, tan neka kwama ko wo more mweu, na mwa fiya kambo mwa yo mwen kani miu.
2TI 1:7 Wori kwama ne bobo yuwa tangbek taiyek la na bikwan kange cika kange taka dorek.
2TI 1:8 Na wori nuware kwenduwe warke dor Teluwe be. Kaka mo Bulus wo ce ci bwabwbeu, nyori ywelum bwi miri na nuwa dotanage dor ne ka fulnkerer, ki bi kwan kwamar.
2TI 1:9 Kwaco fulobe la co bo ki bi cor cak-caker con ma weu kebo ker nangeneb, lan makacek kange luma cak. Co nebo dike burombo mor Almacifu Yesu na nimre kaltiyo kabau.
2TI 1:10 La caneu cin fwetang fuloka kwamako fiye cerkenko Yesu ni fulobo cerkanguweu. Almasifu co ca bou ki diika bwareke, lan bou ki dume man ki diika wo ca futangi mor fulenkee.
2TI 1:11 Co wo ci cok ye ni neka fulenkerer nii tomage kange nii meranka fiye nubo kumtacile wiyeu.
