HEB 6:1 nana wori, labi yoten kang bwanka ker Almashiya ko nabi lam dwika, mani ba merangten ker dobko nangchen toka nuwetik kanghe bilengke mor kwama,
HEB 6:2 kaka kwar merangka yuka munghe, ba yo kang dor ker kwenka tuwek kanghe bolango manki dikau.
HEB 6:3 ban ma wuro mor fwiye no kwama ciyari.
HEB 6:4 wonco dike bwi chi wumom mor fwiye kumeu kibi come, dila chin twim nekakowo cirou dii kwamau, chi fiyamten cuner yuwa tangbeko take,
HEB 6:5 chi twimten luma kerek kwama ke kanghe bikwan duret kalekowo bou tiyeu,
HEB 6:6 la wuro yarumeu atin bwai na yilau kicho dobka bwirangke. dike bwiyeu wori chi kin kulken bibwe kwama ki bwichi tak, chinetenco dotanghe nyanglang.
HEB 6:7 tano bitine no yirau dii kwamare, bitineco atin ne nuboco chi ywel bitine ker chire charito ken wuro co bitine fiya bi bwiyer kwamare.
HEB 6:8 dila tano ci ne chuyak kanghe yerako nyini na cwiyakeri, chi mani ki nanghen chibi dom kanghe chilka, cwiyake chileceu twika kirak.
HEB 6:9 dila nyin toki nyo, dor kumer, kom nubo mi cwicwiyeu, kom ma ker bwira, kero dateneti.
HEB 6:10 kwama kebo mii nero bwire, biya ko toka nannyene kumeko tiye, kanghe dencero kom cwiti dokkom kom ma nubo wuchakenin nanghentiyeu, la chiyeu. weri nico dikero dang chiyaka kerek tiye.
HEB 6:11 nyiti cwii nyo wuyak kume kom dang bikwan neret wuro a dikumen yoka nerekti, chiyaka, yaken ciko dika.
HEB 6:12 kati kom yilam kidilime, kom ma merangka ki nubo yo dige nore koweu, ki bilengkeret cher kanghe birim nere che.
HEB 6:13 kambo kwama ma Ibrahim nin noreu, kambo nore kanghe mani wuro laco dwika ca werumti cikeu, la werum ki dorcer,
HEB 6:14 yiki, “bilengke man mamwen bi bwiyer, man ma naniyak mweko nin bwirom.”
HEB 6:15 kinco nuruwo, Ibrahim bwam nercer binnerdi, yo dika bi bwiyere keu.
HEB 6:16 bilengke nubeo ti weri ki dikero la chiyeu. weri inco dikero dng chiyaka kerek tiye.
HEB 6:17 lana weu, kambo kwama cwiti nachi dang nob kwalib norebowo nyanglang, ci kebo mi fulongka dike ci cwimakatiye, la a mweri.
HEB 6:18 ci ma dike wuro in wori dikero biro yobe mangki fulogkau, biro dangti, yitiki kwama mani cwer-cwerkiti, bo wuro bi cwa yabifiya fiye yurangka, biyilam kibi kwan nerer kambo ken bi lam dike biyoten nero wi dor cereu.
HEB 6:19 bin wiki yoka nerek, nyona dume ceu, yoka nereko wurodo yaken bwim lalang kuwekeu.
HEB 6:20 fiye Yeesu yakenwi kerbereu, cin yilam nii wabe dur wo diriyeu, kambo Malkisadak yoweu.
HEB 7:1 wo cho Maikisadak liya salem nii wabe kwama duktangka wo wamkangi kange Ibrahim yi lauti fiye kwake kange kangum liyab yo chinen bibwiyer.
HEB 7:2 Ibrahim la ne chi dike gwam kullendo cho fiya. denchero Malkisadak” den do wo ki nang liya ken yo tok salem ki nang liya luma.”
HEB 7:3 man ki te'e man ki ne'e man ki nani yak man ki kabang yimek man ki dika dumek cho liya wabe wo maka dika nabi bwe kwama
HEB 7:4 nyori to dwika nii wo ko tukatinim benbo Ibrahim la ne cho dike cho fiyau kullen fiye kwane chinene.
HEB 7:5 yo ki chuwom nani yak lewi kambo chiyo nangen de na nob biwabero che chi wi ki bikwan kerer wi bolang kwama tok ki ciya yo lumanerek fiye nobo wiye, tamwi wi keb chibo Isralawa, tano nyori chi kenne chi no nani yak Ibrahim me.
HEB 7:6 kambo Malkisadak cho kebo nani yak lewi. chon luma nerek wi Ibrahim nin cho ne cho bibwire, cho wuro cho wiki nor.
HEB 7:7 man ki ki kwob kangka bidware cho ki yore lumake durko nin wo lacho kibi dwiyere.
HEB 7:8 wi na wo chaneu nobbo bro yo luma nerer tiye di kange mwa fiya chin bwiyam, dila ki kwama kangeri nii wo yo neka lumati Ibrahim nin neu kambo na chonyeu chi chuwa cheu chi yim nyo
HEB 7:9 la ki nur tokka, lewi wo yo luma nerek ke chon ne luma wi Ibrahim nin
HEB 7:10 dige bwiye lewi ki no mor bwiye ten kwanum chem ki kwama Malkisadak chi wabkangum kange Ibrahim.
HEB 7:11 chan nawo naki anmamdi natakkum nangeen mor nange'en nob bi waber wo lewi yawa che (dige bwiyeu chi ne bolango chinen) no nyori fetikali nii wabbe kange bou ki dir Malkisadak la yilo chi tok bo dir Harunar.
HEB 7:12 na cho nye ki kwama chi fologum nob wabbe beu, bolanko kene an.
HEB 7:13 nyori nii cho chi tok digero buro dor chere na kange naniyang kange, wo kange mambo nangeen wi dor tanjilando wuchengke.
HEB 7:14 wuro nyanglang fiye te'e wiye wo'o bou ner Yahuza, naniang Musa wo chi tok kom wi kange chiye mor nob webbibe.
HEB 7:15 dige chi tok tiye nyanglang ki, chano kange nii wabbi kwanu ki chankangka Malkisadak.
HEB 7:16 nii wabbi fwirko, kebo nii wabbi wo kwanu ki dir ner kaldo wo, la yilam nii wabbi wo nyim chembo man ki dika.
HEB 7:17 nyo mulangum, mulange mor bi fimer ker cher mo niwabbe na yime che mor dir wo Malkisadak.”
HEB 7:18 la bidoti ki kaba yoken cho chwagca win nyo chune che man ki tikali.
HEB 7:19 bwentanno nyo bolango dibo di gero di la nyo ner na kain kab wo fiye chinen laka kwama nin.
HEB 7:20 nyo na wo yor yore yoka nerer mani bwir kero ki weri bwentano chi nob wabbi bo chi tubo kange weridi.
HEB 7:21 la kwama weri ker Yeesu ki. teluwe werum man cha fulong kwaka nere che ti cho niwabbe manki dika.”'
HEB 7:22 nyo dige bwi yeu neeh bilengke kange yorka norek.
HEB 7:23 ki chuwom bwaro nyab nob wabi bo nangen diri. wo cho dige bwi kangum nobo wabibo duche ki win ki win.
HEB 7:24 la nyo cho Yeesu yim chembo manki dika, nangen wabi to chew mani Afolong ti nyo.
HEB 7:25 la nyori cho wi ki nyomka bikwan cherkak chi nobo wo kutauti kwama nin ne ker cher. nyo kankang cho ki dume nyo tok cho konong ti ker chir.
HEB 7:26 nyo na wori nii wabbi durko dabiwen tenne man ki bwirangke man fiye bi tore wuchek cho kom bwichi mor nob bwirangke, cho ki no di fiyen di gwam.
HEB 7:27 man ki bwini kangum nob wabbi bo duryembo, wo ma kweleti kankange, ki kaba dor che gwam la Yeesu mawo kiritti win chwar mabo nobo nin ki wi winti-winti ki wo cho ne dor chere.
HEB 7:28 nyo bulango ki yom nob nyo nyom kako lachinen be na nob wabbi bo che. lan ker werido, wo bob bwikob bolange, yo bwe. wo nyom ka che ko maki dika.
HEB 8:1 nawe dige nyo chwiti nyo toke cho wo: bo wiiki nii wabe durko wo yim kanko chacher fiye yimi nii durka wo dii kwama.
HEB 8:2 cho chin change fiye wuchake, bikurwabe na bilengke che, wo kwama ywele, kebo bibwe nifire.
HEB 8:3 nob wabebo durko gwam chi, nobo tar kwama nin luma ko nobo nẽẽ ka-nge twika kunkuneko. nyori daten a fiya dige a twirangtiye.
HEB 8:4 na Almachiya fo dorbitinerdi mani a yila nii wabeti.
HEB 8:5 wori ka-ngembo wii wo tar twika nuwam fichangero tiye na dige bulangko toke. chiki ma nangen yirum dige kakuloko dii kwama. na wo kwama ma Musa nin biweret, fiya cho chwiti na cho mũũ bikure: toõ, kwama yii ki, “ma diger dong-dong na wo chi merang mwen dor bang-ngereu.”
HEB 8:6 di la nangen do Almachiya yowe la wo chiye gwam. wori cho nii tebere yortum norem, woro chi takum na yortum norem boche.
HEB 8:7 Tano nor kabaro man ki bwirangkeri, la yẽẽ bwi a yoo noro yobe che tiye?
HEB 8:8 na kwama fiya bwiranke dor nober di a tokki man fulon noro fwir ka-nge Israila ka-nge Yahuza.
HEB 8:9 Take mani a yila nawo ma mani ka-nge tenkwanib kimebo, nawo ma ta chi ka-nge. ma chok biten masar. chi tabo nor miro, mo ken man chutang. chi wi nuwa Teluwe.
HEB 8:10 di la wo cho nor miro wo ma ti ka-nge loh Israila, bwiko kume niwo, nuwa Teluwe, ma yoti bolang miko nyii chi, na mulanti mor nere chiye mani yilam kwama chinen, chi kene chiyan yilam nob mib.
HEB 8:11 mani chiya merang kebchiye bo ninti kaka nobo bi dom ka-nge chiye, ki ko nyomom Teluwe? di la gwam chiye chiyan nyomom ye, tabti biduware yamken chiko durko nin.
HEB 8:12 man chii ki nangen chiyero mani wuchake, mani ma kulomti ka-nge bwirangke chiye.”
HEB 8:13 dor takka “fwije” yila neti nor kabako charko, wo chi cho ki chareu yoten lemti.
HEB 9:1 bwen na nor kaba ko wii ki fiye wabe kange bidoti fo dorbitiner.
HEB 9:2 mor bikur, kuwe wii chi yomyowe, kuwe kale cho wo choti ki fiye wuchake, fiye wo talkire yomyowe wii, late kange chari wii.
HEB 9:3 bwi yilak kuwako, kange kuwe wii wo choti ki fiye wuchake.
HEB 9:4 wii ki tanjilan mwiner na nuwan fichangero che. wii ki bwen nore, wo chi kwaltum ki mwine. more che telmwine tomki manna, kange dang Haruna wo fuũwe, kange late tere wo nore che.
HEB 9:5 di kwama kange bwen nore dubi cherobim nob duktangka kange kakilok cheduwe, wuro naweu mani ba dol fwetankati win bweko wine.
HEB 9:6 bwiko ywellum dige wori, nob wabeb bikurebo, ki do, dokuwe bikulro nine kir-kir chi ma nangen chiyeroti.
HEB 9:7 kan liya wabe durko do kuwe yobe tiye, kiritti win chwat mor chore, tam cha no ki buyale wo twiika che na dor chero che, kange bwirangke nobe chiye mani kebo kibi kwake.
HEB 9:8 yuwa tangbeko wuchake nungi nure yaken fiye wuchake fwetangbo, tano bikur kabako tim wiri.
HEB 9:9 wori yilam fwetangka na wo, kangye luma, twiika nuwan fichangero gwam, netiye mani a dok dike dume ne'e wo wabtiye.
HEB 9:10 chari kange dige noka mwere kange chika nirbanka kidemen-kidemen, wori dige yo a manangti, nime na bidoti yorangi.
HEB 9:11 Almachiya bo nyi niiwabe durko ki digero ken bouwe, fiye, bikure durko dimdiye wuchake wo kebo kang nobek mu'uwe, wo kebo fo dorbitinero wo fwelle.
HEB 9:12 kebo ki bwiyal nibe kange nenne di la ki bwiyale che, cho do'o fiye wuchake kiriti win chwat na nobo gwame che, yo'o binen fanka wo dire.
HEB 9:13 tano bwiyal nibe Kane nenne, ka-nge te'eka dor nobo ka-ngum wuchake chiye, nir chiti, ka-nge bwii chiye.
HEB 9:14 Tenkang bwiyale Almachiya wo bo fiye yuwa tangbeko wuchake bak-ni-bak neken dor chero twika ficha-nger, kwama wo nir nerberoti fiye nange do yorbo bwiyam bwiya na bo wab kwama nii dume.
HEB 9:15 cho dige bwiye, Almachiya cho fiye wab kanka noro fwiko, wuro bwi nyo, ma bwaro wo chokkum nobo dimer noro chare, ker bwirangke chi, wuro kwama cho na yo'o nor kwali chi bak-ni-bak.
HEB 9:16 di gwam ka-nge mulang dige ner chere la dube, tam a nyomom buwar niwo mulangi yowe.
HEB 9:17 fiye buro man chi ma nangenti ki dige niwo bwiyame mulangi yowe, man ki nangen tano niwo mulangi yowe ki dumeri.
HEB 9:18 bwen nor kabaro tibo, ki bwiyale nime.
HEB 9:19 di la Musa dim nebo werfunero gwam mor bulange nobo nin gwam, la chon tũũ buyal bẽẽ nenne ka-nge nibe, wari ka-nge mwem, ka-nge yilanko fiyer ka-nge kang bwatiye ki duka bwii che, na cho watangi dor nober ka-nge bifumer werfunero. wi fo yii chi wuro bwiyale nore kwama ne'e kange werfune kumen.”
HEB 9:21 nyo cho te-em bwiyale dor bikure ka-nge gwam kullen do more che wo ci mam nangen wabkati chike
HEB 9:22 dige bulangko tabe, gwam ki bwiyale chi nirti chike, tana chorka bwiyalek maniri, tabka bwirangke man.
HEB 9:23 Tam nyo kulen do na bitenkar dige mor dii kwama na nirum ki twika bichirek. gwam nyo twika ko kwama tam a nirum ki twikako yoryore.
HEB 9:24 Almachiya dobo fiye wuchak chi mũũ ki ka-nge, wuro betenkar dige wo na bilengke che. nyo chon ya mor dii kwama ki dorcer, nimde cho ya kabum kwama ker ber.
HEB 9:25 yabo wii na ne'e dor chero kiritti kila nin, nawo nii wabe bikure matiye, wuro doti fiye wuchake choti-choti ki bwiyale ka-nge bichir.
HEB 9:26 tano nyori tamyo cha nuwa dotange kiriti-kiriti fiye kabak dor bitiner, di na weu kiriti win chi fwetanche, chwile kalewo nin na tum bwirangke, cho chwi cho nẽẽ ken gor chere.
HEB 9:27 nawo chi binen gwam bo bwiya kiriti win chwat, bwiko chek, kum kan bolang.
HEB 9:28 nyo Almachiya wo chi nẽẽ kiriti win chwat, be na cho tum bwrangke nobo kila, yila na yobe che kebo nangen tũũka bwirangke, di la dor nobo wuro nintang choti ki birum nẽẽ na fuloci.
HEB 10:1 nyori warfundo nyrom dike yoryore a boutiye kebo yirombo chuwo ki bwichi nobbo ya'ati kwama nine mani a yila nobti kambo ken ki ker twika wo nob twika mati chor kange chore.
HEB 10:2 na wo nyori twika nuwangeko datenbo a timka? wori chwi ninin nob wabkako chim nirum chi kiritti wiin, chi nyombo bwirang kere.
HEB 10:3 la twirangka nuwangek yilam diker kwaka ker bwirang keret chor kange chor.
HEB 10:4 la bwiyale kwama kange nibe mani a tum bwirang kere ti.
HEB 10:5 fiya kiritti bou dor bitinere chon tokki, twika nuwangek kange neka luma kebo dike kom chitiye, lan bwiyo ka ywel mene,
HEB 10:6 twika kange meka dor bwiangge kebo diker luma kime.
HEB 10:7 la min tokki, “to'o min wo, na wo mulangum dor mir mor bifumere, nan ma dike mo chwitiye.”'
HEB 10:8 ki ka'aba cho tokki “kebo twika nuwangek, kebo luma, kebo twika dor bwirang keret kom chitiye kaka kebo diker kom nuwa luma chek tiye” wuro twika nuwangeko chi mati mor werfune.
HEB 10:9 la chon tokki, “to'o min wo nan ma dike mo chitiye” cho tum dikero mati ki ka'aba na cho bou chi ki a mati na yobbe cheu.
HEB 10:10 wuro chin nirum wuchak mor neka bwiye Yeesu kiritti, kiritti wiin na yilam na gwamme che.
HEB 10:11 kume bwiko kume nob twika nuwangek tim ma kwama nin nangen ti. cho ne twikako chuwo kir-kir, twika nuwangeko wuro twibo bwirang keret wiye.
HEB 10:12 la kiritti ne twika nuwangek kiritti wiin na wo gwam me, cho yiiken kang ko chartiyere kwama.
HEB 10:13 cho ki nin tangi na nob kiyeb chebo yilam fiye fuwa na'a chek.
HEB 10:14 ki twika nuwangek wiin, chon ywel nobbo chi nirum wuchake yilam dikero ken kambo ken, diiri.
HEB 10:15 takeu, yuwatangbeko wuchakeu war binen ker. ki ka'aba chon tokki,
HEB 10:16 “won cho norro ma mani kange chiye bwiko kumeni wuro, teluwe tokki, “man yoti werfun miro ner chir man mulang chinenti mor nere chiye.
HEB 10:17 la chon yokten, bwirang keret chiyero, kange ner chiro bwangtenbo werfuneu, mani a kwati chiko.
HEB 10:18 channeu, no tubka dike buro no wiri, nuwangek bweirang kere mani.
HEB 10:19 nyori ker mibo biki bikwan neret bandoken fiye wuchake ki bwiyale Yeesu.
HEB 10:20 wuro cho nure fwirko nyiime che cha wom binene mor kyelange, wuro dangi bwichi.
HEB 10:21 wori biki nii twiika nuwangek dur lo kwama.
HEB 10:22 nyori bi kutauten bidom ki nere ken, won chiyako dim diye na bilengke che, wori ner bero chin tem manki duti kwaka dikero bwir, bwi beu chin nirum ki mwembo manki dutiye.
HEB 10:23 bitam kibi kwan warka nyo nere be, wori nii wo ma norrou wi ki bilengke.
HEB 10:24 bi to'o nure wo ba nekang kuru ti cwikangka kange maka dikero kenne.
HEB 10:25 bi yilotende mwerkangka beko nawo kangum bo maneu. bi nekang buti bikwang neret kir-kir na wo kom to'o kakuko chuwo dadome.
HEB 10:26 no bo ma bwirang kiritti ki nyomka bwikoba yuwa nyomka bilengke, nuwangek bwirang kere mani tak.
HEB 10:27 nyori kan taito dur bolangere kange kirako chilong-chiloge wo twinob kiyeb kwama.
HEB 10:28 nii wo ko werfun Musaro di chan bwiya cii duwe mani dorwarka nobbo yob kaka ta'ar.
HEB 10:29 warkako wini bwira nyo kom kwatiri daten dor fuwam bibwe kwama, tubo norr kwamaro na dikero wuchake-wori mor bwiyale chuwo chi nirum che-la yila tõ yuwa tangbe luma ka?
HEB 10:30 wori bon nyimom wuro yii ki, ya'aka chunero na mi, man ya'am chunero chuwo takau kwama a ma warka nobbo locheu.
HEB 10:31 diker tayer na yarken kang kwama ki dume;
HEB 10:32 la kwa ki kumeni chumeu, bwiko ka yuwo nyomka, la kom mwirumum doka cherka dotange dure.
HEB 10:33 kom fiya kwenduwe mor nobbo ki bi torr kange dotange, kom nuwa dotange ti na wo kangumbo do'o more che kene.
HEB 10:34 wori kom bunang nobbo fuchinabbo kom chiya ki fwor neret kulen kimero chi yuwome. kom nyomom ki bwikimi kom wi ki kulendo wo yoryori bak-ni-bak.
HEB 10:35 nyori kom mirang de bikwang neret ki mero wi, wuro wiki ya'aka ko dur.
HEB 10:36 kom cwi mwirumka ti, na yiolam no kom dikero kwama cwitiyeri, kan yuwo norro cho ma bineneu.
HEB 10:37 ki kini bi duwar, nii wo bou tiye “bichuwom an bou mani a ma fiyeti.
HEB 10:38 mimbo wuchakeu an fulo ki bilen kere. nocho yilaken ki bwimri mani ma nuwa lumati kange cho.
HEB 10:39 la bo mani mor nobbo wuro yilaken ki bwim fiye twalangka, la boh wi more buro ki bilengke.
HEB 11:1 bilengke co ciya kako ki dike bro bo yo neer dor cireu. co ciya kako ki dike nuwe tobeu.
HEB 11:2 ki ciro co tenkwanib bebo fiya ciyaka fiye kwama wiye.
HEB 11:3 ki bilengke ba nyumom kalewo kwama fwel ki ker cer, wori dike brombo to ti ki nuweu fwelu bo dike to ti ki nuweu.
HEB 11:4 ki bilengke Habila ne kwama chikako ficange la kayinu ceu, wo kwama ciya cinen con ni bilengke. kwama toki yora dor luma cero ca neu, ki bilengke Habila tok kere bwentano con bwiyameu.
HEB 11:5 ki bilengke ci tum Enoch yaken dii na tore bwar”fiya co bo, wore kwama tum co.” kambo na tuceu, ne warke con yo kwama nin neer.
HEB 11:6 na weu, kebo ki bilengkeri mani a lom cinenti won tam nyo nii wo bou ti kwama nineu a ne bilengke kwama wi la con nii co ne nubo do co tiyenin cuner.
HEB 11:7 ki bilengke, nuluyo tomange cak-cakeu dor dikero tobo buriyeu. ki neer kwamar co ywel nebire mwenge na cer locer. ki makako wo kwama kangum kalewo la con yilam nii kwali bilengke ki bilengke ca neu.
HEB 11:8 ki bilengke Ibrahim kambo ci co ceu, bwangten ceri yaken fiye ca yoti na kwaliceu. con ceri co nyombo fiye co yakenti wiyeu.
HEB 11:9 ki bilengke co yim mor bitine nore na fabe co yim mor bikur wabe co kange Ishaku kange Yakub nob kwalib nore bo gwam.
HEB 11:10 co ki ton kaba cinan loro ki kwar kureuwo nii yabi kange mukako kwama.
HEB 11:11 ki bilengke Saraya bentano com bilomeu, Ibrahim yo bikwan na yila teebweu. wo ma nyo bwentano ciram duwaleu, na wo con ciya nii bilengke ne co noreu. ki bilengke Saraya bwen con ciram duwaleu, yo bikwando na co bom bwe, la con ciram na co bo bwe, kambo con tu nii wo ne noreu nii bilengke.
HEB 11:12 na ki nii wo wineu, kiyang con bwiyam-bwiya con bourang tenkwanibo kila-kila na bitirendo biloreu”, man ki kiye ka na yabum bo wo kong cajiyeu.
HEB 11:13 mor bilengke brombo gwam bwiyaranum yobo noro, nyico, bwiko toka kanke yarum ka ciyak kutan, la cin ciya cin fabub, cin nob yameb fo dor bitinere.
HEB 11:14 nubo bro tok dike bro tokum dong-dong ciki do bitine dor cire.
HEB 11:15 na ciki kwa kin co bitine wo ci ceru wiyeri citin fiya yilaka wi.
HEB 11:16 la nyeu, cin cwi bitine ken, wo lo kwama. co dike bwi kwama nuwa bo kwenduwe a co kwama ciye, la con ywel ci nen cinan lor.
HEB 11:17 ki bilengke Ibrahim kambo cuwa ceu, neken Ishaku, co bi bwece win cwar ca nekene. co wo ca yo noreu.
HEB 11:18 co Ibrahim ciyi ce, mor Ishaku tenkweani mwe bo a co tiye.
HEB 11:19 Ibrahim ciya kwama an kungum Ishaku bwar, la nyo ki danke la ki ci ca yo ciye.
HEB 11:20 ki bilengke tak ki dike brombo boutiye Ishaku yo Yakub nin bi bwi yere kange Isuwa,
HEB 11:21 ki bilengke Yakubu bwiyatiri yo bibeyo lo Yusufu nin bibwiyere. yaku wabi nyolum dor dangecer.
HEB 11:22 ki bilengke Yusufu, kambo kumeni ce daotom dikari tob dobkako Israila a dubom masaro tiyeu con yiten ci ker kuktini ceu.
HEB 11:23 ki bilengke Musa kambo ci bou ceri, tebcebo yurangum co cwiyakko taãr, wori cin to co bwe yor-yore. ci cwa bo ker liyaro tokeu.
HEB 11:24 ki bilengke Musa kambo dwiyomeri ko na co co kibibwe bubya firauna.
HEB 11:25 con tum na co nuwa dontange kange nob kwama bo kange wo ca nuwa luma bwirangketi biduwareu.
HEB 11:26 con ciya ki yari bwanka Yeesu keu cwekako dur la dike mwerum kuũ yoka masareu. la coki yo nuwa cecunenr cero nin.
HEB 11:27 ki bilengke Musa dubom Masare, cwa bo tai funer liyar, la con birumum, na kaã mwini co ki to nii mani toreu.
HEB 11:28 ki bilengke con bwangten ki duklume yabkako, kange watangka bwiyaleko, na nii twalka bi bei bayilobe kaba bouri na kare bi bei bayilobe kaba Israilu.
HEB 11:29 ki bilengke ci yab cajiyo baharmaliya na ka mwi ci yab bitine kwicer, kambo masarawa cwi na ci mani nyeri mirangum ci.
HEB 11:30 ki bilengke tiyakko Jeriko yarken bitine, bwiko wo ci kentangum cinan loro kume nibereu.
HEB 11:31 ki bilengke Rahab nawiye buroka, bwiyabo kange nubo ko nuwa kau, wori con nob nurebo ki for nered.
HEB 11:32 ye ma tok ti take? mani a dob yeti na tok ker dor Gidiyo ner, Barak, Simson, Dauda, Samuila kange nob dukumebo.
HEB 11:33 ki bilengke ci cam biten liyabe ki kwene, cin ma nbangedangen bilengker cin yo noro. cin kumom nyi tirome.
HEB 11:34 cin k kired, cin cerum nyi kulene, twam ciki twira tini. yilam kibikwan nyi kwene, cin nob kweneb fabubo.
HEB 11:35 na tubo yo yitub cibowo ci kungan bwareu. kangem nuwa do tange, ci dobo cerka ki dor cir, wori ciki yoneri, kungka nubo tuweu.
HEB 11:36 kangem bo cin buwo ci, kange biluker kange balyangen, kangem bo kuka kanger bwaka ki gwelman.
HEB 11:37 mobang ci ki ter, biyer kangum ci yob, twalci ki kulen, cin yam ki teni kwame kange nibe. cin cu biten nube, cin ne ci dotange.
HEB 11:38 dor bitinero tu ci bo na kange. ci ti bwiye langi yerank kange bangtini. kange mor buwak bangek kange buwakti kanjangek.
HEB 11:39 bwentano nubo bro kwama ciya ki ci ker bilengke ciye, ci yo bo noro.
HEB 11:40 kwama mabinen yabiyo kenti, mani a mati la a ma kange bou.
HEB 12:1 di nyu, nob warkako kentangum be, di bo nyou dige a lã botiyeu chung hagin kange bwiranke bwabanngum be. bo biner chwak torkako yom kabumbeme.
HEB 12:2 bo cho ti Yeesu nin nii fwilikangǝ bilengke gwam-gwame. fwor nerer yom chi meneu, cho birumum bwatiye bware. chwe kangum kwenduwe, cho yim kangko chattiyer den ki la kwama
HEB 12:3 nyo bulangi ki cho wuro mwirum me kurombo nob bwirangkero nin dorcer nyo dila mani mwa yarang netti mu chokum nermwer.
HEB 12:4 bwiri mwo kwab kangbo kange bwirangke wo ya lam bwi yale.
HEB 12:5 mun tabum kange bi tiye maro wo yinen na bwe. bi bwemi ture yiber kange mwerum kwamambo, yilare ki faner tano chi ywel nendi.”
HEB 12:6 kwama ki mwe ni wo chi chwiyeu kange mweka mweka bwewo chi yoweu.
HEB 12:7 mwirum dotangeu na mwe ka kwama ma kange mwo nyo na bwe. bwe winni teche mani mwere?
HEB 12:8 tano chi mwe nen bori wuro nubo gwam matiyeu, di mwo nii bongtu kebo bwe.
HEB 12:9 takeu bin wi ki tee mwor bwiye wo mwebe, bin nuwachi la tenkang tebe wo mwor yuwatangbeko wuchakeu, kange wo dume ba nuwa nyi.
HEB 12:10 tebbebo mwe boti ki ni bi dob kambo chi to dotanne, dila kwama ki mwe bo na ywelbo di nabi ti kangyi wari mwor wuchakke chenin.
HEB 12:11 mwerum kange mani na wo lom-lomme ki ni cho chi mwe nentiyeu dila twiri kabo. diki bwiri ki ne bitutti fwor nere wuchake nubo buro nin yo mwe kake.
HEB 12:12 di fer kang mweko wo yakummeu kange duwen mwero yi bomeu.
HEB 12:13 ywel namweko min nureu ti chere, la na dige muklangum meu mani a kayati an tam.
HEB 12:14 do luma kange nubo gwam kange wuchake, kebo ki chori ni mani a to kwamati.
HEB 12:15 yilam ki chi ni kange a lere lima kwama, kange nitito tweitweye a kire kari kwau dotange, kari nubo ki la yila kayam chuko
HEB 12:16 yila ki chi ni buroka a nore kange bwini bwangka kwama na Isuwa, wo ka timi ker chari miyem dur boka cheke.
HEB 12:17 mun nyimom nyo bidob chi chwiti na chi fiya kwali bwiyer chero, chi fiyabo dã yi loka, duwaleu chin do ki mwem num.
HEB 12:18 mu boubo banga wo mwa te tiye bang twika kirak, kumtachile, kange yuwa, kumtachile.
HEB 12:19 mu boubo chume chu ka konin, kebo diro wo tokker nawo nuwari mani a kenkange kerti a tokken.
HEB 12:20 mani chiya mwirum wefuner: bwentano bichirteibangeri chiyan ma bangum Musa
HEB 12:21 di diger twaiyer bi kolewo Musa tokki min nuwa taimin chwa chi ko.”
HEB 12:22 nyeu, notin bou bang zetune kange chi narlor kwama ki dume, zerusalembo di kwama, kange biben tomange wuchakeu dikate kwob chi bilengti.
HEB 12:23 mun bou mwor mwerkangka bi bei kaba, wo mulam mulange di kwama. mun bo kwama nin, ni bwolange dongdonge.
HEB 12:24 mu bo Yeesu nin ni werfunero fwire kange bwiyale chori tokker yore la bwiyale Abila.
HEB 12:25 to kore ni wo tokkertiyeu. chati no chi bubo no chi ko ni wuro werang chi dor bitinere, bi duware che mani ba buti nabi ko niwo werangbo di kwamari.
HEB 12:26 kini win, dirchero mor dor bitinero. dila na weu chi mabiner nor choki kum kiritti win mani ma makti ka dor bitine, di la kange di kwama.
HEB 12:27 kerowo kiritti winneu, ki dang kwobka digero na a moktiyeu, ni chi cho digerowo fwelfwele, dila dige wuro mani a mokyeu na nowi
HEB 12:28 dila yoka liyare mani. a moktiyeu, be yilam ki. buka kangek nyeu in wabka kwamako yoryore kange wo tennengi nye.
HEB 12:29 kwama be kire twikak.
HEB 13:1 cwika bwiti ko a ca kaba.
HEB 13:2 ko tabre yoka fabubeko, makako nyeu kangem bo nung nob tomangebo wuchake nin yoka la nyombo.
HEB 13:3 kom kwa nubo bro fusunau na dike mwini ko bwam ka-nge ciye. kom kwa ki nubo bro nuwa dotange tiyeu, na mwi ko wani ka-nge ci mor bwiye.
HEB 13:4 naka ayilam ki dur nubo nin gwam la kwangni nakako a yilam cak-cak, wori kwama ma nob burotum ka-nge ka ya tumbo nin boulang.
HEB 13:5 dume ne kume a cerum cwika kiyemek, bwa ne'er ki dike ko cikeu, kwama ki bwici toki mani ma dob komti. kaka mirang kom wi.
HEB 13:6 bo bwa ner na bo fiya bikwan tokkar boki, Teluwe co nii tikalimiu, mani ma cwa taiti. ye nii a ma yeti cike?”
HEB 13:7 kom to nubo dur kumero, nubo yi kom ker kwamar tiyeu na ko yakaka ci fiyeu, kom merang bilengke ciyeu.
HEB 13:8 Yeesu kiritti dong-dong wure, duwen, kwatti diiri.
HEB 13:9 kom tiyanum re ki fabe merangkako kila-kilau, la yori kabo ne'ero a fiya bikwan ki luma kebo ki cari wo tikang bo nubo manangenti cikeu.
HEB 13:10 bon we ki tanjilando wuchakeu wo nubo manangen ti kur wabereu mani a cati wiyeu.
HEB 13:11 la bwiyal bisirembo wo twalang na bwiran ke ceu, nii wabe durko an doken ciko mor fiye wuchakeu, kambo bwici twirangum kale fiye nubo wiyeu.
HEB 13:12 la Yeesu ken nuwa dotange bwingom nyilok cinan lorok, na co nirum nubo wuchak ki bwiyale ce.
HEB 13:13 na nyori bi ya ka-nge co tar mwer kanka bo tum ki kwenduwece.
HEB 13:14 bo man ki cinanloro ka-nge fo bak-nin-bakeu. la nyeu boki to co wuro a bou tiyeu.
HEB 13:15 more ce la bo ne twikako ficang caklang kwamati. caklangkako co bituti nyiyeu, wo duktang co tiyeu.
HEB 13:16 bo tabre ki maka dike ko yor yoreu, ba tikang bwitibeti, la kin cowo kwama nuwa luma tiye.
HEB 13:17 kom bwangten na ko ne nubo durkumero dur ci. ci to dume kume tiye, na nubo a ne kiye kati dor kumere, kom bwangten na nubo kumero ma wuro ki for ne'ered, la kebo ki fir ne'ered, wo yilam ti manki nangen kumeneu.
HEB 13:18 ko kwob nyinen dilo, nyo nyomom nyon wi ki dumene ken, la daten nyo yi dong-dong mor dike gwam.
HEB 13:19 ma ne kom bikwan neered, tikom mani a la wo nan yila kumen fo neereu, kutangbo.
HEB 13:20 la kwama for neereu, wo kungu nii to ka kwameko durko bwareu, Teluwe be Yeesu kiristi ki bwiyale wore diiyeu,
HEB 13:21 Adum kom ki wi dike bro yor-yoreu gwam nako ma dike co cwitiyeu, kom manangenti more nye. dike wo a lom cinen tiyeu, mor Yeesu kiristi, wo duktangka na ce diiri atinyo.
HEB 13:22 na weu ma ne kom bikwan neeredti kebmibo ko mwirumum bwere to wo ma mulang kumen bi dabeu.
HEB 13:23 kom nyomom cin kwim yibe Timoti yama to kom ka-nge co na co bou fo kutanbori.
HEB 13:24 yarum nubo dur kumero gwam ka-nge nob kwama bo cak-cakeu. nubo bro taliya yarum komti.
HEB 13:25 luma a yi ka-nge kom gwam.
1PE 1:1 Biru bwe tomange Yecu fabubo wo kwama coki watanum watange Buntu, galatiya kaya dki ya aciya kange bitiiya.
1PE 1:2 Wo ki nyomka kwama teu kange yuwa tangbek kwama wo nii nirkau kange lomjome kange cor ka bwieyalek Yecu Kritti luma a fiya nen filang mweko ayukten.
1PE 1:3 Bibwiyer ano kwamanin Te cer Yecu Kritti ki cini ceu tenang tenangeu, co ca nebo fwir na yim yonerimbo ki dumeu ki kwenka Yecuk bwar.
1PE 1:4 on co kwatlito manki kayakakeu ca kume mau a ta ti, manki diika, yom dikwama ki kom.
1PE 1:5 Kwama cer kom ki bilenker cer kakowe komti kambo kume boutiyeu.
1PE 1:6 Bilanka ki kom wo bwan no duwal tam koom ko ma fir nerer kidotange nure kila kila.
1PE 1:7 Wo co cuwa ka bilenker kumero fiya nka durek kange duktanka Yecu kritti.
1PE 1:8 Mwa to co bou la mon cwito ci mwa toco nawo la mon nee bilenker cimen mun nuwa luma kero ca tokbeu mon bilange.
1PE 1:9 Na wo moke yoo na mwe diker mwamaneu kibilenker kange cerka dume mweu.
1PE 1:10 Ker cero kako tok ka dor cereu kange luma kwamakeu, kume tii na ce fuwa kumen.
1PE 1:11 Cin doo naci yumom fyan yuwatangbe Yecu cemen a tok tiye. wo ciki yici dikero fiya ci na co ca yii ciyeu, dotange Yecu, wabker diker nanimde co.
1PE 1:12 Yii ci ti nagen do wo ci matiyeu kebo na ciye na kume cin tok ker dor diker wo ca yiim kom waber kwama ki yuwa tangbek kwama yiram dikwama nob tomange ce kwama wuccakkeu ci tokkan ti yoo.
1PE 1:13 Na cori ki bwa dume kume ki mwa for neret cer ki luma ceko a boo kumen tiyeu kakuko Yecu a bou tiyeu.
1PE 1:14 Bibeyo com zomeu ko yare ki dor kumero dikero kom mati ka yumbo fiye.
1PE 1:15 La na co wo coneneri wi wuccak kom ken ko yi wuccak mor yimekume.
1PE 1:16 Mulangum -mulange kiyi wuccak nan ma wucakken.
1PE 1:17 No mon co muke “Tehri” mun manki bulang cek ti manki cwi k duwek dong dong nagen do ni maneu ko yim kalembo ki cwii kang tai.
1PE 1:18 Mon yumom kiwo kebo wo kayati kayau fan kom cike ki kulen dameroka tebkume bo neneu.
1PE 1:19 Nye for kom ki bwiyale kritti wo na be kwame man ki bwiranke kange tekcanka.
1PE 1:20 Kritti cokum coke kwar dor bitinero na weu mukimen ki kalewo yautiye.
1PE 1:21 Kercer ba niye bilenker kwama nen. wo kung co bwareu neco dotange na bilenker kumeu kange yim yonerem ki no kwama nen
1PE 1:22 kom yoke dume kume cak-cak ki lomzome bilenkerero ker cwikanka ki cwikan bwitici mor nere kume.
1PE 1:23 Na wo mo yiloteneu kebo ki dumbo wo kaya ti kaya, dumbo wo mani fwiyereu ki ker kwama, wii ki dume bak nin bak.
1PE 1:24 Yorak ceko na bwi yere yorka ceko na fu tiyer, yorako kwicim di fun tiyero tikkam.
1PE 1:25 Dii ker kwamaro t kwatti diim kerowo co fule kero ca yi kumeu.
1PE 2:1 Nyori yoken firen gwam dikero bwir, gwam biboler, mantum nerkiyet kange yilaka bwiyek.
1PE 2:2 Na bibeyo biduwartini do yiim yuwa tangbe wusakeu, no mobwanten cori mwan dwii mor fuloka.
1PE 2:3 No mun twii teluwe be wiki luma nerekdi.
1PE 2:4 Bo fiye ciwiyeu, con ter dumero nobo kowe, nyori kwama cokum cona dikero ken cinen.
1PE 2:5 Mo keneu na terenti dume ci mu loyuwa tangbe wucakeu na yilam nii wabe kwama wucakeu wo a nee twika nuwang yuwa tangbe wo kwama ciya cikeu fiye yecu kritti nineu
1PE 2:6 Bifimer tum ki o: “To mi yoti mor ciyona ter lunger ci cokum kange ci ciyacike wo ciya kange ceri mani a nuwa kwenduweti”
1PE 2:7 Durko na mwe mone bilenkere, boro nebo bilenkere, “tero wuro nob mukabo kowe co an yilam dor lungero”.
1PE 2:8 Kange “ter yaret kange cwelako a dok ci yare tiye” cin yari wori cin ma bongtu kero nen- wo ci yoci ca maneu.
1PE 2:9 Na co duwaleu cin cokum kom nob liyar wabe kwama, bitine wucake, nobo kwama tam ki ciye naki yi nobo fulen kerero kendo nii wo cuwokom mor kumtacileu ka doken mor filang ca.
1PE 2:10 Kwatti ki kebo nbo ki wiine, nawe kom nob kwamab, kwatti ka nwabo cire duwe ce, nawe ka yuwo cire duwe ce.
1PE 2:11 Kom mi cwiiticweu mi cuwo komti na fabub kange cangam, kom cwaa dilanka bwiye wo te kwenti kange dumeu.
1PE 2:12 Ko yilam ki muleng do ken, mor nobe, Naci toi ci tokomti ki kere bwire, ciyan to muleng do ken kimen na ci ne kwama duttonka bi diye kwama a yilautiye.
1PE 2:13 Ciya kange nob bikwaneb keret ker teluwe ber, ciya kange liyab bo lami Nyeu.
1PE 2:14 Kange liyabo bo dur w ci twomina mwe nob bwiranke kange caklang nobo kendo.
1PE 2:15 Wo maka kwama, maka dikero kendo an nungum nyi nobo tok ker fandaker tiye kange nobo ki kulen nereu.
1PE 2:16 Kom na nob cyerka, ko mare nange ki cyerka kime ko na ki cumom nero bwir, nyori ki yilam canga kwama.
1PE 2:17 Ne nobo gwam dur, cwi kebmibo nuwa tai kwama, ne liyabbo dur.
1PE 2:18 Canngabo ki ciya kange teluwe kimebbo, ki neci dur gwam, ko ciyare koni ka nobbo kenko kange wo cocowe, ki ciya, kange nobbo bwirko ken.
1PE 2:19 Nyo la diker caklakar, no mun nyimum kwama ri niwo birumum ner mor dikero bwiireu nuwa dotange ti mor bileker cer.
1PE 2:20 Nyori mwa fiya nyi nomo ma bwirankerer di mu mwirumum mweka? dii la muma dikero kendi mo nuwa dotange no ci mwenentiri, wo lam caklanka fiye kwama wiye.
1PE 2:21 Na cuwo ci cuwo nene, wori kritti nuwa dotange dor mwer, cin dob mwen nure kange na bwangteng naceko.
1PE 2:22 Co mabo bwiranker kakka cin fiya kerbiboler nyi co!
1PE 2:23 Fiya cuwo cin to co ci tobo nii, fiyaco con nuwa dotange, co yabo cunero cwo, dila, conne bwici nio ma bolangti dong-dongeu.
1PE 2:24 Coki bwici tu bwiran keret bero bwici dor tiyer, nabo fiyare fiye mor bwiran kere, na bo fulo mor cakcake, kideti cero ba fiya lima.
1PE 2:25 Bo gwam bi watangum na kwame lerange, la canneu ba yilanrangu fiye nii yuwa bi cir tiye karge nii to dume be tiye.
1PE 3:1 Mwor nure wuro nobo woo non nawori natubo komkwamredor bwetub kumebbo nen, natubo kom neken ner kumero bwetub kumebonen, tano kannyem cimbo mani ciya bwanka ker kwama kotiri, mulen natubo locinbo tamci, cimanki kertak, Yiilam natubo lociye men.
1PE 3:2 Nyo cin tom fwor nere mwe bijin kemwo nene.
1PE 3:3 Yori kabo bwayilen kumero ayilare na toka nuwe koce kakaa-natobwinnece mwin kange kulen.
1PE 3:4 No daten maka mwor neret na dige yorako manki diika na fwor neret na nimde kwama ce.
1PE 3:5 Nyo dige natubo dimce kako cume wo yoo ner kii kwama di ciki bwici cin neken nabarub cibo bilinkerer.
1PE 3:6 mwor nure woo cera ciya lan cuwo Abraham ki teluwe ce na moo caneu co bi beyo loce no mun maa dignge dateneri dii kange no mu man ki tai dotangeri
1PE 3:7 Mwor nure win, koom nabarubo kom yi kange natub kumebbo ano mwor cwikanka kimek, na bulendo won corbo bwiniyeu, na nawiye, kom neci biduwed na luma kwali dume. Kamati nyo naci nuwa luma dilo kumekoti.
1PE 3:8 Takka ker gwam kume kii dume cerkang bwitiyeu nyo ri nob cwikangka bwiti kume ko neka ciyaka nerkumer kange kungne.
1PE 3:9 Mani mwa ya cuner bwiranketti ki bwiranket, mani mwa ya cunet ti kibi tor ko bitor nyo naki yaken kange bilanka, nawo ci cuneneu nawo mwati fiya bilanka.
1PE 3:10 Nii wo cwiti ci nwa luma tiyeri an to kume ken ca dubum biyen cero tokka kero bwid.
1PE 3:11 Nacuri dubom nure bwira yeu naci ma diker yoriyeu la ca do luma na cilamco.
1PE 3:12 Dii nuwe kwama nii ken la too ceu nuwa bicorcero la tikob kwama boki no nubo ma biran kereu.
1PE 3:13 Wee woo nii wora woo anuwam tiye no man mwaa mwe dikero yoradi?
1PE 3:14 Na no mu nuwa dotange ki den bilenkerdi, cware diker ci cwa tiyeu, ciyare dotange.
1PE 3:15 Nyori neken yecu kritti mor neremweu ki nero wucak. Tii kibati na ciya cowe nii menen ki yee muntim kibikwan fiye kwama wiye. ma yoki mor luma kunde dor bwangten naco.
1PE 3:16 Fiyam yumkako daten nubo ma kukla mweko tiyeu, yim kale mwembo keneu mwor kritti catin nuwa kwenduwe diker bwiyeu na dikero muke ma bweran keret.
1PE 3:17 Daten na kwama cwinki mwan nuwa dotange bilenker na nubo ma bwiran kerer tiyeu.
1PE 3:18 Kritti na bwiyaka kiritti win ki den bwiran kerer. Niwo ki bilenkeu a nuwa dota-nge dorber, nobo manki bilenkereu, nyori naci bou kibo kwama nen. cin dokken co bwar mwor bwiye la ci macodi dume ki yuwa tangbe.
1PE 3:19 Ki yuwa tangbe cin nya ci bweldo biro bwaban'ngum bwaba-nge.
1PE 3:20 Diger dateneu be nwo birom nerem kwama cenciti ki cur nowa ki kumeni nuwa ywel tokombe, la kwama fulo nubo cwabce nubo narub ceri ki kwama mweme.
1PE 3:21 Woo co dankako yuka mwengek cokom nen na we kebo na yuka mwengek ko cokum dwitito bwimweu, La daten kinonka kwama kange kong yecu Almaciya.
1PE 3:22 Kritti ki no kanko cattiyed kwamar incuuken firen di kwama, bwatomange kwama bikwan keret kange bikwan tom nyo an neken co.
1PE 4:1 Nawori kiritti nuwa dotange mor nage kom koywellum bwikume nacokken niwo nuwa dotan-nge mor bwiye ceri cerum mor bwiran kerer.
1PE 4:2 Na wori niwo yi yimbiroti wu yak kala cewoninneu mani fiya ciyaka fiye nubo wiyeu kifiya ciyaka kwama wuyeu.
1PE 4:3 Kadim yimkumembo kaleweu kwarub nawo nubo ywombo kwama cwi makatiyeu yim cwikaduwek, noramkatini noka diker bilantumer, meranka cika ko bwir, kan-nge meranka diker dilangtumer.
1PE 4:4 citotiri lomcinenbo kambo mumwereu. Kangbo dor kan'nge ci mordikero yuran'nge maci kwadiker ciya fiyati dor dikerowo. Nyori ciyantok ker dor mwer.
1PE 4:5 Ciyati kiye diker cimaneu kabum niwo a ma dumenen kan'nge bwar bolang tiyeu.
1PE 4:6 Woncoo dikebwi ker kwamaro ya lam nubomanki dume, dila cin macimen bolang ko mor biye naci fiya cerka kwama nen.
1PE 4:7 Dikerogwam wi bouti bidom, nawori kom mwerum dorkumero nakom kwob dillotinim.
1PE 4:8 Dor diker gwam, kom yilamki cwika bwitikikumek, wori cwika cumwom bweranketi ducce.
1PE 4:9 Kom ci bwini bwitikumero, manki kwanere.
1PE 4:10 Komma bwitikumenen naniwo wab ker kwamarti kibilenkereu. No nii atintok kerdi ayilam ciki tok ker kwamar, tano nii atin wabwabkari, ayilam dong-dong bikwan nero rowo kwama netiyeu.
1PE 4:11 Mawuro gwam na kwama fiya caklanka mor denbiwecr yecu caklanka na yecuce diri atiyo.
1PE 4:12 Kum kebmibo, komkware komk dotan'ngewo kan'nge cwarumbowo fiya komeu nan dikero fwir fiya komwiyeu.
1PE 4:13 Tano dila kom mwerkan dorti kan'nge meciya mor nuwaka dotan'ngecekri, kom yilam kibilangtum morece, cano duktankaceko bouri.
1PE 4:14 Bibwiyer kikuom cano nubo tokomti kiden kirittiddi wori yuwa duktankak kwama ko kange yuwa tangbe kwama noti dor kumer.
1PE 4:15 Nuwaka dotan'nge kumekowe, kan'nge more kume ceu ayilare amwerum twalka dorekocue, kan'nge kwiito ceu, kange na'ngendo bwirkoceu, kan-nge ni mwerka dorekoceu.
1PE 4:16 Tano ninuwa dotan-nge ti wori cin kiritari ciya nuware kwenduwe ciya duktang kwma kidendo curo.
1PE 4:17 kwamalam nawuro bolango biyaterti dor nob kwamabeb cano aterdorberri, ayila nyi kange nubowo bwangtenbo kerr kwamareu?
1PE 4:18 Tano atin bwai naniwo caccakeu fiya certakri, ayilayi kan-nge niwo manki kwama kan-nge ni bwiran kerer?
1PE 4:19 Nawori n ubowo nuwa dotan-nge ker kwamareu ciya yoken dumeceu nii fuleenin ciyama diker dong dong ngeti.
1PE 5:1 Ma mwe nubo woti more kume min kekume dur. Mor bwanka kwama wo nyomom dotan-nge kritti, take mawi win mor nobo ya fiya duktanka wo abo tiyeu.
1PE 5:2 Kom yilam nob bi yuware kwama wo wari kan-nge kom me, kebo ki bi kwan, ayilam mo cwi kwama ti kom wabtiye, kebo na diker kwenduer fiyaka, a yilam mor cwika.
1PE 5:3 Kom yilare teluwe dor nobo kang kumekeu, na cuwori kom yilam na dangke fiye bi yuwaro wiyeu.
1PE 5:4 Na liya biyuware cerkangu di mwan yo needuwe duktankako manki ciraka.
1PE 5:5 Kom bi kalfundo kom nuwa nobo durko gwam kume kom yilam ki lom cumee kom bwanten bwiti. kwama ko nii kunka duwek, cone nob lomkome luma.
1PE 5:6 Kum daken ki dor kumero kan kwama, can kungken kom wori citokomti.
1PE 5:7 Kom cur cinen dotange kume wori co cerkumenti
1PE 5:8 Kom tiki bati bwekelkele kentangenti tulti na tirome, do nii woti ca wootiyeu, cung cimen.
1PE 5:9 Tiki bi kwan bilenker mwer nin, nyomom keb kume mor bilenker wi dor bitine ciki bi ner dotan-nge nenna kume.
1PE 5:10 Biko kom nuwa dotan-nge be dob, kwama nii luma wo cokkom mor liyar duktanka ce fiye kritti an ne kom bi kwan na mwekom.
1PE 5:11 Liyar nace diri diri. Dong dong.
1PE 5:12 Ma tiu cilas yii be nii bilenker ma mulang kume nyo bi dob mor kange ce, mayarum komti, ma nungi diker ma mulang bilenker luma kwama wo titi nyo.
1PE 5:13 Na wiye wo babila, woci cokkom wariyeu, yaru komti. kan-nge Marku yarum komti ken.
1PE 5:14 Kom yarkan bwiti kom ki cwikanka fwor neret na yi wari kan-nge kom gwam kume nii wo mor kritti.
2PE 1:1 cimon Bitru bwe changa kangye bwe tomange yeecu kiriti ki nobo wo yo digyer lumar bilenkerer nawo bi yoweu mulangum ki nobo woyo diger tumar bilenkerer nawo bi yow mwor kwaamar kange nii chokka beko yeecu kiriti.
2PE 1:2 Luma kanga damnerem wo bi fiya yeecu nin nii cok beu a cobten dutche.
2PE 1:3 ki bi kwan chero cin nebo degero gwam wo dumecheu kangye yimbo wucakeu mwor nyomka kwa'amak wo cuwobo mor dugtunkak kangye tenenka chekeu.
2PE 1:4 mwor wuro nyeu, cin nebo norre dur nyeri nabi yilam mor nobo fiya norre mulen kwa'amar nabi cokum dor ki kaya kako kale wo cuika dikero bwir bou ti cikeu
2PE 1:5 ki digerowo bwiyeu, mani kambo mwa dolum tiyeu na cobten neroken ki bilen kereronindi cobten nyomka.
2PE 1:6 kinyom kako nin di chobten taka dorer. ki takadore konin chobten birom nerem, ki birom di chobten yimbo wucake,
2PE 1:7 ki yimbo wucakeu choten ki cuikanka bwitik ki chwika bwitik chobten ki cwika
2PE 1:8 No mulendo buro gwam wi kumendi yila duyom kumendi mani kom yila chombulome ti kaga digero bwiir mwor nyomka Teluwe bek yeecu kriti.
2PE 1:9 dila nii wo manki digero buro weri la weltantigti weitagye nyori cin fugma, tabum kange bwiren kerer cerowo nirom ki bwiyeu.
2PE 1:10 nyori kebmibo komma digero kom dollum tiye nakom nyomom chwor kumero na ti yila ce no batin ma digero birodi, mani ba yarti.
2PE 1:11 nure wuro nin, batin fiya doka mor liyar kwama beg kange nii fulo bew yecu kriti. nyori man nyilam ki bati kang nami kulom kumen digero biro, bwenno nyilam kom nyumom duwaleu bwenno kom tinkiti kwan dor bilenkerero kom ciko naweu.
2PE 1:12 nyori mannyilam ki bati kang nami kulom kumen digero biro, bwen nonyilanm kom nyumom duwaleu bwen nokom tinkibi kwan dor bilenkerero kom ciko nawu.
2PE 1:13 mi kwa tiri dong dong fiye mi wiyeu nomatin nomwor bwiye wurori, mi kwatiri yori kabo in kulom kimen nawo.
2PE 1:14 mi mwor bwiye wuroweu wori min nyu.
2PE 1:15 matin ma digero madullum tiyeu nanto di ki kwama wo makuberi katin kwa digero biro ki neer kang kang.
2PE 1:16 nyori nyi bwangtengbo yulando wo bibwe nifire bow cikeu ki kwama wo nyo yikom bikwan kange boka teluwe beko yecu kriti nyori nyon tomdur ceroki nuwe nye.
2PE 1:17 lacin yo dur kangye dugtanka fiye Teekwama wiyeu ki kwama wo diro bo cinen fiye dugtanka kodur wo yiki wo bwenere mi nuwa luma chek ti dutce.
2PE 1:18 nyo nyiki bwinyo nyin nuwam dirowo yirau dii kwama tunwo ki kwama wo nyi wari kange cwo dor bangero wucakeu.
2PE 1:19 la nyin wi ki ke ti dugumer, wo daten kom yoti nereu natalkireu wo ne tilang ti kumta cile nayumb de celka finikeu ri na tulkachi na ne filang mwor nere kume.
2PE 1:20 mordigero gwam, kom nyumom keti dugumero kangee manwo ayau ti fwetengka nii keu.
2PE 1:21 na cori keti dugumero kange bombo wi fye nifiro wiyeu la yuwa tanbe kwamak dici coci tok ker kwamare.
2PE 2:1 dila nobtomange kwama cwerke bo nobo nin kange nob meranka cwerke anbo kimen. ki an bo ketito yurangum na wuronka ce kange ci an ko teluwe ciye wo tiyen ciye. ci boti ki wuronka wulom dor ciro.
2PE 2:2 Ducce nawo abwanteng nure ciye, kange morece ci anko nur bilenkere wo yilam durre.
2PE 2:3 Morkucuno ciye ci an yuwo diger ducce kimen ki ker bi boler ciro. fuwar ciro biyeken fiye wulom. kange wuronka ciko dabo dum.
2PE 2:4 Nyori kwama dobbo nobtomangem ce wucare woma morkumtacile bwiranke, la nyore kwama tunken ci morkumtacile bware, naci ku, kenci luwe kumtacile tabe, kiduka ningtang bolangti.
2PE 2:5 Yila ci dobbo kale carko, cin yoken nufu wo meran kereti cakcakeu kange nobo niber, fiye cuwo.
2PE 2:6 Ci bo ki mwem wuro ka kale nobo nyombo kwama. Kwama nyori twimbi ten codome kange gomora yilam bwiyem, wuro yilam diker nunkaro fintange nobo wo nyombo kwama.
2PE 2:7 Na lot wo cakcake co nuwa dotange fiye nobo bwanten ner ciyer tiye, nyombo werkun nen.
2PE 2:8 La nii cakcake wo yim tiber cireu, kume kange kume ner cere ti kayai mor dume cakcake ce dor kekero co towe kange co nuwau.
2PE 2:9 Teluwe diye nyimom nure ca cokum nobkwamab ti morcuwaka kange nure ca tam nobo mani cakcake na comwe cibi diye bolange.
2PE 2:10 Wo bilen kere dor nobo ki dilanka bwiyek kange cwe kanka nobo Ki bi kwang keret, dor ciro kucer kange cima dike ci cwiti, maci cwatai nobdutonka.
2PE 2:11 Nobtomange kwama wucake wi ki bikang kange wo la ciye nyori ci bobo ki kiyange fiye teluwe diye nin.
2PE 2:12 Nyori bi ciro manki kwa dikeri cin maci na bii tabi biyem. ci cwekan dikero wo ci nymbe, ci anbwiyam.
2PE 2:13 Ci an fiye nan bwiran nangene ciye ci kwa nuwaka lima ti diye wona lima ce. dor ciro cin twelum, ci nuwo lima nangene ciye bi bolere ti, fiye cuwo ci nuwa lima ti kange kom me.
2PE 2:14 Ci wi ki nuwe burotum natubem, nobburokab, kero bwir mani lacine ner ci kwou nobo wo ti boyorau mornangene ciye bwiranye, nyori cin cuati ner ciro dor kucunur ci bibei cii ka.
2PE 2:15 Cin dubom nur bilen ke, cin ko nyori cin bwanteng nure, Balamu bi bwe Be'ore, ni wo bilan fiya ka yokka mordikero kebo cakcake,
2PE 2:16 Nyori yuwo weranka dor bwiran keret ce, kelba mani tok kere, weran nii tomange kwama wo twelum twele ki dir nifiret.
2PE 2:17 Nobo buro ci na buir man kimwem na bilor wo yuwa mwe meko yeecu cike kumtacile durwi ningtang ci ti.
2PE 2:18 Cin nobtokka kerek koni kange nobcwika dorek. ci bol nobo ti fiye dilanka bwiyek. cibol nobo ti, wuro cwiti naci cwam fiye nobo yimbo yorbe.
2PE 2:19 cin manobo nin cor ciyan cerci, ci ki bwici canga fiye bwiran ke. nyori nii cange fiye dike kwob ner cere.
2PE 2:20 Ni wo cerum kalenm fiye nyomka teluwe kange nii fuloka yeecu yila nyonti mor burotum bo ni neu, damcembo a cuwa bwir tiye anla kabako bwiraka.
2PE 2:21 La cinen diker noci nyombo nure nyime cakcake, kange wo ci nyimom di ci dubom werfundo ci ne ciye.
2PE 2:22 Nuka kereko wo bilenke fiye ci wiye Bicwiye yilaken kwiye ce kange ngyere yilati fiye dwiti”
2PE 3:1 farub mib tomange wo na yobe ce ma mulang kume ne, take gwam ciye na kulum kace na ne kom bi kwan nere
2PE 3:2 be na kom bulamgi ki kero nob tomange kange werfune wo teluwebe kange nii wo yafulo be nee nob tomange be
2PE 3:3 yomom nob buwomeb an bow diye dika kume. ciyan buwo dike ci cwiye
2PE 3:4 ciyan yii kom kin fee nor yilakako? ka ciko tebbebo daken dume, dikero gwam tim ka cikca kwatti ter fwelkake.
2PE 3:5 ci ki mantum tabum fiya no ki ker kwamar dii ko kange Bitru fiya yime mor mweme
2PE 3:6 take mwem wer kale, kale dim ka mwem
2PE 3:7 ka cikna kere, dii ko kange dor bitiner kum kira yome bi diye bolange kange werka nobo bwang ten bo kwama.
2PE 3:8 farub kom tabre kume win fiye Teluwebe diye nine, na coro kwini bikate, coro kwini bikate na kume wine
2PE 3:9 kwama tibrang bo ki norcero, nawo kangem yi ti ki. tibrang tiye, nyeu co bii ner dor mwer co cwibo kange kume a kayam, di la gwam na fiya da yiloka
2PE 3:10 duwal kume kwama a bo na nii kuye. dii ko a cum ki diro dur. tibitinimbo a twim ki kira. tab-tab.
2PE 3:11 nyori tibitininbo wo gwam anwuro, nyeu ka yila nobo wani? kom yii wucak kange cwi kwama.
2PE 3:12 kom ningtang diye boka kwama ko ti, diye co dii kwama an werum ki kira, tibitinimbo wuyak bwiyem kicilen kambo ken.
2PE 3:13 dila nor ce, bo nintang dii kwama fwirko kange dor bitinero fwirko wo nobo cak-cak a yim tiye.
2PE 3:14 nyori faumib, nyeu ko cwi dige wo tiyeu, dibe ko ti bati a fiya nen de ki duti mo tim cakcak kabom cem ki fowor nere.
2PE 3:15 take to birum nee kwama co fulokako, nawo yibe bulu mulange ki yilen do kwama ne co.
2PE 3:16 bulu tok dige wo mor bi fumer ceronin, wo kangem dikero wi wo bwai nyomka. fwandika kange nobo tibo fiye wine bongum digero wo na wo ci ma kangem bifumero ni neu, nur bware ciye
2PE 3:17 na weu farubmib kweri ka nyomom digerowo nyeu, ywelum bwi kume, kati nobo bwangten bo werfunere bol kom, lem bilenkere kume nin. la kom
2PE 3:18 dwi mor luma kange nyomka teluwe nii fuloka Yeecu kiritti duktangka na ce diri-diri
1JO 1:1 dike wo fiya ki kaba, wuro ba nuwau, wuro ba to ki mwebeu, wuro ba to kani beu, fiye ker dumer.
1JO 1:2 dumeu lan fwetanco, bon warker nyon yi kom fulen kerero kwatti diiriyeu, wuro ki no teenmeu lan kwa dir cer
1JO 1:3 wuro nyo to nya nuwa nya kwa dir cer, na kom mwerkang dor kange nyo, mwer kan ka duwek beko ki no kange teeu kange bi bwece Yeecu Almacifu
1JO 1:4 nyo nya mulanng kumen dike buroti na for neerer nyero na dim
1JO 1:5 wonco tanmange nyanuwa fiye co wiyeu, nya kwa dircer kumene kwama filang, kum tacili mani cinen bi duware ce,
1JO 1:6 na bo ki bo mwerkang dor ti kange co, la boya yamti mor kumtaciliri, bo ki cwerke, mani bo ma bilenkerti
1JO 1:7 nobi ya yam bo ti mor filange na wo co mor filange, bo mwekang dor ti bwiti be bwiyal bi bwece Yeecu nirom bwirano ker bero gwang
1JO 1:8 na boki man kibwirankeri, bo ki bol dor ber, bilenker mani more be
1JO 1:9 la na bo tok bwirankerer berori con nii cini, nii cak cake, wo a cutang binen bwiran kerer bero tiyeu, na nirum bo mor bweni cakcakeu,
1JO 1:10 na bo ki ba ma bo bwiran kere di bon tu con nii cwerke ker cero mani
1JO 2:1 bi be yo lomi ma mulang kume woti kati yilo ko ma bwiranka benno kange ma bwiranka ri, bon wi nii fiye te wiyeu, co Yeecu Almacuhu nii be, kebe cakcaen.
1JO 2:2 co ni fanko mur bwiranka be, kebe kabe ki kwace, la kange dor bitine roce gwam.
1JO 2:3 la nyeu co ma nyumom la bon nyumomco na bo bwang ten werfuner cerori.
1JO 2:4 nii wo ki con “nyumom kwama,” la bwangten bo werfuner cereri nii cwerke bilenkero mani wercer.
1JO 2:5 la nii wo bwanten kercereri, bi com cwika kwama ko dii ti nii wo nin la nyo bo nyumom biki no more ce,
1JO 2:6 na nii wo ki co ki no mor kwamari, tam ca yam bo wo Yeecu Almacifu yau.
1JO 2:7 nubo ma cwi- cwiyeu kebo werfunero fwir ma mulan kumentiye, lan co werfundo carko ka nuwam ki kabau.
1JO 2:8 na weu maki mulangkumen werfundo fwir, wom bilen nere mor Almacihu ti cuyi, filanko ti,
1JO 2:9 nii wo ki co ki no mor filangeu na ko kece tiye, ki no mor kumtacili duwal
1JO 2:10 wo na cwi ke ce tiyeri, ki no mor filange, dike a dor kottanka tiyeu mani cinen
1JO 2:11 na wo ko kece tiyeri ki no mor kumtacili yila ki ya kumtacili, nyombo fiye co yom doreu, wori kumtacili fikanum mwe ceu
1JO 2:12 ma mulan kumen wo kom bi beyo lomi ma cwi-cwiyeu wo ni cin cutam kumen bwiran ke kume wi ker denece.
1JO 2:13 man mulang kumen tebbo, wori kom nyumom co, wuro wi tun ki kabau. man mulang kumen kom bi bei bayolobeu wori kom wi kibi kwan la ker kwamaro yimwi more kume, wokom cam turani kange bwerko. man mulan kumen bi be yo, wori kom nyumom teeu.
1JO 2:14 man mulan kumen tebbo, wori kom nyumom co won wi fiya ki kabau, man mulang kumen bi bei ba yilo bei wori kom wi kibi kwan la ker kwamaro yim more kume, la kom cam turani ki bwirko
1JO 2:15 ko cwire kalewo, kaka dike mor kalewo, no na kange cwi kale wori cwika teeka mani more ce.
1JO 2:16 wori dikero gwam fo dor bitinereu, kuru bwiye, dike nuwe dilan tiyeu, kange yim kangka doreko bwir, kebe wo teece na dorbitinero ti cui kange dilanka ceko
1JO 2:17 dor bitinero ti cui kange dilanka ceko na nii ma dike kwama cwitiyeu con nowi kwatti diri
1JO 2:18 bi beyo bi dutinum, kaleu kwemum na wo ka nuwa nii kiye Almacifu wi bou ti la wo nyeu nob kiyeu nob kiyeb Almacifu kila kwerin biye ken la nyeu co nyo nyumom ciko nyoki kaleu kwenume.
1JO 2:19 ci cer bore be, kwati yeu na ci kebo na be, la ci na ci be ri na citin ca kaba kange bo, la na wo cin cerumeu, won nungi ci kebo more be
1JO 2:20 la kumeu kon yom cor ka mwengek yuwa tang be kwama ko nin, la gwam kume kom nyumom bilenke,
1JO 2:21 ma mulang kumem bo miki ka nyom bo bilenker wori kom nyumom la kange cwerke cerubo wibilenkenin
1JO 2:22 we nii cwerkeu, co nii yi Yeecu kebo kiritti nii wo co nii kiye Almacifu. wori co ciya tee co ciya bo bweceu
1JO 2:23 kange nii mani wo ciya bo bwere, wite tee nii wo ciya ki bweri wi ki teu
1JO 2:24 la kange komtak, iako dobti dike ka nuwa ki kabau ayi more kume, na dike ka nuwa ki kaban yikam more kumeri, kom kenen kan yi mor”bwe nin kange mor teeu”
1JO 2:25 noro co nebeu dume diiriyeu,
1JO 2:26 ma mulngkumen kom nure.
1JO 2:27 wo kumeu, corka nuwangekowuro ka yo cineneu wi more kume, ka do kange nii bou na meram kumen. la na cor ka mwangeko ka yo cineneu kurang kumen dikero gwam la bilenker, cwerke mani wi more ci
1JO 2:28 na weu bi be yo lomi ma cwi-cwiyeu, ko no wi more ce kambo ca cer kangu tiyeri bou mana yilam ki yonenri, kebo ki kwen, duwe, kalum cem, ca bou tiyeu.
1JO 2:29 na kom nyumom co cak-cakri, kom nyumom nuwa wo yin yim bo cak-cake tiyeu, cin bom bowe cinen.
1JO 3:1 ko dukum cwi kanbo wo kwama nebeu, la a co moti bi bei kwama cu wo bou nyo co kero wo dor bitinero nyom bobe, wori nyom co bo
1JO 3:2 woma cwii cwiiyeu, na wen bo bi bei kwama. la ci fwetang binen bo keno ba yila nyi ri, bwiri, bon nyumom kanbo Almacifu a cerkangum ti yu, ban yilam na co wori ban to co na wuro co nyeu.
1JO 3:3 nii wo ca wi ki yonenriye luwe fini yeri a yi yimwuca kem, na wo ce co wucakeu.
1JO 3:4 nii wo ca kaba ki ma ka bwirankere di la yabum werfundo wori bwiran ke yabka werfuner
1JO 3:5 kom nyumom Almacifu cenkangum na co tum bwirankere, la co man kibwiranke.
1JO 3:6 nii mani a noti more ce lana a ma bwirankererti, kange nii mani a ca kaba tiki ma ka bwira kere di ki con nyumom co. kaka con tom co
1JO 3:7 bi beyo lomi ma cwii -cwiiyeu ko dobre kange nii a tiyangum ki kom wo ma dii cakcak tiyeu” na wo Almacifu cak-cakeu
1JO 3:8 wo ma bwiran ke tiyeu na bwekelkele, ce wori bwekelkele mam bwiranke fiye ki kaba, co dike bwi bwe kwama cer kangeu we, na co bubam na ngen bwekelkelero
1JO 3:9 na nii wo ci bou co kwama nine ri mani ma bwirankere. wori dum kwamambo wi morece mani a ca kaba tiki maka bwirankere, wori boo con kwama nin
1JO 3:10 wi nyo bo nyom de bi bei kwa kange bwekelkelece ki dimene wuro mani ma diki wulake tiyeu, kebo bi bei kwama, la wo mani cin ke ce tiyeu
1JO 3:11 won co tomange ka nuwa ki kabau, tokti bo cwiti be
1JO 3:12 kebo na kayim wuro na bwekelkeleceu twalum yii ceu, ye bwi co twalum ce? wori nangen cero ka bwir yii ce ceu cakcak
1JO 3:13 ko mare nyumanka kebmibo, na dor bitinero ko komri
1JO 3:14 bon nyumom bon tiya ngum bwar bon yaken dume, wori bo cwii kebbeboti. wori mani ma cwikari, bwiyam bwiya.
1JO 3:15 nii wona ko ke ce tiyeri nii twalka duwek. lakom nyumom dume diiriyeu man na nii twalka duweko ce.
1JO 3:16 la nyomom cwika, la Almacifu neken dumece ken bereu. bo kenen daten bo neken bo neken dume ker yitob beb. la na nii wo kikulen dor bitinereri con to kece ki cwika la nuwa bo cini ce, lanyi cwiika kwama ko more ce?
1JO 3:18 bibeyo lomi ma cwii-cwiiyeu, bo more cwii ka ko tol nyiyereu koni, la bo ma nangen cwiikaro ki bilenker
1JO 3:19 la nyo bon nyumom nob bilen ker bon nyumom neer bero ka co
1JO 3:20 no na neer bero kuwa bobori, kwama la ner bero dwiika, la ki nyomka diker gwam
1JO 3:21 nubo ma cwii cwii na neer bero kuwa bobori, bon wi kab-kab kabum kwama
1JO 3:22 dike ba duweri ban fiya fiye co wiye gwam wori bo bwang ten werfuner ceroti, bo ma dike yo cinen neere ti
1JO 3:23 la nyial ke ce na wer, bo ne bilenker ki der bi bwece Yeecu Almacifu, bo cwii bwiti be na wo ca ne bo werfunereu
1JO 3:24 na wo bwangten ker nyial kwaro tiyeu wi more ce, kwama neneu wimor ni co nyo la ba nyumom con wi more be ki yuwa tangbeca nebeu.
1JO 4:1 tano nyo nob cwi ka miko kom ciyere kange yuwa tangbe no nyori kom cuwa yuwa tanngbeko kom nyimom no kwama ceri la nyo nob dukkumecwer ducce wifo mwor kalewo
1JO 4:2 nyokak nyimom yuwa tongbako gwam ciya kange kiritti Almaciya bou mworon bwiyeri na kwama ce
1JO 4:3 no nyori yuwa tangbako ciya bo kange keritti kobo na kwamace, co yuwa tangbako, wo ko kange Almaciya kom nuwa wi botiye, kweri bi yeken wifo mwor kalewo
1JO 4:4 kom bi beiyo curou nob kwama nine, kweri kom cam kaba diye bwiye” niworu fwer kumereu lawuro fo kalewo bidiwiyer
1JO 4:5 ci na kalece dige ci toktiyeu na kalece, yilo kaleu nuwa citi
1JO 4:6 nyo na kwama ce, gwam ni wo nyimom kwama nurang yoti wuro kebo na kwama cemani nuwarang yoti co fiye nyo nyimom yuwa tangba keni kange yuwa tangba cwerke
1JO 4:7 nob cwika mikko bi cwi butibi dila na kwama ce wono ki cwikadi ci bo cedi kino firen kwama, dila con nyimom kwama
1JO 4:8 ni wo man ki cwi ka cwibo kwama niworo nyombo kwama, dila kwama cwika, nyo more ce ci cwika kwama cwika, nyo morece ci cwika kwama,
1JO 4:9 binene kwama tomu bibwece wo nyo wine fo kalewo dige bwiye nabi bu wi cimen
1JO 4:10 nyo wi more curo cwika wi kebo bo bi cwi kwama dila kwama cwibe co tomu bi bweco na cok binen bwirangker lero
1JO 4:11 nob cwika miko kambo kwama bi langbo nyowe daten bilang butibi
1JO 4:12 ni kange mani wo tom kwama wiye no bi cwiti bwitibiri kwama yimwi more be, dila cwika wi nyimom morebe,
1JO 4:13 cofiye ba nyimom ti ciki no morebe co keneu co ki no morebe dige bwiyeu naco bo yuwa cekko
1JO 4:14 bin tom bin ne bilengke biki kwama bi bwece, na yilam nii fuloka kale
1JO 4:15 gwam niwo ciya kiritti bi bwe kwama ri kwama yim morece co kene co mwor kwama
1JO 4:16 bin nyimom bin ne bilengke cwi ka kwama woru mabinen tiye, kwama cwika, wa yim mwor cwikari yim mwor cwika kwama, kwama la yim mworece
1JO 4:17 nyo no wurori cwika kwama fiyam fiye yime tiber kumet nakom yimki nyomka kambo ken kibi diye warka, kambo co no curo nyie, bona curoken wimwor kalewo
1JO 4:18 twai mani mwor cwika la cwika kendo bouti ki twai, dige bwiye twaiyo ken kange warka dila niwo ki twaiyeu manki cwika ko ken
1JO 4:19 bi cwi bileng lati dige bwiye kwama ten maka cwika beke
1JO 4:20 no nika tok ki ci cwi kwama tiri la ci ko kecetiri nii cwerke, tano niwo cwibo kece wuroci totiyeri, mani ce cwikwama wuro mani cototiyeti
1JO 4:21 wuro co kero nyo cike ci mone, gwam niwo cwi kwama tiye tam nyo ca bilang yice,
1JO 5:1 gwam niwo ne bilingke kiritti co Almaciya bo bowe na kwama ce dila gwam niwo cwi tee con cwi bi bwe tee bowe
1JO 5:2 kambo nyo nyimom nyo cwi bi bei kwama ki kwama nyo cwi kwama dila nyo ma nanger kercer
1JO 5:3 wuro co cwika kwama, coki bi bwangten dircero dige biyeu dir cero kebo wuro na wo a tubinen tiye.
1JO 5:4 gwam niwo na bor kwama ce ki bi cwome ri ki man caka kababo nyo kange kala? wo co caka kaba wo cam kale na bilinge kebe
1JO 5:5 we niwuro fiyam caka kaba kange kale? kan co ni wuro ne bilingke ki kiritti bi bwe kwama,
1JO 5:6 won co wuro wo mwor mwenge kange bwiyale
1JO 5:7 dige bwiye kangem bo wi nyo ta'ar wuro ne bilingke
1JO 5:8 yuwa, kange mwem, kange bwiyale wuro nyo taare ker ciyero win
1JO 5:9 no bin yo ker niber, ker kwama lakidwiyika. wo co ker kwamaro na tok ker dor bi bwece
1JO 5:10 wo ne bilingre kange bi bwe kwama kero wi wari kange kwama co tok bo ki ni cwer ke, nebo bilingke ki ker kwama tok dor bibwece
1JO 5:11 wuro co kero, kwama nebo dume wo man ki dika dume wuro wi mwor bibwe ce
1JO 5:12 gwam niwo ki bwe, wi ki dume
1JO 5:13 mi mulang kumen wuro na kom nyimom kom wi ki dume manki dika wi kumen nubo buro bilangke ki de kwama
1JO 5:14 wuro co kero kibi kwan bi cuko kabum ceme dila tano nonye bilingke cwika cerer atin nebo
1JO 5:15 nyo tok, no bin nyimom co nuwa bo tiri, gwam nobo kinong diger ci mendi bin nyimom gwam dige wuro bi kinong ci mene
1JO 5:16 no ni kange to yice woma bwirangka lobo bworo ceri ca kwab ci nen dulo, kwama atin neco dume mir nun nubo buro kero bwir wo labo bware, bwirang kero kange wo bou ti ki bware mi tok bo mi ca kwab dulo curo nin
1JO 5:17 gwam dige yorbe, bwirarke dila bwirangke kange wi wo laubo bware
1JO 5:18 nyon nyimom nubo bu bo bowe wuro mwor kwama mani ma bwiranre la wuro ci bo wi mwor kwama, yatin cu kom co ni bwirko wo mani ca ma ci nen digerti
1JO 5:19 bin nyimom bi na kwama ce, bin nyimom gwang digero ki no kange bwirko wuro
1JO 5:20 la bin nyimom bi bwe kwama bo, la con ne fwetangka na bi nyimom wuro co na bilingka ce nyo tok bi ki no wuro na bilingkece yila mwor bi bwece kiritti Almaciya. co ki kwama na biling kece, kange na dume ce diiri
1JO 5:21 bibeiyo kom ciyare ki dor ki kume maka fulen.
2JO 1:1 minen nii dur yaken cuko nawiiye ma kwameu kange bi beyo loceu wo mi cuiti mor bilenke kebo ka mokange gwam wuro nyimom bilenkeu.
2JO 1:2 ker bilenkero wo bineneu an yii tibinen diiri
2JO 1:3 lima cire-duwe kange for nerek an yi kange bo fiye tebe kwama kange Yeecu kiritti bi bwe teu mor bilenke kange cwika
2JO 1:4 min bilengi duccu ma fiya kange bi beyo lome yayamti mor bilenke, nawo ma yuwou werfundo tebe nii,
2JO 1:5 na weu mi ken nenti kebo na wo mi mulang mwen werfundo fwir tiye, nyori na woba yuwo ki kabaubi cwi butibo
2JO 1:6 won co cwi kako ki bi yaa yam kange werfundo wo co werfundo na mwa nuwa ki kabau, ki bi ya yam more ce.
2JO 1:7 no bi bolebo ceruu duccu dor bitiner, ciyabo kange Yeecu kiritti wo bou mor bwiye. woro co nii bi bolero kange nii kiiye.
2JO 1:8 ko to bwikimeu kati bi cwrang dikero wo ba ma na ngen cereu, nyo tak ri nabi yuwo
2JO 1:9 ni wo ya yamti kebo mor mwrangka kiritti, nombo kwama wuro ya yamti mor merangka wii ki teu kange bweu.
2JO 1:10 nii wo nobou muneng bou bo ki merangka ko weu, yuwo core mor luwe mwe, yarum core tar
2JO 1:11 wo no yurum ce ri ciya kange merangka ceko bwirko
2JO 1:12 miki dike ducce ma mulang mwen tye, nyori ma cwibo mulang mwen ki diker mulangka dike. miki yo neri bou munen na yii nen nuwa kange nuwa, na bilentum bembo na dim
2JO 1:13 bi beyo lo korya mwe wo cokum me yrum nen ti.
3JO 1:1 ni dur yaken ciko Gayus nin wo mi cwiti mor bilenkeu
3JO 1:2 moni micwitiyeu mi diloti fiye bi bwiyer, kange twaka, nawo dume mwe kwamereu.
3JO 1:3 miki for neret ducce, wori yitub mwebo kangym bo yii ye warke dor bilenke mwe, na wo mo yati mor bilenke
3JO 1:4 mi man ki for nerero wolawo nan nuwa bi beyo lomi ya yamti mor bilenke
3JO 1:5 kom womi cwiti-cwiyeu ka merangkange fabub ri, wone warke dor cwika mweke nuwa nobo nawan kwama nintiye an yori ma no mo ma cinnen tikali ki for neret wo doten nure kwama
3JO 1:7 wori ci cerker denrero wo, ci yuwo diker fiye nobo nyombo kwama nin.
3JO 1:8 na yilam for nangenne wo bilenke ceu.
3JO 1:9 min mulang tomange fiye nobo kwangten kwama tiye wori diyotiriffis wo lo cobo cwika durek more kimeu yuwo bo bo
3JO 1:10 nyori non bou ri, man yii co twam nangen ne ce wo, kange den bero co kangti tiber niber ki ker cero bwirangi nyeu wuro la cinen bo, tak ci ko yuwaka yitub be bo ti, cin nyowam nibo cwiti na ci ma nyeu, nyori co nywa citi mor nubo mwanten kwanten kwama tiye
3JO 1:11 mo niwo mi cwitiye, merang de dikero bwir, merang dikero ken. nuwa ma dikero ken tiye nob kwamab ma dikero kwer tiye nyombo kwama
3JO 1:12 dimitiriya yuwo warka ken nubo nin gwam kange bilenke ki bwici nyo ma nyon warker dor cer, kin nyimom waeke nyeu bilenke
3JO 1:13 miki diker ducce wo ma mulang mwen tiye, nyori ma cwibo mulangmwen ki diker mulangka dike
3JO 1:14 man bou na to nen kutaqnbo, ban tok ker tikob kange tikob fwor neret akange mo farubbo yarum nenti yarum ki den mir
JUD 1:1 Yahuza canga Yeesu Alamasiya, take yi Yakubu, fiye nubo co cowe wiye, Nubo ma cwiye mor kwama Tee cokumcoke na Yeesu Kristi ce.
JUD 1:2 Cireduwe, kange daka neret kange cwika a bwii fiye kumenen.
JUD 1:3 Nubo ma cwiye mi ma nyi bi kwane na mulang kumen ki ker fuloka beko gwam, tam makumen biweret kambo dor bilenker wo ci ne nubo bwantenco tiye Krisiti win cwar yokka man.
JUD 1:4 Di kange nubo curab dou ki dang yurangum yurange, wuro ci mulangi dor warke ciye fiya ki kutanka con man ki bilenker, wuro folongum luma kwama kange kayaka, take cin kanangum nii wine, dur kange Teluwebe, Yeesu Almasiya.
JUD 1:5 Mi cwiti nan bulang kumen bwen duwale kweri kom nyomom dikeco, ki yika kwama fulo nubokangem beten masare, di ki bwi con twallangum nubo nebo bilenke.
JUD 1:6 nob. tomange ce wucakke wuro tabo dur bikwan ciyere di cin dubom fiye ciye kwattiye, kwama bwelmaro diri mor kumtacile fir nimde kakuko durko, wo bolange ce.
JUD 1:7 Ci nyo na saduma kange Gomarata, kange bertinimbo kentangum kange ciyeu wuro neken dor ciyero kayaka, ci bwangten dilankakoti wo kebo wo daten. di cin yilam diker danke wuro ci nuwa kira manki dika.
JUD 1:8 Nyo nob dukumenbo wuro ci kan bwiciye ti, ci cwekan liyab boti take ci tok dikeroti dor wo na duktangkakoce.
JUD 1:9 Di bwen nob tomangebo wucake, dur nob tomangebbo wucake fiya co kwobkanti kange kwalkanka kange bwekelkele dor bilen Musa, letankbo tokka kero kange na warka ko ce dor cer. Nyo co yi ki Di Teluwe a kwenang mwenteng.
JUD 1:10 Di nubo wuro boti ki kunka dor ci nyombe gwam. nubo wuro wiki mulen biyuwaret, ci kwob dorcero nen buwar.
JUD 1:11 Kwanci wari cin bwangten nure kayinu, take cin yarken mor letanka bal'amu ki na ci fiya mwem cin bwiyam mor funere nawo kora ceu.
JUD 1:12 Wuro naba yurangum yurange mor cika kume na cwikace cin nuwa ti ka luma kwenduwe man, tai man. Ka dor cir ci catiye ki kwaci, Ci biloro wo mani bo ki mweme wo yuwako ywa cotiye. cin tini tirangum bitutti man, bilentini kiriti yob, kwomkwobe fiya nintini nin.
JUD 1:13 cin mwelangka mwemek wima wo ki ki bibutetwele, ci kwilangti mor funi kwenduwe ciye. Ciki no nabitirendo certiye wuro ci tank kumtacili fi kiriti kiriti diri diri.
JUD 1:14 Ahnuhu nii na nibere ce teu Adamu nin ma dukume ddor ciyer ki, To Teluwe an boki nob cebo wucakke bikatentini.
JUD 1:15 Co warum ki warka dor nubo gwam, ya mwa nubo mani nuware mor nangen ciyer na bongtu wo ci mani nure wo datenbe kange keti wo cilongi wo nob bwirangke tokangi dor cere.
JUD 1:16 Burombo ci yiti toki kom toke, nob fwennab, wuro bwangten dilanka ciyekoti na cile ce, burombo ma nyalti ki kwilanka, nob wambirub na fiya ka ciyeko.
JUD 1:17 Di la kom nubo ma cwiye kom bulangi, kange ketito wo nob tomange Yeesu Almasiya be ci yi kom nanduwo.
JUD 1:18 Cin yi kom ki, “Mor kume ni cwile, an fiya nob mwankerebo wuro bwanten dilangka ciyekoti na bwini wabe.
JUD 1:19 Nubo wuro nob boti ki yalkangka, takeu, ci bibei dorbitiner, ci man ki yuwa tangbeko wucakke.
JUD 1:20 Di la kom nubo ma cwiye, kom mu dor kumero nen bilenker la gwamme kom na bwayilence, take kom kwob diloti mor yuwa tangbeko wucakke.
JUD 1:21 Kom tam dor kumero mor cwika kwama, tak kom nintang cireduwe teluwe yeesu Almasiya wo boti ki dume diriye.
JUD 1:22 Kom nung cireduwe fiye nubo wo nyomantiye nin. Kom fulo kangembo kira ki cwabrika.
JUD 1:23 Nubo kange kom nung cinen cireduwe ki yila bwik, kom nung yai ka bwen kulendo bwiciyeri.
JUD 1:24 Nawo fiye woki bikwan na ywamkom kottangka, co dok kom ti kom ti kambu duktanka bokaceko man ki duti kange bilanktumbo tenan tenange.
JUD 1:25 Fiye kwama wine nii fulokabe fiye Yeesu Almasiya Teluwe, duktangka, dur kange liyar kange bikwan a no nimde fiyang gwam, nawo kange diri, A ti nyo.

REV 4:1 Bwiko dikero bwro, min too, la nyiiloko dik kwama wumom-wume. Diro ki kaba ma nuwau, namwi namutun-mwen dike yii ti ki, “Bou fo dii nan nung mwen dike a bwiti kumeni weu.
REV 4:2 kang dangchang mi mor yuwa tangbe, la min too kutile lúyare mor dii kwama, nii kange nyiim wi dor cher,
REV 4:3 Nii wo nyim wi dor chereu, cherkang yasfa kange yakutu. kwang-yabe kentangum kutile liyare chuwo. kwang-yabe cherkang.
REV 4:4 Kangum fiti nyim liyarem kumi-yob chulombo naar kentangum kutile liare wo, dor fiti yime buro, nobbo dur kwiri-yob chwhombo naar yiirongum wi ki kulendo fwor kange walbile liyabe milbangtiye chumangum dor chir.
REV 4:5 Fiye kufite liyare wiyeu milbangka cheruu ti wi, diir dike wurongtiye kange kun-nye. Talkiretini nibeer ta kira ti kabum kutile liyare, tal kiretin yuwa tangbe kwaama nibeer.
REV 4:6 Kabum kutile liyare nin wiima (gilache) wo tibati na (crystal) tiber kutile liyareu, kentangum wi kutile liyare, diker ki dume nyo naar bwam ka nuwe, bwii kange kab.
REV 4:7 Dike ki dume kaabau, na turome, dike ki dume na yabe cheu na be nenne, dike ki chume na taare cheuwii ki tikob na nii fir, Ia naare cheu wii ki tikob na fiinge kwenti-kweneu.
REV 4:8 Dike buro ki dume naareu, wirangi ki tangum nukikun-nukkun, bwam ki nuwe dii kange tob. kume kange kakuk, chi dobbo takka, “wuchak, wuchak, wuchak, teluwebe kwaama nii kibi kwang gwamme, cho wure, cho duwen, cho kabe.
REV 4:9 Fiya chuwo dike buro ki dume ne duktongka, dur kange buka kangeke ri, nobbo durko wo kuni yob chulombo naaren, yarken bitine kabum nii wo yiim kutile liyare wab cho wo fuloti bak-ni-bakeu.
REV 4:10 chi yoken wambile liyare chiweu kabum kutile liyare, takti ki,
REV 4:11 laminye mo teluwe be kange kwaama be, yuwo duktong ka kange dur kange bikwan, mo ma ywel dikero gwamme, ki chiyaka mwe chi yime, chi ywelchiye.”
REV 5:1 La min too kangko chattiyere nii wo yim kutile liyare, bifimer mulangum-mulange kab kange bwiko, bifimer mulangum-mulange kab kange bwiko, chrin kwati yrom liyam wi nibeer.
REV 5:2 Min too bwe tomange kwaama wo kibi kwanne, kwa dirti kibi kwang, “We daten a wumom bifimero ti na kim yirombo chi kwatiye?
REV 5:3 Nii mani dii kwaama kaka dor bifiner kaka mor bifie wo lam a wom bifimero ti kaka cha kiyerao dike more cheu.
REV 5:4 Min chii wiiye chillen, wori ma fuya bo nii wo daten a wom bifimero na kiyerangu dike wiye.
REV 5:5 La wiin mor nobbo dureu yii ye ki,”chiire wiye. Too turome dum yafuji, niiye Dauda ma turanni, cho cha wom bifumero kange yirombochi kwatiye”
REV 5:6 Min too be kwame tim tiber fiyé kútile liyare wiye mor dikero buro ki dume naare, mor nobbo durko nin. mo too ri namwi chi twallum-twal. wi ki chume niber kange nuwe niber, wuro chi yuwa tangbe kwaama chi tomi gwam kale.
REV 5:7 chon yá chon tuu bifumero mor kang nii wo yiim kutile liyare.
REV 5:8 Kambo chitum bifumereu, dikero naar ki dumen kange nobbo durko kuri yobb chulombo naareu, yarkam bitine kabum be kwame, gwam chiye wirangi kibi benn kange kange kwele mwine dim ki kwaama ki kunn fichange, mwine dhilo nob kwaama wuchake.
REV 5:9 Chin kaa nuwe ewir, “mon daten tuu bifumero na wumom yiro mbo chi kwatiye, chin biyem nen, ki bwiyale mwe mwa tiyen kwaama nin nobbe gwam olum, nyii kange kale.
REV 5:10 mon ywel chú nob liyare kange nob wabeb na chi bwang kwaama ninten na chi liyar dor kaler.
REV 5:11 Lamin too ri min nuwa dir be bei tomange kwaama duche wo kantgum kutile liyare, kange dike buro ki dume kange nobbo durko,
REV 5:12 Kilaka chiyeko lam bikwate kwob kiritibikate kwob kange kiriti bikate, chin tokker ki diro dur “Lamiyeu mo be kwaame, wochi biyem ri yuwo bikwan, chweka, wicdom dwktongka kange ohaklangka”
REV 5:13 Min nuwa dike chi fuli, dii kwaam, kange kale, kange mor kale kange wo dor wima, gwam dikero more chiye tokti ki, “Fiye nii wo yim kutile liyareu, fiye be kwame ninne, a ne chaklamka, dur, duktongka kange bi kwan liyaret bak-ni-bak”.

REV 8:1 Kituremi bekwome mumom dokka kangeko nibereu, ciitam cine cin dikwama ne kangekenoke bidobe.
REV 8:2 Dila minto nobtomangebo niber birombo tim kabum kwaamemen, ciin ne tencii cumen niber.
REV 8:3 Kange nii tomange bor, kanki kwel mwine wo twiks diker nunne ceu, tiken kabum tangilanner. Diker twike nunko ducce ciinece naci neken war kange dilo nuba ne bilenketiyeu gwamm dor tangi lan twiks diker kuner wo mwineceu kabum kutile liyarem.
REV 8:4 Yilom twika kunembo, kange dilotin wob neka bilinkere, cii kweni dii kabum kwaamam kange nii tomange.
REV 8:5 Nii tomange co tu kwel twika kunneko dinco ki kira fiya tanjilando wiye. Lana nyime mouco bitine dor bitiner, dila kwaka kunnyekowo, kange kunnge kange miblangkako fuwo nyeu, kange jigtongka bitinektak.

REV 8:8 Nii tomange yobe cu cumeceu, dila dikeru durko kange certang ter wo tati tabe kikira ciin mouco mor wima. win mor taare wimau yilam bwityale,
REV 8:9 win mor taare dikero kidume mor munge ciin bwiyam, la bitirendo tenang tenangeu yaruu dii, cati na kiro wenka, dor win mor taare wo cajiyoceu kange tiye bwika mungek.
REV 8:10 Nii tomange yobeu cu cumeceu, la bitirendo tenang tenang'eu yaruu firen dii, tati nakira wenka, dor win mor dikero taar wo cajitinimbocen kange bwili mwen.
REV 8:11 Denbitirenero twei, win mor taare mwem cajimbo yilam twei, dila nubo kila bwiyam wori mwemtinim be yilam twei.
REV 8:12 Nii tomange naareu cu cumeceu, lawin mor taar wo kaku ceu diker kem, wim mor taare wokakuceu kange win mor taar wo bitirendoceu. La win mor taar wo ceu gwaam mmam kumtacile, win mor taar wo kakuceu kange win mor taar wo kumeceu cii lem filnciko.

REV 9:1 Dila nii tomange nung'eu cu cumeceu. Minto bitirendo dii kwama yanu bou dorbitiner. Ciine bitirendowo nyilo nurekowo manikiyikau.
REV 9:2 Wumom nyilo nurekowo maniki yikau, La yilombo cirou na yilombo buwak kirake diore. Kakuk kang yuwako yilam kumta cile, kiker yilomero ceruuti nyilo buwake ninneu.
REV 9:3 Wi mor yilomein dila bikwake wo ciin ceruu bou dorbitiner, ciin neci bikwan nabi ningetinimbeceu mor dorbitiner.
REV 9:4 Ciin yici ciyg nuware yeratimbonin kange biluwofir wiyak kakaa ti twirak, dilla kan nubo mani ki dokka tangek kwaamak tikaob ciibeu.

REV 9:6 Ki kumemiwo nubo ado buwaro, dila maniciya fiyacoti. Ciyanma kuru buware, dila buwaro an cwaci.
REV 9:7 Bikwakeu cer kang tuwa cii tweng cii ywele. Dike kange wi na lalang duwek mwinek, tikob na niffiroce taki.
REV 9:8 Yirir ciiro winyo na natuboceu, nunciiro nawo turomeceu.
REV 9:9 Cii tirangiem ki sulke na kene tak, diir tangumacire na diir nabirer tuwar kwener kila nyeu yanu kwenemboci ywele.
REV 9:10 Ciin wi ki yalak nyonglangi nabi ningetinimboceu, ciin wi kibi kwan yalak ciikonin na ciya nemnubo dotangeti na cwakka nungece.
REV 9:11 Ciin wiki kange naliya dorciir, nii tomange buwakko maniki yika. Dencero ki Ibrancin Abadon, Ki Helengnci ri Afoliyon.
REV 9:12 Kabako cum. Tobwiyok wurokiri wi nye yob birombo boutiyeu.

REV 9:15 Nobtomangebowo naar ciiyo na kangken woceu, kange kakuko wuro kange cwakka wo, kange coro wuro tak, ciin nyamkang ciinen nacii twalum win mor taare niffere.
