REV 13:1 La nyo ma to kange Nmige ki ye cheruti wi chaji, wi ki chumeni kob kange doro niber, wi dor chumechinin biduli ngdule kob, wi dor chumenin dendo wi ki dendo bwir.
REV 13:2 Bi chiro wuro man to wi nyo na naweh natinm chebo wi nyo na bitolo nyi che na nui trome i dirangon wo cho bikwan chero bikwan dur li yareche.
REV 13:3 Win wi mor dorem bi cho, la der chero Bwir chero bim, di la kalewo chi to nyimang ka ki kwama chi bwanten bichiro tiye.
REV 13:4 Chi kene chi ne diracion dur, na cho ne durko durchero. chi ne durko chi tokti ki we na durko! we tank adol maka kiyankti kange he?
REV 13:5 Chi ne durko nyi wuro cho tokker ti na kunka doreko che kange kero bwikna cho fiya bikwan tokka kereng yaken kume kwini na'ar chulon boyob.
REV 13:6 Dila bichnro wom nyi cheu tikang kero bwirti dor kwamak chwekang Den cheroti kange fiye nyi che kange noboro yim di kwama.
REV 13:7 Chi chiya durko nin wo ma kwen kange nob kwama cho cham kaba kange chi, cih necho bikwan nai yank tinimbo nin, kange no ber.
REV 13:8 Gwam nobo yim to kale we chi ta ne cho bidwiyer gwam noboro ki kaka fwwlka kale chi mulang bo dentichero mor bifumerna be kwame che wuro chi biye.
REV 13:9 No kange wi ki tupu ki wori cha nhwa cwam nii wuro chi tuu cho ti yati ki cho fiye changa cho yatiye.
REV 13:10 Gwam nii wo chi ya twal cho ti ki kulene, kulen chi twal cho ti chike kulen chi twal chotiye wuro cho bicha wa kale cheu, birum ner kange bilenke wi ni boro wuchakke.
REV 13:11 La mo to kange, bichir wi che ru ti wi mor bitine. wi ki chume yob cherkang bekwame che yolo chon tokker na na chuwe che.
REV 13:12 Cho mw atum Dur bikwan gwam bichir kaba kabum chem di la cho dok kale kange nobo yim wi yeu chi ya ne bichir kaba dur wuro chi twa chimen twira tamwi na bware che.
REV 13:13 Ma dur bwa yilener cho dok kirako yirau bitine dikwama kabum no bem.
REV 13:14 Wa dang dike chinene cho mane, chon bolang nobo kale chon yi chi ya ma yirom kange ki der kulene di la na chuno bum.
REV 13:15 Chi chiya chimen cha ne fubom dor urom bichronin, naurom bo na tokker, cha dok chi ya twallum gwam nii ko neka bi dwiyer bichironine.
REV 13:16 Cha tok dige tamme, nobo gwam bidwurtinim kange durtinim nobo chuve chuyeu kange nob bwinem no mabwiti ki change kangehiwke chi ya yirom kan chick kange tikob.
REV 13:17 Mani a math yo Lange nii wo manki numbari Mani can ten keneti, keneceu ki nang na dencer.
REV 13:18 Wuro ki chwi yiien no nii kange wi ki yiien di cha ki yem kilatum bichior wuro. kilatum na nii fire che. kilatumbo cho wo 666.
REV 14:1 La man to bekwame tim dor bang chiyona wari kan-nge chonubo wii bikatewin kwini kwob nar turo nar che, buro chi mulang den chi re kan-nge der techere tikob chiyeb.
REV 14:2 Man nuwa dor kang-nge chiyati na dir mwenger chaji chwati kang-nge kunnye kwatiye. Diro ma nuwa cherkan nob gilingili-nge chi kwa gilingili-nge chiyeti.
REV 14:3 Chi ka nuwe fwir kabum kutile liyare kang-nge kabum fule wo kwareche nare kang-nge nubo durtinimbo. kang-nge mani wo tiye, la kan nubo 144,000 wuro chi fan-ngu chi dor bitinere.
REV 14:4 burombo chi wuor chi mam bo kayaka wi kang-nge natubed; la chi warum dur chiyero wuchak kang-nge mulen daunkuram. wuro cho bwawer bekwameti gwam fiye cho ya wiye, chi wo fan-ngu mor nube na chi yiam bilca kabak kwama kang-nge bekwame.
REV 14:5 Chwerke uyambou nji, chi man ki duti.
REV 14:6 Man tô bwetomange wucchake kang-nge kweni tiber dii kwama, wo ki fulen do bak lumi nyeu, a yi dorbitinerotiye, na wo a yii bertinimbo ti gwamme kang-nge nyini, kang-nge nubo.
REV 14:7 Cho bichor ki diro dur, kom nuwa tai kwama, kom ductang cho. la bolang chelco lam. wabcho, cho wo ma diiko kang-nge bitine, kang-nge wima, kang-nge wuchak, bwetoman-nge wuchake wo yobe che, bwa-ngu yiti ki, yarum babila, babila durko yarum, wuro bol nubo irko gwan a nôô mwen bitutti tiye burotum cheme.
REV 14:8 ka-nge betoma-nge kwentiniim bwetoman-nge wuchwce WO yobe che, bwa-ngu yiti ki yarum babila durko yarum, euro bol nuto firko gwan a nōō muen bitutti tiye burotum cheme. kan-ngu chi ki Dirk kuean Keane, yiti ki nawo wab bichir do wo nii kang-nge fulen chereri, yo kulang kangchek kalca tikobchekeri.
REV 14:10 Cho ken chan nōō mwca bituti funere kwang, mwen bitutti WO chi choir chan chak mor kwel funere che, WO no no cheri chiyan necho dotang-nge ki Kris, kang-nge kriako fuwor, kabum nubo wuchak biboi to man-nge kwama kang-nge bekwame.
REV 14:11 Yilom dotang-nge chiye to kweni dii diri-diri, take chi mankind fobka kume Lange kalck-buro chi nubo chi wab bi chirp Lange dubi che, Lange gwam buro yo yirom dene che.
REV 14:12 Euro chi bichor bika mwirumka burombo wuchakke, buro bwamten werfuner kwamara ki bilenke mor yechi.”
REV 14:13 Man nuwa bi chirp dii kwama yiti ki mulang wo, nob bibwiyer nobo bwiyam bwiya wo bwiya mor Teluwer yuwatangbeko wuchakke yii ki long work chin fubom kang-nge dotang-nge chiye, di la nangen chiyero bwang chinenten.
REV 14:14 Ma tori biloro fuorko wo. him biloko nine tamwi bibwenifire. wiiki nēēduwe Maine dorcher kang-nge bilore wo cha bye kangchek.
REV 14:15 Do kang-nge bwetomange wuchakke cheri bikur wabker, chi bi cho bi chirp kibi tūū bilor mwe yoten kang biyeka bito ko wuro kini biyeka bitoko dorbitinero lam.
REV 14:16 La wo him for bilore mobken bilore che dorbitiner, la biyen dorbitineo.
REV 14:17 Kang-nge bwe to mange wuchake cheri mor biker saber feren dii kwama, cho kene wiki bilore cha bye.
REV 14:18 Kang-nge bwetomange wuchake cheri tanjila twita nuwang fichanger wo with ki bi kwan aber kirer. cho bi chirp ki dior kwamkwame wuro rin tankî bilore cha-nye, tūū bilore mwe cha-nyeu mweru bitutti mabi tii Mani wo dorbitiro n'm, mabi BIM”
REV 14:19 Bwetomange wuchake met bilore che, mweru bitutti mabi dorbitinere chorkeu mor tale due wo chi yamum mwen mabi finer kwamar.
REV 14:20 Chi fuwarangum fiye yanka bitutti mabi bwim chinanlor bwiyale chuati fiye yamka bitutti mabi, land NGO na duka nyi tuwak, yaken Mel Kai kwob yob.
REV 15:1 Man Tó kange yirum dii kwama Tenangi ne yumanka; Bibei tomange wuchake niber ki fenjange niber, wo cho fenjange chwabire, ki cho funer kwamaro a diitiye.
REV 15:2 Man Tó dike fiya na cher kanguweu nyo na chaji nuweturome tibati mwer kangum kange kira. Tim kangchaji chi nubo ki trini dor biyuwaro kange cher kang ka chek kange kulangko nung denchere. chi ka nume musa, chan-nge kwama, kange nuwe békwame; Nan-nge muero ka dur ne nyumankati, Té kwama, ni bi kwwane gwam wuchak kam-nge bilenke nure mwe. liya nubo fire.
REV 15:3 Wé mari a nuwa tai mwe tiye téé, nacho dukteug den mwere. Wori ka mó winchwor wo wuchake. Nobo nyombo kwama chiyam bo kabum mwen ci wabnen, wori naangen mwero fwetangiwuchak.
REV 15:4 We mani a cwanentiye Teluwe, na chaklang dimwereu? Mo ki kwamo mun wucak. Kalewo gwam ciya boy na was men na nimde mo, na wo cakcake.
REV 15:5 zwiko dige wurombo ma tó, bi kur waber warka dii kwama.
REV 15:6 Fiye wuchak wuchake, bibei tonange wuchake niber buro tamki fenjage riber chhin bó. chi mera-ngum ki kulen do wuwake kan-nge yuanko chumer wo tiba nyeu, chi chakka-ngum changchang chiyeko ki mwin.
REV 15:7 Win mor fuléwo nar kwache né bibei tomange wuchak ni bere tacha mwine niber olinki funer kwamar wo kwarche diri diriyeu.
REV 15:8 Bkur wabero dir ki yilom duktang ka ih wama kange bikwan cher. ka-nge man a dol dokachecki, fenjange riber wo bibei toma-nge wuchak nibere diminme.
REV 16:1 Man nuwa diro dur co bicor mor ku wabe yi nobtomange wucakeu, ko ya ko coru niber wo funer kwamaro ceu dor bitiner.
REV 16:2 Nii tomange wucake kabau yam coru dike mor kwewa ceu dor bitire, detiyo bwira-bwirau twirmangteneu bou mbo brombo ki cami bisirereu nubo wuro wab frle cereu.
REV 16:3 Nii toange wulakeu yobeu yan coru ce dike mor kwelya ceu mor wima yilam bwiyale na bwiyal nii mmyame, la dikebor ki dume coru dike kwelya ceu mor canjiyaramgeum.
REV 16:4 Nii tomange wucakeu tareu coru dike kwelya ceu mor canjiui kange kwenti mwenge la yilam bunyale.
REV 16:5 Man nuwa nii tomange wucakeu mwemen,” To ki mon nii dong-donge. mo na wo mo nonduwo; wori war bocangko dong-dongeu.
REV 16:6 Wri cin cor bwi-yale wab dukumeb mwebo kange mbo bwangtere ti wucakeu. mon he ci bwiyale ra ci nom dike daten kange ciye.
REV 16:7 La man nuwa tanjilando wucakeu kare, ong tewwe kwama nii bikwane bwolang mweko dong dong. bilenke.
REV 16:8 Nii tomange wucakeu Nareu corn dike mor kwelya ceu dor kakuked, lan ciya ciren twirang nubo ki kira.
REV 16:9 cin twira aĺereko wo kirako twicitiyeu cin nng dikaka ki den kwamar nii kibikwan dor cotireroweu. la ci yilo tenbo na ci re kwama dur.
REV 16:10 La nii tomange rungeu, coru dike mor kwelya ceu dor fiye yime bisireu, la kumta ciliu ciyam liyar cero, ci kirong biyenti cciyeroti ker alener.
REV 16:11 Cii too kwama nii diko ki ker twirero kange detito, duwal ryeu cin ko ra ci y'uaten die bor ci matiyeu.
REV 16:12 Nii tomange wkkureu coru dike mor kwelya ceu mor caji durko yufiretus, mwemcem kuicim, ra ywelum nnre wo liyabo bro yauti nutuwa a domtiyeu.
REV 16:13 Man to yuwa kelkeliko taar wo cerkang bilareu cerauguti mor nyiye bwekl kelerin, kange biciro.
REV 16:14 Cin yuwa kelkelik ci manang dike myumankaro kila kilau. cin cen ciki yam liyabo kila-kuanin dor bitirero wo ra mwermm ci fiye win na ma ka kwereko ce kakmk kwamko duko.
REV 16:15 “ To ii ma bou na niikwiye, nii bibwi-yereco nii yimki batiyeu. dum ki kulen cer, ia mani ca certi kwenjer ra to kwanjer cero.
REV 16:16 cin bou ki ci fintange coti ki armagidoneu kiryi ibrariya.
REV 16:17 Nii tomange wrcake nibereu coru dike mor kwalya cen dor yuwar, la diro durko kange cern mor ku wabe kaange fuyeti yi toki-”Dim.”
REV 16:18 Lan ma miblanka, kange mukaka bitinek, mukka knwu la tangnim bo ro mammanre wiyeu fiyaco bi bwe rifer yim dor bitimeru, makakko ra dur.
REV 16:19 Cinam loro durko kabkangum more taar, ciman dur wab kumta cilibo yamm. la kwama kwaki Babila durko, la re cinan loro corin mwem tiyem bo dim kweleu wo ma ki funeer kwamareu.
REV 16:20 Diyele diramum, la bangtimmbo mari t ti tak.
REV 16:21 Biteten kwaman dwko turongi riyeu yarangu dii dor mmber, la cin tookwama ker cotire teten kwamaro wori tetendo nerci dotange.
REV 17:1 Win mor nob tomange wucak nikbereu bro tabangum ki kwalyatimm mbiru, bou yi ye, man mwen warka bulongeko durko wo mwati nawye burtume wro yim dor meemtimm bo kila-kila nineu.
REV 17:2 Kange co liyabo dor bitinereu ma bwiratum tiye ki nyom burotum cembo yorbeu, dok mbo yim dor bitineren wo masti.
REV 17:3 La nii tomange wucakeu, tu ye mor yuwa tangbek yaken ki mo mor kiye, la man to nawiye yim dor bisirero fiyer dimri denti dilakar. bisiro co wi ki doiro riber kange sume ri kwob.
REV 17:4 Nawiye comerum ki kulen do yiwe kange-fiye cin cor cinen mwin kange tetendo mwin kange tetendo ki kiyemereu. co tam ki kwelmwenge mwine dimki kulen burotumer kange bwiratum kil-kila. kange duti brira tumeceu.
REV 17:5 Tikob ceb den mulangum wi ki yurke. “Babila durko” Nee nos burotumed kange dike bwira dor bitiuereu.
REV 17:6 Ma to nawiye co nom briyale nubo bwang kwama rin tiyeu ma to coti kange rubo ci twali ker den yeecureu, kambo matoce ri la man nyumangi ki bi com.
REV 17:7 la nii tomange wucakeu me ye, ye bwimo nyumang tiye? man yi ren yurke nawiyeu kange bisiro wo tuceu, bisiro wo ki dotiro riber kange cumeri kwobeu.
REV 17:8 Bisiro wo mo to kwattiyeu, mari can, darom a ceruti-mor buwarke cuwau, la can yakan twalan ka. Nubo yim dor bitinereu, ki kulka dor bitinereu. ci an nyuma ngi na ci tobisiro wo wi kwatti mani can, la da-dom bouka.
REV 17:9 Bisor wo ki mbo wo ki yulaneu, doro ribereu bangtini niber wo niber wo nawieu yim dor cire.
REV 17:10 Cin liyab niber tak, liyabo nung yargum, kum win catiye, wineu la bo bouti, la na bouri ca ti na kumtium bo bidobece.
REV 17:11 Bisiro wi kwatti, na wo maniyeu, con liya naraubeu, coki wo kange brombo ribereu
REV 17:12 Cumei wo mo to kwobeu liywab kwob wo ba yo ci bo yo buri, la ci ar yo bikwando na liyabe ciyeu ra kang kereko wine kange bisiro.
REV 17:13 Neerciyero wir cin neker liar ciro kange bikwan ciyero bisiro ni.
REV 17:14 Ci am tekwen kan be bar kwameu, la be bar kwame am cam liya liyabe la war kange co ci bro cocoweu, cok-cokeu kange wob bilenker.
REV 17:15 Nii tomange wiicokeu yi ye, mwembo wo mwa toen ro nawúye burotume yim dor cereu, nob mwerkako kilo-uẃa bitenni kange njini.
REV 17:16 Cumeri m'ber wo mo toweu-ci kange am ko nawiye burotumeu. ci an kwinco na to kwanjer cero ci an narge ceu ci an twim co ki kira gwam.
REV 17:17 Wori kwama yoti reer cirger na ci ma dike co cirye ki ciyaka cek, na ci rener bikwan liyare ciyero bisiro nin, ker kwamaro dim rimre.
REV 17:18 Nawiye mo toweu cocinamloro dirko ki bikwan a ta liyabo dor bitinero tiye.
REV 18:1 Bwiko dige burombo gwam, man to bwetange wuchakke kang-nge yirauti dii kwama. wi ki bikwando dut kambo ken, dorbitnero tiba ki dwamgka chek.
REV 18:2 Cho bi chor ki chiro kwamkwame ki,” yarum, Babila tenaginye yarum! yilam fiye yime kelkelib, kangye fiye mwerangka yuwako bwir
REV 18:3 Nubo gwam nom mwen inabi burotuwchenbo cho. Nob chwekako olorbitine chi chwen kibi kwan chika cher fenjange che fiya kom.
REV 18:4 “Di ma nuwa chiro kang-nge kwama yi ki, “kom cheru more che, nobmoib kom more bwirangke na chiye, kari ferjange che fiya kom.
REV 18:5 Bwiranke chiye mweri cweri lam dii kwama bulangi nand-ngen lam bwira yeu.

REV 18:7 Nawo oho kun dor cherotiye cho chatika chila che, kom ne cho dotang-nge kalaka kang-nge fir rer nyo. Wori chom toki mor nere che “ma yim na liya, maa kebo nawiye bune, mani ma yii kangbuwati.

REV 18:14 Charito kiyeu mu yoten nerroi kange bikwamwi gwam cii cerum munen. mwekor ciin lem, marri afiyacitiak.
REV 18:15 Nob miyekabo durembo wo kulendo biromdoceu cii cwecikeu, ciyati firen kutanghi kange co, ker cwaka dotanyhencek, wiye kange wiye buwa fir neret.

REV 19:1 Bwiko dike tinim buro ri man nuwa diro kange wo cerkang dir nubo ducce dii kwama cii tok ti ki, “halliluya, fuloka duk tangka, kange bikwan na kwama be ce.
REV 19:2 Warke ceu bilenke ri cwika duwe mani, wori cin warker nawiye dor burotume durko wo kangum dor bitiner ro ki burotum cem me. Cin yam nando co ki bwiyale canga tini ce wo co nanwiye ki burotume coreu.
REV 19:3 Ciin tok ker owo yobe ceu. Haliluya yilombo ceru cinen bak-nin bak.
REV 19:4 Nubo dur tinimbo cilombo naareu kange dikero wo ci fweli ki dume naareu ciin yarken bitine cii wab kwama, wo yim dor kutile liyareu. Cii tok ti ki “Ati nyo, Halliluya!”
REV 19:5 La diro ceru kutile liyare nin tok ti ki “Caklang kwama be, kom canga tinni ce gwam, kom nubo ko cwa tiye, nubo ki bi bikwan lkiyare kange wo man ki kibi bikwan liyareu,”.
REV 19:6 La man nuwa diker na dor nober ducce, na diir cuka mwenger na diir kume tak, tok ti ki “halliluya!” Teluwe maliyar ti, kwama be nii bi kwane gwamme.
REV 19:7 Bi ma bititen, bi ne co dur, tak ri bi ne co duktangka wori cika naka be kwame ko nin buu ri nawiye bineu ywelum bwiceu.
REV 19:8 Ciin dub co naci dum bwiceu ki kwilendo ki filang kange wo lalang merek koceu yora dutti maniyeu (wori lalang mereko kendo twiya twiyau ki nung cak-cake nangen nob kwama ko wucakke).
REV 19:9 Nii tomange wucakke yiye ki “Mulangum wi nob bi bwiyere be buro fiya bicuuwor naci ya fiye cika naka be kwamake.” Cin yiye tak ki, “Mulangum wuro” buro bilenke ti kwama ko.
REV 19:10 man yari man canga ken kange mo, kange keb mwebburo tam warke dor Yeesu. ko wab kwama, wori warke dor Yeesu re be warke yuwa tangbe ker dukumer”.
REV 19:11 Di la mato dii kwama wumom la ma tok ri mato tuwa fuworko. Cii ki cuwo nii wo yim dor cereu ki nii ci ciya cike kange bilenke. Cike ma warke mor cak-cake ci ma kwenti.
REV 19:12 Nuwe ceu kino na biyen kirer la con wiki lalang duwek ducce dorcer. cin wiki den mulangum cinen wo no kebo cori kange nii man wo nyome.
REV 19:13 Ci dum ki belle wo cii dokken mor bwiyale. La den cero ki cuwo ti kii ker kwamak.
REV 19:14 Nob kwenebo dii kwamau bwang cinen tenti dor tuwa fuwor tini, cii dum ki kwilen lalang merek ko twiya twiyau wo fuwoce ri manki duti takeu.
REV 19:15 Mor nyire ce kulendo nyiyo cacau ceuti wo cii torang nubo kumtacilleti cikeu ri can ma liyar cer ki dang kiyemerek. ci fuwarang fiya cokka mweb Inabi ti ki dotange funer kwama nii bikwane gwamme.
REV 19:16 Cin wiki den mulangum bellece nen kange ki co “Liya Liyabbe, teluwe, teluwe tini”.
REV 19:17 Man to bwe tomange wuccake tim kakuk. Ci cuwo bi cuwor tikidiro dur fiye bilibetini cuto dor re “ko bou, ko mweri wari caka cika ko dur kwama ce.
REV 19:18 Ko bou ko no wo nang liyatini nang nubo ne bi weret tiye, nang nubo dure, nang tuwa tini kange nubo kwob ci tiye kange nang nubo gwam, wo ki cerka kange cangabbo nubo kwanneu kange buro man kibi kwanneu.
REV 19:19 Man to durtini liyatinimbo dor bitineu kange nob kweneb cebo. Ciki mweri naci te kwen kange wo dor tuware kange nob kweneb ceko.
REV 19:20 Cin tam liya dor bitinere durko kange nob tomangeb dukumer cwerke wo merang diker nyimanka ti kaceu. Ki diker nyimangka tini buro cin bolang buro yom yirom biciro wo kange buro ma tati bak-bakeu
REV 19:21 Ciin twallangum tangnim cem bo ki kulen do ceru nyi nii wo dor tuwereu. Bilibeu gwam-gwam carangum bilentini ceu.
REV 20:1 La min to ni nagen kwama yirauti firen di kwama, wiki diker kang cek.
REV 20:2 La ci too no cwe charko wuro cho bwekelkele bwamco coro kwini bikate.
REV 20:3 Ciin merken co mor buwakke wo manki dikau nung. co kwati dur liyar cerwi dor cer. Nyo na wo kariyilo ci bolangten nubo nyombo ker kwamaere wo adimti coro lam bikate. bwiko wo di tam nyo a nyamkang cimen bi duwar.
REV 20:4 La wi man too fitiyimken nubo wuro yim dor cereu chi nubo chi neci bi kwan bolange. Lami to dume nubowo chi mwatang doreu ki ker Yeesu kang ker kwamar. Ci wabo bicirin kange diro cerkangce, chin ko ywoaka cerkangka tikob ci kang kangcik cin fulongum yim cimbo, cin ca liyar kange bibwekwama coro lam bikate.
REV 20:5 Tang ni nubo bwiyameu, yilaubo ki dume, no coro bikate dimeri na yimde. Wuro co kwenka nubo bwiyameu ki kaba.
REV 20:6 Nii wo fiya calangka wucakeu, co nii wo ki tureni mor kwenka nubo ki kaba. buro wo yobe mani ki bikwan dor nubo wuro. Ciya yilam nubo wab kwama kange bibwe kwama ciya yi liyar kange co ki coro bi kate.
REV 20:7 Lano coro bikate lamdi, ciya cikom bwekelkele furcuna.
REV 20:8 Can cerken kale na co bolang nubo ti wo nyumbo ker kwamareu, kung nari kalewe Gog kange magog mweranci na kwenece kilatum cembo dong dong kange biyabombo caji yeu.
REV 20:9 Cin yati kale wuro ni cin kangtangum fiye nubo ne bilenke wiyeu ci yimwe. La kirako yirau di kwama twirang ci.
REV 20:10 Bwekelkele wo bolcitiyeu merken co mor kire wo furko cabie, fiye ci merum nange nicwerke ni wabka ciya nuwa dotange kume kange kakuk bak-ni-bak.
REV 20:11 Lami to dikero dor ko kange nubo yim dorcere. kalewo kange di kwama cin cwam tikobcem, la cin manki fiye ciya yakentiye.
REV 20:12 Min to nubo kwarangum me nubo dur kange bibei ci tirangum wi kabum na gwomfe la cin wo bifimtini. la ci wom bifimer dumero. Bilendo an macimen bolang ki diker mulangum mor takarau, ki dikero ci maneu.
REV 20:13 Wima nubo wanang mureceu. Bwararo kange lo bibwetinim, nubo bwangten mbwanang mureceu ci macimen bolang dong dong kange diker ci maneu.
REV 20:14 La ci merken wuro kang lobibwiti kira. Wuro co bwaro wo yobbe bitike Kira.
REV 20:15 Kwarub niwo ci fibo dencer mulang mulange mor bifumer dumeri, can merken co kira.
REV 21:1 La min to dii kwam fwir kange dorbitinero fwir, wori dii kwama wo ki ƙabau kange dorbitiner ƙabako cum, kange wima mani.
REV 21:2 Min to cinan loro wucakeu, Urusalima fwirko, wo yirau dii kwama Kwama nin, ywelum ywele na bine ci manten bwayilen ker nina bare cereu.
REV 21:3 Min diro dur dor kutile liyare tok ti ki, “To! fiye yime Kwamau kino wari kange nubo fir tini, tak keu ca yi kange cii. Cii an yilam nubo loce, la Kwama ki bwico an yi kange cii, can yilam Kwama ciye.
REV 21:4 Can wam mwem nuwem ciyembo wiyak nuwe ciye, bwaro mani a kumti tak, kakaa fir neret, kakaa wiye, kakaa dotange. Dikerro car ko cum.
REV 21:5 Co nii wo ci yim dor kutile liyareu yiki,” To! mi yilam ki dikero kwarub fwice.” Con tiki, “Mulangum wuro wori ketito buro daten ciyaka kange bilenke.”
REV 21:6 Cin yiye ciki, “Dike buro dim! Min alpha kange omega, terka kange dika ki niwo nuwa dilo mwe tiyeu man nee co noka ki lime nek fiye mwem dumem bo ceruw tiyeu.
REV 21:7 Nii wo fiya tureniye ri atin ye kwali dikero buro, la man yilam Kwama ce, co can yilam bibwe mi.
REV 21:8 Dila nubo buro tārangi nyeu, nob bwini bilenkeb, nnubo ma dikero ti yei nyeu, nubo twal dortiyeu, nubo ma bwiratum tiyeu, nub buwabbebo, nubo wab fulen tiyeu, kange nob cwerke bo gwam, fiye yime ceu an yila mor kirako diriye. Cuwo bwaro yobeu.
REV 21:9 Wiin mor bibei tomange diikwama nibereu bou mi nen, wo ki kwellini niber dim ki fencangê bwiko nibereu, yiki, “Bou fo. man nang mwen bineu fwirko, Bibwe Kwama
REV 21:10 La cin tuye mor yuwa tangba cu ki mo bangko durko cwemi nye ri cin dang mencinan loro wucakke Urchalima ceru dii Kwama yirauti fiye Kwama nine.
REV 21:11 Uruchalima wiki duktongka Kwamak, wo mim langka ceko kino na bicuka bwayilenne, na terro tiblangti tiblange- wo ki filang na ter dacenner.
REV 21:12 Cin wi ki tiyakko duwi duwe, ki nyilotini kwob cilom bo yob, ki nob tomangebo dii kwamau kwob cilombo yob nyilotini ko nin. Dor nyilo tini cin mulangti tuwe loni kwob cilombo yob wo bibei Icraila ciyeu.
REV 21:13 Cungako twareu nyiloko wi ta'ar, bangkonin nyiloko ta'ar kwacalmen nyiloko wi ta'ar.
REV 21:14 Tiyak cinan loro wiki kwar mukaro kwob cilombo yob, wi dor ciyer takeu dentini nob tomangeb wo Be Kwame Kwama ko kwob cilom bo yobbe.
REV 21:15 Co nii wo tokker kange meu, wiki dang mwin nek naci cuwam cinanloro, nyilo ceko kange tiyak ceko.
REV 21:16 Cinanloro ci muweu, cuwemtum cembo kino donki donki kange, kwiyatum cembo. Cin cuwam cinanloro ki dank cuwakam, bikateu kwob cilombo yob ki cwemer (Cunga ceko, kwiyatum cembo, kange cwemtum cembo dongi dongi)
REV 21:17 Cin cuwam ten tiyak ceko tak, tu tum cembo nako 475.2 ki cuwaka nifirek.( Wo co cuwaka bibei tomange Kwama ko dii kwamau).
REV 21:18 Tiyakko cii muki jaspa, la cinanloro ka den mwiner, wo twelum na nuwe turome.
REV 21:19 Kwar tiyak kero cin man ten bwayilen ki tero ken. Wo ki kabau jaspa, yobe ceu saffir, taare ceu agat, naare ceu emaral
REV 21:20 nunge ceu onis, nukkune ceucardiyus, nibere ceu kimsolat, wo naurube ceu beril, wo teere ceu tofaz, kwobbe ceukirisofaras, wo kwob cilombo wiinee ceu yakinta, kwobcilombo yobe ceu ametis.
REV 21:21 Nyiloko kwob cilombo yob beu co kwilen bwayilenero kwob cilombo yobeu; nyilo ki wiin wiine ci ywelang ki kwilen bwayilenero wiin wiin. nur le tini mor cinan loro nineu ci ywilang ki den mwinner na nuwee turome yanglangeu.
REV 21:22 Mi tobo bikur waber wi mor cinar loro nin, wori Teeluwe nii bikwane gwam kange Bekwameu cii bikur waber cero.
REV 21:23 Cinan loro dobo kakuk kakaa cwiyako na ne filang cinen wori duktangka Kwama ko ne filang koti cinen, la tal kira ceu co Bekwameu.
REV 21:24 Nubo kumtaciliu atin ya-yam mor filang cinanlore ko co. Liyatini dor bitinereu atin borangu ki yora ciyeko more ce.
REV 21:25 Nyilo tini ceu mani a nung ti ki kakuk, takkeu, kume mani wi.
REV 21:26 Ci an bouki yorak kange neka durek nubo kumta ciliu more ce.
REV 21:27 La dike kange man wo ki duti yeu a doti more ce. Gwam nii wo ma dike kange ti wo kwenduwe ceu kakaa ki cwerke a dotiye, dila ka nubo buro den ciyero mulangum mor diker mulangkar dumek Bekwame ke.
REV 22:1 la bibwe tomange wucake, nang men caji mwem dumem wo manki dutiye. ceruti kutile liyar kwama ka-nge be kwameceu
REV 22:2 tiber dor nurero cinar lore. bwatiye dume wi kongeni caji nin, wo ne bituti ti wangko kwob culombo yob mor cwiyake. lallu tiye ceu na twaka nobbeko bitentine.
REV 22:3 ciilka mani tak. kutile liyar kwama ka-nge be kwame ceu, a nowi cinnar loro nin, cangab cebo an ma nangen cangabero.
REV 22:4 ci an to'o tikob cebo, den cero an no'o tikob cib.
REV 22:5 kume ka-nge man tak, mani ciya do'o filang tal kiristi kaka filang kakuker, wori Teluwe kwama an wen cinen. ci an ca liyar bak-ni-bak.
REV 22:6 bwe tomange wucake yii ye, “kero buro ciyam-ciyam cuko, bilengke tak. Teluwe, kwama yuwa tangbe nob dukume, tom nii tomange ce wucake na nung cangab cebo nin dige a bwiti kutangbe.”
REV 22:7 “To'o, mi bouti kutangbo, nii bibwiyere wo tam ker dukumer bifumero weu.”
REV 22:8 mo yuwana, mo ma nuwa, to'o digero weu. fiya cuwo ma nuwa ma to'o ciyau, min yarken kabum nani bibwe tomange wucake wo nangkan men citiyeu.
REV 22:9 la con yii mare nyo, min nii bwanka na mo, ka-nge yitub mweb nob dukumeb ka-nge buro ne bilengke kero wuro mor bifure wo. “wab kwama;”
REV 22:10 yii ye, cumom de ketito, wori kini dadom
REV 22:11 wuri manki cakcaka a ca kaba manki cakcake, nii wo ki dutiye, a ca kaba ki fitongka bwiyek cek. nii wo ki cakcake a ca kaba ki cakcake ce. nii wo wucake a kaba ki wucake ce”
REV 22:12 “To'o mi bouti kutangbo, ya'aka miko wi kang mik, man ya'a nobo gwam dong-dong ka-nge nangendo ci maneu.
REV 22:13 Mo Alpha ka-nge Omega, kaba ka-nge cwile, terka dige ka-nge cwile ce.
REV 22:14 Nob bibwiyer nobbo nirum belle ciye na fiya ciyaka na ci ca bwatiye dume, takeu na ci doken cinnar lor nyiilo cek.
REV 22:15 kaleu, bicwetini, nob buwab, nob fuleneb, nob kayatum, nob twalkab, ka-nge nobo gwam wo bilang maka digero bwir tiye.
REV 22:16 mo Yeesu, min tomu bwe tomange wucake na ne kom warke dige buro na nob bwangka kwama. mo dimer na niya Dauda bitiner burit wo flange.
REV 22:17 yuwa tangbe ka-nge bine cin tokki, “bou” wuro nuwari a toki ak-nge ki, “bou” nii wo nuwa dulomwe tiye ka-nge nii wo cwitiye ca bou na ci fiya mwem dumem luma.
REV 22:18 mi yii nobbo gwam wo nuwa keti dukume bifumere: no ka-nge yokten dor cer di, kwama an yok cinenten finjange mor bifumero weu.
REV 22:19 No ka-nge kwom wi mor ketito wo bifumer dukumereri, kwama an kwob cinen mor tii dume, mor cinar lor wucake, wuro ci mulangi mor bifumere weu.
REV 22:20 Nii wuro warker dor dige bure, yii ki, “ong; mi bouti kutangbo” Ati nyo; bou, Teluwe Yeesu;
REV 22:21 luma Teluwe be Yeesu a yii ka-nge kom gwam. Ati nyo.
